T atha śrī tantrālokaḥ
C prathamamāhnikam
AbhTa vimalakalāśrayābhinavasṛṣṭimahā jananī bharitatanuśca pañcamukhaguptarucirjanakaḥ 
AbhTb tadubhayayāmalasphuritabhāvavisargamayaṃ hṛdayamanuttarāmṛtakulaṃ mama sasphuratāt  
AbhTa naumi citpratibhāṃ devīṃ parāṃ bhairavayoginīm 
AbhTb mātṛmānaprameyāṃśaśūlāmbujakṛtāspadām  
AbhTa naumi devīṃ śarīrasthāṃ nṛtyato bhairavākṛte 
AbhTb prāvṛṇmeghaghanavyomavidyullekhāvilāsinīm  
AbhTa dīptajyotiśchaṭāpluṣṭabhedabandhatrayaṃ sphurat 
AbhTb stājjñānaśūlaṃ satpakṣavipakṣotkartanakṣamam  
AbhTa svātantryaśaktiḥ kramasaṃsisṛkṣā kramātmatā ceti vibhorvibhūtiḥ 
AbhTb tadeva devītrayamantarāstāmanuttaraṃ me prathayatsvarūpam  
AbhTa taddevatāvibhavabhāvimahāmarīcicakreśvarāyitanijasthitireka eva 
AbhTb devīsuto gaṇapatiḥ sphuradindukāntiḥ samyaksamucchalayatānmama saṃvidabdhim  
AbhTa rāgāruṇāṃ granthibilāvakīrṇa yo jālamātānavitānavṛtti 
AbhTb kalombhitaṃ bāhyapathe cakāra stānme sa macchandavibhuḥ prasannaḥ  
AbhTa traiyambakābhihitasantatitāmraparṇīsanmauktikaprakarakāntiviśeṣabhājaḥ 
AbhTb pūrve jayanti guravo guruśāstrasindhukallolakelikalanāmalakarṇadhārāḥ  
AbhTa jayati gurureka eva śrīśrīkaṇṭho bhuvi prathitaḥ 
AbhTb tadaparamūrtirbhagavān maheśvaro bhūtirājaśca  
AbhTa śrīsomānandabodhaśrīmadutpalaviniḥsṛtāḥ 
AbhTb jayanti saṃvidāmodasandarbhā dikprasarpiṇaḥ  
AbhTa tadāsvādabharāveśabṛṃhitāṃ matiṣaṭpadīm 
AbhTb gurorlakṣmaṇaguptasya nādasaṃmohinīṃ numaḥ  
AbhTa yaḥ pūrṇānandaviśrāntasarvaśāstrārthapāragaḥ 
AbhTb sa śrīcukhulako diśyādiṣṭaṃ me gururuttamaḥ  
AbhTa jayatājjagaduddhṛtikṣamosau bhagavatyā saha śaṃbhunātha ekaḥ 
AbhTb yadudīritaśāsanāṃśubhirme prakaṭoyaṃ gahanopi śāstramārgaḥ  
AbhTa santi paddhatayaścitrāḥ srotobhedeṣu bhūyasā 
AbhTb anuttaraṣaḍardhārthakrame tvekāpi nekṣyate  
AbhTa ityahaṃ bahuśaḥ sadbhiḥ śiṣyasabrahmacāribhiḥ 
AbhTb arthito racaye spaṣṭāṃ pūrṇārthā prakriyāmimām  
AbhTa śrībhaṭṭanāthacaraṇābjayugāttathā śrībhaṭṭārikāṃghriyugalādgurusantatiryā 
AbhTb bodhānyapāśaviṣanuttadupāsanotthabodhojjvalobhinavagupta idaṃ karoti  
AbhTa na tadastīha yanna śrīmālinīvijayottare 
AbhTb devadevena nirdiṣṭaṃ svaśabdenātha liṅgataḥ  
AbhTa daśāṣṭādaśavasvaṣṭabhinnaṃ yacchāsanaṃ vibhoḥ 
AbhTb tatsāraṃ trikaśāstraṃ hi tatsāraṃ mālinīmatam  
AbhTa atotrāntargataṃ sarva saṃpradāyojjhitairbudhaiḥ 
AbhTb adṛṣṭa prakaṭīkurmo gurunāthājñayā vayam  
AbhTa abhinavaguptasya kṛtiḥ seyaṃ yasyoditā gurubhirākhyā 
AbhTb trinayanacaraṇasaroruhacintanalabdhaprasiddhiriti  
AbhTa śrīśambhunāthabhāskaracaraṇanipātaprabhāpagatasaṃkocam 
AbhTb abhinavaguptahṛdambujametadvicinuta maheśapūjanahetoḥ  
ādivākyaṃ
AbhTa iha tāvatsamasteṣu śāstreṣu parigīyate 
AbhTb ajñānaṃ saṃsṛterheturjñānaṃ mokṣaikakāraṇam  
AbhTa malamajñānamicchanti saṃsārāṅkurakāraṇam 
AbhTb iti proktaṃ tathā va śrīmalinīvijayottare  
AbhTa viśeṣaṇena buddhisthe saṃsārottarakālike 
AbhTb saṃbhāvanāṃ nirasyaitadabhāve mokṣamabravīt  
AbhTa ajñānamiti na jñānābhāvaścātiprasaṅgataḥ 
AbhTb sa hi loṣṭādikepyasti na ca tasyāsti saṃsṛtiḥ  
AbhTa ato jñeyasya tattvasya sāmastyenāprathātmakam 
AbhTb jñānameva tadajñānaṃ śivasūtreṣu bhāṣitam  
AbhTa caitanyamātmā jñānaṃ ca bandha ityatra sūtrayoḥ 
AbhTb saṃśleṣetarayogāśyāmayamarthaḥ pradarśitaḥ  
AbhTa caitanyamiti bhāvāntaḥ śabdaḥ svātantryamātrakam 
AbhTb anākṣipraviśeṣaṃ sadāha sūtre purātane  
AbhTa dvitīyena tu sūtreṇa kriyāṃ vā karaṇaṃ ca vā 
AbhTb bruvatā tasya cinmātrarūpasya dvaitamucyate  
AbhTa dvaitaprathā tadajñānaṃ tucchatvādbandha ucyate 
AbhTb tata eva samucchedyamityāvṛttyānirūpitam  
AbhTa svatantrātmātiriktastu tuccho tucchopi kaścana 
AbhTb na mokṣo nāma tannāsya pṛthaṅnāmāpi gṛhyate  
AbhTa yattu jñeyasatattvasya pūrṇapūrṇaprathātmakam 
AbhTb taduttarottaraṃ jñānaṃ tattatsaṃsāraśāntidam  
AbhTa rāgādyakaluṣosmyantaḥśūnyohaṃ kartṛtojjhitaḥ 
AbhTb itthaṃ samāsavyāsābhyāṃ jñānaṃ muñcati tāvataḥ  
AbhTa tasmānmuktopyavacchedādavacchedāntarasthiteḥ 
AbhTb amukta eva muktastu sarvāvacchedavarjitaḥ  
AbhTa yattu jñeyasatattvasya jñānaṃ sarvātmanojjhitam 
AbhTb avacchedairna tatkutrāpyajñānaṃ satyamuktidam  
AbhTa jñānājñānasvarūpaṃ yaduktaṃ pratyekamapyadaḥ 
AbhTb dvidhā pauruṣabauddhatvabhidoktaṃ śivaśāsane  
AbhTa tatra puṃso yadajñānaṃ malākhyaṃ tajjamapyaya 
AbhTb svapūrṇacitkriyārūpaśivatāvaraṇātmakam  
AbhTa saṃkocidṛkkriyārūpaṃ tatpaśoravikalpitam 
AbhTb tadajñānaṃ na budghyaṃśodhyavasāyādyabhāvataḥ  
AbhTa ahamitthamidaṃ vedmītyevamadhyavasāyinī 
AbhTb ṣaṭkañcukābilāṇūtthapratibimbanato yadā  
AbhTa dhīrjāyate tadā tādṛgjñānamajñānaśabditam 
AbhTb bauddhaṃ tasya ca tatpauṃsnaṃ poṣaṇīyaṃ ca poṣṭṛca  
AbhTa kṣīṇe tu paśusaṃskāre puṃsaḥ prāptaparasthiteḥ 
AbhTb vikasvaraṃ tadvijñānaṃ pauruṣaṃ nirvikalpakam  
AbhTa vikasvarāvikalpātmajñānaucityena yāvasā 
AbhTb tadbauddhaṃ yasya tatpauṃsnaṃ prāgvatpoṣyaṃ ca poṣṭṛ ca  
AbhTa tatra dīkṣādinā pauṃsnamajñānaṃ dhvaṃsi yadyapi 
AbhTb tathāpi taccharīrānte tajjñānaṃ vyajyate sphuṭam  
AbhTa bauddhajñānena tu yadā bauddhamajñānajṛmbhitam 
AbhTb vilīyate tadā jīvanmuktiḥ karatale sthitā  
AbhTa dīkṣāpi bauddhavijñānapūrvā satyaṃ vimocikā 
AbhTb tena tatrāpi bauddhasya jñānasyāsti pradhānatā  
AbhTa jñānājñānāgataṃ caitaddvitvaṃ svāyambhuve rurau 
AbhTb mataṅgādau kṛtaṃ śrīmatkheṭapālādidaiśikaiḥ  
AbhTa tathāvidhāvasāyātmabauddhavijñānasampade 
AbhTb śāstrameva pradhānaṃ yajjñeyatattvapradarśakam  
AbhTa dīkṣayā galitepyantarajñāne pauruṣātmani 
AbhTb dhīgatasyānivṛttatvādvikalpopi hi saṃbhaveta  
AbhTa dehasadbhāvaparyantamātmabhāvo yato dhiyi 
AbhTb dehāntepi na mokṣaḥ syātpauruṣājñānahānitaḥ  
AbhTa bauddhājñānanivṛttau tu vikalponmūlanāddhruvam 
AbhTb tadaiva mokṣa ityuktaṃ dhātrā śrīmanniśāṭane  
AbhTa vikalpayuktacitastu piṇḍapātācchivaṃ brajet 
AbhTb itarastu tadaiveti śāstrasyātra pradhānataḥ  
AbhTa jñeyasya hi paraṃ tattvaṃ yaḥ prakāśātmakaḥ śivaḥ 
AbhTb nahyaprakāśarūpasya prākāśyaṃ vastutāpi vā  
AbhTa avastutāpi bhāvānāṃ camatkāraikagocarā 
AbhTb yatkuḍyasadṛśī neyaṃ dhīravastvetadityapi  
AbhTa prakāśo nāma yaścāyaṃ sarvatraiva prakāśate 
AbhTb anapahnavanīyatvāt kiṃ tasminmānakalpanaiḥ  
AbhTa pramāṇānyapi vastūnāṃ jīvitaṃ yāni tanvate 
AbhTb teṣāmapi paro jīvaḥ sa eva parameśvaraḥ  
AbhTa sarvāpahnavahevākadharmāpyevaṃ hi vartate 
AbhTb jñānamātmārthamityetanneti māṃ prati bhāsate  
AbhTa apahnutau sādhane vā vastūnāmādyamīdṛśam 
AbhTb yattatra ke pramāṇānāmupapattyupayogite  
AbhTa  missing
AbhTa kāmike tata evoktaṃ hetuvādavivarjitam 
AbhTb tasya devātidevasya parāpekṣā na vidyate  
AbhTa parasya tadapekṣatvātsvatantroyamataḥ sthitaḥ 
AbhTb anapekṣasya vaśino deśakālākṛtikramāḥ  
AbhTa niyatā neti sa vibhurnityo viśvākṛtiḥ śivaḥ 
AbhTb vibhutvātsarvago nityabhāvādādyantavarjitaḥ  
AbhTa viśvākṛtitvāccidacittadvaicitryāvabhāsakaḥ 
AbhTb tatosya bahurūpatvamuktaṃ dīkṣottarādike  
AbhTa bhuvanaṃ vigraho jyotiḥ khaṃ śabdo mantra eva ca 
AbhTb bindunādādisaṃbhinnaḥ ṣaḍvidhaḥ śiva ucyate  
AbhTa yo yadātmakatāniṣṭhastadbhāvaṃ sa prapadyate 
AbhTb vyomādiśabdavijñānātparo mokṣo na saṃśayaḥ  
AbhTa viśvākṛtitve devasya tadetaccopalakṣaṇam 
AbhTb anavacchinnatārūḍhāvavacchedalayesya ca  
AbhTa uktaṃ ca kāmike devaḥ sarvākṛtirnirākṛtiḥ 
AbhTb jaladarpaṇavattena sarvaṃ vyāptaṃ carācaram  
AbhTa na cāsya vimutādyoyaṃ dharmonyonyaṃ vibhidyate 
AbhTb eka evāsya dharmosau sarvākṣepeṇa vartate  
AbhTa tena svātantryaśaktyaiva yukta ityāñjaso vidhiḥ 
AbhTb bahuśaktitvamapyasya tacchaktyaivāviyuktatā  
AbhTa śaktiśca nāma bhāvasya svaṃ rūpaṃ mātṛkalpitam 
AbhTb tenādvayaḥ sa evāpi śaktimatparikalpane  
AbhTa mātṛklṛpte hi devasya tatra tatra vapuṣyalam 
AbhTb ko bhedo vastuto vahnerdagdhṛpaktṛtvayoriva  
AbhTa na vāsau paramārthena na kiṃcidbhāsanādṛte 
AbhTb nahyasti kiṃcittacchaktitadvadbhedopi vāstavaḥ  
AbhTa svaśaktyudrekajanakaṃ tādātmyādvastuno hi yat 
AbhTb śaktistadapi devyevaṃ bhāntyapyanyasvarūpiṇī  
AbhTa śivaścāluptavibhavastathā sṛṣṭovabhāsate 
AbhTb svasaṃvinmātṛmakure svātantryādbhāvanādiṣu  
AbhTa tasmādyena mukhenaiṣa bhātyanaṃśopi tattathā 
AbhTb śaktirityeṣa vastveva śaktitadvatkramaḥ sphuṭaḥ  
AbhTa śrīmatkiraṇaśāstre ca tatpraśnottarapūrvakam 
AbhTb anubhāvo vikalpopi mānaso na manaḥ śive  
AbhTa avijñāya śivaṃ dīkṣā kathamityatra cottaram 
AbhTb kṣudhādyanubhavo naiva vikalpo nahi mānasaḥ  
AbhTa rasādyanadhyakṣatvepi rūpādeva yathā tarum 
AbhTb vikalpo vetti tadvattu nādabindvādinā śivam  
AbhTa bahuśaktitvamasyoktaṃ śivasya yadato mahān 
AbhTb kalātattvapurārṇāṇupadādirbhedavistaraḥ  
AbhTa sṛṣṭisthititirodhānasaṃhārānugrahādi ca 
AbhTb turyamityapi devasya bahuśaktitvajṛmbhitam  
AbhTa jāgratsvapnasuṣuptānyatadatītāni yānyapi 
AbhTb tānyapyamuṣya nāthasya svātantryalaharībharaḥ  
AbhTa mahāmantreśamantreśamantrāḥ śivapurogamāḥ 
AbhTb akalau sakalaśceti śivasyaiva vibhūtayaḥ  
AbhTa tattvagrāmasya sarvasya dharmaḥ syādanapāyavān 
AbhTb ātmaiva hi svabhāvātmetyuktaṃ śrītriśiromate  
AbhTa hṛdisthaṃ sarvadehasthaṃ svabhāvasthaṃ susūkṣmakam 
AbhTb sāmūhyaṃ caiva tattvānāṃ grāmaśabdena kīrtitam  
AbhTa ātmaiva dharma ityuktaḥ śivāmṛtapariplutaḥ 
AbhTb prakāśāvasthitaṃ jñānaṃ bhāvābhāvādimadhyataḥ  
AbhTa svasthāne vartanaṃ jñeyaṃ draṣṭṛtvaṃ vigatāvṛti 
AbhTb viviktavastukathitaśuddhavijñānanirmalaḥ  
AbhTa grāmadharmavṛttiruktastasya sarvaṃ prasiddhyati 
AbhTb ūrdhva tyaktvādho viśetsa rāmastho madhyadeśagaḥ  
AbhTa gatiḥ sthānaṃ svapnajāgradunmeṣaṇanimeṣaṇe 
AbhTb dhāvanaṃ plavanaṃ caiva āyāsaḥ śaktivedanam  
AbhTa buddhibhedāstathā bhāvāḥ saṃjñāḥ karmāṇyanekaśaḥ 
AbhTb eṣa rāmo vyāpakotra śivaḥ paramakāraṇam  
AbhTa kalmaṣakṣīṇamanasā smṛtimātranirodhanāt 
AbhTb dhyāyate paramaṃ dhyeyaṃ gamāgamapade sthitam  
AbhTa paraṃ śivaṃ tu vrajati bhairavākhyaṃ japādapi 
AbhTb tatsvarūpaṃ japaḥ prokto bhāvābhāvapadacyutaḥ  
AbhTa tadatrāpi tadīyena svātantryeṇopakalpitaḥ 
AbhTb dūrāsannādiko bhedaścitsvātantryavyapekṣayā  
AbhTa evaṃ svātantryapūrṇatvādatidurghaṭakāryayam 
AbhTb kena nāma na rūpeṇa bhāsate parameśvaraḥ  
AbhTa nirāvaraṇamābhāti bhātyābṛtanijātmakaḥ 
AbhTb āvṛtānāvṛto bhāti bahudhā bhedasaṃgamāt  
AbhTa iti śaktitrayaṃ nāthe svātantryāparanāmakam 
AbhTb icchādibhirabhikhyābhirgurubhiḥ prakaṭīkṛtam  
AbhTa devo hyanvarthaśāstroktaiḥ śabdaiḥ samupadiśyate 
AbhTb mahābhairavadevoyaṃ patiryaḥ paramaḥ śivaḥ  
AbhTa viśvaṃ bibharti pūraṇadhāraṇayogena tena ca śriyate 
AbhTb savimarśatayā rava rūpataśca saṃsārabhīruhitakṛcca  
AbhTa saṃsārabhītijanitādravātparāmarśatopi hṛdi jātaḥ 
AbhTb prakaṭībhūtaṃ bhavabhayavimarśanaṃ śaktipātato yena  
AbhTa nakṣatraprerakakālatattvasaṃśoṣakāriṇo ye ca 
AbhTb kālagrāsasamādhānarasikamanaḥsu teṣu ca prakaṭaḥ  
AbhTa saṃkocipaśujanabhiye yāsāṃ ravaṇaṃ svakaraṇadevīnām 
AbhTb antarbahiścaturvidhakhecaryādikagaṇasyāpi  
AbhTa tasya svāmī saṃsāravṛttivighaṭanamahābhīmaḥ 
AbhTb bhairava iti gurubhirimairanvarthaiḥ saṃstutaḥ śāstre  
AbhTa heyopādeyakathāvirahe svānandaghanatayocchalanam 
AbhTb krīḍā sarvotkarṣeṇavartanecchā tathā svatantratvam  
AbhTa vyavaharaṇamabhinnepi svātmani bhedena saṃjalpaḥ 
AbhTb nikhilāvabhāsanācca dyotanamasya stutiryataḥ sakalam  
AbhTa tatpravaṇamātmalābhātprabhṛti samastepi kartavye 
AbhTb bodhātmakaḥ samastakriyāmayo dṛkkriyāguṇaśca gatiḥ  
AbhTa iti nirvacanaiḥ śivatanuśāstre gurubhiḥ smṛto devaḥ 
AbhTb śāsanarodhanapālanapācanayogātsa sarvamupakurute 
AbhTc tena patiḥ śreyomaya eva śivo nāśivaṃ kimapi tatra  
AbhTa īdṛgrūpaṃ kiyadapi rudropendrādiṣu sphuredyena 
AbhTb tenāvacchedanude paramamahatpadaviśeṣaṇamupāttam  
AbhTa iti yajjñeyasatattvaṃ darśyate tacchivājñayā 
AbhTb mayā svasaṃvitsattarkapatiśāstratrikakramāt  
AbhTa tasya śaktaya evaitāstisro bhānti parādikāḥ 
AbhTb sṛṣṭau sthitau laye turye tenaitā dvādaśoditāḥ  
AbhTa tāvānpūrṇasvabhāvosau paramaḥ śiva ucyate 
AbhTb tenātropāsakāḥ sākṣāttatraiva pariniṣṭhitāḥ  
AbhTa tāsāmapi ca bhedāṃśanyūnādhikyādiyojanam 
AbhTb tatsvātantryabalādeva śāstreṣu paribhāṣitam  
AbhTa ekavīro yāmalotha triśaktiścaturātmakaḥ 
AbhTb pañcamūrtiḥ ṣaḍātmāyaṃ saptakoṣṭakabhūṣitaḥ  
AbhTa navātmā daśadikchaktirekādaśakalātmakaḥ 
AbhTb dvādaśāramahācakranāyako bhairavastviti  
AbhTa evaṃ yāvatsahasrāre niḥsaṃkhyārepi vā prabhuḥ 
AbhTb viśvacakre maheśāno viśvaśaktirvijṛmbhate  
AbhTa teṣāmapi ca cakrāṇā svavargānugamātmanā 
AbhTb aikyena cakrago bhedastatra tatra nirūpitaḥ  
AbhTa catuṣṣaḍdvirdvigaṇanāyogāttraiśirase mate 
AbhTb ṣaṭcakreśvaratā nāthasyoktā citranijākṛteḥ  
AbhTa nāmāni cakradevīnāṃ tatra kṛtyavibhedataḥ 
AbhTb saumyaraudrākṛtidhyānayogīnyanvarthakalpanāt  
AbhTa ekasya saṃvinnāthasya hyāntarī pratibhā tanuḥ 
AbhTb saumyaṃ vānyanmitaṃ saṃvidūrmicakramupāsyate  
AbhTa asya syātpuṣṭirityeṣā saṃviddevī tathoditāt 
AbhTb dhyānātsaṃjalpasaṃmiśrād vyāpārāccāpi bāhyataḥ  
AbhTa sphuṭībhūtā satī bhāti tasya tādṛkphalapradā 
AbhTb puṣṭiḥ śuṣkasya sarasībhāvo jalamataḥ sitam  
AbhTa anugamya tato dhyānaṃ tatpradhānaṃ pratanyate 
AbhTb ye ca svabhāvato varṇā rasaniḥṣyandino yathā  
AbhTa dantyauṣṭhyadantyaprāyāste kaiścidvarṇaiḥ kṛtāḥ saha 
AbhTb taṃ bījabhāvamāgatya saṃvidaṃ sphuṭayanti tām  
AbhTa puṣṭiṃ kuru rasenainamāpyāyaya tarāmiti 
AbhTb saṃjalpopi vikalpātmā kiṃ tāmeva na pūrayet  
AbhTa amṛteyamidaṃ kṣīramidaṃ sarpirbalāvaham 
AbhTb tenāsya bījaṃ puṣṇīyāmityenāṃ pūrayetkriyām  
AbhTa tasmādviśveśvaro bodhabhairavaḥ samupāsyate 
AbhTb avacchedānavacchidbhyāṃ bhogamokṣārthibhirjanaiḥ  
AbhTa yepyanyadevatābhaktā ityato gururādiśat 
AbhTb ye bodhādvyatiriktaṃ hi kiṃcidyājyatayā viduḥ  
AbhTa tepi vedyaṃ viviñcānā bodhābhedena manvate 
AbhTb tenāvicchinnatāmarśarūpāhantāprathātmanaḥ  
AbhTa svayaṃprathasya na vidhiḥ sṛṣṭyātmāsya ca pūrvagaḥ 
AbhTb vedyā hi devatāsṛṣṭiḥ śakterhetoḥ samutthitā  
AbhTa ahaṃrūpā tu saṃvittirnityā svaprathanātmikā 
AbhTb vidhirniyogastryaṃśā ca bhāvanā codanātmikā  
AbhTa tadekasiddhā indrādyā vidhipūrvā hi devatāḥ 
AbhTb ahaṃbodhastu na tathā te tu saṃvedyarūpatām  
AbhTa unmagnāmeva paśyantastaṃ vidantopi no viduḥ 
AbhTb taduktaṃ na vidurmāṃ tu tattvenātaścalanti te  
AbhTa calanaṃ tu vyavacchinnarūpatāpattireva yā 
AbhTb devāndevayajo yāntītyādi tena nyarūpyata  
AbhTa nimajjya vedyatāṃ ye tu tatra saṃvinmayīṃ sthitim 
AbhTb viduste hyanavacchinnaṃ tadbhaktā api yānti mām  
AbhTa sarvatrātra hyahaṃśabdo bodhamātraikavācakaḥ 
AbhTb sa bhoktṛprabhuśabdābhyāṃ yājyayaṣṭṭatayoditaḥ  
AbhTa yājamānī saṃvideva yājyā nānyeti coditam 
AbhTb na tvākṛtiḥ kutopyanyā devatā na hi socitā  
AbhTa vidhiśca noktaḥ kopyatra mantrādi vṛttidhāma vā 
AbhTb soyamātmānamāvṛtya sthito jaḍapadaṃ gataḥ  
AbhTa āvṛtānāvṛtātmā tu devādisthāvarāntagaḥ 
AbhTb jaḍājaḍasyāpyetasya dvairūpyasyāsti citratā  
AbhTa tasya svatantrabhāvo hi kiṃ kiṃ yanna vicintayet 
AbhTb taduktaṃ triśiraḥśāstre saṃbuddha iti vetti yaḥ  
AbhTc jñeyabhāvo hi ciddharmastacchāyācchādayenna tām  c 
AbhTa tenājaḍasya bhāgasya pudgalāṇvādisaṃjñinaḥ 
AbhTb anāvaraṇabhāgāṃśe vaicitryaṃ bahudhā sthitam  
AbhTa saṃvidrūpe na bhedosti vāstavo yadyapi dhruve 
AbhTb tathāpyāvṛtinirhāsatāratamyātsa lakṣyate  
AbhTa tadvistareṇa vakṣyāmaḥ śaktipātavinirṇaye 
AbhTb samāpya paratāṃ sthaulyaprasaṃge carcayiṣyate  
AbhTa ataḥ kaṃcitpramātāraṃ prati prathayate vibhuḥ 
AbhTb pūrṇameva nijaṃ rūpaṃ kaṃcidaṃśāṃśikākramāt  
AbhTa viśvabhāvaikabhāvātmasvarūpaprathanaṃ hi yat 
AbhTb aṇūnāṃ tatparaṃ jñānaṃ tadanyadaparaṃ bahu  
AbhTa tacca sākṣādupāyena tadupāyādināpi ca 
AbhTb prathamānaṃ vicitrābhirbhaṃgībhiriha bhidyate  
AbhTa tatrāpi svaparadvāradvāritvātsarvaśoṃśaśaḥ 
AbhTb vyavadhānāvyavadhinā bhūyānbhedaḥ pravartate  
AbhTa jñānasya cābhyupāyo yo na tadajñānamucyate 
AbhTb jñānameva tu tatsūkṣmaṃ paraṃ tvicchātmakaṃ matam  
AbhTa upāyopeyabhāvastu jñānasya sthaulyaviśramaḥ 
AbhTb eṣaiva ca kriyāśaktirbandhamokṣaikakāraṇam  
AbhTa tatrādye svaparāmarśe nirvikalpaikadhāmani 
AbhTb yatsphuretprakaṭaṃ sākṣāttadicchākhyaṃ prakīrtitam  
AbhTa yathā visphuritadṛśāmanusandhiṃ vināpyalam 
AbhTb bhāti bhāvaḥ sphuṭastadvatkeṣāmapi śivātmatā  
AbhTa bhūyo bhūyo vikalpāṃśaniścayakramacarcanāt 
AbhTb yatparāmarśamabhyeti jñānopāyaṃ tu tadviduḥ  
AbhTa yattu tatkalpanāklṛptabahirbhūtārthasādhanam 
AbhTb kriyopāyaṃ tadāmnātaṃ bhedo nātrāpavargagaḥ  
AbhTa yato nānyā kriyā nāma jñānameva hi tattathā 
AbhTb rūḍheryogāntatāṃ prāptamiti śrīgamaśāsane  
AbhTa yogo nānyaḥ kriyā nānyā tattvārūḍhā hi yā matiḥ 
AbhTb svacittavāsanāśāntau sā kriyetyabhidhīyate  
AbhTa svacitte vāsanāḥ karmamalamāyāprasūtayaḥ 
AbhTb tāsāṃ śāntinimittaṃ yā matiḥ saṃvitsvabhāvikā  
AbhTa sā dehārambhibāhyasthatattvabrātādhiśāyinī 
AbhTb kriyā saiva ca yogaḥ syāttattvānāṃ cillayīkṛtau  
AbhTa lokepi kila gacchāmītyevamantaḥ sphuraiva yā 
AbhTb sā dehaṃ deśamakṣāṃścāpyāviśantī gatikriyā  
AbhTa tasmātkriyāpi yā nāma jñānameva hi sā tataḥ 
AbhTb jñānameva vimokṣāya yuktaṃ caitadudāhṛtam  
AbhTa mokṣo hi nāma naivānyaḥ svarūpaprathanaṃ hi saḥ 
AbhTb svarūpaṃ cātmanaḥ saṃvinnānyattatra tu yāḥ punaḥ  
AbhTa kriyādikāḥ śaktayastāḥ saṃvidrūpādhikā nahi 
AbhTb asaṃvidrūpatāyogāddharmiṇaścānirūpaṇāt  
AbhTa parameśvaraśāstre hi na ca kāṇādadṛṣṭivat 
AbhTb śaktīnāṃ dharmarūpāṇāmāśrayaḥ kopi kathyate  
AbhTa tataśca dṛkkriyecchādyā bhinnāścecchaktayastathā 
AbhTb ekaḥ śiva itīyaṃ vāgvastuśūnyaiva jāyate  
AbhTa tasmātsaṃvittvamevaitatsvātantryaṃ yattadapyalam 
AbhTb vivicyamānaṃ bahvīṣu paryavasyati śaktiṣu  
AbhTa yataścātmaprathā mokṣastannehāśaṅkyamīdṛśam 
AbhTb nāvaśyaṃ kāraṇātkārya tajjñānyapi na mucyate  
AbhTa yato jñānena mokṣasya yā hetuphalatoditā 
AbhTb na sā mukhyā tato nāyaṃ prasaṃga iti niścitam  
AbhTa evaṃ jñānasvabhāvaiva kriyā sthūlatvamātmani 
AbhTb yato vahati tenāsyāṃ citratā dṛśyatāṃ kila  
AbhTa kriyopāyebhyupāyānāṃ grāhyabāhyavibhedinām 
AbhTb bhedopabhedavaividhyānniḥsaṃkhyatvamavāntarāt  
AbhTa anena caitatpradhvastaṃ yatkecana śaśaṅkire 
AbhTb upāyabhedānmokṣepi bhedaḥ syāditi sūrayaḥ  
AbhTa malatacchaktividhvaṃsatirobhūcyutimadhyataḥ 
AbhTb hetubhedepi no bhinnā ghaṭadhvaṃsādivṛttivat  
AbhTa tadetattrividhatvaṃ hi śāstre śrīpūrvanāmani 
AbhTb ādeśi parameśitrā samāveśavinirṇaye  
AbhTa akiṃciccintakasyaiva guruṇā pratibodhataḥ 
AbhTb utpadyate ya āveśaḥ śāmbhavosāvidīritaḥ  
AbhTa uccārarahitaṃ vastu cetasaiva vicintayan 
AbhTb yaṃ samāveśamāpnoti śāktaḥ sotrābhidhīyate  
AbhTa uccārakaraṇadhyānavarṇasthānaprakalpanaiḥ 
AbhTb yo bhavetsa samāveśaḥ samyagāṇava ucyate  
AbhTa akiṃciccintakasyeti vikalpānupayogitā 
AbhTb tayā ca jhaṭiti jñeyasamāpattirnirūpyate  
AbhTa sā kathaṃ bhavatītyāha guruṇātigarīyasā 
AbhTb jñeyābhimukhabodhena drākprarūḍhatvaśālinā  
AbhTa tṛtīyārthe tasi vyākhyā vā vaiyadhikaraṇyataḥ 
AbhTb āveśaścāsvatantrasya svatadrūpanimajjanāt  
AbhTa paratadrūpatā śambhorādyācchaktyavibhāginaḥ 
AbhTb tenāyamatra vākyārtho vijñeyaṃ pronmiṣatsvayam  
AbhTa vināpi niścayena drāk mātṛdarpaṇabimbitam 
AbhTb mātāramadharīkurvat svāṃ vibhūtiṃ pradarśayat  
AbhTa āste hṛdayanairmalyātiśaye tāratamyataḥ 
AbhTb jñeyaṃ dvidhā ca cinmātraṃ jaḍaṃ cādyaṃ ca kalpitam  
AbhTa itarattu tathā satyaṃ tadvibhāgoyamīdṛśaḥ 
AbhTb jaḍena yaḥ samāveśaḥ sapraticchandakākṛtiḥ  
AbhTa caitanyena samāveśastādātmyaṃ nāparaṃ kila 
AbhTb tenāvikalpā saṃvittirbhāvanādyanapekṣiṇī  
AbhTa śivatādātmyamāpannā samāveśotra śāṃbhavaḥ 
AbhTb tatprasādātpunaḥ paścādbhāvinotra viniścayāḥ  
AbhTa santu tādātmyamāpannā na tu teṣāmupāyatā 
AbhTb vikalpāpekṣayā mānamavikalpamiti bruvan  
AbhTa pratyukta eva siddhaṃ hi vikalpenānugamyate 
AbhTb gṛhītamiti suspaṣṭā niścayasya yataḥ prathā  
AbhTa gṛhṇāmītyavikalpaikyabalāttu pratipadyate 
AbhTb avikalpātmasaṃvittau yā sphurattaiva vastunaḥ  
AbhTa sā siddhirna vikalpāttu vastvapekṣāvivarjitāt 
AbhTb kevalaṃ saṃvidaḥ soyaṃ nairmalyetaraviśramaḥ  
AbhTa yadvikalpānapekṣatvasāpekṣatve nijātmani 
AbhTb niśīthepi maṇijñānī vidyutkālapradarśitān  
AbhTa tāṃstānviśeṣāṃścinute ratnānāṃ bhūyasāmapi 
AbhTb nairmalyaṃ saṃvidaścedaṃ pūrvābhyāsavaśādatho  
AbhTa aniyantreśvarecchāta ityetaccarcayiṣyate 
AbhTb pañcāśadvidhatā cāsya samāveśasya varṇitā  
AbhTa tattvaṣaṭtriṃśakaitatsthasphuṭabhedābhisandhitaḥ 
AbhTb etattattvāntare yatpuṃvidyāśaktyātmakaṃ trayam  
AbhTa ambhodhikāṣṭhājvalanasaṃkhyairbhedairyataḥ kramāt 
AbhTb puṃvidyāśaktisaṃjñaṃ yattatsarvavyāpakaṃ yataḥ  
AbhTa avyāpakebhyastenedaṃ bhedena gaṇitaṃ kila 
AbhTb aśuddhiśuddhyamānatvaśuddhitastu mithopi tat  
AbhTa bhūtānyadhyakṣasiddhāni kāryahetvanumeyataḥ 
AbhTb tattvavargātpṛthagbhūtasamākhyānyata eva hi  
AbhTa sarvapratītisadbhāvagocaraṃ bhūtameva hi 
AbhTb viduścatuṣṭaye cātra sāvakāśe tadāsthitim  
AbhTa rudraśaktisamāveśaḥ pañcadhā nanu carcyate 
AbhTb kovakāśo bhavettatra bhautāveśādivarṇane  
AbhTa prasaṃgādetaditicetsamādhiḥ saṃbhavannayam 
AbhTb nāsmākaṃ mānasāvarjī loko bhinnaruciryataḥ  
AbhTa ucyate dvaitaśāstreṣu parameśādvibheditā 
AbhTb bhūtādīnāṃ yathā sātra na tathā dvayavarjite  
AbhTa yāvānṣaṭtriṃśakaḥ soyaṃ yadanyadapi kiṃcana 
AbhTb etāvatī mahādevī rudraśaktiranargalā  
AbhTa tata eva dvitīyesminnadhikāre nyarūpyata 
AbhTb dharāderviśvarūpatvaṃ pāñcadaśyādibhedataḥ  
AbhTa tasmādyathā purastherthe guṇādyaṃśāṃśikāmukhāt 
AbhTb niraṃśabhāvasaṃbodhastathaivātrāpi budhyatām  
AbhTa ata evāvikalpatvadhrauvyaprābhavavaibhavaiḥ 
AbhTb anyairvā śaktirūpatvāddharmaiḥ svasamavāyibhiḥ  
AbhTa sarvaśopyatha vāṃśena taṃ vibhuṃ parameśvaram 
AbhTb upāsate vikalpaughasaṃskārādye śrutotthitāt  
AbhTa te tattatsvavikalpāntaḥsphurattaddharmapāṭavāt 
AbhTb dharmiṇaṃ pūrṇadharmaughamabhedenādhiśerate  
AbhTa ūcivānata eva śrīvidyādhipatirādarāt 
AbhTb tvatsvarūpamavikalpamakṣajā kalpane na viṣayīkaroti cet 
AbhTc antarullikhitacitrasaṃvido no bhaveyuranubhūtayaḥ sphuṭāḥ  
AbhTa taduktaṃ śrīmataṅgādau svaśaktikiraṇātmakam 
AbhTb atha patyuradhiṣṭhānamityādyuktaṃ viśeṣaṇaiḥ  
AbhTa tasyāṃ divi sudīptātmā niṣkampocalamūrtimān 
AbhTb kāṣṭhā saiva parā sūkṣmā sarvadikkāmṛtātmikā  
AbhTa pradhvastāvaraṇā śāntā vastumātrātilālasā 
AbhTb ādyantoparatā sādhvī mūrtitvenopacaryate  
AbhTa tathopacārasyātraitannimitaṃ saprayojanam 
AbhTb tanmukhā sphuṭatā dharmiṇyāśu tanmayatāsthitiḥ  
AbhTa ta eva dharmāḥ śaktyākhyāstaistairucitarūpakaiḥ 
AbhTb ākāraiḥ paryupāsyante tanmayībhāvasiddhaye  
AbhTa tatra kācitpunaḥ śaktiranantā vā mitāśca vā 
AbhTb ākṣipeddhavatāsattvanyāyāddūrāntikatvataḥ  
AbhTa tena pūrṇasvabhāvatvaṃ prakāśatvaṃ cidātmatā 
AbhTb bhairavatvaṃ viśvaśaktīrākṣipedvyāpakatvataḥ  
AbhTa sadāśivādayastūrdhvavyāptyabhāvādadhojuṣaḥ 
AbhTb śaktīḥ samākṣipeyustadupāsāntikadūrataḥ  
AbhTa itthaṃbhāve ca śāktākhyo vaikalpikapathakramaḥ 
AbhTb iha tūkto yatastasmāt pratiyogyavikalpakam  
AbhTa avikalpapathārūḍho yena yena pathā viśet 
AbhTb dharāsadāśivāntena tena tena śivībhavet  
AbhTa nirmale hṛdaye prāgryasphuradbhūmyaṃśabhāsini 
AbhTb prakāśe tanmukhenaiva saṃvitparaśivātmatā  
AbhTa evaṃ parecchāśaktyaṃśasadupāyamimaṃ viduḥ 
AbhTb śāmbhavākhyaṃ samāveśaṃ sumatyantenivāsinaḥ  
AbhTa śāktotha bhaṇyate cetodhīmanohaṃkṛti sphuṭam 
AbhTb savikalpatayā māyāmayamicchādi vastutaḥ  
AbhTa abhimānena saṃkalpādhyavasāyakrameṇa yaḥ 
AbhTb śāktaḥ sa māyopāyopi tadante nirvikalpakaḥ  
AbhTa paśorvai yāvikalpā bhūrdaśā sā śāmbhavī param 
AbhTb apūrṇā mātṛdaurātmyāttadapāye vikasvarā  
AbhTa evaṃ vaikalpikī bhūmiḥ śākte kartṛtvavedane 
AbhTb yasyāṃ sphuṭe paraṃ tvasyāṃ saṃkocaḥ pūrvanītitaḥ  
AbhTa tathā saṃkocasaṃbhāravilāyanaparasya tu 
AbhTb sā yatheṣṭāntarābhāsakāriṇī śaktirujjvalā  
AbhTa nanu vaikalpikī kiṃ dhīrāṇave nāsti tatra sā 
AbhTb anyopāyātra tūccārarahitatvaṃ nyarūpayat  
AbhTa uccāraśabdenātroktā bahvantena tadādayaḥ 
AbhTb śaktyupāye na santyete bhedābhedau hi śaktitā  
AbhTa aṇurnāma sphuṭo bhedastadupāya ihāṇavaḥ 
AbhTb vikalpaniścayātmaiva paryante nirvikalpakaḥ  
AbhTa nanu dhīmānasāhaṃkṛtpumāṃso vyāpnuyuḥ śivam 
AbhTb nādhovartitayā tena kathitaṃ kathamīdṛśam  
AbhTa ucyate vastutosmākaṃ śiva eva tathāvidhaḥ 
AbhTb svarūpagopanaṃ kṛtvā svaprakāśaḥ punastathā  
AbhTa dvaitaśāstre mataṅgādau cāpyetatsunirūpitam 
AbhTb adhovyāptuḥ śivasyaiva sa prakāśo vyavasthitaḥ  
AbhTa yena buddhimanobhūmāvapi bhāti paraṃ padam  
AbhTa dvāvapyetau samāveśau nirvikalpārṇavaṃ prati 
AbhTb prayāta eva tadrūḍhiṃ vinā naiva hi kiṃcana  
AbhTa saṃvittiphalabhiccātra na prakalpyetyatobravīt 
AbhTb kalpanāyāśca mukhyatvamatraiva kila sūcitam  
AbhTa vikalpāpekṣayā yopi prāmāṇyaṃ prāha tanmate 
AbhTb tadvikalpakramopāttanirvikalpapramāṇatā  
AbhTa ratnatattvamavidvānprāṅniścayopāyacarcanāt 
AbhTb anupāyāvikalpāptau ratnajña iti bhaṇyate  
AbhTa abhedopāyamatroktaṃ śāmbhavaṃ śāktamucyate 
AbhTb bhedābhedātmakopāyaṃ bhedopāyaṃ tadāṇavam  
AbhTa ante jñānetra sopāye samastaḥ karmavistaraḥ 
AbhTb prasphuṭenaiva rūpeṇa bhāvī sontarbhaviṣyati  
AbhTa kriyā hi nāma vijñānānnānyadvastu kramātmatām 
AbhTb upāyavaśataḥ prāptaṃ tatkriyeti puroditam  
AbhTa samyagjñānaṃ ca muktyekakāraṇaṃ svaparasthitam 
AbhTb yato hi kalpanāmātraṃ svaparādivibhūtayaḥ  
AbhTa tulye kālpanikatve ca yadaikyasphuraṇātmakaḥ 
AbhTb guruḥ sa tāvadekātmā siddho muktaśca bhaṇyate  
AbhTa yāvānasya hi saṃtāno gurustāvatsa kīrtitaḥ 
AbhTb samyagjñānamayaśceti svātmanā mucyate tataḥ  
AbhTa tata eva svasaṃtānaṃ jñānī tārayatītyadaḥ 
AbhTb yuktyāgamābhyāṃ saṃsiddhaṃ tāvāneko yato muniḥ  
AbhTa tenātra ye codayanti nanu jñānādvimuktatā 
AbhTb dīkṣādikā kriyā ceyaṃ sā kathaṃ muktaye bhavet  
AbhTa jñānātmā seti cejjñānaṃ yatrasthaṃ taṃ vimocayet 
AbhTb anyasya mocane vāpi bhavetkiṃ nāsamañjasam 
AbhTc iti te mūlataḥ kṣiptā yattvatrānyaiḥ samarthitam  
AbhTa malo nāma kila dravyaṃ cakṣuḥsthapaṭalādivat 
AbhTb tadvihantrī kriyā dīkṣā tvañjanādikakarmavat  
AbhTa tatpurastānniṣetsyāmo yuktyāgamavigarhitam 
AbhTb malamāyākarmaṇāṃ ca darśayiṣyāmahe sthitim  
AbhTa evaṃ śaktitrayopāyaṃ yajjñānaṃ tatra paścimam 
AbhTb mūlaṃ taduttaraṃ madhyamuttarottaramādimam  
AbhTa tatopi paramaṃ jñānamupāyādivivarjitam 
AbhTb ānandaśaktiviśrāntamanuttaramihocyate  
AbhTa tatsvaprakāśaṃ vijñānaṃ vidyāvidyeśvarādibhiḥ 
AbhTb api durlabhasadbhāvaṃ śrīsiddhātantra ucyate  
AbhTa mālinyāṃ sūcitaṃ caitatpaṭaleṣṭādaśe sphuṭam 
AbhTb na caitadaprasannena śaṃkareṇeti vākyataḥ  
AbhTa ityanenaiva pāṭhena mālinīvijayottare 
AbhTb iti jñānacatuṣkaṃ yatsiddhimuktimahodayam 
AbhTc tanmayā tantryate tantrālokanāmnyatra śāsane  
AbhTa tatreha yadyadantarvā bahirvā parimṛśyate 
AbhTb anudghāṭitarūpaṃ tatpūrvameva prakāśate  
AbhTa tathānudghāṭitākārā nirvācyenātmanā prathā 
AbhTb saṃśayaḥ kutracidrūpe niścite sati nānyathā  
AbhTa etatkimiti mukhyesminnetadaṃśaḥ suniścitaḥ 
AbhTb saṃśayostitvanāstyādidharmānudghāṭitātmakaḥ  
AbhTa kimityetasya śabdasya nādhikorthaḥ prakāśate 
AbhTb kiṃ tvanunmudritākāraṃ vastvevābhidadhātyayam  
AbhTa sthāṇurvā puruṣo veti na mukhyostyeṣa saṃśayaḥ 
AbhTb bhūyaḥsthadharmajāteṣu niścayotpāda eva hi  
AbhTa āmarśanīyadvairūpyānudghāṭanavaśātpunaḥ 
AbhTb saṃśayaḥ sa kimityaṃśe vikalpastvanyathā sphuṭaḥ  
AbhTa tenānudghāṭitātmatvabhāvaprathanameva yat 
AbhTb prathamaṃ sa ihoddeśaḥ praśnaḥ saṃśaya eva ca  
AbhTa tathānudghāṭitākārabhāvaprasaravartmanā 
AbhTb prasarantī svasaṃvittiḥ praṣṭrī śiṣyātmatāṃ gatā  
AbhTa tathāntaraparāmarśaniścayātmatirohiteḥ 
AbhTb prasarānantarodbhūtasaṃhārodayabhāgapi  
AbhTa yāvatyeva bhavedbāhyaprasare prasphuṭātmani 
AbhTb anunmīlitarūpā sā praṣṭrī tāvati bhaṇyate  
AbhTa svayamevaṃ vibodhaśca tathā praśnottarātmakaḥ 
AbhTb guruśiṣyapadepyeṣa dehabhedo hyatāttvikaḥ  
AbhTa bodho hi bodharūpatvādantarnānākṛtīḥ sthitāḥ 
AbhTb bahirābhāsayatyeva drāksāmānyaviśeṣataḥ  
AbhTa srakṣyamāṇaviśeṣāṃśākāṃkṣāyogyasya kasyacit 
AbhTb dharmasya sṛṣṭiḥ sāmānyasṛṣṭiḥ sā saṃśayātmikā  
AbhTa srakṣyamāṇo viśeṣāṃśo yadā tūparamettadā 
AbhTb nirṇayo mātṛrucito nānyathā kalpakoṭibhiḥ  
AbhTa tasyātha vastunaḥ svātmavīryākramaṇapāṭavāt 
AbhTb unmudraṇaṃ tayākṛtyā lakṣaṇottaranirṇayāḥ  
AbhTa nirṇītatāvaddharmāṃśapṛṣṭhapātitayā punaḥ 
AbhTb bhūyo bhūyaḥ samuddeśalakṣaṇātmaparīkṣaṇam  
AbhTa dṛṣṭānumānaupamyāptavacanādiṣu sarvataḥ 
AbhTb uddeśalakṣaṇāvekṣātritayaṃ prāṇināṃ sphuret  
AbhTa nirvikalpitamuddeśo vikalpo lakṣaṇaṃ punaḥ 
AbhTb parīkṣaṇaṃ tathādhyakṣe vikalpānāṃ paramparā  
AbhTa nagoyamiti coddeśo dhūmitvādagnimāniti 
AbhTb lakṣyaṃ vyāptyādivijñānajālaṃ tvatra parīkṣaṇam  
AbhTa uddeśoyamiti prācyo gotulyo gavayābhidhaḥ 
AbhTb iti vā lakṣaṇaṃ śeṣaḥ parīkṣopamitau bhavet  
AbhTa svaḥkāma īdṛguddeśo yajetetyasya lakṣaṇam 
AbhTb agniṣṭomādinetyeṣā parīkṣā śeṣavartinī  
AbhTa vikalpasrakṣyamāṇānyarucitāṃśasahiṣṇunaḥ 
AbhTb vastuno yā tathātvena sṛṣṭiḥ soddeśasaṃjñitā  
AbhTa tadaiva saṃviccinute yāvataḥ srakṣyamāṇatā 
AbhTb yato hyakālakalitā saṃdhatte sārvakālikam  
AbhTa srakṣyamāṇasya yā sṛṣṭiḥ prāksṛṣṭāṃśasya saṃhṛtiḥ 
AbhTb anūdyamāne dharme sā saṃvillakṣaṇamucyate  
AbhTa tatpṛṣṭhapātibhūyoṃśasṛṣṭisaṃhāraviśramāḥ 
AbhTb parīkṣā kathyate mātṛrucitā kalpitāvadhiḥ  
AbhTa prākpaśyantyatha madhyānyā vaikharī ceti tā imāḥ 
AbhTb parā parāparā devī caramā tvaparātmikā  
AbhTa icchādi śaktitritayamidameva nigadyate 
AbhTb etatprāṇita evāyaṃ vyavahāraḥ pratāyate  
AbhTa etatpraśnottarātmatve pārameśvaraśāsane 
AbhTb parasaṃbandharūpatvamabhisaṃbandhapañcake  
AbhTa yathoktaṃ ratnamālāyāṃ sarvaḥ parakalātmakaḥ 
AbhTb mahānavāntaro divyo miśronyonyastu pañcamaḥ  
AbhTa bhinnayoḥ praṣṭṛtadvaktroścaikātmyaṃ yatsa ucyate 
AbhTb saṃbandhaḥ paratā cāsya pūrṇaikātmyaprathāmayī  
AbhTa anenaiva nayena syātsaṃbandhāntaramapyalam 
AbhTb śāstravācyaṃ phalādīnāṃ paripūrṇatvayogataḥ  
AbhTa itthaṃ saṃvidiyaṃ devī svabhāvādeva sarvadā 
AbhTb uddeśāditrayaprāṇā sarvaśāstrasvarūpiṇī  
AbhTa tatrocyate puroddeśaḥ pūrvajānujabhedavān 
AbhTb vijñānabhidgatopāyaḥ paropāyastṛtīyakaḥ  
AbhTa śāktopāyo naropāyaḥ kālopāyotha saptamaḥ 
AbhTb cakrodayotha deśādhvā tattvādhvā tattvabhedanam  
AbhTa kalādyadhvādhvopayogaḥ śaktipātatirohitī 
AbhTb dīkṣopakramaṇaṃ dīkṣā sāmayī pautrike vidhau  
AbhTa prameyaprakriyā sūkṣmā dīkṣā sadyaḥsamutkramaḥ 
AbhTb tulādīkṣātha pārokṣī liṅgoddhārobhiṣecanam  
AbhTa antyeṣṭiḥ śrāddhaklṛptiśca śeṣavṛttinirūpaṇam 
AbhTb liṅgārcā bahubhitparvapavitrādi nimittajam  
AbhTa rahasyacaryā mantraugho maṇḍalaṃ mudrikāvidhiḥ 
AbhTb ekīkāraḥ svasvarūpe praveśaḥ śāstramelanam  
AbhTa āyātikathanaṃ śāstropādeyatvanirūpaṇam 
AbhTb iti saptādhikāmenāṃ triṃśataṃ yaḥ sadā budhaḥ  
AbhTa āhnikānāṃ samabhyasyet sa sākṣādbhairavo bhavet 
AbhTb saptatriṃśatsu saṃpūrṇabodho yadbhairavo bhavet  
AbhTa kiṃ citramaṇavopyasya dṛśā bhairavatāmiyuḥ 
AbhTb ityeṣa pūrvajoddeśaḥ kathyate tvanujodhunā  
AbhTa vijñānabhitprakaraṇe bharvasyoddeśanaṃ kramāt 
AbhTb dvitīyasminprakaraṇe gatopāyatvabheditā  
AbhTa viśvacitpratibinbatvaṃ parāmarśodayakramaḥ 
AbhTb mantrādyabhinnarūpatvaṃ paropāye vivicyate  
AbhTa vikalpasaṃskriyā tarkatattvaṃ gurusatattvakam 
AbhTb yogāṅgānupayogitvaṃ kalpitārcādyanādaraḥ  
AbhTa saṃviccakrodayo mantravīrya japyādi vāstavam 
AbhTb niṣedhavidhitulyatvaṃ śāktopāyetra carcyate  
AbhTa buddhidhyānaṃ prāṇatattvasamuccāraścidātmatā 
AbhTb uccāraḥ paratattvāntaḥpraveśapathalakṣaṇam  
AbhTa karaṇaṃ varṇatattvaṃ cetyāṇave tu nirūpyate 
AbhTb cāramānamahorātrasaṃkrāntyādivikalpanam  
AbhTa saṃhāracitratā varṇodayaḥ kālādhvakalpane 
AbhTb cakrabhinmantravidyābhidetaccakrodaye bhavet  
AbhTa parimāṇaṃ purāṇāṃ ca saṃgrahastattvayojanam 
AbhTb etaddeśādhvanirdeśe dvayaṃ tattvādhvanirṇaye  
AbhTa kāryakāraṇabhāvaśca tattvakramanirūpaṇam 
AbhTb vastudharmastattvavidhirjāgradādinirūpaṇam  
AbhTa pramātṛbheda ityetat tattvabhede vicāryate 
AbhTb kalāsvarūpamekatripañcādyaistattvakalpanam  
AbhTa varṇabhedakramaḥ sarvādhāraśaktinirūpaṇam 
AbhTb kalādyadhvavicārāntaretāvatpravivicyate  
AbhTa abhedabhāvanākampahāsau tvadhvopayojane 
AbhTb saṃkhyādhikyaṃ malādīnāṃ tattvaṃ śaktivicitratā  
AbhTa anapekṣitvasiddhiśca tirobhāvavicitratā 
AbhTb śaktipātaparīkṣāyāmetāvānvācyasaṃgrahaḥ  
AbhTa tirobhāvavyapagamo jñānena paripūrṇatā 
AbhTb utkrāntyanupayogitvaṃ dīkṣopakramaṇe sthitam  
AbhTa śiṣyaucityaparīkṣādau sthānabhitsthānakalpanam 
AbhTb sāmānyanyāsabhedorghapātraṃ caitatprayojanam  
AbhTa dravyayogyatvamarcā ca bahirdvārārcanaṃ kramāt 
AbhTb praveśo diksvarūpaṃ ca dehaprāṇādiśodhanam  
AbhTa viśeṣanyāsavaicitryaṃ saviśeṣārghabhājanam 
AbhTb dehapūjā prāṇabuddhicitsvadhvanyāsapūjane  
AbhTa anyaśāstragaṇotkarṣaḥ pūjā cakrasya sarvataḥ 
AbhTb kṣetragrahaḥ pañcagavyaṃ pūjanaṃ bhūgaṇeśayoḥ  
AbhTa astrārcā vahnikāryaṃ cāpyadhivāsanamagnigam 
AbhTb tarpaṇaṃ carusaṃsiddhirdantakāṣṭhāntasaṃskriyā  
AbhTa śivahastavidhiścāpi śayyāklṛptivicāraṇam 
AbhTb svapnasya sāmayaṃ karma samayāśceti saṃgrahaḥ  
AbhTa samayitvavidhāvasminsyātpañcadaśa āhnike 
AbhTb maṇḍalātmānusandhānaṃ nivedyapaśuvistaraḥ  
AbhTa agnitṛptiḥ svasvabhāvadīpanaṃ śiṣyadehagaḥ 
AbhTb adhvanyāsavidhiḥ śodhyaśodhakādivicitratā  
AbhTa dīkṣābhedaḥ paro nyāso mantrasattāprayojanam 
AbhTb bhedo yojanikādeśca ṣoḍaśe syādihāhnike  
AbhTa sūtraklṛptistattvaśuddhiḥ pāśadāhotha yojanam 
AbhTb adhvabhedastathetyevaṃ kathitaṃ pautrike vidhau  
AbhTa jananādivihīnatvaṃ mantrabhedotha susphuṭaḥ 
AbhTb iti saṃkṣiptadīkṣākhye syādaṣṭādaśa āhnike  
AbhTa kalāvekṣā kṛpāṇyādinyāsaścāraḥ śarīragaḥ 
AbhTb brahmavidyāvidhiścaivamuktaṃ sadyaḥsamutkrame  
AbhTa adhikāraparīkṣāntaḥsaṃskārotha tulāvidhiḥ 
AbhTb ityetadvācyasarvasvaṃ syādviṃśatitamāhnike  
AbhTa mṛtajīvadvidhirjālo padeśaḥ saṃskriyāgaṇaḥ 
AbhTb balābalavicāraścetyekaviṃśāhnike vidhiḥ  
AbhTa śravaṇaṃ cābhyanujñānaṃ śodhanaṃ pātakacyutiḥ 
AbhTb śaṅkāccheda iti spaṣṭaṃ vācyaṃ liṅgoddhṛtikrame  
AbhTa parīkṣācāryakaraṇaṃ tadvrataṃ haraṇaṃ mateḥ 
AbhTb tadvibhāgaḥ sādhakatvamabhiṣekavidhau tviyat  
AbhTa adhikāryatha saṃskārastatprayojanamityadaḥ 
AbhTb caturviṃśentyayāgākhye vaktavyaṃ paricarcyate  
AbhTa prayojanaṃ bhogamokṣadānenātra vidhiḥ sphuṭaḥ 
AbhTb pañcaviṃśāhnike śrāddhaprakāśe vastusaṃgrahaḥ  
AbhTa prayojanaṃ śeṣavṛtternityārcā sthaṇḍile parā 
AbhTb liṅgasvarūpaṃ bahudhā cākṣasūtranirūpaṇam  
AbhTa pūjābheda iti vācyaṃ liṅgārcāsaṃprakāśane 
AbhTb naimittikavibhāgastatprayojanavidhistataḥ  
AbhTa parvabhedāstadviśeṣaścakracarcā tadarcanam 
AbhTb gurvādyantadinādyarcāprayojananirūpaṇam  
AbhTa mṛteḥ parīkṣā yogīśīmelakādividhistathā 
AbhTb vyākhyāvidhiḥ śrutavidhirgurupūjāvidhistviyat  
AbhTa naimittikaprakāśākhye pyaṣṭāviṃśāhnike sthitam 
AbhTb adhikāryātmano bhedaḥ siddhapatnīkulakramaḥ  
AbhTa arcāvidhirdautavidhī rahasyopaniṣatkramaḥ 
AbhTb dīkṣābhiṣekau bodhaścetyekonatriṃśa āhnike  
AbhTa mantrasvarūpaṃ tadvīryamiti triṃśe nirūpitam 
AbhTb śūlābjabhedo vyomaśasvastikādinirūpaṇam  
AbhTa vistareṇābhidhātavyamityekatriṃśa āhnike 
AbhTb guṇapradhānatābhedāḥ svarūpaṃ vīryacarcanam  
AbhTa kalābheda iti proktaṃ mudrāṇāṃ saṃprakāśane 
AbhTb dvātriṃśatattvādīśākhyātprabhṛti prasphuṭo yataḥ  
AbhTa na bhedosti tato noktamuddeśāntaramatra tat 
AbhTb mukhyatvena ca vedyatvādadhikārāntarakramaḥ  
AbhTa ityuddeśavidhiḥ proktaḥ sukhasaṃgrahahetave 
AbhTb athāsya lakṣaṇāvekṣe nirūpyete yathākramam  
AbhTa ātmā saṃvitprakāśasthitiranavayavā saṃvidityāttaśaktivrātaṃ tasya svarūpaṃ sa ca nija mahasaśchādanādbaddharūpaḥ 
AbhTb ātmajyotiḥsvabhāvaprakaṭanavidhinā tasya mokṣaḥ sa cāyaṃ citrākārasya citraḥ prakaṭita iha yatsaṃgraheṇārtha eṣaḥ  
AbhTa mithyājñānaṃ timiramasamān dṛṣṭidoṣānprasūte tatsadbhāvādvimalamapi tadbhāti mālinyadhāma 
AbhTb yattu prekṣyaṃ dṛśi parigataṃ taimirīṃ doṣamudrāṃ dūraṃ runddhetprabhavatu kathaṃ tatra mālinyaśaṅkā  
AbhTa bhāvavrāta
haṭhājjanasya hṛdayānyākramya yannartayan bhaṅgībhirvividhābhirātmahṛdayaṃ pracchādya saṃkrīḍase 
AbhTb yastvāmāha jaḍaṃ jaḍaḥ sahṛdayaṃmanyatvaduḥśikṣito manyemuṣya jaḍātmatā stutipadaṃ tvatsāmyasaṃbhāvanāt  
AbhTa iha galitamalāḥ parāvarajñāḥ śivasadbhāvamayā adhikriyante 
AbhTb guravaḥ pravicāraṇe yatastadviphalā dveṣakalaṃkahāniyācñā  
E tantrālokebhinavaracitemutra vijñānasattābhedodgāraprakaṭanapaṭāvāhnikesminsamāptiḥ 
C atha śrītantrālokasya dvitīyamāhnikam
AbhTa yattatrādyaṃ padamaviratānuttarajñaptirūpaṃ 
AbhTb tannirṇetuṃ prakaraṇamidamārabhehaṃ dvitīyam  
AbhTa anupāyaṃ hi yadrūpaṃ kortho deśanayātra vai 
AbhTb sakṛtsyāddeśanā paścādanupāyatvamucyayate  
AbhTa anupāyamidaṃ tattvamityupāyaṃ vinā kutaḥ 
AbhTb svayaṃ tu teṣāṃ tattādṛk kiṃ brūmaḥ kila tānprati  
AbhTa yaccaturdhoditaṃ rūpaṃ vijñānasya vibhorasau 
AbhTb svabhāva eva mantavyaḥ sa hi nityodito vibhuḥ  
AbhTa etāvadbhirasaṃkhyātaiḥ svabhāvairyatprakāśate 
AbhTb kepyaṃśāṃśikayā tena viśantyanye niraṃśataḥ  
AbhTa tatrāpi cābhyupāyādisāpekṣānyatvayogataḥ 
AbhTb upāyasyāpi no vāryā tadanyatvādvicitratā  
AbhTa tatra ye nirmalātmāno bhairavīyāṃ svasaṃvidam 
AbhTb nirupāyāmupāsīnāstadvidhiḥ praṇigadyate  
AbhTa tatra tāvatkriyāyogo nābhyupāyatvamarhati 
AbhTb sa hi tasmātsamudbhūtaḥ pratyuta pravibhāvyate  
AbhTa jñaptāvupāya eva syāditi cejjñaptirucyate 
AbhTb prakāśatvaṃ svaprakāśe tacca tatrānyataḥ katham  
AbhTa saṃvittattvaṃ svaprakāśamityasminkaṃ nu yuktibhiḥ 
AbhTb tadabhāve bhavedviśvaṃ jaḍatvādaprakāśakam  
AbhTa yāvānupāyo bāhyaḥ syādāntaro vāpi kaścana 
AbhTb sa sarvastanmukhaprekṣī tatropāyatvabhākkatham  
AbhTa tyajāvadhānāni nanu kva nāma dhatsevadhānaṃ vicinu svayaṃ tat 
AbhTb pūrṇevadhānaṃ na hi nāma yuktaṃ nāpūrṇamabhyeti ca satyabhāvam  
AbhTa tenāvadhānaprāṇasya bhāvanādeḥ pare pathi 
AbhTb bhairavīye kathaṃkāraṃ bhavetsākṣādupāyatā  
AbhTa yepi sākṣādupāyena tadrūpaṃ praviviñcate 
AbhTb nūnaṃ te sūryasaṃvittyai khadyotādhitsavo jaḍāḥ  
AbhTa kiṃ ca yāvadidaṃ bāhyamāntaropāyasaṃmatam 
AbhTb tatprakāśātmatāmātraṃ śivasyaiva nijaṃ vapuḥ  
AbhTa nīlaṃ pītaṃ sukhamiti prakāśaḥ kevalaḥ śivaḥ 
AbhTb amuṣminparamādvaite prakāśātmani koparaḥ  
AbhTa upāyopeyabhāvaḥ syātprakāśaḥ kevalaṃ hi saḥ  
AbhTa idaṃ dvaitamayaṃ bheda idamadvaitamityapi 
AbhTb prakāśavapurevāyaṃ bhāsate parameśvaraḥ  
AbhTa asyāṃ bhūmau sukhaṃ duḥkhaṃ bandho mokṣaścitarjaḍaḥ 
AbhTb ghaṭakumbhavadekārthāḥ śabdāstepyekameva ca  
AbhTa praśāśe hyaprakāśāṃśaḥ kathaṃ nāma prakāśatām 
AbhTb prakāśamāne tasminvā taddvaitāstasya lopitāḥ  
AbhTa aprakāśetha tasminvā vastutā kathamucyate 
AbhTb na prakāśaviśeṣatvamata evopapadyate  
AbhTa ata ekaprakāśoyamiti vādetra susthite 
AbhTb dūrādāvāritāḥ satyaṃ vibhinnajñānavādinaḥ  
AbhTa prakāśamātramuditamaprakāśaniṣedhanāt 
AbhTb ekaśabdasya na tvarthaḥ saṃkhyā cidvyaktibhedabhāk  
AbhTa naiṣa śaktirmahādevī na paratrāśrito yataḥ 
AbhTb na caiṣa śaktimāndevo na kasyāpyāśrayo yataḥ  
AbhTa naiṣa dhyeyo dhyātrabhāvānna dhyātā dhyeyavarjanāt 
AbhTb na pūjyaḥ pūjakābhāvātpūjyābhāvānna pūjakaḥ  
AbhTa na mantro na ca mantryosau na ca mantrayitā prabhuḥ 
AbhTb na dīkṣā dīkṣako vāpi na dīkṣāvānmaheśvaraḥ  
AbhTa sthānāsananirodhārghasaṃghānāvāhanādikam 
AbhTb visarjanāntaṃ nāstyatra kartṛkarmakriyojjhite  
AbhTa na sanna cāsatsadasanna ca tannobhayojjhitam 
AbhTb durvijñeyā hi sāvasthā kimapyetadanuttaram  
AbhTa ayamityavabhāso hi yo bhāvovacchidātmakaḥ 
AbhTb sa eva ghaṭavalloke saṃstathā naiṣa bhairavaḥ  
AbhTa asattvaṃ cāprakāśatvaṃ na kutrāpyupayogitā 
AbhTb viśvasya jīvitaṃ satyaṃ prakāśaikātmakaśca saḥ  
AbhTa ābhyāmeva tu hetubhyāṃ na dvyātmā na dvayojjhitaḥ 
AbhTb sarvātmanā hi bhātyeṣa kena rūpeṇa mantryatām  
AbhTa śrīmattriśirasi proktaṃ parajñānasvarūpakam 
AbhTb śaktyā garbhāntarvartinyā śaktigarbha paraṃ padam  
AbhTa na bhāvo nāpyabhāvo na dvayaṃ vācāmagocarāt 
AbhTb akathyapadavīrūḍhaṃ śaktisthaṃ śaktivarjitam  
AbhTa iti ye rūḍhasaṃvittiparamārthapavitritāḥ 
AbhTb anuttarapathe rūḍhāstebhyupāyāniyantritāḥ  
AbhTa teṣāmidaṃ samābhāti sarvato bhāvamaṇḍalam 
AbhTb puraḥsthameva saṃvittibhairavāgnivilāpitam  
AbhTa eteṣāṃ sukhaduḥkhāṃśaśaṃkātaṃkavikalpanāḥ 
AbhTb nirvikalpaparāveśamātraśeṣatvamāgatāḥ  
AbhTa eṣāṃ na mantro na dhyānaṃ na pūjā nāpi kalpanā 
AbhTb na samayyādikācāryaparyantaḥ kopi viśramaḥ  
AbhTa samastayantraṇātantratroṭanāṭaṃkadharmiṇaḥ 
AbhTb nānugrahātparaṃ kiṃciccheṣavṛttau prayojanam  
AbhTa svaṃ kartavyaṃ kimapi kalayaṃlloka eṣa prayatnānno pārārthyaṃ prati ghaṭayate kāṃcana svapravṛttim 
AbhTb yastu dhvastākhilabhavamalo bhairavībhāvapūrṇaḥ kṛtyaṃ tasya sphuṭamidamiyallokakartavyamātram  
AbhTa taṃ ye paśyanti tādrūpyakrameṇāmalasaṃvidaḥ 
AbhTb tepi tadrūpiṇastāvatyevāsyānugrahātmatā  
AbhTa etattattvaparijñānaṃ mukhyaṃ yāgādi kathyate 
AbhTb dīkṣāntaṃ vibhunā śrīmatsiddhayogīśvarīmate  
AbhTa sthaṇḍilāduttaraṃ tūraṃ tūrāduttarataḥ paṭaḥ 
AbhTb paṭāddhyānaṃ tato dhyeyaṃ tataḥ syāddhāraṇottarā  
AbhTa tatopi yogajaṃ rūpaṃ tatopi jñānamuttaram 
AbhTb jñānena hi mahāsiddho bhavedyogīśvarastviti  
AbhTa sopi svātantryadhāmnā cedapyanirmalasaṃvidām 
AbhTb anugrahaṃ cikīrṣustadbhāvinaṃ vidhimāśrayet  
AbhTa anugrāhyānusāreṇa vicitraḥ sa ca kathyate 
AbhTb parāparādyupāyaughasaṃkīrṇatvavibhedataḥ  
AbhTa tadarthameva cāsyāpi parameśvararūpiṇaḥ 
AbhTb tadabhyupāyaśāstrādiśravaṇādhyayanādaraḥ  
AbhTa nahi tasya svatantrasya kāpi kutrāpi khaṇḍanā 
AbhTb nānirmalacitaḥ puṃsonugrahastvanupāyakaḥ  
AbhTa śrīmadūrmimahāśāstre siddhasaṃtānarūpake 
AbhTb idamuktaṃ tathā śrīmatsomānandādidaiśikaiḥ  
AbhTa gurorvākyādyuktipracayaracanonmārjanavaśāt samāśvāsācchāstraṃ prati samuditādvāpi kathitāt 
AbhTb vilīne śaṃkābhre tdṛdayagaganodbhāsimahasaḥ prabhoḥ sūryasyeva spṛśata caraṇāndhvāntajayinaḥ  
AbhTa idamanuttaradhāmavivecakaṃ vigalitaupayikaṃ kṛtamāhnikam  
C śrītantrālokasya tṛtīyamāhnikam
AbhTb atha paraupayikaṃ praṇigadyate padamanuttarameva maheśituḥ  b
AbhTa prakāśamātraṃ yatproktaṃ bhairavīyaṃ paraṃ mahaḥ 
AbhTb tatra svatantratāmātramadhikaṃ pravivicyate  
AbhTa yaḥ prakāśaḥ sa sarvasya prakāśatvaṃ prayacchati 
AbhTb na ca tadvyatirekyasti viśvaṃ sadvāvabhāsate  
AbhTa atosau parameśānaḥ svātmavyomanyanargalaḥ 
AbhTb iyataḥ sṛṣṭisaṃhārāḍambarasya pradarśakaḥ  
AbhTa nirmale makure yadvadbhānti bhūmijalādayaḥ 
AbhTb amiśrāstadvadekasmiṃścinnāthe viśvavṛttayaḥ  
AbhTa sadṛśaṃ bhāti nayanadarpaṇāmbaravāriṣu 
AbhTb tathā hi nirmale rūpe rūpamevāvabhāsate  
AbhTa pracchannarāgiṇī kāntapratibimbitasundaram 
AbhTb darpaṇaṃ kucakumbhābhyāṃ spṛśantyapi na tṛpyati  
AbhTa na hi sparśosya vimalo rūpameva tathā yataḥ 
AbhTb nairmalyaṃ cātiniviḍasajātīyaikasaṃgatiḥ  
AbhTa svasminnabhedādbhinnasya darśanakṣamataiva yā 
AbhTb atyaktasvaprakāśasya nairmalyaṃ tadgurūditam  
AbhTa nairmalyaṃ mukhyamekasya saṃvinnāthasya sarvataḥ 
AbhTb aṃśāṃśikātaḥ kvāpyanyadvimalaṃ tattadicchayā  
AbhTa bhāvānāṃ yatpratīghāti vapurmāyātmakaṃ hi tat 
AbhTb teṣāmevāsti sadvidyāmayaṃ tvapratighātakam  
AbhTa tadevamubhayākāramavabhāsaṃ prakāśayan 
AbhTb vibhāti varado bimbapratibimbadṛśākhile  
AbhTa yastvāha netratejāṃsi svacchātpratiphalantyalam 
AbhTb viparyasya svakaṃ vaktraṃ gṛhṇantīti sa pṛcchyate  
AbhTa dehādanyatra yattejastadadhiṣṭhāturātmanaḥ 
AbhTb tenaiva tejasā jñatve korthaḥ syāddarpaṇena tu  
AbhTa viparyastaistu tejobhirgrāhakātmatvamāgataiḥ 
AbhTb rūpaṃ dṛśyeta vadane nije na makurāntare  
AbhTa svamukhe sparśavaccaitadrūpaṃ bhāyānmametyalam 
AbhTb na tvasya spṛśyabhinnasya vedyaikāntasvarūpiṇaḥ  
AbhTa rūpasaṃsthānamātraṃ tatsparśagandharasādibhiḥ 
AbhTb nyagbhūtaireva tadyuktaṃ vastu tatpratibimbitam  
AbhTa nyagbhāvo grāhyatābhāvāttadabhāvopramāṇataḥ 
AbhTb sa cārthasaṃgamābhāvātsopyādarśenavasthiteḥ  
AbhTa ata eva gurutvādirdharmo naitasya lakṣyate 
AbhTb nahyādarśe saṃsthitosau taddṛṣṭau sa upāyakaḥ  
AbhTa tasmāttu naiṣa bhedena yadbhāti tata ucyate 
AbhTb ādhārastatra tūpāyā dīpadṛksaṃvidaḥ kramāt  
AbhTa dīpacakṣurvibodhānāṃ kāṭhinyābhāvataḥ param 
AbhTb sarvataścāpi nairmalyānna vibhādarśavatpṛthak  
AbhTa etacca devadevena darśitaṃ bodhavṛddhaye 
AbhTb mūḍhānāṃ vastu bhavati tatopyanyatra nāpyalam  
AbhTa pratīghāti svatantraṃ no na sthāyyasthāyi cāpi na 
AbhTb svacchasyaivaiṣa kasyāpi mahimeti kṛpālunā  
AbhTa na deśoṃ no rūpaṃ na ca samayayogo na parimā na cānyonyāsaṃgo na ca tadapahānirna ghanatā 
AbhTb na cāvastutvaṃ syānna ca kimapi sāraṃ nijamiti dhruvaṃ mohaḥ śāmyediti niradiśaddarpaṇavidhiḥ  
AbhTa itthaṃ pradarśitemutra pratibimbanavartmani 
AbhTb śabdasya pratibimbaṃ yat pratiśrutketi bhaṇyate  
AbhTa na cāsau śabdajaḥ śabda āgacchattvena saṃśravāt 
AbhTb tenaiva vaktrā dūrasthaiḥ śabdasyāśravaṇādapi  
AbhTa piṭhirādipidhānāṃśaviśiṣṭachidrasaṃgatau 
AbhTb citratvāccāsya śabdasya pratibimbaṃ mukhādivat  
AbhTa idamanyasya vedyasya rūpamityavabhāsate 
AbhTb yathādarśe tathā kenāpyuktamākarṇaye tviti  
AbhTa niyamādbimbasāṃmukhyaṃ pratibimbasya yattataḥ 
AbhTb tanmadhyagāḥ pramātāraḥ śṛṇvanti pratiśabdakam  
AbhTa mukhyagrahaṃ tvapi vinā pratibimbagraho bhavet 
AbhTb svapaścātsthaṃ priyaṃ paśyeṭṭaṅkitaṃ mukure vapuḥ  
AbhTa sāṃmukhyaṃ cocyate tādṛgdarpaṇābhedasaṃsthiteḥ  
AbhTa ataḥ kūpādipiṭhirākāśe tatpratibimbitam 
AbhTb vaktrākāśaṃ saśabdaṃ sadbhāti tatparavaktavat  
AbhTa yathā cādarśapāścātyabhāgastho vetti no mukham 
AbhTb tathā tathāvidhākāśapaścātstho vetti na dhvanim  
AbhTa śabdo na cānabhivyaktaḥ pratibimbati taddhruvam 
AbhTb abhivyaktiśrutī tasya samakālaṃ dvitīyake  
AbhTa kṣaṇe tu pratibimbatvaṃ śrutiśca samakālikā 
AbhTb tulyakālaṃ hi no hastatacchāyārūpaniścayaḥ  
AbhTa itthaṃ pradarśitemutra pratibimbasatattvake 
AbhTb prakṛtaṃ brūmahe tatra pratibimbanamarhati  
AbhTa śabdo nabhasi sānande sparśadhāmani sundaraḥ 
AbhTb sparśonyopi dṛḍhāghātaśūlaśītādikodbhavaḥ 
AbhTc parasthaḥ pratibimbatvātsvadehoddhūlanākaraḥ  
AbhTa na caiṣa mukhyastatkāryapāramparyāprakāśanāt  
AbhTa evaṃ ghrāṇāntare gandho raso dantodake sphuṭaḥ  
AbhTa yathā ca rūpaṃ pratibimbitaṃ dṛśorna cakṣuṣānyena vinā hi lakṣyate 
AbhTb tathā rasasparśanasaurabhādikaṃ na lakṣyatekṣeṇa vinā sthitaṃ tvapi  
AbhTa na cāntare sparśanadhāmani sthitaṃ bahiḥspṛśonyākṣadhiyaḥ sa gocaraḥ  
AbhTa atontikasthasvakatādṛgindriyaprayojanāntaḥkaraṇairyadā kṛtā 
AbhTb tadā tadāttaṃ pratibimbamindriye svakāṃ kriyāṃ sūyata eva tādṛśīm  
AbhTa na tu smṛtānmānasagocarādṛtā bhavetkriyā sā kila vartamānataḥ 
AbhTb ataḥ sthitaḥ sparśavarastadindriye samāgataḥ sanviditastathākriyaḥ  
AbhTa asaṃbhave bāhyagatasya tādṛśaḥ sva eva tasminpratibimbitastathā 
AbhTb karoti tāṃ sparśavaraḥ sukhātmikāṃ sa cāpi kasyāmapi nāḍisaṃtatau  
AbhTa tena saṃvittimakure viśvamātmānamarpayat 
AbhTb nāthasya vadatemuṣya vimalāṃ viśvarūpatām  
AbhTa yathā ca gandharūpaspṛgrasādyāḥ pratibimbitāḥ 
AbhTb tadādhāroparāgeṇa bhānti khaṅge mukhādivat  
AbhTa tathā viśvamidaṃ bodhe pratibimbitamāśrayet 
AbhTb prakāśatvasvatantratvaprabhṛtiṃ dharmavistaram  
AbhTa yathā ca sarvataḥ svacche sphaṭike sarvato bhavet 
AbhTb pratibimbaṃ tathā bodhe sarvataḥ svacchatājuṣi  
AbhTa atyantasvacchatā sā yatsvākṛtyanavabhāsanam 
AbhTb ataḥ svacchatamo bodho na ratnaṃ tvākṛtigrahāt  
AbhTa pratibimbaṃ ca bimbena bāhyasthena samarpyate 
AbhTb tasyaiva pratibimbatve kiṃ bimbamavaśiṣyatām  
AbhTa yadvāpi kāraṇaṃ kiṃcidbimbatvenābhiṣicyate 
AbhTb tadapi pratibimbatvameti bodhenyathā tvasat  
AbhTa itthametatsvasaṃvittidṛḍhanyāyāstrarakṣitam 
AbhTb sāmrājyameva viśvatra pratibimbasya jṛmbhate  
AbhTa nanu bimbasya virahe pratibimbaṃ kathaṃ bhavet 
AbhTb kiṃ kurmo dṛśyate taddhi nanu tadbimbamucyatām  
AbhTa naivaṃ tallakṣaṇābhāvādbimbaṃ kila kimucyate 
AbhTb anyāmiśraṃ svatantraṃ sadbhāsamānaṃ mukhaṃ yathā  
AbhTa svarūpānapahānena pararūpasadṛkṣatām 
AbhTb pratibimbātmatāmāhuḥ khaḍgādarśatalādivat  
AbhTa uktaṃ ca sati bāhyepi dhīrekānekavedanāt 
AbhTb anekasadṛśākārā na tvaneketi saugataiḥ  
AbhTa nanvitthaṃ pratibimbasya lakṣaṇaṃ kiṃ taducyate 
AbhTb anyavyāmiśraṇāyogāttadbhedāśakyabhāsanam 
AbhTc pratibimbamiti prāhurdarpaṇe vadanaṃ yathā  
AbhTa bodhamiśramidaṃ bodhādbhedenāśakyabhāsanam 
AbhTb paratattvādi bodhe kiṃ pratibimbaṃ na bhaṇyate  
AbhTa lakṣaṇasya vyavasthaiṣākasmāccedbimbamucyatām 
AbhTb prājñā vastuni yujyante na tu sāmayike dhvanau  
AbhTa nanu na pratibimbasya vinā bimbaṃ bhavetsthitiḥ 
AbhTb kiṃ tataḥ pratibimbe hi bimbaṃ tādātmyavṛtti na  
AbhTa ataśca lakṣaṇasyāsya proktasya tadasaṃbhave 
AbhTb na hānirhetumātre tu praśnoyaṃ paryavasyati  
AbhTa tatrāpi ca nimittākhye nopādāne kathaṃcana 
AbhTb nimittakāraṇānāṃ ca kadācitkvāpi saṃbhavaḥ  
AbhTa ata eva purovartinyāloke smaraṇādinā 
AbhTb nimittena ghanenāstu saṃkrāntadayitākṛtiḥ  
AbhTa anyathā saṃvidārūḍhā kāntā vicchedayoginī 
AbhTb kasmādbhāti na vai saṃvid vicchedaṃ purato gatā  
AbhTa ata evāntaraṃ kiṃciddhīsaṃjñaṃ bhavatu sphuṭam 
AbhTb yatrāsya vicchidā bhānaṃ saṃkalpasvapnadarśane  
AbhTa ato nimittaṃ devasya śaktayaḥ santu tādṛśe 
AbhTb itthaṃ viśvamidaṃ nāthe bhairavīyacidambare 
AbhTc pratibimbamalaṃ svacche na khalvanyaprasādataḥ  
AbhTa ananyāpekṣitā yāsya viśvātmatvaṃ prati prabhoḥ 
AbhTb tāṃ parāṃ pratibhāṃ devīṃ saṃgirante hyanuttarām  
AbhTa akulasyāsya devasya kulaprathanaśālinī 
AbhTb kaulikī sā parā śaktiraviyukto yayā prabhuḥ  
AbhTa tayoryadyāmalaṃ rūpaṃ sa saṃghaṭṭa iti smṛtaḥ 
AbhTb ānandaśaktiḥ saivoktā yato viśvaṃ visṛjyate  
AbhTa parāparātparaṃ tattvaṃ saiṣā devī nigadyate 
AbhTb tatsāraṃ tacca hṛdayaṃ sa visargaḥ paraḥ prabhuḥ  
AbhTa devīyāmalaśāstre sā kathitā kālakarṣiṇī 
AbhTb mahāḍāmarake yāge śrīparā mastake tathā  
AbhTa śrīpūrvaśāstre sā mātṛsadbhāvatvena varṇitā 
AbhTb saṃghaṭṭesmiṃścidātmatvādyattatpratyavamarśanam  
AbhTa icchāśaktiraghorāṇāṃ śaktīnāṃ sā parā prabhuḥ 
AbhTb saiva prakṣubdharūpā cedīśitrī saṃprajāyate  
AbhTa tadā ghorāḥ parā devyo jātāḥ śaivādhvadaiśikāḥ 
AbhTb svātmapratyavamarśo yaḥ prāgabhūdekavīrakaḥ  
AbhTa jñātavyaviśvonmeṣātmā jñānaśaktitayā sthitaḥ 
AbhTb iyaṃ parāparā devī ghorāṃ yā mātṛmaṇḍalīm  
AbhTa sṛjatyavirataṃ śuddhāśuddhamārgaikadīpikām 
AbhTb jñeyāṃśaḥ pronmiṣankṣobhaṃ yadaiti balavattvataḥ  
AbhTa ūnatābhāsanaṃ saṃvinmātratve jāyate tadā 
AbhTb rūḍhaṃ tajjñeyavargasya sthitiprārambha ucyate  
AbhTa rūḍhireṣā vibodhābdheścitrākāraparigrahaḥ 
AbhTb idaṃ tadbījasaṃdarbhabījaṃ cinvanti yoginaḥ  
AbhTa icchāśaktirdvirūpoktā kṣubhitākṣubhitā ca yā 
AbhTb iṣyamāṇaṃ hi sā vastudvairūpyeṇātmani śrayet  
AbhTa aciradyutibhāsinyā śaktyā jvalanarūpayā 
AbhTb iṣyamāṇasamāpattiḥ sthairyeṇātha dharātmanā  
AbhTa unmeṣaśaktāvastyetajjñeyaṃ yadyapi bhūyasā 
AbhTb tathāpi vibhavasthānaṃ sā na tu prācyajanmabhūḥ  
AbhTa icchāśakterataḥ prāhuścātūrūpyaṃ parāmṛtam 
AbhTb kṣobhāntarasyāsadbhāvānnedaṃ bījaṃ ca kasyacit  
AbhTa prakṣobhakatvaṃ bījatvaṃ kṣobhādhāraśca yonitā 
AbhTb kṣobhakaṃ saṃvido rūpaṃ kṣubhyati kṣobhayatyapi  
AbhTa kṣobhaḥ syājjñeyadharmatvaṃ kṣobhaṇā tadbahiṣkṛtiḥ 
AbhTb antaḥsthaviśvābhinnaikabījāṃśavisisṛkṣutā  
AbhTa kṣobhotadicche tattvecchābhāsanaṃ kṣobhaṇāṃ viduḥ 
AbhTb yadaikyāpattimāsādya tadicchā kṛtinī bhavet  
AbhTa kṣobhādhāramimaṃ prāhuḥ śrīsomānandaputrakāḥ 
AbhTb saṃvidāmīṣaṇādīnāmanudbhinnaviśeṣakam  
AbhTa yajjñeyamātraṃ tadbījaṃ yadyogādbījatā svare 
AbhTb tasya bījasya saivoktā visisṛkṣā ya udbhavaḥ 
AbhTc yato grāhyamidaṃ bhāsyadbhinnakalpaṃ cidātmanaḥ  
AbhTa eṣa kṣobhaḥ kṣobhaṇā tu tūṣṇīṃbhūtānyamātṛgam 
AbhTb haṭhādyadaudāsīnyāṃśacyāvanaṃ saṃvido balāt  
AbhTa jātāpi visisṛkṣāsau yadvimarśāntaraikyataḥ 
AbhTb kṛtārthā jāyate kṣobhādhārotraitatprakīrtitam  
AbhTa tatastadāntaraṃ jñeyaṃ bhinnakalpatvamicchati 
AbhTb viśvabījādataḥ sarva bāhyaṃ bimbaṃ vivartsyati  
AbhTa kṣobhyakṣobhakabhāvasya satattvaṃ darśitaṃ mayā 
AbhTb śrīmanmaheśvareṇoktaṃ guruṇā yatprasādataḥ  
AbhTa prakṛtaṃ brūmahe nedaṃ bījaṃ varṇacatuṣṭayam 
AbhTb nāpi yoniryato naitatkṣobhādhāratvamṛcchati  
AbhTa ātmanyeva ca viśrāntyā tatproktamamṛtātmakam 
AbhTb itthaṃ prāguditaṃ yattatpañcakaṃ tatparasparam  
AbhTa ucchaladvividhākāramanyonyavyatimiśraṇāt 
AbhTb yonuttaraḥ paraḥ spando yaścānandaḥ samucchalan  
AbhTa tāvicchonmeṣasaṃghaṭṭādgacchatotivicitratām 
AbhTb anuttarānandacitī icchāśaktau niyojite  
AbhTa trikoṇamiti tatprāhurvisargāmodasundaram 
AbhTb anuttarānandaśaktī tatra rūḍhimupāgate  
AbhTa trikoṇadvitvayogena vrajataḥ ṣaḍarasthitim 
AbhTb ta evonmeṣayogepi punastanmayatāṃ gate  
AbhTa kriyāśakteḥ sphuṭaṃ rūpamabhivyaṅktaḥ parasparam 
AbhTb icchonmeṣagataḥ kṣobho yaḥ proktastadgaterapi  
AbhTa te eva śaktī tādrūpyabhāginyau nānyathāsthite 
AbhTb nanvanuttaratānandau svātmanā bhedavarjitau  
AbhTa kathametāvatīmenāṃ vaicitrīṃ svātmani śritau 
AbhTb śṛṇu tāvadayaṃ saṃvinnāthoparimitātmakaḥ  
AbhTa anantaśaktivaicitryalayodayakaleśvaraḥ 
AbhTb asthāsyadekarūpeṇa vapuṣā cenmaheśvaraḥ  
AbhTa maheśvaratvaṃ saṃvittvaṃ tadatyakṣyaddhaṭādivat 
AbhTb paricchinnaprakāśatvaṃ jaḍasya kila lakṣaṇam  
AbhTa jaḍādvilakṣaṇo bodho yato na parimīyate 
AbhTb tena bodhamahasindhorullāsinyaḥ svaśaktayaḥ  
AbhTa āśrayantyūrmaya iva svātmasaṃghaṭṭacitratām 
AbhTb svātmasaṃghaṭṭavaicitryaṃ śaktīnāṃ yatparasparam  
AbhTa etadeva paraṃ prāhuḥ kriyāśakteḥ sphuṭaṃ vapuḥ 
AbhTb asmiṃścaturdaśe dhāmni sphuṭībhūtatriśaktike  
AbhTa triśūlatvamataḥ prāha śāstā śrīpūrvaśāsane 
AbhTb nirañjanamidaṃ coktaṃ gurubhistattvadarśibhiḥ  
AbhTa śaktimānañjyate yasmānna śaktirjātu kenacit 
AbhTb icchā jñānaṃ kriyā ceti yatpṛthakpṛthagañjyate  
AbhTa tadeva śaktimatsvaiḥ svairiṣyamāṇādikaiḥ sphuṭam 
AbhTb etattritayamaikyena yadā tu prasphurettadā  
AbhTa na kenacidupādheyaṃ svasvavipratiṣedhataḥ 
AbhTb lolībhūtamataḥ śaktitritayaṃ tattriśūlakam 
AbhTc yasminnāśu samāveśādbhavedyogī nirañjanaḥ  
AbhTa itthaṃ parāmṛtapadādārabhyāṣṭakamīdṛśam 
AbhTb brāhmyādirūpasaṃbhedādyātyaṣṭāṣṭakatāṃ sphuṭam  
AbhTa atrānuttaraśaktiḥ sā svaṃ vapuḥ prakaṭasthitam 
AbhTb kurvantyapi jñeyakalākāluṣyādvindurūpiṇī  
AbhTa uditāyāṃ kriyāśaktau somasūryāgnidhāmani 
AbhTb avibhāgaḥ prakāśo yaḥ sa binduḥ paramo hi naḥ  
AbhTa tattvarakṣāvidhāne ca taduktaṃ parameśinā 
AbhTb hṛtpadmamaṇḍalāntaḥstho naraśaktiśivātmakaḥ  
AbhTa boddhavyo layabhedena vindurvimalatārakaḥ 
AbhTb yosau nādātmakaḥ śabdaḥ sarvaprāṇiṣvavasthitaḥ  
AbhTa adhaūrdhvavibhāgena niṣkriyeṇāvatiṣṭhate 
AbhTb hlādataikṣṇyādi vaicitryaṃ sitaraktādikaṃ ca yat  
AbhTa svayaṃ tannirapekṣosau prakāśo gururāha ca 
AbhTb yanna sūryo na vā somo nāgnirbhāsayatepi ca  
AbhTa na cārkasomavahnīnāṃ tatprakāśādvinā mahaḥ 
AbhTb kimapyasti nijaṃ kiṃ tu saṃviditthaṃ prakāśate  
AbhTa svasvātantryaprabhāvodyadvicitropādhisaṃgataḥ 
AbhTb prakāśo yāti taikṣṇyādimavāntaravicitratām  
AbhTa durdarśanopi gharmāṃśuḥ patitaḥ pāthasāṃ pathi 
AbhTb netrānandatvamabhyeti paśyopādheḥ prabhāvitām  
AbhTa sūryādiṣu prakāśosāvupādhikaluṣīkṛtaḥ 
AbhTb saṃvitprakāśaṃ māheśamata eva hyapekṣate  
AbhTa prakāśamātraṃ suvyaktaṃ sūrya ityucyate sphuṭam 
AbhTb prakāśyavastusārāṃśavarṣi tatsoma ucyate  
AbhTa sūrya pramāṇamityāhuḥ somaṃ meyaṃ pracakṣate 
AbhTb anyonyamaviyuktau tau svatantrāvapyubhau sthitau  
AbhTa bhoktṛbhogyobhayātmaitadanyonyonmukhatāṃ gatam 
AbhTb tato jvalanacidrūpaṃ citrabhānuḥ prakīrtitaḥ  
AbhTa yoyaṃ vahneḥ paraṃ tattvaṃ pramāturidameva tat 
AbhTb saṃvideva tu vijñeyatādātmyādanapekṣiṇī  
AbhTa svatantratvātpramātoktā vicitro jñeyabhedataḥ 
AbhTb somāṃśadāhyavastūtthavaicitryābhāsabṛṃhitaḥ  
AbhTa tata evāgniruditaścitrabhānurmaheśinā 
AbhTb jñeyādyupāyasaṃghātanirapekṣaiva saṃvidaḥ  
AbhTa sthitirmātāhamasmīti jñātā śāstrajñavadyataḥ 
AbhTb ajña eva yato jñātānubhavātmā na rūpataḥ  
AbhTa na tu sā jñātṛtā yasyāṃ śuddhajñeyādyapekṣate 
AbhTb tasyāṃ daśāyāṃ jñātṛtvamucyate yogyatāvaśāt  
AbhTa mānataiva tu sā prācyapramātṛparikalpitā 
AbhTb ucchalantyapi saṃvittiḥ kālakramavivarjanāt  
AbhTa uditaiva satī pūrṇā mātṛmeyādirūpiṇī 
AbhTb pākādistu kriyā kālaparicchedātkramocitā  
AbhTa matāntyakṣaṇavandhyāpi na pākatvaṃ prapadyate 
AbhTb itthaṃ prakāśatattvasya somasūryāgnitā sthitā  
AbhTa api mukhyaṃ tatprakāśamātratvaṃ na vyapohyate 
AbhTb eṣāṃ yatprathamaṃ rūpaṃ hrasvaṃ tatsūrya ucyate  
AbhTa kṣobhānandavaśāddīrghaviśrāntyā soma ucyate 
AbhTb yattatparaṃ plutaṃ nāma somānandātparaṃ sthitam  
AbhTa prakāśarūpaṃ tatprāhurāgneyaṃ śāstrakovidāḥ 
AbhTb atra prakāśamātraṃ yatsthite dhāmatraye sati  
AbhTa uktaṃ vindutayā śāstre śivavindurasau mataḥ 
AbhTb makārādanya evāyaṃ tacchāyāmātradhṛdyathā  
AbhTa ralahāḥ ṣaṇṭhavaisargavarṇarūpatvasaṃsthitāḥ 
AbhTb ikāra eva rephāṃśacchāyayānyo yathā svaraḥ  
AbhTa tathaiva mahaleśādaḥ sonyo dvedhāsvaropi san 
AbhTb asyāntarvisisṛkṣāsau yā proktā kaulikī parā  
AbhTa saiva kṣobhavaśādeti visargātmakatāṃ dhruvam 
AbhTb uktaṃ ca triśiraḥśāstre kalāvyāptyantacarcane  
AbhTa kalā saptadaśī tasmādamṛtākārarūpiṇī 
AbhTb parāparasvasvarūpabindugatyā visarpitā  
AbhTa prakāśyaṃ sarvavastūnāṃ visargarahitā tu sā 
AbhTb śaktikuṇḍalikā caiva prāṇakuṇḍalikā tathā  
AbhTa visargaprāntadeśe tu parā kuṇḍalinīti ca 
AbhTb śivavyometi paramaṃ brahmātmasthānamucyate  
AbhTa visargamātraṃ nāthasya sṛṣṭisaṃhāravibhramāḥ 
AbhTb svātmanaḥ svātmani svātmakṣepo vaisargikī sthitiḥ  
AbhTa visarga evamutsṛṣṭa āśyānatvamupāgataḥ 
AbhTb haṃsaḥ prāṇo vyañjanaṃ ca sparśaśca paribhāṣyate  
AbhTa anuttaraṃ paraṃ dhāma tadevākulamucyate 
AbhTb visargastasya nāthasya kaulikī śaktirucyate  
AbhTa visargatā ca saivāsyā yadānandodayakramāt 
AbhTb spaṣṭībhūtakriyāśaktiparyantā procchalatsthitiḥ  
AbhTa visarga eva tāvānyadākṣiptaitāvadātmakaḥ 
AbhTb iyadrūpaṃ sāgarasya yadanantormisaṃtatiḥ  
AbhTa ata eva visargoyamavyaktahakalātmakaḥ 
AbhTb kāmatattvamiti śrīmatkulaguhvara ucyate  
AbhTa yattadakṣaramavyakta kāntākaṇṭhe vyavasthitam 
AbhTb dhvanirūpamanicchaṃ tu dhyānadhāraṇavarjitam  
AbhTa tatra cittaṃ samādhāya vaśayedyugapajjagat 
AbhTb ata eva visargasya haṃse yadvatsphuṭā sthitiḥ  
AbhTa tadvatsānuttarādīnāṃ kādisāntatayā sthitiḥ 
AbhTb anuttarātkavargasya sūtiḥ pañcātmanaḥ sphuṭam  
AbhTa pañcaśaktyātmatovaśa ekaikatra yathā sphuṭaḥ 
AbhTb icchāśakteḥ svasvarūpasaṃsthāyā ekarūpataḥ  
AbhTa cavargaḥ pañcaśaktyātmā kramaprasphuṭatātmakaḥ 
AbhTb yā tūktā jñeyakāluṣyabhākkṣipracarayogataḥ  
AbhTa dvirūpāyāstato jātaṃ ṭatādyaṃ vargayugmakam 
AbhTb unmeṣātpādivargastu yato viśvaṃ samāpyate  
AbhTa jñeyarūpamidaṃ pañcaviṃśatyantaṃ yataḥ sphuṭam 
AbhTb jñeyatvātsphuṭataḥ proktametāvatsparśarūpakam  
AbhTa icchāśaktiśca yā dvedhā kṣubhitākṣubhitatvataḥ 
AbhTb sā vijātīyaśaktyaṃśapronmukhī yāti yātmatām  
AbhTa saiva śīghrataropāttajñeyakāluṣyarūṣitā 
AbhTb vijātīyonmukhatvena ratvaṃ latvaṃ ca gacchati  
AbhTa tadvadunmeṣaśaktirdvirūpā vaijātyaśaktigā 
AbhTb vakāratvaṃ prapadyeta sṛṣṭisārapravarṣakam  
AbhTa icchaivānuttarānandayātā śīghratvayogataḥ 
AbhTb vāyurityucyate vahnirbhāsanātsthairyato dharā  
AbhTa idaṃ catuṣkamantaḥsthamata eva nigadyate 
AbhTb icchādyantargatatvena svasamāptau ca saṃsthiteḥ  
AbhTa sajātīyakaśaktīnāmicchādyānāṃ ca yojanam 
AbhTb kṣobhātmakamidaṃ prāhuḥ kṣobhākṣobhātmanāmapi  
AbhTa anuttarasya sājātye bhavettu dvitayī gatiḥ 
AbhTb anuttaraṃ yattatraikaṃ taccedānandasūtaye  
AbhTa prabhaviṣyati tadyoge yogaḥ kṣobhātmakaḥ sphuṭaḥ 
AbhTb atrāpyanuttaraṃ dhāma dvitīyamapi sūtaye  
AbhTa na paryāptaṃ tadā kṣobhaṃ vinaivānuttarātmatā 
AbhTb icchā yā karmaṇā hīnā yā caiṣṭavyena rūṣitā  
AbhTa śīghrasthairyaprabhinnena tridhā bhāvamupāgatā 
AbhTb anunmiṣitamunmīlatpronmīlitamiti sthitam  
AbhTa iṣyamāṇaṃ tridhaitasyāṃ tādrūpyasyāparicyuteḥ 
AbhTb tadeva svoṣmaṇā svātmasvātantryapreraṇātmanā  
AbhTa bahirbhāvya sphuṭaṃ kṣiptaṃ śaṣasatritayaṃ sthitam 
AbhTb tata eva sakāresminsphuṭaṃ viśvaṃ prakāśate  
AbhTa amṛtaṃ ca paraṃ dhāma yoginastatpracakṣate 
AbhTb kṣobhādyantavirāmeṣu tadeva ca parāmṛtam  
AbhTa sītkārasukhasadbhāvasamāveśasamādhiṣu 
AbhTb tadeva brahma paramamavibhaktaṃ pracakṣate  
AbhTa uvāca bhagavāneva tacchrīmatkulaguhkare 
AbhTb śaktiśaktimadaikātmyalabdhānvarthābhidhānake  
AbhTa kākacañcupuṭākāraṃ dhyānadhāraṇavarjitam 
AbhTb viṣatattvamanackākhyaṃ tava snehātprakāśitam  
AbhTa kāmasya pūrṇatā tattvaṃ saṃghaṭṭe pravibhāvyate 
AbhTb viṣasya cāmṛtaṃ tattvaṃ chādyatveṇoścyute sati  
AbhTa vyāptrī śaktirviṣaṃ yasmādavyāptuśchādayenmahaḥ 
AbhTb nirañjanaṃ paraṃ dhāma tattvaṃ tasya tu sāñjanam  
AbhTa kriyāśaktyātmakaṃ viśvamayaṃ tasmātsphuredyataḥ 
AbhTb icchā kāmo viṣaṃ jñānaṃ kriyā devī nirañjanam  
AbhTa etattrayasamāveśaḥ śivo bhairava ucyate 
AbhTb atra rūḍhiṃ sadā kuryāditi no guravo jaguḥ  
AbhTa viṣatattve saṃpraviśya na bhūtaṃ na viṣaṃ na ca 
AbhTb grahaḥ kevala evāhamiti bhāvanayā sphuret  
AbhTa nanvatra ṣaṇṭhavarṇebhyo janmoktaṃ tena ṣaṇṭhatā 
AbhTb kathaṃ syāditi cedbrūmo nātra ṣaṇṭhasya sotṛtā  
AbhTa tathāhi tatragā yāsāvicchāśaktirudīritā 
AbhTb saiva sūte svakartavyamantaḥsthaṃ sveṣṭarūpakam  
AbhTa yattvatra rūṣaṇāhetureṣitavyaṃ sthitaṃ tataḥ 
AbhTb bhāgānna prasavastajjaṃ kāluṣyaṃ tadvapuśca tat  
AbhTa jñeyārūṣaṇayā yuktaṃ samudāyātmakaṃ viduḥ 
AbhTb ṣaṇṭhaṃ kṣobhakatākṣobhadhāmatvābhāvayogataḥ  
AbhTa etadvarṇacatuṣkasya svoṣmaṇābhāsanāvaśāt 
AbhTb ūṣmeti kathitaṃ nāma bhairaveṇāmalātmanā  
AbhTa kādihāntamidaṃ prahuḥ kṣobhādhāratayā budhāḥ 
AbhTb yonirūpeṇa tasyāpi yoge kṣobhāntaraṃ vrajet  
AbhTa tannidarśanayogena pañcāśattamavarṇatā 
AbhTb pañcaviṃśakasaṃjñeyaprāgvadbhūmisusaṃsthitam  
AbhTa catuṣkaṃ ca catuṣkaṃ ca bhedābhedagataṃ kramāt 
AbhTb ādyaṃ catuṣkaṃ saṃvitterbhedasaṃdhānakovidam  
AbhTa bhedasyābhedarūḍhyekaheturanyaccatuṣṭayam 
AbhTb itthaṃ yadvarṇajātaṃ tatsarva svaramayaṃ purā  
AbhTa vyaktiyogādvyañjanaṃ tatsvaraprāṇaṃ yataḥ kila 
AbhTb svarāṇāṃ ṣaṭkameveha mūlaṃ syādvarṇasaṃtatau  
AbhTa ṣaḍdevatāstu tā eva ye mukhyāḥ sūryaraśmayaḥ 
AbhTb saurāṇāmeva raśmīnāmantaścāndrakalā yataḥ  
AbhTa atotra dīrghatritayaṃ sphuṭaṃ cāndramasaṃ vapuḥ 
AbhTb candraśca nāma naivānyo bhogyaṃ bhoktuśca nāparam  
AbhTa bhoktaiva bhogyabhāvena dvaividhyātsaṃvyavasthitaḥ 
AbhTb ghaṭasya na hi bhogyatvaṃ svaṃ vapurmātṛgaṃ hi tat  
AbhTa ato mātari yā rūḍhiḥ sāsya bhogyatvamucyate 
AbhTb anuttaraṃ parāmṛśyaparāmarśakabhāvataḥ  
AbhTa saṃghaṭṭarūpatāṃ prāptaṃ bhogyamicchādikaṃ tathā 
AbhTb anuttarānandabhuvāmicchādye bhogyatāṃ gate  
AbhTa saṃdhyakṣarāṇāmudayo bhoktṛrūpaṃ ca kathyate 
AbhTb anuttarānandamayo devo bhoktaiva kathyate  
AbhTa icchādikaṃ bhogyameva tata evāsya śaktitā 
AbhTb bhogyaṃ bhoktari līnaṃ ced bhoktā tadvastutaḥ sphuṭaḥ  
AbhTa ataḥ ṣaṇṇāṃ trikaṃ sāraṃ cidiṣyunmeṣaṇātmakam 
AbhTb tadeva tritayaṃ prāhurbhairavasya paraṃ mahaḥ  
AbhTa tattrikaṃ parameśasya pūrṇā śaktiḥ pragīyate 
AbhTb tenākṣiptaṃ yato viśvamatosminsamupāsite  
AbhTa viśvaśaktāvavacchedavandhye jātamupāsanam 
AbhTb ityeṣa mahimaitāvāniti tāvanna śakyate  
AbhTa aparicchinnaśakteḥ kaḥ kuryācchaktiparicchidām 
AbhTb tasmādanuttaro devaḥ svācchandyānuttaratvataḥ  
AbhTa visargaśaktiyuktatvātsaṃpanno viśvarūpakaḥ 
AbhTb evaṃ pañcāśadāmarśapūrṇaśaktirmaheśvaraḥ  
AbhTa vimarśātmaika evānyāḥ śaktayotraiva niṣṭhitāḥ 
AbhTb ekāśītipadā devī hyatrāntarbhāvayiṣyate  
AbhTa ekāmarśasvabhāvatve śabdarāśiḥ sa bhairavaḥ 
AbhTb āmṛśyacchāyayā yogātsaiva śaktiśca mātṛkā  
AbhTa sā śabdarāśisaṃghaṭṭādbhinnayonistu mālinī 
AbhTb prāgvannavatayāmarśātpṛthagvargasvarūpiṇī  
AbhTa ekaikāmarśarūḍhau tu saiva pañcāśadātmikā 
AbhTb itthaṃ nādānuvedhena parāmarśasvabhāvakaḥ  
AbhTa śivo mātāpitṛtvena kartā viśvatra saṃsthitaḥ 
AbhTb visarga eva śāktoyaṃ śivabindutayā punaḥ  
AbhTa garbhīkṛtānantaviśvaḥ śrayatenuttarātmatām 
AbhTb aparicchinnaviśvāntaḥsāre svātmani yaḥ prabhoḥ  
AbhTa parāmarśaḥ sa evokto dvayasaṃpattilakṣaṇaḥ 
AbhTb anuttaravisargātmaśivaśaktyadvayātmani  
AbhTa parāmarśo nirbharatvādahamityucyate vibhoḥ 
AbhTb anuttarādyā prasṛtirhāntā śaktisvarūpiṇī  
AbhTa pratyāhṛtāśeṣaviśvānuttare sā nilīyate 
AbhTb tadidaṃ viśvamantaḥsthaṃ śaktau sānuttare pare  
AbhTa tattasyāmiti yatsatyaṃ vibhunā saṃpuṭīkṛtiḥ 
AbhTb tena śrītrīśikāśāstre śakteḥ saṃpuṭitākṛtiḥ  
AbhTa saṃvittau bhāti yadviśvaṃ tatrāpi khalu saṃvidā 
AbhTb tadetattritayaṃ dvandvayogātsaṃghātatāṃ gatam  
AbhTa ekameva paraṃ rūpaṃ bhairavasyāhamātmakam 
AbhTb visargaśaktiryā śaṃbhoḥ setthaṃ sarvatra vartate  
AbhTa tata evasamastoyamānandarasavibhramaḥ 
AbhTb tathāhi madhure gīte sparśe vā candanādike  
AbhTa mādhyasthyavigame yāsau hṛdaye spandamānatā 
AbhTb ānandaśaktiḥ saivoktā yataḥ sahṛdayo janaḥ  
AbhTa pūrva visṛjyasakalaṃ kartavyaṃ śūnyatānale 
AbhTb cittaviśrāntisaṃjñoyamāṇavastadanantaram  
AbhTa dṛṣṭaśrutāditadvastupronmukhatvaṃ svasaṃvidi 
AbhTb cittasaṃbodhanāmoktaḥ śāktollāsabharātmakaḥ  
AbhTa tatronmukhatvatadvastusaṃghaṭṭādvastuno hṛdi 
AbhTb rūḍheḥ pūrṇatayāveśānmitacittalayācchive  
AbhTa prāgvadbhaviṣyadaunmukhyasaṃbhāvyamitatālayāt 
AbhTb cittapralayanāmāsau visargaḥ śāmbhavaḥ paraḥ  
AbhTa tattvarakṣāvidhāneto visargatraidhamucyate 
AbhTb hṛtpadmakośamadhyasthastayoḥ saṃghaṭṭa iṣyate  
AbhTa visargontaḥ sa ca proktaścittaviśrāntilakṣaṇaḥ 
AbhTb dvitīyaḥ sa visargastu cittasaṃbodhalakṣaṇaḥ  
AbhTa ekībhūtaṃ vibhātyatra jagadetaccarācaram 
AbhTb grāhyagrāhakabhedo vai kiṃcidatreṣyate yadā  
AbhTa tadāsau sakalaḥ prokto niṣkalaḥ śivayogataḥ 
AbhTb grāhyagrāhakavicchittisaṃpūrṇagrahaṇātmakaḥ  
AbhTa tṛtīyaḥ sa visargastu cittapralayalakṣaṇaḥ 
AbhTb ekībhāvātmakaḥ sūkṣmo vijñānātmātmanirvṛtaḥ  
AbhTa nirūpitoyamarthaḥ śrīsiddhayogīśvarīmate 
AbhTb sātra kuṇḍalinī bījaṃ jīvabhūtā cidātmikā  
AbhTa tajjaṃ dhruvecchonmeṣākhyaṃ trikaṃ varṇāstataḥ punaḥ 
AbhTb ā ityavarṇādityādiyāvadvaisargikī kalā  
AbhTa kakārādisakārāntā visargātpañcadhā sa ca 
AbhTb bahiścāntaśca hṛdaye nādetha parame pade  
AbhTa bindurātmani mūrdhāntaṃ hṛdayādvyāpako hi saḥ 
AbhTb ādimāntyavihīnāstu mantrāḥ syuḥ śaradabhravat  
AbhTa gurorlakṣaṇametāvadādimāntyaṃ ca vedayet 
AbhTb pūjyaḥ sohamiva jñānī bhairavo devatātmakaḥ  
AbhTa ślokagāthādi yatkiṃcidādimāntyayutaṃ tataḥ 
AbhTb tasmādvidaṃstathā sarvaṃ mantratvenaiva paśyati  
AbhTa visargaśaktirviśvasya kāraṇaṃ ca nirūpitā 
AbhTb aitareyākhyavedānte parameśena vistarāt  
AbhTa yallohitaṃ tadagniryadvīryaṃ sūryenduvigraham 
AbhTb a iti brahma paramaṃ tatsaṃghaṭṭodayātmakam  
AbhTa tasyāpi ca paraṃ vīrya pañcabhūtakalātmakam 
AbhTb bhogyatvenānnarūpaṃ ca śabdasparśarasātmakam  
AbhTa śabdopi madhuro yasmādvīryopacayakārakaḥ 
AbhTb taddhi vīryaṃ paraṃ śuddhaṃ visisṛkṣātmakaṃ matam  
AbhTa tadbalaṃ ca tadojaśca te prāṇāḥ sā ca kāntatā 
AbhTb tasmādvīryātprajāstāśca vīrya karmasu kathyate  
AbhTa yajñādikeṣu tadvṛṣṭau sauṣadhīṣvatha tāḥ punaḥ 
AbhTb vīrye tacca prajāsvevaṃ visarge viśvarūpatā  
AbhTa śabdarāśiḥ sa evokto mātṛkā sāca kīrtitā 
AbhTb kṣobhyakṣobhakatāveśānmālinīṃ tāṃ pracakṣate  
AbhTa bījayonisamāpattivisargodayasundarā 
AbhTb mālinī hi parā śaktirnirṇītā viśvarūpiṇī  
AbhTa eṣā vastuta ekaiva parā kālasya karṣiṇī 
AbhTb śaktimadbhedayogena yāmalatvaṃ prapadyate  
AbhTa tasya pratyavamarśo yaḥ paripūrṇohamātmakaḥ 
AbhTb sa svātmani svatantratvādvibhāgamavabhāsayet  
AbhTa vibhāgābhāsane cāsya tridhā vapurudāhṛtam 
AbhTb paśyantī madhyamā sthūlā vaikharītyabhiśabditam  
AbhTa tāsāmapi tridhā rūpaṃ sthūlasūkṣmaparatvataḥ 
AbhTb tatra yā svarasandarbhasubhagā nādarūpiṇī  
AbhTa sā sthūlā khalu paśyantī varṇādyapravibhāgataḥ 
AbhTb avibhāgaikarūpatvaṃ mādhuryaṃ śaktirucyate  
AbhTa sthānavāyvādigharṣotthā sphuṭataiva ca pāruṣī 
AbhTb tadasyāṃ nādarūpāyāṃ saṃvitsavidhavṛttitaḥ  
AbhTa sājātyāntarmattama yībhūtirjhagityevopalabhyate 
AbhTb yeṣāṃ na tanmayībhūtiste dehādinimajjanam  
AbhTa avidanto magnasaṃvinmānāstvahṛdayā iti 
AbhTb yattucarmāvanaddhādi kiṃcittatraiṣa yo dhvaniḥ  
AbhTa sa sphuṭāsphuṭarūpatvānmadhyamā sthūlarūpiṇī 
AbhTb madhyāyāścāvibhāgāṃśasadbhāva iti raktatā  
AbhTa avibhāgasvaramayī yatra syāttatsurañjakam 
AbhTb avibhāgo hi nirvṛtyai dṛśyatāṃ tālapāṭhataḥ  
AbhTa kilāvyaktadhvanau tasminvādane parituṣyati 
AbhTb yā tu sphuṭānāṃ varṇānāmutpattau kāraṇaṃ bhavet  
AbhTa sā sthūlā vaikharī yasyāḥ kāryaṃ vākyādi bhūyasā 
AbhTb asminsthūlatraye yattadanusandhānamādivat  
AbhTa pṛthakpṛthaktattritayaṃ sūkṣmamityabhiśabdyate 
AbhTb ṣaḍjaṃ karomi madhuraṃ vādayāmi bruve vacaḥ  
AbhTa pṛthagevānusandhānatrayaṃ saṃvedyate kila 
AbhTb etasyāpi trayasyādyaṃ yadrupamanupādhimat  
AbhTa tatparaṃ tritayaṃ tatra śivaḥ paracidātmakaḥ 
AbhTb vibhāgābhāsanāyāṃ ca mukhyāstisrotra śaktayaḥ  
AbhTa anuttarā parecchā ca parāparatayā sthitā 
AbhTb unmeṣaśaktirjñānākhyā tvapareti nigadyate  
AbhTa kṣobharūpātpunastāsāmuktāḥ ṣaṭ saṃvidomalāḥ 
AbhTb āsāmeva samāveśātkriyāśaktitayoditāt  
AbhTa saṃvido dvādaśa proktā yāsu sarvaṃ samāpyate 
AbhTb etāvaddevadevasya mukhyaṃ tacchakticakrakam  
AbhTa etāvatā devadevaḥ pūrṇaśaktiḥ sa bhairavaḥ 
AbhTb parāmarśātmakatvena visargākṣepayogataḥ  
AbhTa iyattākalanājjñānāttāḥ proktāḥ kālikāḥ kvacit 
AbhTb śrīsāraśāstre cāpyuktaṃ madhya ekākṣarāṃ parām  
AbhTa pūjayedbhairavātmākhyāṃ yoginīdvādaśāvṛtām 
AbhTb tābhya eva catuḥṣaṣṭiparyantaṃ śakticakrakam  
AbhTa ekārataḥ samārabhya sahasrāraṃ pravartate 
AbhTb tāsāṃ ca kṛtyabhedena nāmāni bahudhāgame  
AbhTa upāsāśca dvayādvaitavyāmiśrākārayogataḥ 
AbhTb śrīmattraiśirame tacca kathitaṃ vistarādbahu  
AbhTa iha no likhitaṃ vyāsabhayāccānupayogataḥ 
AbhTb tā eva nirmalāḥ śuddhā aghorāḥ parikīrtitāḥ  
AbhTa ghoraghoratarāṇāṃ tu sotṛtvācca tadātmikāḥ 
AbhTb sṛṣṭau sthitau ca saṃhāre tadupādhitrayātyaye  
AbhTa tāsāmeva sthitaṃ rūpaṃ bahudhā pravibhajyate 
AbhTb upādhyatītaṃ yadrūpaṃ taddvidhā guravo jaguḥ  
AbhTa anullāsādupādhīnāṃ yadvā praśamayogataḥ 
AbhTb praśamaśca dvidhā śāntyā haṭhapākakrameṇa tu  
AbhTa alaṃ grāsarasākhyena satataṃ jvalanātmanā 
AbhTb haṭhapākapraśamanaṃ yattṛtīyaṃ tadeva ca 
AbhTc upadeśāya yujyeta bhedendhanavidāhakam  
AbhTa nijabodhajaṭharahutabhuji bhāvāḥ sarve samarpitā haṭhataḥ 
AbhTb vijahati bhedavibhāgaṃ nijaśaktyā taṃ samindhānāḥ  
AbhTa haṭhapākena bhāvānāṃ rūpe bhinne vilāpite 
AbhTb aśnantyamṛtasādbhūtaṃ viśvaṃ saṃvittidevatāḥ  
AbhTa tāstṛptāḥ svātmanaḥ pūrṇa hṛdayaikāntaśāyinam 
AbhTb cidvyomabhairavaṃ devamabhedenādhiśerate  
AbhTa evaṃ kṛtyakriyāveśānnāmopāsābahutvataḥ 
AbhTb āsāṃ bahuvidhaṃ rūpamabhedepyavabhāsate  
AbhTa āsāmeva ca devīnāmāvāpodvāpayogataḥ 
AbhTb ekadvitricatuṣpañcaṣaṭsaptāṣṭanavottaraiḥ  
AbhTa rudrārkānyakalāsenāprabhṛtirbhedavistaraḥ 
AbhTb alamanyena bahunā prakṛtetha niyujyate  
AbhTa saṃvidātmani viśvoyaṃ bhāvavargaḥ prapañcavān 
AbhTb pratibimbatayā bhāti yasya viśveśvaro hi saḥ  
AbhTa evamātmani yasyedṛgavikalpaḥ sadodayaḥ 
AbhTb parāmarśaḥ sa evāsau śāṃbhavopāyamudritaḥ  
AbhTa pūrṇāhantāparāmarśo yosyāyaṃ pravivecitaḥ 
AbhTb mantramudrākriyopāsāstadanyā nātra kāścana  
AbhTa bhūyobhūyaḥ samāveśaṃ nirvikalpamimaṃ śritaḥ 
AbhTb abhyeti bhairavībhāvaṃ jīvanmuktyaparābhidham  
AbhTa ita eva prabhṛtyeṣā jīvanmuktirvicāryate 
AbhTb yatra sūtraṇayāpīyamupāyopeyakalpanā  
AbhTa prāktane tvāhnike kācidbhedasya kalanāpi no 
AbhTb tenānupāye tasminko mucyate vā kathaṃ kutaḥ  
AbhTa nirvikalpe parāmarśe śāmbhavopāyanāmani 
AbhTb pañcāśadbhedatāṃ pūrvasūtritāṃ yojayedbudhaḥ  
AbhTa dharāmevāvikalpena svātmani pratibimbitām 
AbhTb paśyanbhairavatāṃ yāti jalādiṣvapyayaṃ vidhiḥ  
AbhTa yāvadante paraṃ tattvaṃ samastāvaraṇordhvagam 
AbhTb vyāpi svatantraṃ sarvajñaṃ yacchivaṃ parikalpitam  
AbhTa tadapyakalpitodārasaṃviddarpaṇabimbitam 
AbhTb paśyanvikalpavikalo bhairavībhavati svayam  
AbhTa yathā raktaṃ puraḥ paśyannirvikalpakasaṃvidā 
AbhTb tattaddvāraniraṃśaikaghaṭasaṃvittisusthitaḥ  
AbhTa tadvaddharādikaikaikasaṃghātasamudāyataḥ 
AbhTb parāmṛśansvamātmānaṃ pūrṇa evāvabhāsate  
AbhTa matta evoditamidaṃ mayyeva pratibimbitam 
AbhTb madabhinnamidaṃ ceti tridhopāyaḥ sa śāmbhavaḥ  
AbhTa sṛṣṭeḥ sthiteḥ saṃhṛteśca tadetatsūtraṇaṃ kṛtam 
AbhTb yatra sthitaṃ yataśceti tadāha spandaśāsane  
AbhTa etāvataiva hyaiśvarya saṃvidaḥ khyāpitaṃ param 
AbhTb viśvātmakatvaṃ cetyanyallakṣaṇaṃ kiṃ nu kathyatām  
AbhTa svātmanyeva cidākāśe viśvamasmyavabhāsayan 
AbhTb sraṣṭā viśvātmaka iti prathayā bhairavātmatā  
AbhTa ṣaḍadhvajātaṃ nikhilaṃ mayyeva pratibimbitam 
AbhTb sthitikartāhamasmīti sphuṭeyaṃ viśvarūpatā  
AbhTa sadoditamahābodhajvālājaṭilatātmani 
AbhTb viśvaṃ dravati mayyetaditi paśyanpraśāmyati  
AbhTa anantacitrasadgarbhasaṃsārasvapnasadmanaḥ 
AbhTb ploṣakaḥ śiva evāhamityullāsī hutāśanaḥ  
AbhTa jagatsarvaṃ mattaḥ prabhavati vibhedena bahudhā tathāpyetadrūḍhaṃ mayi vigalite tvatra na paraḥ 
AbhTb taditthaṃ yaḥ sṛṣṭisthitivilayabhekīkṛtivaśādanaṃśaṃ paśyetsa sphurati hi turīyaṃ padabhitaḥ  
AbhTa tadasminparamopāye śāmbhavādvaitaśālini 
AbhTb kepyeva yānti viśvāsaṃ pasmeśena bhāvitāḥ  
AbhTa snānaṃ vrataṃ dehaśuddhirdhāraṇā mantrayojanā 
AbhTb adhvaklṛptiryāgavidhirhomajapyasamādhayaḥ  
AbhTa ityādikalpanā kāpi nātra bhedena yujyate 
AbhTb parānugrahakāritvamatrasthasya sphuṭaṃ sthitam  
AbhTa yadi tādṛganugrāhyo daiśikasyopasarpati 
AbhTb athāsau tādṛśo na syādbhavabhaktyā ca bhāvitaḥ  
AbhTa taṃ cārādhayate bhāvitādṛśānugraheritaḥ 
AbhTb tadā vicitraṃ dīkṣādividhiṃ śikṣeta koviṃdaḥ  
AbhTa bhāvinyopi hyupāsāstā straivāyānti niṣṭhitim 
AbhTb etanmayatvaṃ paramaṃ prāpyaṃ nirvarṇyateśivam  
AbhTa iti kathitamidaṃ suvistaraṃ paramaṃ śāmbhavamātmavedanam  a
C atha śrītantrāloke caturthamāhnikam
AbhTb atha śāktamupāyamaṇḍalaṃ kathayāmaḥ paramātmasaṃvide  b
AbhTa anantarāhnikoktesminsvabhāve pārameśvare 
AbhTb pravivikṣurvikalpasya kuryātsaṃskāramañjasā  
AbhTa vikalpaḥ saṃskṛtaḥ sūte vikalpaṃ svātmasaṃskṛtam 
AbhTb svatulyaṃ sopi sopyanyaṃ sopyanyaṃ sadṛśātmakam  
AbhTa caturṣveva vikalpeṣu yaḥ saṃskāraḥ kramādasau 
AbhTb asphuṭaḥ sphuṭatābhāvī prasphuṭansphuṭitātmakaḥ  
AbhTa tataḥ sphuṭataro yāvadante sphuṭatamo bhavet 
AbhTb asphuṭādau vikalpe ca bhedopyastyāntarālikaḥ  
AbhTa tataḥ sphuṭatamodāratādrūpyaparivṛṃhitā 
AbhTb saṃvidabhyeti vimalāmavikalpasvarūpatām  
AbhTa ataśca bhairavīyaṃ yattejaḥ saṃvitsvabhāvakam 
AbhTb bhūyo bhūyo vimṛśatāṃ jāyate tatsphuṭātmatā  
AbhTa nanu saṃvitparāmraṣṭrī parāmarśamayī svataḥ 
AbhTb parāmṛśyā kathaṃ tāthārūpyasṛṣṭau tu sā jaḍā  
AbhTa ucyate svātmasaṃvittiḥ svabhāvādeva nirbharā 
AbhTb nāsyāmapāsyaṃ nādheyaṃ kiṃcidityuditaṃ purā  
AbhTa kiṃ tu durghaṭakāritvātsvācchandyānnirmalādasau 
AbhTb svātmapracchādanakrīḍāpaṇḍitaḥ parameśvaraḥ  
AbhTa anāvṛtte svarūpepi yadātmācchādanaṃ vibhoḥ 
AbhTb saiva māyā yato bheda etāvānviśvavṛttikaḥ  
AbhTa tathābhāsanamevāsya dvaitamuktaṃ maheśituḥ 
AbhTb taddvayāpāsanenāyaṃ parāmarśobhidhīyate  
AbhTa durbhedapādapasyāsya mūlaṃ kṛntanti kovidāḥ 
AbhTb dhārārūḍhena sattarkakuṭhāreṇeti niścayaḥ  
AbhTa tāmenāṃ bhāvanāmāhuḥ sarvakāmadughāṃ budhāḥ 
AbhTb sphuṭayedvastu yāpetaṃ manosthapadādapi  
AbhTa śrīpūrvaśāstre tatproktaṃ tarko yogāṅgamuttamam 
AbhTb heyādyālocanāttasmāttatra yatnaḥ praśasyate  
AbhTa mārge cetaḥ sthirībhūtaṃ heyepi viṣayecchayā 
AbhTb prerya tena nayettāvadyāvatpadamanāmayam  
AbhTa mārgotra mokṣopāyaḥ sa heyaḥ śāstrāntaroditaḥ 
AbhTb viṣiṇoti nibadhnāti yecchā niyatisaṃgatam  
AbhTa rāgatattvaṃ tayoktaṃ yat tena tatrānurajyate 
AbhTb yathā sāmrājyasaṃbhogaṃ dṛṣṭvādṛṣṭvāthabādhame  
AbhTa bhoge rajyeta durbuddhistadvanmokṣepi rāgataḥ 
AbhTb sa evāṃśaka ityuktaḥ svabhāvākhyaḥ sa tu sphuṭam  
AbhTa siddhyaṅgamiti mokṣāya pratyūha iti kovidāḥ 
AbhTb śivaśāsanamāhātmyaṃ vidannapyata eva hi  
AbhTa vaiṣṇavādhyeṣu rajyeta mūḍho rāgeṇa rañjitaḥ 
AbhTb yatastāvati sā tasya vāmākhyā śaktiraiśvarī  
AbhTa pāñcarātrikavairiñcasaugatādervijṛmbhate 
AbhTb dṛṣṭāḥ sāmrājyasaṃbhogaṃ nindantaḥ kepi vāliśāḥ  
AbhTa na tu saṃtoṣataḥ sveṣu bhogeṣvāśīḥpravartanāt 
AbhTb evaṃcidbhairavāveśanindātatparamānasāḥ  
AbhTa bhavantyatisughorābhiḥ śaktibhiḥ pātitā yataḥ 
AbhTb tena śāṃbhavamāhātmyaṃ jānanyaḥ śāsanāntare  
AbhTa āśvasto nottarītavyaṃ tena bhedamahārṇavāt 
AbhTb śrīkāmikāyāṃ proktaṃ ca pāśaprakaraṇe sphuṭam  
AbhTa vedasāṃkhyapurāṇajñāḥ pāñcarātraparāyaṇāḥ 
AbhTb ye kecidṛṣayo dhīrāḥ śāstrāntaraparāyaṇāḥ  
AbhTa bauddhārhatādyāḥ sarve te vidyārāgeṇa rañjitāḥ 
AbhTb māyāpāśena baddhatvācchivadīkṣāṃ na vindate  
AbhTa rāgaśabdena ca proktaṃ rāgatattvaṃ niyāmakam 
AbhTb māyīye tacca taṃ tasmiñchāstre niyamayediti  
AbhTa mokṣopi vaiṣṇavāderyaḥ svasaṃkalpena bhāvitaḥ 
AbhTb paraprakṛtisāyujyaṃ yadvāpyānandarūpatā  
AbhTa viśuddhacittamātraṃ vā dīpavatsaṃtatikṣayaḥ 
AbhTb sa savedyāpavedyātmapralayākalatāmayaḥ  
AbhTa taṃ prāpyāpi ciraṃ kālaṃ tadgogābhogabhuktataḥ 
AbhTb tattattvapralayānte tu tadūrdhvāṃ sṛṣṭimāgataḥ  
AbhTa mantratvameti saṃbodhādananteśena kalpitāt 
AbhTb etaccāgre taniṣyāma ityāstāṃ tāvadatra tat  
AbhTa tenājñajanatāklṛptapravādairyo viḍambitaḥ 
AbhTb asadgurau rūḍhacitsa māyāpāśena rañjitaḥ  
AbhTa sopi sattarkayogena nīyate sadguruṃ prati 
AbhTb sattarkaḥ śuddhavidyaiva sā cecchā parameśituḥ  
AbhTa śrīpūrvaśāstre tenoktaṃ sa yiyāsuḥ śivecchayā 
AbhTb bhuktimuktiprasiddhyarthaṃ nīyate sadguruṃ prati  
AbhTa śaktipātastu tatraiṣa kramikaḥ saṃpravartate 
AbhTb sthitvā yosadgurau śāstrāntare vā satpathaṃ śritaḥ  
AbhTa guruśāstragate sattvesattve cātra vibhedakam 
AbhTb śaktipātasya vaicitryaṃ purastātpravivicyate  
AbhTa uktaṃ svacchandaśāstre tat vaiṣṇavādyānpravādinaḥ 
AbhTb sarvānbhramayate māyā sāmokṣe moKṣalipsayā  
AbhTa yastu rūḍhopi tatrodyatparāmarśaviśāradaḥ 
AbhTb sa śuddhavidyāmāhātmyācchaktipātapavitritaḥ  
AbhTa ārohatyeva sanmārgaṃ pratyūhaparivarjitaḥ 
AbhTb sa tāvatkasyacittarkaḥ svata eva pravartate  
AbhTa sa ca sāṃsiddhikaḥ śāstre proktaḥ svapratyayātmakaḥ 
AbhTb kiraṇāyāṃ yadapyuktaṃ gurutaḥ śāstrataḥ svataḥ  
AbhTa tatrottarottaraṃ mukhyaṃ pūrvapūrva upāyakaḥ 
AbhTb yasya svatoyaṃ sattarkaḥ sarvatraivādhikāravān  
AbhTa abhiṣiktaḥ svasaṃvittidevībhirdīkṣitaśca saḥ 
AbhTb sa eva sarvācāryāṇāṃ madhye mukhyaḥ prakīrtitaḥ  
AbhTa tatsaṃnidhāne nānyeṣu kalpiteṣvadhikāritā 
AbhTb sa samastaṃ ca śāstrārthaṃ sattarkādeva manyate  
AbhTa śuddhavidyā hi tannāsti satyaṃ yadyanna bhāsayet 
AbhTb sarvaśāstrārthavettṛtvamakasmāccāsya jāyate  
AbhTa iti śrīpūvavākye tadakasmāditiśabdataḥ 
AbhTb lokāprasiddho yo hetuḥ sokasmāditi kathyate  
AbhTa sa caiṣa parameśānaśuddhavidyāvijṛmbhatam 
AbhTb asya bhodāśca bahavo nirbhittiḥ sahabhittikaḥ  
AbhTa sarvagoṃśagataḥ sopi mukhyāmukhyāṃśaniṣṭhitaḥ 
AbhTb bhittiḥ paropajīvitvaṃ parā prajñātha tatkṛtiḥ  
AbhTa adṛṣṭamaṇḍalopyevaṃ yaḥ kaścidvetti tattvataḥ 
AbhTb sa siddhibhāgbhavennityaṃ sa yogī sa ca dīkṣitaḥ  
AbhTa evaṃ yo vetti tattvena tasya nirvāṇagāminī 
AbhTb dīkṣā bhavediti proktaṃ tacchrītriṃśakaśāsane  
AbhTa akalpito gururjñayaḥ sāṃsiddhika iti smṛtaḥ 
AbhTb yastu tadrūpabhāgātmabhāvanātaḥ paraṃ vinā  
AbhTa śāstravitsa guruḥ śāstre proktokalpitakalpakaḥ 
AbhTb tasyāpi bhedā utkṛṣṭamadhyamandādyupāyataḥ  
AbhTa bhāvanātotha vā dhyānājjapātsvapnādvratāddhuteḥ 
AbhTb prāpnotyakalpitodāramabhiṣekaṃ mahāmatiḥ  
AbhTa śrīmadvājasanīye śrīvīre śrībrahmayāmale 
AbhTb śrīsiddhāyāmidaṃ dhātrā proktamanyatra ca sphuṭam  
AbhTa tasya svecchāpravṛttatvātkāraṇānantateṣyate 
AbhTb kadācidbhaktiyogena karmaṇā vidyayāpi vā  
AbhTa jñānadharmopadeśena mantrairvā dīkṣayāpi vā 
AbhTb evamādyairanekaiśca prakāraiḥ parameśvaraḥ  
AbhTa saṃsāriṇonugṛhṇāti viśvasya jagataḥ patiḥ 
AbhTb mātṛmaṇḍalasaṃbodhātsaṃskārāttapasaḥ priye  
AbhTa dhyānādyogājjapājjñānānmantrārādhanāto vratāt 
AbhTb saṃprāpyaṃ kulasāmānyaṃ jñānaṃ kaulikasiddhidam  
AbhTa tattvajñānātmakaṃ sādhyaṃ yatra yatraiva dṛśyate 
AbhTb sa eva hi gurustatra hetujālaṃ prakalpyatām  
AbhTa tattvajñānādṛte nānyallakṣaṇaṃ brahmayāmale 
AbhTb tatraiva coktaṃ sevāyāṃ kṛtāyāmavikalpataḥ  
AbhTa sādhakasya na cetsiddhiḥ kiṃ kāryamiti codite 
AbhTb ātmīyamasya saṃjñānakrameṇa svātmadīkṣaṇam  
AbhTa sasphuratvaprasiddhyarthaṃ tataḥ sādhyaṃ prasiddhyati 
AbhTb anena svātmavijñānaṃ sasphuratvaprasādhakam  
AbhTa uktaṃ mukhyatayācāryo bhavedyadi na sasphuraḥ 
AbhTb tatraiva ca punaḥ śrīmadraktārādhanakarmaṇi  
AbhTa vidhiṃ proktaṃ sadā kurvanmāsenācārya ucyate 
AbhTb pakṣeṇa sādhakordhārdhātputrakaḥ samayī tathā  
AbhTa dīkṣayejjapayogena raktādevī kramādyataḥ 
AbhTb guroralābhe proktasya vidhimetaṃ samācaret  
AbhTa mate ca pustakādvidyādhyayane doṣa īdṛśaḥ 
AbhTb ukto yastena taddoṣābhāvesau na niṣiddhatā  
AbhTa mantradravyādiguptatve phalaṃ kimiti codite 
AbhTb pustakādhītavidyā ye dīkṣāsamayavarjitāḥ  
AbhTa tāmasāḥ parahiṃsādi vaśyādi ca carantyalam 
AbhTb na ca tattvaṃ vidustena doṣabhāja iti sphuṭam  
AbhTa pūrvaṃ padayugaṃ vācyamanyonyaṃ hetuhetumat 
AbhTb yastu śāstraṃ vinā naiti śuddhavidyākhyasaṃvidam  
AbhTa guroḥ sa śāstramanvicchustaduktaṃ kramamācaret 
AbhTb yena kenāpyupāyena gurumārādhya bhaktitaḥ  
AbhTa taddīkṣākramayogena śāstrārthaṃ vettyasau tataḥ 
AbhTb abhiṣekaṃ samāsādya yo bhavetsa tu kalpitaḥ  
AbhTa sannapyaśeṣapāśaughavinivartanakovidaḥ 
AbhTb yo yathākramayogena kasmiṃścicchāstravastuni  
AbhTa ākasmikaṃ brajedbodhaṃ kalpitākalpito hi saḥ 
AbhTb tasya yokalpito bhāgaḥ sa tu śreṣṭhamaḥ smṛtaḥ  
AbhTa utkarṣaḥ śuddhavidyāṃśatāratamyakṛto yataḥ 
AbhTb yathā bhedenādisiddhācchivānmuktaśivā hyadhaḥ  
AbhTa tathā sāṃsiddhikajñānādāhṛtajñāninodhamāḥ 
AbhTb tatsaṃnidhau nādhikārasteṣāṃ muktaśivātmavat  
AbhTa kiṃ tu tūṣṇīṃsthitiryadvā kṛtyaṃ tadanuvartanam 
AbhTb yastvakalpitarūpopi saṃvādadṛḍhatākṛte  
AbhTa anyato labdhasaṃskāraḥ sa sākṣādbhairavo guruḥ 
AbhTb yataḥ śāstrakramāttajjñaguruprajñānuśīlanāt  
AbhTa ātmapratyayitaṃ jñānaṃ pūrṇatvādbhairavāyate 
AbhTb tena śrīkiraṇoktaṃ yadgurutaḥ śāstrataḥ svataḥ  
AbhTa tripratyayamidaṃ jñānamiti yacca niśāṭane 
AbhTb tatsaṃghātaviparyāsavigrahairbhāsate tathā  
AbhTa karaṇasya vicitratvādvicitrāmeva tāṃ chidam 
AbhTb kartuṃ vāsīṃ ca ṭaṅkaṃ ca krakacaṃ cāpi gṛhṇate  
AbhTa tāvacca chedanaṃ hyekaṃ tathaivādyābhisaṃdhitaḥ 
AbhTb itthameva mitau vācyaṃ karaṇasya svakaṃ vapuḥ
