AbhTa na svatantraṃ svato mānaṃ kuryādadhigamaṃ haṭhāt 
AbhTb pramātrāśvāsaparyanto yatodhigama ucyate  
AbhTa āśvāsaśca vicitrosau śaktipātavaśāttathā 
AbhTb pramitepi pramāṇānāmavakāśostyataḥ sphuṭaḥ  
AbhTa dṛṣṭvā dṛṣṭvā samāśliṣya ciraṃ saṃcarvya cetasā 
AbhTb priyā yaiḥ parituṣyeta kiṃ brūmaḥ kila tānprati  
AbhTa itthaṃ ca mānasaṃplutyāmapi nādhigate gatiḥ 
AbhTb na vyarthatā nānavasthā nānyonyāśrayatāpi ca  
AbhTa evaṃ yogāṅgamiyati tarka eva na cāparam 
AbhTb antarantaḥ parāmarśapāṭavātiśayāya saḥ  
AbhTa ahiṃsā satyamasteyabrahmacaryāparigrahāḥ 
AbhTb iti pañca yamāḥ sākṣātsaṃvittau nopayoginaḥ  
AbhTa tapaḥprabhṛtayo ye ca niyamā yattathāsanam 
AbhTb prāṇāyāmāśca ye sarvametadbāhyavijṛmbhitam  
AbhTa śrīmadvīrāvalau coktaṃ bodhamātre śivātmake 
AbhTb cittapralayabandhena pralīne śaśibhāskare  
AbhTa prāpte ca dvādaśe bhāge jīvāditye svabodhake 
AbhTb mokṣaḥ sa eva kathitaḥ prāṇāyāmo nirarthakaḥ  
AbhTa prāṇāyāmo na kartavyaḥ śarīraṃ yena pīḍyate 
AbhTb rahasyaṃ vetti yo yatra sa muktaḥ sa ca mocakaḥ  
AbhTa pratyāhāraśca nāmāyamarthebhyokṣadhiyāṃ hi yaḥ 
AbhTb anibaddhasya bandhasya tadantaḥ kila kīlanam  
AbhTa cittasya viṣaye kvāpi bandhanaṃ dhāraṇātmakam 
AbhTb tatsadṛgjñānasaṃtāno dhyānamastamitā param  
AbhTa yadā tu jñeyatādātmyameva saṃvidi jāyate 
AbhTb grāhyagrahaṇatādvaitaśūnyateyaṃ samāhitiḥ  
AbhTa tadeṣā dhāraṇādhyānasamādhitritayī parām 
AbhTb saṃvidaṃ prati no kaṃcidupayogaṃ samaśnute  
AbhTa yogāṅgatā yamādestu samādhyantasya varṇyate 
AbhTb svapūrvapūrvopāyatvādantyatarkopayogataḥ  
AbhTa antaḥ saṃvidi rūḍhaṃ hi taddvārā prāṇadehayoḥ 
AbhTb buddhau vārpyaṃ tadabhyāsānnaiṣa nyāyastu saṃvidi  
AbhTa atha vāsmaddṛśi prāṇadhīdehāderapi sphuṭam 
AbhTb sarvātmakatvāttatrasthopyabhyāsonyavyapohanam  
AbhTa deha utplutisaṃpātadharmojjigamiṣārasāt 
AbhTb utplāvyate tadvipakṣapātāśaṅkāvyapohanāt  
AbhTa guruvākyaparāmarśasadṛśe svavimarśane 
AbhTb prabuddhe tadvipakṣāṇāṃ vyudāsaḥ pāṭhacintane  
AbhTa nahyasya guruṇā śakyaṃ svaṃ jñānaṃ śabda eva vā 
AbhTb dhiyi ropayituṃ tena svaprabodhakramo dhruvam  
AbhTa ata eva svapnakāle śrute tatrāpi vastuni 
AbhTb tādātmyabhāvanāyogo na phalāya na bhaṇyate  
AbhTa saṃketānādare śabdaniṣṭhamāmarśanaṃ paṭhiḥ 
AbhTb tadādare tadarthastu cinteti paricarcyatām  
AbhTa tadadvayāyāṃ saṃvittāvabhyāsonupayogavān 
AbhTb kevalaṃ dvaitamālinyaśaṅkānirmūlanāya saḥ  
AbhTa dvaitaśaṅkāśca tarkeṇa tarkyanta iti varṇitam 
AbhTb tattarkasādhanāyāstu yamāderapyupāyatā  
AbhTa uktaṃ śrīpūrvaśastre ca na dvaitaṃ nāpi cādvayam 
AbhTb liṅgapūjādikaṃ sarvamityupakramya śaṃbhunā  
AbhTa vihitaṃ sarvamevātra pratiṣiddhamathāpi vā 
AbhTb prāṇāyāmādikairaṅgairyogāḥ syuḥ kṛttrimā yataḥ  
AbhTa tattenākṛtakasyāsya kalāṃ nārghanti ṣoḍaśīm 
AbhTb kiṃ tvetadatra deveśi niyamena vidhīyate  
AbhTa tattve cetaḥ sthiraṃ kāryaṃ tacca yasya yathāstviti 
AbhTb evaṃ dvaitaparāmarśanāśāya parameśvaraḥ  
AbhTa kvacitsvabhāvamamalamāmṛśannaniśaṃ sthitaḥ 
AbhTb yaḥ svabhāvaparāmarśa indriyārthādyupāyataḥ  
AbhTa vinaiva tanmukhonyo vā svātantryāttadvikalpanam 
AbhTb tacca svacchasvatantrātmaratnanirbhāsini sphuṭam  
AbhTa bhāvaughe bhedasaṃdhātṛ svātmano naiśamucyate 
AbhTb tadeva tu samastārthanirbharātmaikagocaram  
AbhTa śuddhavidyātmakaṃ sarvamevedamahamityalam 
AbhTb idaṃ vikalpanaṃ śuddhavidyārūpaṃ sphuṭātmakam  
AbhTa pratihantīha māyīyaṃ vikalpaṃ bhedabhāvakam 
AbhTb śuddhavidyāparāmarśo yaḥ sa eva tvanekadhā  
AbhTa snānaśuddhyarcanāhomadhyānajapyādiyogataḥ 
AbhTb viśvametatsvasaṃvittirasanirbharitaṃ rasāt  
AbhTa āviśya śuddho nikhilaṃ tarpayedadhvamaṇlam 
AbhTb ullāsibodhahutabhugdagdhaviśvendhanodite  
AbhTa sitabhasmani dehasya majjanaṃ snānamucyate 
AbhTb itthaṃ ca vihitasnānastarpitānantadevataḥ  
AbhTa tatopi dehārambhīṇi tattvāni pariśodhayet 
AbhTb śivātmakeṣvapyeteṣu buddhiryā vyatirekiṇī  
AbhTa saivāśuddhiḥ parākhyātā śuddhistaddhīvimardanam 
AbhTb evaṃ svadehaṃ bodhaikapātraṃ galitabhedakam  
AbhTa paśyansaṃvittimātratve svatantre tiṣṭhati prabhuḥ 
AbhTb yatkiṃcinmānasāhlādi yatra kvāpīndriyasthitau  
AbhTa yojyate brahmasaddhāmni pūjopakaraṇaṃ hi tat 
AbhTb pūjā nāma vibhinnasya bhāvaughasyāpi saṃgatiḥ  
AbhTa svatantravimalānantabhairavīyacidātmanā 
AbhTb tathāhi saṃvideveyamantarbāhyobhayātmanā  
AbhTa svātantryādvartamānaiva parāmarśasvarūpiṇī 
AbhTb sa ca dvādaśadhā tatra sarvamantarbhavedyataḥ  
AbhTa sūrya eva hi somātmā sa ca viśvamayaḥ sthitaḥ 
AbhTb kalādvādaśakātmaiva tatsaṃvitparamārthataḥ  
AbhTa sā ca mātari vijñāne māne karaṇagocare 
AbhTb meye caturvidhaṃ bhāti rūpamāśritya sarvadā  
AbhTa śuddhasaṃvinmayī prācye jñāne śabdanarūpiṇī 
AbhTb karaṇe grahaṇākārā yataḥ śrīyogasaṃcare  
AbhTa ye cakṣurmaṇḍale śvete pratyakṣe parameśvari 
AbhTb ṣoḍaśāraṃ dvādaśāraṃ tatrasthaṃ cakramuttamam  
AbhTa prativāraṇavadrakte tadbahirye taducyate 
AbhTb dvitīyaṃ madhyage ye te kṛṣṇaśvete ca maṇḍale  
AbhTa tadantarye sthite śuddhe bhinnāñjanasamaprabhe 
AbhTb caturdale tu te jñeye agnīṣomātmake priye  
AbhTa mithunatve sthite ye ca cakre dve parameśvari 
AbhTb saṃmīlanonmīlanaṃ te anyonyaṃ vidadhātake  
AbhTa yathā yoniśca liṅgaṃ ca saṃyogātsravatomṛtam 
AbhTb tathāmṛtāgnisaṃyogāddravataste na saṃśayaḥ  
AbhTa taccakrapīḍanādrātrau jyotirbhātyarkasomagam 
AbhTb tāṃ dṛṣṭvā paramāṃ jyotsnāṃ kālajñānaṃ pravartate  
AbhTa sahasrāraṃ bhaveccakraṃ tābhyāmupari saṃsthitam 
AbhTb tataścakrātsamudbhūtaṃ brahmāṇḍaṃ tadudāhṛtam  
AbhTa tatrasthāṃ muñcate dhārāṃ somo hyagnipradīpitaḥ 
AbhTb sṛjatītthaṃ jagatsarvamātmanyātmanyanantakam  
AbhTa ṣoḍaśadvādaśārābhyāmaṣṭāreṣvatha sarvaśaḥ 
AbhTb evaṃ krameṇa sarvatra cakreṣvamṛtamuttamam  
AbhTa somaḥ sravati yāvacca pañcānāṃ cakrapaddhatiḥ 
AbhTb tatpunaḥ pibati prītyā haṃso haṃsa iti sphuran  
AbhTa sakṛdyasya tu saṃśrutyā puṇyapāpairna lipyate 
AbhTb pañcāre savikārotha bhūtvā somasrutāmṛtāt  
AbhTa dhāvati trirasārāṇi guhyacakrāṇyasau vibhuḥ 
AbhTb yato jātaṃ jagallīnaṃ yatra ca svakalīlayā  
AbhTa tatrānandaśca sarvasya brahmacārī ca tatparaḥ 
AbhTb tatra siddhiśca muktiśca samaṃ saṃprāpyate dvayam  
AbhTa ata ūrdhvaṃ punaryāti yāvadbrahmātmakaṃ padam 
AbhTb agnīṣomau samau tatra sṛjyete cātmanātmani  
AbhTa tatrasthastāpitaḥ somo dvedhā jaṅghe vyavasthitaḥ 
AbhTb adhastaṃ pātayedagniramṛtaṃ sravati kṣaṇāt  
AbhTa gulphajānvādiṣu vyaktaṃ kuṭilārkapradīpitā 
AbhTb sā śaktistāpitā bhūyaḥ pañcārādikramaṃ sṛjet  
AbhTa evaṃ śrotrepi vijñeyaṃ yāvatpādāntagocaram 
AbhTb pādāṅguṣṭhātsamārabhya yāvadbrahmāṇḍadarśanam  
AbhTa ityajānannaiva yogī jānanviśvaprabhurbhavet 
AbhTb jvalannivāsau brahmādyairdṛśyate parameśvaraḥ  
AbhTa atra tātparyataḥ proktamakṣe kramacatuṣṭayam 
AbhTb ekaikatra yatastena dvādaśātmakatoditā  
AbhTa na vyākhyātaṃ tu nirbhajya yatotisarahasyakam 
AbhTb meyepi devī tiṣṭhantī māsarāśyādirūpiṇī  
AbhTa ata eṣā sthitā saṃvidantarbāhyobhayātmanā 
AbhTb svayaṃ nirbhāsya tatrānyadbhāsayantīva bhāsate  
AbhTa tataśca prāgiyaṃ śuddhā tathābhāsanasotsukā 
AbhTb sṛṣṭiṃ kalayate devī tannāmnāgama ucyate  
AbhTa tathā bhāsitavastvaṃśarañjanāṃ sā bahirmukhī 
AbhTb svavṛtticakreṇa samaṃ tatopi kalayantyalam  
AbhTa sthitireṣaiva bhāvasya tāmantarmukhatārasāt 
AbhTb saṃjihīrṣuḥ sthiternāśaṃ kalayantī nirucyate  
AbhTa tatopi saṃhārarase pūrṇe vighnakarīṃ svayam 
AbhTb śaṅkāṃ yamātmikāṃ bhāge sūte saṃharatepi ca  
AbhTa saṃhṛtya śaṅkāṃ śaṅkyārthavarjaṃ vā bhāvamaṇḍale 
AbhTb saṃhṛtiṃ kalayatyeva svātmavahnau vilāpanāt  
AbhTa vilāpanātmikāṃ tāṃ ca bhāvasaṃhṛtimātmani 
AbhTb āmṛśatyeva yenaiṣā mayā grastamiti sphuret  
AbhTa saṃhāryopādhiretasyāḥ svasvabhāvo hi saṃvidaḥ 
AbhTb nirupādhini saṃśuddhe saṃvidrūpeṣastamīyate  
AbhTa vilāpitepi bhāvaughe kaṃcidbhāvaṃ tadaiva sā 
AbhTb āśyānayedya evāste śaṅkā saṃskārarūpakaḥ  
AbhTa śubhāśubhatayā soyaṃ soṣyate phalasaṃpadam 
AbhTb pūrvaṃ hi bhogātpaścādvā śaṅkeyaṃ vyavatiṣṭhate  
AbhTa anyadāśyānitamapi tadaiva drāvayediyam 
AbhTb prāyaścittādikarmabhyo brahmahatyādikarmavat  
AbhTa rodhanāddrāvaṇādrūpamitthaṃ kalayate citiḥ 
AbhTb tadapi drāvayedeva tadapyāśyānayedatha  
AbhTa itthaṃ bhogyepi saṃbhukte sati tatkaraṇānyapi 
AbhTb saṃharantī kalayate dvādaśaivāhamātmani  
AbhTa karmabuddhyakṣavargo hi buddhyanto dvādaśātmakaḥ 
AbhTb prakāśakatvātsūryātmā bhinne vastuni jṛmbhate  
AbhTa ahaṃkārastu karaṇamabhimānaikasādhanam 
AbhTb avicchinnaparāmarśī līyate tena tatra saḥ  
AbhTa yathāhi khaṅgapāśādeḥ karaṇasya vibhedinaḥ 
AbhTb abhedini svahastādau layastadvadayaṃ vidhiḥ  
AbhTa tenendriyaughamārtaṇḍamaṇḍalaṃ kalayetsvayam 
AbhTb saṃviddevī svatantratvātkalpitehaṃkṛtātmani  
AbhTa sa eva paramādityaḥ pūrṇakalpastrayodaśaḥ 
AbhTb karaṇatvātprayātyeva kartari pralayaṃ sphuṭam  
AbhTa kartā ca dvividhaḥ proktaḥ kalpitākalpitātmakaḥ 
AbhTb kalpito dehabuddhyādivyavacchedena carcitaḥ  
AbhTa kālāgnirudrasaṃjñāsya śāstreṣu paribhāṣitā 
AbhTb kālo vyavacchittadyukto vahnirbhoktā yataḥ smṛtaḥ  
AbhTa saṃsārāklṛptiklṛptibhyāṃ rodhanāddrāvaṇātprabhuḥ 
AbhTb anivṛttapaśūbhāvastatrāhaṃkṛtpralīyate  
AbhTa sopi kalpitavṛttitvādviśvābhedaikaśālini 
AbhTb vikāsini mahākāle līyatehamidaṃmaye  
AbhTa etasyāṃ svātmasaṃvittāvidaṃ sarvamahaṃ vibhuḥ 
AbhTb iti pravikasadrūpā saṃvittiravabhāsate  
AbhTa tatontaḥsthitasarvātmabhāvabhogoparāgiṇī 
AbhTb paripūrṇāpi saṃvittirakule dhāmni līyate  
AbhTa pramātṛvargo mānaughaḥ pramāśca bahudhā sthitāḥ 
AbhTb meyaugha iti yatsarvamatra cinmātrameva tat  
AbhTa iyatīṃ rūpavaicitrīmāśrayantyāḥ svasaṃvidaḥ 
AbhTb svācchandyamanapekṣaṃ yatsā parā parameśvarī  
AbhTa imāḥ prāguktakalanāstadvijṛmbhocyate yataḥ 
AbhTb kṣepo jñānaṃ ca saṃkhyānaṃ gatirnāda iti kramāt  
AbhTa svātmano bhedanaṃ kṣepo bheditasyāvikalpanam 
AbhTb jñānaṃ vikalpaḥ saṃkhyānamanyato vyatibhedanāt  
AbhTa gatiḥ svarūpārohitvaṃ pratibimbavadeva yat 
AbhTb nādaḥ svātmaparāmarśaśeṣatā tadvilopanāt  
AbhTa iti pañcavidhāmenāṃ kalanāṃ kurvatī parā 
AbhTb devī kālī tathā kālakarṣiṇī ceti kathyate  
AbhTa mātṛsadbhāvasaṃjñāsyāstenoktā yatpramātṛṣu 
AbhTb etāvadantasaṃvittau pramātṛtvaṃ sphuṭībhavet  
AbhTa vāmeśvarītiśabdena proktā śrīniśisaṃcare 
AbhTb itthaṃ dvādaśadhā saṃvittiṣṭhantī viśvamātṛṣu  
AbhTa ekaiveti na kopyasyāḥ kramasya niyamaḥ kvacit 
AbhTb kramābhāvānna yugapattadabhāvātkramopi na  
AbhTa kramākramakathātītaṃ saṃvittattvaṃ sunirmalam 
AbhTb tadasyāḥ saṃvido devyā yatra kvāpi pravartanam  
AbhTa tatra tādātmyayogena pūjā pūrṇaiva vartate 
AbhTb parāmarśasvabhāvatvādetasyā yaḥ svayaṃ dhvaniḥ  
AbhTa sadoditaḥ sa evoktaḥ paramaṃ hṛdayaṃ mahat 
AbhTb hṛdaye svavimarśosau drāvitāśeṣaviśvakaḥ  
AbhTa bhāvagrahādiparyantabhāvī sāmānyasaṃjñakaḥ 
AbhTb spandaḥ sa kathyate śāstre svātmanyucchalanātmakaḥ  
AbhTa kiṃciccalanametāvadananyasphuraṇaṃ hi yat 
AbhTb ūrmireṣā vibodhābdherna saṃvidanayā vinā  
AbhTa nistaraṅgataraṅgādivṛttireva hi sindhutā 
AbhTb sārametatsamastasya yaccitsāraṃ jaḍaṃ jagat  
AbhTa tadadhīnapratiṣṭhatvāttatsāraṃ hṛdayaṃ mahat 
AbhTb tathā hi sadidaṃ brahmamūlaṃ māyāṇḍasaṃjñitam  
AbhTa icchājñānakriyārohaṃ vinā naiva saducyate 
AbhTb tacchaktitritayārohādbhairavīye cidātmani  
AbhTa visṛjyate hi tattasmādbahirvātha visṛjyate 
AbhTb evaṃ sadrūpataivaiṣāṃ satāṃ śaktitrayātmatām  
AbhTa visargaṃ parabodhena samākṣipyaiva vartate 
AbhTb tatsadeva bahīrūpaṃ prāgbodhāgnivilāpitam  
AbhTa antarnadatparāmarśaśeṣībhūtaṃ tatopyalam 
AbhTb khātmatvameva saṃprāptaṃ śaktitritayagocarāt  
AbhTa vedanātmakatāmetya saṃhārātmani līyate 
AbhTb idaṃ saṃhārahṛdayaṃ prācyaṃ sṛṣṭau ca hṛnmatam  
AbhTa etadrūpaparāmarśamakṛtrimamanābilam 
AbhTb ahamityāhureṣaiva prakāśasya prakāśatā  
AbhTa etadvīryaṃ hi sarveṣāṃ mantrāṇāṃ hṛdayātmakam 
AbhTb vinānena jaḍāste syurjīvā iva vinā hṛdā  
AbhTa akṛtrimaitaddhṛdayārūḍho yatkiṃcidācaret 
AbhTb prāṇyādvā mṛśate vāpi sa sarvosya japo mataḥ  
AbhTa yadeva svecchayā sṛṣṭisvābhāvyādbahirantarā 
AbhTb nirmīyate tadevāsya dhyānaṃ syātpāramārthikam  
AbhTa nirākāre hi ciddhāmni viśvākṛtimaye sati 
AbhTb phalārthināṃ kācideva dhyeyatvenākṛtiḥ sthitā  
AbhTa yathā hyabhedātpūrṇepi bhāve jalamupāharan 
AbhTb anyākṛtyapahānena ghaṭamarthayate rasāt  
AbhTa tathaiva parameśānaniyatipravijṛmbhaṇāt 
AbhTb kācidevākṛtiḥ kāṃcit sūte phalavikalpanām  
AbhTa yastu saṃpūrṇahṛdayo na phalaṃ nāma vāñchati 
AbhTb tasya viśvākṛtirdevī sā cāvacchedavarjanāt  
AbhTa kule yogina udriktabhairavīyaparāsavāt 
AbhTb ghūrṇitasya sthitirdehe mudrā yā kācideva sā  
AbhTa antarindhanasaṃbhāramanapekṣyaiva nityaśaḥ 
AbhTb jājvalītyakhilākṣaughaprasṛtograśikhaḥ śikhī  
AbhTa bodhāgnau tādṛśe bhāvā viśantastasya sanmahaḥ 
AbhTb udrecayanto gacchanti homakarmanimittatām  
AbhTa yaṃ kaṃcitparameśānaśaktipātapavitritam 
AbhTb purobhāvya svayaṃ tiṣṭheduktavaddīkṣitastu saḥ  
AbhTa japyādau homaparyante yadyapyekaikakarmaṇi 
AbhTb udeti rūḍhiḥ paramā tathāpītthaṃ nirūpitam  
AbhTa yathāhi tatra tatrāśvaḥ samanimnonnatādiṣu 
AbhTb citre deśe vāhyamāno yātīcchāmātrakalpitām  
AbhTa tathā saṃvidvicitrābhiḥ śāntaghoratarādibhiḥ 
AbhTb bhaṅgībhirabhito dvaitaṃ tyājitā bhairavāyate  
AbhTa yathā puraḥsthe mukure nijaṃ vaktraṃ vibhāvayan 
AbhTb bhūyo bhūyastadekātma vaktraṃ vetti nijātmanaḥ  
AbhTa tathā vikalpamukure dhyānapūjārcanātmani 
AbhTb ātmānaṃ bhairavaṃ paśyannacirāttanmayībhavet  
AbhTa tanmayībhavanaṃ nāma prāptiḥ sānuttarātmani 
AbhTb pūrṇatvasya parā kāṣṭhā setyatra na phalāntaram  
AbhTa phalaṃ sarvamapūrṇatve tatra tatra prakalpitam 
AbhTb akalpite hi pūrṇatve phalamanyatkimucyatām  
AbhTa eṣa yāgavidhiḥ kopi kasyāpi hṛdi vartate 
AbhTb yasya prasīdecciccakraṃ drāgapaścimajanmanaḥ  
AbhTa atra yāge gato rūḍhiṃ kaivalyamadhigacchati 
AbhTb lokairālokyamāno hi dehabandhavidhau sthitaḥ  
AbhTa atra nāthaḥ samācāraṃ paṭaleṣṭādaśebhyadhāt 
AbhTb nātra śuddhirna cāśuddhirna bhakṣyādivicāraṇam  
AbhTa na dvaitaṃ nāpi cādvaitaṃ liṅgapūjādikaṃ na ca 
AbhTb na cāpi tatparityāgo niṣparigrahatāpi vā  
AbhTa saparigrahatā vāpi jaṭābhasmādisaṃgrahaḥ 
AbhTb tattyāgo na vratādīnāṃ caraṇācaraṇaṃ ca yat  
AbhTa kṣetrādisaṃpraveśaśca samayādiprapālanam 
AbhTb parasvarūpaliṅgādi nāmagotrādikaṃ ca yat  
AbhTa nāsminvidhīyate kiṃcinna cāpi pratiṣidhyate 
AbhTb vihitaṃ sarvamevātra pratiṣiddhamathāpi ca  
AbhTa kiṃ tvetadatra deveśi niyamena vidhīyate 
AbhTb tattve cetaḥ sthirīkāryaṃ suprasannena yoginā  
AbhTa tacca yasya yathaiva syātsa tathaiva samācaret 
AbhTb tattve niścalacittastu bhuñjāno viṣayānapi  
AbhTa na saṃspṛśyeta doṣaiḥ sa padmapatramivāmbhasā 
AbhTb viṣāpahārimantrādisaṃnaddho bhakṣayannapi  
AbhTa viṣaṃ na muhyate tena tadvadyogī mahāmatiḥ 
AbhTb aśuddhaṃ hi kathaṃ nāma dehādyaṃ pāñcabhautikam  
AbhTa prakāśatātirikte kiṃ śuddhyaśuddhī hi vastunaḥ 
AbhTb aśuddhasya ca bhāvasya śuddhiḥ syāttādṛśaiva kim  
AbhTa anyonyāśrayavaiyarthyānavasthā itthamatra hi 
AbhTb pṛthivī jalataḥ śuddhyejjalaṃ dharaṇitastathā  
AbhTa anyonyāśrayatā seyamaśuddhatvepyayaṃ kramaḥ 
AbhTb aśuddhājjalataḥ śuddhyeddhareti vyarthatā bhavet  
AbhTa vāyuto vāriṇo vāyostejasastasya vānyataḥ 
AbhTb bahurūpādikā mantrāḥ pāvanātteṣu śuddhatā  
AbhTa mantrāḥ svabhāvataḥ śuddhā yadi tepi na kiṃ tathā 
AbhTb śivātmatā teṣu śuddhiryadi tatrāpi sā na kim  
AbhTa śivātmatvāparijñānaṃ na mantreṣu dharādivat 
AbhTb te tena śuddhā iti cettajjñaptistarhi śuddhatā  
AbhTa yoginaṃ prati sā cāsti bhāveṣviti viśuddhatā 
AbhTb nanu codanayā śuddhyaśuddhyādikaviniścayaḥ  
AbhTa itthamastu tathāpyeṣā codanaiva śivoditā 
AbhTb kā syātsatīti cedetadanyatra pravitānitam  
AbhTa vaidikyā bādhiteyaṃ cedviparītaṃ na kiṃ bhavet 
AbhTb samyakcenmanyase bādho viśiṣṭaviṣayatvataḥ  
AbhTa apavādena kartavyaḥ sāmānyavihite vidhau 
AbhTb śuddhyaśuddhī ca sāmānyavihite tattvabodhini  
AbhTa puṃsi te bādhite eva tathā cātreti varṇitam 
AbhTb nārthavādādiśaṅkā ca vākye māheśvare bhavet  
AbhTa abuddhipūrvaṃ hi tathā saṃsthite satataṃ bhavet 
AbhTb vyomādirūpe nigame śaṅkā mithyārthatāṃ prati  
AbhTa anavacchinnavijñānavaiśvarūpyasunirbharaḥ 
AbhTb śāstrātmanā sthito devo mithyātvaṃ kvāpi nārhati  
AbhTa icchāvānbhāvarūpeṇa yathā tiṣṭhāsurīśvaraḥ 
AbhTb tatsvarūpābhidhānena tiṣṭhāsuḥ sa tathā sthitaḥ  
AbhTa arthavādopi yatrānyavidhyādimukhamīkṣate 
AbhTb tatrāstvasatyaḥ svātantrye sa eva tu vidhāyakaḥ  
AbhTa vidhivākyāntare gacchannaṅgabhāvamathāpi vā 
AbhTb na nirarthakaṃ evāyaṃ saṃnidhergajaḍādivat  
AbhTa svārthapratyāyanaṃ cāsya svasaṃvittyaiva bhāsate 
AbhTb tadapahnavanaṃ kartuṃ śakyaṃ vidhiniṣedhayoḥ  
AbhTa yuktiścātrāsti vākyeṣu svasaṃviccāpyabādhitā 
AbhTb yā samagrārthamāṇikyatattvaniścayakāriṇī  
AbhTa mṛtadehetha dehotthe yā cāśuddhiḥ prakīrtitā 
AbhTb anyatra neti buddhyantāmaśuddhaṃ saṃvidaścyutam  
AbhTa saṃvittādātmyamāpannaṃ sarvaṃ śuddhamataḥ sthitam 
AbhTb śrīmadvīrāvalau coktaṃ śuddhyaśuddhinirūpaṇe  
AbhTa sarveṣāṃ vāhako jīvo nāsti kiṃcidajīvakam 
AbhTb yatkiṃcijjīvarahitamaśuddhaṃ tadvijānata  
AbhTa tasmādyatsaṃvido nātidūre tacchudvimāvahet 
AbhTb avikalpena bhāvena munayopi tathābhavan  
AbhTa lokasaṃrakṣaṇārthaṃ tu tattattvaṃ taiḥ pragopitam 
AbhTb bahiḥ satsvapi bhāveṣu śuddhyaśuddhī na nīlavat  
AbhTa pramātṛdharma evāyaṃ cidaikyānaikyavedanāt 
AbhTb yadi vā vastudharmopi mātrapekṣānibandhanaḥ  
AbhTa sautrāmaṇyāṃ surā hotuḥ śuddhānyasya viparyayaḥ 
AbhTb anena codanānāṃ ca svavākyairapi bādhanam  
AbhTa kvacitsaṃdarśitaṃ brahmahatyāvidhiniṣedhavat 
AbhTb bhakṣyādividhayopyenaṃ nyāyamāśritya carcitāḥ  
AbhTa sarvajñānottarādau ca bhāṣate sma maheśvaraḥ 
AbhTb nararṣidevadruhiṇaviṣṇurudrādyudīritam  
AbhTa uttarottaravaiśiṣṭyāt pūrvapūrvaprabādhakam 
AbhTb na śaivaṃ vaiṣṇavairvākyairbādhanīyaṃ kadācana  
AbhTa vaiṣṇavaṃ brahmasaṃbhūtairnetyādi paricarcayet 
AbhTb bādhate yo vaiparītyātsamūḍhaḥ pāpabhāgbhavet  
AbhTa tasmānmukhyatayā skanda lokadharmānna cācaret 
AbhTb nānyaśāstrasamuddiṣṭaṃ srotasyuktaṃ nije caret  
AbhTa yato yadyapi devena vedādyapi nirūpitam 
AbhTb tathāpi kila saṃkocabhāvābhāvavikalpataḥ  
AbhTa saṃkocatāratamyena pāśavaṃ jñānamīritam 
AbhTb vikāsatāratamyena patijñānaṃ tu bādhakam  
AbhTa idaṃ dvaitamidaṃ neti parasparaniṣedhataḥ 
AbhTb māyīyabhedaklṛptaṃ tatsyādakālpanike katham  
AbhTa uktaṃ bhargaśikhāyāṃ ca mṛtyukālakalādikam 
AbhTb dvaitādvaitavikalpotthaṃ grasate kṛtadhīriti  
AbhTa siddhānte liṅgapūjoktā viśvādhvamayatāvide 
AbhTb kulādiṣu niṣiddhāsau dehe viśvātmatāvide  
AbhTa iha sarvātmake kasmāttadvidhipratiṣedhane 
AbhTb niyamānupraveśena tādātmyapratipattaye  
AbhTa jaṭādi kaule tyāgosya sukhopāyopadeśataḥ 
AbhTb vratacaryā ca mantrārthatādātmyapratipattaye  
AbhTa tanniṣedhastu mantrārthasārvātmyapratipattaye 
AbhTb kṣetrapīṭhopapīṭheṣu praveśo vighnaśāntaye  
AbhTa mantrādyārādhakasyātha tallābhāyopadiśyate 
AbhTb kṣetrādigamanābhāvavidhistu svātmanastathā  
AbhTa vaiśvarūpyeṇa pūrṇatvaṃ jñātumityapi varṇitam 
AbhTb samayācārasadbhāvaḥ pālyatvenopadiśyate  
AbhTa bhedaprāṇatayā tattattyāgāttattvaviśuddhaye 
AbhTb samayādiniṣedhastu mataśāstreṣu kathyate  
AbhTa nirmaryādaṃ svasaṃbodhaṃ saṃpūrṇaṃ buddhyatāmiti 
AbhTb parakīyamidaṃ rūpaṃ dhyeyametattu me nijam  
AbhTa jvālādiliṅgaṃ cānyasya kapālādi tu me nijam 
AbhTb ādiśabdāttapaścaryāvelātithyādi kathyate  
AbhTa nāma śaktiśivādyantametasya mama nānyathā 
AbhTb gotraṃ ca gurusaṃtāno maṭhikākulaśabditaḥ  
AbhTa śrīsaṃtatistryambakākhyā tadardhāmardasaṃjñitā 
AbhTb itthamardhacatasrotra maṭhikāḥ śāṃkare krame  
AbhTa yugakrameṇa kūrmādyā mīnāntā siddhasaṃtatiḥ 
AbhTb ādiśabdena ca gharaṃ pallī pīṭhopapīṭhakam  
AbhTa mudrā chummeti teṣāṃ ca vidhānaṃ svaparasthitam 
AbhTb tādātmyapratipattyai hi svaṃ saṃtānaṃ samāśrayet  
AbhTa bhuñjīta pūjayeccakraṃ parasaṃtāninā nahi 
AbhTb etacca mataśāstreṣu niṣiddhaṃ khaṇḍanā yataḥ  
AbhTa akhaṇḍepi pare tattve bhedenānena jāyate 
AbhTb evaṃ kṣetrapraveśādi saṃtānaniyamāntataḥ  
AbhTa nāsminvidhīyate taddhi sākṣānnaupayikaṃ śive 
AbhTb na tasya ca niṣodho ya nna tattattvasya khaṇḍanam  
AbhTa viśvātmano hi nāthasya svasminrūpe vikalpitau 
AbhTb vidhirniṣedho vā śaktau na svarūpasya khaṇḍane  
AbhTa paratattvapraveśe tu yameva nikaṭaṃ yadā 
AbhTb upāyaṃ vetti sa grāhyastadā tyājyotha vā kvacit  
AbhTa na yantraṇātra kāryeti proktaṃ śrītrikaśāsane 
AbhTb samatā sarvadevānāmovallīmantravarṇayoḥ  
AbhTa āgamanāṃ gatīnāṃ ca sarvaṃ śivamayaṃ yataḥ 
AbhTb sa hyakhaṇḍitasadbhāvaṃ śivatattvaṃ prapaśyati  
AbhTa yo hyakhaṇḍitasadbhāvamātmatattvaṃ prapadyate 
AbhTb ketakīkusumasaurabhe bhṛśaṃ bhṛṅga eva rasiko na makṣikā 
AbhTc bhairavīyaparamādvayārcane kopi rajyati maheśacoditaḥ  
AbhTa asmiṃśca yoge viśrāntiṃ kurvatāṃ bhavaḍambaraḥ 
AbhTb himānīva mahāgrīṣme svayameva vilīyate  
AbhTa alaṃ vātiprasaṅgena bhūyasātiprapañcite 
AbhTb yogyobhinavaguptosminkopi yāgavidhau budhaḥ  
AbhTa ityanuttarapadapravikāse śāktamaupayikamadya viviktam  a
C atha śrītantrāloke pañcamamāhnikam
AbhTb āṇavena vidhinā paradhāma prepsatāmatha nirūpyata etat  b
AbhTa vikalpasyaiva saṃskāre jāte niṣpratiyogini 
AbhTb abhīṣṭe vastuni prāptirniścitā bhogamokṣayoḥ  
AbhTa vikalpaḥ kasyacitsvātmasvātantryādeva susthiraḥ 
AbhTb upāyāntarasāpekṣyaviyogenaiva jāyate  
AbhTa kasyacittu vikalposau svātmasaṃskaraṇaṃ prati 
AbhTb upāyāntarasāpekṣastatroktaḥ pūrvako vidhiḥ  
AbhTa vikalpo nāma cinmātrasvabhāvo yadyapi sthitaḥ 
AbhTb tathāpi niścayātmāsāvaṇoḥ svātantryayojakaḥ  
AbhTa niścayo bahudhā caiṣa tatropāyāśca bhedinaḥ 
AbhTb aṇuśabdena te coktā dūrāntikavibhedataḥ  
AbhTa tatra buddhau tathā prāṇe dehe cāpi pramātari 
AbhTb apāramārthikepyasmin paramārthaḥ prakāśate  
AbhTa yataḥ prakāśāccinmātrāt prāṇādyavyatirekavat 
AbhTb tasyaiva tu svatantratvāddviguṇaṃ jaḍacidvapuḥ  
AbhTa uktaṃ traiśirase caitaddevyai candrārdhamaulinā 
AbhTb jīvaḥ śaktiḥ śivasyaiva sarvatraiva sthitāpi sā  
AbhTa svarūpapratyaye rūḍhā jñānasyonmīlanātparā 
AbhTb tasya cidrūpatāṃ satyāṃ svātantryollāsakalpanāt  
AbhTa paśyañjaḍātmatābhāgaṃ tirodhāyādvayo bhavet 
AbhTb tatra svātantryadṛṣṭyā vā darpaṇe mukhabimbavat  
AbhTa viśuddhaṃ nijacaitanyaṃ niścinotyatadātmakam 
AbhTb buddhiprāṇādito bhinnaṃ caitanyaṃ niścitaṃ balāt  
AbhTa satyatastadabhinnaṃ syāttasyānyonyavibhedataḥ 
AbhTb viśvarūpāvibheditvaṃ śuddhatvādeva jāyate  
AbhTa niṣṭhitaikasphuranmūrtermūrtyantaravirodhataḥ 
AbhTb antaḥ saṃvidi satsarvaṃ yadyapyaparathā dhiyi  
AbhTa prāṇe dehethavā kasmātsaṃkrāmetkena vā katham 
AbhTb tathāpi nirvikalpesminvikalpo nāsti taṃ vinā  
AbhTa dṛṣṭepyadṛṣṭakalpatvaṃ vikalpena tu niścayaḥ 
AbhTb buddhiprāṇaśarīreṣu pārameśvaryamañjasā  
AbhTa vikalpyaṃ śūnyarūpe na pramātari vikalpanam 
AbhTb buddhirdhyānamayī tatra prāṇa uccāraṇātmakaḥ  
AbhTa uccāraṇaṃ ca prāṇādyā vyānāntāḥ pañca vṛttayaḥ 
AbhTb ādyā tu prāṇanābhikhyāparoccārātmikā bhavet  
AbhTa śarīrasyākṣaviṣayaitatpiṇḍatvena saṃsthitiḥ 
AbhTb tatra dhyānamayaṃ tāvadanuttaramihocyate  
AbhTa yaḥ prakāśaḥ svatantroyaṃ citsvabhāvo hṛdi sthitaḥ 
AbhTb sarvatattvamayaḥ proktametacca triśiromate  
AbhTa kadalīsaṃpuṭākāraṃ sabāhyābhyantarāntaram 
AbhTb īkṣate hṛdayāntaḥsthaṃ tatpuṣpamiva tattvavit  
AbhTa somasūryāgnisaṃghaṭṭaṃ tatra dhyāyedananyadhīḥ 
AbhTb taddhyānāraṇisaṃkṣobhānmahābhairavahavyabhuk  
AbhTa hṛdayākhye mahākuṇḍe jājvalan sphītatāṃ vrajet 
AbhTb tasya śaktimataḥ sphītaśakterbhairavatejasaḥ  
AbhTa mātṛmānaprameyākhyaṃ dhāmābhedena bhāvayet 
AbhTb vahnyarkasomaśaktīnāṃ tadeva tritayaṃ bhavet  
AbhTa parā parāparā ceyamaparā ca sadoditā 
AbhTb sṛṣṭisaṃsthitisaṃhāraistāsāṃ pratyekatastridhā  
AbhTa caturthaṃ cānavacchinnaṃ rūpamāsāmakalpitam 
AbhTb evaṃ dvādaśa tā devyaḥ sūryabimbavadāsthitāḥ  
AbhTa ekaikamāsāṃ vahnyarkasomatacchāntibhāsanam 
AbhTb etadānuttaraṃ cakraṃ hṛdayāccakṣurādibhiḥ  
AbhTa vyomabhirniḥsaratyeva tattadviṣayagocare 
AbhTb taccakrabhābhistatrārthe sṛṣṭisthitilayakramāt  
AbhTa somasūryāgnibhāsātma rūpaṃ samavatiṣṭhate 
AbhTb evaṃ śabdādiviṣaye śrotrādivyomavartmanā  
AbhTa cakreṇānena patatā tādātmyaṃ paribhāvayet 
AbhTb anena kramayogena yatra yatra patatyadaḥ  
AbhTa cakraṃ sarvātmakaṃ tattatsārvabhaumamahīśavat 
AbhTb itthaṃ viśvādhvapaṭalamayatnenaiva līyate  
AbhTa bhairavīyamahācakre saṃvittiparivārite 
AbhTb tataḥ saṃskāramātreṇa viśvasyāpi parikṣaye  
AbhTa svātmocchalattayā bhrāmyaccakraṃ saṃcintayenmahat 
AbhTb tatastaddāhyavilayāt tatsaṃskāraparikṣayāt  
AbhTa praśāmyadbhāvayeccakraṃ tataḥ śāntaṃ tataḥ śamam 
AbhTb anena dhyānayogena viśvaṃ cakre vilīyate  
AbhTa tatsaṃvidi tataḥ saṃvidvilīnārthaiva bhāsate 
AbhTb citsvābhāvyāt tato bhūyaḥ sṛṣṭiryaccinmaheśvarī  
AbhTa evaṃ pratikṣaṇaṃ viśvaṃ svasaṃvidi vilāpayan 
AbhTb visṛjaṃśca tato bhūyaḥ śaśvadbhairavatāṃ vrajet  
AbhTa evaṃ triśūlāt prabhṛti catuṣpañcārakakramāt 
AbhTb pañcāśadaraparyantaṃ cakraṃ yogī vibhāvayet  
AbhTa catuṣṣaṣṭiśatāraṃ vā sahasrāramathāpi vā 
AbhTb asaṃkhyārasahasraṃ vā cakraṃ dhyāyedananyadhīḥ  
AbhTa saṃvinnāthasya mahato devasyollāsisaṃvidaḥ 
AbhTb naivāsti kācitkalanā viśvaśaktermaheśituḥ  
AbhTa śaktayosya jagat kṛtsnaṃ śaktimāṃstu maheśvaraḥ 
AbhTb iti māṅgalaśāstre tu śrīśrīkaṇṭho nyarūpayat  
AbhTa ityetat prathamopāyarūpaṃ dhyānaṃ nyarūpayat 
AbhTb śrīśaṃbhunātho me tuṣṭastasmai śrīsumatiprabhuḥ  
AbhTa anayaiva diśānyāni dhyānānyapi samāśrayet 
AbhTb anuttaropāyadhurāṃ yānyāyānti kramaṃ vinā  
AbhTa atha prāṇasya yā vṛttiḥ prāṇanādyā nirūpitā 
AbhTb tadupāyatayā brūmonuttarapravikāsanam  
AbhTa nijānande pramātraṃśamātre hṛdi purā sthitaḥ 
AbhTb śūnyatāmātraviśrānternirānandaṃ vibhāvayet  
AbhTa prāṇodaye prameye tu parānandaṃ vibhāvayet 
AbhTb tatrānantaprameyāṃśapūraṇāpānanirvṛtaḥ  
AbhTa parānandagatastiṣṭhedapānaśaśiśobhitaḥ 
AbhTb tatonantasphuranmeyasaṃghaṭṭaikāntanirvṛtaḥ  
AbhTa samānabhūmimāgatya brahmānandamayo bhavet 
AbhTb tatopi mānameyaughakalanāgrāsatatparaḥ  
AbhTa udānavahnau viśrānto mahānandaṃ vibhāvayat 
AbhTb tatra viśrāntimabhyetya śāmyatyasminmahārciṣi  
AbhTa nirupādhirmahāvyāptirvyānākhyopādhivarjitā 
AbhTb tadā khalu cidānando yo jaḍānupabṛṃhitaḥ  
AbhTa nahyatra saṃsthitiḥ kāpi vibhaktā jaḍarūpiṇaḥ 
AbhTb yatra kopi vyavacchedo nāsti yadviśvataḥ sphurat  
AbhTa yadanāhatasaṃvitti paramāmṛtabṛṃhitam 
AbhTb yatrāsti bhāvanādīnāṃ na mukhyā kāpi saṃgatiḥ  
AbhTa tadeva jagadānandamasmabhyaṃ śaṃbhurūcivān 
AbhTb tatra viśrāntirādheyā hṛdayoccārayogataḥ  
AbhTa yā tatra samyagviśrāntiḥ sānuttaramayī sthitiḥ 
AbhTb ityetaddhṛdayādyekasvabhāvepi svadhāmani  
AbhTa ṣaṭprāṇoccārajaṃ rūpamatha vyāptyā taducyate 
AbhTb prāṇadaṇḍaprayogena pūrvāparasamīkṛteḥ  
AbhTa catuṣkikāmbujālambilambikāsaudhamāśrayet 
AbhTb triśūlabhūmiṃ krāntvāto nāḍitritayasaṅgatām  
AbhTa icchājñānakriyāśaktisamatve praviśet sudhīḥ 
AbhTb ekāṃ vikāsinīṃ bhūyastvasaṃkocāṃ vikasvarām  
AbhTa śrayedbhrūbindunādāntaśaktisopānamālikām 
AbhTb tatrordhvakuṇḍalībhūmau spandanodarasundaraḥ  
AbhTa visargastatra viśrāmyenmatsyodaradaśājuṣi 
AbhTb rāsabhī vaḍavā yadvatsvadhāmānandamandiram  
AbhTa vikāsasaṃkocamayaṃ praviśya hṛdi hṛṣyati 
AbhTb tadvanmuhurlīnasṛṣṭabhāvavrātasunirbharām  
AbhTa śrayedvikāsasaṃkocarūḍhabhairavayāmalām 
AbhTb ekīkṛtamahāmūlaśūlavaisargike hṛdi  
AbhTa parasminneti viśrāntiṃ sarvāpūraṇayogataḥ 
AbhTb atra tatpūrṇavṛttyaiva viśvāveśamayaṃ sthitam  
AbhTa prakāśasyātmaviśrāntāvahamityeva dṛśyatām 
AbhTb anuttaravimarśe prāgvyāpārādivivarjite  
AbhTa cidvimarśaparāhaṃkṛt prathamollāsinī sphuret 
AbhTb tata udyogasaktena sa dvādaśakalātmanā  
AbhTa sūryeṇābhāsayedbhāvaṃ pūrayedatha carcayet 
AbhTb athenduḥ ṣoḍaśakalo visargagrāsamantharaḥ  
AbhTa saṃjīvanyamṛtaṃ bodhavahnau visṛjati sphuran 
AbhTb icchājñānakriyāśaktisūkṣmarandhrasrugagragam  
AbhTa tadevamatadamṛtaṃ divyaṃ saṃviddevīṣu tarpakam 
AbhTb visargāmṛtametāvad bodhākhye hutabhojini  
AbhTa visṛṣṭaṃ cedbhavetsarvaṃ hutaṃ ṣoḍhādhvamaṇḍalam 
AbhTb yatonuttaranāthasya visargaḥ kulanāyikā 
AbhTc tatkṣobhaḥ kādihāntaṃ tatprasarastattvapaddhatiḥ  
AbhTa aṃa iti kuleśvaryā sahito hi kuleśitā 
AbhTb paro visargaviśleṣastanmayaṃ viśvamucyate  
AbhTa vitprāṇaguṇadehāntarbahirdravyamayīmimām 
AbhTb arcayejjuhuyāddhyāyeditthaṃ saṃjīvanīṃ kalām  
AbhTa ānandanāḍīyugalaspandanāvahitau sthitaḥ 
AbhTb enāṃ visarganiḥṣyandasaudhabhūmiṃ prapadyate  
AbhTa śākte kṣobhe kulāveśe sarvanāḍyagragocare 
AbhTb vyāptau sarvātmasaṃkoce hṛdayaṃ praviśetsudhīḥ  
AbhTa somasūryakalājālaparasparanigharṣataḥ 
AbhTb agnīṣomātmake dhāmni visargānanda unmiṣet  
AbhTa alaṃ rahasyakathayā guptametatsvabhāvataḥ 
AbhTb yoginīhṛdayaṃ tatra viśrāntaḥ syātkṛtī budhaḥ  
AbhTa hānādānatiraskāravṛttau rūḍhimupāgataḥ 
AbhTb abhedavṛttitaḥ paśyedviśvaṃ citicamatkṛteḥ  
AbhTa arthakriyārthitādainyaṃ tyaktvā bāhyāntarātmani 
AbhTb kharūpe nirvṛtiṃ prāpya phullāṃ nādadaśāṃ śrayet  
AbhTa vaktramantastayā samyak saṃvidaḥ pravikāsayet 
AbhTb saṃvidakṣamaruccakraṃ jñeyābhinnaṃ tato bhavet  
AbhTa tajjñeyaṃ saṃvidākhyena vahninā pravilīyate 
AbhTb vilīnaṃ tat trikoṇesmiñśaktivahnau vilīyate  
AbhTa tatra saṃvedanodārabindusattāsunirvṛtaḥ 
AbhTb saṃhārabījaviśrānto yogī paramayo bhavet  
AbhTa antarbāhye dvaye vāpi sāmānyetarasundaraḥ 
AbhTb saṃvitspandastriśaktyātmā saṃkocapravikāsavān  
AbhTa asaṃkocavikāsopi tadābhāsanatastathā 
AbhTb antarlakṣyo bahirdṛṣṭiḥ paramaṃ padamaśnute  
AbhTa tataḥ svātantryanirmeye vicitrārthakriyākṛti 
AbhTb vimarśanaṃ viśeṣākhyaḥ spanda aunmukhyasaṃjñitaḥ  
AbhTa tatra viśrāntimāgacchedyadvīryaṃ mantramaṇḍale 
AbhTb śāntyādisiddhayastattadrūpatādātmyato yataḥ  
AbhTa divyo yaścākṣasaṃghoyaṃ bodhasvātantryasaṃjñakaḥ 
AbhTb sonimīlita evaitat kuryātsvātmamayaṃ jagat  
AbhTa mahāsāhasasaṃyogavilīnākhilavṛttikaḥ 
AbhTb puñjībhūte svaraśmyoghe nirbharībhūya tiṣṭhati  
AbhTa akiciccintakastatra spaṣṭadṛgyāti saṃvidam 
AbhTb yadvisphuliṅgāḥ saṃsārabhasmadāhaikahetavaḥ  
AbhTa taduktaṃ parameśena triśirobhairavāgame 
AbhTb śṛṇu devi pravakṣyāmi mantrabhūmyāṃ praveśanam  
AbhTa madhyanāḍyordhvagamanaṃ taddharmaprāptilakṣaṇam 
AbhTb visargāntapadātītaṃ prāntakoṭinirūpitam  
AbhTa adhaḥpravāhasaṃrodhādūrdhvakṣepavivarjanāt 
AbhTb mahāprakāśamudayajñānavyaktipradāyakam  
AbhTa anubhūya pare dhāmni mātrāvṛttyā puraṃ viśet 
AbhTb nistaraṅgāvatīrṇā sā vṛttirekā śivātmikā  
AbhTa catuṣṣaḍdvirdviguṇitacakraṣaṭkasamujjvalā 
AbhTb tatsthaṃ tstho vicārayet khaṃ khaṃ khasthaṃ khasthena saṃviśet  
AbhTa khaṃ khaṃ tyaktvā khamāruhya khasthaṃ khaṃ coccarediti 
AbhTb khamadhyāsyādhikāreṇa padasthāścinmarīcayaḥ  
AbhTa bhāvayedbhāvamantaḥsthaṃ bhāvastho bhāvaniḥspṛhaḥ 
AbhTb bhāvābhāvagatī ruddhvā bhāvābhāvāvarodhadṛk  
AbhTa ātmāṇukulamūlāni śaktirbhūtiścitī ratiḥ 
AbhTb śaktitrayaṃ draṣṭṛdṛśyoparaktaṃ tadvivarjitam  
AbhTa etatkhaṃ daśadhā proktamuccāroccāralakṣaṇam 
AbhTb dhāmasthaṃ dhāmamadhyasthaṃ dhāmodarapuṭīkṛtam  
AbhTa dhāmnā tu bodhayeddhāma dhāma dhāmāntagaṃ kuru 
AbhTb taddhāma dhāmagatyā tu bhedyaṃ dhāmāntamāntaram  
AbhTa bhedopabhedabhedena bhedaḥ kāryastu madhyataḥ 
AbhTb iti praveśopāyoyamāṇavaḥ parikīrtitaḥ  
AbhTa śrīmaheśvaranāthena yo hṛtsthena mamoditaḥ 
AbhTb śrībrahmayāmale coktaṃ śrīmān rāvo daśātmakaḥ  
AbhTa sthūlaḥ sūkṣmaḥ paro hṛdyaḥ kaṇṭhyastālavya eva ca 
AbhTb sarvataśca vibhuryosau vibhutvapadadāyakaḥ  
AbhTa jitarāvo mahāyogī saṃkrāmetparadehagaḥ 
AbhTb parāṃ ca vindati vyāptiṃ pratyahaṃ hyabhyaseta tam  
AbhTa tāvadyāvadarāve sā rāvāllīyeta rāviṇī 
AbhTb atra bhāvanayā dehagatopāyaiḥ pare pathi  
AbhTa vivikṣoḥ pūrṇatāsparśātprāgānandaḥ prajāyate 
AbhTb tatopi vidyudāpātasadṛśe dehavarjite  
AbhTa dhāmni kṣaṇaṃ samāveśādudbhavaḥ prasphuṭaṃ plutiḥ 
AbhTb jalapāṃsuvadabhyastasaṃviddehaikyahānitaḥ  
AbhTa svabalākramaṇāddehaśaithilyāt kampamāpnuyāt 
AbhTb galite dehatādātmyaniścayentarbhukhatvataḥ  
AbhTa nidrāyate purā yāvanna rūḍhaḥ saṃvidātmani 
AbhTb tataḥ satyapade rūḍho viśvātmatvena saṃvidam  
AbhTa saṃvidan ghūrṇate ghūrṇirmahāvyāptiryataḥ smṛtā 
AbhTb ātmanyanātmābhimatau satyāmeva hyanātmani  
AbhTa ātmābhimāno dehādau bandho muktistu tallayaḥ 
AbhTb ādāvanātmanyātmatve līne labdhe nijātmani  
AbhTa ātmanyanātmatānāśe mahāvyāptiḥ pravartate 
AbhTb ānanda udbhavaḥ kampo nindrā ghūrṇiśca pañcakam  
AbhTa ityuktamata eva śrīmālinīvijayottare 
AbhTb pradarśitesminnānandaprabhṛtau pañcake yadā  
AbhTa yogī viśettadā tattaccakreśatvaṃ haṭhādvrajet 
AbhTb yathā sarveśinā bodhenākrāntāpi tanuḥ kvacit  
AbhTa kiṃcitkartuṃ prabhavati cakṣuṣā rūpasaṃvidam 
AbhTb tathaiva cakre kutrāpi praveśātkopi saṃbhavet  
AbhTa ānandacakraṃ vahnyaśri kanda udbhava ucyate 
AbhTb kampo hṛttālu nidrā ca ghūrṇiḥ syādūrdhvakuṇḍalī  
AbhTa etacca sphuṭamevoktaṃ śrīmantraiśirase mate 
AbhTb evaṃ pradarśitoccāraviśrāntihṛdayaṃ param  
AbhTa yattadavyaktaliṅgaṃ nṛśivaśaktyavibhāgavat 
AbhTb atra viśvamidaṃ līnamatrāntaḥsthaṃ ca gamyate  
AbhTa idaṃ tallakṣaṇaṃ pūrṇaśaktibhairavasaṃvidaḥ 
AbhTb dehagādhvasamunmeṣe samāveśastu yaḥ sphuṭaḥ  
AbhTa ahantācchāditonmeṣibhāvedaṃbhāvayuk sa ca 
AbhTb vyaktāvyaktamidaṃ liṅgaṃ mantravīryaṃ parāparam  
AbhTa naraśaktisamunmeṣi śivarūpādvibheditam 
AbhTb yannyakkṛtaśivāhantāsamāveśaṃ vibhedavat  
AbhTa viśeṣaspandarūpaṃ tad vyaktaṃ liṅgaṃ cidātmakam 
AbhTb vyaktātsiddhiprasavo vyaktāvyaktāddvayaṃ vimokṣaśca 
AbhTc avyaktādbalamādyaṃ parasya nānuttare tviyaṃ carcā  
AbhTa ātmākhyaṃ yadvyaktaṃ naraliṅgaṃ tatra viśvamarpayataḥ 
AbhTb vyaktāvyaktaṃ tasmādgalite tasmiṃstadavyaktam  
AbhTa tenātmaliṅgametat parame śivaśaktyaṇusvabhāvamaye 
AbhTb avyakte viśrāmyati nānuttaradhāmagā tviyaṃ carcā  
AbhTa ekasya spandanasyaiṣā traidhaṃ bhedavyavasthitiḥ 
AbhTb atra liṅge sadā tiṣṭhet pūjāviśrāntitatparaḥ  
AbhTa yoginīhṛdayaṃ liṅgamidamānandasundaram 
AbhTb bījayonisamāpattyā sūte kāmapi saṃvidam  
AbhTa atra prayāsavirahātsarvosau devatāgaṇaḥ 
AbhTb ānandapūrṇe dhāmnyāste nityoditacidātmakaḥ  
AbhTa atra bhairavanāthasya sasaṃkocavikāsikā 
AbhTb bhāsate durghaṭā śaktirasaṃkocavikāsinaḥ  
AbhTa etalliṅgasamāpattivisargānandadhārayā 
AbhTb siktaṃ tadeva sadviśvaṃ śaśvannavanavāyate  
AbhTa anuttarebhyupāyotra tādrūpyādeva varṇitaḥ 
AbhTb jvaliteṣvapi dīpeṣu gharmāṃśuḥ kiṃ na bhāsate  
AbhTa artheṣu tadbhogavidhau tadutthe duḥkhe sukhe vā galitābhiśaṅkam 
AbhTb anāviśantopi nimagnacittā jānanti vṛttikṣayasaukhyamantaḥ  
AbhTa satyevātmani citsvabhāvamahasi svānte tathopaktiyāṃ tasmai kurvati tatpracāravivaśe satyakṣavargepi ca 
AbhTb satsvartheṣu sukhādiṣu sphuṭataraṃ yadbhedavandhyodayaṃ yogī tiṣṭhati pūrṇaraśmivibhavastattattvamācīyatām  
AbhTa ityuccāravidhiḥ proktaḥ karaṇaṃ pravivicyate 
AbhTb taccetthaṃ triśiraḥśāstre parameśena bhāṣitam  
AbhTa grāhyagrāhakacidvyāptityāgākṣepaniveśanaiḥ 
AbhTb karaṇaṃ saptadhā prāhurabhyāsaṃ bodhapūrvakam  
AbhTa tadvyāptipūrvamākṣepe karaṇaṃ svapratiṣṭhatā 
AbhTb guruvaktrācca boddhavyaṃ karaṇaṃ yadyapi sphuṭam  
AbhTa tathāpyāgamarakṣārthaṃ tadagre varṇayiṣyate 
AbhTb ukto ya eṣa uccārastatra yosau sphuran sthitaḥ  
AbhTa avyaktānukṛtiprāyo dhvanirvarṇaḥ sa kathyate 
AbhTb sṛṣṭisaṃhārabījaṃ ca tasya mukhyaṃ vapurviduḥ  
AbhTa tadabhyāsavaśādyāti kramādyogī cidātmatām 
AbhTb tathā hyanacke sācke vā kādau sānte punaḥpunaḥ  
AbhTa smṛte proccārite vāpi sā sā saṃvitprasūyāte 
AbhTb bāhyārthasamayāpekṣā ghaṭādyā dhvanayopi ye  
AbhTa tepyarthabhāvanāṃ kuryurmanorājyavadātmani 
AbhTb taduktaṃ parameśena bhairavo vyāpakokhile  
AbhTa iti bhairavaśabdasya saṃtatoccāraṇācchivaḥ 
AbhTb śrīmattraiśirasepyuktaṃ mantroddhārasya pūrvataḥ  
AbhTa smṛtiśca smaraṇaṃ pūrvaṃ sarvabhāveṣu vastutaḥ 
AbhTb mantrasvarūpaṃ tadbhāvyasvarūpāpattiyojakam  
AbhTa smṛtiḥ svarūpajanikā sarvabhāveṣu rañjikā 
AbhTb anekākārarūpeṇa sarvatrāvasthitena tu  
AbhTa svasvabhāvasya saṃprāptiḥ saṃvittiḥ paramārthataḥ 
AbhTb vyaktiniṣṭhā tato viddhi sattā sā kīrtitā parā  
AbhTa kiṃ punaḥ samayāpekṣāṃ vinā ye bījapiṇḍakāḥ 
AbhTb saṃvidaṃ spandapantyete neyuḥ saṃvidupāyatām  
AbhTa vācyābhāvādudāsīnasaṃvitspandātsvadhāmataḥ 
AbhTb prāṇollāsanirodhābhyāṃ bījapiṇḍeṣu pūrṇatā  
AbhTa sukhasītkārasatsamyaksāmyaprathamasaṃvidaḥ 
AbhTb saṃvedanaṃ hi prathamaṃ sparśonuttarasaṃvidaḥ  
AbhTa hṛtkaṇṭhyoṣṭhyatridhāmāntarnitarāṃ pravikāsini 
AbhTb caturdaśaḥ praveśo ya ekīkṛtatadātmakaḥ  
AbhTa tato visargoccārāṃśe dvādaśāntapathāvubhau 
AbhTb hṛdayena sahaikadhyaṃ nayate japatatparaḥ  
AbhTa kandahṛtkaṇṭhatālvagrakauṇḍilīprakriyāntataḥ 
AbhTb ānandamadhyanāḍyantaḥ spandanaṃ bījamāvahet  
AbhTa saṃhārabījaṃ khaṃ hṛtsthamoṣṭhyaṃ phullaṃ svamūrdhani 
AbhTb tejastryaśraṃ tālukaṇṭhe bindurūrdhvapade sthitaḥ  
AbhTa ityenayā budho yuktyā varṇajapyaparāyaṇaḥ 
AbhTb anuttaraṃ paraṃ dhāma praviśedacirāt sudhīḥ  
AbhTa varṇaśabdena nīlādi yadvā dīkṣottare yathā 
AbhTb saṃhāranragnimaruto rudrabinduyutānsmaret  
AbhTa hṛdaye tanmayo lakṣyaṃ paśyetsaptadinādatha 
AbhTb visphuliṅgāgnivannīlapītaraktādicitritam  
AbhTa jājvalīti hṛdambhoje bījadīpaprabodhitam 
AbhTb dīpavajjvalito bindurbhāsate vighanārkavat  
AbhTa svayaṃbhāsātmanānena tādātmyaṃ yātyananyadhīḥ 
AbhTb śivena hematāṃ yadvattāmraṃ sūtena vedhitam  
AbhTa upalakṣaṇametacca sarvamantreṣu lakṣayet 
AbhTb yadyatsaṃkalpasaṃbhūtaṃ varṇajālaṃ hi bhautikam  
AbhTa tat saṃvidādhikyavaśādabhautikamiva sthitam 
AbhTb atastathāvidhe rūpe rūḍho rohati saṃvidi  
AbhTa anācchāditarūpāyāmanupādhau prasannadhīḥ 
AbhTb nīle pīte sukhe duḥkhe saṃvidrūpamakhaṇḍitam  
AbhTa gurubhirbhāṣitaṃ tasmādupāyeṣu vicitratā 
AbhTb uccārakaraṇadhyānavarṇairebhiḥ pradarśitaḥ  
AbhTa anuttarapadaprāptāvabhyupāyavidhikramaḥ 
AbhTb akiṃciccintanaṃ vīryaṃ bhāvanāyāṃ ca sā punaḥ  
AbhTa dhyāne tadapi coccāre karaṇe sopi taddhvanau 
AbhTb sa sthānakalpane bāhyamiti kramamupāśrayet  
AbhTa laṅghanena paro yogī mandabuddhiḥ krameṇa tu 
AbhTb vīryaṃ vinā yathā ṣaṇṭhastasyāpyastyatha vā balam 
AbhTc mṛtadeha iveyaṃ syādbāhyāntaḥparikalpanā  
AbhTa ityāṇavenuttaratābhyupāyaḥ prokto nayaḥ spaṣṭapathena bāhyaḥ  a
C atha śrītantrāloke
AbhTb sthānaprakalpākhyatayā sphuṭastu bāhyobhyupāyaḥ pravivicyatetha  b
AbhTa sthānabhedastridhā proktaḥ prāṇe dehe bahistathā 
AbhTb prāṇaśca pañcadhā dehe dvidhā bāhyāntaratvataḥ  
AbhTa maṇḍalaṃ sthaṇḍilaṃ pātramakṣasūtraṃ sapustakam 
AbhTb liṅgaṃ tūraṃ paṭaḥ pustaṃ pratimā mūrtireva ca  
AbhTa ityekādaśadhā bāhyaṃ punastadbahudhā bhavet 
AbhTb tatra prāṇāśrayaṃ tāvadvidhānamupadiśyate  
AbhTa adhvā samasta evāyaṃ ṣaḍvidhopyativistṛtaḥ 
AbhTb yo vakṣyate sa ekatra prāṇe tāvatpratiṣṭhitaḥ  
AbhTa adhvanaḥ kalanaṃ yattatkramākramatayā sthitam 
AbhTb kramākramau hi citraikakalanā bhāvagocare  
AbhTa kramākramātmā kālaśca paraḥ saṃvidi vartate 
AbhTb kālī nāma parā śaktiḥ saiva devasya gīyate  
AbhTa saiva saṃvidbahiḥ svātmagarbhībhūtau kramākramau 
AbhTb sphuṭayantī prarohaṇa prāṇavṛttiriti sthitā  
AbhTa saṃvinmātraṃ hi yacchuddhaṃ prakāśaparamārthakam 
AbhTb tanmeyamātmanaḥ projjhya viviktaṃ bhāsate nabhaḥ  
AbhTa tadeva śūnyarūpatvaṃ saṃvidaḥ parigīyate 
AbhTb neti neti vimarśena yogināṃ sā parā daśā  
AbhTa sa eva khātmā meyesminbhedite svīkriyonmukhaḥ 
AbhTb patansamucchalattvena prāṇaspandormisaṃjñitaḥ  
AbhTa tenāhuḥ kila saṃvitprākprāṇe pariṇatā tathā 
AbhTb antaḥkaraṇatattvasya vāyurāśrayatāṃ gataḥ  
AbhTa iyaṃ sā prāṇanāśaktirāntarodyogadohadā 
AbhTb spandaḥ sphurattā viśrāntirjīvo hṛtpratibhā matā  
AbhTa sā prāṇavṛttiḥ prāṇādyai rūpaiḥ pañcabhirātmasāt 
AbhTb dehaṃ yatkurute saṃvitpūrṇastenaiṣa bhāsate  
AbhTa prāṇanāvṛttitādātmyasaṃvitkhacitadehajām 
AbhTb ceṣṭāṃ paśyantyato mugdhā nāstyanyaditi manvate  
AbhTa tāmeva bālamūrkhastrīprāyaveditṛsaṃśritām 
AbhTb matiṃ pramāṇīkurvantaścārvākāstattvadarśinaḥ  
AbhTa teṣāṃ tathā bhāvanā caddārḍhyameti nirantaram 
AbhTb taddehabhaṅge suptāḥ syurātādṛgvāsanākṣayāt  
AbhTa tadvāsanākṣaye tveṣāmakṣīṇaṃ vāsanāntaram 
AbhTb buddhaṃ kutaścitsaṃsūte vicitrāṃ phalasampadam  
AbhTa adārḍhyaśaṅkanātprācyavāsanātādavasthyataḥ 
AbhTb anyakartavyaśaithilyātsaṃbhāvyānuśayatvataḥ  
AbhTa atadrūḍhānyajanatākartavyaparilopanāt 
AbhTb nāstikyavāsanāmāhuḥ pāpātpāpīyasīmimām  
AbhTa alamaprastutenātha prakṛtaṃ pravivicyate 
AbhTb yāvānsamasta evāyamadhvā prāṇe pratiṣṭhitaḥ  
AbhTa dvidhā ca sodhvā kriyayā mūrtyā ca pravibhajyate 
AbhTb prāṇa eva śikhā śrīmattriśirasyuditā hi sā  
AbhTa baddhā yāgādikāle tuṃ niṣkalatvācchivātmikā 
AbhTb yatohorātramadhyesyāścaturviṃśatidhā gatiḥ  
AbhTa prāṇavikṣeparandhrākhyaśataiścitraphalapradā 
AbhTb kṣapā śaśī tathāpāno nāda ekatra tiṣṭhati  
AbhTa jīvādityo na codgacchettuṭyardhaṃ sāndhyamīdṛśam 
AbhTb ūrdhvavaktro raviścandrodhomukho vahnirantare  
AbhTa mādhyāhnikī mokṣadā syādvyomamadhyasthito raviḥ 
AbhTb anastamitasāro hi jantucakraprabodhakaḥ  
AbhTa binduḥ prāṇo hyahaścaiva ravirekatra tiṣṭhati 
AbhTb mahāsandhyā tṛtīyā tu supraśāntātmikā sthitā  
AbhTa evaṃ baddhā śikhā yatra tattatphalaniyojikā 
AbhTb ataḥ saṃvidi sarvoyamadhvā viśramya tiṣṭhati  
AbhTa amūrtāyāḥ sarvagatvānniṣkriyāyāśca saṃvidaḥ 
AbhTb mūrtikriyābhāsanaṃ yatsa evādhvā maheśituḥ  
AbhTa adhvā krameṇa yātavye pade saṃprāptikāraṇam 
AbhTb dvaitināṃ bhogyabhāvāttu prabuddhānāṃ yatodyate  
AbhTa iha sarvatra śabdānāmanvarthaṃ carcayedyataḥ 
AbhTb uktaṃ śrīmanniśācāre saṃjñātra trividhā matā  
AbhTa naimittikī prasiddhā ca tathānyā pāribhāṣikī 
AbhTb pūrvatve vā pradhānaṃ syāttatrāntarbhāvayettataḥ  
AbhTa atodhvaśabdasyokteyaṃ niruktirnoditāpi cet 
AbhTb kvacitsvabuddhyā sāpyūhyā kiyallekhyaṃ hi pustake  
AbhTa tatra kriyābhāsanaṃ yatsodhvā kālāhva ucyate 
AbhTb varṇamantrapadābhikhyamatrāstedhvatrayaṃ sphuṭam  
AbhTa yastu mūrtyavabhāsāṃśaḥ sa deśādhvā nigadyate 
AbhTb kalātattvapurābhikhyamantarbhūtamiha trayam  
AbhTa trikadvayetra pratyekaṃ sthūlaṃ sūkṣmaṃ paraṃ vapuḥ 
AbhTb yatosti tena sarvoyamadhvā ṣaḍvidha ucyate  
AbhTa ṣaḍvidhādadhvanaḥ prācyaṃ yadetattritayaṃ punaḥ 
AbhTb eṣa eva sa kālādhvā prāṇe spaṣṭaṃ pratiṣṭhitaḥ  
AbhTa tattavamadhyasthitātkālādanyoyaṃ kāla ucyate 
AbhTb eṣa kālo hi devasya viśvābhāsanakāriṇī  
AbhTa kriyāśaktiḥ samastānāṃ tattvānāṃ ca paraṃ vapuḥ 
AbhTb etadīśvaratattvaṃ tacchivasya vapurucyate  
AbhTa udriktābhogakāryātmaviśvaikātmyamidaṃ yataḥ 
AbhTb etadīśvararūpatvaṃ paramātmani yatkila  
AbhTa tatpramātari māyīye kālatattvaṃ nigadyate 
AbhTb śivādiśuddhavidyāntaṃ yacchivasya svakaṃ vapuḥ  
AbhTa tadeva puṃso māyādirāgāntaṃ kañcukībhavet 
AbhTb anāśritaṃ yato māyā kalāvidye sadāśivaḥ  
AbhTa īśvaraḥ kālaniyatī sadvidyā rāga ucyate 
AbhTb anāśritaḥ śūnyamātā buddhimātā sadāśivaḥ  
AbhTa īśvaraḥ prāṇamātā ca vidyā dehapramātṛtā 
AbhTb anāśrayo hi śūnyatvaṃ jñānameva hi buddhitā  
AbhTa viśvātmatā ca prāṇatvaṃ dehe vedyaikatānatā 
AbhTb tena prāṇapathe viśvākalaneyaṃ virājate  
AbhTa yena rūpeṇa tadvacmaḥ sadbhistadavadhīyatām 
AbhTb dvādaśāntāvadhāvasmindehe yadyapi sarvataḥ  
AbhTa otaprotātmakaḥ prāṇastathāpītthaṃ na susphuṭaḥ 
AbhTb yatno jīvanamātrātmā tatparaśca dvidhā mataḥ  
AbhTa saṃvedyaścāpyasaṃvedyo dvidhetthaṃ bhidyate punaḥ 
AbhTb sphuṭāsphuṭatvāddvaividhyaṃ pratyekaṃ paribhāvayet  
AbhTa saṃvedyajīvanābhikhyaprayatnaspandasundaraḥ 
AbhTb prāṇaḥ kandātprabhṛtyeva tathāpyatra na susphuṭaḥ  
AbhTa kandādhārātprabhṛtyeva vyavasthā tena kathyate 
AbhTb svacchandaśāstre nāḍīnāṃ vāyvādhāratayā sphuṭam  
AbhTa tatrāpi tu prayatnosau na saṃvedyatayā sthitaḥ 
AbhTb vedyayatnāttu hṛdayātprāṇacāro vibhajyate  
AbhTa prabhoḥ śivasya yā śaktirvāmā jyeṣṭhā ca raudrikā 
AbhTb satadanyatamāvātmaprāṇau yatnavidhāyinau  
AbhTa prabhuśaktiḥ kvacinmukhyā yathāṅgamarudīraṇe 
AbhTb ātmaśaktiḥ kvacitkandasaṃkocaspandane yathā  
AbhTa prāṇaśaktiḥ kvacitprāṇacāre hārde yathā sphuṭam 
AbhTb trayaṃ dvayaṃ vā mukhyaṃ syādyogināmavadhāninām  
AbhTa avadhānādadṛṣṭāṃśādbalavattvādatheraṇāt 
AbhTb viparyayopi prāṇātmaśaktīnāṃ mukhyatāṃ prati  
AbhTa vāmā saṃsāriṇāmīśā prabhuśaktirvidhāyinī 
AbhTb jyeṣṭhā tu suprabuddhānāṃ bubhutsūnāṃ ca raudrikā  
AbhTa vāmā saṃsāravamanā jyeṣṭhā śivamayī yataḥ 
AbhTb drāvayitrī rujāṃ raudrī roddhrī cākhilakarmaṇām  
AbhTa sṛṣṭyāditattvamajñātvā na mukto nāpi mocayet 
AbhTb uktaṃ ca śrīyogacāre mokṣaḥ sarvaprakāśanāt  
AbhTa utpattisthitisaṃhārān ye na jānanti yoginaḥ 
AbhTb na muktāste tadajñānabandhanaikādhivāsitāḥ  
AbhTa sṛṣṭyādayaśca te sarve kālādhīnā na saṃśayaḥ 
AbhTb sa ca prāṇātmakastasmāduccāraḥ kathyate sphuṭaḥ  
AbhTa hṛdayātprāṇacāraśca nāsikyadvādaśāntataḥ 
AbhTb ṣaṭtriṃśadaṅgulo jantoḥ sarvasya svāṅgulakramāt  
AbhTa kṣodiṣṭhe vā mahiṣṭhe vā dehe tādṛśa eva hi 
AbhTb vīryamojo balaṃ spandaḥ prāṇacāraḥ samaṃ tataḥ  
AbhTa ṣaṭtriṃśadaṅgule cāre yadgamāgamayugmakam 
AbhTb nālikātithimāsābdatatsaṅghrotra sphuṭaṃ sthitaḥ  
AbhTa tuṭiḥ sapādāṅgulayukprāṇastāḥ ṣoḍaśocchvasan 
AbhTb niḥśvasaṃścātra caṣakaḥ sapañcāṃśeṅguleṅgule  
AbhTa śvāsapraśvāsayornālī proktāhorātra ucyate 
AbhTb navāṅgulāmbudhituṭau praharāstebdhayo dinam  
AbhTa nirgamentarniśenendū tayoḥ saṃdhye tuṭerdale 
AbhTb ketuḥ sūrye vidhau rāhurbhaumādervārabhāginaḥ  
AbhTa praharadvayamanyeṣāṃ grahāṇāmudayontarā 
AbhTb siddhirdavīyasī mokṣobhicāraḥ pāralaukikī  
AbhTa aihikī dūranaikaṭyātiśayā praharāṣṭake 
AbhTb madhyāhnamadhyaniśayorabhijinmokṣabhogadā  
AbhTa nakṣatrāṇāṃ tadanyeṣāmudayo madhyataḥ kramāt 
AbhTb nāgā lokeśamūrtīśā gaṇeśā jalatattvataḥ  
AbhTa pradhānāntaṃ nāyakāśca vidyātattvādhināyakāḥ 
AbhTb sakalādyāśca kaṇṭhyoṣṭhyaparyantā bhairavāstathā  
AbhTa śaktayaḥ pārameśvaryo vāmaśā vīranāyakāḥ 
AbhTb aṣṭāvaṣṭau ye ya itthaṃ vyāpyavyāpakatājuṣaḥ  
AbhTa sthūlasūkṣmāḥ kramātteṣāmudayaḥ praharāṣṭake 
AbhTb dine krūrāṇi saumyāni rātrau karmāṇyasaṃśayam  
AbhTa krūratā saumyatā vābhisandherapi nirūpitā 
AbhTb dinarātrikṣaye muktiḥ sā vyāptidhyānayogataḥ  
AbhTa te coktāḥ parameśena śrīmadvīrāvalīkule 
AbhTb sitāsitau dīrghahrasvau dharmādharmau dinakṣape  
AbhTa kṣīyete yadi taddīkṣā vyāptyā dhyānena yogataḥ 
AbhTb ahorātraḥ prāṇacāre kathito māsa ucyate  
AbhTa dinaṃ kṛṣṇo niśā śuklaḥ pakṣau karmasu pūrvavat 
AbhTb yāḥ ṣoḍaśoktāstithayastāsu ye pūrvapaścime  
AbhTa tayostu viśramordherdhe tithyaḥ pañcadaśetarāḥ 
AbhTb sapāde dvyaṅgule tithyā ahorātro vibhajyate  
AbhTa prakāśaviśramavaśāttāveva hi dinakṣape 
AbhTb saṃvitpratikṣaṇaṃ yasmātprakāśānandayoginī  
AbhTa tau klṛptau yāvati tayā tāvatyeva dinakṣape 
AbhTb yāvatyeva hi saṃvittiruditoditasusphuṭā  
AbhTa tāvāneva kṣaṇaḥ kalpo nimeṣo vā tadastvapi 
AbhTb yāvānevodayo vittervedyaikagrahatatparaḥ  
AbhTa tāvadevāstamayanaṃ veditṛsvātmacarvaṇam 
AbhTb vedye ca bahirantarvā dvaye vātha dvayojjhite  
AbhTa sarvathā tanmayībhūtirdinaṃ vettṛsthatā niśā 
AbhTb veditā vedyaviśrānto vettā tvantarmukhasthitiḥ  
AbhTa purā vicārayanpaścātsattāmātrasvarūpakaḥ 
AbhTb jāgradveditṛtā svapno vettṛbhāvaḥ purātanaḥ  
AbhTa paraḥ suptaṃ kṣaye rātridinayosturyamadvayam 
AbhTb kadācidvastuviśrāntisāmyenātmani carvaṇam  
AbhTa vedyavedakasāmyaṃ tat sā rātridinatulyatā 
AbhTb vedye viśrāntiradhikā dinadairghyāya tatra tu  
AbhTa nyūnā syātsvātmaviśrāntirviparīte viparyayaḥ 
AbhTb svātmautsukye prabuddhe hi vedyaviśrāntiralpikā  
AbhTa itthameva divārātrinyūnādhikyakramaṃ vadet 
AbhTb yathā deheṣvahorātranyūnādhikyādi no samam  
AbhTa tathā pureṣvapītyevaṃ tadviśeṣeṇa noditam 
AbhTb śrītraiyambakasantānavitatāmbarabhāskaraḥ  
AbhTa dinarātrikramaṃ me śrīśaṃbhuritthamapaprathat 
AbhTb śrīsantānagurustvāha sthānaṃ buddhāprabuddhayoḥ  
AbhTa hṛda ārabhya yattena rātrindivavibhājanam 
AbhTb tadasatsitapakṣentaḥ praveśollāsabhāgini  
AbhTa abuddhasthānamevaitaddinatvena kathaṃ bhavet 
AbhTb alaṃ vānena nedaṃ vā mama prāṅmatamatsaraḥ  
AbhTa heye tu darśite śiṣyāḥ satpathaikāntadarśinaḥ 
AbhTb vyākhyātaḥ kṛṣṇapakṣo ya statra prāṇagataḥ śaśī  
AbhTa āpyāyanātmanaikaikāṃ kalāṃ pratitithi tyajet 
AbhTb dvādaśāntasamīpe tu yāsau pañcadaśī tuṭiḥ  
AbhTa sāmāvasyātra sa kṣīṇaścandraḥ prāṇārkamāviśet 
AbhTb uktaṃ śrīkāmikāyāṃ ca nordhvedhaḥ prakṛtiḥ parā 
AbhTc ardhārdhe kramate māyā dvikhaṇḍā śivarūpiṇī  
AbhTa candrasūryātmanā dehaṃ pūrayetpravilāpayet 
AbhTb amṛtaṃ candrarūpeṇa dvidhā ṣoḍaśadhā punaḥ  
AbhTa pivanti ca surāḥ sarve daśapañca parāḥ kalāḥ 
AbhTb amā śeṣaguhāntaḥsthāmāvāsyā viśvatarpiṇī  
AbhTa evaṃ kalāḥ pañcadaśa kṣīyante śaśinaḥ kramāt 
AbhTb āpyāyinyamṛtābrūpatādātmyātṣoḍaśī na tu  
AbhTa tatra pañcadaśī yāsau tuṭiḥ prakṣīṇacandramāḥ 
AbhTb tadūrdhvagaṃ yattuṭyardhaṃ pakṣasaṃdhiḥ sa kīrtitaḥ  
AbhTa tasmādviśramatuṭyardhādāmāvasyaṃ purādalam 
AbhTb paraṃ prātipadaṃ cārdhamiti saṃdhiḥ sa kalpyate  
AbhTa tatra prātipade tasmiṃstuṭyardhārdhe purādalam 
AbhTb āmāvasyaṃ tithicchedātkuryātsūryagrahaṃ viśat  
AbhTa tatrārkamaṇḍale līnaḥ śaśī sravati yanmadhu 
AbhTb taptatvāttatpibedindusahabhūḥ siṃhikāsutaḥ  
AbhTa arkaḥ pramāṇaṃ somastu meyaṃ jñānakriyātmakau 
AbhTb rāhurmāyāpramātā syāttadācchādanakovidaḥ  
AbhTa tata eva tamorūpo vilāpayitumakṣamaḥ 
AbhTb tatsaṃghaṭṭādvayollāso mukhyo mātā vilāpakaḥ  
AbhTa arkendurāhusaṃghaṭṭāt pramāṇaṃ vedyavedakau 
AbhTb advayena tatastena puṇya eṣa mahāgrahaḥ  
AbhTa amāvasyāṃ vināpyeṣa saṃghaṭṭaścenmahāgrahaḥ 
AbhTb yathārke meṣage rāhāvaśvinīstheśvinīdine  
AbhTa āmāvāsyaṃ yadā tvardhaṃ līnaṃ prātipade dale 
AbhTb pratipacca viśuddhā syāttanmokṣo dūrage vidhau  
AbhTa grāsamokṣāntare snānadhyānahomajapādikam 
AbhTb laukikālaukikaṃ bhūyaḥphalaṃ syātpāralaukikam  
AbhTa grāsyagrāsakatākṣobhaprakṣaye kṣaṇamāviśan 
AbhTb mokṣabhāgdhyānapūjādi kurvaṃścandrārkayorgrahe  
AbhTa tithiccheda ṛṇaṃ kāso vṛddhirniḥśvasanaṃ dhanam 
AbhTb ayatnajaṃ yatnajaṃ tu recanādatha rodhanāt  
AbhTa evaṃ prāṇe viśati citsūrya induṃ sudhāmayam 
AbhTb ekaikadhyena bodhāṃśu kalayā paripūrayet  
AbhTa kramasaṃpūraṇāśāliśaśāṅkāmṛtasundarāḥ 
AbhTb tuṭyaḥ pañcadaśaitāḥ syustithayaḥ sitapakṣagāḥ  
AbhTa antyāyāṃ pūrṇamastuṭyāṃ pūrvavatpakṣasandhitā 
AbhTb indugrahaśca pratipatsandhau pūrvapraveśataḥ  
AbhTa aihikaṃ grahaṇe cātra sādhakānāṃ mahāphalam 
AbhTb prāgvadanyadayaṃ māsaḥ prāṇacārebda ucyate  
AbhTa ṣaṭsu ṣaṭsvaṅguleṣvarko hṛdayānmakarādiṣu 
AbhTb tiṣṭhanmāghāḍhikaṃ ṣaṭkaṃ kuryāttaccottarāyaṇam  
AbhTa saṃkrāntitritaye vṛtte bhukte cāṣṭādaśāṅgule 
AbhTb meṣaṃ prāpte ravau puṇyaṃ viṣuvatpāralaukikam  
AbhTa praveśe tu tulāstherke tadeva viṣuvadbhavet 
AbhTb iha siddhipradaṃ caitaddakṣiṇāyanagaṃ tataḥ  
AbhTa garbhatā prodbubhūṣiṣyadbhāvaścāthodbubhūṣutā 
AbhTb udbhaviṣyattvamudbhūtiprārambhopyudbhavasthitiḥ  
AbhTa janma sattā pariṇatirvṛddhirhrāsaḥ kṣayaḥ kramāt 
AbhTb makarādīni tenātra kriyā sūte sadṛkphalam  
AbhTa āmutrike jhaṣaḥ kumbho mantrādeḥ pūrvasevane 
AbhTb catuṣkaṃ kila mīnādyamantikaṃ cottarottaram  
AbhTa praveśe khalu tatraiva śāntipuṣṭyādisundaram 
AbhTb karma syādaihikaṃ tacca dūradūraphalaṃ kramāt  
AbhTa nirgame dinavṛddhiḥ syādviparīte viparyayaḥ 
AbhTb varṣesmiṃstithayaḥ pañca pratyaṅgulamiti kramaḥ  
AbhTa tatrāpyahorātravidhiriti sarvaṃ hi pūrvavat 
AbhTb prāṇīye varṣa etasminkārtikādiṣu dakṣataḥ  
AbhTa pitāmahāntaṃ rudrāḥ syurdvādaśāgretra bhāvinaḥ 
AbhTb prāṇe varṣodayaḥ prokto dvādaśābdodayodhunā  
AbhTa kharasāstithya ekasminnekasminnaṅgule kramāt 
AbhTb dvādaśābdodaye te ca caitrādyā dvādaśoditāḥ  
AbhTa caitre mantroditiḥ sopi tālunyuktodhunā punaḥ 
AbhTb hṛdi caitroditistena tatra mantrodayopi hi  
AbhTa pratyaṅgulaṃ tithīnāṃ tu triśate parikalpite 
AbhTb sapañcāṃśāṅgulebdaḥ syātprāṇe ṣaṣṭyabdatā punaḥ  
AbhTa śatāni ṣaṭ sahasrāṇi caikaviṃśatirityayam 
AbhTb vibhāgaḥ prāṇagaḥ ṣaṣṭivarṣāhorātra ucyate  
AbhTa praharāharniśāmāsaṛtvabdaraviṣaṣṭigaḥ 
AbhTb yaśchedastatra yaḥ sandhiḥ sa puṇyo dhyānapūjane  
AbhTa iti prāṇodaye yoyaṃ kālaḥ śaktyekavigrahaḥ 
AbhTb viśvātmāntaḥsthitastasya bāhye rūpaṃ nirūpyate  
AbhTa ṣaṭ prāṇāścaṣakasteṣāṃ ṣaṣṭirnālī ca tāstathā 
AbhTb tithistattriṃśatā māsaste dvādaśa tu vatsaraḥ  
AbhTa abdaṃ pitryastvahorātra udagdakṣiṇatoyanāt 
AbhTb pitṝṇāṃ yatsvamānena varṣaṃ taddivyamucyate  
AbhTa ṣaṣṭyadhikaṃ ca triśataṃ varṣāṇāmatra mānuṣam 
AbhTb tacca dvādaśabhirhatvā māsasaṃkhyātra labhyate  
AbhTa tāṃ punastriṃśatā hatvāhorātrakalpanā vadet 
AbhTb hatvā tāṃ caikaviṃśatyā sahasraiḥ ṣaṭśatena ca  
AbhTa prāṇasaṃkhyāṃ vadettatra ṣaṣṭyādyabdodayaṃ punaḥ 
AbhTb uktaṃ ca gurubhiḥ śrīmadrauravādisvavṛttiṣu  
AbhTa devānāṃ yadahorātraṃ mānuṣāṇāṃ sa hāyanaḥ 
AbhTb śatatrayeṇa ṣaṣṭyā ca nṝṇāṃ vibudhavatsaraḥ  
AbhTa śrīmatsvacchandaśāstre ca tadeva matamīkṣyate 
AbhTb pitṝṇāṃ tadahorātramityupakramya pṛṣṭhataḥ  
AbhTa evaṃ daivastvahorātra iti hyaikyopasaṃhṛtiḥ 
AbhTb tena ye guravaḥ śrīmatsvacchandoktidvayāditaḥ  
AbhTa pitryaṃ varṣaṃ divyadinamūcurbhrāntā hi te mudhā 
AbhTb divyārkābdasahasrāṇi yugeṣu caturāditaḥ  
AbhTa ekaikahānyā tāvadbhiḥ śataisteṣvaṣṭa saṃdhayaḥ 
AbhTb caturyugaikasaptatyā manvantaste caturdaśa  
AbhTa brahmaṇohastatra cendrāḥ kramādyānti caturdaśa 
AbhTb brahmāhonte kālavahnerjvālā yojanalakṣiṇī  
AbhTa dagdhvā lokatrayaṃ dhūmāttvanyatprasvāpayettrayam 
AbhTb nirayebhyaḥ purā kālavahnervyaktiryatastataḥ  
AbhTa vibhuradhaḥsthitopīśa iti śrīrauravaṃ matam 
AbhTb brahmaniḥśvāsanirdhūte bhasmani svedavāriṇā  
AbhTa tadīyenāplutaṃ viśvaṃ tiṣṭhettāvanniśāgame 
AbhTb tasminniśāvadhau sarve pudgalāḥ sūkṣmadehagāḥ  
AbhTa agnivegeritā loke jane syurlayakevalāḥ 
AbhTb kūṣmāṇḍahāṭakādyāstu krīḍanti mahadālaye  
AbhTa niśākṣaye punaḥ sṛṣṭiṃ kurute tāmasāditaḥ 
AbhTb svakavarṣaśatāntesya kṣayastadvaiṣṇavaṃ dinam  
AbhTa rātriśca tāvatītyevaṃ viṣṇurudraśatābhidhāḥ 
AbhTb kramātsvasvaśatānteṣu naśyantyatrāṇḍalopataḥ  
AbhTa abādyavyaktatattvānteṣvitthaṃ varṣaśataṃ kramāt 
AbhTb dinarātrivibhāgaḥ syāt svasvāyuḥśatamānataḥ  
AbhTa brahmaṇaḥ pralayollāsasahasraistu rasāgnibhiḥ 
AbhTb avyaktastheṣu rudreṣu dinaṃ rātriśca tāvatī  
AbhTa tadā śrīkaṇṭha eva syātsākṣātsaṃhārakṛtprabhuḥ 
AbhTb sarve rudrāstathā mūle māyāgarbhādhikāriṇaḥ  
AbhTa avyaktākhye hyāviriñcācchrīkaṇṭhena sahāsate 
AbhTb nivṛttādhaḥsthakarmā hi brahmā tatrādhare dhiyaḥ  
AbhTa na bhoktā jñodhikāre tu vṛtta eva śivībhavet 
AbhTb sa eṣovāntaralayastatkṣaye sṛṣṭirucyate  
AbhTa sāṃkhyavedādisaṃsiddhāñchrīkaṇṭhastadaharmukhe 
AbhTb sṛjatyeva punastena na samyaṅmuktirīdṛśī  
AbhTa pradhāne yadahorātraṃ tajjaṃ varṣaśataṃ vibhoḥ 
AbhTb śrīkaṇṭhasyāyuretacca dinaṃ kañcukavāsinām  
AbhTa tatkramānniyatiḥ kālo rāgo vidyā kaletyamī 
AbhTb yāntyanyonyaṃ layaṃ teṣāmāyurgāhanikaṃ dinam  
AbhTa taddinaprakṣaye viśvaṃ māyāyāṃ pravilīyate 
AbhTb kṣīṇāyāṃ niśi tāvatyāṃ gahaneśaḥ sṛjetpunaḥ  
AbhTa evamavyaktakālaṃ tu parārdhairdaśabhirjahi 
AbhTb māyāhastāvatī rātrirbhavetpralaya eṣa saḥ  
AbhTa māyākālaṃ parārdhānāṃ guṇayitvā śatena tu 
AbhTb aiśvaro divaso nādaḥ prāṇātmātra sṛjejjagat  
AbhTa tāvatī caiśvarī rātriryatra prāṇaḥ praśāmyati 
AbhTb prāṇagarbhasthamapyatra viśvaṃ sauṣumnavartmanā  
AbhTa prāṇe brahmavile śānte saṃvidyāpyavaśiṣyate 
AbhTb aṃśāṃśikātopyetasyāḥ sūkṣmasūkṣmataro layaḥ  
AbhTa guṇayitvaiśvaraṃ kālaṃ parārdhānāṃ śatena tu 
AbhTb sādāśivaṃ dinaṃ rātrirmahāpralaya eva ca  
AbhTa sadāśivaḥ svakālānte bindvardhendunirodhikāḥ 
AbhTb ākramya nāde līyeta gṛhītvā sacarācaram  
AbhTa nādo nādāntavṛttyā tu bhittvā brahmabilaṃ haṭhāt 
AbhTb śaktitattve layaṃ yāti nijakālaparikṣaye  
AbhTa etāvacchaktitattve tu vijñeyaṃ khalvaharniśam 
AbhTb śaktiḥ svakālavilaye vyāpinyāṃ līyate punaḥ  
AbhTa vyāpinyā taddivārātraṃ līyate sāpyanāśrite 
AbhTb parārdhakoṭyā hatvāpi śaktikālamanāśrite  
AbhTa dinaṃ rātriśca tatkāle parārdhaguṇitepi ca 
AbhTb sopi yāti layaṃ sāmyasaṃjñe sāmanase pade  
AbhTa sa kālaḥ sāmyasaṃjñaḥ syānnityokalyaḥ kalātmakaḥ 
AbhTb yattatsāmanasaṃ rūpaṃ tatsāmyaṃ brahma viśvagam  
AbhTa ataḥ sāmanasātkālānnimeṣonmeṣamātrataḥ 
AbhTb tuṭyādikaṃ parārdhāntaṃ sūte saivātra niṣṭhitam  
AbhTa daśaśatasahasramayutaṃ lakṣaniyutakoṭi sārbudaṃ vṛndam 
AbhTb kharvanikharve śaṃkhābjajaladhimadhyāntamatha parārdhaṃ ca  
AbhTa ityekasmātprabhṛti hi daśadhā daśadhā krameṇa kalayitvā 
AbhTb ekādiparārdhānteṣvaṣṭādaśasu sthitiṃ brūyāt  
AbhTa catvāra ete pralayā mukhyāḥ sargāśca tatkalāḥ 
AbhTb bhūmūlanaiśaśaktisthāstadevāṇḍacatuṣṭayam  
AbhTa kālāgnirbhuvi saṃhartā māyānte kālatattvarāṭ 
AbhTb śrīkaṇṭho mūla ekatra sṛṣṭisaṃhārakārakaḥ  
AbhTa tallayo vāntarastasmādekaḥ sṛṣṭilayeśitā 
AbhTb śrīmānaghoraḥ śaktyante saṃhartā sṛṣṭikṛcca saḥ  
AbhTa tatsṛṣṭau sṛṣṭisaṃhārā niḥsaṃkhyā jagatāṃ yataḥ 
AbhTb antarbhūtāstataḥ śāktī mahāsṛṣṭirudāhṛtā  
AbhTa laye brahmā harī rudraśatānyaṣṭakapañcakam 
AbhTb ityanyonyaṃ kramādyānti layaṃ māyāntakedhvani  
AbhTa māyātattvalaye tvete prayānti paramaṃ padam 
AbhTb māyordhve ye sitādhvasthāsteṣāṃ paraśive layaḥ  
AbhTa tatrāpyaupādhikādbhedāllaye bhedaṃ pare viduḥ 
AbhTb evaṃ tāttveśvare varge līne sṛṣṭau punaḥ pare  
AbhTa tatsādhakāḥ śiveṣṭā vā tatsthānamadhiśerate 
AbhTb brāhmī nāma parasyaiva śaktistāṃ yatra pātayet  
AbhTa sa brahmā viṣṇurudrādyā vaiṣṇavyāderataḥ kramāt 
AbhTb śaktimantaṃ vihāyānyaṃ śaktiḥ kiṃ yāti nedṛśam  
AbhTa chāditaprathitāśeṣa śaktirekaḥ śivastathā 
AbhTb evaṃ visṛṣṭipralayāḥ prāṇa ekatra niṣṭhitāḥ  
AbhTa sopi saṃvidi saṃvicca cinmātre jñeyavarjite 
AbhTb cinmātrameva devī ca sā parā parameśvarī  
AbhTa aṣṭātriṃśaṃ ca tattattvaṃ hṛdayaṃ tatparāparam 
AbhTb tena saṃvittvamevaitatspandamānaṃ svabhāvataḥ  
AbhTa layodayā iti prāṇe ṣaṣṭyabdodayakīrtanam 
AbhTb icchāmātrapratiṣṭheyaṃ kriyāvaicitryacarcanā  
AbhTa kālaśaktistato bāhye naitasyā niyataṃ vapuḥ 
AbhTb svapnasvapne tathā svapne supte saṃkalpagocare  
AbhTa samādhau viśvasaṃhārasṛṣṭikramavivecane 
AbhTb mitopi kila kālāṃśo vitatatvena bhāsate  
AbhTa pramātrabhede bhedetha citro vitatimāpyasau 
AbhTb evaṃ prāṇe yathā kālaḥ kriyāvaicitryaśaktijaḥ  
AbhTa tathāpānepi hṛdayānmūlapīṭhavisarpiṇi 
AbhTb mūlābhidhamahāpīṭhasaṅkocapravikāsayoḥ  
AbhTa brahmādyanāśritāntānāṃ cinute sṛṣṭisaṃhṛtī 
AbhTb śaśvadyadyapyapānoya mitthaṃ vahati kiṃtvasau  
AbhTa avedyayatno yatnena yogibhiḥ samupāsyate 
AbhTb hṛtkandānandasaṃkocavikāsadvādaśāntagāḥ  
AbhTa brahmādayonāśritāntāḥ sevyantetra suyogibhiḥ 
AbhTb ete ca parameśānaśaktitvādviśvavartinaḥ  
AbhTa dehamapyaśnuvānāstatkāraṇānīti kāmike 
AbhTb bālyayauvanavṛddhatvanidhaneṣu punarbhave  
AbhTa muktau ca dehe brahmādyāḥ ṣaḍadhiṣṭhānakāriṇaḥ 
AbhTb tasyānte tu parā devī yatra yukto na jāyate  
AbhTa anena jñātamātreṇa dīkṣānugrahakṛdbhavet 
AbhTb samastakāraṇollāsapade suvidite yataḥ  
AbhTa akāraṇaṃ śivaṃ vindedyattadviśvasya kāraṇam 
AbhTb adhovaktraṃ tvidaṃ dvaitakalaṅkaikāntaśātanam  
AbhTa kṣīyate tadupāsāyāṃ yenordhvādharaḍambaraḥ 
AbhTb atrāpānodaye prāgvatṣaṣṭyabdodayayojanām  
AbhTa yāvatkurvīta tuṭyāderyuktāṅgulavibhāgataḥ 
AbhTb evaṃ samānepi vidhiḥ sa hi hārdīṣu nāḍiṣu  
AbhTa saṃcaransarvatodikkaṃ daśadhaiva vibhāvyate 
AbhTb daśa mukhyā mahānāḍīḥ pūrayanneṣa tadgatāḥ  
AbhTa nāḍyantaraśritā nāḍīḥ krāmandehe samasthitiḥ 
AbhTb aṣṭāsu digdaleṣveṣa krāmaṃstaddikpateḥ kramāt  
AbhTa ceṣṭitānyanukurvāṇo raudraḥ saumyaśca bhāsate 
AbhTb sa eva nāḍītritaye vāmadakṣiṇamadhyage  
AbhTa indvarkāgnimaye mukhye caraṃstiṣṭhatyaharniśam 
AbhTb sārdhanālīdvayaṃ prāṇaśatāni nava yatsthitam  
AbhTa tāvadvahannahorātraṃ caturviṃśatidhā caret 
AbhTb viṣuvadvāsare prātaḥ sāṃśāṃ nālīṃ sa madhyagaḥ  
AbhTa vāmetarodaksavyānyairyāvatsaṃkrāntipañcakam 
AbhTb evaṃ kṣīṇāsu pādonacaturdaśasu nāliṣu  
AbhTa madhyāhne dakṣaviṣuvannavaprāṇaśatīṃ vahet 
AbhTb dakṣodaganyodagdakṣaiḥ punaḥ saṃkrāntipañcakam  
AbhTa navāsuśatamekaikaṃ tato viṣuvaduttaram 
AbhTb pañcake pañcaketīte saṃkrānterviṣuvadbahiḥ  
AbhTa yadvattathāntaḥ saṅkrāntirnavaprāṇaśatāni sā 
AbhTb evaṃ rātrāvapītyevaṃ viṣuvaddivasātsamāt  
AbhTa ārabhyāharniśāvṛddhihrāsasaṅkrāntigopyasau 
AbhTb rātryantadinapūrvāṃśau madhyāhno divasakṣayaḥ  
AbhTa sa śarvaryudayo madhyamudakto viṣutedṛśī 
AbhTb vyāptau viṣeryato vṛttiḥ sāmyaṃ ca vyāptirucyate  
AbhTa tadarhati ca yaḥ kālo viṣuvattadihoditaḥ 
AbhTb viṣuvatprabhṛti hrāsavṛddhī ye dinarātrige  
AbhTa tatkrameṇaiva saṃkrāntihrāsavṛddhī divāniśoḥ 
AbhTb itthaṃ samānamaruto varṣadvayavikalpanam  
AbhTa cāra ekatra nahyatra śvāsapraśvāsacarcanam 
AbhTb samānepi tuṭeḥ pūrvaṃ yāvatṣaṣṭyabdagocaram  
AbhTa kālasaṃkhyā susūkṣmaikacāragā gaṇyate budhaiḥ 
AbhTb saṃdhyāpūrvāhṇamadhyāhnamadhyarātrādi yatkila  
AbhTa antaḥsaṃkrāntigaṃ grāhyaṃ tanmukhyaṃ tatphaloditeḥ 
AbhTb uktaḥ samānagaḥ kāla udāne tu nirūpyate  
AbhTa prāṇavyāptau yaduktaṃ tadudānepyatra kevalam 
AbhTb nāsāśaktyantayoḥ sthāne brahmarandhrordhvadhāmanī  
AbhTa tenodānetra hṛdayānmūrdhanyadvādaśāntagam 
AbhTb tuṭyādiṣaṣṭivarṣāntaṃ viśvaṃ kālaṃ vicārayet  
AbhTa vyāne tu viśvātmamaye vyāpake kramavarjite 
AbhTb sūkṣmasūkṣmocchaladrūpamātraḥ kālo vyavasthitaḥ  
AbhTa sṛṣṭiḥ pravilayaḥ sthemā saṃhāronugraho yataḥ 
AbhTb kramātprāṇādike kāle taṃ taṃ tatrāśrayettataḥ  
AbhTa prāṇacāretra yo varṇapadamantrodayaḥ sthitaḥ 
AbhTb yatnajoyatnajaḥ sūkṣmaḥ paraḥ sthūlaḥ sa kathyate  
AbhTa eko nādātmako varṇaḥ sarvavarṇāvibhāgavān 
AbhTb sonastamitarūpatvādanāhata ihoditaḥ  
AbhTa sa tu bhairavasadbhāvo mātṛsadbhāva eṣa saḥ 
AbhTb parā saikākṣarā devī yatra līnaṃ carācaram  
AbhTa hrasvārṇatrayamekaikaṃ ravyaṅgulamathetarat 
AbhTb praveśa iti ṣaḍvarṇāḥ sūryendupathagāḥ kramāt  
AbhTa ikārokārayorādisandhau saṃdhyakṣaradvayam 
AbhTb eo iti praveśe tu aiau iti dvayaṃ viduḥ  
AbhTa ṣaṇṭhārṇāni praveśe tu dvādaśāntalalāṭayoḥ 
AbhTb gale hṛdi ca bindvarṇavisargau paritaḥsthitau  
AbhTa kādipañcakamādyasya varṇasyāntaḥ sadoditam 
AbhTb evaṃ sasthānavarṇānāmantaḥ sā sārṇasantatiḥ  
AbhTa hṛdyeṣa prāṇarūpastu sakāro jīvanātmakaḥ 
AbhTb binduḥ prakāśo hārṇaśca pūraṇātmatayā sthitaḥ  
AbhTa uktaḥ paroyamudayo varṇānāṃ sūkṣma ucyate 
AbhTb praveśe ṣoḍaśaunmukhye ravayaḥ ṣaṇṭhavarjitāḥ  
AbhTa tadevendvarkamatrānye varṇāḥ sūkṣmodayastvayam 
AbhTb kālordhamātraḥ kādīnāṃ trayastriṃśata ucyate  
AbhTa mātrā hrasvāḥ pañca dīrghāṣṭakaṃ dvistriḥ plutaṃ tu lṝ 
AbhTb ekāśītimimāmardhamātrāṇāmāha no guruḥ  
AbhTa yadvaśādbhagavānekāśītikaṃ mantramabhyadhāt 
AbhTb ekāśītipadā devī śaktiḥ proktā śivātmikā  
AbhTa śrīmātaṅge tathā dharmasaṃghātātmā śivo yataḥ 
AbhTb tathā tathā parāmarśaśakticakreśvaraḥ prabhuḥ  
AbhTa sthūlaikāśītipadajaparāmarśairvibhāvyate 
AbhTb tata eva parāmarśo yāvatyekaḥ samāpyate  
AbhTa tāvattatpadamuktaṃ no suptiṅniyamayāntritam 
AbhTb ekāśītipadodāravimarśaktamabṛṃhitaḥ  
AbhTa sthūlopāyaḥ paropāyastveṣa mātrākṛto layaḥ 
AbhTb ardhamātrā nava nava syuścaturṣu caturṣu yat  
AbhTa aṅguleṣviti ṣaṭtriṃśatyekāśītipadodayaḥ 
AbhTb aṅgule navabhāgena vibhakte navamāśakāḥ  
AbhTa vedā mātrārdhamanyattu dvicatuḥṣaṅguṇaṃ trayam 
AbhTb evamaṅgularandhrāṃśacatuṣkadvayagaṃ laghu  
AbhTa dīrghaṃ plutaṃ kramāddvitriguṇamardhaṃ tatopi hal 
AbhTb kṣakārastryardhamātrātmā mātrikaḥ satathāntarā  
AbhTa viśrāntāvardhamātrāsya tasmiṃstu kalite sati 
AbhTb aṅgulārdhedribhāgena tvardhamātrā purā punaḥ  
AbhTa kṣakāraḥ sarvasaṃyogagrahaṇātmā tu sarvagaḥ 
AbhTb sarvavarṇodayādyantasandhiṣūdayabhāgvibhuḥ  
AbhTa itthaṃ ṣaṭtriṃśake cāre varṇānāmudayaḥ phale 
AbhTb krūre saumye vilomena hādi yāvadapaścimam  
AbhTa hṛdyakāro dvādaśānte hakārastadidaṃ viduḥ 
AbhTb ahamātmakamadvaitaṃ yaḥ prakāśātmaviśramaḥ  
AbhTa śivaśaktyavibhāgena mātraikāśītikā tviyam 
AbhTb dvāsaptatāvaṅguleṣu dviguṇatvena saṃsaret  
AbhTa uktaḥ sūkṣmodayastraidhaṃ dvidhoktastu parodayaḥ 
AbhTb atha sthūlodayorṇānāṃ bhaṇyate guruṇoditaḥ  
AbhTa ekaikamardhapraharaṃ dine vargāṣṭakodayaḥ 
AbhTb rātrau ca hrāsavṛddhyatra kecidāhurna kepi tu  
AbhTa eṣa vargodayo rātrau divā cāpyardhayāmagaḥ 
AbhTb prāṇatrayodaśaśatī pañcāśadadhikā ca sā  
AbhTa adhyardhā kila saṃkrāntirvarge varge divāniśoḥ 
AbhTb tadaikye tūdayaścāraśatānāṃ saptaviṃśatiḥ  
AbhTa nava vargāṃstu ye prāhusteṣāṃ prāṇaśatī svīnviḥ 
AbhTb satribhāgaiva saṃkrāntirvarge pratyekamucyate  
AbhTa aharniśaṃ tadaikye tu śatānāṃ śruticakṣuṣī 
AbhTb sthūlo vargodayaḥ soyamathārṇodaya ucyate  
AbhTa ekaikavarṇe prāṇānāṃ dviśataṃ ṣoḍaśādhikam 
AbhTb bahiścaṣakaṣaṭtriṃśaddina itthaṃ tathāniśi  
AbhTa śatamaṣṭottaraṃ tatra raudraṃ śāktamathottaram 
AbhTb yāmalasthitiyoge tu rudraśaktyavibhāgitā  
AbhTa dinarātryavibhāge tu dṛgvahnyabdhyasucāraṇāḥ 
AbhTb sapañcamāṃśā nāḍī ca bahirvarṇodayaḥ smṛtaḥ  
AbhTa iti pañcāśikā seyaṃ varṇānāṃ paricarcitā 
AbhTb ekonāṃ ye tu tāmāhustanmataṃ saṃpracakṣmahe  
AbhTa vedāścārāḥ pañcamāṃśanyūnaṃ cārārdhamekaśaḥ 
AbhTb varṇedhikaṃ taddviguṇamavibhāge divāniśoḥ  
AbhTa sthūlo varṇodayaḥ soyaṃ purā sūkṣmo nigadyate  
AbhTa iti kālatattvamuditaṃ śāstramukhāgamanijānubhavasiddham  a
C atha śrītantrāloke
AbhTb atha paramarahasyoyaṃ cakrāṇāṃ bhaṇyatebhyudayaḥ  b
AbhTa ityayatnajamākhyātaṃ yatnajaṃ tu nigadyate 
AbhTb bījapiṇḍātmakaṃ sarvaṃ saṃvidaḥ spandanātmatām  
AbhTa vidadhatparasaṃvittāvupāya iti varṇitam 
AbhTb yathāraghaṭṭacakrāgraghaṭīyantraughavāhanam  
AbhTa ekānusaṃdhiyatnena citraṃ yantrodayaṃ bhajet 
AbhTb ekānusaṃdhānabalājjāte mantrodayeniśam  
AbhTa tanmantradevatā yatnāttādātmyena prasīdati 
AbhTb khe rasaikākṣi nityotthe tadardhaṃ dvikapiṇḍake  
AbhTa trike sapta sahasrāṇi dviśatītyudayo mataḥ 
AbhTb catuṣke tu sahasrāṇi pañca caiva catuḥśatī  
AbhTa pañcārṇebdhisahasrāṇi triśatī viṃśatistathā 
AbhTb ṣaṭke sahasratritayaṃ ṣaṭśatī codayo bhavet  
AbhTa saptake trisahasraṃ tu ṣaḍaśītyadhikaṃ smṛtam 
AbhTb śataistu saptaviṃśatyā varṇāṣṭakavikalpite  
AbhTa caturviṃśatiśatyā tu navārṇeṣūdayo bhavet 
AbhTb adhiṣaṣṭyekaviṃśatyā śatānāṃ daśavarṇake  
AbhTa ekānnaviṃśatiśataṃ catuḥṣaṣṭiḥ śivārṇake 
AbhTb aṣṭādaśa śatāni syurudayo dvādaśārṇake  
AbhTa trayodaśārṇe dvāṣaṣṭyā śatāni kila ṣoḍaśa 
AbhTb tricatvāriṃśatā pañcadaśeti bhuvanārṇake  
AbhTa caturdaśaśatī khābdhiḥ syātpañcadaśavarṇake 
AbhTb trayodaśaśatī sārdhā ṣoḍaśārṇe tu kathyate  
AbhTa śatadvādaśikā saptadaśārṇe saikasaptatiḥ 
AbhTb aṣṭādaśārṇe vijñeyā śatadvādaśikā budhaiḥ  
AbhTa caturviṃśatisaṃkhyāke cakre navaśatī bhavet 
AbhTb saptaviṃśatisaṃkhyāte tūdayoṣṭaśatātmakaḥ  
AbhTa dvātriṃśake mahācakre ṣaṭśatī pañcasaptatiḥ 
AbhTb dvicaturviṃśake cakre sārdhāṃ śatacatuṣṭayīm  
AbhTa udayaṃ piṇḍayogajñaḥ piṇḍamantreṣu lakṣayet 
AbhTb catuṣpañcāśake cakre śatānāṃ tu catuṣṭayam  
AbhTa saptatriṃśatsahārdhena triśatyaṣṭāṣṭake bhavet 
AbhTb ardhamardhatribhāgaśca ṣaṭṣaṣṭirdviśatī bhavet  
AbhTa ekāśītipade cakre udayaḥ prāṇacāragaḥ 
AbhTb cakre tu ṣaṇṇavatyākhye sapādā dviśatī bhavet  
AbhTa aṣṭottaraśate cakre dviśatastūdayo bhavet 
AbhTb krameṇetthamidaṃ cakraṃ ṣaṭkṛtvo dviguṇaṃ yadā  
AbhTa tatopi dviguṇeṣṭāṃśasyārdhamadhyardhamekakam 
AbhTb tatopi sūkṣmakuśalairardhārdhādiprakalpane  
AbhTa bhāgaṣoḍaśakasthityā sūkṣmaścārobhilakṣyate 
AbhTb evaṃ prayatnasaṃruddhaprāṇacārasya yoginaḥ  
AbhTa krameṇa prāṇacārasya grāsa evopajāyate 
AbhTb prāṇagrāsakramāvāptakālasaṃkarṣaṇasthitiḥ  
AbhTa saṃvidekaiva pūrṇā syājjñānabhedavyapohanāt 
AbhTb tathā hi prāṇacārasya navasyānudaye sati  
AbhTa na kālabhedajanito jñānabhedaḥ prakalpate 
AbhTb saṃvedyabhedānna jñānaṃ bhinnaṃ śikharivṛttavat  
AbhTa kālastu bhedakastasya sa tu sūkṣmaḥ kṣaṇo mataḥ 
AbhTb saukṣmyasya cāvadhirjñānaṃ yāvattiṣṭhati sa kṣaṇaḥ  
AbhTa anyathā na sa nirvaktuṃ nipuṇairapi pāryate 
AbhTb jñānaṃ kiyadbhavettāvattadabhāvo na bhāsate  
AbhTa tadabhāvaśca no tāvadyāvattatrākṣavartmani 
AbhTb arthe vātmapradeśe vā na saṃyogavibhāgitā  
AbhTa sā cedudayate spandamayī tatprāṇagā dhruvam 
AbhTb bhavedeva tataḥ prāṇaspandābhāve na sā bhavet  
AbhTa tadabhāvānna vijñānābhāvaḥ saivaṃ tu saiva dhīḥ 
AbhTb na cāsau vastuto dīrghā kālabhedavyapohanāt  
AbhTa vastuto hyata eveyaṃ kālaṃ saṃvinna saṃspṛśet 
AbhTb ata ekaiva saṃvittirnānārūpe tathātathā  
AbhTa vindānā nirvikalpāpi vikalpo bhāvagocare 
AbhTb spandāntaraṃ na yāvattaduditaṃ tāvadeva saḥ  
AbhTa tāvāneko vikalpaḥ syādvividhaṃ vastu kalpayan 
AbhTb ye tvitthaṃ na vidusteṣāṃ vikalpo nopapadyate  
AbhTa sa hyeko na bhavetkaścit trijagatyāpi jātucit 
AbhTb śabdārūṣaṇayā jñānaṃ vikalpaḥ kila kathyate  
AbhTa sā ca syātkramikaivetthaṃ kiṃ kathaṃ ko vikalpayet 
AbhTb ghaṭa ityapi neyānsyādvikalpaḥ kā kathā sthitau  
AbhTa na vikalpaśca kopyasti yo mātrāmātraniṣṭhitaḥ 
AbhTb na ca jñānasamūhosti teṣāmayugapatsthiteḥ  
AbhTa tenāstaṅgata evaiṣa vyavahāro vikalpajaḥ 
AbhTb tasmātspandāntaraṃ yāvannodiyāttāvadekakam  
AbhTa vijñānaṃ tadvikalpātmadharmakoṭīrapi spṛśet 
AbhTb ekāśītipadodāraśaktyāmarśātmakastataḥ  
AbhTa vikalpaḥ śivatādāyī pūrvameva nirūpitaḥ 
AbhTb yathā karṇau nartayāmītyevaṃ yatnāttathā bhavet  
AbhTa cakracāragatādyatnāttadvattaccakragaiva dhīḥ 
AbhTb japahomārcanādīnāṃ prāṇasāmyamato vidhiḥ  
AbhTa siddhāmate kuṇḍalinīśaktiḥ prāṇasamonmanā 
AbhTb uktaṃ ca yoginīkaule tadetatparameśinā  
AbhTa padamantrākṣare cakre vibhāgaṃ śaktitattvagam 
AbhTb padeṣu kṛtvā mantrajño japādau phalabhāgbhavet  
AbhTa dvitrisaptāṣṭasaṃkhyātaṃ lopayecchatikodayam 
AbhTb iti śaktisthitā mantrā vidyā vā cakranāyakāḥ  
AbhTa padapiṇḍasvarūpeṇa jñātvā yojyāḥ sadā priye 
AbhTb nityodaye mahātattve udayasthe sadāśive  
AbhTa ayuktāḥ śaktimārge tu na japtāścodayena ye 
AbhTb te na siddhyanti yatnena japtāḥ koṭiśatairapi  
AbhTa mālāmantreṣu sarveṣu mānaso japa ucyate 
AbhTb upāṃśurvā śaktyudayaṃ teṣāṃ na parikalpayet  
AbhTa padamantreṣu sarveṣu yāvattatpadaśaktigam 
AbhTb śakyate satataṃ yuktaistāvajjapyaṃ tu sādhakaiḥ  
AbhTa tāvatī teṣu vai saṃkhyā padeṣu padasaṃjñitā 
AbhTb tāvantamudayaṃ kṛtvā tripadoktyāditaḥ kramāt  
AbhTa dvādaśākhye dvādaśite cakre sārdhaṃ śataṃ bhavet 
AbhTb udayastaddhi sacatuścatvāriṃśacchataṃ bhavet  
AbhTa ṣoḍaśākhye dvādaśite dvānavatyadhike śate 
AbhTb cārārdhena samaṃ proktaṃ śataṃ dvādaśakādhikam  
AbhTa ṣoḍaśākhye ṣoḍaśite bhaveccaturaśītigaḥ 
AbhTb udayo dviśataṃ taddhi ṣaṭpañcāśatsamuttaram  
AbhTa cārāṣṭabhāgāṃstrīnatra kathayantyadhikānbudhāḥ 
AbhTb aṣṭāṣṭake dvādaśite pādārdhaṃ viṃśatiṃ vasūn  
AbhTa udayaḥ saptaśatikā sāṣṭā ṣaṣṭiryato hi saḥ 
AbhTb eṣa cakrodayaḥ proktaḥ sādhakānāṃ hitāvahaḥ  
AbhTa niruddhya mānasīrvṛttīścakre viśrāntimāgataḥ 
AbhTb vyutthāya yāvadviśrāmyettāvaccārodayo hyayam  
AbhTa pūrṇe samudaye tvatra praveśaikātmyanirgamāḥ 
AbhTb traya ityata evoktaḥ siddhau madhyodayo varaḥ  
AbhTa ādyantodayanirmuktā madhyamodayasaṃyutāḥ 
AbhTb mantravidyācakragaṇāḥ siddhibhājo bhavanti hi  
AbhTa mantracakrodayajñastu vidyācakrodayārthavit 
AbhTb kṣipraṃ siddhyediti proktaṃ śrīmaddviṃśatike trike  
AbhTa dvistriścaturvā mātrābhirvidyāṃ vā cakrameva vā 
AbhTb tattvodayayutaṃ nityaṃ pṛthagbhūtaṃ japetsadā  
AbhTa piṇḍākṣarapadairmantramekaikaṃ śaktitattvagam 
AbhTb bahvakṣarastu yo mantro vidyā vā cakrameva vā  
AbhTa śaktisthaṃ naiva taṃ tatra vibhāgastvoṃnamontagaḥ 
AbhTb asmiṃstattvodaye tasmādahorātrastriśastriśaḥ  
AbhTa vibhajyate vibhāgaśca punareva triśastriśaḥ 
AbhTb pūrvodaye tu viśramya dvitīyenollasedyadā  
AbhTa viśeccārdhardhikāyogāttadoktārdhodayo bhavet 
AbhTb yadā pūrṇodayātmā tu samaḥ kālastrike sphuret  
AbhTa praveśaviśrāntyullāse syātsvatryaṃśodayastadā 
AbhTb etyeṣa kālavibhavaḥ prāṇa eva pratiṣṭhitaḥ  
AbhTa sa spade khe sa taccityāṃ tenāsyāṃ viśvaniṣṭhiatiḥ 
AbhTb ataḥ saṃvitpratiṣṭhānau yato viśvalayodayau  
AbhTa śaktyantedhvani tatspandāsaṃkhyātā vāstavī tataḥ 
AbhTb uktaṃ śrīmālinītantre gātre yatraiva kutracit  
AbhTa vikāra upajāyeta tattattvaṃ tattvamuttamam 
AbhTb prāṇe pratiṣṭhitaḥ kālastadāviṣṭā ca yattanuḥ  
AbhTa dehe pratiṣṭhitasyāsya tato rūpaṃ nirūpyate 
AbhTb citspandaprāṇavṛttīnāmantyā yā sthūlatā suṣiḥ  
AbhTa sā nāḍīrūpatāmetya dehaṃ saṃtānayedimam 
AbhTb śrīsvacchandeta evoktaṃ yathā parṇaṃ svatantubhiḥ  
AbhTa vyāptaṃ tadvattanurdvāradvāribhāvena nāḍibhiḥ 
AbhTb pādāṅguṣṭhādikordhvasthabrahmakuṇḍalikāntagaḥ  
AbhTa kālaḥ samastaścaturaśītāvevāṅguleṣvitaḥ 
AbhTb dvādaśāntāvadhiṃ kiṃcitsūkṣmakālasthitiṃ viduḥ  
AbhTa ṣaṇṇavatyāmadhaḥ ṣaḍdvikramāccāṣṭottaraṃ śatam 
AbhTb atra madhyamasaṃcāriprāṇodayalayāntare  
AbhTa viśve sṛṣṭilayāste tu citrā vāyvantarakramāt 
AbhTb ityeṣa sūkṣmaparimarśanaśīlanīyaścakrodayonubhavaśāstradṛśā mayoktaḥ  
C atha śītantrāloke aṣṭamamāhnikaṃ
AbhTb deśādhvanopyatha samāsavikāsayogātsaṃgīyate vidhirayaṃ śivaśāstradṛṣṭaḥ  b
AbhTa vicāritoyaṃ kālādhvā kriyāśaktimayaḥ prabhoḥ 
AbhTb mūrtivaicitryajastajjo deśādhvātha nirūpyate  
AbhTa adhvā samasta evāyaṃ cinmātre saṃpratiṣṭhitaḥ 
AbhTb yattatra nahi viśrāntaṃ tannabhaḥkusumāyate  
AbhTa saṃviddvāreṇa tatsṛṣṭe śūnye dhiyi marutsu ca 
AbhTb nāḍīcakrānucakreṣu barhirdehedhvasaṃsthitiḥ  
AbhTa tatrādhvaivaṃ nirūpyoyaṃ yatastatprakriyākramam 
AbhTb anusaṃdadhadeva drāg yogī bhairavatāṃ vrajet  
AbhTa didṛkṣayaiva sarvārthān yadā vyāpyāvatiṣṭhate 
AbhTb tadā kiṃ bahunoktena ityuktaṃ spandaśāsane  
AbhTa jñātvā samastamadhvānaṃ tadīśeṣu vilāpayet 
AbhTb tān dehaprāṇadhīcakre pūrvavad gālayetkramāt  
AbhTa tatsamastaṃ svasaṃvittau sā saṃvidbharitātmikā 
AbhTb upāsyamānā saṃsārasāgarapralayānalaḥ  
AbhTa śrīmahīkṣottare caitānadhveśān gururabravīt 
AbhTb brahmānantātpradhānāntaṃ viṣṇuḥ puṃsaḥ kalāntagam  
AbhTa rudro granthau ca māyāyāmīśaḥ sādākhyagocare 
AbhTb anāśritaḥ śivastasmādvyāptā tadvyāpakaḥ paraḥ  
AbhTa evaṃ śivatvamāpannamiti matvā nyarūpyata 
AbhTb na prakriyāparaṃ jñānamiti svacchandaśāsane  
AbhTa triśiraḥśāsane bodho mūlamadhyāgrakalpitaḥ 
AbhTb ṣaṭtriṃśattattvasaṃrambhaḥ smṛtirbhedavikalpanā  
AbhTa avyāhatavibhāgosmibhāvo mūlaṃ tu bodhagam 
AbhTb samastatattvabhāvoyaṃ svātmanyevāvibhāgakaḥ  
AbhTa bodhamadhyaṃ bhavetkiṃcidādhārādheyalakṣaṇam 
AbhTb tattvabhedavibhāgena svabhāvasthitilakṣaṇam  
AbhTa bodhāgraṃ tattu vidbodhaṃ nistaraṅgaṃ bṛhatsukham 
AbhTb saṃvidekātmatānītabhūtabhāvapurādikaḥ  
AbhTa avyavacchinnasaṃvittirbhairavaḥ parameśvaraḥ 
AbhTb śrīdevyāyāmale coktaṃ ṣaṭtriṃśattattvasundaram  
AbhTa adhvānaṃ ṣaḍvidhaṃ dhyāyansadyaḥ śivamayo bhavet 
AbhTb yadyapyamuṣya nāthasya saṃvittyanatirekiṇaḥ  
AbhTa pūrṇasyordhvādimadhyāntavyavasthā nāsti vāstavī 
AbhTb tathāpi pratipattṝṇāṃ pratipādayitustathā  
AbhTa svasvarūpānusāreṇa madhyāditvādikalpanāḥ 
AbhTb tataḥ pramātṛsaṃkalpaniyamāt pārthivaṃ viduḥ  
AbhTa tattvaṃ sarvāntarālasthaṃ yatsarvāvaraṇairvṛtam 
AbhTb tadatra pārthive tattve kathyate bhuvanasthitiḥ  
AbhTa netā kaṭāharudrāṇāmanantaḥ kāmasevinām 
AbhTb potārūḍho jalasyāntarmadyapānavighūrṇitaḥ  
AbhTa sa devaṃ bhairavaṃ dhyāyan nāgaiśca parivāritaḥ 
AbhTb kālāgrerbhuvanaṃ cordhve koṭiyojanamucchritam  
AbhTa lokānāṃ bhasmasādbhāvabhayānnordhva sa vīkṣate 
AbhTb sa ca vyāptāpi viśvasya yasmātpluṣyannimāṃ bhuvam  
AbhTa narakebhyaḥ purā vyaktastenāsau tadadho mataḥ 
AbhTb daśa koṭyo vibhorjvālā tadardha śūnyamūrdhvataḥ  
AbhTa tadūrdhve narakādhīśāḥ kramādduḥkhaikavedanāḥ 
AbhTb śdho madhye tadūrdhve ca sthitā bhedāntarairvṛtāḥ  
AbhTa avīcikumbhīpākākhyarauravāsteṣvanukramāt 
AbhTb ekādaśaikādaśa ca daśetyantaḥ śarāgni tat  
AbhTa pratyekameṣāmekonā koṭirucchritirantaram 
AbhTb lakṣamatra khavedāsyasaṃkhyānāmantarā sthitiḥ  
AbhTa kūṣmāṇḍa ūrdhve lakṣonakoṭisthānastadīśitā 
AbhTb śāstraviruddhācaraṇāt kṛṣṇaṃ ye karma vidadhate  
AbhTa tatra bhīmairlokapuruṣaiḥ pīḍyante bhogaparyantam 
AbhTb ye sakṛdapi parameśaṃ śivamekāgreṇa cetasā śaraṇam  
AbhTa yānti na te narakayujaḥ kṛṣṇaṃ teṣāṃ sukhālpatādāyi 
AbhTb sahasranavakotsedhamekāntaramatha kramāt  
AbhTa pātālāṣṭakamekaikamaṣṭame hāṭakaḥ prabhuḥ 
AbhTb pratilokaṃ niyuktātmā śrīkaṇṭho haṭhato bahūḥ  
AbhTa siddhīrdadātyasāvevaṃ śrīmadrauravaśāsane 
AbhTb vratino ye cikarmasthā niṣiddhācārakāriṇaḥ  
AbhTa dīkṣitā api ye luptasamayā naca kurvate 
AbhTb prāyaścittāṃstathā tatsthā vāmācārasya dūṣakāḥ  
AbhTa devāgnidravyavṛttyaṃśajīvinaścottamasthitāḥ 
AbhTb adhaḥsthagāruḍādyanyamantrasevāparāyaṇāḥ  
AbhTa te hāṭakavibhoragre kiṅkarā vividhātmakāḥ 
AbhTb te tu tatrāpi deveśaṃ bhaktyā cetparyupāsate  
AbhTa tadīśatattve līyante kramācca parame śive 
AbhTb anyathā ye tu vartante tadbhoganiratātmakāḥ  
AbhTa te kālavahnisaṃtāpadīnākrandaparāyaṇāḥ 
AbhTb guṇatattve nilīyante tataḥ sṛṣṭimukhe punaḥ  
AbhTa pātyante mātṛbhirghorayātanaughapurassaram 
AbhTb adhamādhamadeheṣu nijakarmānurūpataḥ  
AbhTa mānuṣānteṣu tatrāpi kecinmantravidaḥ kramāt 
AbhTb mucyantenye tu badhyante pūrvakṛtyānusārataḥ  
AbhTa ityeṣa gaṇavṛttānto nāmnā hulahulādinā 
AbhTb proktaṃ bhagavatā śrīmadānandādhikaśāsane  
AbhTa pātālordhve sahasrāṇi viṃśatirbhūkaṭāhakaḥ 
AbhTb siddhātantre tu pātālapṛṣṭhe yakṣīsamāvṛtam  
AbhTa bhadrakālyāḥ puraṃ yatra tābhiḥ krīḍanti sādhakāḥ 
AbhTb tatastamastaptabhūmistataḥśūnyaṃ tatohayaḥ  
AbhTa etāni yātanāsthānaṃ gurumantrādidūṣiṇām 
AbhTb tato bhūmyūrdhva madhya to meruḥ sahasrāṇi sa ṣoḍaśa  
AbhTa magnastanmūlavistārastaddvayenordhvavistṛtiḥ 
AbhTb sahasrābdhivasūcchrāyo haimaḥ sarvāmarālayaḥ  
AbhTa madhyordhvādhaḥ samudvṛttaśarāvacaturaśrakaḥ 
AbhTb bhairavīyaṃ ca talliṅgaṃ dharaṇī cāsya pīṭhikā  
AbhTa sarve devā nilīnā hi tatra tatpūjitaṃ sadā 
AbhTb madhye merusabhā dhātustadīśadiśi ketanam  
AbhTa jyotiṣkaśikharaṃ śaṃbhoḥ śrīkaṇṭhāṃśaśca sa prabhuḥ 
AbhTb avaruhya sahasrāṇi manovatyāścaturdaśa  
AbhTa cakravāṭaścaturdikko meruratra tu lokapāḥ 
AbhTb amarāvatikendrasya pūrvasyāṃ dakṣiṇena tām  
AbhTa atsaraḥsiddhasādhyāstāmuttareṇa vināyakāḥ 
AbhTb tejovatī svadiśyagneḥ purī tāṃ paścimena tu  
AbhTa viśvedevā viśvakarmā kramāttadanugāśca ye 
AbhTb yāmyāṃ saṃyamanī tāṃ tu paścimena kramāt sthitāḥ  
AbhTa mātṛnandā svasaṃkhyātā rudrāstatsādhakāstathā 
AbhTb kṛṣṇāṅgārā nirṛtiśca tāṃ pūrveṇa piśācakāḥ  
AbhTa rakṣāṃsi siddhagandharvāstūttareṇottareṇa tām 
AbhTb vāruṇī śuddhavatyākhyā bhūtaugho dakṣiṇena tām  
AbhTa uttareṇottareṇaināṃ vasuvidyādharāḥ kramāt 
AbhTb vāyorgandhavatī tasyā dakṣiṇe kinnarāḥ punaḥ  
AbhTa vīṇāsarasvatī devī nāradastumburustathā 
AbhTb mahodayendorguhyāḥ syuḥ paścimesyāḥ punaḥ punaḥ  
AbhTa kuberaḥ karmadevāśca tathā tatsādhakā api 
AbhTb yaśasvinī maheśasya tasyāḥ paścimato hariḥ  
AbhTa dakṣiṇe dakṣiṇe brahmāśvinau dhanvantariḥ kramāt 
AbhTb mairave cakravāṭesminnevaṃ mukhyāḥ puroṣṭadhā  
AbhTa antarālagatāstvanyāḥ punaḥ ṣaḍviṃśatiḥ smṛtāḥ 
AbhTb iṣṭāpūrtaratāḥ puṇye varṣeye bhārate narāḥ  
AbhTa te merugāḥ sakṛcchambhuṃ ye vārcanti yathocitam 
AbhTb meroḥ pradakṣiṇāpyodagdikṣu viṣkambhaparvatāḥ  
AbhTa mandaro gandhamādaśca vipulotha supārśvakaḥ 
AbhTb sitapītanīlaraktāste kramātpādaparvatāḥ  
AbhTa etairbhuvamavaṣṭabhya merustiṣṭhati niścalaḥ 
AbhTb caitrarathanandanākhye vaiśrājaṃ pitṛvanaṃ vanānyāhuḥ  
AbhTa raktodamānasasitaṃ bhadraṃ caitaccatuṣṭayaṃ sarasām 
AbhTb vṛkṣāḥ kadambajambvaśvatthanyagrodhakāḥ kramaśaḥ  
AbhTa eṣu ca caturṣvacaleṣu trayaṃ trayaṃ kramaśa etadāmnātam 
AbhTb mervadho lavaṇābdhyantaṃ jambudvīpaḥ samantataḥ  
AbhTa lakṣamātraḥ sa navadhā jāto maryādaparvataiḥ 
AbhTb niṣadho hemakūṭaśca himavāndakṣiṇe trayaḥ  
AbhTa lakṣaṃ sahasranavatistadaśītiriti kramāt 
AbhTb nīlaḥ śvetastriśṛṅgaśca tāvantaḥ savyataḥ punaḥ  
AbhTa meroḥ ṣaḍete maryādācalāḥ pūrvāparāyatāḥ 
AbhTb pūrvato mālyavānpaścādgandhamādanasaṃjñitaḥ  
AbhTa savyottarāyatau tau tu catustriṃśatsahasrakau 
AbhTb aṣṭāvete tatopyanyau dvau dvau pūrvādiṣu kramāt  
AbhTa jāṭharaḥ kūṭahimavadyātrajārudhiśṛṅgiṇaḥ 
AbhTb evaṃ sthito vibhāgotra varṣasiddhyai nirūpyate  
AbhTa samantāccakravāṭādhonarkendu caturaśrakam 
AbhTb sahasranavavistīrṇamilākhyaṃ trimukhāyuṣam  
AbhTa meroḥ paścimato gandhamādo yastasya paścime 
AbhTb ketumālaṃ kulādrīṇāṃ saptakena vibhūṣitam  
AbhTa meroḥ pūrva mālyavānyo bhadrāśvastasya pūrvataḥ 
AbhTb sahasradaśakāyustatsapañcakulaparvatam  
AbhTa pūrvapaścimataḥ savyottarataśca kramādime 
AbhTb dvātriṃśacca catustriṃśatsahasrāṇi nirūpite  
AbhTa merorudak śṛṅgavānyastadbahiḥ kuruvarṣakam 
AbhTb cāpavannavasāhasramāyustatra trayodaśa  
AbhTa kuruvarṣasyottaretha vāyavyebdhau kramāccharāḥ 
AbhTb daśa ceti sahasrāṇi dvīpau candrotha bhadrakaḥ  
AbhTa yau śvetaśṛṅgiṇau merorvāme madhye hiraṇmayam 
AbhTb tayornavakavistīrṇamāyuścārdhatrayodaśa  
AbhTa tatra vai vāmataḥ śvetanīlayo ramyakontare 
AbhTb sahasranavavistīrṇamāyurdvādaśa tāni ca  
AbhTa merordakṣiṇato hemaniṣadhau yau tadantare 
AbhTb haryākhyaṃ navasāhasraṃ tatsahasrādhikāyuṣam  
AbhTa tatraiva dakṣiṇe hemahimavaddvitayāntare 
AbhTb kainnaraṃ navasāhasraṃ tatsahasrādhikāyuṣam  
AbhTa tatraiva dakṣiṇe merorhimavānyasya dakṣiṇe 
AbhTb bhārataṃ navasāhasraṃ cāpavatkarmabhogabhūḥ  
AbhTa ilāvṛtaṃ ketubhadraṃ kuruhairaṇyaramyakam 
AbhTb harikinnaravarṣe ca bhogabhūrna tu karmabhūḥ  
AbhTa atra bāhulyataḥ karmabhūbhāvotrāpyakarmaṇām 
AbhTb paśūnāṃ karmasaṃskāraḥ syāttādṛgdṛḍhasaṃskṛteḥ  
AbhTa saṃbhavantyapyasaṃskārā bhāratenyatra cāpi hi 
AbhTb dṛḍhaprāktanasaṃskārādīśecchātaḥ śubhāśubham  
AbhTa sthānāntarepi karmāsti dṛṣṭaṃ tacca purātane 
AbhTb tatra tretā sadā kālo bhārate tu caturyugam  
AbhTa bhārate navakhaṇḍaṃ ca sāmudreṇāmbhasātra ca 
AbhTb sthalaṃ pañcaśatī tadvajjalaṃ ceti vibhajyate  
AbhTa indraḥ kaśerustāmrābho nāgīyaḥ prāggabhastimān 
AbhTb saumyagāndharvavārāhāḥ kanyākhyaṃ cāsamudrataḥ  
AbhTa kanyādvīpe ca navame dakṣiṇenābdhimadhyagāḥ 
AbhTb upadvīpāḥ ṣaṭ kulādrisaptakena vibhūṣite  
AbhTa aṅgayavamalayaśaṅkuḥ kumudavarāhau ca malayagogastya 
AbhTb tatraiva ca trikūṭe laṅkā ṣaḍamī hyupadvīpāḥ  
AbhTa dvīpopadvīpagāḥ prāyo mlecchā nānāvidhā janāḥ 
AbhTb muktākāñcanaratnāḍhyā iti śrīruruśāsane  
AbhTa bhārate yatkṛtaṃ karma kṣapitaṃ vāpyavīcitaḥ 
AbhTb śivāntaṃ tena muktirvā kanyākhye tu viśeṣataḥ  
AbhTa mahākālādikā rudrakoṭiratraiva bhārate 
AbhTb gaṅgādipañcaśatikā janma tenātra durlabham  
AbhTa anyavarṣeṣu paśuvad bhogātkarmātivāhanam 
AbhTb prāpyaṃ manorathātītamapi bhāratajanmanām  
AbhTa nānāvarṇāśramācārasukhaduḥkhavicitratā 
AbhTb kanyādvīpe yatastena karmabhūḥ seyamuttamā
