AbhTa puṃsā sitāsitānyatra kurvatāṃ kila siddhyataḥ 
AbhTb parāparau svarnirayāviti rauravavārtike  
AbhTa evaṃ meroradho jambūrabhito yaḥ sa vistarāt 
AbhTb syāt saptadaśadhā khaṇḍairnavabhistu samāsataḥ  
AbhTa manoḥ svāyaṃbhuvasyāsan sutā daśa tatastrayaḥ 
AbhTb prāvrajannatha jambvākhye rājā yognīdhranāmakaḥ  
AbhTa tasyābhavannava sutāstatoyaṃ navakhaṇḍakaḥ 
AbhTb nābhiryo navamastasya naptā bharata ārṣabhiḥ  
AbhTa tasyāṣṭau tanayāḥ sākaṃ kanyayā navamoṃśakaḥ 
AbhTb bhuktaistairnavadhā tasmāllakṣayojanamātrakāt  
AbhTa lakṣaikamātro lavaṇastadbāhyesya purodrayaḥ 
AbhTb ṛṣabho dundubhirdhūmraḥ kaṅkadroṇendavo hyudak  
AbhTa varāhanandanāśokāḥ paścāt sahabalāhakau 
AbhTb dakṣiṇa cakramainākau vāḍavontastayoḥ sthitaḥ  
AbhTa abdherdakṣiṇataḥ khākṣisahasrātikramād giriḥ 
AbhTb vidyutvāṃstrisahasrocchridāyāmotra phalāśinaḥ  
AbhTa maladigdhā dīrghakeśaśmaśravo gosadharmakāḥ 
AbhTb nagnāḥ saṃvatsarāśītijīvinastṛṇabhojinaḥ  
AbhTa niryantrāṇi sadā tatra dvārāṇi bilasiddhaye 
AbhTb ityetad gurubhirgītaṃ śrīmadrauravaśāsane  
AbhTa itthaṃ ya eṣa lavaṇasamudraḥ pratipāditaḥ 
AbhTb tadbahiḥ ṣaḍamī dvīpāḥ pratyekaṃ svārṇavairvṛtāḥ  
AbhTa kramadviguṇitāḥ ṣaḍbhirmanuputrairadhiṣṭhitāḥ 
AbhTb śākakuśakrauñcāḥ śalmaligomedhābjamiti ṣaḍdvīpāḥ 
AbhTc kṣīradadhisarpiraikṣavamadirāmadhurāmbukāḥ ṣaḍambudhayaḥ  
AbhTa medhātithirvapuṣmāñjyotiṣmāndyutimatā havī rājā 
AbhTb saṃvara iti śākādiṣu jambudvīpe nyarūpi cāgnīdhraḥ  
AbhTa girisaptakaparikalpitatāvatkhaṇḍāstu pañca śākādyāḥ 
AbhTb puṣkarasaṃjño dvidalo hariyamavaruṇendavotra pūrvādau  
AbhTa tripañcāśacca lakṣāṇi dvikoṭyayutapañcakam 
AbhTb svādvarṇavāntaṃ mervardhādyojananāmiyaṃ pramā  
AbhTa saptamajaladherbāhye haimī bhūḥ koṭidaśakamatha lakṣam 
AbhTb ucchrityā vistārādayutaṃ loketarācalaḥ kathitaḥ  
AbhTa lokālokadigaṣṭaka saṃsthaṃ rudrāṣṭakaṃ salokeśam 
AbhTb kevalamityapi kecillokālokāntare ravirna bahiḥ  
AbhTa pitṛdevapathāvasyodagdakṣiṇagau svajātpare vīthyau 
AbhTb bhānoruttaradakṣiṇamayanadvayametadeva kathayanti  
'sarveṣāmuttaro merurlokālokaśca dakṣiṇaḥ'
AbhTa udayāstamayāvitthaṃ sūryasya paribhāvayet  
AbhTa ardharātromarāvatyāṃ yāmyāyāmastameva ca 
AbhTb madhyandinaṃ tadvāruṇyāṃ saumye sūryodayaḥ smṛtaḥ  
AbhTa udayo yomarāvatyāṃ sordharātro yamālaye 
AbhTb kestaṃ saumye ca madhyāhna itthaṃ sūryagatāgate  
AbhTa pañcatriṃ śatkoṭisaṃkhyā lakṣāṇyekonaviṃśatiḥ 
AbhTb catvāriṃśatsahasrāṇi dhvāntaṃ lokācalādbahiḥ  
AbhTa saptasāgaramānastu garbhodākhyaḥ samudrarāṭ 
AbhTb lokālokasya parato yadgarbhe nikhilaiva bhūḥ  
AbhTa siddhātantretra garbhābdhestīre kauśeyasaṃjñitam 
AbhTb maṇḍalaṃ garuḍastatra siddhapakṣasamāvṛtaḥ  
AbhTa krīḍantiṃ parvatāgre te nava cātra kulādrayaḥ 
AbhTb tata uṣṇodakāstriṃśannadyaḥpātālagāstataḥ  
AbhTa caturdiṅnaimirodyānaṃ yoginīsevitaṃ sadā 
AbhTb tato merustato nāgā meghā hemāṇḍakaṃ tataḥ  
AbhTa brahmaṇoṇḍakaṭāhena merorardhena koṭayaḥ 
AbhTb pañcāśadevaṃ daśasu dicu bhūrlokasaṃjñitam  
AbhTa paśukhagamṛgatarumānuṣasarīsṛpaiḥ ṣaḍbhireṣa bhūrlokaḥ 
AbhTb vyāptaḥ piśācarakṣogandharvāṇāṃ sayakṣāṇām  
AbhTa vidyābhṛtāṃ ca kiṃ vā bahunā sarvasya bhūtasargasya 
AbhTb abhimānato yatheṣṭaṃ bhogasthānaṃ nivāsaśca  
AbhTa bhuvarlokastathā tvārkāllakṣamekaṃ tadantare 
AbhTb daśa vāyupathāste ca pratyekamayutāntarāḥ  
AbhTa ādyo vāyupathastatra vitataḥ paricarcyate 
AbhTb pañcāśadyojanordhve syādṛtarddhirnāma mārutaḥ  
AbhTa āpyāyakaḥ sa jantūnāṃ tataḥ prācetaso bhavet 
AbhTb pañcāśadyojanādūrdhva tasmādūrdhva śatena tu  
AbhTa senānīvāyuratraite mūkameghāstaḍinmucaḥ 
AbhTb ye mahyāḥ krośamātreṇa tiṣṭhanti jalavarṣiṇaḥ  
AbhTa tebhya ūrdhva śatānmeghā bhekādiprāṇivarṣiṇaḥ 
AbhTb pañcāśadūrdhvamoghotra viṣavāripravarṣiṇaḥ  
AbhTa meghāḥ skandodbhavāścānye piśācā oghamārute 
AbhTb tataḥ pañcāśadūrdhvaṃ syurmeghā mārakasaṃjñakāḥ  
AbhTa tatra sthāne mahādevajanmānaste vināyakāḥ 
AbhTb ye haranti kṛtaṃ karma narāṇāmakṛtātmanām  
AbhTa pañcāśadūrdhvaṃ vajrāṅko vāyuratropalāmbudāḥ 
AbhTb vidyādharādhamāścātra vajrāṅke saṃpratiṣṭhitāḥ  
AbhTa ye vidyāpauruṣe ye ca śmaśānādiprasādhane 
AbhTb mṛtāstatsiddhisiddhāste vajrāṃke maruti sthitāḥ  
AbhTa pañcāśadūrdhvaṃ vajrāṃkādvaidyutośanivarṣiṇaḥ 
AbhTb abdā apsarasaścātra ye ca puṇyakṛto narāḥ  
AbhTa bhṛgau vahnau jale ye ca saṃgrāme cānivartinaḥ 
AbhTb gograhe vadhyamokṣe vā mṛtāste vaidyute sthitāḥ  
AbhTa vaidyutādraivatastāvāṃstatra puṣṭivahāmbudāḥ 
AbhTb ūrdhvaṃ ca rogāmbumucaḥ saṃvartāstadanantare  
AbhTa rocanāñjanabhasmādisiddhāstatraiva raivate 
AbhTb krodhodakamucāṃ sthānaṃ viṣāvartaḥ sa mārutaḥ  
AbhTa pañcāśadūrdhvaṃ tatraiva durdinābdā hutāśajāḥ 
AbhTb vidyādharaviśeṣāśca tathā ye parameśvaram  
AbhTa gāndharveṇa sadārcanti viṣāvartetha te sthitāḥ 
AbhTb viṣāvartācchatādūrdhva durjayaḥ śvāsasaṃbhavaḥ  
AbhTa brahmaṇotra sthitā meghāḥ pralaye vātakāriṇaḥ 
AbhTb puṣkarābdā vāyugamā gandharvāśca parāvahe  
AbhTa jīmūtameghāstatsaṃjñāstathā vidyādharottamāḥ 
AbhTb ye ca rūpavratā lokā āvahe te pratiṣṭhitāḥ  
AbhTa mahāvahe tvīśakṛtāḥ prajāhitakarāmbudāḥ 
AbhTb mahāparivahe meghāḥ kapālotthā maheśituḥ  
AbhTa mahāparivahāntoyamṛtarddheḥ prāṅmarutpathaḥ 
AbhTb agnikanyā mātaraśca rudraśaktyā tvadhiṣṭhitāḥ  
AbhTa dvitīye tatpare siddhacāraṇā nijakarmajāḥ 
AbhTb turye devāyudhānyaṣṭau diggajāḥ pañcame punaḥ  
AbhTa ṣaṣṭhe garutmānanyasmiṅgaṅgānyatra vṛṣo vibhuḥ 
AbhTb dakṣastu navame brahmaśaktyā samadhitiniṣṭhitaḥ  
AbhTa daśame vasavo rudrā ādityāśca marutpathe 
AbhTb navayojanasāhasro vigrahorkasya maṇḍalam  
AbhTa triguṇaṃ jñānaśaktiḥ sā tapatyarkatayā prabhoḥ 
AbhTb svarlokastu bhuvarlokāddhruvāntaṃ paribhāṣyate  
AbhTa sūryāllakṣeṇa śītāṃśuḥ kriyāśaktiḥ śivasya sā 
AbhTb candrāllakṣeṇa nākṣatraṃ tato lakṣadvayena tu  
AbhTa pratyekaṃ bhaumataḥ sūryasutānte pañcakaṃ viduḥ 
AbhTb saurāllakṣeṇa saptarṣivargastasmāddhruvastathā  
AbhTa brahmaivāpararūpeṇa brahmasthāne dhruvocalaḥ 
AbhTb medhībhūto vimānānāṃ sarveṣāmupari dhruvaḥ  
AbhTa atra baddhāni sarvāṇyapyūhyantenilamaṇḍale 
AbhTb svassapta mārutaskandhā āmeghādyāḥ pradhānataḥ  
AbhTa itaśca kratuhotrādi kṛtvā jñānavivarjitāḥ 
AbhTb svaryānti tatkṣaye lokaṃ mānuṣyaṃ puṇyaśeṣataḥ  
AbhTa evaṃ bhūmerdhruvāntaṃ syāllakṣāṇi daśa pañca ca 
AbhTb dve koṭī pañca cāśītirlakṣāṇi svargato mahān  
AbhTa mārkaṇḍādyā ṛṣimunisiddhāstatra pratiṣṭhitāḥ 
AbhTb nivartitādhikārāśca devā mahati saṃsthitāḥ  
AbhTa mahāntarāle tatrānye tvadhikārabhujo janāḥ 
AbhTb aṣṭau koṭyo mahallokājjanotra kapilādayaḥ  
AbhTa tiṣṭhanti sādhyāstatraiva bahavaḥ sukhabhāginaḥ 
AbhTb janāttaporkakoṭyotra sanakādyā mahādhiyaḥ  
AbhTa prajāpatīnāṃ tatrādhikāro brahmātmajanmanām 
AbhTb brahmālayastu tapasaḥ satyaḥ ṣoḍaśa koṭayaḥ  
AbhTa tatra sthitaḥ sa svayambhūrviśvamāviṣkarotyadaḥ 
AbhTb satye vedāstathā cānye karmadhyānena bhāvitāḥ  
AbhTa ānandaniṣṭhāstatrordhvekoṭirvairiñcamāsanam 
AbhTb brahmāsanātkoṭiyugmaṃ puraṃ viṣṇornirūpitam  
AbhTa dhyānapūjājapairviṣṇorbhaktā gacchanti tatpadam 
AbhTb vaiṣṇavātsaptakoṭībhirbhuvanaṃ parameśituḥ  
AbhTa rudrasya sṛṣṭisaṃhārakarturbrahmāṇḍavartmani 
AbhTb dīkṣājñānavihīnā ye liṅgārādhanatatparāḥ  
AbhTa te yāntyaṇḍāntare raudraṃ puraṃ nādhaḥ kadācana 
AbhTb tatsthāḥ sarve śivaṃ yānti rudrāḥ śrīkaṇṭhadīkṣitāḥ  
AbhTa adhikārakṣaye sākaṃ rudrakanyāgaṇena te 
AbhTb puraṃ puraṃ ca rudrordhvamuttarottaravṛddhitaḥ  
AbhTa brahmāṇḍādhaśca rudrordhva daṇḍapāṇeḥ puraṃ sa ca 
AbhTb śivecchayā dṛṇātyaṇḍaṃ mokṣamārga karoti ca  
AbhTa śarvarudrau bhīmabhavāvugro devo mahānatha 
AbhTb īśāna iti bhūrlokāt sapta lokeśvarāḥ śivāḥ  
AbhTa sthūlairviśeṣairārabdhāḥ sapta lokāḥ pare punaḥ 
AbhTb sūkṣmairiti guruścaiva rurau samyaṅnyarūpayat  
AbhTa ye brahmaṇādisarge svaśarīrānnirmitāḥ prabhūtākhyāḥ 
AbhTb sthūlāḥ pañca viśeṣāḥ saptāmī tanmayā lokāḥ  
AbhTa parato liṅgādhāraiḥ sūkṣmaistanmātrajairmahābhūtaiḥ 
AbhTb lokānāmāvaraṇairviṣṭabhya parasperaṇa gandhādyaiḥ  
AbhTa kālāgnerdaṇḍapāṇyantamaṣṭānavatikoṭayaḥ 
AbhTb ata ūrdhvaṃ kaṭāhoṇḍe sa ghanaḥ koṭiyojanam  
AbhTa pañcāśatkoṭayaścordhvaṃ bhūpṛṣṭhādadharaṃ tathā 
AbhTb evaṃ koṭiśataṃ bhūḥ syāt sauvarṇastaṇḍulastataḥ  
AbhTa śatarudrāvadhirhuphaṭ bhedayettattu duḥśamam 
AbhTb pratidikkaṃ daśa daśetyevaṃ rudraśataṃ bahiḥ  
AbhTa brahmāṇḍādhārakaṃ tacca svaprabhāveṇa sarvataḥ 
AbhTb aṇḍasvarūpaṃ gurubhiścoktaṃ śrīrauravādiṣu  
AbhTa vyakterabhimukhībhūtaḥ pracyutaḥ śaktirūpataḥ 
AbhTb āvāpavānanirbhakto vastupiṇḍoṇḍa ucyate  
AbhTa tamoleśānuviddhasya kapālaṃ sattvamuttaram 
AbhTb rajonuviddhaṃ nirmṛṣṭaṃ sattvamasyādharaṃ tamaḥ  
AbhTa vastupiṇḍa iti proktaṃ śivaśaktisamūhabhāk 
AbhTb aṇḍaḥ syāditi tadvyaktau saṃmukhībhāva ucyate  
AbhTa tathāpi śivamagnānāṃ śaktīnāmaṇḍatā bhavet 
AbhTb tadartha vākyamaparaṃ tā hi na cyutaśaktitaḥ  
AbhTa tanvakṣādau mā prasāṅkṣīdaṇḍateti padāntaram 
AbhTb tanvakṣādiṣu naivāste kasyāpyāvāpanaṃ yataḥ  
AbhTa tanvakṣasamudāyatve kathamekatvamityataḥ 
AbhTb anirbhakta iti proktaṃ sājātyaparidarśakam  
AbhTa vināpi vastupiṇḍākhyapadenaikaikaśo bhavet 
AbhTb tattveṣvaṇḍasvabhāvatvaṃ nanvevamapi kiṃ na tat  
AbhTa guṇatanmātrabhūtaughamaye tattve prasajyate 
AbhTb ucyate vastuśabdena tanvakṣabhuvanātmakam  
AbhTa rūpamuktaṃ yatastena tatsamūhoṇḍa ucyate 
AbhTb bhavecca tatsamūhatvaṃ patyurviśvavapurbhṛtaḥ  
AbhTa tadartha bhedakānyanyānyupāttānīti darśitam 
AbhTb tāvanmātrāsvavasthāsu māyādhīnedhvamaṇḍale  
AbhTa mā bhūdaṇḍatvamityāhuranye bhedakayojanam 
AbhTb itthamuktaviriñcāṇḍamṛto rudrāḥ śataṃ hi yat  
AbhTa teṣāṃ sve patayo rudrā ekādaśa mahārciṣaḥ 
AbhTb anantotha kapālyāgniryamanairṛtakau balaḥ  
AbhTa śīghro nidhīśo vidyeśaḥ śambhuḥ savīrabhadrakaḥ 
AbhTb madhu madhukṛtaḥ kadambaṃ kesarajālāni yadvadāvṛṇate  
AbhTa tadvatte śivarudrā brahmāṇḍamasaṃkhyaparivārāḥ 
AbhTb śarāṣṭaniyutaṃ koṭirityeṣāṃ sanniveśanam  
AbhTa śrīkaṇṭhādhiṣṭhitāste ca sṛjanti saṃharanti ca 
AbhTb īśvaratvaṃ diviṣadāmiti rauravavārtike  
AbhTa siddhātantre tu hemāṇḍācchatakoṭerbahiḥ śatam 
AbhTb aṇḍānāṃ kramaśo dvidviguṇaṃ rūpyādiyojitam  
AbhTa teṣu krameṇa brahmāṇaḥ saṃsyurdviguṇajīvitāḥ 
AbhTb kṣīyante kramaśaste ca tadante tattvamammayam  
AbhTa dharātotra jalādi syāduttarottarataḥ kramāt 
AbhTb daśadhāhaṅkṛtāntaṃ dhīstasyāḥ syācchatadhā tataḥ  
AbhTa sahasradhā vyaktamataḥ pauṃsnaṃ daśasahasradhā 
AbhTb niyatirlakṣadhā tasmāttasyāstu daśalakṣadhā  
AbhTa kalāntaṃ koṭidhā tasmānmāyā viddaśakoṭidhā 
AbhTb īśvaraḥ śatakoṭiḥ syāttasmātkoṭisahasradhā  
AbhTa sādākhyaṃ vyaśnute tacca śaktirvṛndena saṃkhyayā 
AbhTb vyāpinī sarvamadhvānaṃ vyāpyadevī vyavasthitā  
AbhTa aprameyaṃ tataḥ śuddhaṃ śivatattvaṃ paraṃ viduḥ 
AbhTb jalādeḥ śivatattvāntaṃ na dṛṣṭaṃ kenacicchivāt  
AbhTa ṛte tataḥ śivajñānaṃ paramaṃ mokṣakāraṇam 
AbhTb tathā cāha mahādevaḥ śrīmatsvacchandaśāsane  
AbhTa nānyathā mokṣamāyāti paśurjñānaśatairapi 
AbhTb śivajñānaṃ na bhavati dīkṣāmaprāpya śāṅkarīm  
AbhTa prāktanī pārameśī sā pauruṣeyī ca sā punaḥ 
AbhTb śatarudrordhvato bhadrakālyā nīlaprabhaṃ jayam  
AbhTa na yajñadānatapasā prāpyaṃ kālyāḥ puraṃ jayam 
AbhTb tadbhaktāstatra gacchanti tanmaṇḍalasudīkṣitāḥ  
AbhTa nirbījadīkṣayā mokṣaṃ dadāti parameśvarī 
AbhTb vidyeśāvaraṇe dīkṣāṃ yāvatīṃ kurute nṛṇām  
AbhTa tāvatīṃ gatimāyānti bhuvanetra niveśitāḥ 
AbhTb tataḥ koṭyā vīrabhadro yugāntāgnisamaprabhaḥ  
AbhTa vijayākhyaṃ puraṃ cāsya ye smaranto maheśvaram 
AbhTb jaleṣu maruṣu cāgnau śiraśchedena vā mṛtāḥ  
AbhTa te yānti bodhamaiśānaṃ vīrabhadraṃ mahādyutim 
AbhTb vairabhadrordhvataḥ koṭirviṣkambhādvistṛtaṃ tridhā  
AbhTa rudrāṇḍaṃ sālilaṃ tvaṇḍaṃ śakracāpākṛti sthitam 
AbhTb ā vīrabhadrabhuvanādbhadrakālyālayāttathā  
AbhTa trayodaśabhiranyaiśca bhuvanairupaśobhitam 
AbhTb tato bhuvaḥ sahādreḥ pūrgandhatanmātradhāraṇāt  
AbhTa mṛtā gacchanti tāṃ bhūmiṃ dharitryāḥ paramāṃ budhāḥ 
AbhTb abdheḥ puraṃ tatastvāpyaṃ rasatanmātradhāraṇāt  
AbhTa tataḥ śriyaḥ puraṃ rudrakrīḍāvataraṇeṣvatha 
AbhTb prayāgādau śrīgirau ca viśeṣānmaraṇena tat  
AbhTa sārasvataṃ puraṃ tasmācchabdabrahmavidāṃ padam 
AbhTb rudrocitāstā mukhyatvādrudrebhyonyāstathā sthitāḥ  
AbhTa pureṣu bahudhā gaṅgā devādau śrīḥ sarasvatī 
AbhTb lakulādyamareśāntā aṣṭāvapsu surādhipāḥ  
AbhTa tatastu taijasaṃ tattvaṃ śivāgneratra saṃsthitiḥ 
AbhTb te cainaṃ vahnimāyānti vāhnīṃ ye dhāraṇāṃ śritāḥ  
AbhTa bhairavādiharīndvantaṃ taijase nāyakāṣṭakam 
AbhTb prāṇasya bhuvanaṃ vāyordaśadhā daśadhā tu tat  
AbhTa dhyātvā tyaktvātha vā prāṇān kṛtvā tatraiva dhāraṇām 
AbhTb taṃ viśanti mahātmāno vāyubhūtāḥ khamūrtayaḥ  
AbhTa bhīmādigayaparyantamaṣṭakaṃ vāyutattvagam 
AbhTb khatattve bhuvanaṃ vyomnaḥ prāpyaṃ tadvyomadhāraṇāt  
AbhTa vastrāpadāntaṃ sthāṇvādi vyomatattve surāṣṭakam 
AbhTb adīkṣitā ye bhūteṣu śivatattvābhimāninaḥ  
AbhTa jñānahīnā api prauḍhadhāraṇāsteṇḍato bahiḥ 
AbhTb dharābdhitejonilakhapuragā dīkṣitāśca vā  
AbhTa tāvatsaṃskārayogārthaṃ na paraṃ padamīhitum 
AbhTb tathāvidhāvatāreṣu mṛtāścāyataneṣu ye  
AbhTa tatpadaṃ te samāsādya kramādyānti śivātmatām 
AbhTb punaḥ punaridaṃ coktaṃ śrīmaddevyākhyayāmale  
AbhTa śrīkāmikāyāṃ kaśmīravarṇane coktavānvibhuḥ 
AbhTb sureśvarīmahādhāmni ye mriyante ca tatpure  
AbhTa brāhmaṇādyāḥ saṅkarāntāḥ paśavaḥ sthāvarāntagāḥ 
AbhTb rudrajātaya evaite ityāha bhagavāñchivaḥ  
AbhTa ākāśāvaraṇādūrdhvamahaṅkārādadhaḥ priye 
AbhTb tanmātrādimanontānāṃ purāṇi śivaśāsane  
AbhTa pañcavarṇayutaṃ gandhatanmātramaṇḍalaṃ mahat 
AbhTb ācchādya yojanānekakoṭibhiḥ sthitamantarā  
AbhTa evaṃ rasādimātrāṇāṃ maṇḍalāni svavarṇata 
AbhTb śarvo bhavaḥ paśupatirīśo bhīma iti kramāt  
AbhTa tanmātreśā yadicchātaḥ śabdādyāḥ khādikāriṇaḥ 
AbhTb tataḥ sūryenduvedānāṃ maṇḍalāni vibhurmahān  
AbhTa ugraścetyeṣu patayastebhyorkendū sayājakau 
AbhTb ityaṣṭau tanavaḥ śaṃbhoryāḥ parāḥ parikīrtitāḥ  
AbhTa aparā brahmaṇoṇḍe tā vyāpya sarvaṃ vyavasthitāḥ 
AbhTb kalpe kalpe prasūyante dharādyāstābhya eva tu  
AbhTa tato vāgādikarmākṣayuktaṃ karaṇamaṇḍalam 
AbhTb agnīndraviṣṇumitrāḥ sabrahmāṇasteṣu nāyakāḥ  
AbhTa prakāśamaṇḍalaṃ tasmācchrutaṃ buddhyakṣapañcakam 
AbhTb digvidyudarkavaruṇabhuvaḥ śrotrādidevatāḥ  
AbhTa prakāśamaṇḍalādūrdhvaṃ sthitaṃ pañcārthamaṇḍalam 
AbhTb manomaṇḍalametasmāt somenādhiṣṭhitaṃ yataḥ  
AbhTa bāhyadeveṣvadhiṣṭhātā sāmyaiśvaryasukhātmakaḥ 
AbhTb manodevastato divyaḥ somo vibhurudīritaḥ  
AbhTa tatopi sakalākṣāṇāṃ yonerbuddhyakṣajanmanaḥ 
AbhTb sthūlādicchagalāntāṣṭayuktaṃ cāhaṅkṛteḥ puram  
AbhTa buddhitattvaṃ tato devayonyaṣṭakapurādhipam 
AbhTb paiśācaprabhṛtibrāhmaparyantaṃ tacca kīrtitam  
AbhTa etāni devayonīnāṃ sthānānyeva purāṇyataḥ 
AbhTb avatīryātmajanmānaṃ dhyāyantaḥ saṃbhavanti te  
AbhTa parameśaniyogācca codyamānāśca māyayā 
AbhTb niyāmitā niyatyā ca brahmaṇovyaktajanmanaḥ  
AbhTa vyajyante tena sargādau nāmarūpairanekadhā 
AbhTb svāṃśanaiva mahātmāno na tyajanti svaketanam  
AbhTa uktaṃ ca śivatanāvidamadhikārapadasthitena guruṇā naḥ 
AbhTb aṣṭānāṃ devānāṃ śaktyāvirbhāvayonayo hyetāḥ  
AbhTa tanubhogāḥ punareṣāmadhaḥ prabhūtātmakāḥ proktāḥ 
AbhTb catvāriṃśattulyopabhogadeśādhikāni bhuvanāni  
AbhTa sādhanabhedātkevalamaṣṭakapañcakatayoktāni 
AbhTb etāni bhaktiyogaprāṇatyāgādigamyāni  
AbhTa teṣūmāpatireva prabhuḥ svatantrendriyo vikaraṇātmā 
AbhTb taratamayogena tatopi devayonyaṣṭakaṃ lakṣyaṃ tu  
AbhTa lokānāmakṣāṇi ca viṣayaparicchittikaraṇāni 
AbhTb gandhādermahadantādekādhikyena jātamaiśvaryam  
AbhTa aṇimādyātmakamasminpaiśācādye viriñcānte 
AbhTb jñātvaivaṃ śodhayedbuddhiṃ sārdhaṃ puryaṣṭakendriyaiḥ  
AbhTa krodheśāṣṭakamānīlaṃ saṃvartādyaṃ tato viduḥ 
AbhTb tejoṣṭakaṃ balādhyakṣaprabhṛtikrodhanāṣtakāt  
AbhTa akṛtādi tato buddhau yogāṣṭakamudāhṛtam 
AbhTb svacchandaśāsane tattu mūle śrīpūrvaśāsane  
AbhTa yogāṣṭakapade yattu some śraikaṇṭhameva ca 
AbhTb tato māyāpuraṃ bhūyaḥ śrīkaṇṭhasya ca kathyate  
AbhTa tena dvitīyaṃ bhuvanaṃ tayoḥ pratyekamucyate 
AbhTb tatra māyāpuraṃ devyā yayā viśvamadhiṣṭhitam  
AbhTa pratikalpaṃ nāmabhedairbhaṇyate sā maheśvarī 
AbhTb umāpateḥ puraṃ paścānmātṛbhiḥ parivāritam  
AbhTa śrīkaṇṭha eva parayā mūrtyomāpatirucyate 
AbhTb brāhmyaiśī skandajā hārī vārāhyaindrī saviccikā carcikā  
AbhTa pītā śuklā pītanīle nīlā śuklāruṇā kramāt 
AbhTb agnīśasaumyayāmyāpyapūrvanairṛtagāstu tāḥ  
AbhTa aṃśena mānuṣe loke dhātrā tā hyavatāritāḥ 
AbhTb svacchandāstāḥ parāścānyāḥ pare vyomni vyavasthitāḥ  
AbhTa svacchandaṃ tā niṣevante saptadheyamumā yataḥ 
AbhTb umāpatipurasyordhva sthitaṃ mūrtyaṣṭakaṃ param  
AbhTa śarvādikaṃ yasya sṛṣṭirdharādyā yājakāntataḥ 
AbhTb tābhya īśānamūrtiryā sā merau saṃpratiṣṭhitā  
AbhTa śrīkaṇṭhaḥ sphaṭikādrau sā vyāptā tanvaṣṭakairjagat 
AbhTb ye yogaṃ saguṇaṃ śambhoḥ saṃyatāḥ paryupāsate  
AbhTa tanmaṇḍalaṃ vā dṛṣṭvaiva muktadvaitā hṛtatrayāḥ 
AbhTb guṇānāmādharauttaryācchuddhāśuddhatvasaṃsthiteḥ  
AbhTa tāratamyācca yogasya bhedātphalavicitratā 
AbhTb tato bhogaphalāvāptibhedādbhedoyamucyate  
AbhTa mūrtyaṣṭakopariṣṭāttu suśivā dvādaśoditāḥ 
AbhTb vāmādyekaśivāntāste kuṅkumābhāḥ sutejasaḥ  
AbhTa tadūrdhva vīrabhadrākhyo maṇḍalādhipatiḥ sthitaḥ 
AbhTb yatta sta tsāyujyamāpannaḥ sa tena saha modate  
AbhTa tatopyaṅguṣṭhamātrāntaṃ mahādevāṣṭakaṃ bhavet 
AbhTb buddhitattvamidaṃ proktaṃ devayonyaṣṭakāditaḥ  
AbhTa mahādevāṣṭakānte tad yogāṣṭakamihoditam 
AbhTb tatra śraikaṇṭhamuktaṃ yat tasyaivomāpatistathā  
AbhTa mūrtayaḥ suśivā vīro mahādevāṣṭakaṃ vapuḥ 
AbhTb upariṣṭāddhiyodhaśca prakṛterguṇasaṃjñitam  
AbhTa tattvaṃ tatra tu saṃkṣubdhā guṇāḥ prasuvate dhiyam 
AbhTb na vaiṣamyamanāpannaṃ kāraṇaṃ kāryasūtaye  
AbhTa guṇasāmyatmikā tena prakṛtiḥ kāraṇaṃ bhavet 
AbhTb nanvevaṃ sāpi saṃkṣobhaṃ vinā tānviṣamānguṇān  
AbhTa kathaṃ suvīta tatrādye kṣobhe syādanavasthitiḥ 
AbhTb sāṃkhyasya doṣa evāyaṃ yadi vā tena te guṇāḥ  
AbhTa avyaktamiṣṭāḥ sāmyaṃ tu saṅgamātraṃ na cetarat 
AbhTb asmākaṃ tu svatantreśatathecchākṣobhasaṃgatam  
AbhTa avyaktaṃ buddhitattvasya kāraṇaṃ kṣobhitā guṇāḥ 
AbhTb nanu tattveśvarecchāto yaḥ kṣobhaḥ prakṛteḥ purā  
AbhTa tadeva buddhitattvaṃ syāt kimanyaiḥ kalpitairguṇaiḥ 
AbhTb naitatkāraṇatārūpaparāmarśāvarodhi yat  
AbhTa kṣobhāntaraṃ tataḥ kārya bījocchūnāṅkurādivat 
AbhTb kramāttamorajaḥsattve gurūṇāṃ paṅktayaḥ sthitāḥ  
AbhTa tisro dvātriṃśadekātastriṃśadapyekaviṃśatiḥ 
AbhTb svajñanayogabalataḥ krīḍanto daiśikottamāḥ  
AbhTa trinetrāḥ pāśanirmuktāstetrānugrahakāriṇaḥ 
AbhTb buddheśca guṇaparyantamubhe saptādhike śate  
AbhTa rudrāṇāṃ bhuvanānāṃ ca mukhyatonye tadantare 
AbhTb yogāṣṭakaṃ guṇaskandhe proktaṃ śivatanau punaḥ  
AbhTa yonīratītya gauṇe skandhe syuryogadātāraḥ 
AbhTb akṛtakṛtavibhuviriñcā harirguhaḥ kramavaśāttato devī  
AbhTa karaṇānyaṇimādiguṇāḥ kāryāṇi pratyayaprapañcaśca 
AbhTb avyaktādutpannā guṇāśca sattvādayomīṣām  
AbhTa dharmajñānavirāgānaiśvaryaṃ tatphalāni vividhāni 
AbhTb yacchanti guṇebhyomī puruṣebhyo yogadātāraḥ  
AbhTa tebhyaḥ parato bhuvanaṃ sattvādiguṇāsanasya devasya 
AbhTb sakalajagadekamāturbhartuḥ śrīkaṇṭhanāthasya  
AbhTa yenomāguhanīlabrahmaṛbhukṣakṛtākṛtādibhuvaneṣu 
AbhTb graharūpiṇyā śaktyā prābhvyādhiṣṭhāni bhūtāni  
AbhTa upasaṃjihīrṣuriha yaścaturānanapaṅkajaṃ samāviśya 
AbhTb dagdhvā caturo lokāñjanalokānnirmiṇoti punaḥ  
AbhTa yasyecchātaḥ sattvādiguṇaśarīrā visṛjati rudrāṇī 
AbhTb anukalpo rudrāṇyā vedī tatrejyatenukalpena  
AbhTa paśupatirindropendraviriñcairatha tadupalambhato devaiḥ 
AbhTb gandharvayakṣarākṣasapitṛmunibhiścitritāstathā yāgāḥ  
AbhTa guṇānāṃ yatparaṃ sāmyaṃ tadavyaktaṃ guṇordhvataḥ 
AbhTb krodheśacaṇḍasaṃvartā jyotiḥpiṅgalasūrakau  
AbhTa pañcāntakaikavīrau ca śikhodaścāṣṭa tatra te 
AbhTb gahanaṃ puruṣanidhānaṃ prakṛtirmūlaṃ pradhānamavyaktam  
AbhTa guṇakāraṇamityete māyāprabhavasya paryāyāḥ 
AbhTb yāvantaḥ kṣetrajñāḥ sahajāgantukamalopadigdhacitaḥ  
AbhTa te sarvetra vinihitā rudrāśca tadutthabhogabhujaḥ 
AbhTb mūḍhavivṛttavilīnaiḥ karaṇaiḥ kecittu vikaraṇakāḥ  
AbhTa akṛtādhiṣṭhānatayā kṛtyāśaktāni mūḍhāni 
AbhTb pratiniyataviṣayabhāñji sphuṭāni śāstre vivṛttāni  
AbhTa bhagnāni mahāpralaye sṛṣṭau notpāditāni līnāni 
AbhTb icchādhīnāni punarvikaraṇasaṃjñāni kāryamapyevam  
AbhTa puṃstattve tuṣṭinavakaṃ siddhayoṣṭau ca tatpuraḥ 
AbhTb tāvatya evāṇimādibhuvanāṣṭakameva ca  
AbhTa atattve tattvabuddhyā yaḥ santoṣastuṣṭiratra sā 
AbhTb heyepyādeyadhīḥ siddhiḥ tathā coktaṃ hi kāpilaiḥ  
AbhTa ādhyātmikāścatasraḥ prakṛtyupādānakālabhāgyākhyāḥ 
AbhTb pañca viṣayoparamatorjanarakṣāsaṅgasaṃkṣayavighātaiḥ  
AbhTa ūhaḥ śabdodhyayanaṃ duḥkhavighātāstrayaḥ suhṛtprāptiḥ 
AbhTb dānaṃ ca siddhayoṣṭau siddheḥ pūrvoṅkuśastrividhaḥ  
AbhTa aṇimādyūrdhvatastisraḥ paṅktayo guruśiṣyagāḥ 
AbhTb tatrāpi triguṇacchāyāyogāt tritvamudāhṛtam  
AbhTa nāḍīvidyāṣṭakaṃ cordhvaṃ paṅktīnāṃ syādiḍādikam 
AbhTb puṃsi nādamayī śaktiḥ prasarākhyā ca yatsthitā  
AbhTa na hyakartā pumānkartuḥ kāraṇatvaṃ ca saṃsthitam 
AbhTb akartaryapi vā puṃsi sahakāritayā sthite  
AbhTa śeṣakāryātmataiṣṭavyānyathā satkāryahānitaḥ 
AbhTb tasmāttathāvidhe kārye yā śaktiḥ puruṣasya sā  
AbhTa tāvanti rūpāṇyādāya pūrṇatāmadhigacchati 
AbhTb nāḍyaṣṭakordhve kathitaṃ vigrahāṣṭakamucyate  
AbhTa kāryaṃ heturduḥkhaṃ sukhaṃ ca vijñānasādhyakaraṇāni 
AbhTb sādhanamiti vigrahatāyugaṣṭakaṃ bhavati puṃstattve  
AbhTa bhuvanaṃ dehadharmāṇāṃ daśānāṃ vigrahāṣṭakāt 
AbhTb ahiṃsā satyamasteyaṃ brahmākalkākrudho guroḥ  
AbhTa śuśrūṣāśaucasantoṣā ṛjuteti daśoditāḥ 
AbhTb puṃstattva eva gandhāntaṃ sthitaṃ ṣoḍaśakaṃ punaḥ  
AbhTa ārabhya dehapāśākhyaṃ puraṃ buddhiguṇāstataḥ 
AbhTb tatraivāṣṭāvahaṃkārastridhā kāmādikāstathā  
AbhTa pāśā āgantukagāṇeśavaidyeśvarabheditāḥ 
AbhTb trividhāste sthitāḥ puṃsi mokṣamārgoparodhakāḥ  
AbhTa yatkiṃcitparamādvaitasaṃvitsvātantryasundarāt 
AbhTb parācchivāduktarūpādanyattatpāśa ucyate  
AbhTa tadevaṃ puṃstvamāpanne pūrṇepi parameśvare 
AbhTb tatsvarūpāparijñānaṃ citraṃ hi puruṣāstataḥ  
AbhTa uktānuktāstu ye pāśāḥ paratantroktalakṣaṇāḥ 
AbhTb te puṃsi sarve tāṃstatra śodhayanmucyate bhavāt  
AbhTa puṃsa ūrdhva tu niyatistatrasthāḥ śaṃkarā daśa 
AbhTb hemābhāḥ susitāḥ kālatattve tu daśa te śivāḥ  
AbhTa koṭiḥ ṣoḍaśasāhasraṃ pratyekaṃ parivāriṇaḥ 
AbhTb rāge vīreśabhuvanaṃ gurvantevāsināṃ puram  
AbhTa puraṃ cāśuddhavidyāyāṃ syācchaktinavakojjvalam 
AbhTb manonmanyantagāstāśca vāmādyāḥ parikīrtitāḥ  
AbhTa kalāyāṃ syānmahādevatrayasya puramuttamam 
AbhTb tato māyā tripuṭikā mukhyatonantakoṭibhiḥ  
AbhTa ākrāntā sā bhagabilaiḥ proktaṃ śaivyāṃ tanau punaḥ 
AbhTb aṅguṣṭhamātraparyantaṃ mahādevāṣṭakaṃ niśi  
AbhTa cakrāṣṭakādhipatyena tathā śrīmālinīmate 
AbhTb vāmādyāḥ puruṣādau ye proktāḥ śrīpūrvaśāsane  
AbhTa te māyātattva evoktāstanau śaivyāmanantataḥ 
AbhTb kapālavratinaḥ svāṅgahotāraḥ kaṣṭatāpasāḥ  
AbhTa sarvābhayāḥ khaḍgadhārāvratāstattattvavedinaḥ 
AbhTb kramāttattattvamāyānti yatreśonanta ucyate  
AbhTa uktaṃ ca tasya parataḥ sthānamanantādhipasya devasya 
AbhTb sthitivilayasargakarturguhābhagadvārapālasya  
AbhTa dharmānaṇimādiguṇāñjñānāni tapaḥsukhāni yogāṃśca 
AbhTb māyābilātpradatte puṃsāṃ niṣkṛṣya niṣkṛṣya  
AbhTa tacchaktīddhasvabalā guhādhikārāndhakāraguṇadīpāḥ 
AbhTb sarvenantapramukhā dīpyante śatabhavapramukhāntāḥ  
AbhTa sovyaktamadhiṣṭhāya prakaroti jaganniyogataḥ śambhoḥ 
AbhTb śuddhāśuddhasrotodhikārahetuḥ śivo yasmāt  
AbhTa śivaguṇayoge tasmin mahati pade ye pratiṣṭhitāḥ prathamam 
AbhTb tenantāderjagataḥ sargasthitivilayakartāraḥ  
AbhTa māyābilamidamuktaṃ paratastu guhā jagadyoniḥ 
AbhTb utpattyā teṣvasyāḥ patiśaktikṣobhamanuvidhīyamāneṣu  
AbhTa yonivivareṣu nānākāmasamṛddheṣu bhagasaṃjñā 
AbhTb kāmayate patirenāmicchānuvidhāyinīṃ yadā devīm  
AbhTa pratibhagamavyaktādyāḥ prajāstadāsyāḥ prajāyante 
AbhTb teṣāmatisūkṣmāṇāmetāvattvaṃ na varṇyate vidhiṣu  
AbhTa avavarakāṇyekasminyadvatsāle bahūni baddhāni 
AbhTb yonibilānyekasmiṃstadvanmāyāśiraḥsāle  
AbhTa māyāpaṭalaiḥ sūkṣmaiḥ kuḍyaiḥ pihitāḥ parasparamadṛśyāḥ 
AbhTb nivasanti tatra rudrāḥ sukhinaḥ pratibilamasaṃkhyātāḥ  
AbhTa sthāne sāyujyagatāḥ sāmīpyagatāḥ pare salokasthāḥ 
AbhTb pratibhuvanamevamayaṃ nivāsināṃ gurubhiruddiṣṭaḥ  
AbhTa api sarvasiddhavācaḥ kṣīyerandīrghakālamudgīrṇāḥ 
AbhTb na punaryonyānantyāducyante srotasāṃ saṃkhyāḥ  
AbhTa tasmānnirayādyekaṃ yatproktaṃ dvārapālaparyantam 
AbhTb srotastenānyānyapi tulyavidhānāni vedyāni  
AbhTa avyaktakale guhayā prakṛtikalābhyāṃ vikāra ātmīyaḥ 
AbhTb otaḥ proto vyāptaḥ kalitaḥ pūrṇaḥ parikṣiptaḥ  
AbhTa madhye puṭatrayaṃ tasyā rudrāḥ ṣaḍadharentare 
AbhTb eka ūrdhve ca pañceti dvādaśaite nirūpitāḥ  
AbhTa gahanāsādhyau hariharadaśeśvarau trikalagopatī ṣaḍime 
AbhTb madhyenantaḥ kṣemo dvijeśavidyeśaviśvaśivāḥ  
AbhTa iti pañca teṣu pañcasu ṣaṭsu ca puṭageṣu tatparāvṛttyā 
AbhTb parivarttate sthitiḥ kila devonantastu sarvathā madhye  
AbhTa ūrdhvādharagakapālakapuṭaṣaṭkayugena tatparāvṛttyā 
AbhTb madhyatoṣṭābhirdiksthairvyāpto granthirmataṅgaśāstroktaḥ  
AbhTa śrīsāraśāsane punareṣā ṣaṭpuṭatayā vinirdiṣṭā 
AbhTb granthyākhyamidaṃ tattvaṃ māyākāryaṃ tato māyā  
AbhTa māyātattvaṃ vibhu kila gahanamarūpaṃ samastavilayapadam 
AbhTb tatra na bhuvanavibhāgo yukto granthāvasau tasmāt  
AbhTa māyātattvādhipatiḥ sonantaḥ samuditānvicāryāṇūn 
AbhTb yugapatkṣobhayati niśāṃ sā sūte saṃpuṭairanantaiḥ svaiḥ  
AbhTa tena kalādidharāntaṃ yaduktamāvaraṇajālamakhilaṃ tat 
AbhTb niḥsaṃkhyaṃ ca vicitraṃ māyaivaikā tvabhinneyam  
AbhTa uktaṃ śrīpūrvaśāstre ca dharāvyaktātmakaṃ dvayam 
AbhTb asaṃkhyātaṃ niśāśaktisaṃjñaṃ tvekasvarūpakam  
AbhTa pāśāḥ puroktāḥ praṇavāḥ pañcamānāṣṭakaṃ muneḥ 
AbhTb kulaṃ yoniśca vāgīśī yasyāṃ jāto na jāyate  
AbhTa dīkṣākāledharādhvasthaśuddhau yaccādharādhvagam 
AbhTb anantasya samīpe tu tatsarvaṃ pariniṣṭhitam  
AbhTa sādhyo dātā damano dhyāno bhasmeti bindavaḥ pañca 
AbhTb pañcārthaguhyarudrāṅkuśahṛdayalakṣaṇaṃ ca savyūham  
AbhTa ākarṣādarśau cetyaṣṭakametatpramāṇānām 
AbhTb aluptavibhavāḥ sarve māyātattvādhikāriṇaḥ  
AbhTa māyāmayaśarīrāste bhogaṃ svaṃ paribhuñjate 
AbhTb pralayānte hyanantena saṃhṛtāste tvaharmukhe  
AbhTa anyānantaprasādena vibudhā api taṃ param 
AbhTb suptabuddhaṃ manyamānāḥ svatantrammanyatājaḍāḥ  
AbhTa svātmānameva jānanti hetuṃ māyāntarālagāḥ 
AbhTb ataḥ paraṃ sthitā māyā devī jantuvimohinī  
AbhTa devadevasya sā śaktiratidurghaṭakāritā 
AbhTb nirvairaparipanthinyā tayā bhramitabuddhayaḥ  
AbhTa idaṃ tattvamidaṃ neti vivadantīha vādinaḥ 
AbhTb gurudevāgniśāstreṣu ye na bhaktā narādhamāḥ  
AbhTa satpathaṃ tānparityājya sotpathaṃ nayati dhruvam 
AbhTb asadyuktivicārajñāñchuṣkatarkāvalambinaḥ  
AbhTa bhramayatyeva tānmāyā hyamokṣe mokṣalipsayā 
AbhTb śivadīkṣāsinā cchinnā śivajñānāsinā tathā  
AbhTa na prarohetpunarnānyo hetustacchedanaṃ prati 
AbhTb mahāmāyordhvataḥ śuddhā mahāvidyātha mātṛkā  
AbhTa vāgīśvarī ca tatrasthaṃ vāmādinavasatpuram 
AbhTb vāmā jyeṣṭhā raudrī kālī kalavikaraṇībalavikārike tathā  
AbhTa mathanī damanī manonmanī ca tridṛśaḥ pītāḥ samastāstāḥ 
AbhTb saptakoṭyo mukhyamantrā vidyātattvetra saṃsthitāḥ  
AbhTa ekaikārbudalakṣāṃśāḥ padmākārapurā iha 
AbhTb vidyārājñyastriguṇyādyāḥ sapta saptārbudeśvarāḥ  
AbhTa vidyātattvordhvamaiśaṃ tu tattvaṃ tatra kramordhvagam 
AbhTb śikhaṇḍyādyamanantāntaṃ purāṣṭakayutaṃ puram  
AbhTa śikhaṇḍī śrīgalo mūrtirekanetraikarudrakau 
AbhTb śivottamaḥ sūkṣmarudronanto vidyeśvarāṣṭakam  
AbhTa kramādūrdhvordhvasaṃsthānaṃ saptānāṃ nāyako vibhuḥ 
AbhTb ananta eva dhyeyaśca pūjyaścāpyuttarottaraḥ  
AbhTa mukhyamantreśvarāṇāṃ yat sārdhaṃ koṭitrayaṃ sthitam 
AbhTb tannāyakā ime tena vidyeśāścakravartinaḥ  
AbhTa uktaṃ ca gurubhiritthaṃ śivatanvādyeṣu śāsaneṣvetat 
AbhTb bhagabilaśatakalitaguhāmūrdhāsanagoṣṭaśaktiyugdevaḥ  
AbhTa gahanādyaṃ nirayāntaṃ sṛjati ca rudrāṃśca viniyuṅkte 
AbhTb uddharati manonmanyā puṃsasteṣveva bhavati madhyasthaḥ  
AbhTa te tenodastacitaḥ paratattvālocanebhiniviśante 
AbhTb sa punaradhaḥ pathavartiṣvadhikṛta evāṇuṣu śivena  
AbhTa avasitapativiniyogaḥ sārdhamanekātmamantrakoṭībhiḥ 
AbhTb nirvātyanantanāthastaddhāmāviśati sūkṣmarudrastu  
AbhTa anugṛhyāṇumapūrvaṃ sthāpayati patiḥ śikhaṇḍinaḥ sthāne 
AbhTb ityaṣṭau paripāṭyā yāvaddhāmāni yāti gururekaḥ  
AbhTa tāvadasaṃkhyātānāṃ jantūnāṃ nirvṛtiṃ kurute 
AbhTb teṣṭāvapi śaktyaṣṭakayogāmalajalaruhāsanāsīnāḥ  
AbhTa ālokayanti devaṃ hṛdayasthaṃ kāraṇaṃ paramam 
AbhTb taṃ bhagavantamanantaṃ dhyāyantaḥ svahṛdi kāraṇaṃ śāntam  
AbhTa saptānudhyāyantyapi mantrāṇāṃ koṭayaḥ śuddhāḥ 
AbhTb māyādiravīcyanto bhavastvanantādirucyatepyabhavaḥ  
AbhTa śivaśuddhaguṇādhīkārāntaḥ sopyeṣa heyaśca 
AbhTb atrāpi yato dṛṣṭānugrāhyāṇāṃ niyojyatā śaivī  
AbhTa iṣṭā ca tannivṛttirhyabhavastvadhare na bhūyate yasmāt 
AbhTb patyurapasarpati yataḥ kāraṇatā kāryatā ca siddhebhyaḥ  
AbhTa kañcukavacchivasiddhau tāvatibhavasaṃjñayātimadhyasthau 
AbhTb dharmajñānavirāgaiśyacatuṣṭayapuraṃ tu yat  
AbhTa rūpāvaraṇasaṃjñaṃ tattattvesminnaiśvare viduḥ 
AbhTb vāmā jyeṣṭhā ca raudrīti bhuvanatrayaśobhitam  
AbhTa sūkṣmāvaraṇamākhyātamīśatattve gurūttamaiḥ 
AbhTb aiśātsādāśivaṃ jñānakriyāyugalamaṇḍitam  
AbhTa śuddhāvaraṇamityāhuruktā śuddhāvṛteḥ param 
AbhTb vidyāvṛtistato bhāvābhāvaśaktidvayojjvalā  
AbhTa śaktyāvṛtiḥ pramāṇākhyā tataḥ śāstre nirūpitā 
AbhTb śaktyāvṛtestu tejasvidhruveśābhyāmalaṅkṛtam  
AbhTa tejasvyāvaraṇaṃ vedapurā mānāvṛtistataḥ 
AbhTb mānāvṛteḥ suśuddhāvṛtpuratritayaśobhitā  
AbhTa suśuddhāvaraṇādūrdhva śaivamekapuraṃ bhavet 
AbhTb śivāvṛterūrdhvamāhurmokṣāvaraṇasaṃjñitam  
AbhTa asyāṃ mokṣāvṛtau rudrā ekādaśa nirūpitāḥ 
AbhTb mokṣāvaraṇatastvekapuramāvaraṇaṃ dhruvam  
AbhTa ūrdhve dhruvāvṛtericchāvaraṇaṃ tatra te śivāḥ 
AbhTb īśvarecchāgṛhāntasthāstatpuraṃ caikamucyate  
AbhTa icchāvṛteḥ prabuddhākhyaṃ digrudrāṣṭakacarcitam 
AbhTb prabuddhāvaraṇādūrdhva samayāvaraṇaṃ mahat  
AbhTa bhuvanaiḥ pañcabhirgarbhīkṛtānantasamāvṛti 
AbhTb sāmayātsauśivaṃ tatra sādākhyaṃ bhuvanaṃ mahat  
AbhTa tasminsadāśivo devastasya savyāpasavyayoḥ 
AbhTb jñānakriye parecchā tu śaktirutsaṅgagāminī  
AbhTa sṛṣṭyādipañcakṛtyāni kurute sa tayecchayā 
AbhTb pañca brahmāṇyaṅgaṣaṭkaṃ sakalādyaṣṭakaṃ śivāḥ  
AbhTa daśāṣṭādaśa rudrāśca taireva suśivo vṛtaḥ 
AbhTb sadyo vāmāghorau puruṣeśau brahmapañcakaṃ hṛdayam  
AbhTa mūrdhaśikhāvarmadṛgastramaṅgāni ṣaṭ prāhuḥ 
AbhTb sakalākalaśūnyaiḥ saha kalāḍhyakhamalaṅkṛte kṣapaṇamantyam  
AbhTa kaṇṭhyauṣṭhyamaṣṭamaṃ kila sakalāṣṭakametadāmnātam 
AbhTb oṃ kāraśivau dīpto hetvīśadaśeśakau suśivakālau  
AbhTa sūkṣmasutejaḥśarvāḥ śivāḥ daśaitetra pūrvādeḥ 
AbhTb vijayo niḥśvāsaśca svāyambhuvo vahnivīrarauravakāḥ  
AbhTa mukuṭavisarenduvinduprodgītā lalitasiddharudrau ca 
AbhTb santānaśivau parakiraṇapārameśā iti smṛtā rudrāḥ  
AbhTa sarveṣāmeteṣāṃ jñānāni viduḥ svatulyanāmāni 
AbhTb mantramunikoṭiparivṛta matha vibhuvāmādirudratacchaktiyutam  
AbhTa tārādiśaktijuṣṭaṃ suśivāsanamatisitakajamasaṃkhyadalam 
AbhTb yaḥ śaktirudravargaḥ parivāre viṣṭare ca suśivasya  
AbhTa pratyekamasya nijanijaparivāre parārdhakoṭayosaṃkhyāḥ 
AbhTb māyāmalanirmuktāḥ kevalamadhikāramātrasaṃrūḍhāḥ  
AbhTa suśivāvaraṇe rudrāḥ sarvajñāḥ sarvaśaktisampūrṇāḥ 
AbhTb adhikārabandhavilaye śāntāḥ śivarūpiṇo punarbhavinaḥ  
AbhTa ūrdhve bindvāvṛtirdīptā tatra tatra padmaṃ śaśiprabham 
AbhTb śāntyatītaḥ śivastatra tacchaktyutsaṅgabhūṣitaḥ  
AbhTa nivṛttyādikalāvargaparivārasamāvṛtaḥ 
AbhTb asaṃkhyarudratacchaktipurakoṭibhirāvṛtaḥ  
AbhTa śrīmanmataṅgaśāstre ca layākhyaṃ tattvamuttamam 
AbhTb pāribhāṣikamityetannāmnā bindurihocyate  
AbhTa caturmūrtimayaṃ śubhraṃ yattatsakalaniṣkalam 
AbhTb tasminbhogaḥ samuddiṣṭa ityatredaṃ ca varṇitam  
AbhTa nivṛttyādeḥ susūkṣmatvāddharādyārabdhadehatā 
AbhTb mātuḥ sphūrjanmahājñānalīnatvānna vibhāvyate  
AbhTa udrikta taijasatvena hemno bhūparamāṇavaḥ 
AbhTb yathā pṛthaṅna bhāntyevamūrdhvādhorudradehagāḥ  
AbhTa bindūrdhverdhenduretasya kalā jyotsnā ca tadvatī 
AbhTb kāntiḥ prabhā ca vimalā pañcaitā rodhikāstataḥ  
AbhTa rundhanī rodhanī roddhrī jñānabodhā tamopahā 
AbhTb etāḥ pañca kalāḥ prāhurnirodhinyāṃ gurūttamāh  
AbhTa ardhamātraḥ smṛto bindurvyomarūpī catuṣkalaḥ 
AbhTb tadardhamardhacandrastadaṣṭāṃśena nirodhikā  
AbhTa hetūnbrahmādikān runddhe rodhikāṃ tāṃ tyajettataḥ 
AbhTb nirodhikāmimāṃ bhittvā sādākhyaṃ bhuvanaṃ param  
AbhTa pararūpeṇa yatrāste pañcamantramahātanuḥ 
AbhTb ityardhendunirodhyantabindvāvṛtyūrdhvato mahān  
AbhTa nādaḥ kiñjalkasadṛśo mahadbhiḥ puruṣairvṛtaḥ 
AbhTb catvāri bhuvanānyatra dikṣu madhye ca pañcamam  
AbhTa indhikā dīpikā caiva rodhikā mocikordhvagā 
AbhTb madhyetra padmaṃ tatrordhvagāmī tacchaktibhirvṛtaḥ  
AbhTa nādordhvatastu sauṣumnaṃ tatra tacchaktibhṛtprabhuḥ 
AbhTb tadīśaḥ piṅgalelābhyāṃ vṛtaḥ savyāpasavyayoḥ  
AbhTa yā prabhoraṅkagā devī suṣumnā śaśisaprabhā 
AbhTb grathitodhvā tayā sarva ūrdhvaścādhastanastathā  
AbhTa nādaḥsuṣumnādhārastu bhittvā viśvamidaṃ jagat 
AbhTb adhaḥśaktyā vinirgacchedūrdhvaśaktyā ca mūrdhataḥ  
AbhTa nāḍyā brahmabile līnaḥ sovyaktadhvanirakṣaraḥ 
AbhTb nadansarveṣu bhūteṣu śivaśaktyā hyadhiṣṭhitaḥ  
AbhTa suṣumnordhve brahmabilasaṃjñayāvaraṇaṃ tridṛk 
AbhTb tatra brahmā sitaḥ śūlī pañcāsyaḥ śaśiśekharaḥ  
AbhTa tasyotsaṅge parā devī brahmāṇī mokṣamārgagā 
AbhTb roddhrī dātrī ca mokṣasya tāṃ bhittvā cordhvakuṇḍalī  
AbhTa śaktiḥ suptāhisadṛśī sā viśvādhāra ucyate 
AbhTb tasyāṃ sūkṣmā susūkṣmā ca tathānye amṛtāmite  
AbhTa madhyato vyāpinī tasyāṃ vyāpīśo vyāpinīdharaḥ 
AbhTb śaktitattvamidaṃ yasya prapañcoyaṃ dharāntakaḥ  
AbhTa śivatattvaṃ tatastatra caturdikkaṃ vyavasthitāḥ 
AbhTb vyāpī vyomātmakonantonāthastacchaktibhāginaḥ  
AbhTa madhye tvanāśritaṃ tatra devadevo hyanāśritaḥ 
AbhTb tacchaktyutsaṅgabhṛtsūryaśatakoṭisamaprabhaḥ  
AbhTa śivatattvordhvataḥ śaktiḥ parā sā samanāhvayā 
AbhTb sarveṣāṃ kāraṇānāṃ sā kartṛbhūtā vyavasthitā  
AbhTa bibhartyaṇḍānyanekāni śivena samadhiṣṭhitā 
AbhTb tadārūḍhaḥ śivaḥ kṛtyapañcakaṃ kurute prabhuḥ  
AbhTa samanā karaṇaṃ tasya hetukarturmahośituḥ 
AbhTb anāśritaṃ tu vyāpāre nimittaṃ heturucyate  
AbhTa tayādhitiṣṭhati vibhuḥ kāraṇānāṃ tu pañcakam 
AbhTb anāśritonāthamayamanantaṃ khavapuḥ sadā  
AbhTa sa vyāpinaṃ prerayati svaśaktyā karaṇena tu 
AbhTb karmarūpā sthitā māyā yadadhaḥ śaktikuṇḍalī  
AbhTa nādabindvādikaṃ kāryamityādijagadudbhavaḥ 
AbhTb yatsadāśivaparyantaṃ pārthivādyaṃ ca śāsane  
AbhTa tatsarva prākṛtaṃ proktaṃ vināśotpattisaṃyutam 
AbhTb atha sakalabhuvanamānaṃ yanmahyaṃ nigaditaṃ nijairgurubhiḥ  
AbhTa tadvakṣyate samāsādbuddhau yenāśu saṅkrāmet 
AbhTb aṇḍasyāntaranantaḥ kālaḥ kūṣmāṇḍahāṭakau brahmaharī  
AbhTa rudrāḥ śataṃ savīraṃ bahirnivṛttistu sāṣṭaśatabhuvanā syāt 
AbhTb jalatejaḥsamīranabhohaṃkṛddhīmūlasaptake pratyekam  
AbhTa aṣṭau ṣaṭpañcāśadbhuvanā tena pratiṣṭheti kalā kathitā 
AbhTb atra prāhuḥ śodhyānaṣṭau kecinnijāṣṭakādhipatīn  
AbhTa anye tu samastānāṃ śodhyatvaṃ varṇayanti bhuvanānām 
AbhTb śrībhūtirājamiśrā guravaḥ prāhuḥ punarbahī rudraśatam  
AbhTa aṣṭāvantaḥ sākaṃ śarveṇetīdṛśī nivṛttiriyaṃ syāt 
AbhTb rudrāḥ kālī vīro dharābdhilakṣmyaḥ sarasvatī guhyam  
AbhTa ityaṣṭakaṃ jalenau vahnyatiguhyadvayaṃ maruti vāyoḥ 
AbhTb svapuraṃ gayādi khe ca vyoma pavitrāṣṭakaṃ ca bhuvanayugam  
AbhTa abhimānehaṅkāracchagalādyaṣṭakamathāntarā nabhohaṃkṛt 
AbhTb tanmātrārkenduśratipurāṣṭakaṃ buddhikarmadevānām  
AbhTa daśa tanmātrasamūhe bhuvanaṃ punarakṣavargavinipatite 
AbhTb manasaścetyabhimāne dvāviṃśatireva bhuvanānām  
AbhTa dhiyi daivīnāmaṣṭau kruttejoyogasaṃjñakaṃ trayaṃ tadumā 
AbhTb tatpatiratha mūrtyaṣṭakasuśivadvādaśakavīrabhadrāḥ syuḥ  
AbhTa tadatha mahādevāṣṭakamiti buddhau saptadaśa saṃkhyā 
AbhTb guṇatattve paṅktitrayamiti ṣaṭpañcāśataṃ purāṇi viduḥ  
AbhTa yadyapi guṇasāmyātmani mūle krodheśvarāṣṭakaṃ tathāpi dhiyi 
AbhTb tacchodhitamiti gaṇanāṃ na punaḥ prāptaṃ pratiṣṭhāyām  
AbhTa iti jalatattvānmūlaṃ tattvacaturviṃśatiḥ pratiṣṭhāyām 
AbhTb ambādituṣṭivargastārādyāḥ siddhayoṇimādigaṇaḥ  
AbhTa guravo guruśiṣyā ṛṣivarga iḍādiśca vigrahāṣṭakayuk 
AbhTb gandhādivikārapuraṃ buddhiguṇāṣṭakamahaṃkriyā viṣayaguṇāḥ  
AbhTa kāmādisaptaviṃśakamāgantu tathā gaṇeśavidyeśamayau 
AbhTb iti pāśeṣu puratrayamitthaṃ puruṣetra bhuvanaṣoḍaśakam  
AbhTa niyatau śaṅkaradaśakaṃ kāle śivadaśakamiti puradvitayam 
AbhTb rāge suhṛṣṭabhuvanaṃ guruśiṣyapuraṃ ca vitkalāyugale  
AbhTa bhuvanaṃ bhuvanaṃ niśi puṭapuratrayaṃ vākpuraṃ pramāṇapuram 
AbhTb iti saptaviṃśatipurā vidyā puruṣāditattvasaptakayuk  
AbhTa vāmeśarūpasūkṣmaṃ śuddhaṃ vidyātha śaktitejasvimitiḥ 
AbhTb suviśuddhiśivau mokṣa dhuveṣisaṃbuddhasamayasauśivasaṃjñāḥ  
AbhTa saptadaśapurā śāntā vidyeśasadāśivapuratritayayuktā 
AbhTb bindvardhendunirodhyaḥ parasauśivamindhikādipurasauṣumne  
AbhTa paranādo brahmabilaṃ sūkṣmādiyutordhvakuṇḍalī śaktiḥ 
AbhTb vyāpivyomānantānāthānāśritapurāṇi pañca tataḥ  
AbhTa ṣaṣṭhaṃ ca paramamanāśritamatha samanābhuvanaṣoḍaśī yadi vā 
AbhTb bindvāvaraṇaṃ parasauśivaṃ ca pañcendhikādibhuvanāni  
AbhTa sauṣumnaṃ brahmabilaṃ kuṇḍalinī vyāpipañcakaṃ samanā 
AbhTb iti ṣoḍaśabhuvaneyaṃ tattvayugaṃ śāntyatītā syāt  
AbhTa śrīmanmataṅgaśāstre ca kramoyaṃ purapūgagaḥ 
AbhTb kālāgnirnarakāḥ khābdhiyutaṃ mukhyatayā śatam  
AbhTa kūṣmāṇḍaḥ saptapātālī saptalokī maheśvaraḥ 
AbhTb ityaṇḍamadhyaṃ tadbāhye śataṃ rudrā iti sthitāḥ  
AbhTa sthānānāṃ dviśatī bhūmiḥ saptapañcāśatā yutā 
AbhTb pañcāṣṭakasya madhyāddvātriṃśadbhūtacatuṣṭaye  
AbhTa tanmātreṣu ca pañca syurviśvedevāstatoṣṭakam 
AbhTb pañcamaṃ sendriye garve buddhau devāṣṭakaṃ guṇe  
AbhTa yogāṣṭakaṃ krodhasaṃjñaṃ mūle kāle sanaiyate 
AbhTb patadrugādyāścāṅguṣṭhamātrādyā rāgatattvagāḥ  
AbhTa dvādaśaikaśivādyāḥ syurvidyāyāṃ kalane daśa 
AbhTb vāmādyāstriśatī seyaṃ triparvaṇyabdhirasyayuk  
AbhTa śaivāḥ kecidihānantāḥ śraikaṇṭhā iti saṃgrahaḥ 
AbhTb yatra yadā parabhogān bubhukṣate tatra yojanaṃ kāryam  
AbhTa śodhanamatha taddhānau śeṣaṃ tvantargataṃ kāryam 
AbhTb ityāgamaṃ prathayituṃ darśitametadvikalpitaṃ tena  
AbhTa anyepi bahuvikalpāḥ svadhiyācāryaiḥ samabhyūhyāḥ 
AbhTb śrīpūrvaśāsane punaraṣṭādaśādhikaṃ śataṃ kathitam  
AbhTa tadiha pradhānamadhikaṃ saṃkṣepeṇocyate śodhyam 
AbhTb kālāgniḥ kūṣmāṇḍo narakeśo hāṭakotha bhūtalapaḥ  
AbhTa brahmā munilokeśo rudrāḥ pañcāntarālasthāḥ 
AbhTb adharenantaḥ prācyāḥ kapālivahnyantanirṛtibalākhyāḥ  
AbhTa laghunidhipatividyādhipaśambhūrdhvāntaṃ savīrabhadrapati 
AbhTb ekādaśabhirbāhye brahmāṇḍaṃ pañcabhistathāntarikaiḥ  
AbhTa iti ṣoḍaśapurametannivṛttikalayeha kalanīyam 
AbhTb lakulīśabhārabhūtī diṇḍyāṣāḍhī ca puṣkaranimeṣau  
AbhTa prabhāsasureśāviti salile pratyātmakaṃ saparivāre 
AbhTb bhairavakedāramahākālā madhyāmrajalpākhyāḥ  
AbhTa śrīśailahariścandrāviti guhyāṣṭakamidaṃ mahasi 
AbhTb bhīmendrāṭṭahāsavimalakanakhalanākhalakurusthitigayākhyāḥ  
AbhTa atiguhyāṣṭakametanmaruti ca satanmātrake ca sākṣe ca 
AbhTb sthāṇusuvarṇākhyau kila bhadro gokarṇako mahālayakaḥ  
AbhTa avimuktarudrakoṭī vastrāpada ityadaḥ pavitraṃ khe 
AbhTb sthūlasthūleśaśaṅkuśrutikālañjarāśca maṇḍalabhṛt  
AbhTa mākoṭāṇḍadvitayacchagalāṇḍā aṣṭakaṃ hyahaṅkāre 
AbhTb anyehaṅkārāntastanmātrāṇīndriyāṇi cāpyāhuḥ  
AbhTa dhiyi yonyaṣṭakamuktaṃ prakṛtau yogāṣṭakaṃ kilākṛtaprabhṛti 
AbhTb iti saptāṣṭakabhuvanā pratiṣṭhitiḥ salilato hi mūlāntā  
AbhTa nari vāmo bhīmograu bhaveśavīrāḥ pracaṇḍagaurīśau 
AbhTb ajasānantaikaśivau vidyāyāṃ krodhacaṇḍayugmaṃ syāt  
AbhTa saṃvarto jyotiratho kalāniyatyāṃ ca sūrapañcāntau 
AbhTb vīraśikhīśaśrīkaṇṭhasaṃjñametattrayaṃ ca kāle syāt  
AbhTa samahātejā vāmo bhavodbhavaścaikapiṅgaleśānau 
AbhTb bhuvaneśapuraḥsarakāvaṅguṣṭha ime niśi sthitā hyaṣṭau  
AbhTa aṣṭāviṃśatibhuvanā vidyā puruṣānniśāntamiyam 
AbhTb hālāhalarudrakrudambikāghorikāḥ savāmāḥ syuḥ  
AbhTa vidyāyāṃ vidyeśāstvaṣṭāvīśe sadāśive pañca 
AbhTb vāmā jyeṣṭhā raudrī śaktiḥ sakalā ca śontayam  
AbhTa aṣṭādaśa bhuvanā syāt śāntyatītā tvabhuvanaiva 
AbhTb iti deśādhvavibhāgaḥ kathitaḥ śrīśambhunā samādiṣṭaḥ  
C śrītantrālokasya navamamāhnikam
AbhTb atha tattvapravibhāgo vistarataḥ kathyate kramaprāptaḥ  b
AbhTa yānyuktāni purāṇyamūni vividhaibhadairyadeṣvanvitaṃ rūpaṃ bhāti paraṃ prakāśaniviḍaṃ devaḥ sa ekaḥ śivaḥ 
AbhTb tatsvātantryarasātpunaḥ śivapadādbhede vibhāte paraṃ yadrūpaṃ bahudhānugāmi tadidaṃ tattvaṃ vibhoḥ śāsane  
AbhTa tathāhi kālasadanādvīrabhadrapurāntagam 
AbhTb dhṛtikāṭhinyagarimādyavabhāsāddharātmatā  
AbhTa evaṃ jalāditattveṣu vācyaṃ yāvatsadāśive 
AbhTb svasminkāryetha dharmaughe yadvāpi svasadṛgguṇe  
AbhTa āste sāmānyakalpena tananādvyāptṛbhāvataḥ 
AbhTb tattattvaṃ kramaśaḥ pṛthvīpradhānaṃ puṃśivādayaḥ  
AbhTa dehānāṃ bhuvanānāṃ ca na prasaṅgastato bhavet 
AbhTb śrīmanmataṅgaśāstrādau taduktaṃ parameśinā  
AbhTa tatraiṣāṃ darśyate dṛṣṭaḥ siddhayogīśvarīmate 
AbhTb kāryakāraṇabhāvo yaḥ śivecchāparikalpitaḥ  
AbhTa vastutaḥ sarvabhāvānāṃ karteśānaḥ paraḥ śivaḥ 
AbhTb asvatantrasya kartṛtvaṃ nahi jātūpapadyate  
AbhTa svatantratā ca cinmātravapuṣaḥ parameśituḥ 
AbhTb svatantraṃ ca jaḍaṃ ceti tadanyonyaṃ virudhyate  
AbhTa jāḍyaṃ pramātṛtantratvaṃ svātmasiddhimapi prati 
AbhTb na kartṛtvādṛte cānyat kāraṇatvaṃ hi labhyate  
AbhTa tasminsati hi tadbhāva ityapekṣaikajīvitam 
AbhTb nirapekṣeṣu bhāveṣu svātmaniṣṭhatayā katham  
AbhTa sa pūrvamatha paścātsa iti cetpūrvapaścimau 
AbhTb svabhāvenatiriktau cetsama ityavaśiṣyate  
AbhTa bījamaṅkura ityasmin satattve hetutadvatoḥ 
AbhTb ghaṭaḥ paṭaśceti bhavet kāryakāraṇatā na kim  
AbhTa bījamaṅkurapatrāditayā pariṇameta cet 
AbhTb atatsvabhāvavapuṣaḥ sa svabhāvo na yujyate  
AbhTa sa tatsvabhāva iti cet tarhi bījāṅkurā nije 
AbhTb tāvatyeva na viśrāntau tadanyātyantasaṃbhavāt  
AbhTa tataśca citrākārosau tāvānkaścitprasajyate 
AbhTb astu cet na jaḍenyonyaviruddhākārasaṃbhavaḥ  
AbhTa krameṇa citrākārostu jaḍaḥ kiṃ nu viruddhyate 
AbhTb kramokramo vā bhāvasya na svarūpādhiko bhavet  
AbhTa tathopalambhamātraṃ tau upalambhaśca kiṃ tathā 
AbhTb upalabdhāpi vijñānasvabhāvo yosya sopi hi  
AbhTa kramopalambharūpatvāt krameṇopalabheta cet 
AbhTb tasya tarhi kramaḥ kosau tadanyānupalambhataḥ  
AbhTa svabhāva iti cennāsau svarūpādadhiko bhavet 
AbhTb svarūpānadhikasyāpi kramasya svasvabhāvataḥ  
AbhTa svātantryādbhāsanaṃ syāccet kimanyadbrūmahe vayam 
AbhTb itthaṃ śrīśiva evaikaḥ karteti paribhāṣyate  
AbhTa kartṛtvaṃ caitadetasya tathāmātrāvabhāsanam 
AbhTb tathāvabhāsanaṃ cāsti kāryakāraṇabhāvagam  
AbhTa yathā hi ghaṭasāhityaṃ paṭasyāpyavabhāsate 
AbhTb tathā ghaṭānantaratā kiṃ tu sā niyamojjhitā  
AbhTa ato yanniyamenaiva yasmādābhātyanantaram 
AbhTb tattasya kāraṇaṃ brūmaḥ sati rūpānvayedhike  
AbhTa niyamaśca tathārūpabhāsanāmātrasārakaḥ 
AbhTb bījādaṅkura ityevaṃ bhāsanaṃ nahi sarvadā  
AbhTa yogīcchānantarodbhūtatathābhūtāṅkuro yataḥ 
AbhTb iṣṭe tathāvidhākāre niyamo bhāsate yataḥ  
AbhTa svapne ghaṭapaṭādīnāṃ hetutadvatsvabhāvatā 
AbhTb bhāsate niyamenaiva bādhāśūnyena tāvati  
AbhTa tato yāvati yādrūpyānniyamo bādhavarjitaḥ 
AbhTb bhāti tāvati tādrūpyāddṛḍhahetuphalātmatā  
AbhTa tathābhūte ca niyame hetutadvattvakāriṇi 
AbhTb vastutaścinmayasyaiva hetutā taddhi sarvagam  
AbhTa ata eva ghaṭodbhūtau sāmagrī heturucyate 
AbhTb sāmagrī ca samagrāṇāṃ yadyekaṃ neṣyate vapuḥ  
AbhTa hetubhedānna bhedaḥ syāt phale taccāsamañjasam 
AbhTb yadyasyānuvidhatte tāmanvayavyatirekitām  
AbhTa tattasya hetu cetsoyaṃ kuṇṭhatarko na naḥ priyaḥ 
AbhTb samagrāśca yathā daṇḍasūtracakrakarādayaḥ  
AbhTa dūrāśca bhāvinaścetthaṃ hetutveneti manmahe 
AbhTb yadi tatra bhavenmerurbhaviṣyanvāpi kaścana  
AbhTa na jāyeta ghaṭo nūnaṃ tatpratyūhavyapohitaḥ 
AbhTb yathā ca cakraṃ niyate deśe kāle ca hetutām  
AbhTa yāti karkisumervādyāstadvatsvasthāvadhi sthitāḥ 
AbhTb tathā ca teṣāṃ hetunāṃ saṃyojanaviyojane  
AbhTa niyate śiva evaikaḥ svatantraḥ kartṛtāmiyāt 
AbhTb kumbhakārasya yā saṃvit cakradaṇḍādiyojane  
AbhTa śiva eva hi sā yasmāt saṃvidaḥ kā viśiṣṭatā 
AbhTb kaumbhakārī tu saṃvittiravacchedāvabhāsanāt  
AbhTa bhinnakalpā yadi kṣepyā daṇḍacakrādimadhyataḥ 
AbhTb tasmādekaikanirmāṇe śivo viśvaikavigrahaḥ  
AbhTa karteti puṃsaḥ kartṛtvābhimānopi vibhoḥ kṛtiḥ 
AbhTb ata eva tathābhānaparamārthatayā sthiteḥ  
AbhTa kāryakāraṇabhāvasya loke śāstre ca citratā 
AbhTb māyātovyaktakalayoriti rauravasaṃgrahe  
AbhTa śrīpūrve tu kalātattvādavyaktamiti kathyate 
AbhTb tata eva niśākhyānātkalībhūtādaliṅgakam  
AbhTa iti vyākhyāsmaduktesminsati nyāyetiniṣphalā 
AbhTb loke ca gomayātkīṭāt saṃkalpātsvapnataḥ smṛteḥ  
AbhTa yogīcchāto dravyamantraprabhāvādeśca vṛścikaḥ 
AbhTb anya eva sa cet kāmaṃ kutaścitsvaviśeṣataḥ  
AbhTa sa tu sarvatra tulyastatparāmarśaikyamasti tu 
AbhTb tata eva svarūpepi kramepyanyādṛśī sthitiḥ  
AbhTa śāstreṣu yujyate citrāt tathābhāvasvabhāvataḥ 
AbhTb puṃrāgavitkalākālamāyā jñānottare kramāt  
AbhTa niyatirnāsti vairiñce kalordhve niyatiḥ śratā 
AbhTb puṃrāgavittrayādūrdhvaṃ kalāniyatisaṃpuṭam  
AbhTa kālo māyeti kathitaḥ kramaḥ kiraṇaśāstragaḥ 
AbhTb pumānniyatyā kālaśca rāgavidyākalānvitaḥ  
AbhTa ityeṣa krama uddiṣṭo mātaṅge pārameśvare 
AbhTb kāryakāraṇabhāvīye tattve itthaṃ vyavasthite  
AbhTa śrīpūrvaśāstre kathitāṃ vacmaḥ kāraṇakalpanām 
AbhTb śivaḥ svatantradṛgrūpaḥ pañcaśaktisunirbharaḥ  
AbhTa svātantryabhāsitabhidā pañcadhā pravibhajyate 
AbhTb cidānandeṣaṇājñānakriyāṇāṃ susphuṭatvataḥ  
AbhTa śivaśaktisadeśānavidyākhyaṃ tattvapañcakam 
AbhTb ekaikatrāpi tattvesmin sarvaśaktisunirbhare  
AbhTa tattatprādhānyayogena sa sa bhedo nirūpyate 
AbhTb tathāhi svasvatantratvaparipūrṇatayā vibhuḥ  
AbhTa niḥsaṃkhyairbahubhī rūpairbhātyavacchedavarjanāt 
AbhTb śāṃbhavāḥ śaktijā mantramaheśā mantranāyakāh  
AbhTa mantrā iti viśuddhāḥ syuramī pañca gaṇāḥ kramāt 
AbhTb svasminsvasmin gaṇe bhāti yadyadrūpaṃ samanvayi  
AbhTa tadeṣu tattvamityuktaṃ kālāgnyāderdharādivat 
AbhTb tena yatprāhurākhyānasādṛśyena viḍambitāḥ  
AbhTa gurūpāsāṃ vinaivāttapustakābhīṣṭadṛṣṭayaḥ 
AbhTb brahmā nivṛttyadhipatiḥ pṛthaktattvaṃ na gaṇyate  
AbhTa sadāśivādyāstu pṛthag gaṇyanta iti ko nayaḥ 
AbhTb brahmaviṣṇuhareśānasuśivānāśritātmani  
AbhTa ṣaṭke kāraṇasaṃjñerdhajaratīyamiyaṃ kutaḥ 
AbhTb iti tanmūlato dhvastaṃ gaṇitaṃ nahi kāraṇam  
AbhTa yathā pṛthivyadhipatirnṛpastattvāntaraṃ nahi 
AbhTb tathā tattatkaleśānaḥ pṛthak tattvāntaraṃ katham  
AbhTa tadevaṃ pañcakamidaṃ śuddhodhvā paribhāṣyate 
AbhTb tatra sākṣācchivecchaiva kartryābhāsitabhedikā  
AbhTa īśvarecchāvaśakṣubdhabhogalolikacidgaṇān 
AbhTb saṃvibhaktumaghoreśaḥ sṛjatīha sitetaram  
AbhTa aṇūnāṃ lolikā nāma niṣkarmā yābhilāṣitā 
AbhTb apūrṇaṃmanyatājñānaṃ malaṃ sāvacchidojjhitā  
AbhTa yogyatāmātramevaitadbhāvyavacchedasaṃgrahe 
AbhTb malastenāsya na pṛthaktattvabhāvosti rāgavat  
AbhTa niravacchedakarmāṃśamātrāvacchedatastu sā 
AbhTb rāgaḥ puṃsi dhiyo dharmaḥ karmabhedavicitratā  
AbhTa apūrṇamanyatā ceyaṃ tathārūpāvabhāsanam 
AbhTb svatantrasya śivasyecchā ghaṭarūpo yathā ghaṭaḥ  
AbhTa svātmapracchādanecchaiva vastubhūtastathā malaḥ 
AbhTb yathaivāvyatiriktasya dharāderbhāvitātmatā  
AbhTa tathaivāsyeti śāstreṣu vyatiriktaḥ sthito malaḥ 
AbhTb vyatiriktaḥ svatantrastu na kopi śakaṭādivat  
AbhTa tatsadvitīyā sāśuddhiḥ śivamuktāṇugā na kim 
AbhTb malasya roddhrī kāpyasti śaktiḥ sa cāpyamuktagā  
AbhTa iti nyāyojjhito vādaḥ śraddhāmātraikakalpitaḥ 
AbhTb roddhrī śaktirjaḍasyāsau svayaṃ naiva pravartate  
AbhTa svayaṃ pravṛttau viśvaṃ syāttathā ceśanikā pramā 
AbhTb malasya roddhrīṃ tāṃ śaktimīśaścetsaṃyunakti tat  
AbhTa kīdṛśaṃ pratyaṇumiti praśne nāstyuttaraṃ vacaḥ 
AbhTb malaścāvaraṇaṃ tacca nāvāryasya viśeṣakam  
AbhTa upalambhaṃ vihantyetadghaṭasyeva paṭāvṛtiḥ 
AbhTb malenāvṛtarūpāṇāmaṇūnāṃ yatsatattvakam  
AbhTa śiva eva ca tatpaśyettasyaivāsau malo bhavet 
AbhTb vibhorjñānakriyāmātrasārasyāṇugaṇasya ca  
AbhTa tadabhāvo malo rūpadhvaṃsāyaiva prakalpate 
AbhTb dharmāddharmiṇi yo bhedaḥ samavāyena caikatā  
AbhTa na tadbhavadbhiruditaṃ kaṇabhojanaśiṣyavat 
AbhTb nāmūrtena na mūrtena prāvarītuṃ ca śakyate  
AbhTa jñānaṃ cākṣuṣaraśmīnāṃ tathābhāve saratyapi 
AbhTb sa eva ca malo mūrtaḥ kiṃ jñānena na vedyate  
AbhTa sarvageṇa tataḥ sarvaḥ sarvajñatvaṃ na kiṃ bhajet 
AbhTb yaśca dhvāntātprakāśasyāvṛtistatpratighātibhiḥ  
AbhTa mūrtānāṃ pratighastejoṇūnāṃ nāmūrta īdṛśam 
AbhTb na ca cetanamātmānamasvatantro malaḥ kṣamaḥ  
AbhTa āvarītuṃ na cācyaṃ ca madyāvṛtinidarśanam 
AbhTb uktaṃ bhavadbhirevetthaṃ jaḍaḥ kartā nahi svayam  
AbhTa svatantrasyeśvarasyaitāḥ śaktayaḥ prerikāḥ kila 
AbhTb ataḥ karmavipākajñaprabhuśaktibaleritam  
AbhTa madyaṃ sūte madaṃ duḥkhasukhamohaphalātmakam 
AbhTb na ceśapreritaḥ puṃso mala āvṛṇuyādyataḥ  
AbhTa nirmale puṃsi neśasya prerakatvaṃ tathocitam 
AbhTb tulye nirmalabhāve ca prerayeyurna te katham  
AbhTa tamīśaṃ prati yuktaṃ yad bhūyasāṃ syātsadharmatā 
AbhTb tena svarūpasvātantryamātraṃ malavijṛmbhitam  
AbhTa nirṇītaṃ vitataṃ caitanmayānyatretyalaṃ punaḥ 
AbhTb malobhilāṣaścājñānamavidyā lolikāprathā  
AbhTa bhavadoṣonuplavaśca glāniḥ śoṣo vimūḍhatā 
AbhTb ahaṃmamātmatātaṅko māyāśaktirathāvṛtiḥ  
AbhTa doṣabījaṃ paśutvaṃ ca saṃsārāṅkurakāraṇam 
AbhTb ityādyanvarthasaṃjñābhistatra tatraiṣa bhaṇyate  
AbhTa asmin sati bhavati bhavo duṣṭo bhedātmaneti bhavadoṣaḥ 
AbhTb mañcavadasmin duḥkhasrotoṇūn vahati yatplavastena  
AbhTa śeṣāstu sugamarūpāḥ śabdāstatrārthamūhayeducitam 
AbhTb saṃsārakāraṇaṃ karma saṃsārāṅkura ucyate  
AbhTa caturdaśavidhaṃ bhūtavaiciatryaṃ karmajaṃ yataḥ 
AbhTb ata eva sāṃkhyayogapāñcarātrādiśāsane  
AbhTa ahaṃmameti saṃtyāgo naiṣkarmyāyopadiśyate 
AbhTb niṣkarmā hi sthite mūlamalepyajñānanāmani  
AbhTa vaicitryakāraṇābhāvānnordhva sarati nāpyadhaḥ 
AbhTb kevalaṃ pārimityena śivābhedamasaṃspṛśan  
AbhTa vijñānakevalī proktaḥ śuddhacinmātrasaṃsthitaḥ 
AbhTb sa punaḥ śāṃbhavecchātaḥ śivābhedaṃ parāmṛśan  
AbhTa kramānmantreśatannetṛrūpo yāti śivātmatām 
AbhTb nanu kāraṇametasya karmaṇaścenmalaḥ katham  
AbhTa sa vijñānākalasyāpi na sūte karmasaṃtatim 
AbhTb maivaṃ sa hi malo jñānākale didhvaṃsiṣuḥ katham  
AbhTa hetuḥ syāddhvaṃsamānatvaṃ svātantryādeva codbhavet 
AbhTb didhvaṃsiṣudhvaṃsamānadhvastākhyāsu tisṛṣvatha  
AbhTa daśāsvantaḥ kṛtāvasthāntarāsu svakramasthiteḥ 
AbhTb vijñānākalamantreśatadīśāditvakalpanā  
AbhTa tataśca supte turye ca vakṣyate bahubhedatā 
AbhTb ataḥ pradhvaṃsanaunmukhyakhilībhūtasvaśaktikaḥ  
AbhTa karmaṇo hetutāmetu malaḥ kathamivocyatām 
AbhTb kiṃ ca karmāpi na malādyataḥ karma kriyātmakam  
AbhTa kriyā ca kartṛtārūpāt svātantryānna punarmalāt 
AbhTb yā tvasya karmaṇaścitraphaladatvena karmatā  
AbhTa prasiddhā sā na saṃkocaṃ vinātmani malaśca saḥ 
AbhTb vicitraṃ hi phalaṃ bhinnaṃ bhogyatvenābhimanyate  
AbhTa bhoktaryātmani teneyaṃ bhedarūpā vyavasthitiḥ 
AbhTb iti svakāryaprasave sahakāritvamāśrayan  
AbhTa sāmarthyavyañjakatvena karmaṇaḥ kāraṇaṃ malaḥ 
AbhTb nanvevaṃ karmasadbhāvānmalasyāpi sthiteḥ katham  
AbhTa vijñānākalatā tasya saṃkoco hyasti tādṛśaḥ 
AbhTb maivamadhvastasaṃkocopyasau bhāvanayā dṛḍham  
AbhTa nāhaṃ karteti manvānaḥ karmasaṃskāramujjhati 
AbhTb phaliṣyatīdaṃ karmeti yā dṛḍhā vṛttirātmani  
AbhTa sa saṃskāraḥ phalāyeha na tu smaraṇakāraṇam 
AbhTb apradhvastepi saṃkoce nāhaṃ karteti bhāvanāt  
AbhTa na phalaṃ kṣīvamūḍhādeḥ prāyaścittetha vā kṛte 
AbhTb yanmayādya tapastaptaṃ tadasmai syāditi sphuṭam  
AbhTa abhisaṃdhimataḥ karma na phaledabhisandhitaḥ 
AbhTb tathābhisaṃdhānākhyāṃ tu mānase karma saṃskriyām  
AbhTa phaloparaktāṃ vidadhatkalpate phalasampade 
AbhTb yastu tatrāpi dārḍhyena phalasaṃskāramujjhati  
AbhTa sa tatphalatyāgakṛtaṃ viśiṣṭaṃ phalamaśnute 
AbhTb anayā paripāṭyā yaḥ samastāṃ karmasaṃtatim  
AbhTa anahaṃyutayā projjhet sasaṃkocopi sokalaḥ 
AbhTb nanvitthaṃ duṣkṛtaṃ kiṃcidātmīyamabhisaṃdhitaḥ  
AbhTa parasmai syānna vijñātaṃ bhavatā tāttvikaṃ vacaḥ 
AbhTb tasya bhoktustathā cetsyādabhisaṃdhiryathātmani  
AbhTa tadavaśyaṃ parasyāpi satastadduṣkṛtaṃ bhavet 
AbhTb parābhisaṃdhisaṃvittau svābhisaṃdhirdṛḍhībhavet  
AbhTa abhisaṃdhānavirahe tvasya no phalayogitā 
AbhTb na me duṣkṛtamityeṣā rūḍhistasyāphalāya sā  
AbhTa parābhisandhivicchede svātmanānabhisaṃhitau 
AbhTb dvayorapi phalaṃ na syānnāśahetuvyavasthiteḥ  
AbhTa sukhahetau sukhe cāsya sāmānyādabhisaṃdhitaḥ 
AbhTb nirviśeṣādapi nyāyyā dharmādiphalabhoktṛtā  
AbhTa duḥkhaṃ me duḥkhaheturvā stādityeṣa punarna tu 
AbhTb sāmānyopyabhisaṃdhiḥ syāttadadharmasya nāgamaḥ  
AbhTa prakṛtaṃ brūmahe jñānākalasyoktacarasya yat 
AbhTb anahaṃyutayā sarvā vilīnāḥ karmasaṃskriyāḥ  
AbhTa tasmādasya na karmāsti kasyāpi sahakāritām 
AbhTb malaḥ karotu tenāyaṃ dhvaṃsamānatvamaśnute  
AbhTa apadhvastamalastvantaḥśivāveśavaśīkṛtaḥ 
AbhTb ahaṃbhāvaparopyeti na karmādhīnavṛttitām  
AbhTa uktaṃ śrīpūrvaśāstre ca tadetatparameśinā 
AbhTb malamajñānamicchanti saṃsārāṅkurakāraṇam  
AbhTa dharmādharmātmakaṃ karma sukhaduḥkhādilakṣaṇam 
AbhTb lakṣayetsukhaduḥkhādi svaṃ kārya hetubhāvataḥ  
AbhTa nahi hetuḥ kadāpyāste vinā kārya nijaṃ kvacit 
AbhTb hetutā yogyataivāsau phalānantaryabhāvitā  
AbhTa pūrvakasya tu hetutvaṃ pāramparyeṇa kiṃ ca tat 
AbhTb lakṣyate sukhaduḥkhādyaiḥ samāne dṛṣṭakāraṇe  
AbhTa citrairhetvantaraṃ kiṃcittacca karmeha darśanāt 
AbhTb svāṅge prasādaraukṣyādi jāyamānaṃ svakarmaṇā  
AbhTa dṛṣṭamityanyadehasthaṃ kāraṇaṃ karma kalpyāte 
AbhTb ihāpyanyānyadehasthe sphuṭaṃ karmaphale yataḥ  
AbhTa kṛṣikarma madhau bhogaḥ śaradyanyā ca sā tanuḥ 
AbhTb anusaṃdhāturekasya saṃbhavastu yatastataḥ  
AbhTa tasyaiva tatphalaṃ citraṃ karma yasya purātanam 
AbhTb kṣīvopi rājā sūdaṃ cedādiśetprātarīdṛśam  
AbhTa bhojayetyanusaṃdhānādvinā prāpnoti tatphalam 
AbhTb itthaṃ janmāntaropāttakarmāpyadyānusaṃdhinā  
AbhTa vinā bhuṅkte phalaṃ hetustatra prācyā hyakampatā 
AbhTb ata eva kṛtaṃ karma karmaṇā tapasāpi vā  
AbhTa jñānena vā nirudhyeta phalapākeṣvanunmukham 
AbhTb ārabdhakāryaṃ dehesmin yatpunaḥ karma tatkatham  
AbhTa ucchidyatāmantyadaśaṃ niroddhuṃ nahi śakyate 
AbhTb tatraiva dehe yattvanyadadyagaṃ vā purātanam  
AbhTa karma tajjñānadīkṣādyaiḥ śaṇḍhīkartuṃ prasahyate 
AbhTb tathā saṃskāradārḍhya hi phalāya dṛḍhatā punaḥ  
AbhTa yadā yadā vinaśyeta karmadhvastaṃ tadā tadā 
AbhTb ato mohaparādhīno yadyapyakṛta kiṃcana  
AbhTa tathāpi jñānakāle tatsarvameva pradahyate 
AbhTb uktaṃ ca śrīparehānādānaḥ sarvadṛgulvaṇaḥ  
AbhTa muhūrtānnirdahetsarva dehasthamakṛtaṃ kṛtam 
AbhTb dehasthamiti dehena saha tādātmyamāśritā  
AbhTa svācchandyātsaṃvidevoktā tatrasthaṃ karma dahyate 
AbhTb dehaikyavāsanātyāgāt sa ca viśvātmatāsthiteḥ  
AbhTa akālakalite vyāpinyabhinne yā hi saṃskriyā 
AbhTb saṃkoca eva sānena sopi dehaikatāmayaḥ  
AbhTa etatkārmamalaṃ proktaṃ yena sākaṃ layākalāḥ 
AbhTb syurguhāgahanāntaḥsthāḥ suptā iva sarīsṛpāḥ  
AbhTa tataḥ prabuddhasaṃskārāste yathocitabhāginaḥ 
AbhTb brahmādisthāvarāntesmin saṃsranti punaḥ punaḥ  
AbhTa ye punaḥ karmasaṃskārahānyai prārabdhabhāvanāḥ 
AbhTb bhāvanāpariniṣpattimaprāpya pralayaṃ gatāḥ  
AbhTa mahāntaṃ te tathāntaḥsthabhāvanāpākasauṣṭhavāt 
AbhTb mantratvaṃ pratipadyante citrāccitraṃ ca karmataḥ  
AbhTa asya kārmamalasyeyanmāyāntādhvavisāriṇaḥ 
AbhTb pradhānaṃ kāraṇaṃ proktamajñānātmāṇavo malaḥ  
AbhTa kṣobhosya lolikākhyasya sahakāritayā sphuṭam 
AbhTb tiṣṭhāsāyogyataunmukhyamīśvarecchāvaśācca tat  
AbhTa na jaḍaścidadhiṣṭhānaṃ vinā kvāpi kṣamo yataḥ 
AbhTb aṇavo nāma naivānyatprakāśātmā maheśvaraḥ  
AbhTa cidacidrūpatābhāsī pudgalaḥ kṣetravitpaśuḥ 
AbhTb cidrūpatvācca sa vyāpī nirguṇo niṣkriyastataḥ  
AbhTa yogopāyepsako nityo mūrtivandhyaḥ prabhāṣyate 
AbhTb acittvādajñatā bhedo bhogyādbhoktrantarādatha  
AbhTa teṣāmaṇūnāṃ sa mala īśvarecchāvaśādbhṛśam 
AbhTb prabudhyate tathā coktaṃ śāstre śrīpūrvanāmani  
AbhTa īśvarecchāvaśādasya bhogecchā saṃprajāyate 
AbhTb bhogecchorupakārārthamādyo mantramaheśvaraḥ  
AbhTa māyāṃ vikṣobhya saṃsāraṃ nirmimīte vicitrakam 
AbhTb māyā ca nāma devasya śaktiravyatirekiṇī  
AbhTa bhedāvabhāsasvātantryaṃ tathāhi sa tayā kṛtaḥ 
AbhTb ādyo bhedāvabhāso yo vibhāgamanupeyivān  
AbhTa garbhīkṛtānantabhāvivibhāsā sā parā niśā 
AbhTb sā jaḍā bhedarūpatvāt kāryaṃ cāsyā jaḍaṃ yataḥ  
AbhTa vyāpinī viśvahetutvāt sūkṣmā kāryaikakalpanāt 
AbhTb śivaśaktyavinābhāvānnityaikā mūlakāraṇam  
AbhTa acetanamanekātma sarva kārya yathā ghaṭaḥ 
AbhTb pradhānaṃ ca tathā tasmāt kārya nātmā tu cetanaḥ  
AbhTa ata evādhvani proktā pūrvaṃ māyā dvidhā sthitā 
AbhTb yathā ca māyā devasya śaktirabhyeti bhedinam  
AbhTa tattvabhāvaṃ tathānyopi kalādistattvavistaraḥ 
AbhTb niruddhaśakteryā kiṃcitkartṛtodvalanātmikā  
AbhTa nāthasya śaktiḥ sādhastātpuṃsaḥ kṣeptrī kalocyate 
AbhTb evaṃ vidyādayopyete dharāntāḥ paramārthataḥ  
AbhTa śivaśaktimayā eva proktanyāyānusārataḥ 
AbhTb tathāpi yatpṛthagbhānaṃ kalāderīśvarecchayā  
AbhTa tato jaḍatve kāryatve pṛthaktattvasthitau dhruvam 
AbhTb upādānaṃ smṛtā māyā kvacittatkāryameva ca  
AbhTa tathāvabhāsacitraṃ ca rūpamanyonyavarjitam 
AbhTb yadbhāti kila saṃkalpe tadasti ghaṭavadvahiḥ  
AbhTa khapuṣpādyastitāṃ brūmastato na vyabhicāritā 
AbhTb khapuṣpaṃ kāladiṅmātṛsāpekṣaṃ nāstiśabdataḥ  
AbhTa dharādivat tathātyantābhāvopyevaṃ vivicyatām 
AbhTb yatsaṃkalpyaṃ tathā tasya bahirdehosti cetanaḥ  
AbhTa caitravatsauśivāntaṃ tat sarva tādṛśadehavat 
AbhTb yasya deho yathā tasya tajjātīyaṃ puraṃ bahiḥ  
AbhTa ataḥ suśivaparyantā siddhā bhuvanapaddhatiḥ 
AbhTb ātmanām tatpuraṃ prāpyaṃ deśatvādanyadeśavat  
AbhTa ātmanāmadhvabhoktṛtvaṃ tatoyatnena siddhyati 
AbhTb sā māyā kṣobhamāpannā viśvaṃ sūte samantataḥ  
AbhTa daṇḍāhatevāmalakī phalāni kila yadyapi 
AbhTb tathāpi tu tathā citrapaurvāparyāvabhāsanāt  
AbhTa māyākāryepi tattvaughe kāryakāraṇatā mithaḥ 
AbhTb sā yadyapyanyaśāstreṣu bahudhā dṛśyate sphuṭam  
AbhTa tathāpi mālinīśāstradṛśā tāṃ saṃpracakṣmahe 
AbhTb kalādivasudhāntaṃ yanmāyāntaḥ saṃpracakṣate  
AbhTa pratyātmabhinnamevaitat sukhaduḥkhādibhedataḥ 
AbhTb ekasyāmeva jagati bhogasādhanasaṃhatau  
AbhTa sukhādīnāṃ samaṃ vyakterbhogabhedaḥ kuto bhavet 
AbhTb na cāsau karmabhedena tasyaivānupapattitaḥ  
AbhTa tasmāt kalādiko vargo bhinna eva kadācana 
AbhTb aikyametīśvarecchāto nṛttagītādivādane  
AbhTa eṣāṃ kalāditattvānāṃ sarveṣāmapi bhāvinām 
AbhTb śuddhatvamasti teṣāṃ ye śaktipātapavitritāḥ  
AbhTa kalā hi śuddhā tattādṛk karmatvaṃ saṃprasūyate 
AbhTb mitamapyāśu yenāsmāt saṃsārādeṣa mucyate  
AbhTa rāgavidyākālayatiprakṛtyakṣārthasaṃcayaḥ 
AbhTb itthaṃ śuddha iti procya gururmānastutau vibhuḥ  
AbhTa evameṣā kalādīnāmutpattiḥ pravivicyate 
AbhTb māyātattvāt kalā jātā kiṃcitkartṛtvalakṣaṇā  
AbhTa māyā hi cinmayādbhedaṃ śivādvidadhatī paśoḥ 
AbhTb suṣuptatāmivādhatte tata eva hyadṛkkriyaḥ  
AbhTa kalā hi kiṃcitkartṛtvaṃ sūte svāliṅganādaṇoḥ 
AbhTb tasyāścāpyaṇunānyonyaṃ hyañjane sā prasūyate  
AbhTa sadyonirvāṇadīkṣotthapuṃviśleṣe hi sā satī 
AbhTb śliṣyantyapi ca no sūte tathāpi svaphalaṃ kvacit  
AbhTa ucchūnateva prathamā sūkṣmāṅkurakaleva ca 
AbhTb bījasyāmbvagnimṛtkambutuṣayogāt prasūtikṛt  
AbhTa kalā māyāṇusaṃyogajāpyeṣā nirvikārakam 
AbhTb nāṇuṃ kuryādupādānaṃ kiṃtu māyāṃ vikāriṇīm  
AbhTa malaścāvārako māyā bhāvopādānakāraṇam 
AbhTb karma syāt sahakāryeva sukhaduḥkhodbhavaṃ prati  
AbhTa ataḥ saṃcchannacaitanyasamudbalanakāryakṛt 
AbhTb kalaivānantanāthasya śaktyā saṃpreritā jaḍā  
AbhTa na ceśaśaktirevāsya caitanyaṃ balayiṣyati 
AbhTb tadupodbalitaṃ taddhi na kiṃcitkartṛtāṃ vrajet  
AbhTa seyaṃ kalā na karaṇaṃ mukhyaṃ vidyādikaṃ yathā 
AbhTb puṃsi kartari sā kartrī prayojakatayā yataḥ  
AbhTa alakṣyāntarayoritthaṃ yadā puṃskalayorbhavet 
AbhTb māyāgarbheśaśaktyāderantarajñānamāntaram  
AbhTa tadā māyāpuṃvivekaḥ sarvakarmakṣayādbhavet 
AbhTb vijñānākalatā māyādhastānno yātyadhaḥ pumān  
AbhTa dhīpuṃviveke vijñāte pradhānapuruṣāntare 
AbhTb api na kṣīṇakarmā syāt kalāyāṃ taddhi saṃbhavet  
AbhTa ataḥ sāṃkhyadṛśā siddhaḥ pradhānādho na saṃsaret 
AbhTb kalāpuṃsorviveke tu māyādho naiva gacchati  
AbhTa malādviviktamātmānaṃ paśyaṃstu śivatāṃ vrajet 
AbhTb sarvatra caiśvaraḥ śaktipātotra sahakāraṇam  
AbhTa māyāgarbhādhikārīyo dvayorantye tu nirmalaḥ 
AbhTb seyaṃ kalā kāryabhedādanyaiva hyanumīyate  
AbhTa anyathaikaṃ bhavedviśvaṃ kāryāyetyanyanihnavaḥ 
AbhTb iti mataṅgaśāstrādau yā proktā sā kalā svayam  
AbhTa kiṃcidrūpatayākṣipya kartṛtvamiti bhaṅgitaḥ 
AbhTb kiṃcidrūpaviśiṣṭaṃ yat kartṛtvaṃ tatkathaṃ bhavet  
AbhTa ajñasyeti tataḥ sūte kiṃcijjñatvātmikāṃ vidam 
AbhTb buddhiṃ paśyati sā vidyā buddhidarpaṇacāriṇaḥ  
AbhTa sukhādīn pratyayān mohaprabhṛtīn kāryakāraṇe 
AbhTb karmajālaṃ ca tatrasthaṃ vivinakti nijātmanā  
AbhTa buddhistu guṇasaṃkīrṇā vivekena kathaṃ sukham 
AbhTb duḥkhaṃ mohātmakaṃ vāpi viṣayaṃ darśayedapi  
AbhTa svacchāyāṃ dhiyi saṃkrāmanbhāvaḥ saṃvedyatāṃ katham 
AbhTb tayā vinaiti sāpyanyatkaraṇaṃ puṃsi kartari  
AbhTa nanu cobhayataḥ śubhrādarśadaśīyadhīgatāt 
AbhTb puṃsprakāśādbhāti bhāvaḥ maivaṃ tatpratibimbanam  
AbhTa jaḍameva hi mukhyotha puṃsprakāśosya bhāsanam 
AbhTb bahiḥsthasyaiva tasyāstu buddheḥ kiṃkalpanā kṛtā  
AbhTa abhedabhūmireṣā ca bhedaśceha vicāryate 
AbhTb tasmādbuddhigato bhāvo vidyākaraṇagocaraḥ  
AbhTa bhāvānāṃ pratibimbaṃ ca vedyaṃ dhīkalpanā tataḥ 
AbhTb kiṃcittu kurute tasmānnūnamastyaparaṃ tu tat  
AbhTa rāgatattvamiti proktaṃ yattatraivoparañjakam 
AbhTb na cāvairāgyamātraṃ tattatrāpyāsaktivṛttitaḥ  
AbhTa viraktāvapi tṛptasya sūkṣmarāgavyavasthiteḥ 
AbhTb kālastuṭyādibhiścaitat kartṛtvaṃ kalayatyataḥ  
AbhTa kāryāvacchedi kartṛtvaṃ kālovaśyaṃ kaliṣyati 
AbhTb niyatiryojanāṃ dhatte viśiṣṭe kāryamaṇḍale  
AbhTa vidyā rāgotha niyatiḥ kālaścaitaccatuṣṭayam 
AbhTb kalākāryaṃ bhoktṛbhāve tiṣṭhadbhoktṛtvapūritam  
AbhTa māyā kalā rāgavidye kālo niyatireva ca 
AbhTb kañcukāni ṣaḍuktāni saṃvidastatsthitau paśuḥ  
AbhTa dehapuryaṣṭakādyeṣu vedyeṣu kila vedanam 
AbhTb etatṣaṭkasasaṃkocaṃ yadavedyamasāvaṇuḥ  
AbhTa uktaṃ śivatanuśāstre tadidaṃ bhaṅgyantareṇa punaḥ 
AbhTb āvaraṇaṃ sarvātmagamaśuddhiranyāpyananyarūpeva  
AbhTa śivadahanakiraṇajālairdāhyatvāt sā yatonyarūpaiva 
AbhTb anidaṃpūrvatayā yadrañjayati nijātmanā tatonanyā  
AbhTa sahajāśuddhimatoṇorīśaguhābhyāṃ hi kañcukastrividhaḥ 
AbhTb tasya dvitīyacitiriva svacchasya niyujyate kalā ślakṣṇā  
AbhTa anayā vidvasya paśorupabhogasamarthatā bhavati 
AbhTb vidyā cāsya kalātaḥ śaraṇāntardīpakaprabhevābhūt  
AbhTa sukhaduḥkhasaṃvidaṃ yā vivinakti paśorvibhāgena 
AbhTb rāgaśca kalātattvācchucivastrakaṣāyavat samutpannaḥ  
AbhTa tyaktuṃ vāñchati na yataḥ saṃsṛtisukhasaṃvidānandam 
AbhTb evamavidyāmalinaḥsamarthitastriguṇakañcukabalena  
AbhTa gahanopabhogagarbhe paśuravaśamadhomukhaḥ patati 
AbhTb etena malaḥ kathitaḥ kambukavadaṇoḥ kalādikaṃ tuṣavat  
AbhTa evaṃ kalākhyatattvasya kiṃcitkartṛtvalakṣaṇe 
AbhTb viśeṣabhāge kartṛtvaṃ carcitaṃ bhoktṛpūrvakam  
AbhTa viśeṣaṇatayā yotra kiñcidbhāgastadotthitam 
AbhTb vedyamātraṃ sphuṭaṃ bhinnaṃ pradhānaṃ sūyate kalā  
AbhTa samameva hi bhogyaṃ ca bhoktāraṃ ca prasūyate 
AbhTb kalā bhedābhisaṃdhānādaviyuktaṃ parasparam  
AbhTa bhoktṛbhogyātmatā na syādviyogācca parasparam 
AbhTb vilīnāyāṃ ca tasyāṃ syānmāyāsyāpi na kiṃcana  
AbhTa nanu śrīmadrauravādau rāgavidyātmakaṃ dvayam 
AbhTb sūte kalā hi yugapattatovyaktamiti sthitiḥ  
AbhTa uktamatra vibhātyeṣa kramaḥ satyaṃ tathā hyalam 
AbhTb rajyamāno veda sarva vidaṃścāpyatra rajyate  
AbhTa tathāpi vastusatteyamihāsmābhirnirūpitā 
AbhTb tasyāṃ ca na kramaḥ kopi syādvā sopi viparyayāt  
AbhTa tasmādvipratipattiṃ no kuryācchāstrodite vidhau 
AbhTb evaṃ saṃvedyamātraṃ yat sukhaduḥkhavimohataḥ  
AbhTa bhotsyate yattataḥ proktaṃ tatsāmyātmakamāditaḥ 
AbhTb sukhaṃ sattvaṃ prakāśatvāt prakāśo hlāda ucyate  
AbhTa duḥkhaṃ rajaḥ kriyātmatvād kriyā hi tadatatkramaḥ 
AbhTb mohastamo varaṇakaḥ prakāśābhāvayogataḥ  
AbhTa ta ete kṣobhamāpannā guṇāḥ kārya pratanvate 
AbhTb akṣubdhasya vijātīyaṃ na syāt kāryamadaḥ purā  
AbhTa uktameveti śāstresmin guṇāṃstattvāntaraṃ viduḥ 
AbhTb bhuvanaṃ pṛthagevātra darśitaṃ guṇabhedataḥ  
AbhTa īśvarecchāvaśakṣubdhalolikaṃ puruṣaṃ prati 
AbhTb bhoktṛtvāya svatantreśaḥ prakṛtiṃ kṣobhayed bhṛśam  
AbhTa tena yaccodyate sāṃkhyaṃ muktāṇuṃ prati kiṃ na sā 
AbhTb sūte puṃso vikāritvāditi tannātra bādhakam  
AbhTa guṇebhyo buddhitattvaṃ tat sarvato nirmalaṃ tataḥ 
AbhTb puṃsprakāśaḥ sa vedyotra pratibimbatvamārchati  
AbhTa viṣayapratibimbaṃ ca tasyāmakṣakṛtaṃ bahiḥ 
AbhTb ataddvāraṃ samutprekṣāpratibhādiṣu tādṛśī  
AbhTa vṛttirbodho bhavedbuddheḥ sā cāpyālambanaṃ dhruvam 
AbhTb ātmasaṃvitprakāśasya bodhosau tajjaḍopyalam  
AbhTa buddherahaṃkṛt tādṛkṣe pratibimbitapuṃskṛteḥ 
AbhTb prakāśe vedyakaluṣe yadahaṃmananātmatā  
AbhTa tayā pañcavidhaścaiṣa vāyuḥ saṃrambharūpayā 
AbhTb prerito jīvanāya syādanyathā maraṇaṃ punaḥ  
AbhTa ata eva viśuddhātmasvātantryāhaṃsvabhāvataḥ 
AbhTb akṛtrimādidaṃ tvanyadityuktaṃ kṛtiśabdataḥ  
AbhTa ityayaṃ karaṇaskandhohaṃkārasya nirūpitaḥ 
AbhTb tridhāsya prakṛtiskandhaḥ sāttvarājasatāmasaḥ  
AbhTa sattvapradhānāhaṃkārādbhoktraṃśasparśinaḥ sphuṭam 
AbhTb manobuddhyakṣaṣaṭkaṃ tu jātaṃ bhedastu kathyate  
AbhTa mano yatsarvaviṣayaṃ tenātra pravivakṣitam 
AbhTb sarvatanmātrakartṛtvaṃ viśeṣaṇamahaṃkṛteḥ  
AbhTa buddhyahaṃkṛnmanaḥ prāhurbodhasaṃrabhaṇaiṣaṇe 
AbhTb karaṇaṃ bāhyadevairyannaivāpyantarmukhaiḥ kṛtam  
AbhTa prāṇaśca nāntaḥkaraṇaṃ jaḍatvāt preraṇātmanaḥ 
AbhTb prayatnecchāvibodhāṃśahetutvāditi niścitam  
AbhTa avasāyobhimānaśca kalpanā ceti na kriyā 
AbhTb ekarūpā tatastritvaṃ yuktamantaḥkṛtau sphuṭam  
AbhTa na ca buddhirasaṃvedyā karaṇatvānmano yathā 
AbhTb pradhānavadasaṃvedyabuddhivādastadujjhitaḥ  
AbhTa śabdatanmātrahetutvaviśiṣṭā yā tvahaṃkṛtiḥ 
AbhTb sā śrotre karaṇaṃ yāvadghrāṇe gandhatvabhoditā  
AbhTa bhautikatvamatopyastu niyamādviṣayeṣvalam 
AbhTb ahaṃ śṛṇomi paśyāmi jighrāmītyādisaṃvidi  
AbhTa ahaṃtānugamādāhaṃkārikatvaṃ sphuṭaṃ sthitam 
AbhTb karaṇatvamato yuktaṃ kartraśaspṛktvayogataḥ  
AbhTa karturvibhinnaṃ karaṇaṃ preryatvāt karaṇaṃ kutaḥ 
AbhTb karaṇāntaravāñchāyāṃ bhavettatrānavasthitiḥ  
AbhTa tasmāt svātantryayogena kartā svaṃ bhedayan vapuḥ 
AbhTb karmāśasparśinaṃ svāṃśaṃ karaṇīkurute svayam  
AbhTa karaṇīkṛtatatsvāṃśatanmayībhāvanāvaśāt 
AbhTb karaṇīkurutetyantavyatiriktaṃ kuṭhāravat  
AbhTa tenāśuddhaiva vidyāsya sāmānyaṃ karaṇaṃ purā 
AbhTb jñaptau kṛtau tu sāmānyaṃ kalā karaṇamucyate  
AbhTa nanu śrīmanmataṅgādau kalāyāḥ kartṛtoditā 
AbhTb tasyāṃ satyāṃ hi vidyādyāḥ karaṇatvārhatājuṣaḥ  
AbhTa ucyate kartṛtaivoktā karaṇatve prayojikā 
AbhTb tayā vinā tu nānyeṣāṃ karaṇānāṃ sthitiryataḥ  
AbhTa atosāmānyakaraṇavargāt tatra pṛthak kṛtā 
AbhTb vidyāṃ vinā hi nānyeṣāṃ karaṇānāṃ nijā sthitiḥ  
AbhTa kalāṃ vinā na tasyāśca kartṛtve jñātṛtā yataḥ 
AbhTb kalāvidye tataḥ puṃso mukhyaṃ tatkaraṇaṃ viduḥ  
AbhTa ata eva vihīnepi buddhikarmendriyaiḥ kvacit 
AbhTb andhe paṅgau rūpagatiprakāśo na na bhāsate  
AbhTa kiṃtu sāmānyakaraṇabalādvedyepi tādṛśi 
AbhTb rūpasāmānya evāndhaḥ pratipattiṃ prapadyate  
AbhTa tata eva tvahaṃkārāt tanmātrasparśinodhikam 
AbhTb karmendriyāṇi vākpāṇipāyūpasthāṅghri jajñire  
AbhTa vacmyādade tyajāmyāśu visṛjāmi vrajāmi ca 
AbhTb iti yāhaṃkriyā kāryakṣamā karmendriyaṃ tu tat  
AbhTa tena cchinnakarasyāsti hastaḥ karmendriyātmakaḥ 
AbhTb tasya pradhānādhiṣṭhānaṃ paraṃ pañcāṅguliḥ karaḥ  
AbhTa mukhenāpi yadādānaṃ tatra yat karaṇaṃ sthitam 
AbhTb sa pāṇireva karaṇaṃ vinā kiṃ saṃbhavet kriyā  
AbhTa tathābhāve tu buddhyakṣairapi kiṃ syātprayojanam 
AbhTb darśanaṃ karaṇāpekṣaṃ kriyātvāditi cocyate  
AbhTa parairgamau tu karaṇaṃ neṣyate ceti vismayaḥ 
AbhTb gamanotkṣepaṇādīni mukhyaṃ karmopalambhanam  
AbhTa punarguṇaḥ kriyā tveṣā vaiyākaraṇadarśane 
AbhTb kriyā karaṇapūrveti vyāptyā karaṇapūrvakam  
AbhTa jñānaṃ nādānamityetat sphuṭamāndhyavijṛmbhitam 
AbhTb tasmāt karmendriyāṇyāhustvagvadvyāptṝṇi mukhyataḥ  
AbhTa tatsthāne vṛttimantīti mataṅge guravo mama 
AbhTb nanvanyānyapi karmāṇi santi bhūyāṃsi tatkṛte  
AbhTa karaṇānyapi vācyāni tathā cākṣeṣvaniṣṭhitiḥ 
AbhTb nanvetat kheṭapālādyairnirākāri na karmaṇām  
AbhTa yatsādhanaṃ tadakṣaṃ syāt kiṃtu kasyāpi karmaṇaḥ 
AbhTb etannāsmatkṛtapraśnatṛṣṇāsaṃtāpaśāntaye  
AbhTa nahyasvacchamitaprāyairjalaistṛpyanti barhiṇaḥ 
AbhTb ucyate śrīmatādiṣṭaṃ śaṃbhunātra mamottaram  
AbhTa svacchasaṃvedanodāravikalāprabalīkṛtam 
AbhTb iha karmānusaṃdhānabhedādekaṃ vibhidyate  
AbhTa tatrānusaṃdhiḥ pañcātmā pañca karmendriyāṇyataḥ 
AbhTb tyāgāyādānasaṃpattyai dvayāya dvitayaṃ vinā  
AbhTa svarūpaviśrāntikṛte caturdhā karma yadbahiḥ 
AbhTb pāyupāṇyaṅghrijananaṃ karaṇaṃ taccaturvidham  
AbhTa antaṃ prāṇāśrayaṃ yattu karmātra karaṇaṃ hi vāk 
AbhTb uktāḥ samāsataścaiṣāṃ citrāḥ kāryeṣu vṛttayaḥ  
AbhTa tadetadvyatiriktaṃ hi na karma kvāpi dṛśyate 
AbhTb tatkasyārthe prakalpyeyamindriyāṇāmaniṣṭhitiḥ  
AbhTa etatkartavyacakraṃ tadasāṃkaryeṇa kurvate 
AbhTb akṣāṇi sahavṛttyā tu buddhyante saṃkaraṃ jaḍāḥ  
AbhTa ukta indriyavargoyamahaṃkārāt tu rājasāt 
AbhTb tamaḥpradhānāhaṃkārād bhoktraṃśacchādanātmanaḥ  
AbhTa bhūtādināmnastanmātrapañcakaṃ bhūtakāraṇam 
AbhTb manobuddhyakṣakarmākṣavargastanmātravargakaḥ  
AbhTa ityatra rājasāhaṃkṛdyogaḥ saṃśleṣako dvaye 
AbhTb anye tvāhurmano jātaṃ rājasāhaṃkṛteryataḥ  
AbhTa samastendriyasaṃcāracaturaṃ laghu vegavat 
AbhTb anye tu sāttvikāt svāntaṃ buddhikarmendriyāṇi tu  
AbhTa rājasādgrāhakagrāhyabhāgasparśīni manvate 
AbhTb kheṭapālāstu manyante karmendriyagaṇaḥ sphuṭam  
AbhTa rājasāhaṃkṛterjāto rajasaḥ karmatā yataḥ 
AbhTb śrīpūrvaśāstre tu mano rājasāt sāttvikātpunaḥ  
AbhTa indriyāṇi samastāni yuktaṃ caitadvibhāti naḥ 
AbhTb tathāhi bāhyavṛttīnāmakṣāṇāṃ vṛttibhāsane  
AbhTa ālocane śaktirantaryojane manasaḥ punaḥ 
AbhTb uktaṃ ca guruṇā kuryānmanonuvyavasāyi sat  
AbhTa taddvayālambanā mātṛvyāpārātmakriyā iti 
AbhTb tānmātrastu gaṇo dhvāntapradhānāyā ahaṃkṛteḥ  
AbhTa atrāvivādaḥ sarvasya grāhyopakrama eva hi 
AbhTb pṛthivyāṃ saurabhānyādivicitre gandhamaṇḍale  
AbhTa yatsāmānyaṃ hi gandhatvaṃ gandhatanmātranāma tat 
AbhTb vyāpakaṃ tata evoktaṃ sahetutvāttu na dhruvam  
AbhTa svakāraṇe tirobhūtirdhvaso yattena nādhruvam 
AbhTb evaṃ rasādiśabdāntatanmātreṣvapi yojanā  
AbhTa viśeṣāṇāṃ yatovaśyaṃ daśā prāgaviśeṣiṇī 
AbhTb kṣubhitaṃ śabdatanmātraṃ citrākārāḥ śratīrdadhat  
AbhTa nabhaḥ śabdovakāśātmā vācyādhyāsasaho yataḥ 
AbhTb tadetatsparśatanmātrayogāt prakṣobhamāgatam  
AbhTa vāyutāmeti tenātra śabdasparśobhayātmatā 
AbhTb anye tvāhurdhvaniḥ khaikaguṇastadapi yujyate  
AbhTa yato vāyurnijaṃ rūpaṃ labhate na vināmbarāt 
AbhTb uttarottarabhūteṣu pūrvapūrvasthitiryataḥ  
AbhTa tata eva marudvyomnoraviyogo mithaḥ smṛtaḥ 
AbhTb śabdasparśau tu rūpeṇa samaṃ prakṣobhamāgatau  
AbhTa tejastattvaṃ tribhirdharmaiḥ prāhuḥ pūrvavadeva tat 
AbhTb taistribhiḥ sarasairāpaḥ sagandhairbhūriti kramaḥ  
AbhTa tatra pratyakṣataḥ siddho dharādiguṇasaṃcayaḥ 
AbhTb nahi gandhādidharmaughavyatiriktā vibhāti bhūḥ  
AbhTa yathā guṇaguṇidvaitavādināmekamapyadaḥ 
AbhTb citraṃ rūpaṃ paṭe bhāti kramāddharmāstathā bhuvi  
AbhTa yathā ca vistṛte vastre yugapadbhāti citratā 
AbhTb tathaiva yogināṃ dharmasāmastyenāvabhāti bhūḥ  
AbhTa gandhādiśabdaparyantacitrarūpā dharā tataḥ 
AbhTb upāyabhedādbhātyeṣā kramākramavibhāgataḥ  
AbhTa tata eva kramavyaktikṛto dhībheda ucyate 
AbhTb ṣaṣṭhīprayogo dhībhedādbhedyabhedakatā tathā  
AbhTa tena dharmātiriktotra dharmī nāma na kaścana 
AbhTb tatrānekaprakārāḥ syurgandharūparasāḥ kṣitau  
AbhTa saṃsparśaḥ pākajonuṣṇāśītaḥ śabdo vicitrakaḥ 
AbhTb śauklyaṃ mādhuryaśītatve citrāḥ śabdāśca vāriṇi  
AbhTa śuklabhāsvaratoṣṇatvaṃ citrāḥ śabdāśca pāvake 
AbhTb apākajaścāśītoṣṇo dhvaniścitraśca mārute  
AbhTa varṇātmako dhvaniḥ śabdapratibimbānyathāmbare 
AbhTb yattu na sparśavaddharmaḥ śabda ityādi bhaṇyate  
AbhTa kāṇādaistatsvapratītiviruddhaṃ kena gṛhyatām 
AbhTb paṭahe dhvanirityeva bhātyabādhitameva yat  
AbhTa na ca hetutvamātreṇa tadādānatvavedanāt 
AbhTb śrotraṃ cāsmanmatehaṃkṛtkāraṇaṃ tatra tatra tat  
AbhTa vṛttibhāgīti taddeśaṃ śabdaṃ gṛhṇātyalaṃ tathā 
AbhTb yastvāha śrotramākāśaṃ karṇasaṃyogabheditam  
AbhTa śabdajaḥ śabda āgatya śabdabuddhiṃ prasūyate 
AbhTb tasya mandepi murajadhvanāvākarṇake sati  
AbhTa amutra śrutireṣeti dūre saṃvedanaṃ katham 
AbhTb nahi śabdajaśabdasya dūrādūraravoditeḥ  
AbhTa śrotrākāśagatasyāsti dūrādūrasvabhāvatā 
AbhTb na cāsau prathamaḥ śabdastāvadvyāpīti yujyate  
AbhTa tatrasthaiḥ saha tīvrātmā śrūyamāṇastvanena tu 
AbhTb kathaṃ śrūyeta mandaḥsannahi dharmāntarāśrayaḥ  
AbhTa etaccānyairapākāri bahudheti vṛthā punaḥ 
AbhTb nāyastaṃ patitāghātadāne ko hi na paṇḍitaḥ  
AbhTa amīṣāṃ tu dharādīnāṃ yāvāṃstattvagaṇaḥ purā 
AbhTb guṇādhikatayā tiṣṭhan vyāptā tāvān prakāśate  
AbhTa vyāpyavyāpakatā yaiṣā tattvānāṃ darśitā kila 
AbhTb sā guṇādhikyataḥ siddhā na hetutvānna lāghavāt  
AbhTa ahetunāpi rāgo hi vyāpto vidyādinā sphuṭam 
AbhTb tadvinā na bhavedyattadvyāptamityucyate yataḥ  
AbhTa na lāghavaṃ ca nāmāsti kiṃcidatra svadarśane 
AbhTb guṇādhikyādato jñeyā vyāpyavyāpakatā sphuṭā  
AbhTa yo hi yasmādguṇotkṛṣṭaḥ sa tasmādūrdhva ucyate 
AbhTb ūrdhvatā vyāptṛtā śrīmanmālinīvijaye sphuṭā  
AbhTa ataḥ śivatvātprabhṛti prakāśatāsvarūpamādāya nijātmani dhruvam 
AbhTb samastatattvāvalidharmasaṃcayairvibhāti bhūrvyāptṛtayā sthitairalam  
AbhTa evaṃ jalāderapi śaktitattvaparyantadhāmno vapurasti tādṛk 
AbhTb kiṃ tūttaraṃ śaktitayaiva tattvaṃ pūrva tu taddharmatayeti bhedaḥ  
AbhTa anuttaraprakriyāyāṃ vaitatyena pradarśitam 
AbhTb etat tasmāt tataḥ paśyedvistarārthī vivecakaḥ  
AbhTa iti tattvasyarūpasya kṛtaṃ samyak prakāśanam  
C atha śrītantrāloke daśamamāhnikam
AbhTb ucyate trikaśāstrekarahasyaṃ tattvabhedanam  b
AbhTa teṣāmamīṣāṃ tattvānāṃ svavargeṣvanugāminām 
AbhTb bhedāntaramapi proktaṃ śāstretra śrītrikābhidhe  
AbhTa śaktimacchaktibhedena dharādyaṃ mūlapaścimam 
AbhTb bhidyate pañcadaśadhā svarūpeṇa sahānarāt  
AbhTa kalāntaṃ bhedayugghīnaṃ rudravatpralayākalaḥ 
AbhTb tadvanmāyā ca navadhā jñākalāḥ saptadhā punaḥ  
AbhTa mantrāstadīśāḥ pāñcadhye mantreśapatayastridhā 
AbhTb śivo na bhidyate svaikaprakāśaghanacinmayaḥ  
AbhTa śivo mantramaheśeśamantrā akalayukkalī 
AbhTb śaktimantaḥ sapta tathā śaktayastaccaturdaśa  
AbhTa svaṃ svarūpaṃ pañcadaśaṃ tadbhūḥ pañcadaśātmikā 
AbhTb tathāhi tisro devasya śaktayo varṇitāḥ purā  
AbhTa tā eva mātṛmāmeyatrairūpyeṇa vyavasthitāḥ 
AbhTb parāṃśo mātṛrūpotra pramāṇāṃśaḥ parāparaḥ  
AbhTa meyoparaḥ śaktimāṃśca śaktiḥ svaṃ rūpamityadaḥ 
AbhTb tatra svarūpaṃ bhūmeryatpṛthagjaḍamavasthitam  
AbhTa mātṛmānādyupadhibhirasaṃjātoparāgakam 
AbhTb sakalādiśivāntaistu mātṛbhirvedyatāsya yā  
AbhTa śaktimadbhiranudbhūtaśaktibhiḥ sapta tadbhidaḥ 
AbhTb sakalādiśivāntānāṃ śaktiṣūdrecitātmasu  
AbhTa vedyatājanitāḥ sapta bhedā iti caturdaśa 
AbhTb sakalasya pramāṇāṃśo yosau vidyākalātmakaḥ  
AbhTa sāmānyātmā sa śaktitve gaṇito natu tadbhidaḥ 
AbhTb layākalasya mānāṃśaḥ sa eva paramasphuṭaḥ  
AbhTa jñānākalasya mānaṃ tu galadvidyākalāvṛti 
AbhTb aśuddhavidyākalanādhvaṃsasaṃskārasaṃgatā  
AbhTa prabubhutsuḥ śuddhavidyā santrāṇāṃ karaṇaṃ bhavet 
AbhTb prabuddhā śuddhavidyā tu tatsaṃskāreṇa saṃgatā  
AbhTa mānaṃ mantreśvarāṇāṃ syāttatsaṃskāravivarjitā 
AbhTb mānaṃ mantramaheśānāṃ karaṇaṃ śaktirucyate  
AbhTa svātantryamātrasadbhāvā yā tvicchā śaktiraiśvarī 
AbhTb śivasya saiva karaṇaṃ tayā vetti karoti ca  
AbhTa ā śivātsakalāntaṃ ye mātāraḥ sapta te dvidhā 
AbhTb nyagbhūtodriktaśaktitvāttadbhedo vedyabhedakaḥ  
AbhTa tathāhi vedyatā nāma bhāvasyaiva nijaṃ vapuḥ 
AbhTb caitreṇa vedyaṃ vedmīti kiṃhyatra pratibhāsatām  
AbhTa nanu caitrīyavijñānamātramatra prakāśate 
AbhTb vedyatākhyastu no dharmo bhāti bhāvasya nīlavat  
AbhTa vedyatā ca svabhāvena dharmo bhāvasya cettataḥ 
AbhTb sarvānpratyeva vedyaḥ syāddhaṭanīlādidharmavat  
AbhTa atha vedakasaṃvittibalādvedyatvadharmabhāk 
AbhTb bhāvastathāpi doṣosau kuvindakṛtavastravat  
AbhTa vedyatākhyastu yo dharmaḥ sovedyaścetkhapuṣpavat 
AbhTb vedyaścedasti tatrāpi vedyetatyanavasthitiḥ  
AbhTa tato na kiṃcidvedyaṃ syānmūrchitaṃ tu jagadbhavet 
AbhTb nanu vijñātrupādhyaṃ śo paskṛtaṃ vapurucyatām  
AbhTa bhāvasyārthaprakāśātma yathā jñānamidaṃ tvasat 
AbhTb ekavijñātṛvedyatve na jñātrantaravedyatā  
AbhTa samastajñātṛvedyatve naikavijñātṛvedyatā 
AbhTb tasmānna vedyatā nāma bhāvadharmosti kaścana  
AbhTa bhāvasya vedyatā saiva saṃvido yaḥ samudbhavaḥ 
AbhTb arthagrahaṇarūpaṃ hi yatra vijñānamātmani  
AbhTa samavaiti prakāśyorthastaṃ pratyeṣaiva vedyatā 
AbhTb atra brūmaḥ padārthānāṃ na dharmo yadi vedyatā  
AbhTa avedyā eva te saṃsyurjñāne satyapi varṇite 
AbhTb yathāhi pṛthubudhnādirūpe kumbhasya satyapi  
AbhTa atadātmā paṭo naiti pṛthubudhnādirūpatām 
AbhTb tathā satyapi vijñāne vijñātṛsamavāyini  
AbhTa avedyadharmakā bhāvāḥ kathaṃ vedyatvamāpnuyuḥ 
AbhTb anarthaḥ sumahāṃścaiṣa dṛśyatāṃ vastu yatsvayam  
AbhTa prakāśātma na tatsaṃviccāprakāśā tadāśrayaḥ 
AbhTb aprakāśo manodīpacakṣurādi tathaiva tat  
AbhTa kiṃ tatprakāśatāṃ nāma supte jagati sarvataḥ 
AbhTb jñānasyārthaprakāśatvaṃ nanu rūpaṃ pradīpavat  
AbhTa apūrvamatra viditaṃ narīnṛtyāmahe tataḥ 
AbhTb arthaprakāśo jñānasya yadrūpaṃ tannirūpyatām  
AbhTa arthaḥ prakāśaścedrūpamartho vā jñānameva vā 
AbhTb athārthasya prakāśo yastadrūpamiti bhaṇyate  
AbhTa ṣaṣṭhī kartari cedukto doṣa eva duruddharaḥ 
AbhTb atha karmaṇi ṣaṣṭhyeṣā ṇyarthastatra hṛdi sthitaḥ  
AbhTa tathā cedaṃ darśayāmaḥ kiṃ prakāśaḥ prakāśate 
AbhTb aprakāśopi naivāsau tathāpi ca na kiṃcana  
AbhTa tarhi loke kathaṃ ṇyarthaḥ ucyate cetanasthitau 
AbhTb mukhyo ṇyarthasya viṣayo jaḍeṣu tvaupacārikaḥ  
AbhTa tathāhi gantuṃ śaktopi caitronyāyattatāṃ gateḥ 
AbhTb manvāna eva vaktyasmi gamitaḥ svāmineti hi  
AbhTa svāmyapyasya gatau śaktiṃ buddhvā svādhīnatāṃ sphuṭam 
AbhTb paśyannivṛttimāśaṃkya gamayāmīti bhāṣate  
AbhTa preryaprerakayorevaṃ maulikī ṇyarthasaṃgatiḥ 
AbhTb tadabhiprāyatonyopi loke vyavaharettathā  
AbhTa śaraṃ gamayatītyatra punarvegākhyasaṃskriyām 
AbhTb vidadhatprerakammanya upacāreṇa jāyate  
AbhTa vāyuradriṃ pātayatītyatra dvāvapi tau jaḍau 
AbhTb draṣṭṛbhiḥ prerakapreryavapuṣā parikalpitau  
AbhTa itthaṃ jaḍena saṃbandhe na mukhyā ṇyarthasaṃgatiḥ 
AbhTb āstāmanyatra vitatametadvistarato mayā  
AbhTa arthe prakāśanā seyamupacārastato bhavet 
AbhTb astu cedbhāsate tarhi sa eva patadadrivat  
AbhTa upacāre nimittena kenāpi kila bhūyate 
AbhTb vāyuḥ pātayatītyatra nimittaṃ tatkṛtā kriyā  
AbhTa girau yenaiṣa saṃyoganāśādbhraṃśaṃ prapadyate 
AbhTb iha tu jñānamarthasya na kiṃcitkarameva tat  
AbhTa upacāraḥ kathaṃ nāma bhavetsopi hyavastusan 
AbhTb aprakāśita evārthaḥ prakāśatvopacārataḥ  
AbhTa tādṛgeva śiśuḥ kiṃ hi dahatyagnyupacārataḥ 
AbhTb śiśau vahnyupacāre yadbījaṃ taikṣṇyādi tacca sat  
AbhTa prakāśatvopacāre tu kiṃ bījaṃ yatra satyatā 
AbhTb siddhe hi cetane yukta upacāraḥ sa hi sphuṭam  
AbhTa adhyāropātmakaḥ sopi pratisaṃdhānajīvitaḥ 
AbhTb na cādyāpi kimapyasti cetanaṃ jñānamapyadaḥ  
AbhTa aprakāśaṃ tadanyena tatprakāśepyayaṃ vidhiḥ 
AbhTb nanu pradīpo rūpasya prakāśaḥ kathamīdṛśam  
AbhTa atrāpi na vahantyetāḥ kiṃ nu yuktivikalpanāḥ 
AbhTb yādṛśā svena rūpeṇa dīpo rūpaṃ prakāśayet  
AbhTa tādṛśā svayamapyeṣa bhāti jñānaṃ tu no tathā 
AbhTb pradīpaścaiṣa bhāvānāṃ prakāśatvaṃ dadādhātyalam  
AbhTa anyathā na prakāśerannabhede cedṛśo vidhiḥ 
AbhTb tasmātprakāśa evāyaṃ pūrvoktaḥ paramaḥ śivaḥ  
AbhTa yathā yathā prakāśeta tattadbhāvavapuḥ sphuṭam 
AbhTb evaṃ ca nīlatā nāma yathā kācitprakāśate  
AbhTa tadvaccakāsti vedyatvaṃ tacca bhāvāṃśapṛṣṭhagam 
AbhTb phalaṃ prakaṭatārthasya saṃvidveti dvayaṃ tataḥ  
AbhTa vipakṣato rakṣitaṃ ca saṃdhānaṃ cāpi tanmithaḥ 
AbhTb tathāhi nibhṛtaścauraścaitravedyamiti sphuṭam  
AbhTa buddhvā nādatta evāśu parīpsāvivaśopi san 
AbhTb seyaṃ paśyati māṃ netratribhāgeneti sādaram  
AbhTa svaṃ dehamamṛteneva siktaṃ paśyati kāmukaḥ 
AbhTb na caitajjñānasaṃvittimātraṃ bhāvāṃśapṛṣṭhagam  
AbhTa arthakriyākaraṃ taccenna dharmaḥ konvasau bhavet 
AbhTb yaccoktaṃ vedyatādharmā bhāvaḥ sarvānapi prati  
AbhTa syādityetatsvapakṣaghnaṃ duṣprayogāstravattava 
AbhTb asmākaṃ tu svaprakāśaśivatāmātravādinām  
AbhTa anyaṃ prati cakāstīti vaca eva na vidyate 
AbhTb sarvānprati ca tannīlaṃ sa ghaṭaśceti yadvacaḥ  
AbhTa tadapyaviditaprāyaṃ gṛhītaṃ mugdhabuddhibhiḥ 
AbhTb nahi kālāgnirudrīyakāyāvagatanīlimā  
AbhTa tava nīlaḥ kiṃ nu pīto maivaṃ bhūnnatu nīlakaḥ 
AbhTb na kaṃcitprati nīlosau nīlo vā yaṃ prati sthitaḥ  
AbhTa taṃ pratyeva sa vedyaḥ syātsaṃkalpadvārakontataḥ 
AbhTb yathā cārthaprakāśātma jñānaṃ saṃgīryate tvayā  
AbhTa tathā tajjñātṛvedyatvaṃ bhāvīyaṃ rūpamucyatām 
AbhTb na ca jñātātra niyataḥ kaścijjñāne yathā tava  
AbhTa arthe jñātā yadā yo yastadvedyaṃ vapurucyatām 
AbhTb tattadvijñātṛvedyatvaṃ sarvānpratyeva bhāsatām  
AbhTa ityevaṃ codayanmanye vrajedbadhiradhuryatām 
AbhTb nahyanyaṃ prati vai kaṃcidbhāti sā vedyatā tathā  
AbhTa bhāvasya rūpamityukte keyamasthānavaidhurī 
AbhTb anena nītimārgeṇa nirmūlamapasāritā  
AbhTa anavasthā tathā hyanyairnīlādyaiḥ sadṛśī na sā 
AbhTb vedyatā kiṃtu dharmosau yadyogātsarvadharmavān  
AbhTa dharmī vedyatvamabhyeti sa sattāsamavāyavat 
AbhTb brūṣe yathā hi kurute sattā satyasataḥ sataḥ  
AbhTa samavāyopi saṃśliṣṭaḥ śliṣṭānaśliṣṭatājuṣaḥ 
AbhTb antyo viśeṣo vyāvṛttirūpo vyāvṛttivarjitān  
AbhTa vyāvṛttān śvetimā śuklamaśuklaṃ gamanaṃ tathā 
AbhTb tadvannīlādidharmāṃśayukto dharmī svayaṃ sthitaḥ  
AbhTa avedyo vedyatārūpāddharmādvedyatvamāgataḥ 
AbhTb vedyatā bhāsamānā ca svayaṃ nīlādidharmavat  
AbhTa aprakāśā svaprakāśāddharmādeti prakāśatām 
AbhTb prakāśe khalu viśrāntiṃ viśvaṃ śrayati cettataḥ  
AbhTa nānyā kācidapekṣāsya kṛtakṛtyasya sarvataḥ 
AbhTb yathā ca śivanāthena svātantryādbhāsyate bhidā  
AbhTa nīlādivattathaivāyaṃ vedyatā dharma ucyate 
AbhTb evaṃ siddhaṃ hi vedyatvaṃ bhāvadharmostu kā ghṛṇā
