AbhTa idaṃ tu cintyaṃ sakalaparyantoktapramātṛbhiḥ 
AbhTb vedyatvamekarūpaṃ syāccāturdaśyamataḥ kutaḥ  
AbhTa ucyate paripūrṇaṃ cedbhāvīyaṃ rūpamucyate 
AbhTb tadvibhurbhairavo devo bhagavāneva bhaṇyate  
AbhTa atha tannijamāhātmyakalpitoṃśāṃśikākramaḥ 
AbhTb sahyate kiṃ kṛtaṃ tarhi proktakalpanayānayā  
AbhTa ata eva yadā yena vapuṣā bhāti yadyathā 
AbhTb tadā tathā tattadrūpamityeṣopaniṣatparā  
AbhTa caitreṇa vedyaṃ jānāmi dvābhyāṃ bahubhirapyatha 
AbhTb mantreṇa tanmaheśena śivenodriktaśaktinā  
AbhTa anyādṛśena vetyevaṃ bhāvo bhāti yathā tathā 
AbhTb arthakriyādivaicitryamabhyetyaparisaṃkhyayā  
AbhTa tathā hyekāgrasakalasāmājikajanaḥ khalu 
AbhTb nṛttaṃ gītaṃ sudhāsārasāgaratvena manyate  
AbhTa tata evocyate mallanaṭaprekṣopadeśane 
AbhTb sarvapramātṛtādātmyaṃ pūrṇarūpānubhāvakam  
AbhTa tāvanmātrārthasaṃvittituṣṭāḥ pratyekaśo yadi 
AbhTb kaḥ saṃbhūya guṇasteṣāṃ pramātraikyaṃ bhavecca kim  
AbhTa yadā tu tattadvedyatvadharmasaṃdarbhagarbhitam 
AbhTb tadvastu śuṣkātprāgrūpādanyadyuktamidaṃ tadā  
AbhTa śāstrepi tattadvedyatvaṃ viśiṣṭārthakriyākaram 
AbhTb bhūyasaiva tathāca śrīmālinīvijayottare  
AbhTa tathā ṣaḍvidhamadhvānamanenādhiṣṭhitaṃ smaret 
AbhTb adhiṣṭhānaṃ hi devena yadviśvasya pravedanam  
AbhTa tadīśavedyatvenetthaṃ jñātaṃ prakṛtakāryakṛt 
AbhTb evaṃ siddhaṃ vedyatākhyo dharmo bhāvasya bhāsate  
AbhTa tadanābhāsayoge tu svarūpamiti bhaṇyate 
AbhTb upādhiyogitāśaṅkāmapahastayatosphuṭam  
AbhTa svātmano yena vapuṣā bhātyarthastatsvakaṃ vapuḥ 
AbhTb jānāmi ghaṭamityatra vedyatānuparāgavān  
AbhTa ghaṭa eva svarūpeṇa bhāta ityapadiśyate 
AbhTb nanu tatra svayaṃvedyabhāvo mantrādyapekṣayā  
AbhTa api cāstyeva nanvastu natu sanpratibhāsate 
AbhTb avedyameva kālāgnivapurmeroḥ parā diśaḥ  
AbhTa mameti saṃvidi paraṃ śuddhaṃ vastu prakāśate 
AbhTb bhātatvādvedyamapi tanna vedyatvena bhāsanāt  
AbhTa avedyameva bhānaṃ hi tathā kamanuyuñjmahe 
AbhTb evaṃ pañcadaśātmeyaṃ dharā tadvajjalādayaḥ  
AbhTa avyaktāntā yatostyeṣāṃ sakalaṃ prati vedyatā 
AbhTb yattūcyate kalādyena dharāntena samanvitāḥ  
AbhTa sakalā iti tatkośaṣaṭkodrekopalakṣaṇam 
AbhTb udbhūtāśuddhacidrāgakalādirasakañcukāḥ  
AbhTa sakalālayasaṃjñāstu nyagbhūtākhilakañcukāḥ 
AbhTb jñānākalāstu dhvastaitatkañcukā iti nirṇayaḥ  
AbhTa tena pradhāne vedyepi pumānudbhūtakañcukaḥ 
AbhTb pramātāstyeva sakalaḥ pāñcadaśyamataḥ sthitam  
AbhTa pāñcadaśyaṃ dharādhantarniviṣṭe sakalepi ca 
AbhTb sakalāntaramastyeva prameyetrāpi mātṛ hi  
AbhTa sthūlāvṛtādisaṃkocatadanyavyāptṛtājuṣaḥ 
AbhTb pītādyāḥ sthirakampratvāccaturdaśa dharādiṣu  
AbhTa svarūpībhūtajaḍatāḥ prāṇadehapathe tataḥ 
AbhTb pramātṛtājuṣaḥ proktā dhāraṇā vijayottare  
AbhTa yadā tu meyatā puṃsaḥ kalāntasya prakalpyate 
AbhTb tadudbhūtaḥ kañcukāṃśo meyo nāsya pramātṛtā  
AbhTa ataḥ sakalasaṃjñasya pramātṛtvaṃ na vidyate 
AbhTb trayodaśatvaṃ tacchaktiśaktimaddvayavarjanāt  
AbhTa nyagbhūtakañcuko mātā yuktayatastatra layākalaḥ 
AbhTb māyāniviṣṭo vijñānākalādyāḥ prāgvadeva tu  
AbhTa māyātattve jñeyarūpe kañcukanyagbhavopi yaḥ 
AbhTb sopi meyaḥ kañcukaikyaṃ yato māyā susūkṣmikā  
AbhTa vijñānākala evātra tato mātāpakañcukaḥ 
AbhTb māyāniviṣṭepyakale tathetyekādaśātmatā  
AbhTa vijñānakevale vedye kañcukadhvaṃsasusthite 
AbhTb udbubhūṣuprabodhānāṃ mantrāṇāmeva mātṛtā  
AbhTa tepi mantrā yadā meyāstadā mātā tadīśvaraḥ 
AbhTb sa hyudbhavātpūrṇabodhastasminprāpte tu meyatām  
AbhTa udbhūtapūrṇarūposau mātā mantramaheśvaraḥ 
AbhTb tasminvijñeyatāṃ prāpte svaprakāśaḥ paraḥ śivaḥ  
AbhTa pramātā svakatādātmyabhāsitākhilavedyakaḥ 
AbhTb śivaḥ pramātā no meyo hyanyādhīnaprakāśatā  
AbhTa meyatā sā na tatrāsti svaprakāśo hyasau prabhuḥ 
AbhTb svaprakāśetra kasmiṃścidanabhyupagate sati  
AbhTa aprakāśātprakāśatve hyanavasthā duruttarā 
AbhTb tataśca suptaṃ viśvaṃ syānna caivaṃ bhāsate hi tat  
AbhTa anyādhīnaprakāśaṃ hi tadbhātyanyastvasau śivaḥ 
AbhTb ityasya svaprakāśatve kimanyairyuktiḍambaraiḥ  
AbhTa mānānāṃ hi paro jīvaḥ sa evetyuktamāditaḥ 
AbhTb nanvasti svaprakāśepi śive vedyatvamīdṛśaḥ  
AbhTa upadeśośyopadeṣṭṛtvavyavahāronyathā katham 
AbhTb satyaṃ sa tu tathā sṛṣṭaḥ parameśena vedyatām  
AbhTa nīto mantramaheśādikakṣyāṃ samadhiśāyyate 
AbhTb tathābhūtaśca vedyosau nānavacchinnasaṃvidaḥ  
AbhTa pūrṇasya vedyatā yuktā parasparavirodhataḥ 
AbhTb tathā vedyasvabhāvepi vastuto na śivātmatām  
AbhTa kopi bhāvaḥ projjhatīti satyaṃ tadbhāvanā phalet 
AbhTb śrīpūrvaśāstre tenoktaṃ śivaḥ sākṣānna bhidyate  
AbhTa sākṣātpadenāyamarthaḥ samastaḥ prasphuṭīkṛtaḥ 
AbhTb nanvekarūpatāyuktaḥ śivastadvaśato bhavet  
AbhTa trivedatāmantramahānāthe kātra vivāditā 
AbhTb maheśvareśamantrāṇāṃ tathā kevalinordvayoḥ  
AbhTa anantabhedataikaikaṃ sthitā sakalavatkila 
AbhTb tato layākale meye pramātāsti layākalaḥ  
AbhTa atastrayodaśatvaṃ syāditthaṃ naikādaśātmatā 
AbhTb vijñānākalavedyatvepyanyo jñānākalo bhavet  
AbhTa mātā tadekādaśatā syānnaiva tu navātmatā 
AbhTb evaṃ mantratadīśānāṃ mantreśāntarasaṃbhave  
AbhTa vedyatvānnava sapta syuḥ sapta pañca tu te katham 
AbhTb ucyate satyamastyeṣā kalanā kiṃtu susphuṭaḥ  
AbhTa yathātra sakale bhedo na tathā tvakalādike 
AbhTb anantāvāntaredṛkṣayonibhedavataḥ sphuṭam  
AbhTa caturdaśavidhasyāsya sakalasyāsti bheditā 
AbhTb layākale tu saṃskāramātrātsatyapyasau bhidā  
AbhTa akalena viśeṣāya sakalasyaiva yujyate 
AbhTb vijñānakevalādīnāṃ tāvatyapi na vai bhidā  
AbhTa śivasvācchandyamātraṃ tu bhedāyaiṣāṃ vijṛmbhate 
AbhTb ityāśayena saṃpaśyanviśeṣaṃ sakalādiha  
AbhTa layākalādau novāca trāyodaśyādikaṃ vibhuḥ 
AbhTb nanvastu vedyatā bhāvadharmaḥ kiṃtu layākalau  
AbhTa manvāte neha vai kiṃcittadapekṣā tvasau katham 
AbhTb śrūyatāṃ saṃvidaikātmyatattvesminsaṃvyavasthite  
AbhTa jaḍepi citirastyeva bhotsyamāne tu kā kathā 
AbhTb svabodhāvasare tāvadbhotsyate layakevalī  
AbhTa dvividhaśca prabodhosya mantratvāya bhavāya ca 
AbhTb bhāvanādibalādanyavaiṣṇavādinayoditāt  
AbhTa yathāsvamādharauttaryavicitrātsaṃskṛtastathā 
AbhTb līnaḥ prabuddho mantratvaṃ tadīśatvamathaiti vā  
AbhTa svātantryavarjitā ye tu balānmohavaśīkṛtāḥ 
AbhTb layākalātsvasaṃskārātprabuddhyante bhavāya te  
AbhTa jñānākalopi mantreśamaheśatvāya budhyate 
AbhTb mantrāditvāya vā jātu jātu saṃsṛtayepi vā  
AbhTa avatāro hi vijñāniyogibhāvesya bhidyate 
AbhTb uktaṃ ca bodhayāmāsa sa sisṛkṣurjagatprabhuḥ  
AbhTa vijñānakevalānaṣṭāviti śrīpūrvaśāsane 
AbhTb ataḥ prabhotsyamānatve yānayorbodhayogyatā  
AbhTa tadbalādvedyatāyogyabhāvenaivātra vedyatā 
AbhTb tathāhi gāḍhanidrepi priyenāśaṅkitāgatām  
AbhTa māṃ drakṣyatīti nāṅgeṣu sveṣu mātyabhisārikā 
AbhTb evaṃ śivopi manute etasyaitatpravedyatām  
AbhTa yāsyatīti sṛjāmīti tadānīṃ yogyataiva sā 
AbhTb vedyatā tasya bhāvasya bhoktṛtā tāvatī ca sā  
AbhTa layākalasya citro hi bhogaḥ kena vikalpyate 
AbhTb yathā yathā hi samvittiḥ sa hi bhogaḥ sphuṭosphuṭaḥ  
AbhTa smṛtiyogyopyanyathā vā bhogyabhāvaṃ na tūjjhati 
AbhTb gāḍhanidrāvimūḍhopi kāntāliṅgitavigrahaḥ  
AbhTa bhoktaiva bhaṇyate sopi manute bhoktṛtāṃ purā 
AbhTb utprekṣāmātrahīnopi kāṃcitkulavadhūṃ puraḥ  
AbhTa saṃbhokṣyamāṇāṃ dṛṣṭvaiva rabhasādyāti saṃmadam 
AbhTb tāmeva dṛṣṭvā ca tadā samānāśayabhāgapi  
AbhTa anyastathā na saṃvitte kamatropalabhāmahe 
AbhTb loke rūḍhamidaṃ dṛṣṭirasminkāraṇamantarā  
AbhTa prasīdatīva magneva nirvātīvetivādini 
AbhTb itthaṃ vistaratastattvabhedoyaṃ samudāhṛtaḥ  
AbhTa śaktiśaktimatāṃ bhedādanyonyaṃ tatkṛteṣvapi 
AbhTb bhedeṣvanyonyato bhedāttathā tattvāntaraiḥ saha  
AbhTa bhedopabhedagaṇanāṃ karvato nāvadhiḥ kvacit 
AbhTb tata eva vicitroyaṃ bhuvanādividhiḥ sthitaḥ  
AbhTa pārthivatvepi no sāmyaṃ rudravaiṣṇavalokayoḥ 
AbhTb kā kathānyatra tu bhavedbhoge vāpi svarūpake  
AbhTa sa ca no vistaraḥ sākṣācchakyo yadyapi bhāṣitum 
AbhTb tathāpi mārgamātreṇa kathyamāno vivicyatām  
AbhTa saptānāṃ mātṛśaktīnāmanyonyaṃ bhedane sati 
AbhTb rūpamekānnapañcāśatsvarūpaṃ cādhikaṃ tataḥ  
AbhTa sarvaṃ sarvātmakaṃ yasmāttasmātsakalamātari 
AbhTb layākalādiśaktīnāṃ saṃbhavostyeva tattvataḥ  
AbhTa sa tvasphuṭostu bhedāṃśaṃ dātuṃ tāvatprabhurbhavet 
AbhTb teṣāmapi ca bhedānāmanyonyaṃ bahubhedatā  
AbhTa mukhyānāṃ bhedabhedānāṃ jalādyairbhedane sati 
AbhTb mukhyabhedaprakāreṇa vidherānantyamucyate  
AbhTa sakalasya samudbhūtāścakṣurādisvaśaktayaḥ 
AbhTb nyagbhūtāśca pratanvanti bhedāntaramapi sphuṭam  
AbhTa evaṃ layākalādīnāṃ tatsaṃskārapadoditāt 
AbhTb pāṭavātprakṣayādvāpi bhedāntaramudīyate  
AbhTa nyakkṛtāṃ śaktimāsthāyāpyudāsīnatayā sthitim 
AbhTb anāviśyeva yadvetti tatrānyā vedyatā khalu  
AbhTa āviśyeva nimajjyeva vikāsyeva vighūrṇya ca 
AbhTb vidato vedyatānyaiva bhedotrārthakriyocitaḥ  
AbhTa anyaśaktitirobhāve kasyāścitsusphuṭodaye 
AbhTb bhedāntaramapi jñeyaṃ vīṇāvādakadṛṣṭivat  
AbhTa tirobhāvodbhavau śakteḥ svaśaktyantaratonyataḥ 
AbhTb cetyamānādacetyādvā tanvāte bahubhedatām  
AbhTa evametaddharādīnāṃ tattvānāṃ yāvatī daśā 
AbhTb kācidasti ghaṭākhyāpi tatra saṃdarśitā bhidaḥ  
AbhTa atrāpi vedyatā nāma tādātmyaṃ vedakaiḥ saha 
AbhTb tataḥ sakalavedyosau ghaṭaḥ sakala eva hi  
AbhTa yāvacchivaikavedyosau śiva evāvabhāsate 
AbhTb tāvadekaśarīro hi bodho bhātyeva yāvatā  
AbhTa adhunātra samastasya dharātattvasya darśyate 
AbhTb sāmastya evābhihitaṃ pāñcadaśyaṃ puroditam  
AbhTa dharātattvāvibhedena yaḥ prakāśaḥ prakāśate 
AbhTb sa eva śivanāthotra pṛthivī brahma tanmatam  
AbhTa dharātattvagatāḥ siddhīrvitarītuṃ samudyatān 
AbhTb prerayanti śivecchāto ye te mantramaheśvarāḥ  
AbhTa preryamāṇāstu mantreśā mantrāstadvācakāḥ sphuṭam 
AbhTb dharātattvagataṃ yogamabhyasya śivavidyayā  
AbhTa na tu pāśavasāṃkhyīyavaiṣṇavādidvitādṛśā 
AbhTb aprāptadhruvadhāmāno vijñānākalatājuṣaḥ  
AbhTa tāvattattvopabhogena ye kalpānte layaṃ gatāḥ 
AbhTb sauṣuptāvasthayopetāstetra pralayakevalāḥ  
AbhTa sauṣupte tattvalīnatvaṃ sphuṭameva hi lakṣyate 
AbhTb anyathā niyatasvapnasaṃdṛṣṭirjāyate kutaḥ  
AbhTa sauṣuptamapi citraṃ ca svacchāsvacchādi bhāsate 
AbhTb asvāpsaṃ sukhamityādismṛtivaicitryadarśanāt  
AbhTa yadaiva sa kṣaṇaṃ sūkṣmaṃ nidrāyaiva prabuddhyate 
AbhTb tadaiva smṛtireṣeti nārthajajñānajā smṛtiḥ  
AbhTa tena mūḍhairyaducyeta prabuddhasyāntarāntarā 
AbhTb tūlikādisukhasparśasmṛtireṣeti tatkutaḥ  
AbhTa māhākarmasamullāsasaṃmiśritamalābilāḥ 
AbhTb dharādhirohiṇo jñeyāḥ sakalā iha pudgalāḥ  
AbhTa asyaiva saptakasya svasvavyāpāraprakalpane 
AbhTb prakṣobho yastadevoktaṃ śaktīnāṃ saptakaṃ sphuṭam  
AbhTa śivo hyacyutacidrūpastisrastacchaktayastu yāḥ 
AbhTb tāḥ svātantryavaśopāttagrahītrākāratāvaśāt  
AbhTa tridhā mantrāvasānāḥ syurudāsīnā iva sthitāḥ 
AbhTb grāhyākāroparāgāttu grahītrākāratāvaśāt  
AbhTa sakalāntāstu tāstisra icchājñānakriyā matāḥ 
AbhTb saptadhetthaṃ pramātṛtvaṃ tatkṣobho mānatā tathā  
AbhTa yattu grahītṛtārūpasaṃvitsaṃsparśavarjitam 
AbhTb śuddhaṃ jaḍaṃ tatsvarūpamitthaṃ viśvaṃ trikātmakam  
AbhTa evaṃ jalādyapi vadedbhedairbhinnaṃ mahāmatiḥ 
AbhTb anayā tu diśā prāyaḥ sarvabhedeṣu vidyate  
AbhTa bhedo mantramaheśānteṣveṣa pañcadaśātmakaḥ 
AbhTb tathāpi sphuṭatābhāvātsannapyeṣa na carcitaḥ  
AbhTa etacca sūtritaṃ dhātrā śrīpūrve yadbravīti hi 
AbhTb savyāpārādhipatvenetyādinā jāgradāditām  
AbhTa abhinnepi śiventaḥsthasūkṣmabodhānusārataḥ 
AbhTb adhunā prāṇaśaktisthe tattvajāle vivicyate  
AbhTa bhedoyaṃ pāñcadaśyādiryathā śrīśaṃbhurādiśat 
AbhTb samasterthetra nirgrāhye tuṭayaḥ ṣoḍaśa kṣaṇāḥ  
AbhTa ṣaṭtriṃśadaṅgule cāre sāṃśadvyaṅgulakalpitāḥ 
AbhTb tatrādyaḥ paramādvaito nirvibhāgarasātmakaḥ  
AbhTa dvitīyo grāhakollāsarūpaḥ prativibhāvyate 
AbhTb antyastu grāhyatādātmyātsvarūpībhāvamāgataḥ  
AbhTa pravibhāvyo na hi pṛthagupāntyo grāhakaḥ kṣaṇaḥ 
AbhTb tṛtīyaṃ kṣaṇamārabhya kṣaṇaṣaṭkaṃ tu yatsthitam  
AbhTa tannirvikalpaṃ prodgacchadvikalpācchādanātmakam 
AbhTb tadeva śivarūpaṃ hi paraśaktyātmakaṃ viduḥ  
AbhTa dvitīyaṃ madhyamaṃ ṣaṭkaṃ parāparapadātmakam 
AbhTb vikalparūḍhirapyeṣā kramātprasphuṭatāṃ gatā  
AbhTa ṣaṭketra prathame devyastisraḥ pronmeṣavṛttitām 
AbhTb nimeṣavṛttitāṃ cāśu spṛśantyaḥ ṣaṭkatāṃ gatāḥ  
AbhTa evaṃ dvitīyaṣaṭkepi kiṃ tvatra grāhyavartmanā 
AbhTb uparāgapadaṃ prāpya parāparatayā sthitāḥ  
AbhTa ādyetra ṣaṭke tā devyaḥ svātantryollāsamātrataḥ 
AbhTb jighṛkṣitepyupādhau syuḥ pararūpādavicyutāḥ  
AbhTa asti cātiśayaḥ kaścittāsāmapyuttarottaram 
AbhTb yo vivekadhanairdhīraiḥ sphuṭīkṛtyāpi darśyate  
AbhTa kecittvekāṃ tuṭiṃ grāhye caikāmapi grahītari 
AbhTb tādātmyena vinikṣipya saptakaṃ saptakaṃ viduḥ  
AbhTa tadasyāṃ sūkṣmasaṃvittau kalanāya samudyatāḥ 
AbhTb saṃvedayante yadrūpaṃ tatra kiṃ vāgvikatthanaiḥ  
AbhTa evaṃ dharādimūlāntaṃ prakriyā prāṇagāminī 
AbhTb guruparvakramātproktā bhede pañcadaśātmake  
AbhTa kramāttu bhedanyūnatve nyūnatā syāttuṭiṣvapi 
AbhTb tasyāṃ hrāso vikalpasya sphuṭatā cāvikalpinaḥ  
AbhTa yathā hi ciraduḥkhārtaḥ paścādāttasukhasthitiḥ 
AbhTb vismaratyeva tadduḥkhaṃ sukhaviśrāntivartmanā  
AbhTa tathā gatavikalpepi rūḍhāḥ saṃvedane janāḥ 
AbhTb vikalpaviśrāntibalāttāṃ sattāṃ nābhimanvate  
AbhTa vikalpanirhrāsavaśena yāti vikalpavandhyā paramārthasatyā 
AbhTb saṃvitsvarūpaprakaṭatvamitthaṃ tatrāvadhāne yatatāṃ subuddhiḥ  
AbhTa grāhyagrāhakasaṃvittau saṃbandhe sāvadhānatā 
AbhTb iyaṃ sā tatra tatroktā sarvakāmadughā yataḥ  
AbhTa evaṃ dvayaṃ dvayaṃ yāvannyūnībhavati bhedagam 
AbhTb tāvattuṭidvayaṃ yāti nyūnatāṃ kramaśaḥ sphuṭam  
AbhTa ata eva śivāveśe dvituṭiḥ parigīyate 
AbhTb ekā tu sā tuṭistatra pūrṇā śuddhaiva kevalam  
AbhTa dvitīyā śivaśakti
rūpaiva sarvajñānakriyātmikā 
AbhTb tasyāmavahito yogī kiṃ na vetti karoti vā  
AbhTa tathā coktaṃ kallaṭena śrīmatā tuṭipātagaḥ 
AbhTb lābhaḥ sarvajñakartṛtve tuṭeḥ pātoparā tuṭiḥ  
AbhTa ādyāyāṃ tu tuṭau sarvaṃ sarvataḥ pūrṇamekatām 
AbhTb gataṃ kiṃ tatra vedyaṃ vā kāryaṃ vā vyapadeśabhāk  
AbhTa ato bhedasamullāsakalāṃ prāthamikīṃ budhāḥ 
AbhTb cinvanti pratibhāṃ devīṃ sarvajñatvādisiddhaye  
AbhTa saiva śaktiḥ śivasyoktā tṛtīyādituṭiṣvatha 
AbhTb mantrādidhi
nāthatacchaktimantreśādyāḥ kramoditāḥ  
AbhTa tāsu saṃdadhataścittamavadhānaikadharmakam 
AbhTb tattatsiddhisamāveśaḥ svayamevopajāyate  
AbhTa ata eva yathā bhedabahutvaṃ dūratā tathā 
AbhTb saṃvittau tuṭibāhulyādakṣārthāsaṃnikarṣavat  
AbhTa yathā yathā hi nyūnatvaṃ tuṭīnāṃ hrāsato bhidaḥ 
AbhTb tathā tathātinaikaṭyaṃ saṃvidaḥ syācchivāvadhi  
AbhTa śivatattvamataḥ proktamantikaṃ sarvatomutaḥ 
AbhTb ata eva prayatnoyaṃ tatpraveśe na vidyate  
AbhTa yathā yathā hi dūratvaṃ yatnayogastathā tathā 
AbhTb bhāvanākaraṇādīnāṃ śive niravakāśatām  
AbhTa ata eva hi manyante saṃpradāyadhanā janāḥ 
AbhTb tathā hi dṛśyatāṃ loko ghaṭādervedane yathā  
AbhTa prayatnavānivābhāti tathā kiṃ sukhavedane 
AbhTb āntaratvamidaṃ prāhuḥ saṃvinnaikaṭyaśālitām  
AbhTa tāṃ ca cidrūpatonmeṣaṃ bāhyatvaṃ tannimeṣatām 
AbhTb bhavināṃ tvantikopyevaṃ na bhātītyatidūratā  
AbhTa dūrepi hyantikībhūte bhānaṃ syāttvatra tatkatham 
AbhTb na ca bījāṅkuralatādalapuṣpaphalādivat  
AbhTa kramikeyaṃ bhavetsaṃvitsūtastatra kilāṅkuraḥ 
AbhTb bījāllatā tvaṅkurānno bījādiha sarvataḥ  
AbhTa saṃvittattvaṃ bhāsamānaṃ paripūrṇaṃ hi sarvataḥ 
AbhTb sarvasya kāraṇaṃ proktaṃ sarvatraivoditaṃ yataḥ  
AbhTa tata eva ghaṭepyeṣā prāṇavṛttiryadi sphuret 
AbhTb viśrāmyeccāśu tatraiva śivabīje layaṃ vrajet  
AbhTa na tu kramikatā kācicchivātmatve kadācana 
AbhTb anyanmantrādidhi
nāthādi kāraṇaṃ tattu saṃnidheḥ  
AbhTa śivābhedācca kiṃ cātha dvaite naikaṭyavedanāt 
AbhTb anayā ca diśā sarva sarvadā pravivecayan  
AbhTa bhairavāyata eva drāk ciccakreśvaratāṃ gataḥ 
AbhTb sa itthaṃ prāṇago bhedaḥ khecarīcakragopitaḥ  
AbhTa mayā prakaṭitaḥ śrīmacchāmbhavājñānuvartinā 
AbhTb atraivādhvani vedyatvaṃ prāpte yā saṃvidudbhavet  
AbhTa tasyāḥ svakaṃ yadvaicitryaṃ tadavasthāpadābhidham 
AbhTb jāgratsvapnaḥ suṣuptaṃ ca turyaṃ ca tadatītakam  
AbhTa iti pañca padānyāhurekasminvedake sati 
AbhTb tatra yaiṣā dharātattvācchivāntā tattvapaddhatiḥ  
AbhTa tasyāmekaḥ pramātā cedavaśyaṃ jāgradādikam 
AbhTb taddarśyate śaṃbhunāthaprasādādviditaṃ mayā  
AbhTa yadadhiṣṭheyameveha nādhiṣṭhātṛ kadācana 
AbhTb saṃvedanagataṃ vedyaṃ tajjāgratsamudāhṛtam  
AbhTa caitramaitrādibhūtāni tattvāni ca dharāditaḥ 
AbhTb abhidhākaraṇībhūtāḥ śabdāḥ kiṃ cābhidhā pramā  
AbhTa pramātṛmeyatanmānapramārūpaṃ catuṣṭayam 
AbhTb viśvametadadhiṣṭheyaṃ yadā jāgrattadā smṛtam  
AbhTa tathā hi bhāsate yattannīlamantaḥ pravedane 
AbhTb saṃkalparūpe bāhyasya tadadhiṣṭhātṛ bodhakam  
AbhTa yattu bāhyatayā nīlaṃ cakāstyasya na vidyate 
AbhTb kathaṃcidapyadhiṣṭhātṛbhāvastajjāgraducyate  
AbhTa tatra caitre bhāsamāne yo dehāṃśaḥ sa kathyate 
AbhTb abuddho yastu mānāṃśaḥ sa buddho mitikārakaḥ  
AbhTa prabuddhaḥ suprabuddhaśca pramāmātreti ca kramaḥ 
AbhTb cāturvidhyaṃ hi piṇḍasthanāmni jāgrati kīrtitam  
AbhTa jāgradādi catuṣkaṃ hi pratyekamiha vidyate 
AbhTb jāgrajjāgradabuddhaṃ tajjāgratsvapnastu buddhatā  
AbhTa ityādi turyātītaṃ tu sarvagatvātpṛthakkutaḥ 
AbhTb uktaṃ ca piṇḍagaṃ jāgradabuddhaṃ buddhameva ca  
AbhTa prabuddhaṃ suprabuddhaṃ ca caturvidhamidaṃ smṛtam 
AbhTb meyabhūmiriyaṃ mukhyā jāgradākhyānyadantarā  
AbhTa bhūtatattvābhidhānānāṃ yoṃśodhiṣṭheya ucyate 
AbhTb piṇḍasthamiti taṃ prāhuriti śrīmālinīmate  
AbhTa laukikī jāgradityeṣā saṃjñā piṇḍasthamityapi 
AbhTb yogināṃ yogasiddhyarthaṃ saṃjñeyaṃ paribhāṣyate  
AbhTa adhiṣṭheyasamāpattimadhyāsīnasya yoginaḥ 
AbhTb tādātmyaṃ kila piṇḍasthaṃ mitaṃ piṇḍaṃ hi piṇḍitam  
AbhTa prasaṃkhyānaikarūḍhānāṃ jñānināṃ tu taducyate 
AbhTb sarvatobhadramāpūrṇaṃ sarvato vedyasattayā  
AbhTa sarvasattāsamāpūrṇa viśvaṃ paśyedyato yataḥ 
AbhTb jñānī tatastataḥ saṃvittatvamasya prakāśate  
AbhTa lokayogaprasaṃkhyānatrairūpyavaśataḥ kila 
AbhTb nāmāni trīṇi bhaṇyante svapnādiṣvapyayaṃ vidhiḥ  
AbhTa yattvadhiṣṭhānakaraṇabhāvamadhyāsya vartate 
AbhTb vedyaṃ satpūrvakathitaṃ bhūtatattvābhidhāmayam  
AbhTa tatsvapno mukhyato jñeyaṃ tacca vaikalpike pathi 
AbhTb vaikalpikapathārūḍhavedyasāmyāvabhāsanāt  
AbhTa lokarūḍhopyasau svapnaḥ sāmyaṃ cābāhyarūpatā 
AbhTb utprekṣāsvapnasaṃkalpasmṛtyunmādādidṛṣṭiṣu  
AbhTa vispaṣṭaṃ yadvedyajātaṃ jāgranmukhyatayaiva tat 
AbhTb yattu tatrāpyavispaṣṭaṃ spaṣṭādhiṣṭhātṛ bhāsate  
AbhTa vikalpāntaragaṃ vedyaṃ tatsvapnapadamucyate 
AbhTb tadaiva tasya vettyeva svayameva hyabāhyatām  
AbhTa pramātrantarasādhārabhāvahānyasthirātmate 
AbhTb tatrāpi cāturvidhyaṃ tat prāgdiśaiva prakalpayet  
AbhTa gatāgataṃ suvikṣiptaṃ saṃgataṃ susamāhitam 
AbhTb atrāpi pūrvavannāma laukikaṃ svapna ityadaḥ  
AbhTa bāhyābhimatabhāvānāṃ svāpo hyagrahaṇaṃ matam 
AbhTb sarvādhvanaḥ padaṃ prāṇaḥ saṃkalpovagamātmakaḥ  
AbhTa padaṃ ca tatsamāpatti padasthaṃ yogino viduḥ 
AbhTb vedyasattāṃ bahirbhūtāmanapekṣyaiva sarvataḥ  
AbhTa vedye svātantryabhāg jñānaṃ svapnaṃ vyāptitayā bhajet 
AbhTb mānabhūmiriyaṃ mukhyā svapno hyāmarśanātmakaḥ  
AbhTa vedyacchāyovabhāso hi meyedhiṣṭhānamucyate 
AbhTb yattvadhiṣṭhātṛbhūtādeḥ pūrvoktasya vapurdhruvam  
AbhTa bījaṃ viśvasya tattūṣṇīṃbhūtaṃ sauṣuptamucyate 
AbhTb anubhūtau vikalpe ca yosau draṣṭā sa eva hi  
AbhTa na bhāvagrahaṇaṃ tena suṣṭhu suptatvamucyate 
AbhTb tatsāmyāllaukikīṃ nidrāṃ suṣuptaṃ manvate budhāḥ  
AbhTa bījabhāvothāgrahaṇaṃ sāmyaṃ tūṣṇīṃsvabhāvatā 
AbhTb mukhyā mātṛdaśā seyaṃ suṣuptākhyā nigadyate  
AbhTa rūpakatvācca rūpaṃ tattādātmyaṃ yoginaḥ punaḥ 
AbhTb rūpasthaṃ tatsamāpattyaudāsīnyaṃ rūpiṇāṃ viduḥ  
AbhTa prasaṃkhyānavataḥ kāpi vedyasaṃkocanātra yat 
AbhTb nāsti tena mahāvyāptiriyaṃ tadanusārataḥ  
AbhTa udāsīnasya tasyāpi vedyaṃ yena caturvidham 
AbhTb bhūtādi tadupādhyutthamatra bhedacatuṣṭayam  
AbhTa uditaṃ vipulaṃ śāntaṃ suprasannamathāparam 
AbhTb yattu pramātmakaṃ rūpaṃ pramāturupari sthitam  
AbhTa pūrṇatāgamanaunmukhyamaudāsīnyātparicyutiḥ 
AbhTb tatturyamucyate śaktisamāveśo hyasau mataḥ  
AbhTa sā saṃvitsvaprakāśā tu kaiściduktā prameyataḥ 
AbhTb mānānmātuśca bhinnaiva tadarthaṃ tritayaṃ yataḥ  
AbhTa meyaṃ māne mātari tat sopi tasyāṃ mitau sphuṭam 
AbhTb viśrāmyatīti saivaiṣā devī viśvaikajīvitam  
AbhTa rūpaṃ dṛśāhamityaṃśatrayamuttīrya vartate 
AbhTb dvāramātrāśritopāyā paśyāmītyanupāyikā  
AbhTa pramātṛtā svatantratvarūpā seyaṃ prakāśate 
AbhTb saṃvitturīyarūpaivaṃ prakāśātmā svayaṃ ca sā  
AbhTa tatsamāveśatādātmye mātṛtvaṃ bhavati sphuṭam 
AbhTb tatsamāveśoparāgānmānatvaṃ meyatā punaḥ  
AbhTa tatsamāveśanaikaṭyāttrayaṃ tattadanugrahāt 
AbhTb vedyādibhedagalanāduktā seyamanāmayā  
AbhTa mātrādyanugrahādādhā
nātsavyāpāreti bhaṇyate 
AbhTb jāgradādyapi devasya śaktitvena vyavasthitam  
AbhTa aparaṃ parāparaṃ ca dvidhā tatsā parā tviyam 
AbhTb rūpakatvādudāsīnāccyuteyaṃ pūrṇatonmukhī  
AbhTa daśā tasyāṃ samāpattī rūpātītaṃ tu yoginaḥ 
AbhTb pūrṇataunmukhyayogitvādviśvaṃ paśyati tanmayaḥ  
AbhTa prasaṃkhyātā pracayatasteneyaṃ pracayo matā 
AbhTb naitasyāmaparā turyadaśā saṃbhāvyate kila  
AbhTa saṃvinna kila vedyā sā vittvenaiva hi bhāsate 
AbhTb jāgradādyāstu saṃbhāvyāstisrosyāḥ prāgdaśā yataḥ  
AbhTa tritayānugrahātseyaṃ tenoktā trikaśāsane 
AbhTb manonmanamanantaṃ ca sarvārthamiti bhedataḥ  
AbhTa yattu pūrṇānavacchinnavapurānandanirbharam 
AbhTb turyātītaṃ tu tatprāhustadeva paramaṃ padam  
AbhTa nātra yogasya sadbhāvo bhāvanāderabhāvataḥ 
AbhTb aprameyeparicchinne svatantre bhāvyatā kutaḥ  
AbhTa yogādyabhāvatastena nāmāsminnādiśadvibhuḥ 
AbhTb prasaṃkhyānabalāttvetadrūpaṃ pūrṇatvayogataḥ  
AbhTa anuttarādiha proktaṃ mahāpracayasaṃjñitam 
AbhTb pūrṇatvādeva bhedānāmasyāṃ saṃbhāvanā na hi  
AbhTa tannirāsāya naitasyāṃ bheda ukto viśeṣaṇam 
AbhTb satatoditamityetatsarvavyāpitvasūcakam  
AbhTa na hyeka eva bhavati bhedaḥ kvacana kaścana 
AbhTb turyātīte bheda ekaḥ satatodita ityayam  
AbhTa mūḍhavādastena siddhamavibheditvamasya tu 
AbhTb śrīpūrvaśāstre tenoktaṃ padasthamaparaṃ viduḥ  
AbhTa mantrāstatpatayaḥ seśā rūpasthamiti kīrtyate 
AbhTb rūpātītaṃ parā śaktiḥ savyāpārāpyanāmayā  
AbhTa niṣprapañco nirābhāsaḥ śuddhaḥ svātmanyavasthitaḥ 
AbhTb sarvātītaḥ śivo jñeyo yaṃ viditvā vimucyate  
AbhTa iti śrīsumatiprajñācandrikāśāntatāmasaḥ 
AbhTb śrīśaṃbhunāthaḥ sadbhāvaṃ jāgradādau nyarūpayat  
AbhTa anye tu kathayantyeṣāṃ bhaṅgīmanyādṛśīṃ śritāḥ 
AbhTb yadrūpaṃ jāgradādīnāṃ tadidānīṃ nirūpyate  
AbhTa tatrākṣavṛttimāśritya bāhyākāragraho hi yaḥ 
AbhTb tajjāgratsphuṭamāsīnamanubandhi punaḥ punaḥ  
AbhTa ātmasaṃkalpanirmāṇaṃ svapno jāgradviparyayaḥ 
AbhTb layākalasya bhogosau malakarmavaśānnatu  
AbhTa sthirībhavenniśābhāvātsuptaṃ saukhyādyavedane 
AbhTb jñānākalasya malataḥ kevalādbhogamātrataḥ  
AbhTa bhedavantaḥ svatobhinnāścikīrṣyante jaḍājaḍāḥ 
AbhTb turye tatra sthitā mantratannāthādhīśvarāstrayaḥ  
AbhTa yāvadbhairavabodhāntaḥpraveśanasahiṣṇavaḥ 
AbhTb bhāvā vigaladātmīyasārāḥ svayamabhedinaḥ  
AbhTa turyātītapade saṃsyuriti pañcadaśātmake 
AbhTb yasya yadyatsphuṭaṃ rūpaṃ tajjāgraditi manyatām  
AbhTa yadevāsthiramābhāti sapūrvaṃ svapna īdṛśaḥ 
AbhTb asphuṭaṃ tu yadābhāti suptaṃ tattatpuropi yat  
AbhTa trayasyāsyānusaṃdhistu yadvaśādupajāyate 
AbhTb sraksūtrakalpaṃ tatturyaṃ sarvabhedeṣu gṛhyatām  
AbhTa yattvadvaitabharollāsadrāvitāśeṣabhedakam 
AbhTb turyātītaṃ tu tatprāhuritthaṃ sarvatra yojayet  
AbhTa layākale tu svaṃ rūpaṃ jāgrattatpūrvavṛtti tu 
AbhTb svapnādīti kramaṃ sarvaṃ sarvatrānusaredbudhaḥ  
AbhTa ekatrāpi prabhau pūrṇe citturyātītamucyate 
AbhTb ānandasturyamicchaiva bījabhūmiḥ suṣuptatā  
AbhTa jñānaśaktiḥ svapna uktaḥ kriyāśaktistu jāgṛtiḥ 
AbhTb na caivamupacāraḥ syātsarvaṃ tatraiva vastutaḥ  
AbhTa na cenna kvāpi mukhyatvaṃ nopacāropi tatkvacit 
AbhTb etacchrīpūrvaśāstre ca sphuṭamuktaṃ maheśinā  
AbhTa tatra svarūpaṃ śaktiśca sakalaśceti tattrayam 
AbhTb iti jāgradavastheyaṃ bhede pañcadaśātmake  
AbhTa akalau svapnasauṣupte turyaṃ mantrādivargabhāk 
AbhTb turyātītaṃ śaktiśaṃbhū trayodaśābhidhe punaḥ  
AbhTa svarūpaṃ jāgradanyattu prāgvatpralayakevale 
AbhTb svaṃ jāgratsvapnasupte dve turyādyatra ca pūrvavat  
AbhTa vijñānākalabhedepi svaṃ mantrā mantranāyakāḥ 
AbhTb tadīśāḥ śaktiśaṃbhvitthaṃ pañca syurjāgradādayaḥ  
AbhTa saptabhede tu mantrākhye svaṃ mantreśā maheśvarāḥ 
AbhTb śaktiḥ śaṃbhuśca pañcoktā avasthā jāgradādayaḥ  
AbhTa svarūpaṃ mantramāheśī śaktirmantramaheśvaraḥ 
AbhTb śaktiḥ śaṃbhurimāḥ pañca mantreśe pañcabhedake  
AbhTa svaṃ kriyā jñānamicchā ca śaṃbhuratra ca pañcamī 
AbhTb maheśabhede trividhe jāgradādi nirūpitam  
AbhTa vyāpārādādhipatyācca taddhānyā prerakatvataḥ 
AbhTb icchānivṛtteḥ svasthatvācchiva ekopi pañcadhā  
AbhTa ityeṣa darśitosmābhistattvādhvā vistarādatha 
C atha śrītantrāloke ekādaśamāhnikam
AbhTb kalādhvā vakṣyate śrīmacchāṃbhavājñānusārataḥ  b
AbhTa yathā pūrvoktabhuvanamadhye nijanijaṃ gaṇam 
AbhTb anuyatparato bhinnaṃ tattvaṃ nāmeti bhaṇyate  
AbhTa tathā teṣvapi tattveṣu svavargenugamātmakam 
AbhTb vyāvṛttaṃ paravargācca kaleti śivaśāsane  
AbhTa kecidāhuḥ punaryāsau śaktirantaḥ susūkṣmikā 
AbhTb tattvānāṃ sā kaletyuktā dharaṇyāṃ dhārikā yathā  
AbhTa atra pakṣadvaye vastu na bhinnaṃ bhāsate yataḥ 
AbhTb anugāmi na sāmānyamiṣṭaṃ naiyāyikādivat  
AbhTa anye vadanti dīkṣādau sukhasaṃgrahaṇārthataḥ 
AbhTb śivena kalpito vargaḥ kaleti samayāśrayaḥ  
AbhTa kṛtaśca devadevena samayoparamārthatām 
AbhTb na gacchatīti nāsatyo na cānyasamayodayaḥ  
AbhTa nivṛttiḥ pṛthivītattve pratiṣṭhāvyaktagocare 
AbhTb vidyā niśānte śāntā ca śaktyanteṇḍamidaṃ catuḥ  
AbhTa śāntātītā śive tattve kalātītaḥ paraḥ śivaḥ 
AbhTb nahyatra vargīkaraṇaṃ samayaḥ kalanāpi vā  
AbhTa yujyate sarvatodikkaṃ svātantryollāsadhāmani 
AbhTb svātantryāttu nijaṃ rūpaṃ boddhṛdharmādavicyutam  
AbhTa upadeśatadāveśaparamārthatvasiddhaye 
AbhTb bodhyatāmānayandevaḥ sphuṭameva vibhāvyate  
AbhTa yatotaḥ śivatattvepi kalāsaṃgatirucyate 
AbhTb aṇḍaṃ ca nāma bhuvanavibhāgasthitikāraṇam  
AbhTa prāhurāvaraṇaṃ tacca śaktyantaṃ yāvadasti hi 
AbhTb yadyapi prāk śivākhyepi tattve bhuvanapaddhatiḥ  
AbhTa uktā tathāpyapratighe nāsminnāvṛtisaṃbhavaḥ 
AbhTb nanvevaṃ dharaṇīṃ muktvā śaktau prakṛtimāyayoḥ  
AbhTa api cāpratighatvepi kathamaṇḍasya saṃbhavaḥ 
AbhTb atrāsmadguravaḥ prāhuryatpṛthivyādipañcakam  
AbhTa pratyakṣamidamābhāti tatonyannāsti kiṃcana 
AbhTb meyatve sthūlasūkṣmatvānmānatve karaṇatvataḥ  
AbhTa kartṛtollāsataḥ kartṛbhāve sphuṭatayoditam 
AbhTb triṃśattattvaṃ vibhedātma tadabhedo niśā matā  
AbhTa kāryatvakaraṇatvādivibhāgagalane sati 
AbhTb vikāsotkasvatantratve śivāntaṃ pañcakaṃ jaguḥ  
AbhTa śrīmatkālottarādau ca kathitaṃ bhūyasā tathā 
AbhTb pañcaitāni tu tattvāni yairvyāptamakhilaṃ jagat  
AbhTa pañcamantratanau tena sadyojātādi bhaṇyate 
AbhTb īśānāntaṃ tatra tatra dharādigaganāntakam  
AbhTa śivatattvamataḥ śūnyātiśūnyaṃ syādanāśrivṛtam 
AbhTb yattu sarvāvibhāgātma svatantraṃ bodhasundaram  
AbhTa saptatriṃśaṃ tu tatprāhustattvaṃ paraśivābhidham 
AbhTb tasyāpyuktanayādvedyabhāvetra parikalpite  
AbhTa yadāste hyanavacchinnaṃ tadaṣṭātriṃśamucyate 
AbhTb na cānavasthā hyevaṃ syāddṛśyatāṃ hi mahātmabhiḥ  
AbhTa yadvedyaṃ kiṃcidābhāti tatkṣaye yatprakāśate 
AbhTb tattattvamiti nirṇītaṃ ṣaṭtriṃśaṃ hṛdi bhāsate  
AbhTa tatkiṃ na kiṃcidvā kiṃcidityākāṅkṣāvaśe vapuḥ 
AbhTb cidānandasvatantraikarūpaṃ taditi deśane  
AbhTa saptatriṃśaṃ samābhāti tatrākāṅkṣā ca nāparā 
AbhTb taccāpi klṛptavedyatvaṃ yatra bhāti sa cinmayaḥ  
AbhTa aṣṭātriṃśattamaḥ sopi bhāvanāyopadiśyate 
AbhTb yadi nāma tataḥ saptatriṃśa eva punarbhavet  
AbhTa avibhāgasvatantratvacinmayatvādidharmatā 
AbhTb samaiva vedyīkaraṇaṃ kevalaṃ tvadhikaṃ yataḥ  
AbhTa dharāyāṃ guṇatattvānte māyānte kramaśaḥ sthitāḥ 
AbhTb gandho raso rūpamantaḥ sūkṣmabhāvakrameṇa tu  
AbhTa iti sthite naye śaktitattvāntepyasti saukṣmyabhāk 
AbhTb sparśaḥ kopi sadā yasmai yoginaḥ spṛhayālavaḥ  
AbhTa tatsparśānte tu saṃvittiḥ śuddhacidvyomarūpiṇī 
AbhTb yasyāṃ rūḍhaḥ samabhyeti svaprakāśātmikāṃ parām  
AbhTa ato vindurato nādo rūpamasmādato rasaḥ 
AbhTb ityuktaṃ kṣobhakatvena spande sparśastu no tathā  
AbhTa mataṃ caitanmaheśasya śrīpūrve yadabhāṣata 
AbhTb dhārikāpyāyinī boddhrī pavitrī cāvakāśadā  
AbhTa ebhiḥ śabdairvyavaharan nivṛttyādernijaṃ vapuḥ 
AbhTb pañcatattvavidhiḥ proktastritattvamadhunocyate  
AbhTa vijñānākalaparyantamātmā vidyeśvarāntakam 
AbhTb śeṣe śivastritattve syādekatattve śivaḥ param  
AbhTa imau bhedāvubhau tattvabhedamātrakṛtāviti 
AbhTb tattvādhvaivāyamitthaṃ ca na ṣaḍadhvasthiteḥ kṣatiḥ  
AbhTa prakṛt pumānyatiḥ kālo māyā vidyeśasauśivau 
AbhTb śivaśca navatattvepi vidhau tattvādhvarūpatā  
AbhTa evamaṣṭādaśākhyepi vidhau nyāyaṃ vadetsudhīḥ 
AbhTb yatra yatra hi bhogecchā tatprādhānyopayogataḥ  
AbhTa anyāntarbhāvanātaśca dīkṣānantavibhedabhāk 
AbhTb tena ṣaṭtriṃśato yāvadekatattvavidhirbhavet  
AbhTa tattvādhvaiva sa devena prokto vyāsasamāsataḥ 
AbhTb ekatattvavidhiścaiṣa suprabuddhaṃ guruṃ prati  
AbhTa śiṣyaṃ ca gatabhogāśamuditaḥ śaṃbhunā yataḥ 
AbhTb bhedaṃ visphārya visphārya śaktyā svacchandarūpayā  
AbhTa svātmanyabhinne bhagavānnityaṃ viśramayan sthitaḥ 
AbhTb itthaṃ tryātmādhvano bhedaḥ sthūlasūkṣmaparatvataḥ  
AbhTa meyabhāgagataḥ proktaḥ puratattvakalātmakaḥ 
AbhTb adhunā mātṛbhāgasthaṃ rūpaṃ tredhā nirūpyate  
AbhTa yatpramāṇātmakaṃ rūpamadhvano mātṛbhāgagam 
AbhTb padaṃ hyavagamātmatvasamāveśāttaducyate  
AbhTa tadeva ca padaṃ mantraḥ prakṣobhātpracyutaṃ yadā 
AbhTb guptabhāṣī yato mātā tūṣṇīṃbhūto vyavasthitaḥ  
AbhTa tathāpi na vimarśātma rūpaṃ tyajati tena saḥ 
AbhTb pramāṇātmavimarśātmā mānavatkṣobhabhāṅnatu  
AbhTa mantrāṇāṃ ca padānāṃ ca tenoktaṃ trikaśāsane 
AbhTb abhinnameva svaṃ rūpaṃ niḥspandakṣobhite param  
AbhTa audāsīnyaparityāge prakṣobhānavarohaṇe 
AbhTb varṇādhvā mātṛbhāge syāt pūrvaṃ yā kathitā pramā  
AbhTa sā tu pūrṇasvarūpatvādavibhāgamayī yataḥ 
AbhTb tata ekaikavarṇatvaṃ tattve tattve kṣamāditaḥ  
AbhTa kṛtvā śaive pare proktāḥ ṣoḍaśārṇā visargataḥ 
AbhTb tatra śaktiparispandastāvān prāk ca nirūpitaḥ  
AbhTa saṃkalayyocyate sarvamadhunā sukhasaṃvide 
AbhTb padamantravarṇamekaṃ puraṣoḍaśakaṃ dhareti ca nivṛttiḥ 
AbhTc tattvārṇamagninayanaṃ rasaśarapuramastramantrapadamanyā  
AbhTa munitattvārṇaṃ dvikapadamantraṃ vasvakṣibhuvanamaparakalā 
AbhTb agnyarṇatattvamekakapadamantraṃ sainyabhuvanamiti turyā  
AbhTa ṣoḍaśa varṇāḥ padamantratattvamekaṃ ca śāntyatīteyam 
AbhTb abhinavaguptenāryātrayamuktaṃ saṃgrahāya śiṣyebhyaḥ  
AbhTa soyaṃ samasta evādhvā bhairavābhedavṛttimān 
AbhTb tatsvātantryātsvatantratvamaśnuvānovabhāsate  
AbhTa tathāhi mātṛrūpastho mantrādhveti nirūpitaḥ 
AbhTb tathāhi cidvimarśena grastā vācyadaśā yadā  
AbhTa śivajñānakriyāyattamananatrāṇatatparā 
AbhTb aśeṣaśaktipaṭalīlīlālāmpaṭyapāṭavāt  
AbhTa cyutā mānamayādrūpāt saṃvinmantrādhvatāṃ gatā 
AbhTb pramāṇarūpatāmetya prayātyadhvā padātmatām  
AbhTa tathā hi māturviśrāntirvarṇānsaṃghaṭya tānbahūn 
AbhTb saṃghaṭṭanaṃ ca kramikaṃ saṃjalpātmakameva tat  
AbhTa vikalpasya svakaṃ rūpaṃ bhogāveśamayaṃ sphuṭam 
AbhTb ataḥ pramāṇatārūpaṃ padamasmadgururjagau  
AbhTa pramāṇarūpatāveśamaparityajya meyatām  
AbhTa gacchankalanayā yogādadhvā proktaḥ kalātmakaḥ 
AbhTb śuddhe prameyatāyoge sūkṣmasthūlatvabhāgini  
AbhTa tattvādhvabhuvanādhvatve krameṇānusaredguruḥ 
AbhTb prameyamānamātṝṇāṃ yadrūpamupari sthitam  
AbhTa pramātmātra sthitodhvāyaṃ varṇātmā dṛśyatāṃ kila 
AbhTb ucchalatsaṃvidāmātraviśrāntyāsvādayoginaḥ  
AbhTa sarvābhidhānasāmarthyādaniyantritaśaktayaḥ 
AbhTb sṛṣṭāḥ svātmasahottherthe dharāparyantabhāgini  
AbhTa āmṛśantaḥ svacidbhūmau tāvatorthānabhedataḥ 
AbhTb varṇaughāste pramārūpāṃ satyāṃ bibhrati saṃvidam  
AbhTa bālāstiryakpramātāro yepyasaṃketabhāginaḥ 
AbhTb tepyakṛtrimasaṃskārasārāmenāṃ svasaṃvidam  
AbhTa bhinnabhinnāmupāśritya yānti citrāṃ pramātṛtām 
AbhTb asyā cākṛtrimānantavarṇasaṃvidi rūḍhatām  
AbhTa saṃketā yānti cettepi yāntyasaṃketavṛttitām 
AbhTb anayā tu vinā sarve saṃketā bahuśaḥ kṛtāḥ  
AbhTa aviśrāntatayā kuryuranavasthāṃ duruttarām 
AbhTb bālo vyutpādyate yena tatra saṃketamārgaṇāt  
AbhTa aṅgulyādeśanepyasya nāvikalpā tathā matiḥ 
AbhTb vikalpaḥ śabdamūlaśca śabdaḥ saṃketajīvitaḥ  
AbhTa tenānanto hyamāyīyo yo varṇagrāma īdṛśaḥ 
AbhTb saṃvidvimarśasacivaḥ sadaiva sa hi jṛmbhate  
AbhTa yata eva ca māyīyā varṇāḥ sūtiṃ vitenire 
AbhTb ye ca māyīyavarṇeṣu vīryatvena nirūpitāḥ  
AbhTa saṃketanirapekṣāste prameti parigṛhyatām 
AbhTb tathā hi paravākyeṣu śruteṣvāvriyate nijā  
AbhTa pramā yasya jaḍosau no tatrārthebhyeti mātṛtām 
AbhTb śukavatsa paṭhatyeva paraṃ tatkramitaikabhāk  
AbhTa svātantryalābhataḥ svākyapramālābhe tu boddhṛtā 
AbhTb yasya hi svapramābodho vipakṣodbhedanigrahāt  
AbhTa vākyādivarṇapuñje sve sa pramātā vaśībhavet 
AbhTb yathā yathā cākṛtakaṃ tadrūpamatiricyate  
AbhTa tathā tathā camatkāratāratamyaṃ vibhāvyate 
AbhTb ādyāmāyīyavarṇāntarnimagne cottarottare  
AbhTa sakete pūrvapūrvāṃśamajjane pratibhābhidaḥ 
AbhTb ādyodrekamahattvepi pratibhātmani niṣṭhitāḥ  
AbhTa dhruvaṃ kavitvavaktṛtvaśālitāṃ yānti sarvataḥ 
AbhTb yāvaddhāmani saṃketanikārakalanojjhite  
AbhTa viśrāntaścinmaye kiṃ kiṃ na vetti kurute na vā 
AbhTb ata eva hi vāksiddhau varṇānāṃ samupāsyatā  
AbhTa sarvajñatvādisiddhau vā kā siddhiryā na tanmayī 
AbhTb taduktaṃ varadena śrīsiddhayogīśvarīmate  
AbhTa tena guptena guptāste śeṣā varṇāstviti sphuṭam 
AbhTb evaṃ māmātṛmānatvameyatvairyovabhāsate  
AbhTa ṣaḍvidhaḥ svavapuḥśuddhau śuddhiṃ sodhvādhigacchati 
AbhTb ekena vapuṣā śuddhau tatraivānyaprakāratām  
AbhTa antarbhāvyācarecchuddhimanusaṃdhānavān guruḥ 
AbhTb anantarbhāvaśaktau tu sūkṣmaṃ sūkṣmaṃ tu śodhayet  
AbhTa tadviśuddhaṃ bījabhāvāt sūte nottarasaṃtatim 
AbhTb śodhanaṃ bahudhā tattadbhogaprāptyekatānatā  
AbhTa tadādhipatyaṃ tattyāgastacchivātmatvavedanam 
AbhTb tallīnatā tannirāsaḥ sarvaṃ caitatkramākramāt  
AbhTa ata eva ca te mantrāḥ śodhakāścitrarūpiṇaḥ 
AbhTb siddhāntavāmadakṣādau citrāṃ śuddhiṃ vitanvate  
AbhTa anuttaratrikānāmakramamantrāstu ye kila 
AbhTb te sarve sarvadāḥ kintu kasyācit kvāpi mukhyatā  
AbhTa ataḥ śodhakabhāvena śāstre śrīpūrvasaṃjñite 
AbhTb parāparādimantrāṇāmadhvanyuktā vyavasthitiḥ  
AbhTa śodhakatvaṃ ca mālinyā devīnāṃ tritayasya ca 
AbhTb devatrayasya vaktrāṇāmaṅgānāmaṣṭakasya ca  
AbhTa kiṃ vātibahunā dvāravāstvādhāragurukrame 
AbhTb lokapāstravidhau mantrān muktvā sarvaṃ viśodhakam  
AbhTa yaccaitadadhvanaḥ proktaṃ śodhyatvaṃ śoddhṛtā ca yā 
AbhTb sā svātantryācchivābhede yuktetyuktaṃ ca śāsane  
AbhTa sarvametadvibhātyeva parameśitari dhruve 
AbhTb pratibimbasvarūpeṇa na tu bāhyatayā yataḥ  
AbhTa cidvyomnyeva śive tattaddehādimatirīdṛśī 
AbhTb bhinnā saṃsāriṇāṃ rajjau sarpasragvīcibuddhivat  
AbhTa yataḥ prāgdehamaraṇasiddhāntaḥ svapnagocaraḥ 
AbhTb dehāntarādirmaraṇe kīdṛgvā dehasaṃbhavaḥ  
AbhTa svapnepi pratibhāmātrasāmānyaprathanābalāt 
AbhTb viśeṣāḥ pratibhāsante na bhāvyantepi te yathā  
AbhTa śālagrāmopalāḥ keciccitrākṛtibhṛto yathā 
AbhTb tathā māyādibhūmyantalekhācitrahṛdaścitaḥ  
AbhTa nagarārṇavaśailādyāstadicchānuvidhāyinaḥ 
AbhTb na svayaṃ sadasanto no kāraṇākāraṇātmakāḥ  
AbhTa niyateścirarūḍhāyāḥ samucchedātpravartanāt 
AbhTb arūḍhāyāḥ svatantroyaṃ sthitaścidvyomabhairavaḥ  
AbhTa ekacinmātrasaṃpūrṇabhairavābhedabhāgini 
AbhTb evamasmītyanāmarśo bhedako bhāvamaṇḍale  
AbhTa sarvapramāṇairno siddhaṃ svapne kartrantaraṃ yathā 
AbhTb svasaṃvidaḥ svasiddhāyāstathā sarvatra buddhyatām  
AbhTa cittacitrapurodyāne krīḍedevaṃ hi vetti yaḥ 
AbhTb ahameva sthito bhūtabhāvatattvapurairiti  
AbhTa evaṃ jāto mṛtosmīti janmamṛtyuvicitratāḥ 
AbhTb ajanmanyamṛtau bhānti cittabhittau svanirmitāḥ  
AbhTa parehasaṃvidāmātraṃ paralokehalokate 
AbhTb vastutaḥ saṃvido deśaḥ kālo vā naiva kiṃcana  
AbhTa abhaviṣyadayaṃ sargo mūrtaścenna tu cinmayaḥ 
AbhTb tadavekṣyata tanmadhyāt kenaikopi dharādharaḥ  
AbhTa bhūtatanmātravargāderādhārādheyatākrame 
AbhTb ante saṃvinmayī śaktiḥ śivarūpaiva dhāriṇī  
AbhTa tasmātpratītirevetthaṃ kartrī dhartrī ca sā śivaḥ 
AbhTb tato bhāvāstatra bhāvāḥ śaktirādhārikā tataḥ  
AbhTa sāṃkalpikaṃ nirādhāramapi naiva patatyadhaḥ 
AbhTb svādhāraśaktau viśrāntaṃ viśvamitthaṃ vimṛśyatām  
AbhTa asyā ghanāhamityādirūḍhireva dharāditā 
AbhTb yāvadante cidasmīti nirvṛttā bhairavātmatā  
AbhTa maṇāvindrāyudhe bhāsa iva nīlādayaḥ śive 
AbhTb paramārthata eṣāṃ tu nodayo na vyayaḥ kvacit  
AbhTa deśe kāletra vā sṛṣṭirityetadasamañjasam 
AbhTb cidātmanā hi devena sṛṣṭirdikkālayorapi  
AbhTa jāgarābhimate sārdhahastatritayagocare 
AbhTb prahare ca pṛthak svapnāścitradikkālamāninaḥ  
AbhTa ata eva kṣaṇaṃ nāma na kiṃcidapi manmahe 
AbhTb kriyākṣaṇe vāpyekasmin bahvyaḥ saṃsyurdrutāḥ kriyāḥ  
AbhTa tena ye bhāvasaṃkocaṃ kṣaṇāntaṃ pratipedire 
AbhTb te nūnamenayā nāḍyā śūnyadṛṣṭyavalambinaḥ  
AbhTa tadya eṣa sato bhāvāñ śūnyīkartuṃ tathāsataḥ 
AbhTb sphuṭīkartuṃ svatantratvādīśaḥ sosmatprabhuḥ śivaḥ  
AbhTa taditthaṃ parameśāno viśvarūpaḥ pragīyate 
AbhTb na tu bhinnasya kasyāpi dharāderupapannatā  
AbhTa uktaṃ caitatpuraiveti na bhūyaḥ pravivicyate 
AbhTb bhūyobhiścāpi bāhyārthadūṣaṇaiḥ pravyaramyata  
AbhTa taditthameṣa nirṇītaḥ kalādervistarodhvanaḥ  
C atha śrītantrāloke dvādaśamāhnikam
AbhTb athādhvanosya prakṛta upayogaḥ prakāśyate  b
AbhTa itthamadhvā samastoyaṃ yathā saṃvidi saṃsthitaḥ 
AbhTb taddvārā śūnyadhīprāṇanāḍīcakratanuṣvatho  
AbhTa bahiśca liṅgamūrtyagnisthaṇḍilādiṣu sarvataḥ 
AbhTb tathā sthitaḥ samastaśca vyastaścaiṣa kramākramāt  
AbhTa āsaṃvittattvamābāhyaṃ yoyamadhvā vyavasthitaḥ 
AbhTb tatra tatrocitaṃ rūpaṃ svaṃ svātantryeṇa bhāsayet  
AbhTa sarvaṃ sarvatra rūpaṃ ca tasyāpi na na bhāsate 
AbhTb nahyavaccheditāṃ kvāpi svapnepi viṣahāmahe  
AbhTa evaṃ viśvādhvasaṃpūrṇaṃ kālavyāpāracitritam 
AbhTb deśakālamayaspandasadma dehaṃ vilokayet  
AbhTa tathā vilokyamānosau viśvāntardevatāmayaḥ 
AbhTb dhyeyaḥ pūjyaśca tarpyaśca tadāviṣṭo vimucyate  
AbhTa itthaṃ ghaṭaṃ paṭaṃ liṅgaṃ sthaṇḍilaṃ pustakaṃ jalam 
AbhTb yadvā kiṃcitkvacitpaśyettatra tanmayatāṃ vrajet  
AbhTa tatrārpaṇaṃ hi vastūnāmabhedenārcanaṃ matam 
AbhTb tathā saṃpūrṇarūpatvānusaṃdhirdhyānamucyate  
AbhTa saṃpūrṇatvānusaṃdhānamakampaṃ dārḍhyamānayan 
AbhTb tathāntarjalpayogena vimṛśañjapabhājanam  
AbhTa tatrārpitānāṃ bhāvānāṃ svakabhedavilāpanam 
AbhTb kurvaṃstadraśmisadbhāvaṃ dadyāddhomakriyāparaḥ  
AbhTa tathaivaṃkurvataḥ sarvaṃ samabhāvena paśyataḥ 
AbhTb niṣkampatā vrataṃ śuddhaṃ sāmyaṃ nandiśikhoditam  
AbhTa tathārcanajapadhyānahomavratavidhikramāt 
AbhTb paripūrṇāṃ sthitiṃ prāhuḥ samādhiṃ guravaḥ purā  
AbhTa atra pūjājapādyeṣu bahirantardvayasthitau 
AbhTb dravyaughe na vidhiḥ kopi na kāpi pratiṣiddhatā  
AbhTa kalpanāśuddhisaṃdhyādernopayogotra kaścana 
AbhTb uktaṃ śrītrikasūtre ca jāyate yajanaṃ prati  
AbhTa avidhijño vidhijñaścetyevamādi suvistaram 
AbhTb yadā yathā yena yatra svā samvittiḥ prasīdati  
AbhTa tadā tathā tena tatra tattadbhogyaṃ vidhiśca saḥ 
AbhTb laukikālaukikaṃ sarvaṃ tenātra viniyojayet  
AbhTa niṣkampatve sakampastu kampaṃ nirhrāsayedbalāt 
AbhTb yathā yenābhyupāyena kramādakramatopi vā  
AbhTa vicikitsā galatyantastathāsau yatnavānbhavet 
AbhTb dhīkarmākṣagatā devīrniṣiddhaireva tarpayet  
AbhTa vīravrataṃ cābhinandediti bhargaśikhāvacaḥ 
AbhTb tathāhi śaṅkā mālinyaṃ glāniḥ saṃkoca ityadaḥ  
AbhTa saṃsārakārāgārāntaḥ sthūlasthūṇāghaṭāyate 
AbhTb mantrā varṇasvabhāvā ye dravyaṃ yatpāñcabhautikam  
AbhTa yaccidātma prāṇijātaṃ tatra kaḥ saṃkaraḥ katham 
AbhTb saṃkarābhāvataḥ keyaṃ śaṅkā tasyāmapi sphuṭam  
AbhTa na śaṅketa tathā śaṅkā vilīyetāvahelayā 
AbhTb śrīsarvācāravīrālīniśācarakramādiṣu  
AbhTa śāstreṣu vitataṃ caitattatra tatrocyate yataḥ 
AbhTb śaṅkayā jāyate glāniḥ śaṅkayā vighnabhājanam  
AbhTa uvācotpaladevaśca śrīmānasmadgurorguruḥ 
AbhTb sarvāśaṅkāśaniṃ mārgaṃ numo māheśvaraṃ tviti  
AbhTa anuttarapadāptaye tadidamāṇavaṃ darśitābhyupāyamativistarānnanu vidāṃkurudhvaṃ budhāḥ 
C atha śrītantrāloke trayodaśamāhnikam
AbhTb athādhikṛtibhāhanaṃ ka iha vā kathaṃ vetyalaṃ vivecayitumucyate vividhaśaktipātakramaḥ  b
AbhTa tatra kecidiha prāhuḥ śaktipāta imaṃ vidhim 
AbhTb taṃ pradarśya nirākṛtya svamataṃ darśayiṣyate  
AbhTa tatredaṃ dṛśyamānaṃ satsukhaduḥkhavimohabhāk 
AbhTb viṣamaṃ sattathābhūtaṃ samaṃ hetuṃ prakalpayet  
AbhTa sovyaktaṃ tacca sattvādinānārūpamacetanam 
AbhTb ghaṭādivatkāryamiti heturekosya sā niśā  
AbhTa sā jaḍā kāryatādrūpyātkāryaṃ cāsyāṃ sadeva hi 
AbhTb kalādidharaṇīprāntaṃ jāḍyātsā sūtayekṣamā  
AbhTa teneśaḥ kṣobhayedenāṃ kṣobhosyāḥ sūtiyogyatā 
AbhTb puṃsaḥ prati ca sā bhogyaṃ sūtenādīn pṛthagvidhān  
AbhTa puṃsaśca nirviśeṣatve muktāṇūn prati kiṃ na tat 
AbhTb nimittaṃ karmasaṃskāraḥ sa ca teṣu na vidyate  
AbhTa iti cetkarmasaṃskārābhāvasteṣāṃ kutaḥ kila 
AbhTb na bhogādanyakarmāṃśaprasaṅgo hi duratyayaḥ  
AbhTa yugapatkarmaṇāṃ bhogo naca yuktaḥ krameṇa hi 
AbhTb phaledyatkarma tatkasmātsvaṃ rūpaṃ saṃtyajetkvacit  
AbhTa jñānātkarmakṣayaścettatkuta īśvaracoditāt 
AbhTb dharmādyadi kutaḥ sopi karmataścettaducyatām  
AbhTa nahi karmāsti tādṛkṣaṃ yena jñānaṃ pravartate 
AbhTb karmajatve ca tajjñānaṃ phalarāśau pateddhruvam  
AbhTa anyakarmaphalaṃ prācyaṃ karmarāśiṃ ca kiṃ dahet 
AbhTb īśasya dveṣarāgādiśūnyasyāpi kathaṃ kvacit  
AbhTa tathābhisaṃdhirnānyatra bhedahetorabhāvataḥ 
AbhTb nanvitthaṃ pradahejjñānaṃ karmajālāni karma hi  
AbhTa ajñānasahakārīdaṃ sūte svargādikaṃ phalam 
AbhTb ajñānaṃ jñānato naśyedanyakarmaphalādapi  
AbhTa upavāsādikaṃ cānyadduṣṭakarmaphalaṃ bhavet 
AbhTb niṣphalīkurute duṣṭaṃ karmetyaṅgīkṛtaṃ kila  
AbhTa ajñānamiti yatproktaṃ jñānābhāvaḥ sa cetsa kim 
AbhTb prāgabhāvothavā dhvaṃsa ādye kiṃ sarvasaṃvidām  
AbhTa kasyāpi vātha jñānasya prācyaḥ pakṣastvasaṃbhavī 
AbhTb na kiṃcidyasya vijñānamudapādi tathāvidhaḥ  
AbhTa nāṇurasti bhave hyasminnanādau konvayaṃ kramaḥ 
AbhTb bhāvinaḥ prāgabhāvaśca jñānasyeti sthite sati  
AbhTa muktāṇorapi sostyeva janmataḥ prāgasau naca 
AbhTb jñānaṃ bhāvi vimuktesminniti ceccarcyatāmidam  
AbhTa kasmājjñānaṃ na bhāvyatra nanu dehādyajanmataḥ 
AbhTb tatkasmātkarmaṇaḥ kṣaiṇyāttatkutojñānahānitaḥ  
AbhTa ajñānasya kathaṃ hāniḥ prāgabhāve hi saṃvidaḥ 
AbhTb ajñānaṃ prāgabhāvosau na bhāvyutpattyasaṃbhavāt  
AbhTa kasmānna bhāvi tajjñānaṃ nanu dehādyajanmataḥ 
AbhTb ityeṣa sarvapakṣaghno niśitaścakrakabhramaḥ  
AbhTa atha pradhvaṃsa evedamajñānaṃ tatsadā sthitam 
AbhTb muktāṇuṣviti teṣvastu māyākāryavijṛmbhitam  
AbhTa athājñānaṃ nahyabhāvo mithyājñānaṃ tu tanmatam 
AbhTb tadeva karmaṇāṃ svasminkartavye sahakāraṇam  
AbhTa vaktavyaṃ tarhi kiṃ karma yadā sūte svakaṃ phalam 
AbhTb tadaiva mithyājñānena satā hetutvamāpyate  
AbhTa atha yasminkṣaṇe karma kṛtaṃ tatra svarūpasat 
AbhTb mithyājñānaṃ yadi tatastādṛśātkamarṇaḥ phalam  
AbhTa prākpakṣe pralaye vṛtte prācyasṛṣṭipravartane 
AbhTb dehādyabhāvānno mithyājñānasya kvāpi saṃbhavaḥ  
AbhTa uttarasminpunaḥ pakṣe yadā yadyena yatra vā 
AbhTb kriyate karma tatsarvamajñānasacivaṃ tadā  
AbhTa avaśyamiti kasyāpi na karmaprakṣayo bhavet 
AbhTb yadyapi jñānavānbhūtvā vidhatte karma kiṃcana  
AbhTa viphalaṃ syāttu tatpūrvakarmarāśau tu kā gatiḥ 
AbhTb atha pralayakāle pi citsvabhāvatvayogataḥ  
AbhTa aṇūnā saṃbhavatyeva jñānaṃ mithyeti tatkutaḥ 
AbhTb svabhāvāditi cenmukte śive vā kiṃ tathā nahi  
AbhTa yaccādarśanamākhyātaṃ nimittaṃ pariṇāmini 
AbhTb pradhāne taddhi saṃkīrṇavaivittayobhayayogataḥ  
AbhTa darśanāya pumarthaikayogyatāsacivaṃ dhiyaḥ 
AbhTb ārabhya sate dharaṇīparyantaṃ tatra yaccitaḥ  
AbhTa buddhivṛttyaviśiṣṭatvaṃ puṃsprayāśarprasādataḥ 
AbhTb prakāśanāddhiyorthena saha bhogaḥ sa bhaṇyate  
AbhTa buddhirevāsmi vikṛtidharmikānyastu kopyasau 
AbhTb madvilakṣaṇa ekātmetyevaṃ vaivi yasaṃvidi  
AbhTa pumarthasya kṛtatvena sahakāriviyogataḥ 
AbhTb taṃ pumāṃsaṃ prati naiva sūte kiṃtvanyameva hi  
AbhTa atra puṃsotha mūlasya dharmodarśanatā dvayoḥ 
AbhTb athaveti vikalpoyamāstāmetattu bhaṇyatām  
AbhTa bhogo vivekaparyanta iti yattatra kovadhiḥ 
AbhTb vivekalābhe nikhilasūtidṛgyadi sāpi kim  
AbhTa sāmānyena viśeṣairvā prācye syādekajanmataḥ 
AbhTb uttare na kadācitsyādbhāvikālasya yogataḥ  
AbhTa kaiścideva viśeṣaiścetsarveṣāṃ yugapadbhavet 
AbhTb vivekonādisaṃyogātkā hyanyonyaṃ vicitratā  
AbhTa tasmātsāṃkhyadṛśāpīdamajñānaṃ naiva yujyate 
AbhTb ajñānena vinā bandhamokṣau naiva vyavasthayā  
AbhTa yujyete tacca kathitayuktibhirnopapadyate 
AbhTb bhāyākarmāṇudevecchāsadbhāvepi sthite tataḥ  
AbhTa na bandhamokṣayoryogo bhedahetorasaṃbhavāt 
AbhTb tasmādajñānaśabdena jñatvakartṛtvadharmaṇām  
AbhTa cidaṇūnāmāvaraṇaṃ kiṃcidvācyaṃ vipaścitā 
AbhTb āvāraṇātmanā siddhaṃ tatsvarūpādabhedavat  
AbhTa bhede pramāṇābhāvācca tadekaṃ nikhilātmasu 
AbhTb tacca kasmātprasūtaṃ syānmāyātaścetkathaṃ nu sā  
AbhTa kvacideva suvītaitanna tu muktātmanītyayam 
AbhTb prācyaḥ paryanuyogaḥ syānnimittaṃ cenna labhyate  
AbhTa utpattyabhāvatastena nityaṃ naca vinaśyati 
AbhTb tata evaikatāyāṃ cānyātmasādhāraṇatvataḥ  
AbhTa na vāvastvarthakāritvānna cittatsaṃvṛtitvataḥ 
AbhTb na caitenātmanāṃ yogo hetumāṃstadasaṃbhavāt  
AbhTa tenaikaṃ vastu sannityaṃ nityasaṃbaddhamātmabhiḥ 
AbhTb jaḍaṃ malaṃ tadajñānaṃ saṃsārāṅkurakāraṇam  
AbhTa tasya roddhrī yadā śaktirudāste śivaraśmibhiḥ 
AbhTb tadāṇuḥ spṛśyate spṛṣṭaḥ svake jñānakriye sphuṭe  
AbhTa samāviśedayaṃ sūryakāntorkeṇeva coditaḥ 
AbhTb roddhryāśca śaktermādhyasthyatāratamyavaśakramāat  
AbhTa vicitratvamataḥ prāhurabhivyaktau svasaṃvidaḥ 
AbhTb sa eṣa śaktipātākhyaḥ śāstreṣu paribhāṣyate  
AbhTa atrocyate malastāvaditthameṣa na yujyate 
AbhTb iti pūrvāhṇike proktaṃ punaruktau tu kiṃ phalam  
AbhTa malasya pākaḥ ko yaṃ syānnāśaśceditarātmanām 
AbhTb sa eko mala ityukternairmalyamanuṣajyate  
AbhTa atha pratyātmaniyatonādiśca prāgabhāvavat 
AbhTb malo naśyettathāpyeṣa nāśo yadi sahetukaḥ  
AbhTa hetuḥ karmeśvarecchā vā karma tāvanna tādṛśam 
AbhTb īśvarecchā svatantrā ca kvacideva tathaiva kim  
AbhTa ahetukosya nāśaścetprāgevaiṣa vinaśyatu 
AbhTb kṣaṇāntaraṃ sadṛk sūte iti cetsthirataiva sā  
AbhTa na ca nityasya bhāvasya hetvanāyattajanmanaḥ 
AbhTb nāśo dṛṣṭaḥ prāgabhāvastvavastviti tathāstu saḥ  
AbhTa athāsya pāko nāmaiṣa svaśaktipratibaddhatā 
AbhTb sarvānprati tathaiṣa syādruddhaśaktirviṣāgnivat  
AbhTa punarudbhūtaśaktau ca svakāryaṃ syādviṣāgnivat 
AbhTb muktā api na muktāḥ syuḥ śaktiṃ cāsya na manmahe  
AbhTa roddhrīti cetkasya nṛṇāṃ jñatvakartṛtvayoryadi 
AbhTb sadbhāvamātrādroddhṛtve śivamuktāṇvasaṃbhavaḥ  
AbhTa saṃnidhānātiriktaṃ ca na kiṃcitkurute malaḥ 
AbhTb ātmanā pariṇāmitvādanityatvaprasaṅgataḥ  
AbhTa jñatvakartṛtvamātraṃ ca pudgalā na tadāśrayāḥ 
AbhTb taccedāvāritaṃ hanta rūpanāśaḥ prasajyate  
AbhTa āvāraṇaṃ cādṛśyatvaṃ na ca tadvastunonyatām 
AbhTb karoti ghaṭavajjñānaṃ nāvarītuṃ ca śakyate  
AbhTa jñānenāvaraṇīyena tadevāvaraṇaṃ katham 
AbhTb na jñāyate tathā ca syādāvṛtirnāmamātrataḥ  
AbhTa roddhryāśca śakteḥ kastasya pratibandhaka īśvaraḥ 
AbhTb yadyapekṣāvirahitastatra prāgdattamuttaram  
AbhTa karmasāmyamapekṣyātha tasyecchā saṃpravartate 
AbhTb tasyāpi rūpaṃ vaktavyaṃ samatā karmaṇāṃ hi kā  
AbhTa bhogaparyāyamāhātmyātkāle kvāpi phalaṃ prati 
AbhTb virodhātkarmaṇī ruddhe tiṣṭhataḥ sāmyamīdṛśam  
AbhTa taṃ ca kālāṃśakaṃ devaḥ sarvajño vīkṣya taṃ malam 
AbhTb runddhe lakṣyaḥ sa kālaśca sukhaduḥkhādivarjanaiḥ  
AbhTa naitatkramikasaṃśuddhavyāmiśrākārakarmabhiḥ 
AbhTb tathaiva deye svaphale keyamanyonyaroddhṛtā  
AbhTa rodhe tayośca jātyāyurapi na syādataḥ patet 
AbhTb deho bhogadayoreva nirodha iti cennanu  
AbhTa jātyāyuṣpradakarmāṃśasaṃnidhau yadi śaṃkaraḥ 
AbhTb malaṃ runddhe bhogadātuḥ karmaṇaḥ kiṃ bibheti saḥ  
AbhTa śataśopi hlādatāpaśūnyāṃ saṃcinvate daśām 
AbhTb na ca bhaktirasāveśamiti bhūmnā vilokitam  
AbhTa athāpi kālamāhātmyamapekṣya parameśvaraḥ 
AbhTb tathā karoti vaktavyaṃ kālosau kīdṛśastviti  
AbhTa kiṃ cānādirayaṃ bhogaḥ karmānādi sapudgalam 
AbhTb tataśca bhogaparyāyakālaḥ sarvasya niḥsamaḥ  
AbhTa ādimattve hi kasyāpi vargādasmādbhavediyam 
AbhTb vaicitrī bhuktametena kalpametena tu dvayam  
AbhTa iyato bhogaparyāyātsyātsāmyaṃ karmaṇāmiti 
AbhTb anena nayabījena manye vaicitryakāraṇam  
AbhTa jagataḥ karma yatklaptaṃ tattathā nāvakalpate 
AbhTb anādimalasaṃcchannā aṇavo dṛkkriyātmanā  
AbhTa sarve tulyāḥ kathaṃ citrāṃ śritāḥ karmaparamparām 
AbhTb bhogalolikayā cetsā vicitreti kuto nanu  
AbhTa anādi karmasaṃskāravaicitryāditi cetpunaḥ 
AbhTb vācyaṃ tadeva vaicitryaṃ kuto niyatirāgayoḥ  
AbhTa mahimā cedayaṃ tau kiṃ nāsamañjasyabhāginau 
AbhTb īśvarecchānapekṣā tu bhedaheturna kalpate  
AbhTa athānāditvamātreṇa yuktihīnena sādhyate 
AbhTb vyavastheyamalaṃ tarhi malenāstu vṛthāmunā  
AbhTa tathāhi karma tāvanno yāvanmāyā na pudgale 
AbhTb vyāpriyeta na cāhetustadvṛttistanmito malaḥ  
AbhTa itthaṃ ca kalpite māyākārye karmaṇi hetutām 
AbhTb anādi karma cedgacchetkiṃ malasyopakalpanam  
AbhTa nanu mābhūnmalastarhi citrākāreṣu karmasu 
AbhTb santatyāvartamāneṣu vyavasthā na prakalpate  
AbhTa ādau madhye ca citratvātkarmaṇāṃ na yathā samaḥ 
AbhTb ātmākāropi kopyeṣa bhāvikāle tathā bhavet  
AbhTa itthamucchinna evāyaṃ bandhamokṣādikaḥ kramaḥ 
AbhTb ajñānādbandhanaṃ mokṣo jñānāditi parīkṣitam  
AbhTa virodhe svaphale caite karmaṇī samaye kvacit 
AbhTb udāsāte yadi tataḥ karmaitatpratibudhyatām  
AbhTa śivaśaktinipātasya kovakāśastu tāvatā 
AbhTb kvāpi kāle tayoretadaudāsīnyaṃ yadā tataḥ  
AbhTa kālāntare tayostadvadvirodhasyānivṛttitaḥ 
AbhTb ataśca na phaletānte tābhyāṃ karmāntaraṇi ca  
AbhTa ruddhāni prāptakālatvādgatābhyāmupabhogyatām 
AbhTb evaṃ sadaiva vārtāyāṃ dehapāte tathaiva ca  
AbhTa jāte vimokṣa ityāstāṃ śaktipātādikalpanā 
AbhTb athodāsīnatatkarmadvayayogakṣaṇāntare  
AbhTa karmāntaraṃ phalaṃ sūte tatkṣaṇepi tathā na kim 
AbhTb kṣaṇāntaretha te eva pratibandhavivarjite  
AbhTa phalataḥ pratibandhasya varjanaṃ kiṃkṛtaṃ tayoḥ 
AbhTb karmasāmyaṃ svarūpeṇa na ca tattāratamyabhāk  
AbhTa na śiveccheti tatkārye śaktipāte na tadbhavet 
AbhTb tirobhāvaśca nāmāyaṃ sa kasmādudbhavetpunaḥ  
AbhTa karmasāmyena yatkṛtyaṃ prāgevaitatkṛtaṃ kila 
AbhTb hetutve ceśvarecchāyā vācyaṃ pūrvavadeva tu  
AbhTa etenānyepi yepekṣyā īśecchāyāṃ prakalpitāḥ 
AbhTb dhvastāstepi hi nityānyahetvahetvādidūṣaṇāt  
AbhTa vairāgyaṃ bhogavairasyaṃ dharmaḥ kopi vivekitā 
AbhTb satsaṅgaḥ parameśānapūjādyabhyāsanityatā  
AbhTa āpatprāptistannirīkṣā dehe kiṃcicca lakṣaṇam 
AbhTb śāstrasevā bhogasaṃghapūrṇatā jñānamaiśvaram  
AbhTa ityapekṣyaṃ yadīśasya dūṣyametacca pūrvavat 
AbhTb vyabhicāraśca sāmastyavyastatvābhyāṃ svarūpataḥ  
AbhTa anyonyānupraveśaścānupapattiśca bhūyasī 
AbhTb tasmānna manmahe koyaṃ śaktipātavidheḥ kramaḥ  
AbhTa itthaṃ bhrāntiviṣāveśamūrcchānirmokadāyinīm 
AbhTb śrīśaṃbhuvadanodgīrṇāṃ vacmyāgamamahauṣadhīm  
AbhTa devaḥ svatantraścidrūpaḥ prakāśātmā svabhāvataḥ 
AbhTb rūpapracchādanakrīḍāyogādaṇuranekakaḥ  
AbhTa sa svayaṃ kalpitākāravikalpātmakakarmabhiḥ 
AbhTb badhnātyātmānameveha svātantryāditi varṇitam  
AbhTa svātantryamahimaivāyaṃ devasya yadasau punaḥ 
AbhTb svaṃ rūpaṃ pariśuddhaṃ satspṛśatyapyaṇutāmayaḥ  
AbhTa na vācyaṃ tu kathaṃ nāma kasmiṃścitpuṃsyasau tathā 
AbhTb nahi nāma pumānkaścidyasminparyanuyujyate  
AbhTa deva eva tathāsau cet svarūpaṃ cāsya tādṛśam 
AbhTb tādṛkprathāsvabhāvasya svabhāve kānuyojyatā  
AbhTa āhāsmatparameṣṭhī ca śivadṛṣṭau gurūttamaḥ 
AbhTb pañcaprakārakṛtyoktiśivatvānnijakarmaṇe  
AbhTa pravṛttasya nimittānāmapareṣāṃ kva mārgaṇam 
AbhTb channasvarūpatābhāse puṃsi yadyādṛśaṃ phalam  
AbhTa tatrāṇoḥ sata evāsti svātantryaṃ karmatohi tat 
AbhTb īśvarasya ca yā svātmatirodhitsā nimittatām  
AbhTa sābhyeti karmamalayoratonādivyavasthitiḥ 
AbhTb tirodhiḥ pūrṇarūpasyāpūrṇatvaṃ tacca pūraṇam  
AbhTa prati bhinnena bhāvena spṛhāto lolikā malaḥ 
AbhTb viśuddhasvaprakāśātmaśivarūpatayā vinā  
AbhTa na kiṃcidyujyate tena heturatra maheśvaraḥ 
AbhTb itthaṃ sṛṣṭisthitidhvaṃsatraye māyāmapekṣate  
AbhTa kṛtyai malaṃ tathā karma śivecchaiveti susthitam 
AbhTb yattu kasmiṃścana śivaḥ svena rūpeṇa bhāsate  
AbhTa tatrāsya nāṇuge tāvadapekṣye malakarmaṇī 
AbhTb aṇusvarūpatāhānau tadgataṃ hetutāṃ katham  
AbhTa vrajenmāyānapekṣatvamata evopapādayet 
AbhTb tena śuddhaḥ svaprakāśaḥ śiva evātra kāraṇam  
AbhTa sa ca svācchandyamātreṇa tāratamyaprakāśakaḥ 
AbhTb kulajātivapuṣkarmavayonuṣṭhānasaṃpadaḥ  
AbhTa anapekṣya śive bhaktiḥ śaktipātophalārthinām 
AbhTb yā phalārthitayā bhaktiḥ sā karmādyamapekṣate  
AbhTa tatotra syātphale bhedo nāpavarge tvasau tathā 
AbhTb bhogāpavargadvitayābhisaṃdhāturapi sphuṭam  
AbhTa prāgbhāgepekṣate karma citratvānnottare punaḥ 
AbhTb anābhāsitarūpopi tadābhāsitayeva yat  
AbhTa sthitvā mantrādi saṃgṛhya tyajetsosya tirobhavaḥ 
AbhTb śrīsāraśāstre bhagavānvastvetatsamabhāṣata  
AbhTa dharmādharmātmakairbhāvairanekairveṣṭayetsvayam 
AbhTb asandehaṃ svamātmānamavīcyādiśivāntake  
AbhTa tadvacchaktisamūhena sa eva tu viveṣṭayet 
AbhTb svayaṃ badhnāti deveśaḥ svayaṃ caiva vimuñcati  
AbhTa svayaṃ bhoktā svayaṃ jñātā svayaṃ caivopalakṣayet 
AbhTb svayaṃ bhuktiśca muktiśca svayaṃ devī svayaṃ prabhuḥ  
AbhTa svayamekākṣarā caiva yathoṣmā kṛṣṇavartmanaḥ 
AbhTb vastūktamatra svātantryātsvātmarūpaprakāśanam  
AbhTa śrīmanniśākulepyuktaṃ mithyābhāvitacetasaḥ 
AbhTb malamāyāvicāreṇa kliśyante svalpabuddhayaḥ  
AbhTa sphaṭikopalago reṇuḥ kiṃ tasya kurutāṃ priye 
AbhTb vyomnīva nīlaṃ hi malaṃ malaśaṃkāṃ tatastyajet  
AbhTa śrīmānvidyāguruścāha pramāṇastutidarśane 
AbhTb dharmādharmavyāptivināśāntarakāle śakteḥ pāto gāhanikairyaḥ pratipannaḥ  
AbhTa taṃ svecchātaḥ saṃgiramāṇāḥ stavakādyāḥ svātantryaṃ tattvayyanapekṣaṃ kathayeyuḥ 
AbhTb tāratamyaprakāśo yastīvramadhyamamandatāḥ  
AbhTa tā eva śaktipātasya pratyekaṃ traidhamāsthitāḥ 
AbhTb tīvratīvraḥ śaktipāto dehapātavaśātsvayam  
AbhTa mokṣapradastadaivānyakāle vā tāratamyataḥ 
AbhTb madhyatīvrātpunaḥ sarvamajñānaṃ vinivartate  
AbhTa svayameva yato vetti bandhamokṣatayātmatām 
AbhTb tatprātibhaṃ mahājñānaṃ śāstrācāryānapekṣi yat  
AbhTa pratibhācandrikāśāntadhvāntaścācāryacandramāḥ 
AbhTb tamastāpau hanti dṛśaṃ visphāryānandanirbharām  
AbhTa sa śiṣṭaḥ karmakartṛtvācchiṣyonyaḥ karmabhāvataḥ 
AbhTb śiṣṭaḥ sarvatra ca smārtapadakālakulādiṣu  
AbhTa uktaḥ svayaṃbhūḥ śāstrārthapratibhāpariniṣṭhitaḥ 
AbhTb yanmūlaṃ śāsanaṃ tena na riktaḥ kopi jantukaḥ  
AbhTa tatrāpi tāratamyotthamānantyaṃ dārḍhyakamprate 
AbhTb yuktiḥ śāstraṃ gururvādobhyāsa ityādyapekṣate  
AbhTa kampamānaṃ hi vijñānaṃ svayameva punarvrajet 
AbhTb kasyāpi dārḍhyamanyasya yuktyādyaiḥ kevaletaraiḥ  
AbhTa yathā yathā parāpekṣātānavaṃ prātibhe bhavet 
AbhTb tathā tathā gururasau śreṣṭho vijñānapāragaḥ  
AbhTa anyataḥ śikṣitānantajñānopi pratibhābalāt 
AbhTb yadvetti tatra tatrāsya śivatā jyāyasī ca sā  
AbhTa na cāsya samayitvādikramo nāpyabhiṣecanam 
AbhTb na santānādi no vidyāvrataṃ prātibhavartmanaḥ  
AbhTa ādividvānmahādevastenaiṣodhiṣṭhito yataḥ 
AbhTb saṃskārāstadadhiṣṭhānasiddhyai tattasya tu svataḥ  
AbhTa devībhirdīkṣitastena sabhaktiḥ śivaśāsane 
AbhTb dṛḍhatākampratābhedaiḥ sopi svayamatha vratāt  
AbhTa tapojapādergurutaḥ svasaṃskāraṃ prakalpayet 
AbhTb yato vājasineyākhya uktaṃ siñcetsvayaṃ tanum  
AbhTa ityādyupakramaṃ yāvadante tatpariniṣṭhitam 
AbhTb abhiṣikto bhavedevaṃ na bāhyakalaśāmbubhiḥ  
AbhTa śrīsarvavīraśrībrahmayāmalādau ca tattathā 
AbhTb nirūpitaṃ maheśena kiyadvā likhyatāmidam  
AbhTa itthaṃ prātibhavijñānaṃ kiṃ kiṃ kasya na sādhayet 
AbhTb yatprātibhādvā sarvaṃ cetyūce śeṣamahāmuniḥ  
AbhTa anye tvāhurakāmasya prātibho gururīdṛśaḥ 
AbhTb sāmagrījanyatā kāmye tenārimansaṃskṛto guruḥ  
AbhTa niyatermahimā naiva phale sādhye nivartate 
AbhTb abhiṣiktaścīrṇavidyāvratastena phalapradaḥ  
AbhTa asadetaditi prāhurguravastattvadarśinaḥ 
AbhTb śrīsomānandakalyāṇabhavabhūtipurogamāḥ  
AbhTa tathāhi trīśikāśāstravivṛtau tebhyadhurbudhāḥ 
AbhTb sāṃsiddhikaṃ yadvijñānaṃ taccintāratnamucyate  
AbhTa tadabhāve tadarthaṃ tadāhṛtaṃ jñānamādṛtam 
AbhTb evaṃ yo veda tattvena tasya nirvāṇagāminī  
AbhTa dīkṣā bhavatyasandigdhā tilājyāhutivarjitā 
AbhTb adṛṣṭamaṇḍalopyevaṃ yaḥ kaścidvetti tattvataḥ  
AbhTa sa siddhibhāgbhavennityaṃ sa yogī sa ca dīkṣitaḥ 
AbhTb avidhijño vidhānajño jāyate yajanaṃ prati  
AbhTa ityādibhistrīśikoktairvākyairmāheśvaraiḥ sphuṭam 
AbhTb jñānaṃ dīkṣādisaṃskārasatattvamiti varṇitam  
AbhTa jñānopāyastu dīkṣādikriyā jñānaviyoginām 
AbhTb ityetadadhunaivāstā svaprastāve bhaviṣyati  
AbhTa guruśāstrapramāṇāderapyupāyatvamaṃjasā 
AbhTb pratibhā paramevaiṣā sarvakāmadughā yataḥ  
AbhTa upāyayogakramato nirupāyamathākramam 
AbhTb yadrūpaṃ tatparaṃ tattvaṃ tatra tatra suniścitam  
AbhTa yastu prātibhabāhyātmasaṃskāradvayasundaraḥ 
AbhTb uktonanyopakāryatvātsa sākṣādvarado guruḥ  
AbhTa svamuktimātre kasyāpi yāvadviśvavimocane 
AbhTb pratibhodeti khadyotaratnatārendusūryavat  
AbhTa tataḥ prātibhasaṃvittyai śāstramasmatkṛtaṃ tvidam 
AbhTb yobhyasyetsa gururnaiva vastvarthā hi viḍambakāḥ  
AbhTa paropajīvitābuddhyā sarva itthaṃ na bhāsate 
AbhTb taduktyā na vinā vetti śaktipātasya māndyataḥ  
AbhTa sphuṭametacca śāstreṣu teṣu teṣu nirūpyate 
AbhTb kiraṇāyāṃ tathoktaṃ ca gurutaḥ śāstrataḥ svataḥ  
AbhTa jñānayogyāstathā keciccaryāyogyāstathāpare 
AbhTb śrīmannandiśikhātantre vitatyaitannirūpitam  
AbhTa praśnottaramukheneti tadabhagnaṃ nirūpyate 
AbhTb anirdeśyaḥ śivastatra kobhyupāyo nirūpyatām  
AbhTa iti praśne kṛte devyā śrīmāñchaṃbhurnyarūpayam 
AbhTb upāyotra vivekaikaḥ sa hi heyaṃ vihāpayan  
AbhTa dadātyasya ca suśroṇi prātibhaṃ jñānamuttamam 
AbhTb yadā pratibhayā yuktastadā muktaśca mocayet  
AbhTa paraśaktinipātena dhvastamāyāmalaḥ pumān 
AbhTb nanu prāgdīkṣayā mokṣodhunā tu prātibhātkatham  
AbhTa iti devyā kṛte praśne prāvartata vibhorvacaḥ 
AbhTb dīkṣayā mucyate jantuḥ prātibhena tathā priye  
AbhTa gurvāyattā tu sā dīkṣā badhyabandhanamokṣaṇe 
AbhTb prātibhosya svabhāvastu kevalībhāvasiddhidaḥ  
AbhTa kevalasya dhruvaṃ muktiḥ paratattvena sā nanu 
AbhTb nṛśaktiśivamuktaṃ hi tattvatrayamidaṃ tvayā  
AbhTa nā badhyo bandhane śaktiḥ karaṇaṃ kartṛtāṃ spṛśat 
AbhTb śivaḥ karteti tatproktaṃ sarvaṃ gurvāgamādaṇoḥ  
AbhTa punarvivekāduktaṃ taduttarottaramucyatām 
AbhTb kathaṃ vivekaḥ kiṃ vāsya devadeva vivicyate  
AbhTa ityukte parameśānyā jagādādiguruḥ śivaḥ 
AbhTb śivāditattvatritayaṃ tadāgamavaśādguroḥ  
AbhTa adhrottaragairvākyaiḥ siddhaṃ prātibhatāṃ vrajet 
AbhTb dīkṣāsicchinnapāśatvādbhāvanābhāvitasya hi  
AbhTa vikāsaṃ tattvamāyāti prātibhaṃ tadudāhṛtam 
AbhTb bhasmacchannāgnivatsphauṭyaṃ prātibhe gauravāgamāt  
AbhTa bījaṃ kāloptasaṃsiktaṃ yathā vardheta tattathā 
AbhTb yogayāgajapairuktairguruṇā prātibhaṃ sphuṭet  
AbhTa vivekotīndriyastveṣa yadāyāti vivecanam 
AbhTb paśupāśapatijñānaṃ svayaṃ nirbhāsate tadā  
AbhTa prātibhe tu samāyāte jñānamanyattu sendriyam 
AbhTb vāgakṣiśrutigamyaṃ cāpyanyāpekṣaṃ varānane  
AbhTa tattyajedbuddhimāsthāya pradīpaṃ tu yathā divā 
AbhTb prādurbhūtavivekasya syāccidindriyagocare  
AbhTa dūrācchrutyādivedhādivṛddhikrīḍāvicitritā 
AbhTb sarvabhāvavivekāttu sarvabhāvaparāṅmukhaḥ  
AbhTa krīḍāsu suviraktātmā śivabhāvaikabhāvitaḥ 
AbhTb māhātmyametatsuśroṇi prātibhasya vidhīyate  
AbhTa svacchāyādarśavatpaśyedbahirantargataṃ śivam 
AbhTb heyopādeyatattvajñastadā dhyāyennijāṃ citim  
AbhTa siddhijālaṃ hi kathitaṃ parapratyayakāraṇam 
AbhTb ihaiva siddhāḥ kāyānte mucyeranniti bhāvanāt  
AbhTa parabhāvanadārḍhyāttu jīvanmukto nigadyate 
AbhTb etatte prātibhe bhede lakṣaṇaṃ samudāhṛtam  
AbhTa śāpānugrahakāryeṣu tathābhyāsena śaktayā 
AbhTb teṣūdāsīnatāyāṃ tu mucyate mocayetparān  
AbhTa bhūtendriyādiyogena baddhoṇuḥ saṃsareddhruvam 
AbhTb sa eva pratibhāyuktaḥ śaktitattvaṃ nigadyate  
AbhTa tatpātāveśato muktaḥ śiva eva bhavārṇavāt 
AbhTb nanvācāryātsendriyaṃ tajjñānamuktamatīndriyam  
AbhTa vivekajaṃ ca tadbuddhyā tatkathaṃ syānnirindriyam 
AbhTb iti pṛṣṭobhyadhātsvāntadhiyorjāḍyaikavāsanāt  
AbhTa akṣatvaṃ pravivekena tacchittau bhāsakaḥ śivaḥ 
AbhTb saṃskāraḥ sarvabhāvānāṃ paratā parikīrtitā  
AbhTa manobuddhī na bhinne tu kasmiṃścitkāraṇāntare 
AbhTb viveke kāraṇe hyete prabhuśaktyupavṛṃhite  
AbhTa na manobuddhihīnastu jñānasyādhigamaḥ priye 
AbhTb parabhāvāttu tatsūkṣmaṃ śaktitattvaṃ nigadyate  
AbhTa vivekaḥ sarvabhāvānāṃ śuddhabhāvānmahāśayaḥ 
AbhTb buddhitattvaṃ tu triguṇamuttamādhamamadhyamam  
AbhTa aṇimādigataṃ cāpi bandhakaṃ jaḍamindriyam 
AbhTb nanu prātibhato muktau dīkṣayā kiṃ śivādhvare  
AbhTa ūcejñānā hi dīkṣāyāṃ bālavāliśayoṣitaḥ 
AbhTb pāśacchedādvimucyante prabuddhyante śivādhvare  
AbhTa tasmāddīkṣā bhavatyeṣu kāraṇatvena sundari 
AbhTb dīkṣayā pāśamokṣe tu śuddhabhāvādvivekajam  
AbhTa ityeṣa paṭhito granthaḥ svayaṃ ye boddhumakṣamāḥ 
AbhTb teṣāṃ śivoktisaṃvādādbodho dārḍhyaṃ vrajediti  
AbhTa śrīmanniśāṭane cātmaguruśāstravaśāttridhā 
AbhTb jñānaṃ mukhyaṃ svopalabdhi vikalpārṇavatāraṇam  
AbhTa mantrātmabhūtadravyāśadivyatattvādigocarā 
AbhTb śaṃkā vikalpamūlā hi śāmyetsvapratyayāditi  
AbhTa enamevārthamantaḥsthaṃ gṛhītvā mālinīmate 
AbhTb evamasyātmanaḥ kāle kasmiṃścidyogyatāvaśāt  
AbhTa śaivī saṃbadhyate śaktiḥ śāntā muktiphalapradā 
AbhTb tatsaṃbandhāttataḥ kaścittatkṣaṇādapavṛjyate  
AbhTa ityuktvā tīvratīvrākhyaviṣayaṃ bhāṣate punaḥ 
AbhTb ajñānena sahaikatvaṃ kasyacidvinivartate  
AbhTa rudraśaktisamāviṣṭaḥ sa yiyāsuḥ śivecchayā 
AbhTb bhuktimuktiprasiddhyarthaṃ nīyate sadguruṃ prati  
AbhTa tamārādhya tatastuṣṭāddīkṣāmāsādya śāṅkarīm 
AbhTb tatkṣaṇādvopabhogādvā dehapātācchivaṃ vrajet  
AbhTa asyārthā ātmanaḥ kācitkalanāmarśanātmikā 
AbhTb svaṃ rūpaṃ prati yā saiva kopi kāla ihoditaḥ  
AbhTa yogyatā śivatādātmyayogārhatvamihocyate 
AbhTb pūrvaṃ kiṃ na tathā kasmāttadaiveti na saṃgatam  
AbhTa tathābhāsanamujjhitvā na hi kālosti kaścana 
AbhTb svātantryāttu tathābhāse kālaśaktirvijṛmbhatām  
AbhTa natu paryanuyuktyai sā śive tanmahimoditā 
AbhTb nanu śaivī mahāśaktiḥ saṃbaddhaivātmabhiḥ sthitā 
AbhTc satyaṃ sācchādanātmā tu śāntā tveṣā svarūpadṛk  
AbhTa kṣobho hi bheda evaikyaṃ praśamastanmayī tataḥ  
AbhTa tayā śāntyā tu saṃbaddhaḥ sthitaḥ śaktisvarūpabhāk 
AbhTb tyaktāṇubhāvo bhavati śivastacchaktidārḍhyataḥ  
AbhTa tatrāpi tāratamyādivaśācchīghracirāditaḥ 
AbhTb dehapāto bhavedasya yadvā kāṣṭhāditulyatā  
AbhTa samastavyavahāreṣu parācīnitacetanaḥ 
AbhTb tīvratīvramahāśaktisamāviṣṭaḥ sa sidhyati  
AbhTa evaṃ prāgviṣayo grantha iyānanyatra tu sphuṭam 
AbhTb granthāntaraṃ madhyatīvraśaktipātāṃśasūcakam  
AbhTa ajñānarūpatā puṃsi bodhaḥ saṃkocite hṛdi 
AbhTb saṃkoce vinivṛtte tu svasvabhāvaḥ prakāśate  
AbhTa rudraśaktisamāviṣṭa ityanenāsya varṇyate 
AbhTb cihnavargo ya uktotra rudre bhaktiḥ suniścalā  
AbhTa mantrasiddhiḥ sarvatattvavaśitvaṃ kṛtyasaṃpadaḥ 
AbhTb kavitvaṃ sarvaśāstrārthaboddhṛtvamiti tatkramāt  
AbhTa svatāratamyayogātsyādeṣāṃ vyastasamastatā 
AbhTb tatrāpi bhuktau muktau ca prādhānyaṃ carcayedbudhaḥ  
AbhTa sa ityanto grantha eṣa dvitīyaviṣayaḥ sphuṭaḥ 
AbhTb anyastu mandatīvrākhyaśaktipātavidhiṃ prati  
AbhTa mandatīvrācchaktibalādyiyāsāsyopajāyate 
AbhTb śivecchāvaśayogena sadguruṃ prati sopi ca  
AbhTa atraiva lakṣitaḥ śāstre yaduktaṃ parameṣṭhinā 
AbhTb yaḥ punaḥ sarvatattvāni vettyetāni yathārthataḥ  
AbhTa sa gururmatsamaḥ prokto mantravīryaprakāśakaḥ 
AbhTb dṛṣṭāḥ saṃbhāvitāstena spṛṣṭāśca prītacetasā  
AbhTa narāḥ pāpaiḥ pramucyante saptajanmakṛtairapi 
AbhTb ye punardīkṣitāstena prāṇinaḥ śivacoditāḥ  
AbhTa te yatheṣṭaṃ phalaṃ prāpya padaṃ gacchantyanāmayam 
AbhTb kiṃ tattvaṃ tattvavedī ka ityāmarśanayogataḥ  
AbhTa pratibhānātsuḥṛtsaṅgādgurau jigamiṣurbhavet 
AbhTb evaṃ jigamiṣāyogādācāryaḥ prāpyate sa ca  
AbhTa tāratamyādiyogena saṃsiddhaḥ saṃskṛtopi ca 
AbhTb prāgbhedabhāgī jhaṭiti kramātsāmastyatoṃśataḥ  
AbhTa ityādibhedabhinno hi gurorlābha ihoditaḥ 
AbhTb tasmāddīkṣāṃ sa labhate sadya eva śivapradām  
AbhTa jñānarūpāṃ yathā vetti sarvameva yathārthataḥ 
AbhTb jīvanmuktaḥ śivībhūtastadaivāsau nigadyate  
AbhTa dehasaṃbandhitāpyasya śivatāyai yataḥ sphuṭā 
AbhTb asyāṃ bhedo hi kathanātsaṅgamādavalokanāt  
AbhTa śāstrātsaṃkramaṇātsāmyacaryāsaṃdarśanāccaroḥ 
AbhTb mantramudrādimāhātmyātsamastavyastabhedataḥ  
AbhTa kriyayā vāntarākārarūpaprāṇapraveśataḥ 
AbhTb tadā ca dehasaṃsthopi sa mukta iti bhaṇyate  
AbhTa uktaṃ ca śāstrayoḥ śrīmadratnamālāgamākhyayoḥ 
AbhTb yasminkāle tu guruṇā nirvikalpaṃ prakāśitam  
AbhTa tadaiva kila muktosau yantraṃ tiṣṭhati kevalam 
AbhTb prārabdhṛkarmasaṃbandhāddehasya sukhiduḥkhite  
AbhTa na viśaṅketa tacca śrīgamaśāstre nirūpitam 
AbhTb avidyopāsito deho hyanyajanmasamudbhuvā  
AbhTa karmaṇā tena bādhyante jñāninopi kalevare 
AbhTb jātyāyurbhogadasyaikapraghaṭṭakatayā sthitiḥ  
AbhTa uktaikavacanāddhiśca yatastenetisaṃgatiḥ 
AbhTb abhyāsayuktisaṃkrāntivedhaghaṭṭanarodhataḥ  
AbhTa hutervā mantrasāmarthyātpāśacchedaprayogataḥ 
AbhTb sadyonirvāṇadāṃ kuryātsadyaḥprāṇaviyojikām  
AbhTa tatra tveṣosti niyama āsanne maraṇakṣaṇe 
AbhTb tāṃ kuryānnānyathārabdhṛ karma yasmānna śuddhyati  
AbhTa uktaṃ ca pūrvamevaitanmaṃtrasāmarthyayogataḥ 
AbhTb prāṇairviyojitopyeṣa bhuṅkte śeṣaphalaṃ yataḥ  
AbhTa tajjanmaśeṣaṃ vividhamativāhya tataḥ sphuṭam 
AbhTb karmāntaranirodhena śīghramevāpavṛjyate  
AbhTa tasmātprāṇaharīṃ dīkṣāṃ nājñātvā maraṇakṣaṇam 
AbhTb vidadhyātparameśājñālaṅghanaikaphalā hi sā  
AbhTa ekastrikoyaṃ nirṇītaḥ śaktipātepyathāparaḥ 
AbhTb tīvramadhye tu dīkṣāyāṃ kṛtāyāṃ na tathā dṛḍhām  
AbhTa svātmano vetti śivatāṃ dehānte tu śivo bhavet 
AbhTb uktaṃ ca niśisaṃcārayogasaṃcāraśāstrayoḥ  
AbhTa vikalpāttu tanau sthitvā dahānte śivatāṃ vrajet 
AbhTb madhyamadhye śaktipāte śivalābhotsukopi san  
AbhTa bubhukṣuryatra yuktastadbhuktvā dehakṣaye śivaḥ 
AbhTb mandamadhye tu tatraiva tattve kvāpi niyojitaḥ  
AbhTa dehānte tattvagaṃ bhogaṃ bhuktvā paścācchivaṃ vrajet 
AbhTb tatrāpi tāratamyasya saṃbhavācciraśīghratā  
AbhTa bahvalpabhogayogaśca dehabhūmālpatākramaḥ 
AbhTb tīvramande madhyamande mandamande bubhukṣutā  
AbhTa kramānmukhyātimātreṇa vidhinaityantataḥ śivam 
AbhTb anye yiyāsurityādigranthaṃ prāggranthasaṃgatam  
AbhTa kurvanti madhyatīvrākhyaśaktisaṃpātagocaram 
AbhTb yadā pratibhayāviṣṭopyeṣa saṃvādayojanām  
AbhTa icchanyiyāsurbhavati tadā nīyeta sadgurum 
AbhTb na sarvaḥ pratibhāviṣṭaḥ śaktyā nīyeta sadgurum  
AbhTa iti brūte yiyāsutvaṃ vaktavyaṃ nānyathā dhruvam 
AbhTb rudraśaktisamāviṣṭo nīyate sadguruṃ prati  
AbhTa tena prāptavivekotthajñānasaṃpūrṇamānasaḥ 
AbhTb dārḍhyasaṃvādarūḍhyāderyiyāsurbhavati sphuṭam  
AbhTa uktaṃ nandiśikhātantre prācyaṣaṭke maheśinā 
AbhTb abhilāṣaḥ śive deve paśūnāṃ bhavate tadā  
AbhTa yadā śaivābhimānena yuktā vai paramāṇavaḥ 
AbhTb tadaiva te vimuktāstu dīkṣitā guruṇā yataḥ  
AbhTa prāptimātrācca te siddhasādhyā iti hi gamyate 
AbhTb tamārādhyeti tu grantho mandatīvraikagocaraḥ  
AbhTa navadhā śaktipātoyaṃ śaṃbhunāthena varṇitaḥ 
AbhTb idaṃ sāramiha jñeyaṃ paripūrṇacidātmanaḥ  
AbhTa prakāśaḥ paramaḥ śaktipātovacchedavarjitaḥ 
AbhTb tathāvidhopi bhogāṃśāvacchedenopalakṣitaḥ  
AbhTa aparaḥ śaktipātosau paryante śivatāpradaḥ 
AbhTb ubhayatrāpi karmādermāyāntarvartino yataḥ  
AbhTa nāsti vyāpāra ityevaṃ nirapekṣaḥ sa sarvataḥ 
AbhTb tena māyāntarāle ye rudrā ye ca tadūrdhvataḥ  
AbhTa svādhikārakṣaye taistairbhairavībhūyate haṭhāt 
AbhTb ye māyayā hyanākrāntāste karmādyanapekṣiṇaḥ  
AbhTa śaktipātavaśādeva tāṃ tāṃ siddhimupāśritāḥ 
AbhTb nanu pūjājapadhyānaśaṃkarāsevanādibhiḥ  
AbhTa te mantrāditvamāpannāḥ kathaṃ karmānapekṣiṇaḥ 
AbhTb maivaṃ tathāvidhottīrṇaśivadhyānajapādiṣu  
AbhTa pravṛttireva prathamameṣāṃ kasmādvivicyatām 
AbhTb karmatatsāmyavairāgyamalapākādi dūṣitam  
AbhTa īśvarecchā nimittaṃ cecchaktipātaikahetutā 
AbhTb japādikā kriyāśaktirevetthaṃ natu karma tat  
AbhTa karma tallokarūḍhaṃ hi yadbhogamavaraṃ dadat 
AbhTb tirodhatte bhoktṛrūpaṃ saṃjñāyā tu na no bharaḥ  
AbhTa teṣāṃ bhogotkatā kasmāditi ceddattamuttaram 
AbhTb citrākāraprakāśoyaṃ svatantraḥ parameśvaraḥ  
AbhTa svātantryāttu tirobhāvabandho bhogesya bhoktṛtām 
AbhTb puṣṇansvaṃ rūpameva syānmalakarmādivarjitam  
AbhTa uktaṃ seyaṃ kriyāśaktiḥ śivasya paśuvartinī 
AbhTb bandhayitrīti tatkarma kathyate rūpalopakṛt  
AbhTa jñātā sā ca kriyāśaktiḥ sadyaḥ siddhyupapādikā 
AbhTb avicchinnasvātmasaṃvitprathā siddhirihocyate  
AbhTa sā bhogamokṣasvātantryamahālakṣmīrihākṣayā 
AbhTb viṣṇvādirūpatā deve yā kācitsā nijātmanā  
AbhTa bhedayogavaśānmāyāpadamadhyavyavasthitā 
AbhTb tena tadrūpatāyogācchaktipātaḥ sthitopi san  
AbhTa tāvantaṃ bhogamādhatte paryante śivatāṃ natu 
AbhTb yathā svātantryato rājāpyanugṛhṇāti kaṃcana  
AbhTa īśaśaktisamāveśāttathā viṣṇvādayopyalam 
AbhTb māyāgarbhādhikārīyaśaktipātavaśāttataḥ  
AbhTa kopi pradhānapuruṣavivekī prakṛtergataḥ 
AbhTb utkṛṣṭāttata evāśu kopi buddhā vivekitām  
AbhTa kṣaṇātpuṃsaḥ kalāyāśca puṃmāyāntaravedakaḥ 
AbhTb kalāśrayasyāpyatyantaṃ karmaṇo vinivartanāt  
AbhTa jñānākalaḥ prāktanastu karmī tasyāśrayasthiteḥ 
AbhTb sa paraṃ prakṛterbudhne sṛṣṭiṃ nāyāti jātucit  
AbhTa māyādhare tu sṛjyetānanteśena pracodanāt 
AbhTb vijñānākalatāṃ prāptaḥ kevalādadhikārataḥ  
AbhTa malānmantratadīśādibhāvameti sadā śivāt 
AbhTb patyuḥ parasmādyastveṣa śaktipātaḥ sa vai malāt  
AbhTa ajñānākhyādviyokteti śivabhāvaprakāśakaḥ 
AbhTb nānyena śivabhāvo hi kenacitsaṃprakāśate  
AbhTa svacchandaśāstre tenoktaṃ vādināṃ tu śatatrayam 
AbhTb triṣaṣṭyabhyadhikaṃ bhrāntaṃ vaiṣṇavādyaṃ niśāntare  
AbhTa śivajñānaṃ kevalaṃ ca śivatāpattidāyakam 
AbhTb śivatāpattiparyantaḥ śaktipātaśca carcyate  
AbhTa anyathā kiṃ hi tatsyādyacchaivyā śaktyānadhiṣṭhitam 
AbhTb teneha vaiṣṇavādīnāṃ nādhikāraḥ kathaṃcana  
AbhTa te hi bhedaikavṛttitvādabhede dūravarjitāḥ 
AbhTb svātantryāttu maheśasya tepi cecchivatonmukhāḥ  
AbhTa dviguṇā saṃskriyāstyeṣāṃ liṅgoddhṛtyātha dīkṣayā 
AbhTb duṣṭādhivāsavigame puṣpaiḥ kumbhodhivāsyate  
AbhTa dviguṇosya sa saṃskāro netthaṃ śuddhe ghaṭe vidhiḥ 
AbhTb itthaṃ śrīśaktipātoyaṃ nirapekṣa ihoditaḥ  
AbhTa anayaiva diśā neyaṃ mataṅgakiraṇādikam 
AbhTb granthagauravabhītyā tu tallikhitvā na yojitam  
AbhTa purāṇepi ca tasyaiva prasādādbhaktiriṣyate 
AbhTb yayā yānti parāṃ siddhiṃ tadbhāvagatamānasāḥ  
AbhTa evakāreṇa karmādisāpekṣatvaṃ niṣidhyate 
AbhTb prasādo nirmalībhāvastena saṃpūrṇarūpatā  
AbhTa ātmanā tena hi śivaḥ svayaṃ pūrṇaḥ prakāśate 
AbhTb śivībhāvamahāsiddhisparśavandhye tu kutracit  
AbhTa vaiṣṇavādau hi yā bhaktirnāsau kevalataḥ śivāt 
AbhTb śivo bhavati tatraiṣa kāraṇaṃ na tu kevalaḥ  
AbhTa nirmalaścāpi tu prāptāvacchitkarmādyapekṣakaḥ 
AbhTb yayā yānti parāṃ siddhimityasyedaṃ tu jīvitam  
AbhTa śrīmānutpaladevaścāpyasmākaṃ paramo guruḥ 
AbhTb śaktipātasamaye vicāraṇaṃ prāptamīśa na karoṣi karhicit  
AbhTa adya māṃ prati kimāgataṃ yataḥ svaprakāśanavidhau vilambase 
AbhTb karhicitprāptaśabdābhyāmanapekṣitvamūcivān  
AbhTa durlabhatvamarāgitvaṃ śaktipātavidhau vibhoḥ 
AbhTb aparārdhena tasyaiva śaktipātasya citratām  
AbhTa vyavadhānacirakṣiprabhedādyairupavarṇitaiḥ 
AbhTb śrīmatāpyaniruddhena śaktimunmīlinīṃ vibhoḥ  
AbhTa vyācakṣāṇena mātaṅge varṇitā nirapekṣatā 
AbhTb sthāvarāntepi devasya svarūponmīlanātmikā  
AbhTa śaktiḥ patantī sāpekṣā na kvāpīti suvistarāt 
AbhTb evaṃ vicitrepyetasmiñchaktipāte sthite sati  
AbhTa tāratamyādibhirbhedaiḥ samayyādivicitratā 
AbhTb kaścidrudrāśatāmātrāpādanāttatprasādataḥ  
AbhTa śivatvaṃ kramaśo gacchet samayī yo nirūpyate 
AbhTb kaścicchuddhādhvabandhaḥ san putrakaḥ śīghramakramāt  
AbhTa bhogavyavadhinā kopi sādhakaściraśīghrataḥ 
AbhTb kaścitsaṃpūrṇakartavyaḥ kṛtyapañcakabhāgini  
AbhTa rūpe sthito guruḥ sopi bhogamokṣādibhedabhāk 
AbhTb samayyādicatuṣkasya samāsavyāsayogataḥ  
AbhTa kramākramādibhirbhedaiḥ śaktipātasya citratā 
AbhTb kramikaḥ śaktipātaśca siddhānte vāmake tataḥ  
AbhTa dakṣe mate kule kaule ṣaḍardhe hṛdaye tataḥ 
AbhTb ullaṅghanavaśādvāpi jhaṭityakramameva vā  
AbhTa uktaṃ śrībhairavakule pañcadīkṣāsusaṃskṛtaḥ 
AbhTb gururullaṅghitādhaḥsthasrotā vai trikaśāstragaḥ  
AbhTa jñānācārādibhedena hyuttarādharatā vibhuḥ 
AbhTb śāstreṣvadīdṛśacchrīmatsarvācārahṛdādiṣu  
AbhTa vāmamārgābhiṣiktastu daiśikaḥ paratattvavit 
AbhTb tathāpi bhairave tantre punaḥ saṃskāramarhati  
AbhTa śaivavaimalasiddhāntā ārhatāḥ kārukāśca ye 
AbhTb sarve te paśavo jñeyā bhairave mātṛmaṇḍale  
AbhTa kulakālīvidhau coktaṃ vaiṣṇavānā viśeṣataḥ 
AbhTb bhasmaniṣṭhāprapannānāmityādau naiva yogyatā  
AbhTa svacchandaśāstre saṃkṣepāduktaṃ ca śrīmaheśinā 
AbhTb anyaśāstrarato yastu nāsau siddhiphalapradaḥ  
AbhTa samayyādikramāllabdhābhiṣeko hi gururmataḥ 
AbhTb sa ca śaktivaśāditthaṃ vaiṣṇavādiṣu konvayaḥ  
AbhTa chadmāpaśravaṇādyaistu tajjñānaṃ gṛhṇato bhavet 
AbhTb prāyaścittamatastādṛgadhikāryatra kiṃ bhavet  
AbhTa phalākāṅkṣāyutaḥ śiṣyastadekāyattasiddhikaḥ 
AbhTb dhruvaṃ pacyeta narake prāyaścittyupasevanāt  
AbhTa tirobhāvaprakāroyaṃ yattādṛśi niyojitaḥ 
AbhTb gurau śivena tadbhaktiḥ śaktipātosya nocyate  
AbhTa yadātu vaicitryavaśājjānīyāttasya tādṛśam 
AbhTb viparītapravṛttatvaṃ jñānaṃ tasmādupāharet  
AbhTa taṃ ca tyajetpāpavṛttiṃ bhavettu jñānatatparaḥ 
AbhTb yathā caurādgṛhītvārthaṃ taṃ nigṛhṇāti bhūpatiḥ  
AbhTa vaiṣṇavādestathā śaivaṃ jñānamāhṛtya sanmatiḥ 
AbhTb sa hi bhedaikavṛttitvaṃ śivajñāne śrutepyalam  
AbhTa nojjhatīti dṛḍhaṃ vāmādhiṣṭhitastatpaśūttamaḥ 
AbhTb śivenaiva tirobhāvya sthāpito niyaterbalāt  
AbhTa kathaṅkāraṃ patipadaṃ prayātu paratantritaḥ 
AbhTb svacchandaśāstre proktaṃ ca vaiṣṇavādiṣu ye ratāḥ  
AbhTa bhramayatyeva tānmāyā hyamokṣe mokṣalipsayā 
AbhTb vaiṣṇavādiḥ śaivaśāstraṃ melayannijaśāsane  
AbhTa dhruvaṃ saṃśayamāpanna ubhayabhraṣṭatāṃ vrajet 
AbhTb svadṛṣṭau paradṛṣṭau ca samayollaṅghanādasau  
AbhTa pratyavāyaṃ yatobhyeti carettannedṛśaṃ kramam 
AbhTb uktaṃ śrīmadgahvare ca parameśena tādṛśam  
AbhTa nānyaśāstrābhiyuktaṣu śivajñānaṃ prakāśate 
AbhTb tanna saiddhāntiko vāme nāsau dakṣe sa no mate  
AbhTa kulakaule trike nāsau pūrvaḥ pūrvaḥ paratra tu 
AbhTb avacchinnonavacchedaṃ no vettyānantyasaṃsthitaḥ  
AbhTa sarvaṃsahastatodhaḥstha ūrdhvasthodhikṛto guruḥ 
AbhTb svātmīyādharasaṃsparśātprāṇayannadharāḥ kriyāḥ  
AbhTa saphalīkurute yattadūrdhvastho gururuttamaḥ 
AbhTb adhaḥsthadṛksthopyetādṛggurusevī bhavetsa yaḥ  
AbhTa tādṛkśaktinipāteddho yo drāgūrdhvamimaṃ nayet 
AbhTb tattadgirinadīprāyāvacchinne kṣetrapīṭhake  
AbhTa uttarottaravijñāne nādhikāryadharodharaḥ 
AbhTb uttarottaramācāryaṃ vidannapyadharodharaḥ  
AbhTa kurvannadhikriyāṃ śāstralaṅghī nigrahabhājanam 
AbhTb śaktipātabalādeva jñānayogyavicitratā  
AbhTa śrautaṃ cintāmayaṃ dvyātma bhāvanāmayameva ca 
AbhTb jñānaṃ taduttaraṃ jyāyo yato mokṣaikakāraṇam  
AbhTa tattvebhya uddhṛtiṃ kvāpi yojanaṃ sakalekale 
AbhTb kathaṃ kuryādvinā jñānaṃ bhāvanāmayamuttamam  
AbhTa yogī tu prāptatattattvasiddhirapyuttame pade 
AbhTb sadāśivādye svabhyastajñānitvādeva yojakaḥ  
AbhTa adhareṣu ca tattveṣu yā siddhiryogajāsya sā 
AbhTb vimocanāyāṃ nopāyaḥ sthitāpi dhanadāravat  
AbhTa yastūtpannasamastādhvasiddhiḥ sahi sadāśivaḥ 
AbhTb sākṣādeṣa kathaṃ martyānmocayedgurutāṃ vrajan  
AbhTa tenoktaṃ mālinītantre vicārya jñānayogite 
AbhTb yataśca mokṣadaḥ proktaḥ svabhyastajñānavānbudhaiḥ  
AbhTa tasmātsvabhyastavijñānataivaikaṃ gurulakṣaṇam 
AbhTb vibhāgastveṣa me proktaḥ śaṃbhunāthena darśyate  
AbhTa mokṣajñānaparaḥ kuryādguruṃ svabhyastavedanam 
AbhTb anyaṃ tyajetprāptamapi tathācoktaṃ śivena tat  
AbhTa āmodārthī yathā bhṛṅgaḥ puṣpātpuṣpāntaraṃ vrajet 
AbhTb vijñānārthī tathā śiṣyo gurorgurvantaraṃ vrajet  
AbhTa śaktihīnaṃ guruṃ prāpya mokṣajñāne kathaṃ śrayet 
AbhTb naṣṭamūle drume devi kutaḥ puṣpaphalādikam  
AbhTa uttarottaramutkarṣalakṣmīṃ paśyannapi sthitaḥ 
AbhTb adhame yaḥ pade tasmātkonyaḥ syāddaivadagdhakaḥ  
AbhTa yastu bhogaṃ ca mokṣaṃ ca vāñchedvijñānameva ca 
AbhTb svabhyastajñāninaṃ yogasiddhaṃ sa gurumāśrayet  
AbhTa tadabhāve tu vijñānamokṣayorjñāninaṃ śrayet 
AbhTb bhuktyaṃśe yoginaṃ yastatphalaṃ dātuṃ bhavetkṣamaḥ  
AbhTa phaladānākṣame yoginyapāyaikopadeśini 
AbhTb varaṃ jñānī yobhyupāyaṃ diśedapica mocayet  
AbhTa jñānī na pūrṇa evaiko yadi hyaṃśāṃśikākramāt 
AbhTb jñānānyādāya vijñānaṃ kurvītākhaṇḍamaṇḍalam  
AbhTa tenāsaṃkhyāngurūnkuryātpūraṇāya svasaṃvidaḥ 
AbhTb dhanyastu pūrṇavijñānaṃ jñānārthī labhate gurum  
AbhTa nānāgurvāgamasrotaḥpratibhāmātramiśritam 
AbhTb kṛtvā jñānārṇavaṃ svābhirvipruṅgiḥ plāvayenna kim  
AbhTa ā tapanānmoṭakāntaṃ yasya mesti gurukramaḥ 
AbhTb tasya me sarvaśiṣyasya nopadeśadaridratā  
AbhTa śrīmatā kallaṭenetthaṃ guruṇā tu nyarūpyata 
AbhTb ahamapyata evādhaḥśāstradṛṣṭikutūhalāt  
AbhTa tārkikaśrautabauddhārhadvaiṣṇavādīnnaseviṣi 
AbhTb lokādhyātmātimārgādikarmayogavidhānataḥ  
AbhTa saṃbodhotkarṣabāhulyātkramotkṛṣṭānvibhāvayet 
AbhTb śrīpūrvaśāstre praṣṭāro munayo nāradādayaḥ  
AbhTa prāgvaiṣṇavāḥ saugatāśca siddhāntādividastataḥ 
AbhTb kramāttrikārthavijñānacandrotsukitadṛṣṭayaḥ  
AbhTa tasmānna gurubhūyastve viśaṅketa kadācana 
AbhTb gurvantararate mūḍhe āgamāntarasevake  
AbhTa pratyavāyo ya āmnātaḥ sa itthamiti gṛhyatām 
AbhTb yo yatra śāstredhikṛtaḥ sa tatra gururucyate  
AbhTa tatrānadhikṛto yastu tadgurvantaramucyate 
AbhTb yathā tanmaṇḍalāsīno maṇḍalāntarabhūpatim  
AbhTa svamaṇḍalajigīṣuḥ sansevamāno vinaśyati 
AbhTb tathottarottarajñānasiddhiprepsuḥ samāśrayan  
AbhTa adharādharamācāryaṃ vināśamadhigacchati 
AbhTb evamevordhvavartiṣṇorāgamātsiddhivāñchakaḥ  
AbhTa māyīyaśāstranirato vināśaṃ pratipadyate 
AbhTb uktaṃ ca śrīmadānande karma saṃśritya bhāvataḥ  
AbhTa jugupsate tattasmiṃśca viphalenyatsamāśrayet 
AbhTb dināddinaṃ hrasaṃstvevaṃ pacyate rauravādiṣu  
AbhTa yastūrdhvordhvapathaprepsuradharaṃ gurumāgamam 
AbhTb jihāsecchaktipātena sa dhanyaḥ pronmukhīkṛtaḥ  
AbhTa ata eveha śāstreṣu śaiveṣveva nirūpyate 
AbhTb śāstrāntarārthānāśvastānprati saṃskārako vidhiḥ  
AbhTa ataścāpyuttamaṃ śaivaṃ yonyatra patitaḥ sahi 
AbhTb ihānugrāhya ūrdhvordhvaṃ netastu patitaḥ kvacit  
AbhTa ata eva hi sarvajñairbrahmaviṣṇvādibhirnije 
AbhTb na śāsane samāmnātaṃ liṅgoddhārādi kiṃcana  
AbhTa itthaṃ viṣṇvādayaḥ śaivaparamārthaikavedinaḥ 
AbhTb kāṃścitprati tathādikṣuste mohādvimatiṃ śritāḥ  
AbhTa tathāvidhāmeva matiṃ satyasaṃsparśanākṣamām 
AbhTb dṛṣṭvaiṣāṃ brahmaviṣṇvādyairbuddhairapi tathoditam  
AbhTa ityeṣa yuktyāgamataḥ śaktipāto vivecitaḥ 
C atha śrītantrāloke caturdaśamāhnikam
AbhTa tirobhāvasvarūpaṃ tu kathyamānaṃ vivicyatām 
AbhTb svabhāvāt parameśāno niyatyaniyatikramam  
AbhTa spṛśanprakāśate yena tataḥ svacchanda ucyate 
AbhTb niyatiṃ karmaphalayorāśrityaiṣa maheśvaraḥ  
AbhTa sṛṣṭisaṃsthitisaṃhārānvidhattevāntarasthitīn 
AbhTb mahāsarge punaḥ sṛṣṭisaṃhārānantyaśālini  
AbhTa ekaḥ sa devo viśvātmā niyatityāgataḥ prabhuḥ 
AbhTb avāntare yā ca sṛṣṭiḥ sthitiścātrāpyayantritam  
AbhTa nojjhatyeṣa vapustyaktaniyatiśca sthitotra tat 
AbhTb niyatyaiva yadā caiṣa svarūpācchādanakramāt  
AbhTa bhuṅkte duḥkhavimohādi tadā karmaphalakramaḥ 
AbhTb tyaktvā tu niyamaṃ kārmaṃ duḥkhamohaparītatām  
AbhTa bibhāsayiṣurāsteyaṃ tirodhānenapekṣakaḥ 
AbhTb yathā prakāśasvātantryāt pratibuddhopyabuddhavat  
AbhTa āste tadvadanuttīrṇopyuttīrṇa iva ceṣṭate 
AbhTb yathā ca buddhastāṃ mūḍhaceṣṭāṃ kurvannapi dviṣan  
AbhTa hṛdyāste mūḍha evaṃ hi prabuddhānāṃ viceṣṭitam 
AbhTb śrīvidyādhipatiścāha mānastotre tadīdṛśam  
AbhTa ye yauṣmāke śāsanamārge kṛtadīkṣāḥ saṃgacchanto mohavaśādvipratipattim 
AbhTb nūnaṃ teṣā nāsti bhavadbhānuniyogaḥ saṅkocaḥ kiṃ sūryakaraistāmarasānām  
AbhTa jñātajñeyā dhātṛpadasthā api santo ye tvanmārgātkāpathagāstepi na samyaka 
AbhTb prāyasteṣāṃ laiṅgikabuddhyādisamuttho mithyābodhaḥ sarpavasādīpajakalpaḥ  
AbhTa yasmādviddhaṃ sūtakamukhyena nu tāmraṃ tadyadbhūyaḥ svāṃ prakṛtiṃ no samupeyāt 
AbhTb no taiḥ pītaṃ bhūtalasaṃsthairamṛtaṃ tadyeṣāṃ tṛṭkṣudduḥkhavibādhāḥ punarasmin  
AbhTa tataḥ prabuddhaceṣṭāsau mantracaryārcanādikā 
AbhTb dveṣeddhāntardahatyenaṃ dāhaḥ śaṅkaiva sā yataḥ  
AbhTa na cāsya karmamahimā tādṛgyenetthamāsta saḥ 
AbhTb kiṃ hi tatkarma kasmādvā pūrveṇātra samo vidhiḥ  
AbhTa tasmātsā parameśecchā yayāyaṃ mohitastathā 
AbhTb anantakālasaṃvedyaduḥkhapātratvamīhate  
AbhTa tatrāpi cecchāvaicitryādihāmutrobhayātmakaḥ 
AbhTb duḥkhasyāpi vibhedosti ciraśaighryakṛtastathā  
AbhTa kālakāmāndhakādīnāṃ paulastyapuravāsinām 
AbhTb tathānyeṣāṃ tirobhāvastāvadduḥkho hyamutra ca  
AbhTa anyopi ca tirobhāvaḥ samayollaṅghanātmakaḥ 
AbhTb yaduktaṃ parameśena śrīmadānandagahvare  
AbhTa samayollaṅghanāddevi kravyādatvaṃ śataṃ samāḥ 
AbhTb tatrāpi mandatīvrādibhedādbahuvidhaḥ kramaḥ  
AbhTa svātantryācca maheśasya tirobhūtopyasau svayam 
AbhTb paradvāreṇa vābhyeti bhūyonugrahamapyalam  
AbhTa bhūyonugrahataḥ prāyaścittādyācaraṇe sati 
AbhTb anusāreṇa dīkṣādau kṛte syācchivatāmayaḥ  
AbhTa tirobhūtaḥ paretāsurapi bandhusuhṛdgurūn 
AbhTb ālambya śaktipātena dīkṣādyairanugṛhyate  
AbhTa tatrāpi kālaśīghratvaciratvādivibhedatām 
AbhTb tathaiti śaktipātosau yenāyāti śivātmatām  
AbhTa itthaṃ sṛṣṭisthitidhvaṃsatirobhāvamanugrahaḥ 
AbhTb iti pañcasu kartṛtvaṃ śivatvaṃ saṃvidātmanaḥ  
AbhTa pañcakṛtyasvatantratvasaṃpūrṇasvātmamāninaḥ 
AbhTb yoginorcājapadhyānayogāḥ saṃsyuḥ sadoditāḥ  
AbhTa aindrajālikavṛttānte na rajyeta kadācana 
AbhTb sādāśivopi yo bhogo bandhaḥ sopyucitātmanām  
AbhTa jñātṛtvameva śivatā svātantryaṃ tadihocyate 
AbhTb kulālavattu kartṛtvaṃ na mukhyaṃ tadadhiṣṭhiteḥ  
AbhTa iti jñātvā grahītavyā naiva jātvapi khaṇḍanā 
AbhTb śivohaṃ cenmadicchānuvarti kiṃ na jagattviti  
AbhTa mamecchāmanuvartantāmityatrāhaṃvidi sphuret 
AbhTb śivo vā parameśāno dehādiratha nirmitaḥ  
AbhTa śivasya tāvadastyetaddehastveṣa tathā tvayā 
AbhTb kṛtaḥ kānyā dehatāsya tatkiṃ syādvācyatāpadam  
AbhTa uktaṃ ca siddhasantānaśrīmadūrmimahākule 
AbhTb pavanabhramaṇaprāṇavikṣepādikṛtaśramāḥ  
AbhTa kuhakādiṣu ye bhrāntāste bhrāntāḥ parame pade
