AbhTb sarvatra bahumānena yāpyutkrāntirvimuktaye  
AbhTa proktā sā sāraśāstreṣu bhogopāyatayoditā 
AbhTb yadi sarvagatā devo vadotkramya kva yāsyati  
AbhTa athāsarvagatastarhi ghaṭatulyastadā bhavet 
AbhTb utkrāntividhiyogoyamekadeśena kathyate  
AbhTa niraṃśe śivatattve tu kathamutkrāntisaṃgatiḥ 
AbhTb yathā dharādau vāyvante bhṛgvambvagnyupavāsakaiḥ  
AbhTa ātmano yojanaṃ vyomni tadvadutkrāntivartanā 
AbhTb tasmānnotkramayejjīvaṃ paratattvasamīhayā  
AbhTa śrīpūrvaśāstre tūktaṃ yadutkrānterlakṣaṇaṃ na tat 
AbhTb muktyupāyatayā kiṃtu bhogahānyai tathaiṣaṇāt  
AbhTa japadhyānādisaṃsiddhaḥ svātantryācchaktipātataḥ 
AbhTb bhogaṃ prati viraktaśceditthaṃ dehaṃ tyajediti  
AbhTa svacchandamṛtyorapi yad bhīṣmādeḥ śrūyate kila 
AbhTb bhogavairasyasaṃprāptau jīvitāntopasarpaṇam  
AbhTa yogamantrāmṛtadravyavarādyaiḥ siddhibhāktanuḥ 
AbhTb hātuṃ nahyanyathā śakyā vinoktakramayogataḥ  
AbhTa uktaṃ ca mālinītantre parameśena tādṛśam 
AbhTb sarvamapyathavā bhogaṃ manyamāno virūpakam  
AbhTa ityādi vadatā sarvairalakṣyāntaḥsatattvakam 
AbhTb evaṃ sṛṣṭyādikartavyasvasvātantryopadeśanam  
AbhTa yatsaiva mukhyadīkṣā syācchiṣyasya śivadāyinī 
AbhTb uktaṃ śrīniśicāre ca bhairavīyeṇa tejasā  
AbhTa vyāptaṃ viśvaṃ prapaśyanti vikalpojjhitacetasaḥ 
AbhTb vikalpayuktacittastu piṇḍapātācchivaṃ vrajet  
AbhTa bāhyadīkṣādiyogena caryāsamayakalpanaiḥ 
AbhTb avikalpastathādyaiva jīvanmukto na saṃśayaḥ  
AbhTa saṃsārajīrṇatarumūlakalāpakalpasaṃkalpasāntaratayā paramārthavahneḥ 
AbhTb syurvisphuliṅgakaṇikā api cettadante dedīpyate vimalabodhahutāśarāśiḥ  
AbhTa itthaṃ dīkṣopakramoyaṃ darśitaḥ śāstrasaṃmataḥ 
C atha śrītantrāloke pañcadaśamāhnikam
AbhTa athaitadupayogāya yāgastāvannirūpyate 
AbhTb tatra dīkṣaiva bhoge ca muktau cāyātyupāyatām  
AbhTa svayaṃ saṃskārayogādvā tadaṅgaṃ tatpradarśyate 
AbhTb yo yatrābhilaṣedbhogān sa tatraiva niyojitaḥ  
AbhTa siddhibhāṅmantraśaktyeti śrīmatsvāyaṃbhuve vibhuḥ 
AbhTb yogyatāvaśato yatra vāsanā yasya tatra saḥ  
AbhTa yojyo na cyavate tasmāditi śrīmālinīmate 
AbhTb vadanbhogādyupāyatvaṃ dīkṣāyāḥ prāha no guruḥ  
AbhTa na cādhikāritā dīkṣāṃ vinā yogesti śāṅkare 
AbhTb na ca yogādhikāritvamekamevānayā bhavet  
AbhTa api mantrādhikāritvaṃ muktiśca śivadīkṣayā 
AbhTb ityasminmālinīvākye sākṣānmokṣābhyupāyatā  
AbhTa dīkṣāyāḥ kathitā prācyagranthena punarucyate 
AbhTb pāramparyeṇa saṃskṛtyā mokṣabhogābhyupāyatā  
AbhTa yeṣāmadhyavasāyosti na vidyāṃ pratyaśaktitaḥ 
AbhTb sukhopāyamidaṃ teṣāṃ vidhānamuditaṃ guroḥ  
AbhTa iti śrīmanmataṅgākhye hyuktā mokṣābhyupāyatā 
AbhTb samyagjñānasvabhāvā hi vidyā sākṣādvimocikā  
AbhTa uktaṃ tatraiva tattvānāṃ kāryakāraṇabhāvataḥ 
AbhTb heyādeyatvakathane vidyāpāda iti sphuṭam  
AbhTa tatrāśaktāstu ye teṣāṃ dīkṣācaryāsamādhayaḥ 
AbhTb te vidyāpūrvakā yasmāttasmājjñānyuttamottamaḥ  
AbhTa jñānaṃ ca śāstrāttaccāpi śrāvyo nādīkṣito yataḥ 
AbhTb atosya saṃskriyāmātropayogo dīkṣayā kṛtaḥ  
AbhTa yatra tatrāstu guruṇā yojitosau phalaṃ punaḥ 
AbhTb svavijñānocitaṃ yāti jñānītyuktaṃ purā kila  
AbhTa yasya tvīśaprasādena divyā kācana yogyatā 
AbhTb guroḥ śiśośca tau naiva prati dīkṣopayogitā  
AbhTa jñānameva tadā dīkṣā śrītraiśikanirūpaṇāt 
AbhTb sarvaśāstrārthavettṛtvamakasmāccāsya jāyate  
AbhTa iti śrīmālinīnītyā yaḥ sāṃsiddhikasaṃvidaḥ 
AbhTb sa uttamādhikārī syājjñānavānhi gururmataḥ  
AbhTa ātmane vā parebhyo vā hitārthī cetayedidam 
AbhTb ityuktyā mālinīśāstre tatsarvaṃ prakaṭīkṛtam  
AbhTa jñānayogyāstathā keciccaryāyogyāstathāpare 
AbhTb dīkṣāyogyā yogayogyā iti śrīkairaṇe vidhau  
AbhTa tatroktalakṣaṇaḥ karmayogajñānaviśāradaḥ 
AbhTb uttarottaratābhūmyutkṛṣṭo gururudīritaḥ  
AbhTa sa ca prāguktaśaktyanyatamapātapavitritam 
AbhTb parīkṣya pṛṣṭvā vā śiṣyaṃ dīkṣākarma samācaret  
AbhTa uktaṃ svacchandaśāstre ca śiṣyaṃ pṛcchedguruḥ svayam 
AbhTb phalaṃ prārthayase yādṛktādṛksādhanamārabhe  
AbhTa vāsanābhedataḥ sādhyaprāptirmantrapracoditā 
AbhTb mantramudrādhvadravyāṇāṃ home sādhāraṇā sthitiḥ  
AbhTa vāsanābhedato bhinnaṃ śiṣyāṇāṃ ca guroḥ phalam 
AbhTb sādhako dvividhaḥ śaivadharmā lokojjhitasthitiḥ  
AbhTa lokadharmī phalākāṃkṣī śubhasthaścāśubhojjhitaḥ 
AbhTb dvidhā mumukṣurnirbījaḥ samayādivivarjitaḥ  
AbhTa bālabāliśavṛddhastrībhogabhugvyādhitādikaḥ 
AbhTb anyaḥ sabījo yasyetthaṃ dīkṣoktā śivaśāsane  
AbhTa vidvaddvandvasahānāṃ tu sabījā samayātmikā 
AbhTb dīkṣānugrāhikā pālyā viśeṣasamayāstu taiḥ  
AbhTa abhāvaṃ bhāvayetsamyakkarmaṇāṃ prācyabhāvinām 
AbhTb mumukṣornirapekṣasya prārabdhrekaṃ na śādhayet  
AbhTa sādhakasya tu bhūtyarthamitthameva viśodhayet 
AbhTb śivadharmiṇyasau dīkṣā lokadharmāpahāriṇī  
AbhTa adharmarūpiṇāmeva na śubhānāṃ tu śodhanam 
AbhTb lokadharmiṇyasau dīkṣā mantrārādhanavarjitā  
AbhTa prārabdhadehabhede tu bhuṅktesāvaṇimādikam 
AbhTb bhuktvordhvaṃ yāti yatraiṣa yuktotha sakalekale  
AbhTa samayācārapāśaṃ tu nirbījāyāṃ viśodhayet 
AbhTb dīkṣāmātreṇa muktiḥ syādbhaktyā deve gurau sadā  
AbhTa sadyonirvāṇadā seyaṃ nirbījā yeti bhaṇyate 
AbhTb atītānāgatārabdhapāśatrayaviyojikā  
AbhTa dīkṣāvasāne śuddhasya dehatyāge paraṃ padam 
AbhTb dehatyāge sabījāyāṃ karmābhāvādvipadyate  
AbhTa samayācārapāśaṃ tu dīkṣitaḥ pālayetsadā 
AbhTb evaṃ pṛṣṭvā parijñāya vicārya ca guruḥ svayam  
AbhTa ucitāṃ saṃvidhitsustāṃ vāsanāṃ tādṛśīṃ śrayet 
AbhTb āyātaśaktipātasya dīkṣāṃ prati na daiśikaḥ  
AbhTa avajñāṃ vidadhīteti śaṃbhunājñā nirūpitā 
AbhTb svadhanena daridrasya kuryāddīkṣāṃ guruḥ svayam  
AbhTa api dūrvāmbubhiryadvā dīkṣāyai bhikṣate śiśuḥ 
AbhTb bhikṣopāttaṃ nijaṃ vātha dhanaṃ prāggurave śiśuḥ  
AbhTa dadyādyena viśuddhaṃ tadyāgayogyatvamaśnute 
AbhTb tatrādau śivatāpattisvātantryāveśa eva yaḥ  
AbhTa sa eva hi guruḥ kāryastatosau dīkṣaṇe kṣamaḥ 
AbhTb śivatāveśitā cāsya bahūpāyā pradarśitā  
AbhTa kramikā bāhyarūpā tu snānanyāsārcanādibhiḥ 
AbhTb bahvīṣu tāsu tāsveṣa kriyāsu śivatāṃ hṛdi  
AbhTa saṃdadhaddṛḍhamabhyeti śivabhāvaṃ prasannadhīḥ 
AbhTb śivībhūto yadyadicchettattatkartuṃ samīhate  
AbhTa śivābhimānitopāyo bāhyo heturna mokṣadaḥ 
AbhTb śivoyaṃ śiva evāsmītyevamācāryaśiṣyayoḥ  
AbhTa hetutadvattayā dārḍhyābhimāno mocako hyaṇoḥ 
AbhTb nādhyātmena vinā bāhyaṃ nādhyātmaṃ bāhyavarjitam  
AbhTa siddhyejjñānakriyābhyāṃ taddvitīyaṃ saṃprakāśate 
AbhTb śrībrahmayāmale deva iti tena nyarūpayat  
AbhTa śrīmadānandaśāstre ca nāśuddhiḥ syādvipaścitaḥ 
AbhTb kintu snānaṃ suvastratvaṃ tuṣṭisaṃjananaṃ bhavet  
AbhTa tatra prasiddhadehādimātṛnirmalatākramāt 
AbhTb ayatnatontarantaḥ syānnairmalya snāyatāṃ tataḥ  
AbhTa snānaṃ ca devadevasya yanmūrtyaṣṭakamucyate 
AbhTb tatraivaṃ mantradīptentarmaladāhe nimajjanam  
AbhTa tatreṣṭamantrahṛdayo gorajontaḥ padatrayam 
AbhTb gatvāgatya bhajetsnānaṃ pārthivaṃ dhṛtidāyakam  
AbhTa astramantritamṛddhūtamalaḥ pañcāṅgamantritaiḥ 
AbhTb jalairmūrdhādipādāntaṃ kramādākṣālayettataḥ  
AbhTa nimajjetsāṅgamūlākhyaṃ japannā tanmayatvataḥ 
AbhTb utthāyāśeṣasajjyotirdevatāgarbhamambare  
AbhTa sūryaṃ jalena mālinyā tarpayedviśvatarpakam 
AbhTb devānpitṝnmunīnyakṣān rakṣāṃsyanyacca bhautikam  
AbhTa sarvaṃ saṃtarpayetprāṇo vīryātmā sa ca bhāskaraḥ 
AbhTb tato japetparāmekāṃ prāguktoccārayogataḥ  
AbhTa ā tanmayatvasaṃvitterjalasnānamidaṃ matam 
AbhTb agnyutthaṃ bhasma śastreṇa japtvā malanivarhaṇam  
AbhTa kavaktrahṛdguhyapade pañcāṅgairbhasma mantritam 
AbhTb bhasmamuṣṭiṃ sāṅgamūlajaptāṃ mūrdhni kṣipettataḥ  
AbhTa hastapādau jalenaiva prakṣālyācamanādikam 
AbhTb tarpaṇaṃ japa ityevaṃ bhasmasnānaṃ hi taijasam  
AbhTa gorajovatyanudrikte vāyau hlādini mantravāk 
AbhTb gatyāgatiprayoge vā vāyavyaṃ snānamācaret  
AbhTa amale gagane vyāpinyekāgrībhūtadṛṣṭikaḥ 
AbhTb smaranmantraṃ yadāsīta kānyā nirmalatā tataḥ  
AbhTa yadi vā nirmalādvyomnaḥ patatā vāriṇā tanum 
AbhTb sparśayenmantrajapayuṅ nābhasaṃ snānamīdṛśam  
AbhTa evaṃ somārkatejaḥsu śivabhāvena bhāvanāt 
AbhTb nimajjandhautamālinyaḥ kva vā yogyo na jāyate  
AbhTa ātmaiva parameśāno nirācāramahāhradaḥ 
AbhTb viśvaṃ nimajjya tatraiva tiṣṭhecchuddhaśca śodhakaḥ  
AbhTa iti snānāṣṭakaṃ śuddhāvuttarottaramuttamam 
AbhTb sarvatra paścāttaṃ mantramekībhūtamupāharet  
AbhTa ghṛtyāpyāyamalaploṣavīryavyāptimṛjisthitīḥ 
AbhTb abhedaṃ ca kramādeti snānāṣṭakaparo muniḥ  
AbhTa etā hyanugrahātmāno mūrtayoṣṭau śivātmikāḥ 
AbhTb svarūpaśivarūpābhyāṃ dhyānāttattatphalapradāḥ  
AbhTa anena vidhinārcāyāṃ kandādhārādiyojanām 
AbhTb kurvanvyāsasamāsābhyāṃ dharādestatphalaṃ bhajet  
AbhTa tathāhi yogasaṃcāre mantrāḥ syurbhuvi pārthivāḥ 
AbhTb āpye āpyā yāvadamī śive śivamayā iti  
AbhTa śrīnirmaryādaśāstrepi taditthaṃ sunirūpitam 
AbhTb dharādeśca viśeṣosti vīrasādhakasaṃmataḥ  
AbhTa raṇareṇurvīrajalaṃ vīrabhasma mahāmarut 
AbhTb śmaśānāraṇyagaganaṃ candrārkau tadupāhitau  
AbhTa ātmā nirdhūtaniḥśeṣavikalpātaṅkasusthitaḥ 
AbhTb snānārcādāvityupāsyaṃ vīrāṇāṃ vigrahāṣṭakam  
AbhTa śrīmantriśirasi proktaṃ madyaśīdhusurādinā 
AbhTb susvādunā prasannena tanunā susugandhinā  
AbhTa kandalādigatenāntarbahiḥ saṃskārapañcakam 
AbhTb kṛtvā nirīkṣaṇaṃ prokṣya tāḍanāpyāyaguṇṭhanam  
AbhTa mantracakrasya tanmadhye pūjāṃ vipruṭpratarpaṇam 
AbhTb tenātmasekaḥ kalaśamudrayā cābhiṣecanam  
AbhTa devatātarpaṇaṃ dehaprāṇobhayapathāśritam 
AbhTb sarvatīrthatapoyajñadānādi phalamaśnute  
AbhTa madyasnāne sādhakendro mumukṣuḥ kevalībhavet 
AbhTb yataḥ śivamayaṃ madyaṃ sarve mantrāḥ śivodbhavāḥ  
AbhTa śivaśaktyorna bhedosti śaktyutthāstu marīcayaḥ 
AbhTb tāsāmānandajanakaṃ madyaṃ śivamayaṃ tataḥ  
AbhTa prabuddhe saṃvidaḥ pūrṇe rūpedhikṛtibhājanam 
AbhTb mantradhyānasamādhānabhedātsnānaṃ tu yanna tat  
AbhTa yuktaṃ snānaṃ yato nyāsakarmādau yogyatāvaham 
AbhTb asya snānāṣṭakasyāsti bāhyāntaratayā dvitā  
AbhTa āntaraṃ tadyathordhvendudhārāmṛtapariplavaḥ 
AbhTb yato randhrordhvagāḥ sārdhamaṅgulaṃ vyāpya saṃsthitāḥ  
AbhTa mūrtayoṣṭāvapi proktāḥ pratyekaṃ dvādaśāntataḥ 
AbhTb eṣāmekatamaṃ snānaṃ kuryāddvitryādiśopivā  
AbhTa iti snānavidhiḥ prokto bhairaveṇāmalīkṛtau 
AbhTb snānānantarakartavyamathedamupadiśyate  
AbhTa bhāvaṃ prasannamālocya vrajedyāgagṛhaṃ tataḥ 
AbhTb parvatāgranadītīraikaliṅgādi yaducyate  
AbhTa tadbāhyamiha tatsiddhiviśeṣāya na muktaye 
AbhTb ābhyantaraṃ nagāgrādi dehāntaḥ prāṇayojanam  
AbhTa sādhakānāmupāyaḥ syātsiddhaye natu muktaye 
AbhTb pīṭhasthānaṃ sadā yāgayogyaṃ śāstreṣu bhaṇyate  
AbhTa tacca bāhyāntarādrūpādbahirdehe ca susphuṭam 
AbhTb yataḥ śrīnaiśasañcāre parameśo nyarūpayat  
AbhTa tasyecchā pīṭhamādhāro yatrasthaṃ sacarācaram 
AbhTb agryaṃ tatkāmarūpaṃ syādbindunādadvayaṃ tataḥ  
AbhTa nādapīṭhaṃ pūrṇagirirdakṣiṇe vāmataḥ punaḥ 
AbhTb pīṭhamuḍḍayanaṃ bindurmukhyaṃ pīṭhatrayaṃ tvidam  
AbhTa jñeyaṃ saṃkalpanārūpamardhapīṭhamataḥ param 
AbhTb śāktaṃ kuṇḍalinī vedakalaṃ ca tryupapīṭhakam  
AbhTa devīkoṭṭojjayinyau dve tathā kulagiriḥ paraḥ 
AbhTb lālanaṃ baindavaṃ vyāptiriti saṃdohakatrayam  
AbhTa puṇḍravardhanavārendre tathaikāmramidaṃ bahiḥ 
AbhTb navadhā kathitaṃ pīṭhamantarbāhyakrameṇa tat  
AbhTa kṣetrāṣṭakaṃ kṣetravido hṛdambhojadalāṣṭakam 
AbhTb prayāgo varaṇā paścādaṭṭahāso jayantikā  
AbhTa vārāṇasī ca kāliṅgaṃ kulūtā lāhulā tathā 
AbhTb upakṣetrāṣṭakaṃ prāhurhṛtpadmāgradalāṣṭakam  
AbhTa virajairuḍikā hālā elā pūḥ kṣīrikā purī 
AbhTb māyākhyā marudeśaśca bāhyābhyantararūpataḥ  
AbhTa hṛtpadmadalasandhīnāmupasaṃdohakāṣṭatā 
AbhTb jālandharaṃ ca naipālaṃ kaśmīrā gargikā haraḥ  
AbhTa mlecchadigdvāravṛttiśca kurukṣetraṃ ca kheṭakam 
AbhTb dvipathaṃ dvayasaṃghaṭṭāttripathaṃ trayamelakāt  
AbhTa catuṣpathaṃ śaktimato layāttatraiva manvate 
AbhTb nāsāntatālurandhrāntametaddehe vyavasthitam  
AbhTa bhrūmadhyakaṇṭhahṛtsaṃjñaṃ madhyamaṃ tadudāhṛtam 
AbhTb nābhikandamahānandadhāma tatkaulikaṃ trayam  
AbhTa parvatāgraṃ nadītīramekaliṅgaṃ tadeva ca 
AbhTb kiṃ vātibahunā sarvaṃ saṃvittau prāṇagaṃ tataḥ  
AbhTa tato dehasthitaṃ tasmāddehāyatanago bhavet 
AbhTb bāhye tu tādṛśāntaḥsthayogamārgaviśāradāḥ  
AbhTa devyaḥ svabhāvājjāyante pīṭhaṃ tadvāhyamucyate 
AbhTb yathā svabhāvato mlecchā adharmapathavartinaḥ  
AbhTa tatra deśe niyatyetthaṃ jñānayogau sthitau kvacit 
AbhTb yathācātanmayopyeti pāpitāṃ taiḥ samāgamāt  
AbhTa tathā pīṭhasthitopyeti jñānayogādipātratām 
AbhTb mukhyatvena śarīrentaḥ prāṇe saṃvidi paśyataḥ  
AbhTa viśvametatkimanyaiḥ syādbahirbhramaṇaḍambaraiḥ 
AbhTb ityevamantarbāhye ca tattaccakraphalārthinām  
AbhTa sthānabhedo vicitraśca sa śāstre saṃkhyayojjhitaḥ 
AbhTb śrīvīrāvalihṛdaye sapta sthānāni śaktikamalayugam  
AbhTa surapathacatuṣpathākhyaśmaśānamekāntaśūnyavṛkṣau ca 
AbhTb iti nirvacanaguṇasthityupacāradṛśā vibodha evoktaḥ  
AbhTa tadadhiṣṭhite ca cakre śārīre bahiratho bhavedyāgaḥ 
AbhTb muktaye tanna yāgasya sthānabhedaḥ prakalpyate  
AbhTa deśopāyā na sā yasmātsā hi bhāvaprasādataḥ 
AbhTb uktaṃ ca śrīniśācāre siddhisādhanakāṅkṣiṇām  
AbhTa sthānaṃ mumukṣuṇā tyājyaṃ sarpakañcukavattvidam 
AbhTb muktirna sthānajanitā yadā śrotrapathaṃ gatam  
AbhTa gurostattvaṃ tadā muktistaddārḍhyāya tu pūjanam 
AbhTb yatra yatra hṛdambhojaṃ vikāsaṃ pratipadyate  
AbhTa tatraiva dhāmni bāhyentaryāgaśrīḥ pratitiṣṭhati 
AbhTb nānyatragatyā mokṣosti sojñānagranthikartanāt  
AbhTa tacca saṃvidvikāsena śrīmadvīrāvalīpade 
AbhTb guravastu vimuktau vā siddhau vā vimalā matiḥ  
AbhTa heturityubhayatrāpi yāgauko yanmanoramam 
AbhTb niyatiprāṇatāyogātsāmagrītastu yadyapi  
AbhTa siddhayo bhāvavaimalyaṃ tathāpi nikhilottamam 
AbhTb vimalībhūtahṛdayo yattatra pratibimbayet  
AbhTa sādhyaṃ tadasya dārḍhyena saphalatvāya kalpate 
AbhTb uktaṃ śrīsāraśāstre ca nirvikalpo hi sidhyati  
AbhTa kliśyante savikalpāstu kalpoktepi kṛte sati 
AbhTb tadākramya balaṃ mantrā ayamevodayaḥ sphuṭaḥ  
AbhTa ityādibhiḥ spandavākyairetadeva nirūpitam 
AbhTb tasmātsiddhyai vimuktyai vā pūjājapasamādhiṣu  
AbhTa tatsthānaṃ yatra viśrāntisundaraṃ hṛdayaṃ bhavet 
AbhTb yāgaukaḥ prāpya śuddhātmā bahireva vyavasthitaḥ  
AbhTa nyāsaṃ sāmānyataḥ kuryādbahiryāgaprasiddhaye 
AbhTb mātṛkāṃ mālinīṃ vātha dvitayaṃ vā kramākramāt  
AbhTa sṛṣṭyapyayadvayaiḥ kuryādekaikaṃ saṃghaśo dviśaḥ 
AbhTb lalāṭavaktre dṛkkarṇanāsāgaṇḍaradauṣṭhage  
AbhTa dvaye dvaye śikhājihve visargāntāstu ṣoḍaśa 
AbhTb dakṣānyayoḥ skandhabāhukarāṅgulinakhe kacau  
AbhTa vargau ṭatau kramātkaṭyāmūrvādiṣu niyojayet 
AbhTb pavargaṃ pārśvayoḥ pṛṣṭhe jaṭhare hṛdyatho nava  
AbhTa tvagraktamāṃsasūtrāsthivasāśukrapurogamān 
AbhTb ityeṣa mātṛkānyāso mālinyāstu nirūpyate  
AbhTa na śikhā ṛ ṝ ḷ ḷḷ ca śiromālā tha mastakam 
AbhTb netrāṇi cordhve dhonye ī ghrāṇaṃ mudre ṇu ṇū śrutī  
AbhTa bakavargaiā vaktradantajihvāgiri kramāt 
AbhTb vabhayāḥ kaṇṭhadakṣādiskandhayorbhujayorḍaḍhau  
AbhTa ṭho hastayorjhañau śākhā jraṭau śūlakapālake 
AbhTb pa hṛcchalau stanau kṣīramā sa jīvo visargayuk  
AbhTa prāṇo havarṇaḥ kathitaḥ ṣakṣāvudaranābhigau 
AbhTb maśāntā kaṭiguhyoruyugmagā jānunī tathā  
AbhTa eaikārau tatparau tu jaṅghe caraṇagau daphau 
AbhTb ityeṣā mālinī devī śaktimatkṣobhitā yataḥ  
AbhTa kṛtyāveśāttataḥ śāktī tanuḥ sā paramārthataḥ 
AbhTb anyonyaṃ bījayonīnāṃ kṣobhādvaisargikodayāt  
AbhTa kāṃ kāṃ siddhiṃ na vitaretkiṃ vā nyūnaṃ na pūrayet 
AbhTb yonibījārṇasāṃkaryaṃ bahudhā yadyapi sthitam  
AbhTa tathāpi nādiphāntoyaṃ kramo mukhyaḥ prakīrtitaḥ 
AbhTb phakārādisamuccārānnakārāntedhvamaṇḍalam  
AbhTa saṃhṛtya saṃvidyā pūrṇā sā śabdairvarṇyate katham 
AbhTb ataḥ śāstreṣu bahudhā kulaputtalikādibhiḥ  
AbhTa bhedairgītā hi mukhyeyaṃ nādiphānteti mālinī 
AbhTb śabdarāśerbhairavasya yānucchūnatayāntarī  
AbhTa sā māteva bhaviṣyattvāttenāsau mātṛkoditā 
AbhTb mālinī mālitā rudrairdhārikā siddhimokṣayoḥ  
AbhTa phaleṣu puṣpitā pūjyā saṃhāradhvaniṣaṭpadī 
AbhTb saṃhāradānādānādiśaktiyuktā yato ralau  
AbhTa ekatvena smarantīti śaṃbhunātho nirūcivān 
AbhTb śabdarāśirmālinī ca śivaśaktyātmakaṃ tvidam  
AbhTa ekaikatrāpi pūrṇatvācchivaśaktisvabhāvatā 
AbhTb tena bhraṣṭe vidhau vīrye svarūpe vānayā param  
AbhTa mantrā nyastāḥ punarnyāsātpūryante tatphalapradāḥ 
AbhTb uktaṃ śrīpūrvatantre ca viśeṣavidhihīnite  
AbhTa nyasyecchāktaśarīrārthaṃ bhinnayoni tu mālinīm 
AbhTb viśeṣaṇamidaṃ hetau hetvarthaśca nirūpitaḥ  
AbhTa yatheṣṭaphalasiddhyai cetyatraivedamabhāṣata 
AbhTb sāñjanā api ye mantrā gāruḍādyā na te param  
AbhTa mālinyā pūritāḥ sidhdyai balādeva tu muktaye 
AbhTb tasmātphalepsurapyanya mantraṃ nyasyātra mālinīm  
AbhTa nyasyejjaptvāpica japedayatnādapavṛktaye 
AbhTb ityevaṃ mātṛkāṃ nyasyenmālinīṃ vā kramāddvayam  
AbhTa siddhimuktyanusārādvā varṇānvā yugapaddvayoḥ 
AbhTb akṣahrīṃ naphahrīmetau piṇḍau saṃghāvihānayoḥ  
AbhTa vācakau nyāsa etābhyāṃ kṛte nyāsethavaikakaḥ 
AbhTb eṣa cāṅgatanubrahmayukto vā tadviparyayaḥ  
AbhTa sāmudāyikavinyāse pṛthak piṇḍāvimau kramāt 
AbhTb akramādathavā nyasyedekamevātha yojayet  
AbhTa kriyayā siddhikāmo yaḥ sa kriyāṃ bhūyasīṃ caret 
AbhTb anīpsurapi yastasmai bhūyase svaphalāya sā  
AbhTa yastu dhyānajapābhyāsaiḥ siddhīpsuḥ sa kriyāṃ param 
AbhTb saṃskṛtyai svecchayā kuryāt prāṅnayenātha bhūyasīm  
AbhTa mumukṣuratha tasmai vā yathābhīṣṭaṃ samācaret 
AbhTb śivatāpattirevārtho hyeṣāṃ nyāsādikarmaṇām  
AbhTa evaṃ nyāsaṃ vidhāyārghapātre vidhimupācaret 
AbhTb uktanītyaiva tatpaścāt pūjayennyastavācakaiḥ  
AbhTa yataḥ samastabhāvānāṃ śivātsiddhimayādatho 
AbhTb pūrṇādavyatirekitvaṃ kārakāṇāmihārcayā  
AbhTa samastaṃ kārakavrātaṃ śivābhinnaṃ pradarśitam 
AbhTb pūjodāharaṇe sarvaṃ vyaśnute gamanādyapi  
AbhTa yathāhi vāhakaṭakabhramasvātantryamāgataḥ 
AbhTb aśvaḥ saṃgrāmarūḍhopi tāṃ śikṣāṃ nātivartate  
AbhTa tathārcanakriyābhyāsaśivībhāvitakārakaḥ 
AbhTb gacchaṃstiṣṭhannapi dvaitaṃ kārakāṇāṃ vyapojjhati  
AbhTa tathaikyābhyāsaniṣṭhasyākramādviśvamidaṃ haṭhāt 
AbhTb saṃpūrṇaśivatākṣobhanarīnartadiva sphuret  
AbhTa uvāca pūjanastotre hyasmākaṃ paramo guruḥ 
AbhTb aho svādurasaḥ kopi śivapūjāmayotsavaḥ  
AbhTa ṣaṭtriṃśatopi tattvānāṃ kṣobho yatrollasatyalam 
AbhTb tadetādṛkpūrṇaśivaviśvāveśāya yercanam  
AbhTa kurvanti te śivā eva tānpūrṇānprati kiṃ phalam 
AbhTb vināpi jñānayogābhyāṃ kriyā nyāsārcanādikā  
AbhTa itthamaikyasamāpattidānātparaphalapradā 
AbhTb sādhakasyāpi tatsadvipradamantraikatāṃ gatam  
AbhTa viśvaṃ vrajadavighnatvaṃ svāṃ siddhiṃ śīghramāvahet 
AbhTb uktaṃ ca parameśena na vidhirnārcanakramaḥ  
AbhTa kevalaṃ smaraṇātsiddhirvāñchiteti matādiṣu 
AbhTb tadevaṃ tanmayībhāvadāyinyarcākriyā yataḥ  
AbhTa samastakārakaikātmyaṃ tenāsyāḥ paramaṃ vapuḥ 
AbhTb yaṣṭrādhārasya tādātmyaṃ sthānaśuddhividhikramāt  
AbhTa yaṣṭṛyājyatadādhārakaraṇādānasaṃpradāḥ 
AbhTb nyāsakrameṇa śivatātādātmyamadhiśerate  
AbhTa arghapātramapādānaṃ tasmādādīyate yataḥ 
AbhTb yacca tatsthaṃ jalādyetatkaraṇaṃ śodhanercane  
AbhTa arghapātrāmbuvipruḍbhiḥ spṛṣṭaṃ sarvaṃ hi śudhyati 
AbhTb śivārkakarasaṃsparśātkānyā śuddhirbhaviṣyati  
AbhTa ūce śrīpūrvaśāstre tadarghapātravidhau vibhuḥ 
AbhTb na cāsaṃśodhitaṃ vastu kiṃcidapyupakalpayet  
AbhTa tena śuddhaṃ tu sarvaṃ yadaśuddhamapi tacchuci 
AbhTb aśuddhatā ca vijñeyā paśutacchāsanāśayāt  
AbhTa svatādavasthyātpūrvasmādathavāpyupakalpitāt 
AbhTb tena yadyadihāsannaṃ saṃvidaścidanugrahāt  
AbhTa kiyatopi tadatyantaṃ yogyaṃ yāgetra jīvavat 
AbhTb anena nayayogena yadāsattividūrate  
AbhTa saṃvideti tadā tatra yogyāyogyatvamādiśet 
AbhTb vīrāṇāmata eveha mithaḥ svapratimāmṛtam  
AbhTa tattadyāgavidhāviṣṭaṃ gurubhirbhāvitātmabhiḥ 
AbhTb unmajjayati nirmagnāṃ saṃvidaṃ yattu suṣṭhu tat  
AbhTa arcāyai yogyamānando yasmādunmagnatā citaḥ 
AbhTb tenācidrūpadehādiprādhānyavinimajjakam  
AbhTa ānandajananaṃ pūjāyogyaṃ hṛdayahāri yat 
AbhTb ataḥ kulakramottīrṇatrikasāramatādiṣu  
AbhTa madyakādambarīśīdhudravyādermahimā param 
AbhTb lokasthitiṃ racayituṃ madyādeḥ paśuśāsane  
AbhTa proktā hyaśuddhistatraiva tasya kvāpi viśuddhatā 
AbhTb pañcagavye pavitratvaṃ somacarṇanapātrayoḥ  
AbhTa vidhiścāvabhṛthasnānaṃ haste kṛṣṇaviṣāṇitā 
AbhTb na patnyā ca vinā yāgaḥ sarvadaivatatulyatā  
AbhTa surāhutirbrahmasatre vapāntrahṛdayāhutiḥ 
AbhTb pāśaveṣvapi śāstreṣu tadadarśi maheśinā  
AbhTa ghorāndhyahaimananiśāmadhyagāciradīptivat 
AbhTb bhakṣyo haṃso na bhakṣyosāviti ripratipattiṣu  
AbhTa smārtīṣu vijayatyeko yaḥ śivābhedaśuddhikaḥ 
AbhTb ajñatvavedādarśitvarāgadveṣādayo hyamī  
AbhTa munīnāṃ vacasi svasminprāmāṇyonmūlanakṣamāḥ 
AbhTb vedepi yadabhakṣyaṃ tadbhakṣyamityupadiśyate  
AbhTa na vidhipratiṣedhākhyadharmayorekamāspadam 
AbhTb atha tatra na tadbhakṣyaṃ tadā tena tathā tataḥ  
AbhTa evaṃ viṣayabhedānno śivokterbādhikā śrutiḥ 
AbhTb kvacidviṣayatulyatvādbādhyabādhakatā yadi  
AbhTa tadbādhyā śrutireveti prāgevaitannirūpitam 
AbhTb prakṛtaṃ brūmahe kṛtvā nyāsaṃ dehārghapātrayoḥ  
AbhTa sāmānyamarghapātrāmbhovipruḍbhiḥ prokṣya cākhilam 
AbhTb yāgopakaraṇaṃ paścādbāhyayāgaṃ samācaret  
AbhTa prabhāmaṇḍalake khe vā suliptāyāṃ ca vā bhuvi 
AbhTb triśūlārkavṛṣāndikasthā mātaraḥ kṣetrapaṃ yajet  
AbhTa yoginīśca pṛthaṅmantrairoṃnamonāmayojitaiḥ 
AbhTb ekoccāreṇa vā bāhyaparivāretiśabditāḥ  
AbhTa tāro nāma caturthyantaṃ namaścetyarcane manuḥ 
AbhTb evaṃ bahiḥ pūjayitvā dvāraṃ prokṣya prapūjayet  
AbhTa triśiraḥśāsanādau ca sa dṛṣṭo vidhirucyate 
AbhTb gaṇeśalakṣmyau dvārordhve dakṣe vāme tayoḥ punaḥ  
AbhTa madhye vāgīśvarīṃ diṇḍimahodarayugaṃ tathā 
AbhTb kramātsvadakṣavāmasthaṃ tathaitena krameṇa ca  
AbhTa ekaikaṃ pūjayetsamyaṅ nandikālau trimārgagām 
AbhTb kālindīṃ chāgameṣāsyau svadakṣāddvāḥsthaśākhayoḥ  
AbhTa adhodehalyananteśādhāraśaktīśca pūjayet 
AbhTb dvāramadhye sarasvatyā mahāstraṃ pūjayedamī  
AbhTa padmādhāragatāḥ sarvepyuditā vighnanāśakāḥ 
AbhTb pūjane pūrvavanmantro dīpakadvayakalpitaḥ  
AbhTa arghapuṣpasamālambhadhūpanaivedyavandanaiḥ 
AbhTb pūjāṃ kuryādihārghaścāpyuttamadravyayojitaḥ  
AbhTa ekoccāreṇa vā kuryāddvāḥsthadaivatapūjanam 
AbhTb rahasyapūjāṃ cetkuryāttadbāhyaparivārakam  
AbhTa dvāḥsthāṃśca pūjayedantardevāgre kalpanākramāt 
AbhTb kṣiptvāstrajaptaṃ kusumaṃ jvaladveśmani vghnanut  
AbhTa praviśya śivaraśmīddhadṛśā veśmāvalokayet 
AbhTb diśostreṇa ca badhnīyācchādayedvarmaṇākhilāḥ  
AbhTa tatrottarāśābhimukho mumukṣustādṛśāya vā 
AbhTb viśettathā hyaghorāgniḥ pāśānpluṣyati bandhakān  
AbhTa yadyapyasti na diṅnāma kācitpūrvāparādikā 
AbhTb pratyayo hi na tasyāḥ syādekasyā anupāhiteḥ  
AbhTa upādhiḥ pūrvatādiṣṭa iti cettatkṛtaṃ diśā 
AbhTb upādhimātraṃ tu tathā vaicitryāya kathaṃ bhavet  
AbhTa tasmātsaṃvitprakāśoyaṃ mūrtyābhāsanabhāgataḥ 
AbhTb pūrvādidigvibhāgākhyavaicitryollekhadurmadaḥ  
AbhTa tatra yadyatprakāśena sadā svīkaraṇe kṣamam 
AbhTb tadevordhvaṃ prakāśātma sparśāyogyamadhaḥ punaḥ  
AbhTa kiṃcitprakāśatā madhyaṃ tato vai diksamudbhavaḥ 
AbhTb kiṃcitprakāśayogyasya saṃmukhaṃ prasaratpuraḥ  
AbhTa parāṅmukhaṃ tu tatpaścāditi digdvayamāgatam 
AbhTb prakāśaḥ saṃmukhaṃ vastu gṛhītvodriktaraśmikaḥ  
AbhTa yatra tiṣṭhoddakṣiṇaṃ tatprakāśasyānukūlyataḥ 
AbhTb dakṣiṇasya puraḥsaṃsthaṃ vāmamityupadiśyate  
AbhTa tatprakāśitameyendusparśasaumyaṃ tadeva hi 
AbhTb evamāśācatuṣkesminmadhyaviśrāntiyogataḥ  
AbhTa catuṣkamanyattenāṣṭau diśastattadadhiṣṭhitāḥ 
AbhTb evaṃ prakāśamātresminvarade parame śive  
AbhTa digvibhāgaḥ sthito loke śāstrepica tathocyate 
AbhTb kramātsadāśivādhīśaḥ pañcamantratanuryataḥ  
AbhTa īśanraghoravāmākhyasadyodhobhedato diśaḥ 
AbhTb īśa ūrdhvaṃ prakāśatvātpūrvaṃ vaktraṃ prasāri yat  
AbhTa puruṣo dakṣiṇācaṇḍo vāmā vāmastu saumyakaḥ 
AbhTb parāṅmukhatayā sadyaḥ paścimā paribhāṣyate  
AbhTa pātālavaktramadharamaprakāśatayā sthiteḥ 
AbhTb khamarudvahnijalabhūkhāni vaktrāṇyamuṣya hi  
AbhTa mukhyatvena khamevordhvaṃ prakāśamayamucyate 
AbhTb tadeva mukhyatodhastādaprakāśaṃ yataḥ sphuṭam  
AbhTa madhye tu yatprakāśaṃ tanna prakāśyaṃ na cetarat 
AbhTb prakāśatvāddiśyamānamatosmindikcatuṣṭayam  
AbhTa pañcamantratanurnātha itthaṃ viśvadigīśvaraḥ 
AbhTb tatopīśastathā rudro viṣṇurbrahmā tathā sthitaḥ  
AbhTa ūrdhvābhivyaktyayogyatvādviṣṇordhātuśca pañcamam 
AbhTb na vaktraṃ tau bhedamayau sṛṣṭisthitiprabhū yataḥ  
AbhTa digvibhāgastu tajjosti vadanānāṃ catuṣṭayāt 
AbhTb pañcamasya yujitve tau parityaktanijātmakau  
AbhTa tato brahmāṇḍamadhyepi jñānaśaktirvibho raviḥ 
AbhTb diśāṃ vibhāgaṃ kurute prakāśaghanavṛttimān  
AbhTa tathāhi viṣuvadyoge yataḥ pūrvaṃ pradṛśyate 
AbhTb tatpūrva yatra tacchāyā tatpaścimamudāhṛtam  
AbhTa tasmiñjigamiṣorasya yatsavyaṃ tattu dakṣiṇam 
AbhTb tatraiṣa caṇḍatejobhirbhāti jājvalyamānavat  
AbhTa tatpurovarti vāmaṃ tu tadbhāsā khacitaṃ manāk 
AbhTb tata eva hi somyaṃ tannacāpi hyaprakāśakam  
AbhTa yatrāsāvastamabhyeti tatpaścimamiti sthitiḥ 
AbhTb tatraiva paścime yeṣāṃ prākprakāśāvalokanam  
AbhTa tadeva pūrvameteṣāṃ yathādhvani nirūpitam 
AbhTb sā sā dikca tathā tasya phaladāpi viparyaye  
AbhTa vicitre phalasaṃpattiḥ prakāśādhīnikā yataḥ 
AbhTb itthaṃ sūryāśrayā diksyātsā vicitrāpi tādṛśī  
AbhTa adhiṣṭhitā maheśena citratadrūpadhāriṇā 
AbhTb kiṃ vātibahunā yosau yaṣṭā tatsaṃmukhāditaḥ  
AbhTa diśopi pravibhajyante prāksavyottarapaścimāḥ 
AbhTb svānusārakṛtaṃ taṃ ca digvibhāgaṃ sadā śivaḥ  
AbhTa adhitiṣṭhatyarkamiva sa vicitravapuryataḥ 
AbhTb svotthā api diśaḥ sveśāḥ śakrādyā hyadhiśerate  
AbhTa te hi prakāśaśaktyaṃśāḥ prakāśānuvidhāyinaḥ 
AbhTb prakāśasya yadaiśvaryaṃ sa indro yattu tanmahaḥ  
AbhTa sogniryantṛtvabhīmatve yamo rakṣastadūnimā 
AbhTb prakāśyaṃ varuṇastacca cāñcalyādvāyurucyate  
AbhTa bhāvasañcayayogena vitteśastatkṣaye vibhuḥ 
AbhTb adṛṣṭavigrahonanto brahmordhve vṛṃhako vibhuḥ  
AbhTa prakāśasyaiva śaktyaṃśā lokapāstena kīrtitāḥ 
AbhTb itthaṃ svādhīnarūpāpi diksaurī tūpadiśyate  
AbhTa tatra sarvo hi niṣkampaṃ prakāśatvaṃ prapadyate 
AbhTb sarvagopyanilo yadvadvyajanenopavījitaḥ  
AbhTa prabuddhaḥ svāṃ kriyāṃ kuryāddharmanirṇodanādikām 
AbhTb tadvatsarvagatāḥ sarvā aindyādyāḥ śaktayaḥ sphuṭam  
AbhTa sādhakāśvāsasaṃbuddhāstattatsveṣṭaphalapradāḥ 
AbhTb evaṃ saurī digīśānabrahmaviṣṇvīśasauśivaiḥ  
AbhTa adhiṣṭhitā samāśvāsadārḍhyāttattatphalapradā 
AbhTb sādhako yacca vā kṣetraṃ maṇḍalaṃ veśma vā bhajet  
AbhTa sthitastadanusāreṇa madhyībhavati śaṃkaraḥ 
AbhTb sa hi sarvamadhiṣṭhātā mādhyasthyeneti tasya yaḥ  
AbhTa sauraḥ prakāśastatpūrvamitthaṃ syāddigvyavasthitiḥ 
AbhTb tanmadhyasthitanāthasya grahītuṃ dakṣiṇaṃ mahaḥ  
AbhTa udaṅmukhaḥ syāt pāścātyaṃ grahītuṃ pūrvatomukhaḥ 
AbhTb upaviśya nijasthāne dehaśuddhiṃ samācaret  
AbhTa aṅguṣṭhāgrātkālavahnijvālābhāsvaramutthitam 
AbhTb astraṃ dhyātvā tacchikhābhirbahirantardahettanum  
AbhTa dāhaśca dhvaṃsa evokto dhvaṃsakaṃ mantrasaṃjñitam 
AbhTb tejastathābhilāpākhyasvavikalparasombhitam  
AbhTa tena mantrāgninā dāho dehe puryaṣṭake tathā 
AbhTb dehapuryaṣṭakāhantāvidhvaṃsādeva jāyate  
AbhTa nahi sadbhāvamātreṇa dehosāvanyadehavat 
AbhTb ahantāyāṃ hi dehatvaṃ sā dhvastā taddaheddhruvam  
AbhTa taddehasaṃskārabharo bhasmatvenātha yaḥ sthitaḥ 
AbhTb taṃ varmavāyunādhūya tiṣṭhecchuddhacidātmani  
AbhTa tasmindhruve nistaraṅge samāpattimupāgataḥ 
AbhTb saṃvidaḥ sṛṣṭidharmitvādādyāmeti taraṅgitām  
AbhTa saiva mūrtiriti khyātā tārasadbinduhātmikā 
AbhTb tato navātmadevena nyāsastattvodayātmakaḥ  
AbhTa aṅgavaktrāṇi tasyaiva svasthāneṣu niyojayet 
AbhTb atha mātṛkayā prāgvattattattvasphuṭatātmakaḥ  
AbhTa tritattvanyāsatā cāsya pṛṣṭhe kakṣyātrayāgate 
AbhTb tatoghorāṣṭakanyāsaḥ śirastaccaraṇātmakam  
AbhTa tatopi śivasadbhāvanyāsaḥ svāṃgasya saṃyutaḥ 
AbhTb ittha kṛte pañcakesminyattanmukhyatayā bhavet  
AbhTa upāsyamarcyaṃ tatsāṅgaṃ ṣaṣṭhe nyāse niyojayet 
AbhTb tenātra nyāsayogyosau bhagavānratiśekharaḥ  
AbhTa ūrdhve nyāsyo navākhyasya mukhyatvenyonyadhāmatā 
AbhTb evaṃ bhairavasadbhāvanāthe mukhyatayā yadi  
AbhTa upāsyatā tattatsthāna prāṅnyāsyo ratiśekharaḥ 
AbhTb itthaṃ śrīpūrvaśāstre me saṃpradāyaṃ nyarūpayat  
AbhTa śaṃbhunātho nyāsavidhau devo hi kathamanyathā 
AbhTb nyāsa vivarjyatemuṣminnaṅgānyapyasya santi hi  
AbhTa mūrtiḥ sṛṣṭistritattvaṃ cetyaṣṭau mūrtyaṅgasaṃyutāḥ 
AbhTb śivaḥ sāṅgaśca vijñeyo nyāsaḥ ṣoḍhā prakīrtitaḥ  
AbhTa asyopari tataḥ śāktaṃ nyāsaṃ kuryācca ṣaḍvidham 
AbhTb parāparāṃ savaktrāṃ prāktataḥ prāgiti mālinīm  
AbhTa paścātparāditritayaṃ śikhāhṛtpādagaṃ kramāt 
AbhTb tataḥ kavaktrakaṇṭheṣu hṛnnābhīguhyaūrutaḥ  
AbhTa jānupādepyaghoryādyaṃ tato vidyāṅgapañcakam 
AbhTb tatastvāvāhayecchaktiṃ mātṛsadbhāvarūpiṇīm  
AbhTa yogeśvarīṃ parāṃ pūrṇāṃ kālasaṃkarṣiṇīṃ dhruvām 
AbhTb aṅgavaktraparīvāraśaktidvādaśakādhikām  
AbhTa sādhyānuṣṭhānabhedena nyāsakāle smaredguruḥ 
AbhTb paraiva devītritayamadhye yābhedinī sthitā  
AbhTa sānavacchedacinmātrasadbhāveyaṃ prakīrtitā 
AbhTb sāraśāstre yāmale ca devyāstena prakīrtitaḥ  
AbhTa mūrtiḥ savaktrā śaktiśca śaktitrayamathāṣṭakam 
AbhTb pañcāṅgāni parā śaktirnyāsaḥ śāktopi ṣaḍvidhaḥ  
AbhTa yāmaloyaṃ mahānyāsaḥ siddhimuktiphalapradaḥ 
AbhTb muktyekārthī punaḥ pūrvaṃ śāktaṃ nyāsaṃ samācaret  
AbhTa guravastvāhuritthaṃ yannyāsadvayamudāhṛtam 
AbhTb mumukṣuṇā tu pādādi tatkāryaṃ saṃhṛtikramāt  
AbhTa yāvantaḥ kīrtitā bhedāḥ śaṃbhuśaktyaṇuvācakāḥ 
AbhTb tāvatsvapyeṣu mantreṣu nyāsaḥ ṣoḍhaiva kīrtitaḥ  
AbhTa kiṃtvāvāhyastu yo mantraḥ sa tatrāṅgasamanvitaḥ 
AbhTb ṣaṣṭhaḥ syāditi sarvatra ṣoḍhaivāyamudāhṛtaḥ  
AbhTa mudrāpradarśanaṃ paścātkāyena manasā girā 
AbhTb pañcāvasthā jāgradādyāḥ ṣaṣṭhyanuttaranāmikā  
AbhTa ṣaṭkāraṇaṣaḍātmatvātṣaṭtriṃśattattvayojanam 
AbhTb evaṃ ṣoḍhāmahānyāse kṛte viśvamidaṃ haṭhāt  
AbhTa dehe tādātmyamāpannaṃ śuddhāṃ sṛṣṭiṃ prakāśayet 
AbhTb mūrtinyāsātsamārabhya yā sṛṣṭiḥ prasṛtātra sā  
AbhTa abhedamānīya kṛtā śuddhā nyāsabalakramāt 
AbhTb tena yecodayanmūḍhāḥ pāśadāhavidhūnane  
AbhTa kṛte śānte śive rūḍhaḥ punaḥ kimavarohati 
AbhTb iti te dūrato dhvastāḥ paramārthaṃ hi śāṃbhavam  
AbhTa na vidusta svasaṃvittisphurattāsāravarjitāḥ 
AbhTb na khalveṣa śivaḥ śānto nāma kaścidvibhedavān  
AbhTa sarvetarādhvavyāvṛtto ghaṭatulyosti kutracit 
AbhTb mahāprakāśarūpā hi yeyaṃ saṃvidvijṛmbhate  
AbhTa sa śivaḥ śivataivāsya vaiśvarūpyāvabhāsitā 
AbhTb tathābhāsanayogotaḥ svarasenāsya jṛmbhate  
AbhTa bhāsyamānotra cābhedaḥ svātmano bheda eva ca 
AbhTb bhede vijṛmbhite māyā māyāmāturvijṛmbhate  
AbhTa abhede jṛmbhatesyaiva māyāmātuḥ śivātmatā 
AbhTb māyāpramātā tadrūpavikalpābhyāsapāṭavāt  
AbhTa śiva eva tadabhyāsaphalaṃ nyāsādi kīrtitam 
AbhTb yathāhi duṣṭakarmāsmītyevaṃ bhāvayatastathā  
AbhTa tathā śivohaṃ nānyosmītyevaṃ bhāvayatastathā 
AbhTb etadevocyate dārḍhyaṃ vimarśahṛdayaṅgamam  
AbhTa śivaikātmyavikalpaughadvārikā nirvikalpatā 
AbhTb anyathā tasya śuddhasya vimarśaprāṇavartinaḥ  
AbhTa kathaṃ nāmāvimṛṣṭaṃ syādrūpaṃ bhāsanadharmaṇaḥ 
AbhTb tenātidurghaṭaghaṭāsvatantrecchāvaśādayam  
AbhTa bhānapi prāṇabuddhyādiḥ svaṃ tathā na vikalpayet 
AbhTb pratyutātisvatantrātmaviparītasvadharmatām  
AbhTa vināśyanīśāyattatvarūpāṃ niścitya majjati 
AbhTb tataḥ saṃsārabhāgīyatathāniścayaśātinīm  
AbhTa nityādiniścayadvārāmavikalpāṃ sthitiṃ śrayet 
AbhTb ye tu tīvratamodriktaśaktinirmalatājuṣaḥ  
AbhTa na te dīkṣāmanunyāsakāriṇaśceti varṇitam 
AbhTb evaṃ viśvaśarīraḥ sanviśvātmatvaṃ gataḥ sphuṭam  
AbhTa nyāsamātrāt tathābhūtaṃ dehaṃ puṣpādinārcayet 
AbhTb pṛthaṅmantrairvistareṇa saṃkṣepānmūlamantrataḥ  
AbhTa dhūpanaivedyatṛptyādyaistathā vyāsasamāsataḥ 
AbhTb saṃsāravāmācāratvātsarvaṃ vāmakareṇa tu  
AbhTa kuryāttarpaṇayogaṃ ca daiśikastadanāmayā 
AbhTb vāmaśabdena guhyaṃ śrīmataṅgādāvapīritam  
AbhTa vāmācāraparo mantrī yāgaṃ kuryāditi sphuṭam 
AbhTb śrīmadbhargaśikhāśāstre tathā śrīgamaśāsane  
AbhTa sarvatīrtheṣu yatpuṇyaṃ sarvayajñeṣu yatphalam 
AbhTb tatphalaṃ koṭiguṇitamanāmātarpaṇātpriye  
AbhTa śrīmannandiśikhāyāṃ ca śrīmadānandaśāsane 
AbhTb taduktaṃ srukca pūrṇāyāṃ sruvaśvājyāhutau bhavet  
AbhTa śeṣaṃ vāmakareṇaiva pūjāhomajapādikam 
AbhTb evamānandasaṃpūrṇaṃ sarvaunmukhyavivarjitam  
AbhTa yāgena dehaṃ miṣpādya bhāvayeta śivātmakam 
AbhTb galite viṣayaunmukhye pārimitye vilāpite  
AbhTa dehe kimavaśiṣyeta śivānandarasādṛte 
AbhTb śivānandarasāpūrṇaṃ ṣaṭtriṃśattattvanirbharam  
AbhTa dehaṃ divāniśaṃ paśyannarcayansyācchivātmakaḥ 
AbhTb viśvātmadehaviśrāntitṛptastalliṅganiṣṭhitaḥ  
AbhTa bāhyaṃ liṅgavratakṣetracaryādi nahi vāñchati 
AbhTb tāvanmātrāttvaviśrānteḥ saṃvidaḥ kathitāḥ kriyāḥ  
AbhTa uttarā bāhyayāgāntāḥ sādhyā tvatra śivātmatā 
AbhTb tatorghapātraṃ kartavyaṃ śivābhedamayaṃ param  
AbhTa ānandarasasaṃpūrṇaṃ viśvadaivatatarpaṇam 
AbhTb yathaiva dehe dāhādipūjāntaṃ tadvadeva hi  
AbhTa arghapātrepi kartavyaṃ samāsavyāsayogataḥ 
AbhTb kāni dravyāṇi yāgāya ko nvargha iti noditam  
AbhTa siddhikāmasya tatsiddhau sādhanaiva hi kāraṇam 
AbhTb muktikāmasya no kiṃcinniṣiddhaṃ vihitaṃ ca no  
AbhTa yadeva hṛdyaṃ tadyogyaṃ śivasaṃvidabhedane 
AbhTb kṛtvārghapātraṃ tadvipruṭprokṣitaṃ kusumādikam  
AbhTa kṛtvā ca tena svātmānaṃ pūjayetparamaṃ śivam 
AbhTb arghapātrārcanādattapuṣpasaṃkīrṇatābhayāt  
AbhTa nārghapātretra kusumaṃ kuryāddevārcanākṛte 
AbhTb arghapātre tadamṛtībhūtamambveva pūjitam  
AbhTa mantrāṇāṃ tṛptaye yāgadravyaśuddhyai ca kevalam 
AbhTb evaṃ dehaṃ pūjayitvā prāṇadhīśūnyavigrahān  
AbhTa anyonyatanmayībhūtān pūjayecchivatādṛśe 
AbhTb tatra prāṇāśraye nayāse buddhyā viracite sati  
AbhTa śūnyādhiṣṭhānataḥ sarvamekayatnena pūjyate 
AbhTb nyasyedādhāraśaktiṃ tu nābhyadhaścaturaṅgulām  
AbhTa dharāṃ surodaṃ tejaśca meyapārapratiṣṭhiteḥ 
AbhTb potarūpaṃ marutkandasvabhāvaṃ viśvasūtraṇāt  
AbhTa pratyekamaṅgulaṃ nyasyeccatuṣkaṃ vyomagarbhakam 
AbhTb īṣatsamantādamalamidamāmalasārakam  
AbhTa tato daṇḍamanantākhyaṃ kalpayellambikāvadhi 
AbhTb tanmātrādikalāntaṃ tadūrdhve granthirniśātmakaḥ  
AbhTa tatra māyāmaye granthau dharmādharmādyamaṣṭakam 
AbhTb vahniprāgādi māyā hi tatsūtirvibhavastu dhīḥ  
AbhTa māyāgrantherūrdhvabhūmau triśūlādhaścatuṣkikām 
AbhTb śuddhavidyātmikāṃ dhyāyecchadanadvayasaṃyutām  
AbhTa tacca tattvaṃ sthitaṃ bhāvyaṃ lambikābrahmarandhrayoḥ 
AbhTb prakāśayogo hyatraivaṃ dṛkśrotrarasanādikaḥ  
AbhTa dakṣānyāvartato nyasyecchaktīnāṃ navakadvayam 
AbhTb vidyāpadmetra taccoktamapi prāgdarśyate punaḥ  
AbhTa vāmā jyeṣṭhā raudrī kālī kalabalavikarike balamathanī 
AbhTb bhūtadamanī ca manonmanikā śāntā śakracāparuciratra syāt  
AbhTa vibhvī jñaptikṛtīcchā vāgīśī jvālinī tathā vāmā 
AbhTb jyeṣṭhā raudrītyetāḥ prāgdalataḥ kāladahanavatsarvāḥ  
AbhTa dalakesaramadhyeṣu sūryendudahanatrayam 
AbhTb nijādhipairbrahmaviṣṇuharaiścādhiṣṭhitaṃ smaret  
AbhTa māyottīrṇaṃ hi yadrūpaṃ brahmādīnāṃ puroditam 
AbhTb āsanaṃ tvetadeva syānnatu māyāñjanāñjitam  
AbhTa rudrordhve ceśvaraṃ devaṃ tadūrdhve ca sadāśivam 
AbhTb nyasyetsa ca mahāpreta iti śāstreṣu bhaṇyate  
AbhTa samastatattvavyāptṛtvānmahāpretaḥ prabodhataḥ 
AbhTb prakarṣagamanāccaiṣa līno yannādharaṃ vrajet  
AbhTa vidyāvidyeśinaḥ sarve hyuttarottaratāṃ gatāḥ 
AbhTb sadāśivībhūya tataḥ paraṃ śivamupāśritāḥ  
AbhTa ataḥ sadāśivo nityamūrdhvadṛgbhāsvarātmakaḥ 
AbhTb kṛśo meyatvadaurbalyātpretoṭṭahasanāditaḥ  
AbhTa tasya nābhyutthitaṃ mūrdharandhratrayavinirgatam 
AbhTb nādāntātma smarecchaktivyāpinīsamanojjvalam  
AbhTa arātrayaṃ dviṣaṭkāntaṃ tatrāpyaunmanasaṃ trayam 
AbhTb paṅkajānāṃ sitaṃ saptatriṃśadātmedamāsanam  
AbhTa atra sarvāṇi tattvāni bhedaprāṇāni yattataḥ 
AbhTb āsanatvena bhinnaṃ hi saṃvido viṣayaḥ smṛtaḥ  
AbhTa etānyeva tu tattvāni līnāni parabhairave 
AbhTb tādātmyenātha sṛṣṭāni bhidevārcyatvayojane  
AbhTa śrīmadbhairavabodhaikyalābhasvātantryavanti tu 
AbhTb etānyeva tu tattvāni pūjakatvaṃ prayāntyalam  
AbhTa pūjakaḥ paratattvātmā pūjyaṃ tattvaṃ parāparam 
AbhTb sṛṣṭatvādaparaṃ tattvajālamāsanatāspadam  
AbhTa vidyākalāntaṃ siddhānte vāmadakṣiṇaśāstrayoḥ 
AbhTb sadāśivāntaṃ samanāparyantaṃ matayāmale  
AbhTa unmanāntamihākhyātamityetatparamāsanam 
AbhTb arcayitvāsanaṃ pūjyā gurupaṅktistu bhāvivat  
AbhTa tatrāsane purā mūrtibhūtāṃ sārdhākṣarāṃ dvayīm 
AbhTb nyasyedvyāptṛtayetyuktaṃ siddhayogīśvarīmate  
AbhTa sadāśivaṃ mahāpretaṃ mūrtiṃ sārdhākṣarāṃ yajet 
AbhTb paratvena parāmūrdhve gandhapuṣpādibhistviti  
AbhTa vidyāmūrtimathātmākhyāṃ dvitīyāṃ parikalpayet 
AbhTb madhye bhairavasadbhāvaṃ dakṣiṇe ratiśekharam  
AbhTa navātmānaṃ vāmatastaddevīvadbhairavatrayam 
AbhTb madhye parāṃ pūrṇacandrapratimāṃ dakṣiṇe punaḥ  
AbhTa parāparāṃ raktavarṇāṃ kiṃcidagrāṃ na bhīṣaṇām 
AbhTb aparāṃ vāmaśṛṅge tu bhīṣaṇāṃ kṛṣṇapiṅgalām  
AbhTa prāgvaddvidhātra ṣoḍhaiva nyāso dehe yathā kṛtaḥ 
AbhTb tataḥ sāṃkalpikaṃ yuktaṃ vapurāsāṃ vicintayet  
AbhTa kṛtyabhedānusāreṇa dvicatuḥṣaḍbhujādikam 
AbhTb kapālaśūlakhaṭvāṅgavarābhayaghaṭādikam  
AbhTa vāmadakṣiṇasaṃsthānacitratvātparikalpayet 
AbhTb vastuto viśvarūpāstā devyo bodhātmikā yataḥ  
AbhTa anavacchinnacinmātrasārāḥ syurapavṛktaye 
AbhTb sarvaṃ tatoṅgavaktrādi lokapālāstrapaścimam  
AbhTa madhye devyabhidhā pūjyā trayaṃ bhavati pūjitam 
AbhTb tato madhyagatāttasmādbodharāśeḥ sadaivatāt  
AbhTa aṅgādi niḥsṛtaṃ pūjyaṃ visphuliṅgātmakaṃ pṛthak 
AbhTb madhyagā kila yā devī saiva sadbhāvarūpiṇī  
AbhTa kālasaṃkarṣiṇī ghorā śāntā miśrā ca sarvataḥ 
AbhTb siddhātantre ca saikārṇā parā devīti kīrtitā  
AbhTa parā tu mātṛkā devī mālinī madhyagoditā 
AbhTb madhye nyasyetsūryaruciṃ sarvākṣaramayīṃ parām  
AbhTa tasyāḥ śikhāgre tvaikārṇāṃ tasyāścāṅgādikaṃ tviti 
AbhTb tato viśvaṃ viniṣkrāntaṃ pūjitaṃ dakṣiṇottare  
AbhTa syādeva pūjitaṃ tena sakṛnmadhye prapūjayet 
AbhTb śrīdevyāyāmale coktaṃ yāge ḍāmarasaṃjñite  
AbhTa nāsāgre trividhaṃ kālaṃ kālasaṃkarṣiṇī sadā 
AbhTb mukhasthā śvāsaniḥśvāsakalanī hṛdi karṣati  
AbhTa pūrakaiḥ kumbhakairdhatte grasate recakena tu 
AbhTb kālaṃ saṃgrasate sarvaṃ recakenotthitā kṣaṇāt  
AbhTa icchāśaktiḥ parā nāmnā śaktitritayabodhinī 
AbhTb yājyā karṣati yatsarvaṃ kālādhāraprabhañjanam  
AbhTa iha kila dṛkkarmecchāḥ śiva uktāstāstu vedyakhaṇḍanake 
AbhTb sthūle sūkṣme kramaśaḥ sakalapralayākalau bhavataḥ  
AbhTa śuddhā eva tu suptā jñānākalatāṃ gatāḥ prabuddhāstu 
AbhTb pravibhinnakatipayātmakavedyavido mantra ucyante  
AbhTa bhinne tvakhile vedye mantreśāstanmaheśāstu 
AbhTb bhinnābhinne tadiyān suśivāntodhvoditaḥ prete  
AbhTa tā eva galati bhedaprasare kramaśo vikāsamāyāntyaḥ 
AbhTb anyonyāsaṃkīrṇāstvarātrayaṃ galitabhedikāstu tataḥ  
AbhTa padmatrayyaunmanasī tadidaṃ syādāsanatvena 
AbhTb tā evānyonyātmakabhedāvacchedanājihāsutayā  
AbhTa kila śaktitadvadādiprabhidā pūjyatvamāyātāḥ 
AbhTb bhedagalanādyakoṭerārabhya yato nijaṃ nijaṃ rūpam  
AbhTa bibhrati tāstu tritvaṃ tāsāṃ sphuṭameva lakṣyeta 
AbhTb saṃbhāvyavedyakāluṣyayogatonyonyalabdhasaṃkarataḥ  
AbhTa prāk prasphuṭaṃ tribhāvaṃ nāgacchannatra tu tathā na 
AbhTb anyonyātmakabhedāvacchedanakalanasaṃgrasiṣṇutayā 
AbhTc svātantryamātrasārā saṃvitsā kālakarṣiṇī kathitā  
AbhTa saiva ca bhūyaḥ svasmātsaṃkarṣati kālamiha bahiṣkurute 
AbhTb saṃkarṣiṇīti kathitā mātṛṣveteṣu sadbhāvaḥ  
AbhTa tattvaṃ sattā prāptirmātṛṣu meyonayā saṃśca 
AbhTb viśvajananīṣu śaktiṣu paramārtho hi svatantratāmātram  
AbhTa eṣaṇavidikriyātmakametatpūjyaṃ yatonavacchinnam 
AbhTb yasminsarvāvacchedadiśopi syuḥ samākṣiptāḥ  
AbhTa avikalpamiha na yāti hi pūjyatvaṃ naca vikalpa ekatra 
AbhTb bahavo dharmāstasmād yo dharmastāvato dharmān  
AbhTa ākṣipati tatra rūḍhaḥ sarvotkṛṣṭodharasthitāstvanye 
AbhTb iti bhairavaparapūjātattvaṃ śrīḍāmare mahāyāge  
AbhTa svayameva suprasannaḥ śrīmān śaṃbhurmamādikṣat 
AbhTb bāhyayāge tu padmānāṃ tritayepi prapūjayet  
AbhTa astrāntaṃ parivāraughamiti no daiśikāgamaḥ 
AbhTb agnīśarakṣovāyvantadikṣu vidyāṅgapañcakam  
AbhTa śaktyaṅgāni śivāṅgāni tathaivātra punardvaye 
AbhTb astraṃ nyasyeccaturdikkaṃ madhye locanasaṃjñakam  
AbhTa patrāṣṭakeṣṭakayugamaghorādeḥ svayāmalam 
AbhTb tathā dvādaśakaṃ ṣaṭkaṃ catuṣkaṃ miśritaṃ dviśaḥ  
AbhTa sarvaśo dviguṇādītthamāvṛtitvena pūjayet 
AbhTb lokapālāṃstataḥ sāstrānsvadikṣu daśasu kramāt  
AbhTa itthaṃ triśūlaparyantadevītādātmyavṛttitaḥ 
AbhTb tiṣṭhannatrārpayanviśvaṃ tarpayeddevatāgaṇam  
AbhTa tato japaṃ prakurvīta pratimantraṃ dvipañcadhā 
AbhTb ekaikasya tryātmakatvādabhedāccāpi sarvaśaḥ  
AbhTa nābhihṛtkaṇṭhatālūrdhvakuṇḍe jvalanavatsmaran 
AbhTb mantracakraṃ tatra viśvaṃ jvahvansaṃpādayeddhutim  
AbhTa dīkṣākarmaṇi kartavye dīkṣāṃ yenādhvanā guruḥ 
AbhTb cikīrṣurdeha evādau bhūyastaṃ mukhyatorpayet  
AbhTa dvādaśāntamidaṃ prāgraṃ triśūlaṃ mūlataḥ smaran 
AbhTb devīcakrāgragaṃ tyaktakramaḥ khecaratāṃ vrajet  
AbhTa mūlādhārāddviṣaṭkāntavyomāgrāpūraṇātmikā 
AbhTb khecarīyaṃ khasaṃcārasthitibhyāṃ khāmṛtāśanāt  
AbhTa amuṣmācchāmbhavācchūlāddhrāsayeccaturaṅgulam 
AbhTb śākte tatopyāṇave tattriśūlatritayaṃ sthitam  
AbhTa tattriśūlatrayordhvordhvadevīcakrārpitātmakaḥ 
AbhTb kiṃ kiṃ na jāyate kiṃ vā na vetti na karoti vā  
AbhTa ekaikāmathavā devīṃ mantraṃ vā padmagaṃ yajet 
AbhTb yāmalaikyāṅgavaktrādisadasattāvikalpataḥ  
AbhTa itthaṃ prāṇādvyomapadaparyantaṃ cetanaṃ nijam 
AbhTb śivībhāvyārcanāyogāttato bāhyaṃ vidhiṃ caret  
AbhTa bahiryāgasya mukhyatve siddhyādiparikalpite 
AbhTb antaryāgaḥ saṃskriyāyai hyanyathārcayitā paśuḥ  
AbhTa yastu siddhyādivimukhaḥ sa bahiryajati prabhum 
AbhTb antarmahāyāgarūḍhyai tayaivāsau kṛtārthakaḥ  
AbhTa kṛtvāntaryāgamādāya dhānyādyastreṇa mantritam 
AbhTb dikṣu kṣipedvighnanude saṃhṛtyaiśīṃ diśaṃ nayet  
AbhTa nirīkṣaṇaṃ prokṣaṇaṃ ca tāḍanāpyāyane tathā 
AbhTb viguṇṭhanaṃ ca saṃskārāḥ sādhārāstriśiromate  
AbhTa gomūtragomayadadhikṣīrājyaṃ mantrayenmukhaiḥ 
AbhTb ūrdhvāntairaṅgaṣaṭkena kuśāmbvetena cokṣayet  
AbhTa bhūmiṃ śeṣaṃ ca śiṣyārthaṃ sthāpayetpañcagavyakam 
AbhTb pañca gavyāni yatrāsminkuśāmbuni taducyate  
AbhTa pañcagavyaṃ jalaṃ śāstre bāhyāśuddhivimardakam 
AbhTb laukikyāmaviśuddhau hi mṛditāyāmathāntarīm  
AbhTa aśuddhiṃ dagdhumāstheyaṃ mantrādi yadalaukikam 
AbhTb phādināntāṃ smareddevīṃ pṛthivyādiśivāntagām  
AbhTa puṣpāñjaliṃ kṣipenmadhye dhūpagandhāsavādi ca 
AbhTb tathaiva dadyādyāgaukomadhye tenāśu vigraham  
AbhTa samastaṃ devatācakramadhiṣṭhātṛ prakalpyate 
AbhTb anantanāle dharmādipatre sadvaidyakarṇike  
AbhTa ṣaḍutthe gandhapuṣpādyairgaṇeśaṃ hyaiśagaṃ yajet 
AbhTb atthitaṃ vighnasaṃśāntyai pūjayitvā visarjayet  
AbhTd tataḥ kumbhaṃ parāmodidravadravyaprapūritam  
AbhTa pūjitaṃ carcitaṃ mūlamanunā mantrayecchatam 
AbhTb asinā karkarīṃ pūrvamastrayāgo na cetkṛtaḥ  
AbhTa tamaiśānyāṃ yajetkumbhaṃ vāmasthakalaśānvitam 
AbhTb tataḥ sauradigāśrityā sāstrāṃllokeśvarānyajet  
AbhTa gandhapuṣpopahārādyairvidhinā mantrapūrvakam 
AbhTb tataḥ śiṣyosikalaśīhasto dhārāṃ prapātayan  
AbhTa guruṇā kumbhahastenānuvrajyo vadatā tvidam 
AbhTb bho bhoḥ śakra tvayā svasyāṃ diśi vighnapraśāntaye  
AbhTa sāvadhānena karmāntaṃ bhavitavyaṃ śivājñayā 
AbhTb tryakṣare nirṛtiprāye nāmni bhoḥśabdamekakam  
AbhTa apāsayedyato mantraśchandobaddhoyamīritaḥ 
AbhTb tata aiśyāṃ diśi sthāpyaḥ sa kumbho vikiropari  
AbhTa dakṣiṇe cāstravārdhānī sthāpyā kumbhasya sāṃpratam 
AbhTb kumbhasthāmbusamāpattivṛṃhitaṃ mantravṛndakam  
AbhTa tejomātrātmanā dhyātaṃ sarvamāpyāyayedvidhim 
AbhTb ataḥ kumbhe mantragaṇaṃ sarvaṃ saṃpūjayedguruḥ  
AbhTa pūrveṇa vidhināstraṃ ca karkaryāṃ vighnanudyajet 
AbhTb madhyegṛhaṃ tato gandhamaṇḍale pūjayedguruḥ  
AbhTa trikaṃ yāmalataikyābhyāmekaṃ vā mantradaivatam 
AbhTb agnikāryavidhānāya tataḥ kuṇḍaṃ prakalpayet  
AbhTa śuddhamantrādisaṃjalpasaṃkalpotthamapūrvakam 
AbhTb śivasya yā kriyāśaktistatkuṇḍamiti bhāvanāt  
AbhTa paramaḥ khalu saṃskāro vināpyanyaiḥ kriyākramaiḥ 
AbhTb evaṃ dehe sthaṇḍile vā liṅge pātre jalenale  
AbhTa puṣpādiṣu śiśau mukhyaḥ saṃskāraḥ śivatādṛśe 
AbhTb uktaṃ śrīyogasaṃcāre tathāhi parameśinā  
AbhTa caturdaśavidhe bhūte puṣpe dhūpe nivedane 
AbhTb dīpe jape tathā home sarvatraivātra caṇḍikā  
AbhTa juhoti japati preddhe pūjayedvihasedvrajet 
AbhTb āhāre maithune saiva dehasthā karmakāriṇī  
AbhTa tādṛśīṃ ye tu no rūḍhāṃ saṃvittimadhiśerate 
AbhTb akramāttatprasiddhyarthaṃ kramiko vidhirucyate  
AbhTa ahaṃ śivo mantramayaḥ saṃkalpā me tadātmakāḥ 
AbhTb tajjaṃ ca kuṇḍavahnyādi śivātmeti sphuṭaṃ smaret  
AbhTa ata eva hi tatrāpi dārḍhyādārḍhyāvalokanāt 
AbhTb kriyamāṇe kṛte vāpi saṃskriyālpetarāpivā  
AbhTa yathāhi kaścitpratibhādaridrobhyāsapāṭavāt 
AbhTb vākyaṃ gṛhṇāti kopyādau tathātrāpyavabudhyatām  
AbhTa ullekhasekakuṭṭanalepacaturmārgamakṣavṛtiparikalanam 
AbhTb staraparidhiviṣṭarasthitisaṃskārā daśāstrataḥ kuṇḍagatāḥ  
AbhTa madhyagrahaṇaṃ darbhadvayena kuśasaṃvṛtiśca bhittīnām 
AbhTb prāṅmukharekhātritayordhvarekhikāḥ kuśasamāvṛtiśca bahiḥ  
AbhTa śastalatāścaturaśraṃ daśalokeśārcanāsanavidhiśca 
AbhTb sadmāsādanamastrāgnitejasā rakṣaṇaṃ ca kuṇḍasya  
AbhTa bhūmeḥ śivāgnidhṛtyai śaktirvighnāpasāraṇaṃ cārthāḥ 
AbhTb tatastu pūjite kuṇḍe kriyāśaktitayā sphuṭam  
AbhTa mātṛkāṃ mālinīṃ vāpi nyasyetsaṃkalparūpiṇīm 
AbhTb saṃkalpadevyā yatsṛṣṭidhāma tryaśraṃ kriyātmakam  
AbhTa jñānaśukrakaṇaṃ tatra triḥ prakṣobhya vinikṣipet 
AbhTb icchātaḥ kṣubhitaṃ jñānaṃ vimarśātmakriyāpade  
AbhTa rūḍhaṃ jñatvādipañcāṅgavispaṣṭaṃ jājvalītyalam 
AbhTb tenāṅgapañcakaireva hutiṃ dadyātsakṛtsakṛt  
AbhTa janmādyakhilasaṃskāraśuddhognistāvatā bhavet 
AbhTb pañcāṅgameva pṛthvyādirūpaṃ kaṭhinatādikāḥ  
AbhTa śaktīrdadhadvahnigatāḥ kuryādgarbhādikāḥ kriyāḥ 
AbhTb tatokhilādhvasaddevīcakragarbhāṃ parāparām  
AbhTa smaranpūrṇāhutivaśātpūrayedagnisaṃskriyāḥ 
AbhTb tathā mantreśayuksatyasaṃkalpamahasā jvalan  
AbhTa vahnistacchivasaṃkalpatādātmyācchivatātmakaḥ 
AbhTb ityetatsaṃskriyātattvaṃ śrīśaṃbhurme nyarūpayat  
AbhTa mayāpi darśitaṃ śuddhabuddhayaḥ praviviñcatām 
AbhTb tenātra ye codayanti yathā bālasya saṃskriyā  
AbhTa bahnau vahnestathānyatretyanavasthaiva saṃskṛteḥ 
AbhTb te nirutthānavihatā nayesmingurudarśane  
AbhTa jātegnau saṃskṛte śaive śabdarāśiṃ ca mālinīm 
AbhTb pitarau pūjayitvā svaṃ śuddhaṃ dhāma visarjayet  
AbhTa śuddhāgnerbhāgamādāya carvarthaṃ sthāpayetpṛthak 
AbhTb athavāgneḥ śikhāṃ vāmaprāṇenādāya hṛjjuṣā  
AbhTa cidagninaikyamānīya kṣipeddakṣeṇa saṃskṛtām 
AbhTb śiva ityabhimānena dṛḍhena hi vilokanam  
AbhTa sarvasya saṃskriyā tattvaṃ tattasmai yadyatomalam 
AbhTb navāhutīratho dadyānnavātmasahitena tu  
AbhTa śivāgnaye tārapūrvaṃ svāhāntaṃ saṃskriyā bhavet 
AbhTb śivacaitanyasāmānyavyoparūpenale tataḥ  
AbhTa prāgvadādhāramādheyaṃ devīcakraṃ ca yojayet 
AbhTb sruvaṃ srucaṃ ca saṃpaśyedadhovaktrau kramādguruḥ  
AbhTa śivaśaktitayābhyarcyau tathetthaṃ saṃskriyānayoḥ 
AbhTb tattvasaṃdarśanānnānyatsaṃskārasyāsti jīvitam  
AbhTa iti vaktuṃ sruvādīśaḥ śrīpūrve na samaskarot 
AbhTb tatastilairmṛgīṃ madhyānāmāṅguṣṭhavaśādguruḥ  
AbhTa kṛtvā mūlaṃ tarpayet śatenājyasruvaistathā 
AbhTb aṅgavaktraṃ ṣaḍaṃśena śeṣāṃścāpi daśāṃśataḥ  
AbhTa sahasrādikahomopi tṛptyai vittānusārataḥ 
AbhTb sati vittepi lobhādigrasto bāhyapradhānatām  
AbhTa prathayaṃścidguṇībhāvācchaktipātaṃ na vindati 
AbhTb uktaṃ svacchandatantre taddīkṣitopi na mokṣabhāk  
AbhTa nanu yattasya dīkṣāyāṃ kṛtaṃ karmāsya kiṃ phalam 
AbhTb tatrāhurgamaśāstrajñā vāmāśaktimayāstadā  
AbhTa mantrā badhnanti taṃ samyagbhavakārāmahāgṛhe 
AbhTb yā tvanugrāhikā śaktisteṣāṃ sā gurudīpitā  
AbhTa śodhayeta svaśāstrasthaniṣkāmollaṅghanakriyām 
AbhTb tata ūrdhvādharanyāsādanyonyaunmukhyasundaram  
AbhTa sruksruvaṃ śivaśaktyātmādāyājyāmṛtapūritam 
AbhTb samacittaprāṇatanuraikātmyavidhiyogataḥ  
AbhTa vāmaṃ srugdaṇḍagaṃ hastaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ sopayāmakam 
AbhTb kaṇṭhādhogaṃ vinikṣipya dṛḍhamāpīḍya yatnavān  
AbhTa adhaḥ kuryātsrucaṃ prāṇamūrdhvordhvaṃ saṃniyojayan 
AbhTb yāvaddviṣaṭkaparyante bodhāgnau candracakrataḥ  
AbhTa srugagrātparamaṃ hlādi patedamṛtamuttamam 
AbhTb tāvadvahnau mantramukhe vauṣaḍantāṃ hutiṃ kṣipet  
AbhTa ya ūrdhve kila saṃbodhaḥ kuṇḍe sa pratibimbitaḥ 
AbhTb vahniḥ prāṇaḥ sruksruvau ca snehaḥ saṃkalpacidrasaḥ  
AbhTa itthaṃ jñātvāditaḥ kuṇḍasruksruvājyamanūnbhṛśam 
AbhTb dvādaśāntavibodhāgnau ruddhvā pūrṇāhutiṃ kṣipet  
AbhTa yathā yathā hi gaganamutpatetkalahaṃsakaḥ 
AbhTb jale binbaṃ bruḍatyasya tathetyatrāpyayaṃ vidhiḥ  
AbhTa svābhāvikaṃ sthiraṃ caiva dravaṃ dīptaṃ calaṃ nabhaḥ 
AbhTb māyā bindustathaivātmā nādaḥ śaktiḥ śivastathā  
AbhTa itthaṃ vyāpyavyāpakato vibhedyābhyantarāntam 
AbhTb tadadhaḥsthāni pṛthvyādimūlāntāni tathā pumān  
AbhTa avidyārāganiyatikālamāyākalāstathā 
AbhTb aṇurvidyā tadīśeśau sādākhyaṃ śaktikuṇḍalī  
AbhTa vyāpinī samanaunmanyaṃ tatonāmani yojayet 
AbhTb recakastho madhyanāḍīsandhividgururityadaḥ  
AbhTa proktaṃ traiśirase tantre parayojanavarṇane 
AbhTb tataḥ prāksthāpitānyastamantrasaṃskṛtavahninā  
AbhTa caruḥ sādhyothavā śiṣyairhomena samakālakaḥ 
AbhTb carau ca vīradravyāṇi laukikānyathavecchayā  
AbhTa carusiddhau samastāśca kriyā hṛnmantrayogataḥ 
AbhTb tataścaruṃ samādāya gururājyena pūritām  
AbhTa srucaṃ sruvaṃ vā kṛtvaiva bhuktimuktyanusārataḥ 
AbhTb devānāmatha śaktīnāṃ yantrāṇāṃ tu trayaṃ trayam  
AbhTa saptamaṃ mātṛsadbhāvaṃ kramādekaikaśaḥ paṭhan 
AbhTb svā ityamṛtavarṇena vahnau hutvājyaśeṣakam  
AbhTa carau hetyagnirūpeṇa juhuyāttatpunaḥ punaḥ 
AbhTb bhojyabhojakacarvagnyoritthamekānusandhitaḥ  
AbhTa svāhāpratyavamarśātsyātsamantrādadvayaṃ param 
AbhTb eṣa saṃpātasaṃskāraścarorbhoktā hyadhiṣṭhitaḥ  
AbhTa bhogyasya paramaṃ sāraṃ bhogyaṃ narnarti yatnataḥ 
AbhTb samamekānusandhānātpātato bhoktṛbhogyayoḥ  
AbhTa anyonyatra ca saṃpātātsaṃgamāccetthamucyate 
AbhTb sthaṇḍile kubhbhakarkaryorbhāgaṃ bhāgaṃ nivedayet  
AbhTa bhāgenāgnau mantratṛptirdvayaṃ śiṣyātmanoratha 
AbhTb itthaṃ vihitakartavyo vijñāpyeśaṃ tadīritaḥ  
AbhTa śaktipātakramācchiṣyānsaṃskartuṃ niḥsaredbahiḥ 
AbhTb tatraiṣāṃ pañcagavyaṃ ca caruṃ daśanamārjanam  
AbhTa tasya pātaḥ śubhaḥ prācīsaumyaiśāpyordhvadiggataḥ 
AbhTb aśubhonyatra tatrāstrahomopyaṣṭaśataṃ bhavet  
AbhTa netramantritasadvastrabaddhanetrānacañcalān 
AbhTb ananyahṛdayībhūtānbalāditthaṃ nirodhataḥ  
AbhTa muktāratnādikusumasaṃpūrṇāñjalikānguruḥ 
AbhTb praveśya sthaṇḍilopāgra upaveśyaiva jānubhiḥ  
AbhTa prakṣepayedañjaliṃ taṃ taiḥ śiṣyairbhāvitātmabhiḥ 
AbhTb añjali punarāpūrya teṣāṃ lāghavataḥ paṭam  
AbhTa dṛśornivārayetsopi śiṣyo jhaṭiti paśyati 
AbhTb jhaṭityālokite māntraprabhāvollāsite sthale  
AbhTa tadāveśavaśācchiṣyastanmayatvaṃ prapadyate 
AbhTb yathā hi raktahṛdayastāṃstānkāntāguṇānsvayam  
AbhTa paśyatyevaṃ śaktipātasaṃskṛto mantrasannidhim 
AbhTb cakṣurādīndriyāṇāṃ hi sahakāriṇi tādṛśe  
AbhTa satyatyantamadṛṣṭe prāgapi jāyeta yogyatā 
AbhTb kṛtaprajñā hi vinyastamantraṃ dehaṃ jalaṃ sthalam  
AbhTa pratimādi ca paśyanto viduḥ saṃnidhyasaṃnidhī 
AbhTb nyastamantrāṃśusubhagātkiṃcidbhūtādimudritāḥ  
AbhTa trasyantīveti tattaccidakṣaistatsahakāribhiḥ 
AbhTb tataḥ sa dakṣiṇe haste dīptaṃ sarvādhvapūritam  
AbhTa mantracakraṃ yajedvāmapāṇinā pāśadāhakam 
AbhTb taṃ śiṣyasya karaṃ mūrdhni dehanyastādhvasaṃtateḥ  
AbhTa nyasyetkrameṇa sarvāṃṅgaṃ tenaivāsya ca saṃspṛśet 
AbhTb uktaṃ dīkṣottare caitajjvālāsaṃpātaśobhinā  
AbhTa dattena śivahastena samayī sa vidhīyate 
AbhTb sāyujyamīśvare tattve jīvatodhītiyogyatā  
AbhTa śrīdevyāthāmale tūktamaṣṭārāntastriśūlake 
AbhTb cakre bhairavasannābhāvaghorādyaṣṭakārake  
AbhTa bāhyāpare parānemau madhyaśūlaparāpare 
AbhTb jvālākuleruṇe bhrāmyanmātṛpraṇavabhīṣaṇe  
AbhTa cintite tu bahirhaste saṃdṛṣṭe samayī bhavet 
AbhTb pāśastobhādyastu sadya uccikramiṣurasya tam  
AbhTa prāṇairviyojakaṃ mūrdhni kṣipetsaṃpūjya tadbahiḥ 
AbhTb anena śivahastena samayī bhavati sphuṭam  
AbhTa tasyaiva bhāvividhivattattvapāśaviyojane 
AbhTb putrakatvaṃ sa ca pare tattve yojyastu daiśikaiḥ  
AbhTa sa eva mantrajātijño japahomāditattvavit 
AbhTb nirvāṇakalaśenādau tata īśvarasaṃjñinā  
AbhTa abhiṣiktaḥ sādhakaḥ syādbhogāntesya pare layaḥ 
AbhTb etairguṇaiḥ samāyukto dīkṣitaḥ śivaśāsane  
AbhTa catuṣpātsaṃhitābhijñastantrāṣṭādaśatatparaḥ 
AbhTb daśatantrātimārgajña ācāryaḥ sa vidhīyate  
AbhTa pṛthivīmāditaḥ kṛtvā nirvāṇāntesya yojanām 
AbhTb abhiṣekavidhau kuryādācāryasya gurūttamaḥ  
AbhTa etairvākyairidaṃ coktaṃ samayī rājaputravat 
AbhTb sarvatraivādhikārī syātputrakādipadatraye  
AbhTa putrako daiśikatve tu tulyayojaniko bhavet 
AbhTb adhikārī sa na punaḥ sādhane bhinnayojane  
AbhTa etattantre samayyādikramādāptottarakriyaḥ 
AbhTb ācāryo na punarbauddhavaiṣṇavādiḥ kadācana  
AbhTa evaṃ prasaṅgānnirṇītaṃ prakṛtaṃ tu nirūpyate 
AbhTb śivahastavidhiṃ kṛtvā tena saṃpluṣṭapāśakam  
AbhTa śiṣyaṃ vidhāya viśrāntiparyantaṃ dhyānayogataḥ 
AbhTb tataḥ kumbhestrakalaśe vahnau svātmani taṃ śiśum  
AbhTa praṇāmaṃ kārayetpaścādbhūtamātṛbaliṃ kṣipet 
AbhTb tataḥ śaṃkaramabhyarcya śayyāmastrābhimantritām  
AbhTa kṛtvāsyāṃ śiṣyamāropya nyastamantraṃ vidhāya ca 
AbhTb śiṣyahṛccakraviśrāntiṃ kṛtvā taddvādaśāntagaḥ  
AbhTa bhavetkṣīṇakalājālaḥ svaradvādaśakodayāt 
AbhTb tataḥ praveśapracitakalāṣoḍaśakojjvalaḥ  
AbhTa saṃpūrṇasvātmaciccandro viśrāmyeddhṛdaye śiśoḥ 
AbhTb svayaṃ vyutthānaparyantaṃ dvādaśāntaṃ tato vrajet  
AbhTa punarviśecca hṛccakramitthaṃ nidrāvidhikramaḥ 
AbhTb āyātanidraḥ śiṣyosau nirmalau śaśibhāskarau  
AbhTa hṛccakre pratisaṃdhatte balātpūrṇakṛśātmakau 
AbhTb haṭhanirmalacandrārkaprakāśaḥ satyamīkṣate  
AbhTa svapnaṃ bhāviśubhānyatvasphuṭībhāvanakovidam 
AbhTb uktaṃ ca pūrṇāṃ ca kṛśāṃ dhyātvā dvādaśagocare  
AbhTa praviśya hṛdaye dhyāye tsuptaḥ svācchandyamāpnuyāt 
AbhTb āyātanidre ca śiśau gururabhyarcya śaṅkaram  
AbhTa caruṃ bhuñjīta sasakhā tatodyāddantadhāvanam 
AbhTb svapyācca mantraraśmīddhahṛccakrārpitamānasaḥ  
AbhTa prātarguruḥ kṛtāśeṣanityobhyarcitaśaṃkaraḥ 
AbhTb śiṣyātmanoḥ svapnadṛṣṭāvarthau vitte balābalāt  
AbhTa svadṛṣṭaṃ balavannānyatsaṃbodhodrekayogataḥ 
AbhTb bodhasāmye punaḥ svapnasāmyaṃ syādguruśiṣyayoḥ  
AbhTa devāgnigurutatpūjākāraṇopaskarādikam 
AbhTb hṛdyā strī madyapānaṃ cāpyāmamāṃsasya bhakṣaṇam  
AbhTa raktapānaṃ śiraśchedo raktaviṇmūtralepanam 
AbhTb parvatāśvagajaprāyahṛdyayugyādhirohaṇam  
AbhTa yatprītyai syādapi prāyastattacchubhamudāhṛtam 
AbhTb taṃ khyāpayettuṣṭivṛddhyai hlādo hi paramaṃ phalam  
AbhTa atonyadaśubhaṃ tatra homoṣṭaśatakostrataḥ 
AbhTb aśubhaṃ nāśubhamiti śiṣyebhyo kathayedguruḥ  
AbhTa rūḍhāṃ hi śaṅkāṃ vicchettuṃ yatnaḥ saṃghaṭate mahān 
AbhTb yeṣāṃ tu śaṅkāvilayasteṣāṃ svapnavaśotthitam  
AbhTa śubhāśubhaṃ na kiṃcitsyāt syuścetthaṃ citratāvaśāt 
AbhTb sphuṭaṃ paśyati sattvātmā rājaso liṅgamātrataḥ  
AbhTa na kiṃcittāmasastasya sukhaduḥkhācchubhāśubham 
AbhTb nanvatra tāmaso nāma kathaṃ yogyo vidhau bhavet  
AbhTa maiva mā vigrahaṃ kaścitkvacitkasyāpi vai guṇaḥ 
AbhTb sarvasāttvikaceṣṭopi bhojane yadi tāmasaḥ  
AbhTa kiṃ tataḥ sodhamaḥ kivāpyutkṛṣṭastadviparyayaḥ 
AbhTb āyātaśaktipātopi dīkṣitopi guṇasthiteḥ  
AbhTa vicitrātmā bhavedeva mukhye tvarthe samāhitaḥ 
AbhTb tato guruḥ śiśormantrapūrvakaṃ devatārcanam  
AbhTa deśayetsa ca tatkuryātsaṃskuryāttaṃ tato guruḥ 
AbhTb hṛdādicakraṣaṭkasthānbrahmādīn ṣaṭ samāhitaḥ  
AbhTa spṛśecchiśoḥ prāṇavṛttyā pratyekaṃ cāṣṭa saṃskriyāḥ 
AbhTb hṛdayādidviṣaṭkāntaṃ bodhasparśapavitritaḥ  
AbhTa āhārabījabhāvādidoṣadhvaṃsādbhaveddvijaḥ 
AbhTb vasuvedākhyasaṃskārapūrṇa itthaṃ dvijaḥ sthitaḥ  
AbhTa garbhādhānaṃ puṃsavanaṃ sīmanto jātakarma ca 
AbhTb nāma niṣkrāmaṇaṃ cānnapraśaścūḍā tathāṣṭamī  
AbhTa vratabandhaiṣṭike maujjībhautike saumikaṃ kramāt 
AbhTb godānamiti vedendusaṃskriyā brahmacaryataḥ  
AbhTa pratyudvāhaḥ pañcadaśaḥ sapta pākamakhāstvataḥ 
AbhTb aṣṭakāḥ pārvaṇī śrāddhaṃ śrāvaṇyāgrāyaṇīdvayam  
AbhTa caitrī cāśvayujī paścāt saptaiva tu havirmakhāḥ 
AbhTb ādheyamagnihotraṃ ca paurṇamāsaḥ sadarśakaḥ  
AbhTa cāturmāsyaṃ paśūdbandhaḥ sautrāmaṇyā saha tvamī 
AbhTb agniṣṭomotipūrvotha sokyyaḥ ṣoḍaśivājapau  
AbhTa āptoryāmātirātrau ca saptaitāḥ somasaṃsthitāḥ 
AbhTb hiraṇyapādādimakhaḥ sahasreṇa samāvṛtaḥ  
AbhTa aṣṭatriṃśastvaśvamedho gārhasthyamiyatā bhavet 
AbhTb vānasthyapārivrājye ca catvāriṃśadamī matāḥ  
AbhTa dayā kṣamānasūyā ca śuddhiḥ satkṛtimaṅgale 
AbhTb akārpaṇyāspṛhe cātmaguṇāṣṭakamidaṃ smṛtam  
AbhTa mekhalā daṇḍamajinatryāyuṣe vahnyupāsanam 
AbhTb saṃdhyā bhikṣeti saṃskārāḥ sapta sapta vratāni ca  
AbhTa bhauteśapāśupatye dve gāṇeśaṃ gāṇapatyakam 
AbhTb unmattakāsidhārākhyaghṛteśāni caturdaśa  
AbhTa ete tu vratabandhasya saṃskārā aṅginaḥ smṛtāḥ 
AbhTb pārivrājyasya garbhe syādantyeṣṭiriti saṃskṛtaḥ  
AbhTa dvijo bhavettato yogyo rudrāṃśāpādanāya saḥ 
AbhTb etānprāṇakrameṇaiva saṃskārānyojayedguruḥ  
AbhTa athavāhutiyogena tilādyairmantrapūrvakaiḥ 
AbhTb praṇavo hṛdayaṃ nāma śodhayāmyagnivallabhā  
AbhTa evaṃ krameṇa mūrdhādyairaṅgairatatpunaḥ punaḥ 
AbhTb yataściddharma evāsau śāntyādyātmā dvijanmatā  
AbhTa tena rudratayā saṃvittatkrameṇaiva jāyate 
AbhTb yathā hemādidhātūnāṃ pāke kramavaśādbhavet  
AbhTa rajatādi tathā saṃvitsaṃskāre dvijatāntare 
AbhTb yonirna kāraṇaṃ tatra śāntātmā dvija ucyate  
AbhTa muninā mokṣadharmādāvetacca pravivecitam 
AbhTb mukuṭādiṣu śāstreṣu devenāpi nirūpitam  
AbhTa saṃvido dehasaṃbhedātsadṛśātsadṛśodayāt 
AbhTb bhūmābhiprāyataḥ smārte dvijanmā dvijayoḥ sutaḥ  
AbhTa antyajātīyadhīvādijananījanmalābhataḥ 
AbhTb utkṛṣṭacittā ṛṣayaḥ kiṃ brāhmaṇyena bhājanam  
AbhTa ata evārthasattattvadeśinyasminna diśyate 
AbhTb rahasyaśāstre jātyādisamācāro hi śāmbhave  
AbhTa pāśavāni tu śāstrāṇi vāmaśaktyātmakānyalam 
AbhTb sṛṣṭyāṃcisiddhaye śaṃbhoḥ śaṅkātatphalakḷptaye  
AbhTa āpāditadvijatvasya dvādaśānte nijaikyataḥ 
AbhTb sparśamātrānna viśrāntyā jhaṭityevāvarohataḥ  
AbhTa rudrāṃśāpādanaṃ yena samayī saṃskṛto bhavet 
AbhTb adhītau śravaṇe nityaṃ pūjāyāṃ gurusevane  
AbhTa samayyadhikṛtonyatra guruṇā vibhumarcayet 
AbhTb tamāpāditarudrāṃśaṃ samayān śrāvayedguruḥ  
AbhTa aṣṭāṣṭakātmakāndevyāyāmalādau nirūpitān 
AbhTb avādokaraṇaṃ gūḍhiḥ pūjā tarpaṇabhāvane  
AbhTa hananaṃ mohanaṃ ceti samayāṣṭakamaṣṭadhā 
AbhTb svabhāvaṃ mantratantrāṇāṃ samayācāramelakam  
AbhTa asatpralāpaṃ paruṣamanṛtaṃ nāṣṭadhā vadet 
AbhTb aphalaṃ ceṣṭitaṃ hiṃsāṃ paradārābhimarśanam  
AbhTa garvaṃ dambhaṃ bhūtaviṣavyādhitantraṃ nacācaret 
AbhTb svaṃ mantramakṣasūtraṃ ca vidyāṃ jñānasvarūpakam  
AbhTa samācārānguṇānkleśānsiddhiliṅgāni gūhayet 
AbhTb guruṃ śāstraṃ devavahnī jñānavṛddhāṃstriyo vratam  
AbhTa guruvargaṃ yathāśaktyā pūjayedaṣṭakaṃ tvidam 
AbhTb dīnānkliṣṭānpitṝnkṣetrapālānprāṇigaṇān khagān  
AbhTa śmāśānikaṃ bhūtagaṇaṃ dehadevīśca tarpayet 
AbhTb śivaṃ śaktiṃ tathātmānaṃ mudrāṃ mantrasvarūpakam  
AbhTa saṃsārabhuktimuktīśca guruvaktrāttu bhāvayet 
AbhTb rāgaṃ dveṣamasūyāṃ ca saṃkocerṣyābhimānitāḥ  
AbhTa samayapratibhettṝṃstadanācārāṃśca ghātayet 
AbhTb paśumārgasthitānkrūrāndveṣiṇaḥ piśunāñjaḍān  
AbhTa rājñaścānucarānpāpānvighnakartṝṃśca mohayet 
AbhTb śākinyaḥ pūjanīyāśca tāścetthaṃ śrīgamoditāḥ  
AbhTa sāhasaṃ dviguṇaṃ yāsāṃ kāmaścaiva caturguṇaḥ 
AbhTb lobhaścāṣṭaguṇastāsāṃ śaṅkyaṃ śākinya ityalam  
AbhTa kulāmnāyasthitā vīradravyabāhyāstu ye na taiḥ 
AbhTb paśubhiḥ saha vastavyamiti śrīmādhave kule  
AbhTa devatācakragurvagniśāstraṃ sāmyātsadārcayet 
AbhTb aniveditametebhyo na kiṃcidapi bhakṣayet  
AbhTa etaddravyaṃ nāpaharedguruvargaṃ prapūjayet 
AbhTb sa ca tadbhrātṛbhāryātukprāyo vidyākṛto bhavet  
AbhTa na yonisaṃbandhakṛto laukikaḥ sa paśuryataḥ 
AbhTb tasyābhiṣvaṅgabhūmistu gurvārādhanasiddhaye  
AbhTa arcyo na svamahimnā tu tadvargo guruvatpunaḥ 
AbhTb gurornindāṃ na kurvīta tasyai hetuṃ nacācaret  
AbhTa naca tāṃ śṛṇuyānnainaṃ kopayennāgratosya ca 
AbhTb vinājñayā prakurvīta kiṃcittatsevanādṛte  
AbhTa laukikālaukikaṃ kṛtyaṃ krodhaṃ krīḍāṃ tapo japam 
AbhTb gurūpabhuktaṃ yatkiṃcicchayyāvastrāsanādikam  
AbhTa nopabhuñjīta tatpadbhyāṃ na spṛśetkiṃtu vandayet 
AbhTb śrīmattraiśirasepyuktaṃ kṛcchracāndrāyaṇādibhiḥ  
AbhTa araṇye kāṣṭhavattiṣṭhedasidhārāvratopi san 
AbhTb niyamastho yamasthopi tatpadaṃ nāśnute param  
AbhTa gurvārādhanasaktastu manasā karmaṇā girā 
AbhTb prāpnoti gurutastuṣṭāt pūrṇaṃ śreyo mahādbhutam  
AbhTa himapātairyathā bhūmiśchāditā sā samantataḥ 
AbhTb mārutaśleṣasaṃyogādaśmavattiṣṭhate sadā  
AbhTa yamādau niścale tadvadbhāva ekastu gṛhyate 
AbhTb gurostvārādhitātpūrṇaṃ prasarajjñānamāpyate  
AbhTa sarvatovasthitaṃ cittvaṃ jñeyasthaṃ yasya tatkathā 
AbhTb sadya eva nayedūrdhvaṃ tasmādārādhayedgurum  
AbhTa śrīsārepyasya saṃbhāṣātpātakaṃ naśyati kṣaṇāt 
AbhTb tasmātparīkṣya yatnena śāstroktyā jñānalakṣaṇaiḥ  
AbhTa śāstrācāreṇa varteta tena saṅgaṃ tathā kuru 
AbhTb snehājjātu vadejjñānaṃ lobhānna hriyate hi saḥ  
AbhTa tena tuṣṭena tṛpyanti devāḥ pitara evaca 
AbhTb uttīrya narakādyānti sadyaḥ śivapuraṃ mahat  
AbhTa bhuṅkte tiṣṭhedyatra gṛhe vrajecchivapuraṃ tu saḥ 
AbhTb iti jñātvā sadā pitrye śrāddhe svaṃ gurumarcayet  
AbhTa bhuñjīta sa svayaṃ cānyānādiśettatkṛte guruḥ 
AbhTb yo dīkṣitastu śrāddhādau svatantraṃ vidhimācaret  
AbhTa tasya tanniṣphalaṃ sarvaṃ samayena ca laṅghyate 
AbhTb saiddhāntikārpitaṃ caṇḍīyogyaṃ dravyaṃ vivarjayet  
AbhTa śākinīvācakaṃ śabdaṃ na kadācitsamuccaret 
AbhTb striyaḥ pūjyā virūpāstu vṛddhāḥ śilpopajīvikāḥ  
AbhTa antyā vikāritāṅgyaśca veśyāḥ svacchandaceṣṭitāḥ 
AbhTb tathāca śrīgame proktaṃ pūjanīyāḥ prayatnataḥ  
AbhTa nirācārāḥ sarvabhakṣyā dharmādharmavivarjitāḥ 
AbhTb svacchandagāḥ palāśinyo lampaṭā devatā iva  
AbhTa veśyāḥ pūjyāstadgṛhaṃ ca prayāgotra yajetkramam 
AbhTb strīṣu tannācaretkicidyena tābhyo jugupsate  
AbhTa ato na nagnāstāḥ paśyennacāpi prakaṭastanīḥ 
AbhTb vṛddhāyāḥ saṃsthitāyā vā na jugupseta mudrikām  
AbhTa vaikṛtyaṃ tatra saurūpyaṃ melakaṃ na prakāśayet 
AbhTb devamūrtiṃ śūnyatanuṃ pūjayettripathādiṣu  
AbhTa sarvaparvasu sāmānyaviśeṣeṣu viśeṣataḥ 
AbhTb pūjā guroranadhyāyo melake lobhavarjanam  
AbhTa na jugupseta madyādi vīradravyaṃ kadācana 
AbhTb na nindedatha vandeta nityaṃ tajjoṣiṇastathā  
AbhTa upadeśāya na doṣā hṛdayaṃ cenna vidviṣet 
AbhTb vijātīyavikalpāṃśotpuṃsanāya yateta ca  
AbhTa guroḥ śāstrasya devīnāṃ nāma mantre yatastataḥ 
AbhTb arcātonyatra noccāryamāhūtaṃ tarpayettataḥ  
AbhTa āgatasya ca mantrasya na kuryāttarpaṇaṃ yadi 
AbhTb haratyardhaśarīraṃ tadityūce bhagavānyataḥ  
AbhTa śrīmadūrmau ca devīnāṃ vīrāṇāṃ ceṣṭitaṃ na vai 
AbhTb prathayenna jugupseta vadennādravyapāṇikaḥ  
AbhTa śrīpūrvaṃ nāma vaktavyaṃ gurordravyakareṇa ca 
AbhTb gurvādīnāṃ na laṅghyā ca chāyā na tairthikaiḥ saha  
AbhTa jalpaṃ kurvansvaśāstrārthaṃ vadennāpica sūcayet 
AbhTb nityādviśeṣapūjāṃ ca kuryānnaimittike vidhau  
AbhTa tatopi madhye varṣasya tatopi hi pavitrake 
AbhTb anyastamantro nāsīta sevyaṃ śāstrāntaraṃ ca no  
AbhTa aprarūḍhaṃ hi vijñānaṃ kampetetarabhāvanāt 
AbhTb gṛhopaskaraṇāstrāṇi davatāyāgayogataḥ  
AbhTa arcyānīti na padbhyāṃ vai spṛśennāpi vilaṅghyet 
AbhTb guruvarge gṛhāyāte viśeṣaṃ kaṃcidācaret  
AbhTa dīkṣitānāṃ na nindādi kuryādvidveṣapūrvakam 
AbhTb upadeśāya no doṣaḥ sa hyavidveṣapūrvakaḥ  
AbhTa na vaṣṇavādikādhaḥsthadṛṣṭibhiḥ saṃvasedalam 
AbhTb sahabhojanaśayyādyarnaiṣāṃ prakaṭayetsthitim  
AbhTa uktaṃ śrīṃmādhavakule śāsanāntarasaṃsthitān 
AbhTb vedoktiṃ vaiṣṇavoktiṃ ca tairuktaṃ varjayetsadā  
AbhTa akulīneṣu saṃparkāttatkulātpatanādbhayam 
AbhTb ekapātre kulāmnāye tasmāttānparivarjayet  
AbhTa pramādācca kṛte sakhye goṣṭhyāṃ cakraṃ tu pūjayet 
AbhTb śrīmadūrmau ca kathitamāgamāntarasevake  
AbhTa gurvantararate mūḍhe devadravyopajīvake 
AbhTb śaktihiṃsākare duṣṭe saṃparkaṃ naiva kārayet  
AbhTa na vikalpena dīkṣādau vrajedāyatanādikam 
AbhTb uktāsthāśithilatve yannimittaṃ naiva taccaret  
AbhTa śāsanasthānpurājātyā na paśyennāpyudīrayet 
AbhTb naca vyavaharetsarvāñchivābhedena kevalam  
AbhTa sadvidyaiḥ sākamāsīta jñānadīptyai yateta ca 
AbhTb nāsaṃskṛtāṃ vrajettajjaṃ viphalatvaṃ nacānayet  
AbhTa melakārdhaniśācaryā janavarjaṃ ca tannahi 
AbhTb māṃsādidāhagandhaṃ ca jighreddevīpriyo hyasau  
AbhTa gurvājñāṃ pālayansarvaṃ tyajenmantramayo bhavet 
AbhTb śāstrapūjājapadhyānavivekatadupakriyāḥ  
AbhTa akurvanniṣphalāṃ naiva ceṣṭeta trividhāṃ kriyām 
AbhTb mantratantrairna vādaṃ ca kuryānno bhakṣayedviṣam  
AbhTa samayānāṃ vilope ca guruṃ pṛcchedasannidhau 
AbhTb tadvargaṃ nijasantānamanyaṃ tasyāpyasaṃnidhau  
AbhTa tenoktamanutiṣṭhecca nirvikalpaṃ prayatnataḥ 
AbhTb yataḥ śāstrādisaṃbodhatanmayīkṛtamānasaḥ  
AbhTa śiva eva gururnāsya vāgasatyā viniḥsaret 
AbhTb śivasya svātmasaṃskṛtyai prahvībhāvo guroḥ punaḥ  
AbhTa hlādāyetyubhayārthāya tattuṣṭiḥ phaladā śiśoḥ 
AbhTb gurvāyattaikasiddhirhisamayyapi vibodhabhāk  
AbhTa tadbodhabahumānena vidyādgurutamaṃ gurum 
AbhTb ataḥ saṃprāpya vijñānaṃ yo gurau bāhyamānavān  
AbhTa nāsau vijñānaviśvasto nāsatyaṃ bhraṣṭa eva saḥ 
AbhTb jñānānāśvastacittaṃ taṃ vacomātreṇa śāstritam  
AbhTa bhaktaṃ ca nārcayejjātu hṛdā vijñānadūṣakam 
AbhTb tādṛk ca na guruḥ kāryastaṃ kṛtvāpi parityajet  
AbhTa mukhyabuddhyā na saṃpaśyedvaiṣṇavādigatāngurūn 
AbhTb tathāca śrīmadūrmyākhye guroruktaṃ viśeṣaṇam  
AbhTa gurvājñā prāṇasaṃdehe nopekṣyā no vikalpyate 
AbhTb kauladīkṣā kaulaśāstraṃ tattvajñānaṃ prakāśitam  
AbhTa yenāsau gururityukto hyanye vai nāmadhāriṇaḥ 
AbhTb śrīmadānandaśāstre ca tathaivoktaṃ viśeṣaṇam  
AbhTa yasmāddīkṣā mantraśāstraṃ tattvajñānaṃ sa vai guruḥ 
AbhTb tiṣṭhedavyaktaliṅgaśca na liṅgaṃ dhārayet kvacit  
AbhTa na liṅgibhiḥ samaṃ kaiścitkuryādācāramelanam 
AbhTb kevalaṃ liṅginaḥ pālyā na bībhatsyā virūpakāḥ  
AbhTa śrīmadrātrikule coktaṃ mokṣaḥ śaṅkāpahānitaḥ 
AbhTb aśuddhavāsasnayaiṣā mokṣavārtāpi durlabhā  
AbhTa na likhenmantrahṛdayaṃ śrīmanmāloditaṃ kila 
AbhTb tadaṅgāduddharenmantraṃ natu lekhe vilekhayet  
AbhTa atattvebhiniveśaṃ ca na kuryātpakṣapātataḥ 
AbhTb jātividyākulācāradehadeśaguṇārthajān  
AbhTa grahāngrahānivāṣṭau drāktyajedgahvararśitān 
AbhTb tathā śrīniśicārādau hayatvenopadarśitān  
AbhTa brāhmaṇohaṃ mayā vedaśāstroktādaparaṃ katham 
AbhTb anuṣṭheyamayaṃ jātigrahaḥ paranirodhakaḥ  
AbhTa evamanyepyudāhāryāḥ kulagahvaravartmanā 
AbhTb atatsvabhāve tādrūpyaṃ darśayannavaśepi yaḥ  
AbhTa svarūpācchādakaḥ sotra graho graha ivoditaḥ 
AbhTb saṃvitsvabhāve no jātiprabhṛtiḥ kāpi kalpanā  
AbhTa rūpaṃ sā tvasvarūpeṇa tadrūpaṃ chādayatyalam 
AbhTb yā kācitkalpanā saṃvittattvasyākhaṇḍitātmanaḥ  
AbhTa saṃkocakāriṇī sarvaḥ sa grahastāṃ parityajet 
AbhTb śrīmadānandaśāstre ca kathitaṃ parameṣṭhinā  
AbhTa nirapekṣaḥ prabhurvāmo na śuddhyā tatra kāraṇam 
AbhTb devītṛptirmakhe raktamāṃsairno śaucayojanāt  
AbhTa dvijāntyajaiḥ samaṃ kāryā carcāntepi marīcayaḥ 
AbhTb avikārakṛtastena vikalpānnirayo bhavet  
AbhTa sarvadevamayaḥ kāyaḥ sarvaprāṇiṣviti sphuṭam 
AbhTb śrīmadbhirnakuleśādyairapyetatsunirūpitam  
AbhTa śarīramevāyatanaṃ nānyadāyatanaṃ vrajet 
AbhTb tīrthamekaṃ smarenmantramanyatīrthāni varjayet  
AbhTa vidhimenaṃ sukhaṃ jñātvā vidhijālaṃ parityajet 
AbhTb samādhirniścayaṃ muktvā na cānyenopalabhyate  
AbhTa iti matvā vidhānajñaḥ saṃmohaṃ parivarjayet 
AbhTb mantrasya hṛdayaṃ muktvā na cānyatparamaṃ kvacit  
AbhTa iti matvā vidhānajño mantrajālaṃ parityajet 
AbhTb naivedyaṃ prāśayennadyāstaccheṣaṃ ca jale kṣipet  
AbhTa tairbhukte na bhaveddoṣo jalajaiḥ pūrvadīkṣitaiḥ 
AbhTb avayaśpālanīyatvātparattvena saṃgamāt  
AbhTa jñānaprāptyabhyupāyatvātsamayāste prakīrtitāḥ 
AbhTb evaṃ saṃśrāvya samayāndevaṃ saṃpūjya daiśikaḥ  
AbhTa visarjayetsvacidvyomni śānte mūrtivilāpanāt 
AbhTb yadi putrakadīkṣāsya na kāryā samanantaram  
AbhTa tadābhiṣiñcetsāstreṇa śivakumbhena taṃ śiśum 
AbhTb ātmānaṃ ca tato yasmājjalamūrtirmaheśvaraḥ  
AbhTa mantrayuṅnikhilāpyāyī kāryaṃ tadabhiṣecanam 
AbhTb iti samayadīkṣaṇamidaṃ prakāśitaṃ vistarācca saṃkṣepāt 
C atha śrītantrāloke ṣoḍaśamāhnikam
AbhTa atha putrakatvasiddhyai nirūpyate śivanirūpito tra vidhiḥ 
AbhTb yadā tu samayasthasya putrakatve niyojanam 
AbhTc gurutve sādhakatve vā kartumicchati daiśikaḥ  
AbhTa tadādhivāsaṃ kṛtvāhni dvitīye maṇḍalaṃ likhet 
AbhTb sāmudāyikayāgetha tathānyatra yathoditam  
AbhTa ṣaḍaṣṭataddviguṇitacaturviṃśatisaṃkhyayā 
AbhTb cakrapañcakamākhyātaṃ śāstre śrīpūrvasaṃjñite  
AbhTa dvātriṃśattaddviguṇitaṃ śrīmattraiśirase mate 
AbhTb asaṃkhyacakrasaṃbandhaḥ śrīsiddhādau nirūpitaḥ  
AbhTa tasmādyathātathā yāgaṃ yāvaccakreṇa saṃmitam 
AbhTb pūjayedyena tenātra triśūlatrayamālikhet  
AbhTa triśūlatritaye devītrayaṃ paryāyavṛttitaḥ 
AbhTb madhyasavyānyabhedena pūrṇaṃ saṃpūjitaṃ bhavet  
AbhTa vartanā maṇḍalasyāgre saṃkṣepādupadekṣyate 
AbhTb ālikhya maṇḍalaṃ gandhavastreṇaivāsya mārjanam  
AbhTa kṛtvā snāto guruḥ prāgvanmaṇḍalāgretra devatāḥ 
AbhTb bāhyagāḥ pūjayeddvāradeśe ca dvāradevatāḥ  
AbhTa maṇḍalasya purobhāge tadaiśānadiśaḥ kramāt 
AbhTb āgneyyantaṃ gaṇeśādīn kṣetrapāntānprapūjayet  
AbhTa gaṇapatiguruparamākhyāḥ parameṣṭhī pūrvasiddhavākkṣetrapatiḥ 
AbhTb iti saptakamākhyātaṃ gurupaṅktividhau prapūjyamasmadgurubhiḥ  
AbhTa tata ājñāṃ gṛhītvā tu puṣpadhūpādipūjitam 
AbhTb pūjyamādhāraśaktyādi śūlamūlātprabhṛtyalam  
AbhTa śivāntaṃ sitapadmānte triśūlānāṃ traye kramāt 
AbhTb madhyaśūle madhyagaḥ syātsadbhāvaḥ parayā saha  
AbhTa vāme cāparayā sākaṃ navātmā dakṣagaṃ param 
AbhTb triśūle dakṣiṇe madhyaśṛṅgastho ratiśekharaḥ  
AbhTa syātparāparayā sākaṃ dakṣe bhairavasatpare 
AbhTb vāme triśūle madhyastho navātmāparayā saha  
AbhTa syātpare parayā sākaṃ vāmāre saṃśca bhairavaḥ 
AbhTb itthaṃ sarvagatatve śrīparādevyāḥ sthite sati  
AbhTa yāgo bhavetsusaṃpūrṇastadadhiṣṭhānamātrataḥ 
AbhTb ekaśūlepyato yāge cintayettadadhiṣṭhitam  
AbhTa avidhijño vidhānajña ityevaṃ trīśikoditam 
AbhTb tato madhye tathā dakṣe vāme śṛṅge ca sarvataḥ  
AbhTa lokapālāstraparyantamekātmatvena pūjayet 
AbhTb paratvena ca sarvāsāṃ devatānāṃ prapūjayet  
AbhTa śrīmantaṃ mātṛsadbhāvabhaṭṭārakamanāmayam 
AbhTb tatopi bhogayāgena vidyāṅgaṃ bhairavāṣṭakam  
AbhTa yāmalaṃ cakradevīśca svasthāne pūjayedbahiḥ 
AbhTb lokapālānastrayutāngandhapuṣpāsavādibhiḥ  
AbhTa pūjayetparayā bhaktyā vittaśāṭhyavivarjitaḥ 
AbhTb tataḥ kumbhāstrakalaśīmaṇḍalasthānalātmanām  
AbhTa pañcānāmanusandhānaṃ kuryādadvayabhāvanāt 
AbhTb ye tu tāmadvayavyāptiṃ na vindanti śivātmikām  
AbhTa mantranāḍīprayogeṇa te viśantyadvaye pathi 
AbhTb svadakṣiṇena niḥsṛtya maṇḍalasthasya vāmataḥ  
AbhTa praviśyānyena niḥsṛtya kumbhasthe karkarīgate 
AbhTb vahnisthe ca krameṇetthaṃ yāvatsvasminsvavāmataḥ  
AbhTa mūlānusandhānabalātprāṇatantūmbhane sati 
AbhTb itthamaikyasphurattātmā vyāptisaṃvitprakāśate  
AbhTa tato viśeṣapūjāṃ ca kuryādadvayabhāvitām 
AbhTb yacchivādvayapīyūṣasaṃsiktaṃ paramaṃ hi tat  
AbhTa tenārghapuṣpagandhāderāsavasya paśoratha 
AbhTb yā śivādvayatādṛṣṭiḥ sā śuddhiḥ paramīkṛtiḥ  
AbhTa nivedayedvibhoragre jīvāndhātūṃstadutthitān 
AbhTb siddhānasiddhānvyāmiśrānyadvā kiṃciccarācaram  
AbhTa dṛṣṭaprokṣitasaṃdraṣṭṛprālabdhopāttayojitaḥ 
AbhTb nirvāpito vīrapaśuḥ soṣṭadhottaratottamaḥ  
AbhTa yathottaraṃ na dātavyamayogyebhyaḥ kadācana 
AbhTb śivopayuktaṃ hi havirna sarvo bhoktumarhati  
AbhTa yastu dīkṣāvihīnopi śivecchāvidhicoditaḥ 
AbhTb bhaktyāśnāti sa saṃpūrṇaḥ samayī syātsubhāvitaḥ  
AbhTa dṛṣṭovalokitaścaiva kiraṇeddhadṛgarpaṇāt 
AbhTb prokṣitaḥ kevalaṃ hyarghapātravipruḍbhirukṣitaḥ  
AbhTa saṃdraṣṭā darśitāśeṣasamyakpūjitamaṇḍalaḥ 
AbhTb prālabdha uktatritayasaṃskṛtaḥ sopi dhūnayet  
AbhTa kampeta prasravetstabdhaḥ pralīno vā yathottaram 
AbhTb upātto yāgasānnidhye śamitaḥ śastramārutaiḥ  
AbhTa yojitaḥ kāraṇatyāgakrameṇa śivayojanāt 
AbhTb nirvāpitaḥ kṛtābhyāsaguruprāṇamanorpaṇāt  
AbhTa dakṣiṇenāgninā saumyakalājālavilāpanāt 
AbhTb tathāhyādau paraṃ rūpamekībhāvena saṃśrayet  
AbhTa tasmādāgneyacāreṇa jvālāmālāmucāviśet 
AbhTb paśorvāmena candrāṃśujālaṃ tāpena gālayet  
AbhTa nābhicakretha viśrāmyetprāṇaraśmigaṇaiḥ saha 
AbhTb paro bhūtvā svaśaktyātra jīvaṃ jīvena veṣṭayet  
AbhTa svacitsūryeṇa saṃtāpya drāvayet kalāṃ kalām 
AbhTb tato drutaṃ kalājālaṃ prāpayyaikatvamātmani  
AbhTa samastatattvasaṃpūrṇamāpyāyanavidhāyinam 
AbhTb unmūlayeta saṃrambhātkarmabaddhamamuṃ rasāt  
AbhTa tata unmūlanodveṣṭayogādvāmaṃ paribhraman 
AbhTb kuṇḍalyamṛtasaṃpūrṇasvakaprāṇaprasevakaḥ  
AbhTa vāmāvartakramopāttahṛtpadmāmṛtakesaraḥ 
AbhTb hṛtkarṇikārūḍhilābhādojodhātuṃ vilāpitam  
AbhTa śuddhasomātmakaṃ sāramīṣallohitapītalam 
AbhTb ādāya karihastāgrasadṛśe prāṇavigrahe  
AbhTa niḥsṛtya jhaṭiti svātmavāmamārgeṇa saṃviśet 
AbhTb āpyāyayannapānākhyacandracakrahṛdambuje  
AbhTa sthitaṃ taddevatācakraṃ tena sāreṇa tarpayet 
AbhTb anena vidhinā sarvānrasaraktādikāṃstathā  
AbhTa dhātūnsamāharetsaṃghakramādekaikaśothavā 
AbhTb kevalaṃ tvathavāgnīnduravisaṃghaṭṭamadhyagam  
AbhTa jyotīrūpamatha prāṇaśaktyākhyaṃ jīvamāharet 
AbhTb jīvaṃ samarasīkuryāddevīcakreṇa bhāvanāt  
AbhTa tadeva tarpaṇaṃ mukhyaṃ bhogyabhoktrātmataiva sā 
AbhTb agnisaṃpuṭaphullārṇatryaśrakālātmako mahān  
AbhTa piṇḍo raktādisāraughacālanākarṣaṇādiṣu 
AbhTb itthaṃ viśrāntiyogena ghaṭikārdhakrame sati  
AbhTa āvṛttiśatayogena paśornirvāpaṇaṃ bhavet 
AbhTb kṛtvā katipayaṃ kālaṃ tatrābhyāsamananyadhīḥ  
AbhTa yathā cintāmaṇau proktaṃ tena rūpeṇa yogavit 
AbhTb niḥśaṅkaḥ siddhimāpnoti gopyaṃ tatprāṇavatsphuṭam  
AbhTa parokṣepi paśāvevaṃ vidhiḥ syādyojanaṃ prati 
AbhTb praveśito yāgabhuvi hatastatraiva sādhitaḥ  
AbhTa cakrajuṣṭaśca tatraiva sa vīrapaśurucyate 
AbhTb yastvanyatrāpi nihataḥ sāmastyenāṃśatopivā  
AbhTa devāya vinivedyeta sa vai bāhyapaśurmataḥ 
AbhTb rājyaṃ lābhotha tatsthairyaṃ śive bhaktistadātmatā  
AbhTa śivajñānaṃ mantralokaprāptistatparivāratā 
AbhTb tatsāyujyaṃ paśoḥ sāmyādbāhyādervīradharmaṇaḥ  
AbhTa puṣpādayopi tallābhabhāginaḥ śivapūjayā 
AbhTb ekopāyena deveśo viśvānugrahaṇātmakaḥ  
AbhTa yāgenaivānugṛhṇāti kiṃ kiṃ yanna carācaram 
AbhTb tenāvīropi śaṅkādiyuktaḥ kāruṇikopica  
AbhTa na hiṃsābuddhimādadhyātpaśukarmaṇi jātucit 
AbhTb paśormahopakāroyaṃ tadātvepyapriyaṃ bhavet  
AbhTa vyādhicchedauṣadhatapoyojanātra nidarśanam 
AbhTb śrīmanmṛtyuñjaye proktaṃ pāśacchede kṛte paśoḥ  
AbhTa malatrayaviyogena śarīraṃ na prarohati 
AbhTb dharmādharmaughavicchedāccharīraṃ cyacate kila  
AbhTa tenaitanmāraṇaṃ noktaṃ dīkṣeyaṃ citrarūpiṇī 
AbhTb rūḍhapāśasya yaḥ prāṇairviyogo māraṇaṃ hi tat  
AbhTa iyaṃ tu yojanaiva syātpaśordevāya tarpaṇe 
AbhTb tasmāddevoktimāśritya paśūndadyādbahūniti  
AbhTa niveditaḥ punaḥprāptadeho bhūyoniveditaḥ 
AbhTb ṣaṭkṛtva itthaṃ yaḥ sotra ṣaḍjanmā paśuruttamaḥ  
AbhTa yathā pākakramācchuddhaṃ hema tadvatsa kīrtitaḥ 
AbhTb kāṃ siddhiṃ naiva vitaretsvayaṃ kiṃvā na mucyate  
AbhTa uktaṃ tvānandaśāstre yo mantrasaṃskāravāṃstyajet 
AbhTb samayānkutsayeddevīrdadyānmantrānvinā nayāt  
AbhTa dīkṣāmantrādikaṃ prāpya tyajetputrādimohitaḥ 
AbhTb tato manuṣyatāmetya punarevaṃ karotyapi  
AbhTa itthamekādisaptāntajanmāsau dvividho dvipāt 
AbhTb catuṣpādvā paśurdevīcarukārthaṃ prajāyate  
AbhTa dātrarpitosau taddvārā yāti sāyujyataḥ śivam 
AbhTb iti saṃbhāvya citraṃ tatpaśūnāṃ praviceṣṭitam  
AbhTa bhogyīcikīrṣitaṃ naiva kuryādanyatra taṃ paśum 
AbhTb nāpi naiṣa bhavedyogya iti buddhvāpasārayet  
AbhTa taṃ paśuṃ kiṃtu kāṅkṣā cedviśeṣe taṃ tu ḍhaukayet 
AbhTb tāvatastānpaśūndadyāttathācoktaṃ maheśinā  
AbhTa paśorvapāmedasī ca gālite vahnimadhyataḥ 
AbhTb arpayecchakticakrāya paramaṃ tarpaṇaṃ matam  
AbhTa hṛdantramuṇḍāṃsayakṛtpradhānaṃ vinivedayet 
AbhTb karṇikākuṇḍalīmajjaparśu mukhyataraṃ ca vā  
AbhTa tatognau tarpaṇaṃ kuryānmantracakrasya daiśikaḥ 
AbhTb tannivedya ca devāya tato vijñāpayetprabhum  
AbhTa gurutvena tvayaivāhamājñātaḥ parameśvara 
AbhTb sākṣātsvapnopadeśādyairjapairgurumukhena vā  
AbhTa anugrāhyāstvayā śiṣyāḥ śivaśaktipracoditāḥ 
AbhTb tadete tadvidhāḥ prāptāstvamebhyaḥ kurvanugraham  
AbhTa samāveśaya māṃ svātmaraśmibhiryadahaṃ śivaḥ 
AbhTb evaṃ bhavatviti tataḥ śivoktimabhinandayet  
AbhTa śivābhinnamathātmānaṃ pañcakṛtyakaraṃ smaret 
AbhTb svātmanaḥ karaṇaṃ mantrānmūrtiṃ cānujighṛkṣayā  
AbhTa tato baddhvā sitoṣṇīṣaṃ hastayorarcayetkramāt 
AbhTb anyonyaṃ pāśadāhāya śuddhatattvavisṛṣṭaye  
AbhTa tejorūpeṇa mantrāṃśca śivahaste samarcayet 
AbhTb garbhāvaraṇagānaṅgaparivārāsanojjhitān  
AbhTa ātmānaṃ bhāvayetpaścādekakaṃ jalacandravat 
AbhTb kṛtyopādhivaśādbhinnaṃ ṣoḍhābhinnaṃ tu vastutaḥ  
AbhTa maṇḍalasthohamevāyaṃ sākṣī cākhilakarmaṇām 
AbhTb śuddhā hi draṣṭṛtā śambhormaṇḍale kalpitā mayā  
AbhTa homādhikaraṇatvena vahnāvahamavasthitaḥ 
AbhTb yadātmateddhā mantrāḥ syuḥ pāśaploṣavidhāvalam  
AbhTa sāmānyatejorūpāntarāhūtā bhuvaneśvarāḥ 
AbhTb tarpitāḥ śrāvitāścāṇornādhikāraṃ pratanvate  
AbhTa ā yāgāntamahaṃ kumbhe saṃsthito vighnaśāntaye 
AbhTb sāmānyarūpatā yena viśeṣāpyāyakāriṇī  
AbhTa śiṣyadehe ca tatpāśaśithilatvaprasiddhaye 
AbhTb sa hi svecchāvaśātpāśānvidhunvanniva vartate  
AbhTa sākṣātsvadehasaṃsthohaṃ kartānugrahakarmaṇām 
AbhTb jñānakriyāsvatantratvāddīkṣākarmaṇi peśalaḥ  
AbhTa bhinnakāryākṛtivrātendriyacakrānusandhimān 
AbhTb eko yathāhaṃ vahnyādiṣaḍrūposmi tathā sphuṭam  
AbhTa evamālocya yenaiṣodhvanā dīkṣāṃ cikīrṣati 
AbhTb anusaṃhitaye śiṣyavarjaṃ pañcasu taṃ yajet  
AbhTa anusandhibalānte ca samāsavyāsabhedataḥ 
AbhTb kuryādatyantamabhyastamanyāntarbhāvapūritam  
AbhTa tatopi cintayā bhūyonusandadhyācchivātmatām 
AbhTb ahameva paraṃ tattvaṃ naca paddhaṭavat kvacit  
AbhTa mahāprakāśastattena mayi sarvamidaṃ jagat 
AbhTb naca tatkenacidbāhyapratibimbavadarpitam  
AbhTa kartāhamasya tannānyādhīnaṃ ca madadhiṣṭhitam 
AbhTb itthaṃbhūtamahāvyāptisaṃvedanapavitritaḥ  
AbhTa matsamatvaṃ gato janturmukta ityabhidhīyate 
AbhTb tāpanirgharṣasekādipāramparyeṇa vahnitām  
AbhTa yathāyogolako yāti gururevaṃ śivātmatām 
AbhTb tataḥ puraḥsthitaṃ yadvā purobhāvitavigraham  
AbhTa parokṣadīkṣaṇe yadvā darbhādyaiḥ kalpite mṛte 
AbhTb śiṣye vīkṣyārcya puṣpādyairnyasedadhvānamasya tam  
AbhTa yenādhvanā mukhyatayā dīkṣāmicchati daiśikaḥ 
AbhTb taṃ dehe nyasya tatrāntarbhāvyamanyaditi sthitiḥ  
AbhTa śodhyādhvani ca vinyaste tatraiva pariśodhakam 
AbhTb nyasedyathepsitaṃ mantraṃ śodhyaucityānusārataḥ  
AbhTa kvacicchodhyaṃ tvavinyasya śodhakanyāsamātrataḥ 
AbhTb svayaṃ śuddhyati saṃśodhyaṃ śodhakasya prabhāvataḥ  
AbhTa aparaṃ parāparaṃ ca paraṃ ca vidhimicchayā 
AbhTb tadyojanānusāreṇa śritvā nyāsaḥ ṣaḍadhvanaḥ  
AbhTa lalāṭāntaṃ vedavasau randhrāntaṃ rasarandhrake 
AbhTb vasukhendau dvādaśāntamityeṣa trividho vidhiḥ  
AbhTa krameṇa kathyate dṛṣṭaḥ śāstre śrīpūrvasaṃjñite 
AbhTb tatra tattveṣu vinyāso gulphānte caturaṅgule  
AbhTa dharā jalādimūlāntaṃ pratyekaṃ dvyaṅgulaṃ kramāt 
AbhTb rasaśrutyaṅgulaṃ nābherūrdhvamitthaṃ ṣaḍaṅgule  
AbhTa puṃsaḥ kalāntaṃ ṣaṭtattvīṃ pratyekaṃ tryaṅgule kṣipet 
AbhTb aṣṭādaśāṅgulaṃ tvevaṃ kaṇṭhakūpāvasānakam  
AbhTa sadāśivāntaṃ māyādicatuṣkaṃ caturaṅgule 
AbhTb pratyekamityabdhivasusaṃkhyamālikadeśataḥ  
AbhTa śivatattvaṃ tataḥ paścāttejorūpamanākulam 
AbhTb sarveṣāṃ vyāpakatvena sabāhyābhyantaraṃ smaret  
AbhTa jalāddhyantaṃ sārdhayugmaṃ mūlaṃ tryaṅgulamityataḥ 
AbhTb dvādaśāṅgulatādhikyādvidhireṣa parāparaḥ  
AbhTa jalāddhyantaṃ tryaṅgule cedavyaktaṃ tu catuṣṭaye 
AbhTb taccaturviṃśatyādhikyātparopyaṣṭaśate vidhiḥ  
AbhTa trividhonmānakaṃ vyaktaṃ vasudigbhyo ravikṣayāt 
AbhTb mayatantre tathācoktaṃ tattatsvaphalavāñchayā  
AbhTa navapañcacatustryekatattvanyāse svayaṃ dhiyā 
AbhTb nyāsaṃ prakalpayettāvattattvāntarbhāvacintanāt  
AbhTa kalāpañcakavedāṇḍanyāsonenaiva lakṣitaḥ 
AbhTb uktaṃ ca triśirastantre svādhārasthaṃ yathāsthitam  
AbhTa dvādaśāṅgulamutthānaṃ dehātītaṃ samaṃ tataḥ 
AbhTb dvāsaptatirdaśa dve ca dehasthaṃ śirasontataḥ  
AbhTa pādādārabhya suśroṇi anāhatapadāvadhi 
AbhTb dehātītepi viśrāntyā saṃvitteḥ kalpanāvaśāt  
AbhTa dehatvamiti tasmātsyādutthānaṃ dvādaśāṅgulam 
AbhTb iti nirṇetumatraitaduktamaṣṭottaraṃ śatam  
AbhTa puranyāsotha gulphāntaṃ bhūḥ purāṇyatra ṣoḍaśa 
AbhTb tasmādekāṅgulavyāptyā pratyekaṃ lakulāditaḥ  
AbhTa dviraṇḍāntaṃ tryaṅgulaṃ tu cchagalāṇḍamathābdhiṣu 
AbhTb devayogāṣṭake dve hi pratyekāṅgulapādataḥ  
AbhTa iti pradhānaparyantaṃ ṣaṭcatvāriṃśadaṅgulam 
AbhTb ṣaṭpañcāśatpurāṇītthaṃ prāgdharāyāṃ tu ṣoḍaśa  
AbhTa tatopyardhāṅgulavyāptyā ṣaṭpurāṇyaṅgulatraye 
AbhTb catvāri yugma ekasminnekaṃ ca puramaṅgule  
AbhTa sarāge puṃspurāṇīśasaṃkhyānītthaṃ ṣaḍaṅgule 
AbhTb krodheśapuramekasmindvaye cāṇḍamiyaṃ ca vit  
AbhTa saṃvartajyotiṣorevaṃ kalātattvagayoḥ kramāt 
AbhTb śūrapañcāntapurayorniyatau caikayugmatā  
AbhTa śrīpūrvaśāstre taccoktaṃ parameśena śaṃbhunā 
AbhTb uttarādikramādadvyekabhedo vidyādike traye  
AbhTa asāratvātkramasyādau niyatiḥ parataḥ kalā 
AbhTb athavānyonyasaṃjñābhyāṃ tattvayorvyapadeśyatā  
AbhTa ekavīraśikheśaśrīkaṇṭhāḥ kāle trayastraye 
AbhTb kālasya pūrvaṃ vinyāso niyaterabhidhīyate  
AbhTa athavānyonyasaṃjñābhirvyapadeśo hi dṛśyate 
AbhTb evaṃ pumādiṣaṭtattvī vinyastāṣṭādaśāṅgule  
AbhTa tatopyaṅguṣṭhamātrāntaṃ māyātattvasthamaṣṭakam 
AbhTb pratyekamardhāṅgulataḥ syādaṅgulacatuṣṭaye  
AbhTa itthaṃ dvyakṣṇi purāṇyaṣṭāviṃśatiḥ puruṣānniśi 
AbhTb puratrayaṃ dvayostryaṃśanyūnāṅgulamiti kramāt  
AbhTa dvayordvayaṃ pañcapurī vaidyīye caturaṅgule 
AbhTb tata aiśapurāṇyaṣṭau catuṣkerdhāṅgulakramāt  
AbhTa tatastrīṇi dvaye dve ca dvayoritthaṃ catuṣṭaye 
AbhTb sādāśivaṃ pañcakaṃ syāditthaṃ vasvekakaṃ ravau  
AbhTa ṣoḍaśakaṃ rasaviśikhaṃ vasudvikaṃ vasuśaśīti puravargāḥ 
AbhTb vedā rasābdhi yugmākṣi ca ravayastatra cāṅgulāḥ kramaśaḥ  
AbhTa aṣṭādaśādhikaśataṃ purāṇi dehetra caturaśītimite 
AbhTb vinyastāni taditthaṃ śeṣe tu vyāpakaṃ śivaṃ tattvam  
AbhTa iti vidhiraparaḥ kathitaḥ parāparākhyo rasaśrutisthāne 
AbhTb aṣṭaśaraṃ saṃkhyānaṃ khamunikṛtaṃ tatpare vidhau jñeyam  
AbhTa lakulāderyogāṣṭakaparyantasyātra bhuvanapūgasya 
AbhTb adhikīkuryādgaṇanāvaśena bhāgaṃ vidhidvaye kramaśaḥ  
AbhTa aparādividhitraitādatha nyāsaḥ padādhvanaḥ 
AbhTb pūrvaṃ daśapadī coktā svatantrā nyasyate yadā  
AbhTa tayaiva dīkṣā kāryā cettadeyaṃ nyāsakalpanā 
AbhTb tattvādimukhyatāyogāddīkṣāyāṃ tu padāvalī  
AbhTa tattattvādyanusāreṇa tatrāntarbhāvyate tathā 
AbhTb svapradhānatvayoge tu dīkṣāyāṃ padapaddhatim  
AbhTa nyasyetkrameṇa tattvādivadanānavalokinīm 
AbhTb caturṣvaṣṭāsu cāṣṭāsu daśasvatha daśasvatha  
AbhTa daśasvatho pañcadaśasvatha vedaśarenduṣu 
AbhTb dharāpadānnavapadīṃ mātṛkāmālinīgatām  
AbhTa yojayedvyāptṛ daśamaṃ padaṃ tu śivasaṃjñitam
