AbhTb dharāpadaṃ varjayitvā pañca yāni padāni tu  
AbhTa vidhidvayaṃ syānnikṣipya dvādaśa dvādaśāṅgulān 
AbhTb mantrādhvanopyeṣa eva vidhirvinyāsayojane  
AbhTa vyāptimātraṃ hi bhidyetetyuktaṃ prāgeva tattathā 
AbhTb varṇādhvanotha vinyāsaḥ kathyatetra vidhitraye  
AbhTa ekaṃ caturṣu pratyekaṃ dvayoraṅgulayoḥ kramāt 
AbhTb trayoviṃśativarṇī syāt ṣaḍvarṇyekaikaśastriṣu  
AbhTa pratyekamatha catvāraścaturṣviti vilomataḥ 
AbhTb mālinīmātṛkārṇāḥ syurvyāptṛ śaivaṃ rasendutaḥ  
AbhTa varjayitvādyavarṇaṃ tu tattvavatsyādravīnnavīn 
AbhTb tāṃ trayoviṃśatau varṇeṣvapyanyatsyādvidhidvayam  
AbhTa śrīpūrvaśāstre tenādau tattveṣūktaṃ vidhitrayam 
AbhTb atidiṣṭaṃ tu tadbhinnābhinnavarṇadvaye samam  
AbhTa dvividhopi hi varṇānāṃ ṣaḍvidho bheda ucyate 
AbhTb tattvamārgavidhānena jñātavyaḥ paramārthataḥ  
AbhTa upadeśātideśābhyāṃ yaduktaṃ tatpadādiṣu 
AbhTb bhūyotidiṣṭaṃ tatraiva śāstresmaddhṛdayeśvare  
AbhTa padamantrakalādīnāṃ pūrvasūtrānusārataḥ 
AbhTb tritayatvaṃ prakurvīta tattvavarṇoktavartmanā  
AbhTa uktaṃ tatpadamantreṣu kalāsvatha nirūpyate 
AbhTb caturṣu rasavede dvāviṃśatau dvādaśasvatha  
AbhTa nivṛttyādyāścatasraḥ syurvyāptrī syācchāntyatītikā 
AbhTb dvitīyasyāṃ kalāyāṃ tu dvādaśa dvādaśāṅgulān  
AbhTa kramātkṣiptvā vidhidvaitaṃ parāparaparātmakam 
AbhTb caturaṇḍavidhistvādiśabdeneha pragṛhyate  
AbhTa kalācatuṣkavattena tasminvācyaṃ vidhitrayam 
AbhTb evaṃ ṣaḍvidhamadhvānaṃ śodhyaśiṣyatanau purā  
AbhTa nyasyaikatamamukhyatvānnyasyecchodhakasaṃmatam 
AbhTb adhvanyāsanamantraughaḥ śodhako hyeka āditaḥ  
AbhTa śabdarāśirmālinī ca samastavyastato dvidhā 
AbhTb ekavīratayā yadvā ṣaṭkaṃ yāmalayogataḥ  
AbhTa pañcavaktrī śaktitadvadbhedātṣoḍhā punardvidhā 
AbhTb ekākiyāmalatvenetyevaṃ sā dvādaśātmikā  
AbhTa ṣaḍaṅgī sakalānyatvāddvividhā vaktravatpunaḥ 
AbhTb dvādaśatvena guṇitā caturviṃśatibhedikā  
AbhTa aghorādyaṣṭake dve ca tṛtīyaṃ yāmalodayāt 
AbhTb mātṛsadbhāvamantraśca kevalaḥ śruticakragaḥ  
AbhTa ekadvitricaturbhedāttrayodaśabhidātmakaḥ 
AbhTb ekavīratayā soyaṃ caturdaśatayā sthitaḥ  
AbhTa anāmasaṃhṛtisthairyasṛṣṭicakraṃ caturvidham 
AbhTb devatābhirnijābhistanmātṛsadbhāvavṛṃhitam  
AbhTa itthaṃ śodhakavargoyaṃ mantrāṇāṃ saptatiḥ smṛtā 
AbhTb ṣaḍardhaśāstreṣu śrīmatsāraśāstre ca kathyate  
AbhTa aghorādyaṣṭakeneha śodhanīyaṃ vipaścitā 
AbhTb athavaikākṣarāmantrairathavā mātṛkākramāt  
AbhTa bhairavīyahṛdā vāpi khecarīhṛdayena vā 
AbhTb bhairaveṇa mahādevi tvatha vaktrāṅgapañcakaiḥ  
AbhTa yena yena hi mantreṇa tantresminnudbhavaḥ kṛtaḥ 
AbhTb tenaiva dīkṣayenmantrī ityājñā pārameśvarī  
AbhTa evaṃ śodhakabhedena saptatiḥ kīrtitā bhidaḥ 
AbhTb śodhyanyāsaṃ vinā mantrairetairdīkṣā yadā bhavet  
AbhTa tadā saptatidhā jñeyā jananādivivarjitā 
AbhTb śodhyabhedotha vaktavyaḥ saṃkṣepātsopi kathyate  
AbhTa ekatripañcaṣaṭtriṃśadbhedāttāttvaścaturvidhaḥ 
AbhTb pañcaikabhedāccādhvānastathaivāṇḍacatuṣṭayam  
AbhTa evaṃ daśavidhaṃ śodhyaṃ triṃśaddhā tadvidhitrayāt 
AbhTb śodhyaśodhakabhedena śatāni tvekaviṃśatiḥ  
AbhTa atrāpi nyāsayogena śodhyedhvani tathākṛteḥ 
AbhTb śataikaviṃśatibhidā jananādyujjhitā bhavet  
AbhTa jananādimayī tāvatyevaṃ śatadṛśi śrutiḥ 
AbhTb syātsaptatyadhikā sāpi dravyavijñānabhedataḥ  
AbhTa dvidheti pañcāśītiḥ syācchatānyadhikakhābdhikā 
AbhTb bhogamokṣānusandhānāddvividhā sā prakīrtitā  
AbhTa aśubhasyaiva saṃśuddhyā śubhasyāpyatha śodhanāt 
AbhTb dvidhā bhogaḥ śubhe śuddhiḥ kālatrayavibhedini  
AbhTa ekadvisāmastyavaśātsaptadhetyaṣṭadhā bhujiḥ 
AbhTb guruśiṣyakramātsopi dvidhetyevaṃ vibhidyate  
AbhTa pratyakṣadīkṣaṇe yasmāddvayorekānusandhitaḥ 
AbhTb tādṛgdīkṣāphalaṃ pūrṇaṃ visaṃvāde tu viplavaḥ  
AbhTa parokṣamṛtadīkṣādau gururevānusandhimān 
AbhTb kriyājñānamahimnā taṃ śiṣyaṃ dhāmnīpsite nayet  
AbhTa avibhinne kriyājñāne karmaśuddhau tathaiva te 
AbhTb anusandhiḥ punarbhinnaḥ karma yasmāttadātmakam  
AbhTa śrīmatsvacchandaśāstre ca vāsanābhedataḥ phalam 
AbhTb śiṣyāṇāṃ ca guroścoktamabhinnepi kriyādike  
AbhTa bhogasya śodhakācchodhyādanusandheśca tādṛśāt 
AbhTb vaicitryamasti bhedasya vaicitryaprāṇatā yataḥ  
AbhTa tathāhi vaktrairyasyādhvā śuddhastaireva yojitaḥ 
AbhTb bhoktumiṣṭe kvacittattve sa bhoktā tadbalānvitaḥ  
AbhTa śubhānāṃ karmaṇāṃ cātra sadbhāve bhogacitratā 
AbhTb tādṛgeva bhavetkarmaśuddhau tvanyaiva citratā  
AbhTa bhogaśca sadyautkrāntyā dehenaivātha saṃgataḥ 
AbhTb tadaivābhyāsato vāpi dehānte vetyasau catuḥ  
AbhTa prāktanāṣṭabhidā yogāddvātriṃśadbheda ucyate 
AbhTb mokṣa ekopi bījasya samayākhyasya tādṛśam  
AbhTa bālādikaṃ jñātaśīghramaraṇaṃ śaktivarjitam 
AbhTb vṛddhaṃ voddiśya śaktaṃ vā śodhanāśodhanāddvidhā  
AbhTa sadyautkrāntitastraidhaṃ sā cāsannamṛtau guroḥ 
AbhTb kāryetyājñā maheśasya śrīmadgahvarabhāṣitā  
AbhTa dṛṣṭvā śiṣyaṃ jarāgrastaṃ vyādhinā paripīḍitam 
AbhTb utkramayya tatastvenaṃ paratattve niyojayet  
AbhTa pañcatriṃśadamī bhedā gurorvā guruśiṣyayoḥ 
AbhTb uktadvaividhyakalanātsaptatiḥ parikīrtitāḥ  
AbhTa etairbhedaiḥ puroktāṃstānbhedāndīkṣāgatānguruḥ 
AbhTb hatvā vadetprasaṃkhyānaṃ svabhyastajñānasiddhaye  
AbhTa pañcāśītiśatī yā catvāriṃśatsamuttarā kathitā 
AbhTb tāṃ saptatyā bhittvā dīkṣābhedānsvayaṃ kalayet  
AbhTa pañcakamiha lakṣāṇāṃ ca saptanavatiḥ sahasraparisaṃkhyā 
AbhTb aṣṭau śatāni dīkṣābhedoyaṃ mālinītantre  
AbhTa saptatidhā śoddhṛgaṇastriṃśaddhā śodhya ekatattvādiḥ 
AbhTb sāṇḍaḥ ṣaḍadhvarūpastathetikartavyatā caturbhedā  
AbhTa dravyajñānamayī sā jananādivivarjitātha tadyuktā 
AbhTb pañcatriṃśaddhā punareṣā bhogāpavargasandhānāt  
AbhTa yasmāddvātriṃśaddhā bhogaḥ śubhaśuddhyaśuddhikālabhidā 
AbhTb mokṣastredhā dviguṇā saptatiritikāryatābhedāḥ  
AbhTa śodhanaśodhyavibhedāditikartavyatvabhedataścaiṣā 
AbhTb dīkṣā bahudhā bhinnā śodhyavihīnā tu saptatidhā  
AbhTa mantrāṇāṃ sakaletarasāṅganiraṅgādibhedasaṃkalanāt 
AbhTb śyodhyasya ca tattvādeḥ pañcadaśādyuktabhedaparigaṇanāt  
AbhTa bhedānāṃ parigaṇanā na śakyate kartumityasaṃkīrṇāḥ 
AbhTb bhedāḥ saṃkīrṇāḥ punaranye bhūyastvakāriṇo bahudhā  
AbhTa śodhakaśodhyādīnāṃ dvitrādivibhedasadbhāvāt 
AbhTb bhoge sādhye yadyadbahu kartavyaṃ tadāśrayenmatimān  
AbhTa kāraṇabhūyastvaṃ kila phalabhūyastvāya kiṃ citram 
AbhTb apavarge natu bhedastenāsminvāsanādṛḍhatvajuṣā  
AbhTa alpāpyāśrayaṇīyā kriyātha vijñānamātre vā 
AbhTb abhinavaguptaguruḥ punarāha hi sati vittadeśakālādau  
AbhTa apavargepi hi vistīrṇakarmavijñānasaṃgrahaḥ kāryaḥ 
AbhTb cidvṛttervaicitryāccāñcalyepi krameṇa sandhānāt  
AbhTa tasmiṃstasminvastuni rūḍhiravaśyaṃ śivātmikā bhavati 
AbhTb tattvamidametadātmakametasmātproddhṛto mayā śiṣyaḥ  
AbhTa itthaṃ kramasaṃvittau mūḍhopi śivātmako bhavati 
AbhTb kramikatathāvidhaśivatānugrahasubhagaṃ ca daiśikaṃ paśyan  
AbhTa śiśurapi tadabhedadṛśā bhaktibalāccābhyupaiti śivabhāvam 
AbhTb yadyapi vikalpavṛtterapi mokṣaṃ dīkṣayaiva dehānte  
AbhTa śāstre provāca vibhustathāpi dṛḍhavāsanā yuktā 
AbhTb mokṣepyasti viśeṣaḥ kriyālpabhūyastvajaḥ salokādiḥ  
AbhTa iti kecittadayuktaṃ sa vicitro bhoga eva kathitaḥ syāt 
AbhTb saṃskāraśeṣavartanajīvitamadhyesya samayalopādyam  
AbhTa nāyāti vighnajālaṃ kriyābahutvaṃ mumukṣostat 
AbhTb yasmāt sabījadīkṣāsaṃskṛtapuruṣasya samayalopādye  
AbhTa bhukte bhogānmokṣo naivaṃ nirbījadīkṣāyām 
AbhTb iti kecinmanyante yuktaṃ taccāpi yatsmṛtaṃ śāstre  
AbhTa samayollaṅghanāddevi kravyādatvaṃ śataṃ samāḥ  
AbhTa tasmāduruśiṣyamatau śivabhāvanirūḍhivitaraṇasamartham 
AbhTb kramikaṃ tattvoddharaṇādi karma mokṣepi yuktamativitatam  
AbhTa yastu sadā bhāvanayā svabhyastajñānavānguruḥ sa śiśoḥ 
AbhTb apavargāya yathecchaṃ yaṃ kaṃcidupāyamanutiṣṭhet  
AbhTa evaṃ śiṣyatanau śodhyaṃ nyasyādhvānaṃ yathepsitam 
AbhTb śodhakaṃ mantramupari nyasyettattvānusārataḥ  
AbhTa dvayormātṛkayostattvasthityā varṇakramaḥ purā 
AbhTb kathitastaṃ tathā nyasyettattattattvaviśuddhaye  
AbhTa varṇādhvā yadyapi proktaḥ śodhyaḥ pāśātmakastu saḥ 
AbhTb māyīyaḥ śodhakastvanyaḥ śivātmā paravāṅmayaḥ  
AbhTa uvāca sadyojyotiśca vṛttau svāyambhuvasya tat 
AbhTb bāḍhameko hi pāśātmā śabdonyaśca śivātmakaḥ  
AbhTa tasmāttasyaiva varṇasya yuktā śodhakaśodhyatā 
AbhTb śrīpūrvaśāstre cāpyuktaṃ te tairāliṅgitā iti  
AbhTa sadyojātādivaktrāṇi hṛdādyaṅgāni pañca ca 
AbhTb ṣaṭkṛtvo nyasya ṣaṭtriṃśannyāsaṃ kuryāddharāditaḥ  
AbhTa parāparāyā vailomyāddharāyāṃ syātpadatrayam 
AbhTb tato jalādahaṅkāre pañcāṣṭakasamāśrayāt  
AbhTa padāni pañca dhīmūlapuṃrāgākhye traye trayam 
AbhTb ekaṃ tvaśuddhavitkāladvaye caikaṃ niyāmake  
AbhTa kalāmāyādvaye caikaṃ padamuktamiha kramāt 
AbhTb vidyeśvarasadāśaktiśiveṣu padapañcakam  
AbhTa ekonaviṃśatiḥ seyaṃ padānāṃ syātparāparā 
AbhTb sārdhaṃ caikaṃ caikaṃ sārdhaṃ dve dve śaśī dṛgatha yugmam  
AbhTa trāṇi dṛgabdhiścandraḥ śrutiḥ śaśī pañca vidhumahaścandrāḥ 
AbhTb ekānnaviṃśatau syādakṣarasaṃkhyā padeṣviyaṃ devyāḥ  
AbhTa haldvayayutavasucitraguparisaṃkhyātasvavarṇāyāḥ 
AbhTb mūlāntaṃ sārdhavarṇaṃ syānmāyāntaṃ varṇamekakam  
AbhTa śaktyantamekamaparānyāse vidhirudīritaḥ 
AbhTb māyāntaṃ haltataḥ śaktiparyante svara ucyate  
AbhTa niṣkale śivatattve vai paro nyāsaḥ paroditaḥ 
AbhTb parāparāpadānyeva hyaghoryādyaṣṭakadvaye  
AbhTa mantrāstadanusāreṇa tattveṣvetaddvayaṃ kṣipet 
AbhTb piṇḍākṣarāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ varṇasaṃkhyā vibhedataḥ  
AbhTa avyaktāntaṃ svare nyasyā śeṣaṃ śeṣeṣu yojayet 
AbhTb bījāni sarvatattveṣu vyāptṛtvena prakalpayet  
AbhTa piṇḍānāṃ bījavannyāsamanye tu pratipedire 
AbhTb akṛte vātha śodhyasya nyāse vastubalāt sthiteḥ  
AbhTa śodhakanyāsamātreṇa sarvaṃ śodhyaṃ viśudhyati 
AbhTb śrīmanmṛtyuñjayādau ca kathitaṃ parameṣṭhinā  
AbhTa adhunā nyāsamātreṇa bhūtaśuddhiḥ prajāyate 
AbhTb dehaśuddhyarthamapyetattulyametena vastutaḥ  
AbhTa anyaprakaraṇoktaṃ yadyuktaṃ prakaraṇāntare 
AbhTb jñāpakatvena sākṣādvā tatkiṃ nānyatra gṛhyate  
AbhTa mālinīmātṛkāṅgasya nyāso yorcāvidhau purā 
AbhTb proktaḥ kevalasaṃśoddhṛmantranyāse sa eva tu  
AbhTa tripadī dvayordvayoḥ syātpratyekamathāṣṭasu śrutipadāni 
AbhTb dikcandracandrarasaraviśaraśaradṛgdṛṅmṛgāṅkaśaśigaṇane  
AbhTa aṅgulamāne devyā aṣṭādaśa vaibhavena padamanyat 
AbhTb aparaṃ mānamidaṃ syāt kevalaśodhakamanunyāse  
AbhTa turyapadātpadaṣaṭke mānadvitayaṃ parāparaparākhyam 
AbhTb dvādaśakaṃ dvādaśakaṃ tattvopari pūrvavattvanyat  
AbhTa kevalaśodhakamantranyāsābhiprāyato mahādevaḥ 
AbhTb tattvakramoditamapi nyāsaṃ punarāha tadviruddhamapi  
AbhTa niṣkale padamekārṇaṃ yāvattrīṇi tu pārthive 
AbhTb ityādinā tattvagatakramanyāsa udīritaḥ  
AbhTa punaśca mālinītantre vargavidyāvibhedataḥ 
AbhTb dvidhā padānītyuktvākhyannyāsamanyādṛśaṃ vibhuḥ  
AbhTa ekaikaṃ dvyaṅgulaṃ jñeyaṃ tatra pūrvaṃ padatrayam 
AbhTb aṣṭāṅgulāni catvāri daśāṅgulamataḥ param  
AbhTa dvyaṅgule dve pade cānye ṣaḍaṅgulamataḥ param 
AbhTb dvādaśāṅgulamanyacca dvenye pañcāṅgule pṛthak  
AbhTa padadvayaṃ catuṣparva tathānye dve dviparvaṇī 
AbhTb evaṃ parāparādevyāḥ svatantro nyāsa ucyate  
AbhTa vidyādvayaṃ śiṣyatanau vyāptṛtvenaiva yojayet 
AbhTb iti darśayituṃ nāsya pṛthaṅnyāsaṃ nyarūpayat  
AbhTa evaṃ śodhakamantrasya nyāse tadraśmiyogataḥ 
AbhTb pāśajālaṃ vilīyeta taddhyānabalato guroḥ  
AbhTa śodhyatattve samastānāṃ yonīnāṃ tulyakālataḥ 
AbhTb jananādbhogataḥ karmakṣaye syādapavṛktatā  
AbhTa dehaistāvadbhirasyāṇościtraṃ bhokturapi sphuṭam 
AbhTb manonusandhirno viśvasaṃyogapravibhāgavat  
AbhTa niyatyā manaso dehamātre vṛttistataḥ param 
AbhTb nānusandhā yataḥ saikasvāntayuktākṣakalpitā  
AbhTa pradeśavṛtti ca jñānamātmanastatra tatra tat 
AbhTb bhogyajñānaṃ nānyadeheṣvanusandhānamarhati  
AbhTa yadā tu manasastasya dehavṛtterapi dhruvam 
AbhTb yogamantrakriyādeḥ syādvaimalyaṃ tadvidā tadā  
AbhTa yathāmalaṃ mano dūrasthitamapyāśu paśyati 
AbhTb tathā pratyayadīkṣāyāṃ tattadbhuvanadarśanam  
AbhTa jananādiviyuktāṃ tu yadā dīkṣāṃ cikīrṣati 
AbhTb tadāsmāduddharāmīti yuktamūhaprakalpanam  
AbhTa yadā śodhyaṃ vinā śoddhṛnyāsastatrāpi mantrataḥ 
AbhTb jananādikramaṃ kuryāttattvasaṃśleṣavarjitam  
AbhTa ekākiśoddhṛnyāse ca jananādivivarjane 
AbhTb tacchoddhṛsaṃpuṭaṃ nāma kevalaṃ parikalpayet  
AbhTa dravyayogena dīkṣāyāṃ tilājyākṣatataṇḍulam 
AbhTb tattanmantreṇa juhuyājjanmayogaviyogayoḥ  
AbhTa yadā vijñānadīkṣāṃ tu kuryācchiṣyaṃ tadā bhṛśam 
AbhTb tanmantrasaṃjalpabalāt paśyedā cāvikalpakāt  
AbhTa vikalpaḥ kila saṃjalpamayo yatsa vimarśakaḥ 
AbhTb mantrātmāsau vimarśaśca śuddhopāśavatātmakaḥ  
AbhTa nityaścānādivaradaśivābhedopakalpitaḥ 
AbhTb tadyogāddaiśikasyāpi vikalpaḥ śivatāṃ vrajet  
AbhTa śrīsāraśāstre tadidaṃ parameśena bhāṣitam 
AbhTb arthasya pratipattiryā grāhyagrāhakarūpiṇī  
AbhTa sā eva mantraśaktistu vitatā mantrasantatau 
AbhTb parāmarśasvabhāvetthaṃ mantraśaktirudāhṛtā  
AbhTa parāmarśo dvidhā śuddhāśuddhatvānmantrabhedakaḥ 
AbhTb uktaṃ śrīpauṣkarenye ca brahmaviṣṇvādayoṇḍagāḥ  
AbhTa prādhānikāḥ sāñjanāste sāttvarājasatāmasāḥ 
AbhTb tairaśuddhaparāmarśāttanmayībhāvito guruḥ  
AbhTa vaiṣṇavādiḥ paśuḥ prokto na yogyaḥ patiśāsane 
AbhTb ye mantrāḥ śuddhamārgasthāḥ śivabhaṭṭārakādayaḥ  
AbhTa śrīmanmataṅgādidṛśā tanmayo hi guruḥ śivaḥ 
AbhTb nanu svatantrasaṃjalpayogādastu vimarśitā  
AbhTa prākkutaḥ sa vimarśāccetkutaḥ sopi nirūpaṇe 
AbhTb ādyastathāvikalpatvapradaḥ syādupadeṣṭṛtaḥ  
AbhTa yaḥ saṃkrāntobhijalpaḥ syāttasyāpyanyopadeṣṭṛtaḥ 
AbhTb pūrvapūrvakramāditthaṃ ya evādiguroḥ purā  
AbhTa saṃjalpo hyabhisaṃkrāntaḥ sodyāpyastīti gṛhyatām 
AbhTb yastathāvidhasaṃjalpabalātkopi svatantrakaḥ  
AbhTa vimarśaḥ kalpyate sopi tadātmaiva suniścitaḥ 
AbhTb ghaṭakumbha itītthaṃ vā yadi bhedo nirūpyate  
AbhTa sopyanyakalpanādāyī hyanādṛtyaḥ prayatnataḥ 
AbhTb paṇāyate karotīti vikalpasyocitau sphuṭam  
AbhTa karapāṇyabhijalpau tau saṃkīryetāṃ kathaṃ kila 
AbhTb śabdācchabdāntare tena vyutpattirvyavadhānataḥ  
AbhTa vyavahārāttu sā sākṣāccitropākhyāvimarśinī 
AbhTb tadvimarśodayaḥ prācyasvavimarśamayaḥ sphuret  
AbhTa yāvadbālasya saṃvittirakṛtrimavimarśane 
AbhTb tena tanmantraśabdārthaviśeṣotthaṃ vikalpanam  
AbhTa śabdāntarotthādbhedena paśyatā mantra ādṛtaḥ 
AbhTb yaccāpi bījapiṇḍāderuktaṃ prāgbodharūpakam  
AbhTa tattasyaiva kutonyasya tatkasmādanyakalpanā 
AbhTb etadarthaṃ guroryatnāllakṣaṇe tatra tatra tat  
AbhTa lakṣaṇaṃ kathitaṃ hyeṣa mantratantraviśāradaḥ 
AbhTb tena mantrārthasaṃbodhe mantravārtikamādarāt  
AbhTa ūhāpohaprayogaṃ vā sarvathā gururācaret 
AbhTb mantrārthavidabhāve tu sarvathā mantratanmayam  
AbhTa guruṃ kuryāt tadabhyāsāttatsaṃkalpamayo hyasau 
AbhTb tatsamānābhisaṃjalpo yadā mantrārthabhāvanāt  
AbhTa gurorbhavettadā sarvasāmye ko bheda ucyatām 
AbhTb aṃśenāpyatha vaiṣamye na tatorthakriyā hi sā  
AbhTa gomayātkīṭataḥ kīṭa ityevaṃ nyāyato yadā 
AbhTb saṃjalpāntaratopyarthakriyāṃ tāmeva paśyati  
AbhTa tadaiṣa satyasaṃjalpaḥ śiva eveti kathyate 
AbhTb sa yadvakti tadeva syānmantro bhogāpavargadaḥ  
AbhTa naiṣobhinavaguptasya pakṣo mantrārpitātmanaḥ 
AbhTb yorthakriyāmāha bhinnāṃ kīṭayorapi tādṛśoḥ  
AbhTa mantrārpitamanāḥ kiṃcidvadanyattu viṣaṃ haret 
AbhTb tanmantra eva śabdaḥ sa paraṃ tatra ghaṭādivat  
AbhTa kāntāsaṃbhogasaṃjalpasundaraḥ kāmukaḥ sadā 
AbhTb tatsaṃskṛtopyanyadeṣa kurvansvātmani tṛpyati  
AbhTa tathā tanmantrasaṃjalpabhāvitonyadapi bruvan 
AbhTb anicchurapi tadrūpastathā kāryakaro dhruvam  
AbhTa vikalpayannapyekārthaṃ yatonyadapi paśyati 
AbhTb viṣāpahārimantrādītyuktaṃ śrīpūrvaśāsane  
AbhTa yadi vā viṣanāśepi hetubhedādvicitratā 
AbhTb dhātvāpyāyādikānantakāryabhedādbhaviṣyati  
AbhTa tadevaṃ mantrasaṃjalpavikalpābhyāsayogataḥ 
AbhTb bhāvyavastusphuṭībhāvaḥ saṃjalpahrāsayogataḥ  
AbhTa vastveva bhāvayatyeṣa na saṃjalpamimaṃ punaḥ 
AbhTb gṛhṇāti bhāsanopāyaṃ bhāte tatra tu tena kim  
AbhTa evaṃ saṃjalpanirhrāse suparisphuṭatātmakam 
AbhTb akṛttrimavimarśātma sphuredvastvavikalpakam  
AbhTa nirvikalpā ca sā saṃvidyadyathā paśyati sphuṭam 
AbhTb tattathaiva tathātmatvādvastunopi bahiḥsthiteḥ  
AbhTa viśeṣatastvamāyīyaśivatābhedaśālinaḥ 
AbhTb mokṣebhyupāyaḥ saṃjalpo bandhamokṣau tataḥ kila  
AbhTa vikalpepi guroḥ samyagabhinnaśivatājuṣaḥ 
AbhTb avikalpakaparyantapratīkṣā nopayujyate  
AbhTa tadvimarśasvabhāvā hi sā vācyā mantradevatā 
AbhTb mahāsaṃvitsamāsannetyuktaṃ śrīgamaśāsane  
AbhTa nikaṭasthā yathā rājñāmanyeṣāṃ sādhayantyalam 
AbhTb siddhiṃ rājopagāṃ śīghramevaṃ mantrādayaḥ parām  
AbhTa uktābhiprāyagarbhaṃ taduktaṃ śrīmālinīmate 
AbhTb mantrāṇāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ kasmādityukte munibhiḥ kila  
AbhTa yogamekatvamicchanti vastunonyena vastunā 
AbhTb tadvastu jñeyamityuktaṃ heyatvādiprasiddhaye  
AbhTa tatprasiddhyai śivenoktaṃ jñānaṃ yadupavarṇitam 
AbhTb sabījayogasaṃsiddhyai mantralakṣaṇamapyalam  
AbhTa na cādhikāritā dīkṣāṃ vinā yogesti śāṅkare 
AbhTb kriyājñānavibhedena sā ca dvedhā nigadyate  
AbhTa dvividhā sā prakartavyā tena caitadudāhṛtam 
AbhTb naca yogādhikāritvamekamevānayā bhavet  
AbhTa api mantrādhikāritvaṃ muktiśca śivadīkṣayā 
AbhTb anenaitadapi proktaṃ yogī tattvaikyasiddhaye  
AbhTa mantramevāśrayenmūlaṃ nirvikalpāntamādṛtaḥ 
AbhTb mantrābhyāsena bhogaṃ vā mokṣaṃ vāpi prasādhayan  
AbhTa tatrādhikāritālabdhyai dīkṣāṃ gṛhṇīta daiśikāt 
AbhTb tena mantrajñānayogabalādyadyatprasādhayet  
AbhTa tatsyādasyānyatattvepi yuktasya guruṇā śiśoḥ 
AbhTb dīkṣā hyasyopayujyeta saṃskriyāyāṃ sa saṃskṛtaḥ  
AbhTa svabalenaiva bhogaṃ vā mokṣaṃ vā labhate budhaḥ 
AbhTb tena vijñānayogādibalī prāk samayī bhavan  
AbhTa putrako vā na tāvānsyādapitu svabalocitaḥ 
AbhTb yastu vijñānayogādivandhyaḥ sondho yathā pathi  
AbhTa daiśikāyatta eva syādbhoge muktau ca sarvathā 
AbhTb dīkṣā ca kevalā jñānaṃ vināpi nijamāntaram  
AbhTa mocikaiveti kathitaṃ yuktyā cāgamataḥ purā 
AbhTb yastu dīkṣākṛtāmevāpekṣya yojanikāṃ śiśuḥ  
AbhTa sphuṭībhūtyai taducitaṃ jñānaṃ yogamathāśritaḥ 
AbhTb sopi yatraiva yuktaḥ syāttanmayatvaṃ prapadyate  
AbhTa gurudīkṣāmantraśāstrādhīnasarvasthitistataḥ 
AbhTb duṣṭānāmeva sarveṣāṃ bhūtabhavyabhaviṣyatām  
AbhTa karmaṇāṃ śodhanaṃ kāryaṃ bubhukṣorna śubhātmanām 
AbhTb yaḥ punarlaukikaṃ bhogaṃ rājyasvargādikaṃ śiśuḥ  
AbhTa tyaktvā lokottaraṃ bhogamīpsustasya śubheṣvapi 
AbhTb tatra dravyamayīṃ dīkṣāṃ kurvannājyatilādikaiḥ  
AbhTa karmāsya śodhayāmīti juhuyāddaiśikottamaḥ 
AbhTb jñānamayyāṃ tu dīkṣāyāṃ tadviśuddhyati sandhitaḥ  
AbhTa guroḥ svasaṃvidrūḍhasya balāttatprakṣayo bhavet 
AbhTb yadāsyāśubhakarmāṇi śuddhāni syustadā śubham  
AbhTa svatāratamyāśrayaṇādadhvamadhye prasūtidam 
AbhTb śubhapākakramopāttaphalabhogasamāptitaḥ  
AbhTa yatraiṣa yojitastatstho bhāvikarmakṣaye kṛte 
AbhTb bhāvināṃ cādyadehasthadehāntaravibhedinām  
AbhTa aśubhāṃśaviśuddhau syādbhogasyaivānupakṣayaḥ 
AbhTb bhuñjānasyāsya satataṃ bhogānmāyālayāntataḥ  
AbhTa na duḥkhaphaladaṃ dehādyadhvamadhyepi kiṃcana 
AbhTb tato māyālaye bhuktasamastasukhabhogakaḥ  
AbhTa niṣkale sakale vaiti layaṃ yojanikābalāt 
AbhTb iti prameyaṃ kathitaṃ dīkṣā kāle guroryathā  
C atha śrītantrāloke saptadaśamāhnikam
AbhTa atha bhairavatādātmyadāyinīṃ prakriyāṃ bruve 
AbhTb evaṃ maṇḍalakumbhāgniśiṣyasvātmasu pañcasu  
AbhTa gṛhītvā vyāptimaikyena nyasyādhvānaṃ ca śiṣyagam 
AbhTb karmamāyāṇumalinatrayaṃ bāhau gale tathā  
AbhTa śikhāyāṃ ca kṣipetsūtragranthiyogena daiśikaḥ 
AbhTb tasyātadrūpatābhānaṃ malo granthiḥ sa kīrtyate  
AbhTa itipratītidārḍhyārthaṃ bahirgranthyupakalpanam 
AbhTb bāhū karmāspadaṃ viṣṇurmāyātmā galasaṃśritaḥ  
AbhTa adhovahā śikhāṇutvaṃ tenetthaṃ kalpanā kṛtā 
AbhTb naraśaktiśivākhyasya trayasya bahubhedatām  
AbhTa vaktuṃ tristriguṇaṃ sūtraṃ granthaye parikalpayet 
AbhTb tejojalānnatritayaṃ tredhā pratyekamapyadaḥ  
AbhTa śrutyante kepyataḥ śuklakṛṣṇaraktaṃ prapedire 
AbhTb tatognau tarpitāśeṣamantre cidvyomamātrake  
AbhTa sāmānyarūpe tattvānāṃ kramācchuddhiṃ samācaret 
AbhTb tatra svamantrayogena dharāmāvāhayetpurā  
AbhTa iṣṭvā puṣpādibhiḥ sarpistilādyairatha tarpayet 
AbhTb tattattvavyāpikāṃ paścānmāyātattvādhidevatām  
AbhTa māyāśaktiṃ svamantreṇāvāhyābhyarcya pratarpayet 
AbhTb āvāhane mātṛkārṇaṃ mālinyarṇaṃ ca pūjane  
AbhTa kuryāditi guruḥ prāha svarūpāpyāyanadvayāt 
AbhTb tāro varṇotha saṃbuddhipadaṃ tvāmityataḥ param  
AbhTa uttamaikayutaṃ karmapadaṃ dīpakamapyataḥ 
AbhTb tabhyaṃ nāma caturthyantaṃ tatopyucitadīpakam  
AbhTa ityūhamantrayogena tattatkarma pravartayet 
AbhTb āvāhanānantaraṃ hi karma sarvaṃ nigadyate  
AbhTa āvāhanaṃ ca saṃbodhaḥ svasvabhāvavyavasthiteḥ 
AbhTb bhāvasyāhaṃmayasvātmatādātmyāveśyamānatā  
AbhTa śāktī bhūmiśca saivoktā yasyāṃ mukhyāsti pūjyatā 
AbhTb abhātatvādabhedācca nahyasau nṛśivātmanoḥ  
AbhTa jaḍābhāseṣu tattveṣu saṃvitsthityai tato guruḥ 
AbhTb āvāhanavibhaktiṃ prāk kṛtvā turyavibhaktitaḥ  
AbhTa namaskārāntatāyogātpūrṇāṃ sattāṃ prakalpayet 
AbhTb tataḥ pūrṇasvabhāvatvaṃ tadrūpodrekayogataḥ  
AbhTa dhyeyodreko bhaveddhyātṛprahvībhāvavaśādyataḥ 
AbhTb āvāhyeṣṭvā pratarpyeti śrīsvacchande nirūpitam  
AbhTa anenaiva pathāneyamityasmadguravo jaguḥ 
AbhTb paratvena tu yatpūjyaṃ tatsvatantracidātmakam  
AbhTa anavacchitprakāśatvānna prakāśyaṃ tu kutracit 
AbhTb tasya hyetatprapūjyatvadhyeyatvādi yadullaset  
AbhTa tasyaiva tatsvatantratvaṃ yātidurghaṭakāritā 
AbhTb saṃbodharūpe tattasmin kathaṃ saṃbodhanā bhavet  
AbhTa prakāśanāyāṃ na syātprakāśasya prakāśatā 
AbhTb saṃbodhanavibhaktyaiva vinā karmādiśaktitām  
AbhTa svātantryāttaṃ darśayituṃ tatrohamimamācaret 
AbhTb devamāvāhayāmīti tato devāya dīpakam  
AbhTa prāgyuktyā pūrṇatādāyi namaḥsvāhādikaṃ bhavet 
AbhTb nutiḥ pūrṇatvamagnīndusaṃghaṭṭāpyāyatā param  
AbhTa āpyāyakaṃ ca procchālaṃ vauṣaḍādi pradīpayet 
AbhTb tatra bāhyepi tādātmyaprasiddhaṃ karma codyate  
AbhTa yadi karmapadaṃ tanno gururabhyūhayetkvacit 
AbhTb anābhāsitatadvastubhāsanāya niyujyate  
AbhTa mantraḥ kiṃ tena tatra syātsphuṭaṃ yatrāvabhāsi tat 
AbhTb tena prokṣaṇasaṃsekajapādividhiṣu dhruvam  
AbhTa tatkarmābhyūhanaṃ kuryātpratyuta vyavadhātṛtām 
AbhTb bahistathātmatābhāve kāryaṃ karmapadohanam  
AbhTa tṛptāvāhutihutabhukpāśaploṣacchidādiṣu 
AbhTb yatroddiṣṭe vidhau paścāttadanantaiḥ kriyātmakaiḥ  
AbhTa aṃśaiḥ sādhyaṃ na tatroho dīkṣaṇādividhiṣviva 
AbhTb tataḥ śiṣyasya tattattvasthānestreṇa pratāḍanam  
AbhTa kṛtvātha śivahastena hṛdayaṃ parimarśayet 
AbhTb tataḥ svanāḍīmārgeṇa hṛdayaṃ prāpya vai śiśoḥ  
AbhTa śiṣyātmanā sahaikatvaṃ gatvādāya ca taṃ hṛdā 
AbhTb puṭitaṃ haṃsarūpākhyaṃ tatra saṃhāramudrayā  
AbhTa kuryādātmīyahṛdayasthitamapyavabhāsakam 
AbhTb śiṣyadehasya tejobhī raśmimātrāviyogataḥ  
AbhTa svabandhasthānacalanāt svatantrasthānalābhataḥ 
AbhTb svakarmāparatantratvātsarvatrotpattimarhati  
AbhTa tenātmahṛdayānītaṃ prākkṛtvā pudgalaṃ tataḥ 
AbhTb māyāyāṃ taddharātattvaśarīrāṇyasya saṃsṛjet  
AbhTa tatrāsya garbhādhānaṃ ca yuktaṃ puṃsavanādibhiḥ 
AbhTb garbhaniṣkrāmaparyantairekāṃ kurvīta saṃskriyām  
AbhTa jananaṃ bhogabhoktṛtvaṃ militvaikātha saṃskriyā 
AbhTb tatosya teṣu bhogeṣu kuryāttanmayatāṃ layam  
AbhTa tatastattattvapāśānāṃ vicchedaṃ samupācaret 
AbhTb saṃskārāṇāṃ catuṣkesminnaparāṃ ca parāparām  
AbhTa mantrāṇāṃ pañcadaśakaṃ parāṃ vā yojayetkramāt 
AbhTb pivanyādyaṣṭakaṃ śastrādikaṃ ṣaṭkaṃ parā tathā  
AbhTa iti pañcadaśaite syuḥ kramāllīnatvasaṃskṛtau 
AbhTb aparāmantramuktvā prāgamukātmana ityatha  
AbhTa garbhādhānaṃ karomīti punarmantraṃ tameva ca 
AbhTb svāhāntamuccarandadyādāhutitritayaṃ guruḥ  
AbhTa paraṃ parāparāmantramamukātmana ityatha 
AbhTb jātasya bhogabhoktṛtvaṃ karomyatha parāparām  
AbhTa ante svāheti proccārya vitarettisra āhutīḥ 
AbhTb uccārya pivanīmantramamukātmana ityatha  
AbhTa bhoge layaṃ karomīti punarmantraṃ tameva ca 
AbhTb svāhāntamāhutīstisro dadyādājyatilādibhiḥ  
AbhTa eṣa eva vamanyādau vidhiḥ pañcadaśāntake 
AbhTb pūrvaṃ parātmakaṃ mantramamukātmana ityatha  
AbhTa pāśācchedaṃ karomīti parāmantraḥ punastataḥ 
AbhTb huṃ svāhā phaṭ samuccārya dadyāttisropyathāhutīḥ  
AbhTa saṃskārāṇāṃ catuṣkesminye mantrāḥ kathitā mayā 
AbhTb teṣu karmapadātpūrvaṃ dharātattvapadaṃ vadet  
AbhTa tato dharātattvapatimāmantryeṣṭvā pratarpya ca 
AbhTb śivābhimānasaṃrabdho gururevaṃ samādiśet  
AbhTa tattveśvara tvayā nāsya putrakasya śivājñayā 
AbhTb pratibandhaḥ prakartavyo yātuḥ padamanāmayam  
AbhTa tato yadi samīheta dharātattvāntarālagam 
AbhTb pṛthak śodhayituṃ mantrī bhuvanādyadhvapañcakam  
AbhTa aparāmantrataḥ prāgvattisrastisrastadāhutīḥ 
AbhTb dadyātpuraṃ śodhayāmītyūhayuktaṃ prasannadhīḥ  
AbhTa evaṃ kalāmantrapadavarṇeṣvapi vicakṣaṇaḥ 
AbhTb tisrastisro hutīrdadyāt pṛthak sāmastyatopivā  
AbhTa tataḥ pūrṇāhutiṃ dattvā parayā vauṣaḍantayā 
AbhTb aparāmantrataḥ śiṣyamuddhṛtyātmahṛdaṃ nayet  
AbhTa yadā tvekena śuddhena tadantarbhāvacintanāt 
AbhTb na pṛthak śodhayettattvanāthasaṃśravaṇātparam  
AbhTa tadā pūrṇāṃ vitīryāṇumutkṣipyātmani yojayet 
AbhTb tātsthyātmasaṃsthyayogāya tayaivāparayāhutīḥ  
AbhTa sakarmapadayā dadyāditi kecittu manvate 
AbhTb anye tu guravaḥ prāhurbhāvanāmayamīdṛśam  
AbhTa nātra bāhyāhutirdeyā daiśikasya pṛthak punaḥ 
AbhTb dadyādvā yadi no doṣaḥ syādupāyaḥ sa bhāvane  
AbhTa evaṃ prāktanatātsthyātmasaṃsthatve yojayedguruḥ 
AbhTb tataḥ śiṣyahṛdaṃ neyaḥ sa ātmā tāvatodhvanaḥ  
AbhTa śuddhastaddārḍhyasiddhyai ca pūrṇā syātparayā punaḥ 
AbhTb mahāpāśupataṃ pūrvaṃ vilomasya viśuddhaye  
AbhTa juhomi punarastreṇa vauṣaḍanta iti kṣipet 
AbhTb punaḥ pūrṇāṃ tato māyāmabhyarcyātha visarjayet  
AbhTa dharātattvaṃ viśuddhaṃ sajjalena śuddharūpiṇā 
AbhTb bhāvayenmiśritaṃ vāri śuddhiyogyaṃ tato bhavet  
AbhTa tathā tattatpurātattvamiśraṇāduttarottaram 
AbhTb sarvā śivībhavettattvāvalī śuddhānyathā pṛthak  
AbhTa pṛthaktvaṃ ca malo māyābhidhānastasya saṃbhave 
AbhTb karmakṣayepi no muktirbhavedvidyeśvarādivat  
AbhTa tatopi jalatattvasya vahnau vyomni cidātmake 
AbhTb āhvānādyakhilaṃ yāvattejasyasya vimaśraṇam  
AbhTa evaṃ kramātkalātattve śuddhe pāśaṃ bhujāśritam 
AbhTb chindyātkalā hi sā kiṃcitkartṛtvonmīlanātmikā  
AbhTa karmākhyamalajṛmbhātmā taṃ ca granthiṃ srugagragam 
AbhTb pūrṇāhutyā samaṃ vahnimantratejasi nirdahet  
AbhTa mantro hi viśvarūpaḥ sannupāśrayavaśāttathā 
AbhTb vyaktarūpastato vahnau pāśaploṣavidhāyakaḥ  
AbhTa pluṣṭo līnasvabhāvosau pāśastaṃ prati śambhuvat 
AbhTb parameśamahātejaḥśeṣamātratvamaśnute  
AbhTa karmapāśetra hotavye pūrṇayāsya śubhāśubham 
AbhTb aśubhaṃ vā bhavadbhūtaṃ bhāvi vātha samastakam  
AbhTa dahāmi phaṭtrayaṃ vauṣaḍiti pūrṇāṃ vinikṣipet 
AbhTb evaṃ māyāntasaṃśuddhau kaṇṭhapāśaṃ ca homayet  
AbhTa pūrṇasya tasya māyākhyaṃ pāśabhedaprathātmakam 
AbhTb dahāmi phaṭtrayaṃ vauṣaḍiti pūrṇāṃ kṣipedguruḥ  
AbhTa nirbījā yadi kāryā tu tadātraivāparāṃ kṣipet 
AbhTb pūrṇāṃ samayapāśākhyabījadāhapadānvitām  
AbhTa gurau deve tathā śāstre bhaktiḥ kāryāsya nahyasau 
AbhTb samayaḥ śaktipātasya svabhāvo hyeṣa no pṛthak  
AbhTa māyānte śuddhimāyāte vāgīśī yā purābhavat 
AbhTb māyā śaktimayī saiva vidyāśaktitvamaśnute  
AbhTa tacchuddhavidyāmāhūya vidyāśaktiṃ niyojayet 
AbhTb evaṃ krameṇa saṃśuddhe sadāśivapadepyalam  
AbhTa śikhāṃ granthiyutāṃ chittvā malamāṇavakaṃ dahet 
AbhTb yatodhikārabhogākhyau dvau pāśau tu sadāśive  
AbhTa ityuktyāṇavapāśotra māyīyastu niśāvadhiḥ 
AbhTb śiṣyo yathocitaṃ snāyādācāmeddaiśikaḥ svayam  
AbhTa āṇavākhye vinirdagdhe hyadhovāhiśikhāmale 
AbhTb tataḥ prāguktasakalaprameyaṃ paricintayan  
AbhTa śiṣyadehādimātmīyadehaprāṇādiyojitam 
AbhTb kṛtvātmadehaprāṇāderviśvamantaranusmaret  
AbhTa uktaprakriyayā caivaṃ dṛḍhabuddhirananyadhīḥ 
AbhTb prāṇasthaṃ deśakālādhvayugaṃ prāṇaṃ ca śaktigam  
AbhTa tāṃ ca saṃvidgatāṃ śuddhāṃ saṃvidaṃ śivarūpiṇīm 
AbhTb śiṣyasaṃvidabhinnāṃ ca mantravahnyādyabhedinīm  
AbhTa dhyāyan prāgvatprayogeṇa śivaṃ sakalaniṣkalam 
AbhTb dvyātmakaṃ vā kṣipetpūrṇāṃ praśāntakaraṇena tu  
AbhTa uktaṃ traiśirase tantre sarvasaṃpūraṇātmakam 
AbhTb mūlādudayagatyā tu śivenduparisaṃplutam  
AbhTa janmāntamadhyakuharamūlasrotaḥsamutthitam 
AbhTb śivārkaraśmibhistīvraiḥ kṣubdhaṃ jñānāmṛtaṃ tu yat  
AbhTa tena saṃtarpayetsamyak praśāntakaraṇena tu 
AbhTb śūnyadhāmābjamadhyasthaprabhākiraṇabhāsvaraḥ  
AbhTa ādheyādhāraniḥspandabodhaśāstraparigrahaḥ 
AbhTb janmādheyaprapañcaikasphoṭasaṃghaṭṭaghaṭṭanaḥ  
AbhTa mūlasthānātsamārabhya kṛtvā someśamantagam 
AbhTb khamivātiṣṭhate yāvatpraśāntaṃ tāvaducyate  
AbhTa uktaṃ śrīpūrvaśāstre ca srucamāpūrya sarpiṣā 
AbhTb kṛtvā śiṣyaṃ tathātmasthaṃ mūlamantramanusmaran  
AbhTa śivaṃ śaktiṃ tathātmānaṃ śiṣyaṃ sarpistathānalam 
AbhTb ekīkurvañchanairgaccheddvādaśāntamananyadhīḥ  
AbhTa tatra kumbhakamāsthāya dhyāyansakalaniṣkalam 
AbhTb tiṣṭhettāvadanudvigno yāvadājyakṣayo bhvet  
AbhTa evaṃ yuktaḥ pare tattve guruṇā śivamūrtinā 
AbhTb na bhūyaḥ paśutāmeti dagdhamāyānibandhanaḥ  
AbhTa dehapāte punaḥ prepsedyadi tattveṣu kutracit 
AbhTb bhogān samastavyastatvabhedairante paraṃ padam  
AbhTa tadā tattattvabhūmau tu tatsaṃkhyāyāmananyadhīḥ 
AbhTb punaryojanikāṃ kuryātpūrṇāhutyantareṇa tu  
AbhTa muktipradā bhogamokṣapradā vā yā prakīrtitā 
AbhTb dīkṣā sā syātsabījatvanirbījātmatayā dvidhā  
AbhTa bāle nirjñātamaraṇe tvaśakte vā jarādibhiḥ 
AbhTb kāryā nirbījikā dīkṣā śaktipātabalodaye  
AbhTa nirbījāyāṃ sāmayāṃstu pāśānapi viśodhayet 
AbhTb kṛtanirbījadīkṣastu devāgnigurubhaktibhāk  
AbhTa iyataiva śivaṃ yāyāt sadyo bhogān vibhujya vā 
AbhTb śrīmaddīkṣottare coktaṃ cāre ṣaṭtriṃśadaṅgule  
AbhTa tattvānyāpādamūrdhāntaṃ bhuvanāni tyajetkramāt 
AbhTb tuṭimātraṃ niṣkalaṃ tadadehaṃ tadahaṃparam  
AbhTa śaktyā tatra kṣipāmyenamiti dhyāyaṃstu dīkṣayet 
AbhTb sabījāyāṃ tu dīkṣāyāṃ samayānna viśodhayet  
AbhTa viśeṣastvayametasyāṃ yāvajjīvaṃ śiśorguruḥ 
AbhTb śeṣavṛttyai śuddhatattvasṛṣṭiṃ kurvīta pūrṇayā  
AbhTa abhinnācchivasaṃbodhajaladheryugapatsphurat 
AbhTb pūrṇāṃ kṣipaṃstattvajālaṃ dhyāyedbhārūpakaṃ sṛtam  
AbhTa viśuddhatattvasṛṣṭiṃ vā kuryātkumbhābhiṣecanāt 
AbhTb tathā dhyānabalādeva yadvā pūrṇābhiṣecanaiḥ  
AbhTa pṛthivī sthirarūpāsya śivarūpeṇa bhāvitā 
AbhTb sthirīkaroti tāmeva bhāvanāmiti śuddhyati  
AbhTa jalamāpyāyayatyenāṃ tejo bhāsvaratāṃ nayet 
AbhTb marudānandasaṃsparśaṃ vyoma vaitatyamāvahet  
AbhTa evaṃ tanmātravargopi śivatāmaya iṣyate 
AbhTb parānandamahāvyāptiraśeṣamalavicyutiḥ  
AbhTa śive gantṛtvamādānamupādeyaśivastutiḥ 
AbhTb śivāmodabharāsvādadarśanasparśanānyalam  
AbhTa tadākarṇanamityevamindriyāṇāṃ viśuddhatā 
AbhTb saṃkalpādhyavasāmānāḥ prakāśo raktisaṃsthitī  
AbhTa śivātmatvena yatseyaṃ śuddhatā mānasādike 
AbhTb niyamo rañjanaṃ kartṛbhāvaḥ kalanayā saha  
AbhTa vedanaṃ heyavastvaṃśaviṣaye suptakalpatā 
AbhTb itthaṃ śivaikyarūḍhasya ṣaṭkañcukagaṇopyayam  
AbhTa śuddha eva pumān prāptaśivabhāvo viśuddhyati 
AbhTb vidyeśādiṣu tattveṣu naiva kācidaśuddhatā  
AbhTa ityevaṃ śuddhatattvānāṃ sṛṣṭyā śiṣyopi tanmayaḥ 
AbhTb bhaveddhyetatsūcitaṃ śrīmālinīvijayottare  
AbhTa bandhamokṣāvubhāvetāvindriyāṇi jagurbudhāḥ 
AbhTb nigṛhītāni bandhāya vimuktāni vimuktaye  
AbhTa etāni vyāpake bhāve yadā syurmanasā saha 
AbhTb muktāni kvāpi viṣaye rodhādbandhāya tāni tu  
AbhTa ityevaṃ dvividho bhāvaḥ śuddhāśuddhaprabhedataḥ 
AbhTb indriyāṇāṃ samākhyātaḥ siddhayogīśvare mate  
AbhTa śrīmān vidyāgurustvāha pramāṇastutidarśane 
AbhTb samastamantrairdīkṣāyāṃ niyamastveṣa kathyate  
AbhTa māyāntaśuddhau sarvāḥ syuḥ kriyā hyaparayā sadā 
AbhTb dvyātmayā sakalānte tu niṣkale parayaiva tu  
AbhTa īśānte ca pivanyādi sakalānteṅgapañcakam 
AbhTb ityevaṃvidhimālocya karma kuryādgurūttamaḥ  
AbhTa purādhvani hutīnāṃ yā saṃkhyeyaṃ tattvavarṇayoḥ 
AbhTb tāmeva dviguṇīkuryātpadādhvani caturguṇām  
AbhTa kramānmantrakalāmārge dviguṇā dviguṇā kramāt 
AbhTb yāvattritattvasaṃśuddhau syādviṃśatiguṇā tataḥ  
AbhTa pratikarma bhavetṣaṣṭirāhutīnāṃ tritattvake 
AbhTb ekatattve śataṃ prāhurāhutīnāṃ tu sāṣṭakam  
AbhTa vilomakarmaṇā sākaṃ yāḥ pūrṇāhutayaḥ smṛtāḥ 
AbhTb tāsāṃ sarvādhvasaṃśuddhau saṃkhyānyatvaṃ na kiṃcana  
AbhTa ityeṣā kathitā dīkṣā jananādisamanvitā  
C atha śrītantrāloke aṣṭādaśamāhnikam
AbhTa atha saṃkṣiptadīkṣeyaṃ śivatāpattidocyate 
AbhTb na rajo nādhivāsotra na bhūkṣetraparigrahaḥ 
AbhTc yatra tatra pradeśe tu pūjayitvā guruḥ śivam  
AbhTa adhvānaṃ manasā dhyātvā dīkṣayettattvapāragaḥ 
AbhTb jananādivihīnāṃ tu yena yenādhvanā guruḥ  
AbhTa kuryātsa ekatattvāntāṃ śivabhāvaikabhāvitaḥ 
AbhTb parāmantrastatosyeti tattvaṃ saṃśodhayāmyatha  
AbhTa svāheti pratitattvaṃ syācchuddhe pūrṇāhutiṃ kṣipet 
AbhTb evaṃ mantrāntaraiḥ kuryātsamastairathavoktavat  
AbhTa parāsaṃpuṭitaṃ nāma svāhāntaṃ prathamāntakam 
AbhTb śataṃ sahasraṃ sāṣṭaṃ vā tena śaktyaiva homayet  
AbhTa tataḥ pūrṇeti saṃśodhyahīnamuttamamīdṛśam 
AbhTb dīkṣākarmoditaṃ tatra tatra śāstre maheśinā  
AbhTa pratyekaṃ mātṛkāyugmavarṇaistattvāni śodhayet 
AbhTb yadi vā piṇḍamantreṇa sarvamantreṣvayaṃ vidhiḥ  
AbhTa yathā yathā ca svabhyastajñānastanmayatātmakaḥ 
AbhTb gurustathā tathā kuryāt saṃkṣiptaṃ karma nānyathā  
AbhTa śrībrahmayāmale coktaṃ saṃkṣiptepi hi bhāvayet 
AbhTb vyāptiṃ sarvādhvasāmānyāṃ kiṃtu yāge na vistaraḥ  
AbhTa atanmayībhūtamiti vikṣiptaṃ karma sandadhat 
AbhTb kramāttādātmyametīti vikṣiptaṃ vidhimācaret  
AbhTa saṃkṣipto vidhiruktoyaṃ kṛpayā yaḥ śivoditaḥ 
AbhTb dīkṣottare kairaṇe ca tatra tatrāpi śāsane  
C atha śrītantrāloke ekānnaviṃśamāhnikam
AbhTa atha sadyaḥsamutkrāntipradā dīkṣā nirūpyate 
AbhTb tatkṣaṇāccopabhogādvā dehapāte śivaṃ vrajet 
AbhTc ityuktyā mālinīśāstre sūcitāsau maheśinā  
AbhTa dehapāte samīpasthe śaktipātasphuṭatvataḥ 
AbhTb āsādya śāṃkarīṃ dīkṣāṃ tasmāddīkṣākṣaṇātparam  
AbhTa śivaṃ vrajedityarthotra pūrvāparavivecanāt 
AbhTb vyākhyātaḥ śrīmatāsmākaṃ guruṇā śambhumūrtinā  
AbhTa yadā hyāsannamaraṇe śaktipātaḥ prajāyate 
AbhTb tatra mandetha gurvādisevayāyuḥ kṣayaṃ vrajet  
AbhTa athavā bandhumitrādidvārā sāsya vibhoḥ patet 
AbhTb pūrvaṃ vā samayī naiva parāṃ dīkṣāmavāptavān  
AbhTa āptadīkṣopi vā prāṇāñjihāsuḥ kleśavarjitam 
AbhTb antyāngurustadā kuryātsadyautkrāntidīkṣaṇam  
AbhTa natvapakvamale nāpi śeṣakārmikavigrahe 
AbhTb kuryādutkramaṇaṃ śrīmadgahvare ca nirūpitam  
AbhTa dṛṣṭvā śiṣyaṃ jarāgrastaṃ vyādhinā paripīḍitam 
AbhTb utkramayya tatastvenaṃ paratattve niyojayet  
AbhTa viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyatve kāmacāravidhānataḥ 
AbhTb pūrvoktamarthajātaṃ śrīśambhunātra nirūpitam  
AbhTa vidhiṃ pūrvoditaṃ sarvaṃ kṛtvā samayaśuddhitaḥ 
AbhTb kṣurikāmasya vinyasyejjvalantīṃ marmakartarīm  
AbhTa kṛtvā pūrvoditaṃ nyāsaṃ kālānalasamaprabham 
AbhTb saṃhṛtikramataḥ sārdhaṃ sṛkchindiyugalena tu  
AbhTa āgneyīṃ dhāraṇāṃ kṛtvā sarvamarmapratāpanīm 
AbhTb pūrayedvāyunā dehamaṅguṣṭhānmastakāntakam  
AbhTa tamutkṛṣya tatoṅguṣṭhādūrdhvāntaṃ vakṣyamāṇayā 
AbhTb kṛntenmarmāṇi randhrāntāt kālarātryā visarjayet  
AbhTa anena kramayogena yojito hutivarjitaḥ 
AbhTb samayyapyeti tāṃ dīkṣāmiti śrīmālinīmate  
AbhTa ṣoḍaśādhāraṣaṭcakralakṣyatrayakhapañcakāt 
AbhTb kvacidanyataratrātha prāguktapaśukarmavat  
AbhTa praviśya mūlaṃ kandādeśchindannaikyavibhāvanāt 
AbhTb pūrṇāhutiprayogeṇa sveṣṭe dhāmni niyojayet  
AbhTa jñānatriśūlaṃ saṃdīptaṃ dīptacakratrayojjvalam 
AbhTb cintayitvāmunā tasya vedanaṃ bodhanaṃ bhramam  
AbhTa dīpanaṃ tāḍanaṃ todaṃ calanaṃ ca punaḥ punaḥ 
AbhTb kandādicakragaṃ kuryādviśeṣeṇa hṛdambuje  
AbhTa dvādaśānte tataḥ kṛtvā binduyugmagate kṣipet 
AbhTb nirlakṣye vā pare dhāmni saṃyuktaḥ parameśvaraḥ  
AbhTa na tasya kuryātsaṃskāraṃ kaṃcidityāha gahvare 
AbhTb devaḥ kimasya pūrṇasya śrāddhādyairiti bhāvitaḥ  
AbhTa śrīmaddīkṣottare tveṣa vidhirvahnipuṭīkṛtaḥ 
AbhTb haṃsaḥ pumānadhastasya rudrabindusamanvitaḥ  
AbhTa śiṣyadehe niyojyaitadanudvagnaḥ śataṃ japet 
AbhTb utkramyordhvanimeṣeṇa śiṣya itthaṃ paraṃ vrajet  
AbhTa eṣa eva vidhiḥ śrīmatsiddhayogīśvarīmate 
AbhTb iyamutkrāmaṇī dīkṣā kartavyā yogino guroḥ  
AbhTa anabhyastaprāṇacāraḥ kathamenāṃ kariṣyati 
AbhTb vakṣyamāṇāṃ brahmavidyāṃ sakalāṃ niṣkalombhitām  
AbhTa karṇesya vā paṭhedbhūyo bhūyo vāpyatha pāṭhayet 
AbhTb svayaṃ ca karma kurvīta tattvaśuddhyādikaṃ guruḥ  
AbhTa mantrakriyābalātpūrṇāhutyetthaṃ yojayetpare 
AbhTb yogābhyāsamakṛtvāpi sadyautkrāntidāṃ guruḥ  
AbhTa jñānamantrakriyādhyānabalātkartuṃ bhavetprabhuḥ 
AbhTb anayotkramyate śiṣyo balādevaikakaṃ kṣaṇam  
AbhTa kālasyollaṅghya bhogo hi kṣaṇikosyāstu kiṃ tataḥ 
AbhTb sadyautkrāntidā cānyā yasyāṃ pūrṇāhutiṃ tadā  
AbhTa dadyādyadāsya prāṇāḥ syurdhruvaṃ niṣkramaṇecchavaḥ 
AbhTb vināpi kriyayā bhāvibrahmavidyābalādguruḥ  
AbhTa karṇajāpaprayogeṇa tattvakañcukajālataḥ 
AbhTb niḥsārayanyathābhīṣṭe sakale niṣkale dvaye  
AbhTa tattve vā yatra kutrāpi yojayetpudgalaṃ kramāt 
AbhTb samayī putrako vāpi paṭhedvidyāmimāṃ tathā  
AbhTa tatpāṭhāttu samayyuktāṃ rudrāṃśāpattimaśnute 
AbhTb etau jape cādhyayane yasmādadhikṛtāvubhau  
AbhTa nādhyāpanopadeśe vā sa eṣodhyayanādṛte 
AbhTb paṭhatostvanayorvastusvabhāvāttasya sā gatiḥ  
AbhTa yathā niṣiddhabhūtādikarmā mantraṃ smaransvayam 
AbhTb āviṣṭepi kvacinnaiti lopaṃ kartṛtvavarjanāt  
AbhTa yathā ca vācayañśāstraṃ samayī śūnyaveśmani 
AbhTb na lupyate tadantaḥsthaprāṇivargopakārataḥ  
AbhTa tathā svayaṃ paṭhanneṣa vidyāṃ vastusvabhāvataḥ 
AbhTb tasminmukte na lupyeta yato kiṃcitkarotra saḥ  
AbhTa nanu cādīkṣitāgre sa noccarecchāstrapaddhatim  
AbhTa hanta kuḍyāgratopyasya niṣedhastvatha kathyate 
AbhTb paryudāsena yaḥ śrotumavadhārayituṃ kṣamaḥ  
AbhTa sa evātra niṣiddho no kuḍyakīṭapatatriṇaḥ 
AbhTb tarhi pāṣāṇatulyosau vilīnendriyavṛttikaḥ  
AbhTa tasyāgre paṭhatastasya niṣedhollaṅghanā katham 
AbhTb sa tu vastusvabhāvena galitākṣopi budhyate  
AbhTa akṣānapekṣayaivāntaścicchaktyā svaprakāśayā 
AbhTb prāgdehaṃ kila tityakṣurnottaraṃ cādhitaṣṭhivān  
AbhTa madhye prabodhakabalāt pratibudhyet pudgalaḥ 
AbhTb mantrāḥ śabdamayāḥ śuddhavimarśātmatayā svayam  
AbhTa arthātmanā cāvabhāntastadarthapratibodhakāḥ 
AbhTb tenāsya galitākṣasya prabodho jāyate svayam  
AbhTa svacitsamānajātīyamantrāmarśanasaṃnidheḥ 
AbhTb yathā hyalpajavo vāyuḥ sajātīyavimiśritaḥ  
AbhTa javī tathātmā saṃsuptāmarśopyevaṃ prabudhyate 
AbhTb prabuddhaḥ sa ca saṃjāto na cādīkṣita ucyate  
AbhTa dīkṣā hi nāma saṃskāro na tvanyatsosti cāsya hi 
AbhTb ata eva nijaṃ śāstraṃ paṭhati kvāpi sāmaye  
AbhTa tacchrutvā kopi dhanyaścenmucyate nāsya sā kṣatiḥ 
AbhTb śāstranindāṃ maiṣa kārṣīddvayoḥ pātityadāyinīm  
AbhTa ityevaṃparametannādīkṣitāgre paṭhediti 
AbhTb yathā ca samayī kāṣṭhe loṣṭe vā mantrayojanām  
AbhTa kurvaṃstasmiṃścalatyeti na lopaṃ tadvadatra hi 
AbhTb yatosya pratyayaprāptiprepsoḥ samayinastathā  
AbhTa pravṛttasya svabhāvena tasminmukte na vai kṣatiḥ 
AbhTb sādhakastu sadā sādhye phale niyatiyantraṇāt  
AbhTa makṣikāśrutamantropi prāyaścittaucitīṃ caret 
AbhTb itthaṃ sadyaḥsamutkrāntiryoktā tāmājñayā guroḥ  
AbhTa samayyādirapi proktakāle proktārthasiddhaye 
AbhTb svayaṃ kuryātsamabhyastaprāṇacāragamāgamaḥ  
AbhTa akṛtādhikṛtirvāpi guruḥ samayaśuddhaye 
AbhTb adhastanapadāvastho natu jñāneddhacetanaḥ  
AbhTa itīyaṃ sadyautkrāntiḥ sūcitā mālinīmate 
AbhTb svayaṃ vā guruṇā vātha kāryatvena maheśinā  
AbhTa sarvaṃ bhogaṃ virūpaṃ tu matvā dehaṃ tyajedyadi 
AbhTb tadā tena krameṇāśu yojitaḥ samayī śivaḥ  
AbhTa ukteyaṃ sadyautkrāntiryā gopyā prāṇavadbudhaiḥ  
C atha śrītantrāloke viṃśatitamamāhnikam
AbhTb atha dīkṣāṃ bruve mūḍhajanāśvāsapradāyinīm  
AbhTa trikoṇe vahnisadane vahnivarṇojjvalebhitaḥ 
AbhTb vāyavyapuranirdhūte kare savye sujājvale  
AbhTa bījaṃ kiṃcidgṛhītvaitattathaiva hṛdayāntare 
AbhTb kare ca dahyamānaṃ saccintayettajjapaikayuk  
AbhTa vahnidīpitaphaṭkāradhoraṇīdāhapīḍitam 
AbhTb bījaṃ nirbījatāmeti svasūtikaraṇākṣamam  
AbhTa taptaṃ naitatprarohāya tenaiva pratyayena tu 
AbhTb malamāyākhyakarmāṇi mantradhyānakriyābalāt  
AbhTa dagdhāni na svakāryāya nirbījapratyayaṃ tvimam 
AbhTb sa śrīmānsuprasanno me śaṃbhunātho nyarūpayat  
AbhTa bījasyāpyatra kāryā ca yojanā kṛpayā guroḥ 
AbhTb yato dīkṣā sudīptatvātsthāvarāṇyapi mocayet  
AbhTa yo gururjapahomārcādhyānasiddhatvamātmani 
AbhTb jñātvā dīkṣāṃ carettasya dīkṣā sapratyayā smṛtā  
AbhTa avadhūte nirācāre tattvajñe natvayaṃ vidhiḥ 
AbhTb sācāraiḥ kriyate dīkṣā yā dṛṣṭapratyayānvitā  
AbhTa nirācāreṇa dīkṣāyāṃ pratyayastu na gadyate 
AbhTb jñānaṃ svapratyayaṃ yasmānna phalāntaramarhati  
AbhTa dhyānādi tu phalātsādhyamiti siddhāmatoditam 
AbhTb tulāśuddhiparīkṣāṃ vā kuryātpratyayayoginīm  
AbhTa yathā śrītantrasadbhāve kathitā parameśinā 
AbhTb śrīpūrvaśāstrepyeṣā ca sūcitā parameśinā  
AbhTa ānanda udbhavaḥ kampo nidrā ghūrṇiśca pañcamī 
AbhTb ityevaṃvadatā śaktitāratamyābhidhāyinā  
AbhTa udbhavo laghubhāvena dehagrahatirohiteḥ 
AbhTb deho hi pārthivo mukhyastadā mukhyatvamujjhati  
AbhTa bhāvilāghavamantreṇa śiṣyaṃ dhyātvā samutplutam 
AbhTb karmāṇi tatrāśeṣāṇi pūrvoktānyācaredguruḥ  
AbhTa uktā seyaṃ tulāśuddhidīkṣā pratyayadāyinī 
C atha śrītantrāloke ekaviṃśatitamamāhnikam
AbhTb parokṣasaṃsthitasyātha dīkṣākarma nigadyate  
AbhTa bhuktimuktiprasiddhyarthaṃ nīyate sadguruṃ prati 
AbhTb ityasminmālinīvākye pratiḥ sāṃmukhyāvācakaḥ  
AbhTa sāṃmukhyaṃ cāsya śiṣyasya tatkṛpāspadatātmakam 
AbhTb tamārādhyeti vacanaṃ kṛpāhetūpalakṣaṇam  
AbhTa tatsaṃbandhāttataḥ kaścittatkṣaṇādapavṛjyate 
AbhTb ityasyāyamapi hyartho mālinīvākyasanmaṇeḥ  
AbhTa tatkṣaṇāditi nāsyāsti yiyāsādikṣaṇāntaram 
AbhTb kiṃtvevameva karuṇānighnastaṃ gururuddharet  
AbhTa gurusevākṣīṇatanordīkṣāmaprāpya pañcatām 
AbhTb gatasyātha svayaṃ mṛtyukṣaṇoditatathāruceḥ  
AbhTa athavādharatantrādidīkṣāsaṃskārabhāginaḥ 
AbhTb prāptasāmayikasyātha parāṃ dīkṣāmavindataḥ  
AbhTa ḍimbāhatasya yogeśībhakṣitasyābhicārataḥ 
AbhTb mṛtasya guruṇā yantratantrādinihatasya vā  
AbhTa bhraṣṭasvasamayasyātha dīkṣāṃ prāptavatopyalam 
AbhTb bandhubhāryāsuhṛtputragāḍhābhyarthanayogataḥ  
AbhTa svayaṃ tadviṣayotpannakaruṇābalatopi vā 
AbhTb vijñātatanmukhāyātaśaktipātāṃśadharmaṇaḥ  
AbhTa gururdīkṣāṃ mṛtoddhārīṃ kurvīta śivadāyinīm 
AbhTb śrīmṛtyuñjayasiddhādau taduktaṃ parameśinā  
AbhTa adīkṣite nṛpatyādāvalase patite mṛte 
AbhTb bālāturastrīvṛddhe ca mṛtoddhāraṃ prakalpayet  
AbhTa vidhiḥ sarvaḥ pūrvamuktaḥ sa tu saṃkṣipta iṣyate 
AbhTb gurvādipūjārahito bāhye bhogāya sā yataḥ  
AbhTa adhivāsacarukṣetraṃ śayyāmaṇḍalakalpane 
AbhTb nopayogyatra tacchiṣyasaṃskriyāsvapnadṛṣṭaye  
AbhTa mantrasaṃnidhisaṃtṛptiyogāyātra tu maṇḍalam 
AbhTb bhūyodine ca devārcā sākṣānnāsyopakāri tat  
AbhTa kriyopakaraṇasthānamaṇḍalākṛtimantrataḥ 
AbhTb dhyānayogaikatadbhaktijñānatanmayabhāvataḥ  
AbhTa tatpraviṣṭasya kasyāpi śiṣyāṇāṃ ca gurostathā 
AbhTb ekādaśaite kathitāḥ saṃnidhānāya hetavaḥ  
AbhTa uttarottaramutkṛṣṭāstathā vyāmiśraṇāvaśāt 
AbhTb kriyātibhūyasī puṣpādyuttamaṃ lakṣaṇānvitam  
AbhTa ekaliṅgādi ca sthānaṃ yatrātmā saṃprasīdati 
AbhTb maṇḍalaṃ tritriśūlābjacakraṃ yanmantramaṇḍale  
AbhTa anāhūtepi dṛṣṭaṃ satsamayitvaprasādhanam 
AbhTb taduktaṃ mālinītantre siddhaṃ samayamaṇḍalam  
AbhTa yena saṃdṛṣṭamātreti siddhamātrapadadvayāt 
AbhTb ākṛtirdīptarūpā yā mantrastadvatsudīptikaḥ  
AbhTa śiṣṭaṃ spaṣṭamato neha kathitaṃ vistarātpunaḥ 
AbhTb kṛtvā maṇḍalamabhyarcya tatra devaṃ kuśairatha  
AbhTa gomayenākṛtiṃ kuryācchiṣyavattāṃ nidhāpayet 
AbhTb tatastasyāṃ śodhyamekamadhvānaṃ vyāptibhāvanāt  
AbhTa prakṛtyantaṃ vinikṣipya punarenaṃ vidhiṃ caret 
AbhTb mahājālaprayogeṇa sarvasmādadhvamadhyataḥ  
AbhTa cittamākṛṣya tatrasthaṃ kuryāttadvidhirucyate 
AbhTb mūlādhārādudetya prasṛtasuvitatānantanāḍyadhvadaṇḍaṃ vīryeṇākramya nāsāgaganaparigataṃ vikṣipan vyāptumīṣṭe 
AbhTc yāvaddhūmābhirāmapracitataraśikhājālakenādhvacakraṃ saṃchādyābhīṣṭajīvānayanamiti mahājālanāmā prayogaḥ  
AbhTa etenācchādanīyaṃ vrajati paravaśaṃ saṃmukhīnatvamādau pañcādānīyate cetsakalamatha tatopyadhvamadhyādyatheṣṭam 
AbhTb ākṛṣṭāvuddhṛtau vā mṛtajanaviṣaye karṣaṇīyetha jīve yogaḥ śrīśaṃbhunāthāgamaparigamito jālanāmā mayoktaḥ  
AbhTa ciravighaṭite senāyugmeyathāmilite punarhayagajanaraṃ svāṃ svāṃ jātiṃ rasādabhidhāvati 
AbhTb karaṇapavanairnāḍīcakraistathaiva samāgatairnijanijarasādekībhāvyaṃ svajālavaśīkṛtaiḥ  
AbhTa mahājālasamākṛṣṭo jīvo vijñānaśālinā 
AbhTb svaḥpretatiryaṅnirayāṃstadaivaiṣa vimuñcati  
AbhTa tajjñānamantrayogāptaḥ puruṣaścaiṣa kṛtrimam 
AbhTb yogīva sādhyahṛdayāttadā tādātmyamujjhati  
AbhTa sthāvarādidaśāścitrāstatsalokasamīpatāḥ 
AbhTb tyajecceti na citraṃ sa evaṃ yaḥ karmaṇāpi vā  
AbhTa adhikāriśarīratvānmānuṣye tu śarīragaḥ 
AbhTb na tadā mucyate dehāddehānte tu śivaṃ vrajet  
AbhTa tasmindehe tu kāpyasya jāyate śāṅkarī parā 
AbhTb bhaktirūhācca vijñānādācāryādvāpyasevitāt  
AbhTa taddehasaṃsthitopyeṣa jīvo jālabalādimam 
AbhTb dārbhādidehaṃ vyāpnoti svādhiṣṭhityāpyacetayan  
AbhTa yogamantrakriyājñānabhūyobalavaśātpunaḥ 
AbhTb manuṣyadehamapyeṣa tadaivāśu vimuñcati  
AbhTa suptakalpopyadehopi yo jīvaḥ sopi jālataḥ 
AbhTb ākṛṣṭo dārbhamāyāti dehaṃ phalamayaṃ ca vā  
AbhTa jātīphalādi yatkiṃcittena vā dehakalpanā 
AbhTb antarbahirdvayaucityāttadatrotkṛṣṭamucyate  
AbhTa tato jālakramānītaḥ sa jīvaḥ suptavatsthitaḥ 
AbhTb manoviśiṣṭadehādisāmagrīprāptyabhāvataḥ  
AbhTa na spandate na jānāti na vakti na kilecchati 
AbhTb tādṛśasyaiva saṃskārān sarvān prāgvatprakalpayet  
AbhTa nirbījadīkṣāyogena sarvaṃ kṛtvā puroditam 
AbhTb vidhiṃ yojanikāṃ pūrṇāhutyā sākaṃ kṣipecca tam  
AbhTa dārbhādidehe mantrāgnāvarpite pūrṇayā saha 
AbhTb muktapāśaḥ śivaṃ yāti punarāvṛttivarjitaḥ  
AbhTa sapratyayā tviyaṃ yatra spandate darbhajā tanuḥ 
AbhTb tatra prāṇamanomantrārpaṇayogāttathā bhavet  
AbhTa sābhyāsasya tadapyuktaṃ balāśvāsi na tatkṛte 
AbhTb mṛtoddhāroditaireva yathāsaṃbhūti hetubhiḥ  
AbhTa jīvatparokṣadīkṣāpi kāryā nirbījikā tu sā 
AbhTb tasyāṃ darbhākṛtiprāyakalpane jālayogataḥ  
AbhTa saṃkalpamātreṇākarṣo jīvasya mṛtibhītitaḥ 
AbhTb śiṣṭaṃ prāgvatkuśādyutthākāraviploṣavarjitam  
AbhTa pārimityādanaiśvaryātsādhye niyatiyantraṇāt 
AbhTb jālākṛṣṭirvinābhyāsaṃ rāgadveṣānna jāyate  
AbhTa parokṣa evātulyābhirdīkṣābhiryadi dīkṣitaḥ 
AbhTb tatrottaraṃ syādbalavatsaṃskārāya tvadhastanam  
AbhTa bhuktiyojanikāyāṃ tu bhūyobhirgurubhistathā 
AbhTb kṛtāyāṃ bhogavaicitryaṃ hetuvaicitryayogataḥ  
AbhTa parokṣadīkṣaṇe māyottīrṇe bhogāya yojayet 
AbhTb bhogānīpsā durlabhā hi satī vā bhogahānaye  
AbhTa uktaṃ hi svānyasaṃvittyoḥ svasaṃvidbalavattarā 
AbhTb bādhakatve bādhikāsau sāmyaudāsīnyayostathā  
AbhTa śrīmān dharmaśivopyāha pārokṣyāṃ karmapaddhatau 
AbhTb parokṣadīkṣaṇe samyak pūrṇāhutividhau yadi  
AbhTa agniściṭiciṭāśabdaṃ sadhūmaṃ pratimuñcati 
AbhTb dhatte nīlāmbudacchāyāṃ muhurjvalati śāmyati  
AbhTa vistaro ghorarūpaśca mahīṃ dhāvati cāpyadhaḥ 
AbhTb dhvāṃkṣādyaśravyaśabdo vā tadā taṃ lakṣayedguruḥ  
AbhTa brahmahatyādibhiḥ pāpaistatsaṅgaiścopapātakaiḥ 
AbhTb tadā tasya na kartavyā dīkṣāsminnakṛte vidhau  
AbhTa navātmā phaṭpuṭāntaḥsthaḥ punaḥ pañcaphaḍanvitaḥ 
AbhTb amukasyeti pāpāni dahāmyanu phaḍaṣṭakam  
AbhTa iti sāhasriko homaḥ kartavyastilataṇḍulaiḥ 
AbhTb ante pūrṇā ca dātavyā tatosmai dīkṣayā guruḥ  
AbhTa parayojanaparyantaṃ kuryāttattvaviśodhanam 
AbhTb pratyakṣepi sthitasyāṇoḥ pāpino bhagavanmayīm  
AbhTa śaktiṃ prāptavato jyeṣṭhāmevameva vidhiṃ caret 
AbhTb yadi vā daiśikaḥ samyaṅ na dīptastasya tatpurā  
AbhTa prāyaścittaistathā dānaiḥ prāṇāyāmaiśca śodhanam 
AbhTb kṛtvā vidhimimāṃ cāpi dīkṣāṃ kuryādaśaṅkitaḥ  
AbhTa sarvathā vartamānopi tattvavinmocayetpaśūn 
AbhTb icchayaiva śivaḥ sākṣāttasmāttaṃ pūjayetsadā  
AbhTa śāṭhyaṃ tatra na kāryaṃ ca tatkṛtvādho vrajecchiśuḥ 
AbhTb na punaḥ kīrtayettasya pāpaṃ kīrtayitā vrajet  
AbhTa nirayaṃ varjayettasmāditi dīkṣottare vidhiḥ 
AbhTb eṣā parokṣadīkṣā dvidhoditā jīvaditarabhedena  
C atha śrītantrāloke dvāviṃśatitamamāhnikam
AbhTb liṅgoddhārākhyāmatha vacmaḥ śivaśāsanaikanirdiṣṭām  
AbhTa uktaṃ śrīmālinītantre kila pārthivadhāraṇām 
AbhTb uktvā yo yojito yatra sa tasmānna nivartate  
AbhTa yogyatāvaśasaṃjātā yasya yatraiva śāsanā 
AbhTb sa tatraiva niyoktavyo dīkṣākāle tatastvasau  
AbhTa phalaṃ sarvaṃ samāsādya śive yuktopavṛjyate 
AbhTb ayuktopyūrdhvasaṃśuddhiṃ saṃprāpya bhuvaneśataḥ  
AbhTa śuddhaḥ śivatvamāyāti dagdhasaṃsārabandhanaḥ 
AbhTb uktvā puṃdhāraṇāṃ coktametadvaidāntikaṃ mayā  
AbhTa kapilāya purā proktaṃ prathame paṭale tathā 
AbhTb anena kramayogena saṃprāptaḥ paramaṃ padam  
AbhTa na bhūyaḥ paśutāmeti śuddhe svātmani tiṣṭhati 
AbhTb ato hi dhvanyaterthoyaṃ śivatattvādhareṣvapi  
AbhTa tattveṣu yojitasyāsti punaruddharaṇīyatā 
AbhTb samastaśāstrakathitavastuvaiviktyadāyinaḥ  
AbhTa śivāgamasya sarvebhyopyāgamebhyo viśiṣṭatā 
AbhTb śivajñānena ca vinā bhūyopi paśutodbhavaḥ  
AbhTa kramaśca śaktisaṃpāto malahāniryiyāsutā 
AbhTb dīkṣā bodho heyahānirupādeyalayātmatā  
AbhTa bhogyatvapāśavatyāgaḥ patikartṛtvasaṃkṣayaḥ 
AbhTb svātmasthitiścetyevaṃ hi darśanāntarasaṃsthiteḥ  
AbhTa proktamuddharaṇīyatvaṃ śivaśaktīritasya hi 
AbhTb atha vaiṣṇavabauddhāditantrāntādharavartinām  
AbhTa yadā śivārkaraśmyoghairvikāsi hṛdayāmbujam 
AbhTb liṅgoddhṛtistadā pūrvaṃ dīkṣākarma tataḥ param  
AbhTa prāgliṅgāntarasaṃsthopi dīkṣātaḥ śivatāṃ vrajet 
AbhTb tatropavāsya taṃ cānyadine sādhāramantrataḥ  
AbhTa sthaṇḍile pūjayitveśaṃ śrāvayettasya vartanīm 
AbhTb eṣa prāgabhavalliṅgī coditastvadhunā tvayā  
AbhTa prasannena tadetasmai kuru samyaganugraham 
AbhTb svaliṅgatyāgaśaṅkotthaṃ prāyaścittaṃ ca māsya bhūt  
AbhTa acirāttvanmayībhūya bhogaṃ mokṣaṃ prapadyatām 
AbhTb evamastvityathājñāṃ ca gṛhīrvā vratamasya tat  
AbhTa apāsyāmbhasi nikṣipya snapayedanurūpataḥ 
AbhTb snātaṃ saṃprokṣayedarghapātrāmbhobhiranantaram  
AbhTa pañcagavyaṃ dantakāṣṭhaṃ tatastasmai samarpayet 
AbhTb tatastaṃ baddhanetraṃ ca praveśya praṇipātayet  
AbhTa praṇavo mātṛkā māyā vyomavyāpī ṣaḍakṣaraḥ 
AbhTb bahurūpotha netrākhyaḥ sapta sādhāraṇā amī  
AbhTa teṣāṃ madhyādekatamaṃ mantramasmai samarpayet 
AbhTb sopyahorātramevainaṃ japedalpabhugapyabhuk  
AbhTa mantramasmai samarpyātha sādhāravidhisaṃskṛte 
AbhTb vahnau tarpitatanmantre vrataśuddhiṃ samācaret  
AbhTa pūjitenaiva mantreṇa kṛtvā nāmāsya saṃpuṭam 
AbhTb prāyaścittaṃ śodhayāmi phaṭsvāhetyūhayogataḥ  
AbhTa śataṃ sahasraṃ vā hutvā punaḥ pūrṇāhutiṃ tathā 
AbhTb prayogādvauṣaḍantāṃ ca kṣiptvāhūya vrateśvaram  
AbhTa tāro vrateśvarāyeti namaścetyenamarcayet 
AbhTb śrāvayecca tvayā nāsya kāryaṃ kiṃcicchivājñayā  
AbhTa tato vrateśvarastarpyaḥ svāhāntena tataśca saḥ 
AbhTb kṣamayitvā visṛjyaḥ syāttatogneśca visarjanam  
AbhTa tacchrāvaṇaṃ ca devāya kṣamasveti visarjanam 
AbhTb tatastṛtīyadivase prāgvatsarvo vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ  
AbhTa adhivāsādikaḥ sveṣṭadīkṣākarmāvasānakaḥ 
AbhTb prāgliṅgināṃ mokṣadīkṣā sādhikāravivarjitā  
AbhTa sādhakācāryatāmārge na yogyāste punarbhuvaḥ 
AbhTb punarbhuvopi jñāneddhā bhavanti gurutāspadam  
AbhTa mokṣāyaiva na bhogāya bhogāyāpyabhyupāyataḥ 
AbhTb ityuktavānsvapaddhatyāmīśānaśivadaiśikaḥ  
AbhTa śrīdevyā yāmalīyoktitattvasamyakpravedakaḥ 
AbhTb gurvantasyāpyadhodṛṣṭiśāyinaḥ saṃskriyāmimām  
AbhTa kṛtvā rahasyaṃ kathayennānyathā kāmike kila 
AbhTb anyatantrābhiṣiktepi rahasyaṃ na prakāśayet  
AbhTa svatantrasthopi gurvanto gurumajñamupāśritaḥ 
AbhTb tatra paścādanāśvastastatrāpi vidhimācaret  
AbhTa ajñācāryamukhāyātaṃ nirvīryaṃ mantrameṣa yat 
AbhTb japtavānsa guruścātra nādhikāryuktadūṣaṇāt  
AbhTa tatosya śuddhiṃ prākkṛtvā tato dīkṣāṃ samācaret 
AbhTb adhodarśanasaṃsthena guruṇā dīkṣitaḥ purā  
AbhTa tīvraśaktivaśātpaścādyadā gacchetsa sadgurum 
AbhTb tadāpyasya śiśorevaṃ śuddhiṃ kṛtvā sa sadguruḥ  
AbhTa dīkṣādikarma nikhilaṃ kuryāduktavidhānataḥ 
AbhTb prāptopi sadgururyogyabhāvamasya na vetti cet  
AbhTa vijñānadāne tacchiṣyo yogyatāṃ darśayennijām 
AbhTb sarvathā tvabruvanneṣa bruvāṇo vā viparyayam  
AbhTa ajño vastuta eveti tattyaktvetthaṃ vidhiṃ caret 
AbhTb na tirobhāvaśaṅkātra kartavyā buddhiśālinā  
AbhTa adhaḥspṛktvaṃ tirobhūtirnordhvopāyavivecanam 
AbhTb siddhānte dīkṣitāstantre daśāṣṭādaśabhedini  
AbhTa bhairavīye catuḥṣaṣṭau tānpaśūndīkṣayettrike 
AbhTb siddhavīrāvalīsāre bhairavīye kulepi ca  
AbhTa pañcadīkṣākramopāttā dīkṣānuttarasaṃjñitā 
AbhTb tena sarvodharasthopi liṅgoddhṛtyānugṛhyate  
AbhTa yopi hṛtsthamaheśānacodanātaḥ suvistṛtam 
AbhTb śāstrajñānaṃ samanvicchetsopi yāyādbahūngurūn  
AbhTa taddīkṣāścāpi gṛhṇīyādabhiṣecanapaścimāḥ 
AbhTb jñānopodbalikāstā hi tattajjñānavatā kṛtāḥ  
AbhTa uktaṃ ca śrīmate śāstre tatra tatra ca bhūyasā 
AbhTb āmodārthī yathā bhṛṅgaḥ puṣpātpuṣpāntaraṃ vrajet  
AbhTa vijñānārthī tathā śiṣyo gurorgurvantaraṃ tviti 
AbhTb gurūṇāṃ bhūyasāṃ madhye yato vijñānamuttamam  
AbhTa prāptaṃ sosya gururdīkṣā nātra mukhyā hi saṃvidi 
AbhTb sarvajñānanidhānaṃ tu guruṃ saṃprāpya susthitaḥ  
AbhTa tamevārādhayeddhīmāṃstattajjijñāsanonmukhaḥ 
AbhTb iti dīkṣāvidhiḥ prokto liṅgoddharaṇapaścimaḥ  
C atha śrītantrāloke trayoviṃśatitamamāhnikam
AbhTb athābhiṣekasya vidhiḥ kathyate pārameśvaraḥ  
AbhTa yaiṣā putrakadīkṣoktā gurusādhakayorapi 
AbhTb saivādhikāriṇī bhogyatattvayuktimatī kramāt  
AbhTa svabhyastajñāninaṃ santaṃ bubhūṣumatha bhāvinam 
AbhTb yogyaṃ jñātvā svādhikāraṃ gurustasmai samarpayet  
AbhTa yo naivaṃ veda naivāsāvabhiṣiktopi daiśikaḥ 
AbhTb samayyādikrameṇeti śrīmatkāmika ucyate  
AbhTa yo na vedādhvasandhānaṃ ṣoḍhā bāhyāntarasthitam 
AbhTb sa gururmocayenneti siddhayogīśvarīmate  
AbhTa sarvalakṣaṇahīnopi jñānavān gururiṣyate 
AbhTb jñānaprādhānyamevoktamiti śrīkacabhārgave  
AbhTa padavākyapramāṇajñaḥ śivabhaktyekatatparaḥ 
AbhTb samastaśivaśāstrārthaboddhā kāruṇiko guruḥ  
AbhTa na svayaṃbhūstasya coktaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ parameśinā 
AbhTb abhakto jīvitadhiyā kurvannīśānadhiṣṭhitaḥ  
AbhTa paścātmanā svayaṃbhūṣṇurnādhikārī sa kutracit 
AbhTb bhasmāṅkuro vratisuto duḥśīlātanayastathā  
AbhTa kuṇḍo golaśca te duṣṭā uktaṃ devyākhyayāmale 
AbhTb punarbhūścānyaliṅgo yaḥ punaḥ śaive pratiṣṭhitaḥ  
AbhTa śrīpūrvaśāstre na tveṣa niyamaḥ kopi coditaḥ 
AbhTb yathārthatattvasaṃghajñastathā śiṣye prakāśakaḥ  
AbhTa yaḥ punaḥ sarvatattvāni vettītyādi ca lakṣaṇam 
AbhTb yogacāre ca yadyatra tantre coditamācaret  
AbhTa tathaiva siddhaye seyamājñeti kila varṇitam 
AbhTb yastu karmitayācāryastatra kāṇādivarjanam  
AbhTa yataḥ kārakasāmagryātkarmaṇo nādhikaḥ kvacit 
AbhTb devyā yāmalaśāstre ca kāñcyādiparivarjanam  
AbhTa taddṛṣṭadoṣātkrodhādeḥ samyakjñātaryasau kutaḥ 
AbhTb guravastu svayaṃbhvādi varjyaṃ yadyāmalādiṣu  
AbhTa karmyabhiprāyataḥ sarvaṃ taditi vyācacakṣire 
AbhTb ato deśakulācāradehalakṣaṇakalpanām  
AbhTa anādṛtyaiva saṃpūrṇajñānaṃ kuryādgururgurum 
AbhTb prāgvatsaṃpūjya hutvā ca śrāvayitvā cikīrṣitam  
AbhTa tatobhiṣiñcettaṃ śiṣyaṃ catuḥṣaṣṭyā tataḥ sakṛt 
AbhTb tanmantrarasatoyena pūrvoktavidhinā guruḥ  
AbhTa vibhavena suvistīrṇaṃ tatastasmai vadetsvakam 
AbhTb sarvaṃ kartavyasāraṃ yacchāstrāṇāṃ paramaṃ rahaḥ  
AbhTa anugrāhyāstvayā śiṣyāḥ śivaśaktipracoditāḥ 
AbhTb uktaṃ jñānottare caitadbrāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā viśaḥ  
AbhTa napuṃsakāḥ striyaḥ śūdrā ye cānyepi tadarthinaḥ 
AbhTb te dīkṣāyāṃ na mīmāṃsyā jñānakāle vicārayet  
AbhTa jñānamūlo guruḥ proktaḥ saptasatrīṃ pravartayet 
AbhTb dīkṣā vyākhyā kṛpā maitrī śāstracintā śivaikatā  
AbhTa annādidānamityetatpālayetsaptasatrakam 
AbhTb abhiṣekavidhau cāsmai karaṇīkhaṭikādikam  
AbhTa sarvopakaraṇavrātamarpaṇīyaṃ vipaścite 
AbhTb sobhiṣikto guruṃ paścāddakṣiṇābhiḥ prapūjayet  
AbhTa jñānahīno guruḥ karmī svādhikāraṃ samarpya no 
AbhTb dīkṣādyadhikṛtiṃ kuryādvinā tasyājñayā punaḥ  
AbhTa ityevaṃ śrāvayetsopi namaskṛtyābhinandayet 
AbhTb tataḥ prabhṛtyasau pūrvo gurustyaktādhikārakaḥ  
AbhTa yathecchaṃ vicaredvyākhyādīkṣādau yantraṇojjhitaḥ 
AbhTb kurvanna bādhyate yasmāddīpāddīpavadīdṛśaḥ  
AbhTa santāno nādhikārasya cyavokurvanna bādhyate 
AbhTb prāk ca kurvanvihanyeta siddhātantre taducyate  
AbhTa yathārthamupadeśaṃ tu kurvannācārya ucyate 
AbhTb na cāvajñā kriyākāle saṃsāroddharaṇaṃ prati  
AbhTa na dīkṣeta guruḥ śiṣyaṃ tattvayuktastu garvataḥ 
AbhTb yosya syānnarake vāsa iha ca vyādhito bhavet  
AbhTa prāptābhiṣekaḥ sa guruḥ ṣaṇmāsānmantrapaddhatim 
AbhTb sarvāṃ tantroditāṃ dhyāyejjapeccātanmayatvataḥ  
AbhTa yadaiva tanmayībhūtastadā vīryamupāgataḥ 
AbhTb chindyātpāśāṃstato yatnaṃ kuryāttanmayatāsthitau  
AbhTa hṛccakrādutthitā sūkṣmā śaśisphaṭikasaṃnibhā 
AbhTb lekhākārā nādarūpā praśāntā cakrapaṅktigā  
AbhTa dvādaśānte nirūḍhā sā sauṣumne tripathāntare 
AbhTb tatra hṛccakramāpūrya japenmantraṃ jvalatprabham  
AbhTa cakṣurlomādirandhraughavahajjvālaurvasaṃnibham 
AbhTb yāvacchāntaśikhākīrṇaṃ viśvājyapravilāpakam  
AbhTa tadājyadhārāsaṃtṛptamānābhikuharāntaram 
AbhTb evaṃ mantrā mokṣadāḥ syurdīptā buddhāḥ sunirmalāḥ  
AbhTa mūlakandanabhonābhihṛtkaṇṭhālikatālugam 
AbhTb ardhendurodhikānādatadantavyāpiśaktigam  
AbhTa samanonmanaśuddhātmaparacakrasamāśritam 
AbhTb yatra yatra japeccakre samastavyastabhedanāt  
AbhTa tatra tatra mahāmantra iti devyākhyayāmale 
AbhTb vidyāvratamidaṃ proktaṃ mantravīryaprasiddhaye  
AbhTa tacca tādātmyameveti yaduktaṃ spandaśāsane 
AbhTb tadākramya balaṃ mantrāḥ sarvajñabalaśālinaḥ  
AbhTa pravartantedhikārāya karaṇānīva dehinām 
AbhTb kṛtavidyāvrataḥ paścāddīkṣāvyākhyādi sarvataḥ  
AbhTa kuryādyogyeṣu śiṣyeṣu nāyogyeṣu kadācana 
AbhTb rahasye yojayedvipraṃ parīkṣya viparītataḥ  
AbhTa ācārācchaktimapyeva nānyathetyūrmiśāsane 
AbhTb nityādyalpālpakaṃ kuryādyaduktaṃ brahmayāmale  
AbhTa cīrṇavidyāvrataḥ sarvaṃ manasā vā smaretpriye 
AbhTb dehasaṃbandhasaṃchannasārvajñyo dambhabhājanam  
AbhTa avidandīkṣamāṇopi na duṣyeddaiśikaḥ kvacit 
AbhTb jñātvā tvayogyatāṃ nainaṃ dīkṣeta pratyavāyitām  
AbhTa buddhvā jñāne śāstrasiddhigurutvādau ca taṃ punaḥ 
AbhTb bhūya eva parīkṣeta tattadaucityaśālinam  
AbhTa tatra tatra niyuñjīta natu jātu viparyayāt 
AbhTb nanu tadvastvayogyasya tatrecchā jāyate kutaḥ  
AbhTa tadīśādhiṣṭhitecchaiva yogyatāmasya sūcayet 
AbhTb satyaṃ kāpi prabuddhāsāvicchā rūḍhiṃ na gacchati  
AbhTa vidyudvatpāpaśīlasya yathā pāpāpavarjane 
AbhTb rūḍhyarūḍhī tadicchāyā api śaṃbhuprasādataḥ  
AbhTa aprarūḍhatathecchākastata eva na bhājanam 
AbhTb yaḥ samyagjñānamādāya guruviśvāsavarjitaḥ  
AbhTa lokaṃ viplāvayennāsmiñjñāte vijñānamarpayet 
AbhTb ajñātepi punarjñāte vijñānaharaṇaṃ caret  
AbhTa punaḥpunaryadā jñāto viśvāsaparivarjitaḥ 
AbhTb tadā tamagrato dhyāyetsphurantaṃ candrasūryavat  
AbhTa tato nijahṛdambhojabodhāmbarataloditām 
AbhTb svarbhānumalināṃ dhyāyedvāmāṃ śaktiṃ vimohanīm  
AbhTa vāmācārakrameṇaināṃ niḥsṛtāṃ sādhyagāminīm 
AbhTb cintayitvā tayā grastaprakāśaṃ taṃ vicintayet  
AbhTa anena kramayogena mūḍhabuddherdurātmanaḥ 
AbhTb vijñānamantravidyādyāḥ prakurvantyapakāritām  
AbhTa nanu vijñānamātmasthaṃ kathaṃ hartuṃ kṣamaṃ bhavet 
AbhTb ato vijñānaharaṇaṃ kathaṃ śrīpūrva ucyate  
AbhTa ucyate nāsya śiṣyasya vijñānaṃ rūḍhimāgatam 
AbhTb tathātve haraṇaṃ kasmātpūrṇayogyatvaśālinaḥ  
AbhTa kiṃtveṣa vāmayā śaktyā mūḍho gāḍhaṃ vibhoḥ kṛtaḥ 
AbhTb svabhāvādeva tenāsya vidyādyamapakārakam  
AbhTa guruḥ punaḥ śivābhinnaḥ sanyaḥ pañcavidhāṃ kṛtim 
AbhTb kuryādyadi tataḥ pūrṇamadhikāritvamasya tat  
AbhTa ato yathā śuddhatattvasṛṣṭisthityormalātyaye 
AbhTb yojanānugrahe kāryacatuṣkedhikṛto guruḥ  
AbhTa śivābhedena tatkuryāttadvatpañcamamapyayam 
AbhTb tirobhāvābhidhaṃ kṛtyaṃ tathāsau śivatātmakaḥ  
AbhTa ata eva śive śāstre jñāne cāśvāsabhājanam 
AbhTb gurormūḍhatayā kopadhāmāpi na tirohitaḥ  
AbhTa gururhi kupito yasya sa tirohita ucyate 
AbhTb saṃsārī satu devo hi gururna ca mṛṣāvidaḥ  
AbhTa tata eva ca śāstrādidūṣako yadyapi krudhā 
AbhTb na dahyatesau guruṇā tathāpyeṣa tirohitaḥ  
AbhTa asmadgurvāgamastveṣa tirobhūte svayaṃ śiśau 
AbhTb na kupyenna śapeddhīmān sa hyanugrāhakaḥ sadā  
AbhTa īśecchācoditaḥ pāśaṃ yadi kaṇṭhe nipīḍayet 
AbhTb kimācāryeṇa tatrāsya kāryā syātsahakāritā  
AbhTa śivābhinnopi hi gururanugrahamayīṃ vibhoḥ 
AbhTb mukhyāṃ śaktimupāsīnonugṛhṇīyātsa sarvathā  
AbhTa svātantryamātrajñaptyai tu kathitaṃ śāstra īdṛśam 
AbhTb na kāryaṃ patatāṃ hastālambaḥ sahyo na pātanam  
AbhTa ata eva svatantratvādicchāyāḥ punarunmukham 
AbhTb prāyaścittairviśodhyainaṃ dīkṣeta kṛpayā guruḥ  
AbhTa ūrdhvadṛṣṭau prapannaḥ sannanāśvastastataḥ param 
AbhTb adhaḥśāstraṃ prapadyāpi na śreyaḥpātratāmiyāt  
AbhTa adhodṛṣṭau prapannastu tadanāśvastamānasaḥ 
AbhTb ūrdhvaśāsanabhāk pāpaṃ taccojjhecca śivībhavet  
AbhTa rājñe druhyannamātyāṅgabhūtopi hi vihanyate 
AbhTb viparyayastu netyevamūrdhvāṃ dṛṣṭiṃ samāśrayet  
AbhTa śrīpūrvaśāstre tenoktaṃ yāvattenaiva noddhṛtaḥ 
AbhTb atra hyarthoyametāvatpūrvoktajñānavṛṃhitaḥ  
AbhTa gurustāvatsa evātra tacchabdenāvamṛśyate 
AbhTb tādṛksvabhyastavijñānabhājordhvapadaśālinā  
AbhTa anuddhṛtasya na śreya etadanyagurūddhṛteḥ 
AbhTb ata evāmbujanmārkadṛṣṭāntotra nirūpitaḥ  
AbhTa trijagajjyotiṣo hyanyattejonyacca niśākṛtaḥ 
AbhTb jñānamanyattrikaguroranyattvadharavartinām  
AbhTa ata eva purābhūtagurvabhāvo yadā tadā 
AbhTb tadanyaṃ lakṣaṇopetamāśrayetpunarunmukhaḥ  
AbhTa sati tasmiṃstūnmukhaḥ sankasmājjahyādyadi sphuṭam 
AbhTb syādanyatarago doṣo yodhikārāpaghātakaḥ  
AbhTa doṣaśceha na lokastho doṣatvena nirūpyate 
AbhTb ajñānakhyāpanāyuktakhyāpanātmā tvasau mataḥ  
AbhTa śiṣyasyāpi tathābhūtajñānānāśvastarūpatā 
AbhTb mukhyo doṣastadanye hi doṣāstatprabhavā yataḥ  
AbhTa na dhvastavyādhikaḥ ko hi bhiṣajaṃ bahu manyate 
AbhTb asūyurnūnamadhvastavyādhiḥ svasthāyate balāt  
AbhTa evaṃ jñānasamāśvastaḥ kiṃ kiṃ na gurave caret 
AbhTb no cennūnamaviśvasto viśvasta iva tiṣṭhati  
AbhTa ajñānādaya evaite doṣā na laukikā guroḥ 
AbhTb iti khyāpayituṃ proktaṃ mālinīvijayottare  
AbhTa na tasyānveṣayedvṛttaṃ śubhaṃ vā yadi vāśubham 
AbhTb sa eva tadvijānāti yuktaṃ cāyuktameva vā  
AbhTa akāryeṣu yadā saktaḥ prāṇadravyāpahāriṣu 
AbhTb tadā nivāraṇīyosau praṇatena vipaścitā  
AbhTa viśeṣaṇamakāryāṇāmuktābhiprāyameva yat 
AbhTb tenātivāryamāṇopi yadyasau na nivartate  
AbhTa tadānyatra kvacidgatvā śivamevānucintayet 
AbhTb na hyasya sa gurutve syāddoṣo yenoṣare kṛṣim  
AbhTa kuryādvrajenniśāyāṃ vā sa tvarthaprāṇahārakaḥ 
AbhTb tadīyāpriyabhīrustu paraṃ tādṛśamācaret  
AbhTa yatastadapriyaṃ naiṣa śṛṇuyāditi bhāṣitam 
AbhTb śrīmātaṅge taduktaṃ ca nādhītaṃ bhūmabhītitaḥ  
AbhTa yaccaitaduktametāvatkartavyamiti taddhruvam 
AbhTb tīvraśaktigṛhītānāṃ svayameva hṛdi sphuret  
AbhTa upadeśastvayaṃ mandamadhyaśakternijāṃ kramāt 
AbhTb śaktiṃ jvalayituṃ proktaḥ sā hyevaṃ jājvalītyalam  
AbhTa dṛḍhānurāgasubhagasaṃrambhābhogabhāginaḥ 
AbhTb svollāsi smarasarvasyaṃ dārḍhyāyānyatra dṛśyate  
AbhTa nanveṣa kasmāddṛṣṭāntaḥ kimetenāśubhaṃ kṛtam 
AbhTb citspandaḥ sarvago bhinnādupādheḥ sa tathā tathā  
AbhTa bhavetkopi tirobhūtaḥ punarunmukhitopi san 
AbhTb vināpi daiśikātprāgvatsvayameva vimucyate  
AbhTa prakārastveṣa nātroktaḥ śaktipātabalādgataḥ 
AbhTb asaṃbhāvyatayā cātra dṛḍhakopaprasādavat  
AbhTa ityeṣa yo guroḥ prokto vidhistaṃ pālayedguruḥ 
AbhTb anyathā na śivaṃ yāyācchrīmatsāre ca varṇitam  
AbhTa anyāyaṃ ye prakurvanti śāstrārthaṃ varjayantyalam 
AbhTb terdhanārīśapuragā guravaḥ samayacyutāḥ  
AbhTa anyatrāpyadhikāraṃ ca neyādvidyeśatāṃ vrajet 
AbhTb anyatra samayatyāgātkravyādatvaṃ śataṃ samāḥ  
AbhTa iyattatratyatātparyaṃ siddhāntagururunnayaḥ 
AbhTb bhavetpiśācavidyeśaḥ śuddha eva tu tāntrikaḥ  
AbhTa ṣaḍardhadaiśikaścārdhanārīśabhuvanasthitiḥ 
AbhTb eṣā karmapradhānānāṃ gurūṇāṃ gatirucyate  
AbhTa jñānināṃ caiṣa no bandha iti sarvatra varṇitam 
AbhTb sādhakasyābhiṣekepi sarvoyaṃ kathyate vidhiḥ  
AbhTa adhikārārpaṇaṃ nātra naca vidyāvrataṃ kila 
AbhTb sādhyamantrārpaṇaṃ tvatra svopayogikriyākrame  
AbhTa samastepyupadeśaḥ syānnijopakaraṇārpaṇam 
AbhTb abhiṣekavidhirnirūpitaḥ parameśena yathā nirūpitaḥ  
C atha śrītantrāloke caturviṃśatitamamāhnikam
AbhTb atha śāmbhavaśāsanoditāṃ sarahasyāṃ śṛṇutāntyasaṃskriyām  b
AbhTa sarveṣāmadharasthānāṃ gurvantānāmapi sphuṭam 
AbhTb śaktipātātpurāproktātkuryādantyeṣṭidīkṣaṇam  
AbhTa ūrdhvaśāsanagānāṃ ca samayopahatātmanām 
AbhTb antyeṣṭidīkṣā kartavyā guruṇā tattvavedinā  
AbhTa samayācāradoṣeṣu pramādātskhalitasya hi 
AbhTb antyeṣṭidīkṣā kāryeti śrīdīkṣottaraśāsane  
AbhTa yatkiṃcitkathitaṃ pūrvaṃ mṛtoddhārābhidhe vidhau 
AbhTb pratimāyāṃ tadevātra sarvaṃ śavatanau caret  
AbhTa śrīsiddhātantrakathito vidhireṣa nirūpyate 
AbhTb antimaṃ yadbhavetpūrvaṃ tatkṛtvāntimamādimam  
AbhTa saṃhṛtyaikaikamiṣṭiryā sāntyeṣṭirdvitayī matā 
AbhTb pūjādhyānajapāpluṣṭasamaye natu sādhake  
AbhTa piṇḍapātādayaṃ muktaḥ khecaro vā bhavetpriye 
AbhTb ācārye tattvasaṃpanne yatra tatra mṛte sati  
AbhTa antyeṣṭirnaiva vidyeta śuddhacetasyamūrdhani 
AbhTb mantrayogādibhirye ca māritā narake tu te  
AbhTa kāryā teṣāmihāntyeṣṭirguruṇātikṛpālunā 
AbhTb na maṇḍalādikaṃ tvatra bhavecchamāśānike vidhau  
AbhTa kecittadapi kartavyamūcire pretasadmani 
AbhTb pūjayitvā vibhuṃ sarvaṃ nyāsaṃ pūrvavadācaret  
AbhTa saṃhārakramayogena caraṇānmūrdhapaścimam 
AbhTb tathaiva bodhayedenaṃ kriyājñānasamādhibhiḥ  
AbhTa bindunā rodhayettattvaṃ śaktibījena vedhayet 
AbhTb ghaṭṭayennādadeśe tu triśūlena tu tāḍayet  
AbhTa suṣumnāntargatenaiva visargeṇa punaḥ punaḥ 
AbhTb tāḍayeta kalāḥ sarvāḥ kampatesau tataḥ paśuḥ  
AbhTa utkṣipedvāmahastaṃ vā tatastaṃ yojayetpare 
AbhTb pratyayena vinā mokṣo hyaśraddheyo vimohitaiḥ  
AbhTa tadarthametaduditaṃ natu mokṣopayogyadaḥ 
AbhTb ityūce parameśaḥ śrīkulagahvaraśāsane  
AbhTa sādhyonumeyo mokṣādiḥ pratyayairyadatīndriyaḥ 
AbhTb dīkṣottare ca puryaṣṭavargārpaṇamihoditam  
AbhTa tadvidhiḥ śrutipatrebje madhye devaṃ sadāśivam 
AbhTb īśarudraharibrahmacatuṣkaṃ prāgdigāditaḥ  
AbhTa pūjayitvā śrutisparśau rasaṃ gandhaṃ vapurdvayam 
AbhTb dhyahaṃkṛtī manaśceti brahmādiṣvarpayetkramāt  
AbhTa eteṣāṃ tarpaṇaṃ kṛtvā śatahomena daiśikaḥ 
AbhTb eṣā sāṃnyāsikī dīkṣā puryaṣṭakaviśodhanī  
AbhTa puryaṣṭakasyābhāve ca na svarganarakādayaḥ 
AbhTb tathā kṛtvā na kartavyaṃ laukikaṃ kiṃcanāpi hi  
AbhTa uktaṃ śrīmādhavakule śāsanastho mṛteṣvapi 
AbhTb piṇḍapātodakāsrvādi laukikaṃ parivarjayet  
AbhTa śivaṃ saṃpūjya cakrārcāṃ yathāśakti samācaret 
AbhTb kramāttridaśamatriṃśatriṃśavatsaravāsare  
AbhTa ityuktontyeṣṭiyāgoyaṃ parameśvarabhāṣitaḥ  
C atha śrītantrāloke pañcaviṃśatitamamāhnikam
AbhTb atha śrāddhavidhiḥ śrīmatṣaḍardhokto nigadyate  b
AbhTa siddhātantre sūcitosau mūrtiyāganirūpaṇe 
AbhTb antyeṣṭyā suviśuddhānāmaśuddhānāṃ ca tadvidhiḥ  
AbhTa tryahe turyehni daśame māsi māsyādyavatsare 
AbhTb varṣe varṣe sarvakālaṃ kāryastatsvaiḥ sa pūrvavat  
AbhTa tatra prāgvadyajeddevaṃ homayedanale tathā 
AbhTb tato naivedyameva prāggṛhītvā hastagocare  
AbhTa gururannamayīṃ śaktiṃ vṛṃhikāṃ vīryarūpiṇīm 
AbhTb dhyātvā tayā samāviṣṭaṃ taṃ sādhyaṃ cintayetsudhīḥ  
AbhTa tatosya yaḥ pāśavoṃśo bhogyarūpastamarpayet 
AbhTb bhoktaryekātmabhāvena śiṣya itthaṃ śivībhavet  
AbhTa bhogyatānyā tanurdeha iti pāśātmakā matāḥ 
AbhTb śrāddhe mṛtoddhṛtāvantayāge teṣāṃ śivīkṛtiḥ  
AbhTa ekenaiva vidhānena yadyapi syātkṛtārthatā 
AbhTb tathāpi tanmayībhāvasiddhyai sarvaṃ vidhiṃ caret  
AbhTa bubhukṣostu kriyābhyāsabhūmānau phalabhūmani 
AbhTb hetu tato mṛtoddhāraśrāddhādyasmai samācaret  
AbhTa tattvajñānārkavidhvastadhvāntasya tu na kopyayam 
AbhTb antyeṣṭiśrāddhavidhyādirupayogī kadācana  
AbhTa teṣāṃ tu guru tadvargavargyasabrahmacāriṇām 
AbhTb tatsantānajuṣāmaikyadinaṃ parvadinaṃ bhavet  
AbhTa yadāhi bodhasyodrekastadā parvāha pūraṇāt 
AbhTb janmaikyadivasau tena parvaṇī bodhasiddhitaḥ  
AbhTa putrakopi yadā kasmaicana syādupakārakaḥ 
AbhTb tadā mātuḥ pituḥ śaktervāmadakṣāntarālagāḥ  
AbhTa nāḍīḥ pravāhayeddevāyārpayeta niveditam 
AbhTb śrīmadbharuṇatantre ca tacchivena nirūpitam  
AbhTa tadvāhakālāpekṣā ca kāryā tadrūpasiddhaye 
AbhTb svācchandyenātha tatsiddhiṃ vidhinā bhāvinā caret  
AbhTa yasya kasyāpi vā śrāddhe gurudevāgnitarpaṇam 
AbhTb sacakreṣṭi bhavecchrauto natu syātpāśavo vidhiḥ  
AbhTa śrīmaukuṭe tathā coktaṃ śivaśāstre sthitopi yaḥ 
AbhTb pratyeti vaidike bhagnaghaṇṭāvanna sa kiṃcana  
AbhTa tathoktadevapūjādicakrayāgāntakarmaṇā 
AbhTb rudratvametyasau janturbhogāndivyānsamaśnute  
AbhTa atha vacmaḥ sphuṭaṃ śrīmatsiddhaye nāḍicāraṇam 
AbhTb yā vāhayitumiṣyeta nāḍī tāmeva bhāvayet  
AbhTa bhāvanātanmayībhāve sā nāḍī vahati sphuṭam 
AbhTb yadvā vāhayituṃ yeṣṭā tadaṅgaṃ tena pāṇinā  
AbhTa āpīḍya kukṣiṃ namayetsā vahennāḍikā kṣaṇāt 
AbhTb evaṃ śrāddhamukhenāpi bhogamokṣobhayasthitim  
AbhTa kuryāditi śivenoktaṃ tatra tatra kṛpālunā 
AbhTb śaktipātodaye jantoryenopāyena daiśikaḥ  
AbhTa karotyuddharaṇaṃ tattannirvāṇāyāsya kalpate 
AbhTb uddhartā devadevo hi sa cācintyaprabhāvakaḥ  
AbhTa upāyaṃ gurudīkṣādidvāramātreṇa saṃśrayet 
AbhTb uktaṃ śrīmanmataṅgākhye munipraśnādanantaram  
AbhTa muktirvivekāttattvānāṃ dīkṣāto yogato yadi 
AbhTb caryāmātrātkathaṃ sā syādityataḥ samamuttaram  
AbhTa prahasyoce vibhuḥ kasmādbhrāntiste parameśituḥ 
AbhTb sarvānugrāhakatvaṃ hi saṃsiddhaṃ dṛśyatāṃ kila  
AbhTa prāptamṛtyorviṣavyādhiśastrādi kila kāraṇam 
AbhTb alpaṃ vā bahu vā tadvadanudhyā muktikāraṇam  
AbhTa muktyarthamupacaryante bāhyaliṅgānyamūni tu 
AbhTb iti jñātvā na sandeha itthaṃ kāryo vipaścitā  
AbhTa iyataiva kathaṃ muktiriti bhaktiṃ parāṃ śrayet 
AbhTb uktaḥ śrāddhavidhirbhrāntigarātaṅkavimardanaḥ  
C atha śrītantrāloke ṣaḍviṃśamāhnikam
AbhTb athocyate śeṣavṛttirjīvatāmupayoginī  b
AbhTa dīkṣā bahuprakāreyaṃ śrāddhāntā yā prakīrtitā 
AbhTb sā saṃskriyāyai mokṣāya bhogāyāpi dvayāya vā  
AbhTa tatra saṃskārasiddhyai yā dīkṣā sākṣānna mocanī 
AbhTb anusaṃdhivaśādyā ca sākṣānmoktrī sabījikā  
AbhTa tayobhayyā dīkṣitā ye teṣāmājīvavartanam 
AbhTb vaktavyaṃ putrakādīnāṃ tanmayatvaprasiddhaye  
AbhTa bubhukṣorvā mumukṣorvā svasaṃvidguruśāstrataḥ 
AbhTb pramāṇādyā saṃskriyāyai dīkṣā hi guruṇā kṛtā  
AbhTa tataḥ sa saṃskṛtaṃ yogyaṃ jñātvātmānaṃ svaśāsane 
AbhTb taduktavastvanuṣṭhānaṃ bhuktyai muktyai ca sevate  
AbhTa ācāryapratyayādeva yopi syādbhuktimuktibhāk 
AbhTb tatpratyūhodayadhvastyai brūyāttasyāpi vartanam  
AbhTa svasaṃvidgurusaṃvittyostulyapratyayabhāgapi 
AbhTb śeṣavṛttyā samādeśyastadvighnādipraśāntaye  
AbhTa yaḥ sarvathā parāpekṣāmujjhitvā tu sthito nijāt 
AbhTb pratyayādyopi cācāryapratyayādeva kevalāt  
AbhTa tau sāṃsiddhikanirbījau ko vadeccheṣavṛttaye 
AbhTb kramāttanmayatopāyagurvarcanaratau tu tau  
AbhTa tatraiṣāṃ śeṣavṛttyarthaṃ nityanaimittike dhruve 
AbhTb kāmyavarjaṃ yataḥ kāmāścitrāścitrābhyupāyakāḥ  
AbhTa tatra nityo vidhiḥ sandhyānuṣṭhānaṃ devatāvraje 
AbhTb gurvagniśāstrasahite pūjā bhūtadayetyayam  
AbhTa naimittikastu sarveṣāṃ parvaṇāṃ pūjanaṃ japaḥ 
AbhTb viśeṣavaśataḥ kiṃca pavitrakavidhikramaḥ  
AbhTa ācāryasya ca dīkṣeyaṃ bahubhedā vivecitā 
AbhTb vyākhyādikaṃ ca tattasyādhikaṃ naimittikaṃ dhruvam  
AbhTa tatrādau śiśave vrūyādgururnityavidhiṃ sphuṭam 
AbhTb tadyogyatāṃ samālokya vitatāvitatātmanām  
AbhTa mukhyetarādimantrāṇāṃ vīryavyāptyādiyogyatām 
AbhTb dṛṣṭvā śiṣye tamevāsmai mūlamantraṃ samarpayet  
AbhTa tacchāstradīkṣito hyeṣa niryantrācāraśaṅkitaḥ 
AbhTb na mukhye yogya ityanyasevātaḥ syāttu yogyatā  
AbhTa sādhakasya bubhukṣostu sādhakībhāvinopivā 
AbhTb puṣpapātavaśātsiddho mantrorpyaḥ sādhyasiddhaye  
AbhTa vitate guṇabhūte vā vidhau diṣṭe punarguruḥ 
AbhTb jñātvāsmai yogyatāṃ sāraṃ saṃkṣiptaṃ vidhimācaret  
AbhTa tatraiṣa niyamo yadyanmāntraṃ rūpaṃ na tadguruḥ 
AbhTb likhitvā prathayecchiṣye viśeṣādūrdhvaśāsane  
AbhTa mantrā varṇātmakāste ca parāmarśātmakāḥ saca 
AbhTb gurusaṃvidabhinnaśvetsaṃkrāmetsā tataḥ śiśau  
AbhTa lipisthitastu yo mantro nirvīryaḥ sotra kalpitaḥ 
AbhTb saṃketabalato nāsya pustakātprathate mahaḥ  
AbhTa pustakādhītavidyāścetyuktaṃ siddhāmate tataḥ 
AbhTb ye tu pustakalabdhepi mantre vīryaṃ prajānate  
AbhTa te bhairavīyasaṃskārāḥ proktāḥ sāṃsiddhikā iti 
AbhTb iti jñātvā guruḥ samyak paramānandaghūrṇitaḥ  
AbhTa tādṛśe tādṛśe dhāmni pūjayitvā vidhiṃ caret 
AbhTb yathānyaśiṣyānuṣṭhānaṃ nānyaśiṣyeṇa budhyate  
AbhTa tathā kuryādgururguptihānirdoṣavatī yataḥ 
AbhTb devīnāṃ tritayaṃ śuddhaṃ yadvā yāmalayogataḥ  
AbhTa devīmekāmatho śuddhāṃ vadedvā yāmalātmikām 
AbhTb tatra mantraṃ sphuṭaṃ vaktrādguruṇopāṃśu coditam  
AbhTa avadhāryā pravṛttestamabhyasyenmanasā svayam 
AbhTb tataḥ suśikṣitāṃ sthānadehāntaḥśodhanatrayīm  
AbhTa nyāsaṃ dhyānaṃ japaṃ mudrāṃ pūjāṃ kuryātprayatnataḥ 
AbhTb tatra prabhāte saṃbudhya sveṣṭāṃ prāgdevatāṃ smaret  
AbhTa kṛtāvaśyakakartavyaḥ śuddho bhūtvā tato gṛham 
AbhTb āśrityottaradigvaktraḥ sthānadehāntaratraye  
AbhTa śuddhiṃ vidhāya mantrāṇāṃ yathāsthānaṃ niveśanam 
AbhTb mudrāpradarśanaṃ dhyānaṃ bhedābhedasvarūpataḥ  
AbhTa dehāsudhīvyomabhūṣu manasā tatra cārcanam 
AbhTb japaṃ cātra yathāśakti devāyaitannivedanam  
AbhTa tanmayībhāvasiddhyarthaṃ pratisandhyaṃ samācaret 
AbhTb anye tu prāgudakpaścāddaśadikṣu catuṣṭayīm  
AbhTa sandhyānāmāhuretacca tāntrikīyaṃ na no matam 
AbhTb yāsau kālādhikāre prāk sandhyā proktā catuṣṭayī  
AbhTa tāmevāntaḥ samādhāya sāndhyaṃ vidhimupācaret 
AbhTb sandhyācatuṣṭayīkṛtyamekasyāmathavā śiśuḥ  
AbhTa kuryātsvādhyāyavijñānagurukṛtyāditatparaḥ 
AbhTb sandhyādhyānoditānantatanmayībhāvayuktitaḥ  
AbhTa tatsaṃskāravaśātsarvaṃ kālaṃ syāttanmayo hyasau 
AbhTb tato yatheṣṭakālesau pūjāṃ puṣpāsavādibhiḥ  
AbhTa sthaṇḍilādau śiśuḥ kuryādvibhavādyanurūpataḥ 
AbhTb suśuddhaḥ sanvidhiṃ sarvaṃ kṛtvāntarajapāntakam  
AbhTa arghapātraṃ purā yadvadvidhāya sveṣṭamantrataḥ 
AbhTb tena sthaṇḍilapuṣpādi sarvaṃ saṃprokṣayedbudhaḥ  
AbhTa tatastatraiva saṃkalpya dvārāsanagurukramam 
AbhTb pūjayecchivatāviṣṭaḥ svadehārcāpuraḥsaram  
AbhTa tatastatsthaṇḍilaṃ vīdhravyomasphaṭikanirmalam 
AbhTb bodhātmakaṃ samālokya tatra svaṃ devatāgaṇam  
AbhTa pratibimbatayā paśyedbimbatvena ca bodhataḥ 
AbhTb etadāvāhanaṃ mukhyaṃ vyajanānmarutāmiva  
AbhTa sarvagopi marudyadvadvyajanenopajīvitaḥ 
AbhTb arthakṛtsarvagaṃ mantracakraṃ rūḍhestathā bhavet  
AbhTa catuṣkapañcāśikayā tadetattattvamucyate 
AbhTb śrīnirmaryādaśāstre ca tadetadvibhunoditam  
AbhTa devaḥ sarvagato deva nirmaryādaḥ kathaṃ śivaḥ 
AbhTb āvāhyate kṣamyate vetyevaṃpṛṣṭobravīdvibhuḥ  
AbhTa vāsanāvāhyate devi vāsanā ca visṛjyate 
AbhTb paramārthena devasya nāvāhanavisarjane  
AbhTa āvāhito mayā devaḥ sthaṇḍile ca pratiṣṭhitaḥ 
AbhTb pūjitaḥ stuta ityevaṃ hṛṣṭvā devaṃ visarjayet  
AbhTa prāṇināmaprabuddhānāṃ santoṣajananāya vai 
AbhTb āvāhanādikaṃ teṣāṃ pravṛttiḥ kathamanyathā  
AbhTa kālena tu vijānanti pravṛttāḥ patiśāsane 
AbhTb anukrameṇa devasya prāptiṃ bhuvanapūrvikām  
AbhTa jñānadīpadyutidhvastasamastājñānasañcayāḥ 
AbhTb kuto vānīyate devaḥ kutra vā nīyatepi saḥ  
AbhTa sthūlasūkṣmādibhedena sa hi sarvatra saṃsthitaḥ 
AbhTb āvāhite mantragaṇe puṣpāsavanivedanaiḥ  
AbhTa dhūpaiśca tarpaṇaṃ kāryaṃ śraddhābhaktibalocitaiḥ 
AbhTb dīptānāṃ śaktinādādimantrāṇāmāsavaiḥ palaiḥ  
AbhTa raktaiḥ prāk tarpaṇa paścāt puṣpadhūpādivistaraiḥ 
AbhTb āgatasya tu mantrasya na kuryāttarpaṇaṃ yadi  
AbhTa haratyardhaśarīraṃ sa ityuktaṃ kila śambhunā 
AbhTb yadyadevāsya manasi vikāsitvaṃ prayacchati  
AbhTa tenaiva kuryātpūjāṃ sa iti śambhorviniścayaḥ 
AbhTb sādhakānāṃ bubhukṣūṇāṃ vidhirniyatiyantritaḥ  
AbhTa mumukṣūṇāṃ tattvavidāṃ sa eva tu nirargalaḥ 
AbhTb kārye viśeṣamādhitsurviśiṣṭaṃ kāraṇaṃ spṛśet  
AbhTa raktakarpāsatūlecchustulyatadbījapuñjavat 
AbhTb santi bhoge viśeṣāśca vicitrāḥ kāraṇeritāḥ  
AbhTa deśakālānusandhānaguṇadravyakriyādibhiḥ 
AbhTb svalpā kriyā bhūyasī vā hṛdayāhlādadāyibhiḥ  
AbhTa bāhyaiḥ saṃkalpajairvāpi kārakaiḥ parikalpitā 
AbhTb mumukṣorna viśeṣāya naiḥśreyasavidhiṃ prati  
AbhTa nahi brahmaṇi śaṃsanti bāhulyālpatvadurdaśāḥ 
AbhTb citaḥ svātantryasāratvāt tasyānandaghanatvataḥ  
AbhTa kriyā syāttanmayībhūtyai hṛdayāhlādadāyibhiḥ 
AbhTb śivābhedabharādbhāvavargaḥ ścyotati yaṃ rasam  
AbhTa tameva parame dhāmni pūjanāyārpayedbudhaḥ 
AbhTb stotreṣu bahudhā caitanmayā proktaṃ nijāhnike  
AbhTa adhiśayya pāramārthikabhāvaprasaraprakāśamullasati 
AbhTb yā paramāmṛtadṛk tvāṃ tayārcayante rahasyavidaḥ  
AbhTa kṛtvādhāradharāṃ camatkṛtirasaprokṣākṣaṇakṣālitāmāttairmānasataḥ svabhāvakusumaiḥ svāmodasandohibhiḥ 
AbhTb ānandāmṛtanirbharasvahṛdayānarghārghapātrakramāt tvāṃ devyā saha dehadevasadane devārcayeharniśam  
AbhTa nānāsvādarasāmimāṃ trijagatīṃ hṛccakrayantrārpitāmūrdhvādhyastavivekagauravabharānniṣpīḍya niḥṣyanditam 
AbhTb yatsaṃvitparamāmṛtaṃ mṛtijarājanmāpahaṃ jṛmbhate tena tvāṃ haviṣā pareṇa parame saṃtarpayeharniśam  
AbhTa iti ślokatrayopāttamarthamantarvibhāvayan 
AbhTb yena kenāpi bhāvena tarpayeddevatāgaṇam  
AbhTa mudrāṃ pradarśayetpaścānmanasā vāpi yogataḥ 
AbhTb vacasā mantrayogena vapuṣā saṃniveśataḥ  
AbhTa kṛtvā japaṃ tataḥ sarvaṃ devatāyai samarpayet 
AbhTb taccoktaṃ kartṛtātattvanirūpaṇavidhau purā  
AbhTa tato visarjanaṃ kāryaṃ bodhaikātmyaprayogataḥ 
AbhTb kṛtvā vā vahnigāṃ mantratṛptiṃ proktavidhānataḥ  
AbhTa dvārapīṭhaguruvrātasamarpitanivedanāt 
AbhTb ṛtenyatsvayamaśnīyādagādhembhasyatha kṣipet  
AbhTa prāṇino jalajāḥ pūrvadīkṣitāḥ śambhunā svayam 
AbhTb vidhinā bhāvinā śrīmanmīnanāthāvatāriṇā  
AbhTa mārjāramūṣikādyairyadadīkṣaiścāpi bhakṣitam 
AbhTb tacchaṅkātaṅkadānena vyādhaye narakāya ca  
AbhTa atastattvavidā dhvastaśaṅkātaṅkopi paṇḍitaḥ 
AbhTb prakaṭaṃ nedṛśaṃ kuryāllokānugrahavāñchayā  
AbhTa śrīmanmatamahāśāstre taduktaṃ vibhunā svayam 
AbhTb svayaṃ tu śaṅkāsaṅkocaniṣkāsanaparāyaṇaḥ  
AbhTa bhavettathā yathānyeṣāṃ śaṅkā no manasi sphuret 
AbhTb mārjayitvā tataḥ snānaṃ puṣpeṇātha prapūjayet  
AbhTa puṣpādi sarvaṃ tatsthaṃ tadagādhāmbhasi nikṣipet 
AbhTb uktaḥ sthaṇḍilayāgoyaṃ nityakarmaṇi śambhunā  
C atha śrītantrāloke saptaviṃśatitamamāhnikam
AbhTb athocyate liṅgapūjā sūcitā mālinīmate  b
AbhTa eteṣāmūrdhvaśāstroktamantrāṇāṃ na pratiṣṭhitam 
AbhTb bahiṣkuryāttato hyete rahasyatvena siddhidāḥ  
AbhTa svavīryānandamāhātmyapraveśavaśaśālinīm 
AbhTb ye siddhiṃ dadate teṣāṃ bāhyatvaṃ rūpavicyutiḥ  
AbhTa kiṃca coktaṃ samāveśapūrṇo bhoktrātmakaḥ śivaḥ 
AbhTb bhogalāmpaṭyabhāgbhogavicchede nigrahātmakaḥ  
AbhTa śāntatvanyakkriyodbhūtajighatsāvṛṃhitaṃ vapuḥ 
AbhTb svayaṃ pratiṣṭhitaṃ yena sosyābhoge vinaśyati  
AbhTa uktaṃ jñānottarāyāṃ ca tadetatparameśinā 
AbhTb śivo yāgapriyo yasmādviśeṣānmātṛmadhyagaḥ  
AbhTa tasmādrahasyaśāstreṣu ye mantrāstānbudho bahiḥ 
AbhTb na pratiṣṭhāpayejjātu viśeṣādvyaktarūpiṇaḥ  
AbhTa ata eva mṛtasyārthe pratiṣṭhānyatra yoditā 
AbhTb sātra śāstreṣu no kāryā kāryā sādhāraṇī punaḥ  
AbhTa ā tanmayatvasaṃsiddherā cābhīṣṭaphalodayāt 
AbhTb putrakaḥ sādhako vyaktamavyaktaṃ vā samāśrayet  
AbhTa putrakairgururabhyarthyaḥ sādhakastu svayaṃ vidan 
AbhTb yadi tatsthāpayenno cettenāpyarthyo gururbhavet  
AbhTa guruścātra nirodhākhye kāla itthaṃ vibhau vadet 
AbhTb jīvatyasminphalāntaṃ tvaṃ tiṣṭherjīvāvadhīti vā  
AbhTa liṅgaṃ ca bāṇaliṅgaṃ vā ratnajaṃ vātha mauktikam 
AbhTb pauṣpamānnamatho vāstraṃ gandhadravyakṛtaṃ ca vā  
AbhTa natu pāṣāṇajaṃ liṅgaṃ śilpyutthaṃ parikalpayet 
AbhTb dhātūtthaṃ ca suvarṇotthavarjamanyadvivarjayet  
AbhTa na cātra liṅgamānādi kvacidapyupayujyate 
AbhTb udāravīryairmantrairyadbhāsitaṃ phaladaṃ hi tat  
AbhTa tasyāpi sthaṇḍilādyuktavidhinā śuddhimācaret 
AbhTb mantrārpaṇaṃ tathaiva syānnirodhastūktayuktitaḥ  
AbhTa agnau ca tarpaṇaṃ bhūriviśeṣāddakṣiṇā guroḥ 
AbhTb dīnāditṛptirvibhavādyāga ityadhiko vidhiḥ  
AbhTa sarveṣvavyaktaliṅgeṣu pradhānaṃ syādakalpitam 
AbhTb tathā ca tatra tatroktaṃ lakṣaṇe pārameśvare  
AbhTa sūtre pātre dhvaje vastre svayambhūbāṇapūjite 
AbhTb nadīprasravaṇotthe ca nāhvānaṃ nāpi kalpanā  
AbhTa pīṭhaprasādamantrāṃśavelādiniyamo naca 
AbhTb vyaktaṃ vā citrapustādau devadārusuvarṇajam  
AbhTa atha dīkṣitasacchilpikṛtaṃ sthāpayate guruḥ 
AbhTb athavā lakṣaṇopetamūrdhatatkarparāśritam  
AbhTa paṅkticakrakaśūlābjavidhinā tūramāśrayet 
AbhTb tallakṣaṇaṃ bruve śrīmatpicuśāstre nirūpitam  
AbhTa tūre yogaḥ sadā śastaḥ siddhido doṣavarjite 
AbhTb jālakairjarjarai randhrairdantairūnādhikai rujā  
AbhTa yukte ca tūre hāniḥ syāt taddhīne yāga uttamaḥ 
AbhTb kāmya eva bhavettūramiti kecitprapedire  
AbhTa guravastu vidhau kāmye yatnāddoṣāṃstyajediti 
AbhTb vyācakṣate picuproktaṃ na nitye karmaṇītyadaḥ  
AbhTa śrīsiddhātantra uktaṃ ca tūralakṣaṇamuttamam 
AbhTb ekādikacatuṣkhaṇḍe gomukhe pūrṇacandrake  
AbhTa padmagorocanāmuktānīrasphaṭikasaṃnibhe 
AbhTb ekādipañcasadrandhravidyārekhānvite śubhe  
AbhTa na rūkṣavakraśakaladīrghanimnasabinduke 
AbhTb ślakṣṇayā vajrasūcyātra sphuṭaṃ devīgaṇānvitam  
AbhTa sarvaṃ samālikhetpūjyaṃ sarvāvayavasundaram 
AbhTb etadevānusartavyamarghapātrepi lakṣaṇam  
AbhTa śrībrahmayāmalepyuktaṃ pātraṃ gomukhamuttamam 
AbhTb gajakūrmatalaṃ kumbhavṛttaśaktikajākṛti  
AbhTa akṣasūtramatho kuryāttatraivābhyarcayetkramam 
AbhTb vīradhātujalodbhūtamuktāratnasuvarṇajam  
AbhTa akṣasūtraṃ kramotkṛṣṭaṃ raudrākṣaṃ vā viśeṣataḥ 
AbhTb śataṃ tithyuttaraṃ yadvā sāṣṭaṃ yadvā tadardhakam  
AbhTa tadardhaṃ vātha pañcāśadyuktaṃ tatparikalpayet 
AbhTb vaktrāṇi pañca citspandajñānecchākṛtisaṃgateḥ  
AbhTa pañcadhādyantagaṃ caikyamityupāntyākṣago vidhiḥ 
AbhTb śaktitadvatprabhedena tatra dvairūpyamucyate  
AbhTa tato dviguṇamāne tu dvirūpaṃ nyāsamācaret 
AbhTb tatopi dviguṇe sṛṣṭisaṃhṛtidvitayena tam  
AbhTa mātṛkāṃ mālinīṃ vātha nyasyetkhaśarasaṃmite 
AbhTb uttame tu dvayīṃ nyasyennyasya pūrvaṃ pracoditān  
AbhTa dīkṣāyāṃ mukhyato mantrāṃstānpañcadaśa daiśikaḥ 
AbhTb yadi vā tattvabhuvanakalāmantrapadārṇajaiḥ  
AbhTa saṃkhyābhedaiḥ kṛte sūtre taṃ taṃ nyāsaṃ guruścaret 
AbhTb kṛtvākṣasūtraṃ tasyāpi sarvaṃ sthaṇḍilavadbhavet  
AbhTa pūjitena ca tenaiva japaṃ kuryādatandritaḥ 
AbhTb vidhiruktastvayaṃ śrīmanmālinīvijayottare  
AbhTa cakravadbhramayannetadyadvakti sa japo bhavet 
AbhTb yadīkṣate juhotyetadbodhāgnau saṃpraveśanāt  
AbhTa athavārghamahāpātraṃ kuryāttaccottaraṃ param 
AbhTb nārikelamatho bailvaṃ sauvarṇaṃ rājataṃ ca vā  
AbhTa tasyāpyeṣa vidhiḥ sarvaḥ pratiṣṭhādau prakīrtitaḥ 
AbhTb tanniṣkamparasaiḥ pūrṇaṃ kṛtvāsminpūjayetkramam  
AbhTa adhomukhaṃ sadā sthāpyaṃ pūjitaṃ pūjane punaḥ 
AbhTb tatpātramunmukhaṃ tacca riktaṃ kuryānna tādṛśam
