AbhTa pūjānte tadrasāpūrṇamātmānaṃ pravidhāya tat 
AbhTb adhomukhaṃ ca saṃpūjya sthāpayet vicakṣaṇaḥ  
AbhTa khaṅgaṃ kṛpāṇikāṃ yadvā kartarīṃ makuraṃ ca vā 
AbhTb vimalaṃ tattathā kuryācchrīmatkālīmukhoditam  
AbhTa śrībhairavakulepyuktaṃ kulaparvaprapūjane 
AbhTb sthaṇḍilegnau paṭe liṅge pātre padmetha maṇḍale  
AbhTa mūrtau ghaṭestrasaṃghāte dhaṭe sūtretha pūjayet 
AbhTb svena svenopacāreṇa saṅkaraṃ varjayediti  
AbhTa yathāpsu śāntaye mantrāstadvadastrādiṣu dhruvam 
AbhTb śatrucchedādikartāraḥ kāmyotaḥ saṅkarojjhitaḥ  
AbhTa akāmasya tu te tattatsthānopādhivaśāddhruvam 
AbhTb pāśakartanasaṃśuddhatattvāpyāyādikāriṇaḥ  
AbhTa athavā pustakaṃ tādṛgrahaḥśāstrakramombhitam 
AbhTb suśuddhaṃ dīkṣitakṛtaṃ tatrāpyeṣa vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ  
AbhTa itthaṃ svayaṃpratiṣṭheṣu yāvadyāvatsthitirbhavet 
AbhTb vibhavaistarpaṇaṃ śuddhistāvadvicchedavarjanam  
AbhTa ata eva yadā bhūridinaṃ maṇḍalakalpanam 
AbhTb tadā dine dine kuryādvibhavaistarpaṇaṃ bahu  
AbhTa pratiṣṭhāyāṃ ca sarvatra guruḥ pūrvoditaṃ param 
AbhTb satattvamanusandhāya saṃnidhiṃ sphuṭamācaret  
AbhTa siddhe tu tanmayībhāve phale putrakasādhakaiḥ 
AbhTb anyasmai taddvayādanyatarasmai tatsamarpyate  
AbhTa tasyāpyeṣa vidhiḥ sarvastadalābhe tu sarvathā 
AbhTb agādhembhasi tatkṣepyaṃ kṣamayitvā visṛjya ca  
AbhTa ityeṣa svapratiṣṭhānavidhiḥ śivanirūpitaḥ 
AbhTb parapratiṣṭhite liṅge bāṇīyetha svayaṃbhuvi  
AbhTa sarvamāsanapakṣe prāṅnyasya saṃpūjayetkramam 
AbhTb śuddhāśuddhādhvajāḥ sarve mantrāḥ sarvaḥ śivāntakaḥ  
AbhTa adhvā cehāsane proktastatsarvatrārcayedidam 
AbhTb āvāhanavisṛṣṭī tu tatra prāgvatsamācaret  
AbhTa uktaṃ tantrepyaghoreśe svacchande vibhunā tathā 
AbhTb athavā pratyahaṃ proktamānārdhārdhaniyogataḥ  
AbhTa kṛtveṣṭaṃ maṇḍalaṃ tatra samastaṃ kramamarcayet 
AbhTb bahuprakārabhinnasya liṅgasyārcā nirūpitā  
C atha śrītantrāloke aṣṭāviṃśamāhnikam
AbhTb iti nityavidhiḥ prokto naimittikamathocyate  b
AbhTa niyataṃ bhāvi yannityaṃ tadityasminvidhau sthite 
AbhTb mukhyatvaṃ tanmayībhūtiḥ sarvaṃ naimittikaṃ tataḥ  
AbhTa dinādikalpanotthe tu naiyatye sarvanityatā 
AbhTb dinamāsarkṣavarṣādinaiyatyāducyate tadā  
AbhTa aśaṅkitavyāvaśyantāsattākaṃ jātucidbhavam 
AbhTb pramātraniyataṃ prāhurnaimittikamidaṃ budhāḥ  
AbhTa sandhyādi parvasaṃpūjā pavitrakamidaṃ sadā 
AbhTb nityaṃ niyatarūpatvātsarvasmin śāsanāśrite  
AbhTa jñānaśāstragurubhrātṛtadvargaprāptayastathā 
AbhTb tajjanmasaṃskriyābhedāḥ svajanmotsavasaṃgatiḥ  
AbhTa śrāddhaṃ vipatpratīkāraḥ pramododbhutadarśanam 
AbhTb yoginīmelakaḥ svāṃśasantānādyaiśca melanam  
AbhTa śāstravyākhyāpurāmadhyāvasānāni kramodayaḥ 
AbhTb devatādarśanaṃ svāpnamājñā samayaniṣkṛtiḥ  
AbhTa iti naimittikaṃ śrīmattantrasāre nirūpitam 
AbhTb trayoviṃśatibhedena viśeṣārcānibandhanam  
AbhTa tatra parvavidhiṃ brūmo dvidhā parva kulākulam 
AbhTb kulāṣṭakakṛtaṃ pūrvaṃ proktaṃ śrīyogasaṃcare  
AbhTa abdhīndu munirityetanmāheśyā brahmasantateḥ 
AbhTb pratipatpañcadaśyau dve kaumāryā rasavahniyuk  
AbhTa abdhirakṣīndu vaiṣṇavyā aindryāstvastraṃ trayodaśī 
AbhTb vārāhyā randhrarudrau dve caṇḍyā vasvakṣiyugmakam  
AbhTa dve dve tithī tu sarvāsāṃ yogeśyā daśamī punaḥ 
AbhTb tasyā apyaṣṭamī yasmāddvitithiḥ sā prakīrtitā  
AbhTa anyāścākulaparvāpi vaiparītyena lakṣitam 
AbhTb kulaparveti tadbrūmo yathoktaṃ bhairave kule  
AbhTa haiḍare trikasadbhāve trikakālīkulādike 
AbhTb yoyaṃ prāṇāśritaḥ pūrvaṃ kālaḥ proktaḥ suvistarāt  
AbhTa sa cakrabhedasaṃcāre kāṃcit sūte svasaṃvidam 
AbhTb svasaṃvitpūrṇatālābhasamayaḥ parva bhaṇyate  
AbhTa parva pūraṇa ityeva yadvā pṝ pūraṇārthakaḥ 
AbhTb parvaśabdo niruktaśca parva tatpūraṇāditi  
AbhTa haiḍaretra ca śabdoyaṃ dvidhā nāntetaraḥ śrutaḥ 
AbhTb taccakracāraniṣṇātā ye kecit pūrṇasaṃvidaḥ  
AbhTa tanmelakasamāyuktāste tatpūjāparāḥ sadā 
AbhTb yopyatanmaya eṣopi tatkāle svakramārcanāt  
AbhTa tadyoginīsiddhasaṅghamelakāt tanmayībhavet 
AbhTb yathā prekṣaṇake tattaddraṣṭṛsaṃvidabheditām  
AbhTa kramoditāṃ sadya eva labhate tatpraveśanāt 
AbhTb yogābhyāsakramopāttāṃ tathā pūrṇāṃ svasaṃvidam  
AbhTa labhante sadya evaitatsaṃvidaikyapraveśanāt 
AbhTb tatkālaṃ cāpi saṃvitteḥ pūrṇatvāt kāmadogdhṛtā  
AbhTa tena tattatphalaṃ tatra kāle saṃpūjayācirāt 
AbhTb yathā ciropāttadhanaḥ kurvannutsavamādarāt  
AbhTa atithiṃ sonugṛhṇāti tatkālābhijñamāgatam 
AbhTb tathā suphalasaṃsiddhyai yoginīsiddhanāyakāḥ  
AbhTa yatnavantopi tatkālābhijñaṃ tamanugṛhṇate 
AbhTb uktaṃ ca tatra teneha kule sāmānyatetyalam  
AbhTa yasya yaddhṛdaye devi vartate daiśikājñayā 
AbhTb mantro yogaḥ kramaścaiva pūjanāt siddhido bhavet  
AbhTa kulācāreṇa deveśi pūjyaṃ siddhivimuktaye 
AbhTb ye parvasveṣu deveśi tarpaṇaṃ tu viśeṣataḥ  
AbhTa gurūṇāṃ devatānāṃ ca na kurvanti pramādataḥ 
AbhTb durācārā hi te duṣṭāḥ paśutulyā varānane  
AbhTa abhāvānnityapūjāyā avaśyaṃ hyeṣu pūjayet 
AbhTb aṭanaṃ jñānaśaktyādilābhārthaṃ yatprakīrtitam  
AbhTa śaktiyāgaśca yaḥ prokto vaśyākarṣaṇamāraṇam 
AbhTb tatsarvaṃ parvadivaseṣvayatnenaiva siddhyati  
AbhTa tatsāmānyaviśeṣābhyāṃ ṣoḍhā parva nirūpitam 
AbhTb māsasyādyaṃ pañcamaṃ ca śrīdinaṃ paribhāṣyate  
AbhTa utkṛṣṭatvāt parvadinaṃ śrīpūrvatvena bhāṣyate 
AbhTb samayo hyeṣa yadguptaṃ tannānupapadaṃ vadet  
AbhTa turyāṣṭamānyabhuvanacaramāṇi dvayorapi 
AbhTb pakṣayoriha sāmānyasāmānyaṃ parva kīrtitam  
AbhTa yadeteṣu dineṣveva bhaviṣyadgrahabhātmakaḥ 
AbhTb ubhayātmā viśeṣaḥ syāttatsāmānyaviśeṣatā  
AbhTa sā caikādaśadhaikasminnekasminvibhunoditā 
AbhTb sajātīyā tu sotkṛṣṭetyevaṃ śambhurnyarūpayat  
AbhTa kṛṣṇayugaṃ vahnisitaṃ śrutikṛṣṇaṃ vahnisitamiti pakṣāḥ 
AbhTb arkendujīvacandrā budhayugmendvarkakaviguruvidhu syāt  
AbhTa paraphalguścaitramaghe tiṣyaḥ prākphalgukarṇaśatabhiṣajaḥ 
AbhTb mūlaprājāpatye viśākhikā śravaṇasaṃjñayā bhāni  
AbhTa randhre tithyarkapare vasurandhre śaśivṛṣāṅkarasarandhrayugam 
AbhTb prathamaniśāmadhyaniśe madhyāhnaśarā dinodayo madhyadinam  
AbhTa prathamaniśeti ca samayo mārgaśiraḥprabhṛtimāseṣu 
AbhTb kanyāntyajātha veśyā rāgavatī tattvavedinī dūtī  
AbhTa vyāsasamāsāt kramaśaḥ pūjyāścakrenuyāgākhye 
AbhTb sarvatra ca parvadine kuryādanuyāgacakramatiśayataḥ  
AbhTa guptāguptavidhānādiyāgacaryākrameṇa sampūrṇam 
AbhTb anuyāgaḥ kila mukhyaḥ sarvasminneva karmaviniyoge  
AbhTa anuyāgakālalābhe tasmātprayateta tatparamaḥ 
AbhTb bhagrahasamayaviśeṣo nāśvayuje kopi tena tadvarjam  
AbhTa velābhagrahakalanā kathitaikādaśasu māseṣu 
AbhTb phālgunamāse śuklaṃ yatproktaṃ dvādaśīdinaṃ parva  
AbhTa agratithivedhayogo mukhyatamosau viśeṣotra 
AbhTb divasaniśe kila kṛtvā tribhāgaśaḥ prathamamadhyamāparavibhāgaḥ  
AbhTa pūjākālastatra tribhāgite mukhyatamaḥ kālaḥ 
AbhTb yadi saṃghaṭeta velā mukhyatamā bhagrahau tathā cakram  
AbhTa tadyāga ādiyāgastatkāmyaṃ pūjayaiva parvasu siddhyet 
AbhTb dinavelābhagrahakalpanena tatrāpi saumyaraudratvam  
AbhTa jñātvā sādhakamukhyastattatkāryaṃ tadā tadā kuryāt 
AbhTb ukto yorcākālastaṃ cedullaṅghya bhagrahatithiḥ syāt  
AbhTa tamanādṛtya viśeṣaṃ pradhānayetsāmayamiti kecit 
AbhTb neti tvasmadguravo viśeṣarūpā hi tithiriha na velā  
AbhTa saṃvedyarūpaśaśadharabhāgaḥ saṃvedakārkakaranikaraiḥ 
AbhTb yāvānyāvati pūrṇaḥ sā hi tithirbhagrahaiḥ sphuṭībhavati  
AbhTa tasmānmukhyātra tithiḥ sā ca viśeṣyā graharkṣayogena 
AbhTb velātra na pradhānaṃ yuktaṃ caitattathāhi parameśaḥ  
AbhTa śrītrikabhairavakulaśāstreṣūce na parvadivaseṣu 
AbhTb velāyogaṃ kaṃcana tithibhagrahayogato hyanyam  
AbhTa tithistu pūjyā pradhānarūpatvāt 
AbhTb śvetābhāve kṛṣṇacchāgālambhaṃ hi kathayanti  
AbhTa yatpunarūrmiprabhṛtini śāstre veloditāpi tatkāmyam 
AbhTb mukhyatayoddiśya vidhiṃ tathāca tatra pauṣaparvadine  
AbhTa kṛtvārcanamardhaniśi dhyātvā japtvā bahirgatasya yathā 
AbhTb ādeśaḥ phalati tathā māghe cakrādvacaḥ phalati  
AbhTa acirādabhīṣṭasiddhiḥ pañcasu maitrī dhanaṃ ca melāpaḥ 
AbhTb cakrasthāne krodhāt pāṣāṇasphoṭanena ripunāśaḥ  
AbhTa siddhādeśaprāptirmārgāntaṃ kathyate vibhunā 
AbhTb bhagrahayogābhāve velāṃ tu titheravaśyamīkṣeta  
AbhTa sā hi tathā sphuṭarūpā titheḥ svabhāvodayaṃ dadyāt 
AbhTb bhagrahatithivelāṃśānuyāyi sarvāṅgasundaraṃ tu dinam  
AbhTa yadi labhyeta tadāsminviśeṣatamapūjanaṃ racayet 
AbhTb naca kāmyameva kevalametatparivarjane yataḥ kathitaḥ  
AbhTa samayavilopaḥ śrīmadbhairavakula ūrmiśāstre ca 
AbhTb duṣṭā hi durācārāḥ paśutulyāḥ parva ye na viduḥ  
AbhTa naca kāmyasyākaraṇe syājjātu pratyavāyitvam 
AbhTb tatrānuyāgasiddhyarthaṃ cakrayāgo nirūpyate  
AbhTa mūrtiyāga iti prokto yaḥ śrīyogīśvarīmate 
AbhTb nityaṃ naimittikaṃ karma yadatroktaṃ maheśinā  
AbhTa sarvatra cakrayāgotra mukhyaḥ kāmye viśeṣataḥ 
AbhTb jñānī yogī ca puruṣaḥ strī vāsminmūrtisaṃjñake  
AbhTa yoge prayatnato yojyastaddhi pātramanuttaram 
AbhTb tatsaṃparkātpūrṇatā syāditi traiśirasādiṣu  
AbhTa tena sarvaṃ hutaṃ ceṣṭaṃ trailokyaṃ sacarācaram 
AbhTb jñānine yogine vāpi yo dadāti karoti vā  
AbhTa dīkṣottarepi ca proktamannaṃ brahmā raso hariḥ 
AbhTb bhoktā śiva iti jñānī śvapacānapyathoddhareat  
AbhTa sarvatattvamayo bhūtvā yadi bhuṅkte sa sādhakaḥ 
AbhTb tena bhojitamātreṇa sakṛtkoṭistu bhojitā  
AbhTa atha tattvavidetasminyadi bhuñjīta tat priye 
AbhTb parisaṃkhyā na vidyeta tadāha bhagavāñchivaḥ  
AbhTa bhojyaṃ māyātmakaṃ sarvaṃ śivo bhoktā sa cāpyaham 
AbhTb evaṃ yo vai vijānāti daiśikastattvapāragaḥ  
AbhTa taṃ dṛṣṭvā devamāyāntaṃ krīḍantyoṣadhayo gṛhe 
AbhTb nivṛttamadyaivāsmābhiḥ saṃsāragahanārṇavāt  
AbhTa yadasya vaktraṃ saṃprāptā yāsyāmaḥ paramaṃ padam 
AbhTb anyepānabhujo hyūrdhve prāṇopānastvadhomukhaḥ  
AbhTa tasminbhoktari deveśi dātuḥ kulaśatānyapi 
AbhTb āśveva parimucyante narakādyātanārṇavāt  
AbhTa śrīmanniśāṭanepyuktaṃ kathanānveṣaṇādapi 
AbhTb śrotrābhyantarasaṃprāpte guruvaktrādvinirgate  
AbhTa muktastadaiva kāle tu yantraṃ tiṣṭhati kevalam 
AbhTb surāpaḥ steyahārī ca brahmahā gurutalpagaḥ  
AbhTa antyajo vā dvijo vātha bālo vṛddho yuvāpi vā 
AbhTb paryantavāsī yo jñānī deśasyāpi pavitrakaḥ  
AbhTa tatra saṃnihito devaḥ sadevīkaḥ sakiṅkaraḥ 
AbhTb tasmātprādhānyataḥ kṛtvā guruṃ jñānaviśāradam  
AbhTa mūrtiyāgaṃ carettasya vidhiryogīśvarīmate 
AbhTb pavitrārohaṇe śrāddhe tathā parvadineṣvalam  
AbhTa sūryacandroparāgādau laukikeṣvapi parvasu 
AbhTb utsave ca vivāhādau viprāṇāṃ yajñakarmaṇi  
AbhTa dīkṣāyāṃ ca pratiṣṭhāyāṃ samayānāṃ viśodhane 
AbhTb kāmanārthaṃ ca kartavyo mūrtiyāgaḥ sa pañcadhā  
AbhTa kevalo yāmalo miśraścakrayugvīrasaṅkaraḥ 
AbhTb kevalaḥ kevalaireva gurubhirmiśritaḥ punaḥ  
AbhTa sādhakādyaiḥ sapatnīkairyāmalaḥ sa dvidhā punaḥ 
AbhTb patnīyogāt krayānītaveśyāsaṃyogatothavā  
AbhTa cakriṇyādyāśca vakṣyante śaktiyogādyathocitāḥ 
AbhTb tatsaṃyogāccakrayukto yāgaḥ sarvaphalapradaḥ  
AbhTa sarvaistu sahito yāgo vīrasaṅkara ucyate 
AbhTb madhye gururbhavetteṣāṃ guruvargastadāvṛtiḥ  
AbhTa tisra āvṛtayo bāhye samayyantā yathākramam 
AbhTb paṅktikrameṇa vā sarve madhye teṣāṃ guruḥ sadā  
AbhTa tadā tadgandhadhūpasraksamālambhanavāsasā 
AbhTb pūjyaṃ cakrānusāreṇa tattaccakramidaṃ tviti  
AbhTa ekārake yathā cakre ekavīravidhiṃ smaret 
AbhTb dvyare yāmalamanyatra trikamevaṃ ṣaḍasrake  
AbhTa ṣaḍyoginīḥ saptakaṃ ca saptāreṣṭāṣṭake ca vā 
AbhTb anyadvā tādṛśaṃ tatra cakre tādṛksvarūpiṇi  
AbhTa tataḥ pātrelisaṃpūrṇe pūrvaṃ cakraṃ yajetsudhīḥ 
AbhTb ādhārayukte nādhārarahitaṃ tarpaṇaṃ kvacit  
AbhTa ādhāreṇa vinā bhraṃśo naca tuṣyanti raśmayaḥ 
AbhTb pretarūpaṃ bhavetpātraṃ śāktāmṛtamathāsavaḥ  
AbhTa bhoktrī tatra tu yā śaktiḥ sa śambhuḥ parameśvaraḥ 
AbhTb aṇuśaktiśivātmetthaṃ dhyātvā saṃmilitaṃ trayam  
AbhTa tatastu tarpaṇaṃ kāryamāvṛterāvṛteḥ kramāt 
AbhTb pratisaṃcarayogena punarantaḥ praveśayet  
AbhTa yāvadgurvantikaṃ taddhi pūrṇaṃ bhramaṇamucyate 
AbhTb tatrādau devatāstarpyāstato vīrā iti kramaḥ  
AbhTa vīraśca vīraśaktiścetyevamasmadgurukramaḥ 
AbhTb tatovadaṃśānvividhān māṃsamatsyādisaṃyutān  
AbhTa agre tatra pravikiret tṛptyantaṃ sādhakottamaḥ 
AbhTb pātrābhāve punarbhadraṃ vellitāśuktimeva ca  
AbhTa pātre kurvīta matimāniti siddhāmate kramaḥ 
AbhTb dakṣahastena bhadraṃ syādvellitā śuktirucyate  
AbhTa dakṣahastasya kurvīta vāmopari kanīyasīm 
AbhTb tarjanyaṅguṣṭhayogena dakṣādho vāmakāṅgulīḥ  
AbhTa niḥsandhibandhau dvāvitthaṃ vellitā śuktirucyate 
AbhTb ye tatra pānakāle tu bindavo yānti medinīm  
AbhTa taistuṣyanti hi vetālaguhyakādyā gabhastayaḥ 
AbhTb dhārayā bhairavastuṣyet karapānaṃ paraṃ tataḥ  
AbhTa praveśotra na dātavyaḥ pūrvameva hi kasyacit 
AbhTb pramādāttu praviṣṭasya vicāraṃ naiva carcayet  
AbhTa evaṃ kṛtvā kramādyāgamante dakṣiṇayā yutam 
AbhTb samālambhanatāmbūlavastrādyaṃ vitaredbudhaḥ  
AbhTa rūpakārdhāt paraṃ hīnāṃ na dadyāddakṣiṇāṃ sudhīḥ 
AbhTb samayibhyaḥ kramāddvidviguṇā gurvantakaṃ bhavet  
AbhTa eṣa syānmūrtiyāgastu sarvayāgapradhānakaḥ 
AbhTb kāmye tu saṃvidhau saptakṛtvaḥ kāryastathāvidhaḥ  
AbhTa jānanti prathamaṃ gehaṃ tatastasya samarthatām 
AbhTb balābalaṃ tataḥ paścādvismayantetra mātaraḥ  
AbhTa tatopi saṃnidhīyante prīyante varadāstataḥ 
AbhTb devīnāmatha nāthasya parivārayujopyalam  
AbhTa vallabho mūrtiyāgoyamataḥ kāryo vipaścitā 
AbhTb rāktau gupte gṛhe vīrāḥ śaktayonyonyamapyalam  
AbhTa asaṃketayujo yojyā devatāśabdakīrtanāt 
AbhTb alābhe mūrticakrasya kumārīreva pūjayet  
AbhTa kāmyārthe tu na tāṃ vyaṅgāṃ stanapuṣpavatīṃ tathā 
AbhTb pratipacchrutisaṃjñe ca caturthī cottarātraye  
AbhTa haste ca pañcamī ṣaṣṭhī pūrvāsvatha punarvasau 
AbhTb saptamī tatparā pitrye rohiṇyāṃ navamī tathā  
AbhTa mūle tu dvādaśī brāhme bhūtāśvinyāṃ ca pūrṇimā 
AbhTb dhaniṣṭhāyāmamāvasyā soyamekādaśātmakaḥ  
AbhTa arkāditrayaśukrānyatamayuktopyahargaṇaḥ 
AbhTb yogaparveti vikhyāto rātrau vā dina eva vā  
AbhTa yogaparvaṇi kartavyo mūrtiyāgastu sarvathā 
AbhTb yaḥ sarvānyogaparvākhyān vāsarān pūjayetsudhīḥ  
AbhTa mūrtiyāgena sopi syāt samayī maṇḍalaṃ vinā 
AbhTb ityeṣa mūrtiyāgaḥ śrīsiddhayogīśvarīmate  
AbhTa athocyate śivenoktaḥ pavitrakavidhiḥ sphuṭaḥ 
AbhTb śrīratnamālātriśiraḥśāstrayoḥ sūcitaḥ punaḥ  
AbhTa śrīsiddhāṭanasadbhāvamālinīsāraśāsane 
AbhTb tatra prādhānyataḥ śrīmanmālokto vidhirucyate  
AbhTa kṣīrābdhimathanodbhūtaviṣanidrāvimūrcchitaḥ 
AbhTb nāgarājaḥ svabhuvane meghakāle sma nāvasat  
AbhTa kevalaṃ tu pavitroyaṃ vāyubhakṣaḥ samāḥ śatam 
AbhTb divyaṃ daśaguṇaṃ nāthaṃ bhairavaṃ paryapūjayat  
AbhTa vyajijñapacca taṃ tuṣṭaṃ nāthaṃ varṣāsvahaṃ nije 
AbhTb pātāle nāsituṃ śaktaḥ sopyenaṃ parameśvaraḥ  
AbhTa nāgaṃ nijajaṭājūṭapīṭhagaṃ paryakalpayat 
AbhTb tataḥ samastadevaughairdhāritosau svamūrdhani  
AbhTa mahatāṃ mahitānāṃ hi nādbhuta viśvapūjyatā 
AbhTb tasmānmaheśiturmūrdhni devatānāṃ ca sarvaśaḥ  
AbhTa ātmanaśca pavitraṃ taṃ kuryādyāgapuraḥsaram 
AbhTb daśa koṭyo na pūjānāṃ pavitrārohaṇe samāḥ  
AbhTa vṛthā dīkṣā vṛthā jñānaṃ gurvārādhanameva ca 
AbhTb vinā pavitrādyenaitaddharennāgaḥ śivājñayā  
AbhTa tasmātsarvaprayatnena sa kāryaḥ kulavedibhiḥ 
AbhTb āṣāḍhaśuklānmithunakarkaṭasthe ravau vidhiḥ  
AbhTa kartavyaḥ sonirodhena yāvatsā tulapūrṇimā 
AbhTb tulopalakṣitasyāntyaṃ kārtikasya dinaṃ matam  
AbhTa kulaśabdaṃ paṭhantonye vyākhyābhedaṃ prakurvate 
AbhTb nityātantravidaḥ kṛṣṇaṃ kārtikāccaramaṃ dinam  
AbhTa kulasya nityācakrasya pūrṇatvaṃ yatra tanmatam 
AbhTb māghaśuklāntyadivasaḥ kulaparveti tanmatam  
AbhTa pūrṇatvaṃ tatra candrasya sā tithiḥ kulapūrṇimā 
AbhTb dakṣiṇottaragaḥ kālaḥ kulākulatayoditaḥ  
AbhTa kulasya tasya carame dine pūrṇatvamucyate 
AbhTb dakṣiṇāyanaṣaṇmāsakartavyatvamato vidhau  
AbhTa pavitrake prakāśatvasiddhyai kṛṣṇasya vartmanaḥ 
AbhTb tadetadbahuśāstroktaṃ rūpaṃ devo nyarūpayat  
AbhTa ekenaiva padena śrīratnamālākulāgame 
AbhTb tadatra samaye sarvavidhisaṃpūraṇātmakaḥ  
AbhTa pavitrakavidhiḥ kāryaḥ śuklapakṣe tu sarvathā 
AbhTb pūraṇaṃ śaktiyogena śaktyātma ca sitaṃ dalam  
AbhTa dakṣiṇāyanasājātyāt tena tadvidhirucyate 
AbhTb ekadvitricatuḥpañcaṣaḍlataikatamaṃ mahat  
AbhTa hemaratnāṅkitagranthi kuryānmuktāpavitrakam 
AbhTb sauvarṇasūtraṃ triguṇaṃ saikagranthiśataṃ gurau  
AbhTa pare gurau tu tryadhikamadhyabdhi parameṣṭhini 
AbhTb prāksiddhācāryayogeśa viṣaye tu rasādhikam  
AbhTa aṣṭādhikaṃ śivasyoktaṃ citraratnaprapūritam 
AbhTb vidyāpīṭhākṣasūtrādau guruvacchivavat punaḥ  
AbhTa vaṭuke kanakābhāve raupyaṃ tu parikalpayet 
AbhTb pāṭṭasūtramatha kṣaumaṃ kārpāsaṃ tritritānitam  
AbhTa tasmānnavaguṇāt sūtrāttriguṇādikramāt kuru 
AbhTb caṇḍāṃśuguṇaparyantaṃ tatopi triguṇaṃ ca vā  
AbhTa tenāṣṭādaśatantūtthamadhamaṃ madhyamaṃ punaḥ 
AbhTb aṣṭottaraśataṃ tasmāt triguṇaṃ tūttamaṃ matam  
AbhTa granthayastattvasaṃkhyātāḥ ṣaḍadhvakalanāvaśāt 
AbhTb yadvā vyāsasamāsābhyāṃ citrāḥ sadgandhapūritāḥ  
AbhTa viśeṣavidhinā pūrvaṃ pūjayitvārpayettataḥ 
AbhTb pavitrakaṃ samastādhvaparipūrṇatvabhāvanāt  
AbhTa gurvātmanorjānunābhikaṇṭhamūrdhāntagaṃ ca vā 
AbhTb tato mahotsavaḥ kāryo gurupūjāpuraḥsaraḥ  
AbhTa tarpyāḥ śāsanagāḥ sarve dakṣiṇāvastrabhojanaiḥ 
AbhTb mahotsavaḥ prakartavyo gītanṛttātmako mahān  
AbhTa cāturmāsyaṃ saptadinaṃ tridinaṃ vāpyalābhataḥ 
AbhTb tadante kṣamayeddevaṃ maṇḍalādi visarjayet  
AbhTa vahniṃ ca paścātkartavyaścakrayāgaḥ puroditaḥ 
AbhTb māse māse caturmāse varṣe vāpi pavitrakam  
AbhTa sarvathaiva prakartavyaṃ yathāvibhavavistaram 
AbhTb vittābhāve punaḥ kāryaṃ kāśairapi kuśombhitaiḥ  
AbhTa sati vitte punaḥ śāṭhyaṃ vyādhaye narakāya ca 
AbhTb nityapūjāsu pūrṇatvaṃ parvapūjāprapūraṇāt  
AbhTa tatrāpi paripūrṇatvaṃ pavitrakasamarcanāt 
AbhTb pavitrakavilope tu prāyaścittaṃ japetsudhīḥ  
AbhTa suśuddhaḥ sanpunaḥ kuryādityājñā parameśituḥ 
AbhTb atha triśirasi prokto likhyate tadvidhiḥ sphuṭaḥ  
AbhTa triprameyasya śaivasya pañcapañcātmakasya vā 
AbhTb daśāṣṭādaśabhedasya ṣaṭsrotasa ihocyate  
AbhTa ye narāḥ samayabhraṣṭā guruśāstrādidūṣakāḥ 
AbhTb nityanaimittikādyanyaparvasandhivivarjitāḥ  
AbhTa akāmāt kāmato vāpi sūkṣmapāpapravartinaḥ 
AbhTb teṣāṃ praśamanārthāya pavitraṃ kriyate śive  
AbhTa śrāvaṇādau kārtikānte śuklapakṣe śubhaprade 
AbhTb natu duḥkhaprade kṛṣṇe kartṛrāṣṭranṛpādiṣu  
AbhTa pāṭṭasūtraṃ tu kauśeyaṃ kārpāsaṃ kṣaumameva ca 
AbhTb cāturāśramikāṇāṃ tu subhruvā kartitokṣitam  
AbhTa tridhā tu triguṇīkṛtya mānasaṃkhyāṃ tu kārayet 
AbhTb aṣṭottaraṃ tantuśataṃ tadardhaṃ vā tadardhakam  
AbhTa hrāsastu pūrvasaṃkhyāyā daśabhirdaśabhiḥ kramāt 
AbhTb navabhiḥ pañcabhiḥ saptaviṃśatyā vā śivāditaḥ  
AbhTa yādṛśastantuvinyāso granthīnkuryāttu tāvataḥ 
AbhTb catuḥsamaviliptāṃstānathavā kuṅkumena tu  
AbhTa vyakte jānutaṭāntaṃ syālliṅge pīṭhāvasānakam 
AbhTb arcāsu śobhanaṃ mūrghni tritattvaparikalpanāt  
AbhTa dvādaśagranthiśaktīnāṃ brahmavaktrārciṣāmapi 
AbhTb vidyāpīṭhe cale liṅge sthaṇḍile ca gurorgaṇe  
AbhTa ghaṇṭāyāṃ sruksruve śiṣyaliṅgiṣu dvāratoraṇe 
AbhTb svadehe vahnipīṭhe ca yathāśobhaṃ tadiṣyate  
AbhTa prāsāde yāgagehe ca kārayennavaraṅgikam 
AbhTb vidyāpīṭhe tu khaśarāḥ pratimāliṅgapīṭhagam  
AbhTa vasuvedaṃ ca ghaṇṭāyāṃ śarākṣyaṣṭādaśa sruve 
AbhTb vedākṣi sruci ṣaṭtriṃśat prāsāde maṇḍape raviḥ  
AbhTa rasendu snānagehebdhinetre dhyānagṛhe gurau 
AbhTb sapta sādhakagāḥ pañca putrake sapta sāmaye  
AbhTa catvārothānyaśāstrasthe śiṣye pañcakamucyate 
AbhTb liṅgināṃ kevalo granthistoraṇe daśa kalpayet  
AbhTa dvāreṣvaṣṭau granthayaḥ syuḥ kṛtvetthaṃ tu pavitrakam 
AbhTb pūjayitvā mantrajālaṃ tatsthatvātmasthate tataḥ  
AbhTa pavitrakāṇāṃ saṃpādya kuryātsaṃpātasaṃskriyām 
AbhTb tataḥ saṃvatsaraṃ dhyāyedbhairavaṃ chidrasākṣiṇam  
AbhTa dattvā pūrṇāhutiṃ devi praṇamenmantrabhairavam 
AbhTb oṃ samastakriyādoṣapūraṇeśa vrataṃ prati  
AbhTa yatkiṃcidakṛtaṃ duṣṭaṃ kṛtaṃ vā mātṛnandana 
AbhTb tatsarvaṃ mama deveśa tvatprasādātpraṇaśyatu  
AbhTa sarvathā raśmicakreśa namastubhyaṃ prasīda me 
AbhTb anena dadyāddevāya nimantraṇapavitrakam  
AbhTa yoginīkṣetramātṝṇāṃ baliṃ dadyāttato guruḥ 
AbhTb pañcagavyaṃ caruṃ dantakāṣṭhaṃ śiṣyaiḥ samantataḥ  
AbhTa ācārya nidrāṃ kurvīta prātarutthāya cāhnikam 
AbhTb tato vidhiṃ pūjayitvā pavitrāṇi samāharet  
AbhTa dantakāṣṭhaṃ mṛcca dhātrī samṛddhātrī sahāmbunā 
AbhTb catuḥsamaṃ ca taiḥ sārdhaṃ bhasma pañcasu yojayet  
AbhTa prāgdakṣapaścimordhvasthavāmavaktreṣu vai kramāt 
AbhTb pañcaitāni pavitrāṇi sthāpayecceśagocare  
AbhTa kuśedhma pañcagavyaṃ ca śarvāgre viniyojayet 
AbhTb vāmāmṛtādisaṃyuktaṃ naivedyaṃ trividhaṃ tataḥ  
AbhTa dadyādasṛk tathā madyaṃ pānāni vividhāni ca 
AbhTb tato homo mahākṣmājamāṃsaistilayutairatho  
AbhTa tilairghṛtayutairyadvā taṇḍulairatha dhānyakaiḥ 
AbhTb śarkarākhaṇḍasaṃyuktapañcāmṛtapariplutaiḥ  
AbhTa mūlaṃ sahasraṃ sāṣṭoktaṃ triśaktau brahmavaktrakam 
AbhTb arciṣāṃ tu śataṃ sāṣṭaṃ tataḥ pūrṇāhutiṃ kṣipet  
AbhTa tatoñjalau pavitraṃ tu gṛhītvā prapaṭhedidam 
AbhTb akāmādathavā kāmādyanmayā na kṛtaṃ vibho  
AbhTa tadacchidraṃ mamāstvīśa pavitreṇa tavājñayā 
AbhTb mūlamantraḥ pūrayeti kriyāniyamamityatha  
AbhTa vauṣaḍantaṃ pavitraṃ ca dadyādbindvavasānakam 
AbhTb nādāntaṃ samanāntaṃ cāpyunmanāntaṃ kramāttrayam  
AbhTa evaṃ catuṣṭayaṃ dadyādanulomena bhautikaḥ 
AbhTb naiṣṭhikastu vilomena pavitrakacatuṣṭayam  
AbhTa yatkiñcidvividhaṃ vastracchatrālaṅkaraṇādikam 
AbhTb tannivedyaṃ dīpamālāḥ suvarṇatilabhājanam  
AbhTa vastrayugmayutaṃ sarvasampūraṇanimittataḥ 
AbhTb bhojanīyāḥ pūjanīyāḥ śivabhaktāstu śaktitaḥ  
AbhTa catustridvyekamāsādidinaikāntaṃ mahotsavam 
AbhTb kuryāttato na vrajeyuranyasthānaṃ kadācana  
AbhTa tatastu daiśikaḥ pūjyo gāmasmai kṣīriṇīṃ navām 
AbhTb dadyātsuvarṇaratnādirupyavastravibhūṣitām  
AbhTa vadedguruśca saṃpūrṇo vidhistava bhavatviti 
AbhTb vaktavyaṃ devadevasya punarāgamanāya ca  
AbhTa tato visarjanaṃ kāryaṃ guptamābharaṇādikam 
AbhTb naivedyaṃ gururādāya yāgārthe tanniyojayet  
AbhTa caturṇāmapi sāmānyaṃ pavitrakamiti smṛtam 
AbhTb nāsmādvrataṃ paraṃ kiñcit kā vāsya stutirucyate  
AbhTa śeṣaṃ tvagādhe vāryoghe kṣipenna sthāpayetsthiram 
AbhTb atha naimittikavidhiryaḥ purāsūtrito mayā  
AbhTa sa bhaṇyate tatra kāryā devasyārcā viśeṣataḥ 
AbhTb cakrayāgaśca kartavyaḥ pūrvoktavidhinā budhaiḥ  
AbhTa tatra yadyannijābhīṣṭabhogamokṣopakārakam 
AbhTb pāramparyeṇa sākṣādvā bhaveccidacidātmakam  
AbhTa tatpūjyaṃ tadupāyāśca pūjyāstanmayatāptaye 
AbhTb tadupāyopi saṃpūjyo mūrtikālakriyādikaḥ  
AbhTa upeyasūtisāmarthyamupāyatvaṃ tadarcanāt 
AbhTb tadrūpatanmayībhāvādupeyaṃ śīghramāpnuyāt  
AbhTa yathā yathā ca naikaṭyamupāyeṣu tathā tathā 
AbhTb avaśyaṃbhāvi kāryatvaṃ viśeṣāccārcanādike  
AbhTa jñānasya kasyacitprāptirbhogamokṣopakāriṇaḥ 
AbhTb yadā tanmukhyamevoktaṃ naimittikadinaṃ budhaiḥ  
AbhTa tadupāyaḥ śāstramatra vaktāpyaupayiko guruḥ 
AbhTb tadvidyopi gurubhrātā saṃvādājjñānadāyakaḥ  
AbhTa guroḥ patnī tathā bhrātā putra ityādiko gaṇaḥ 
AbhTb na yonisaṃbandhavaśādvidyāsaṃbandhajastu saḥ  
AbhTa vīryāruṇaparīṇāmadehāhantāpratiṣṭhitāḥ 
AbhTb dehopakārasantānā jñāteye pariniṣṭhitāḥ  
AbhTa tathāca smṛtiśāstreṣu santaterdāyahāritā 
AbhTb yuktaiva tāvānsa hyukto bhedāddūrāntikatvataḥ  
AbhTa ye tu tyaktaśarīrāsthā bodhāhambhāvabhāginaḥ 
AbhTb bodhopakārasantānadvayātte bandhutājuṣaḥ  
AbhTa tatretthaṃ prāgyadā paśyecchaktyunmīlitadṛkkriyaḥ 
AbhTb dehastāvadayaṃ pūrvapūrvopādānanirmitaḥ  
AbhTa ātmā vikārarahitaḥ śāśvatatvādahetukaḥ 
AbhTb svātantryāt punarātmīyādayaṃ channa iva sthitaḥ  
AbhTa punaśca prakaṭībhūya bhairavībhāvabhājanam 
AbhTb tatrāsya prakaṭībhāve bhuktimuktyātmake bhṛśam  
AbhTa ya upāyaḥ samucito jñānasantāna eṣa saḥ 
AbhTb kramasphuṭībhavattādṛksadṛśajñānadhārayā  
AbhTa galadvijātīyatayā prāpyaṃ śīghraṃ hi labhyate 
AbhTb evaṃ cānādisaṃsārocitavijñānasantateḥ  
AbhTa dhvaṃse lokottaraṃ jñānaṃ santānāntaratāṃ śrayet 
AbhTb asaṃsārocitodāratathāvijñānasantateḥ  
AbhTa kāraṇaṃ mukhyamādyaṃ tadguruvijñānamātmagam 
AbhTb atyantaṃ svaviśeṣāṇāṃ tatrārpaṇavaśāt sphuṭam  
AbhTa upādānaṃ hi tadyuktaṃ dehabhede hi satyapi 
AbhTb dehasantatigau bhedābhedau vijñānasantateḥ  
AbhTa na tathātvāya yogīcchāviṣṭaśāvaśarīravat 
AbhTb yoginaḥ paradehādijīvattāpādane nijam  
AbhTa dehamatyajato nānājñānopādānatā na kim 
AbhTb tena vijñānasantānaprādhānyādyaunasantateḥ  
AbhTa anyonyaṃ gurusantāno yaḥ śivajñānaniṣṭhitaḥ 
AbhTb itthaṃ sthite trayaṃ mukhyaṃ kāraṇaṃ sahakāri ca  
AbhTa ekakāraṇakāryaṃ ca vastvityeṣa gurorgaṇaḥ 
AbhTb guruḥ kāraṇamatroktaṃ tatpatnī sahakāriṇī  
AbhTa yato niḥśaktikasyāsya na yāgedhikṛtirbhavet 
AbhTb antaḥsthodārasaṃvittiśakterbāhyāṃ vināpi tām  
AbhTa sāmarthyaṃ yogino yadvadvināpi sahakāriṇam 
AbhTb ekajanyā bhrātaraḥ syustatsadṛgyastu kopi saḥ  
AbhTa punaḥ paramparāyogādguruvargopi bhaṇyate 
AbhTb mukhya eṣa tu santānaḥ pūjyo mānyaśca sarvadā  
AbhTa gurvādīnāṃ ca sambhūtau dīkṣāyāṃ prāyaṇepi ca 
AbhTb yadahastaddhi vijñānopāyadehādikāraṇam  
AbhTa evaṃ svajanmadivaso vijñānopāya ucyate 
AbhTb tādṛgbhogāpavargādihetordehasya kāraṇam  
AbhTa dīkṣādikaśca saṃskāraḥ svātmano yatra cāhni tat 
AbhTb bhavejjanmadinaṃ mukhyaṃ jñānasantānajanmataḥ  
AbhTa svakaṃ mṛtidinaṃ yattu tadanyeṣāṃ bhaviṣyati 
AbhTb naimittikaṃ mṛto yasmācchivābhinnastadā bhavet  
AbhTa tatra prasaṅgānmaraṇasvarūpaṃ brūmahe sphuṭam 
AbhTb vyāpakopi śivaḥ svecchākḷptasaṅkocamudraṇāt  
AbhTa vicitraphalakarmaughavaśāttattaccharīrabhāk 
AbhTb śarīrabhāktvaṃ caitāvadyattadgarbhasthadehagaḥ  
AbhTa saṃvitteḥ śūnyarūḍhāyāḥ prathamaḥ prāṇanodayaḥ 
AbhTb garbhasthadehanirmāṇe tasyaiveśvaratā punaḥ  
AbhTa asaṅkocasya tanvādikartā teneśa ucyate 
AbhTb sa vāyvātmā dṛḍhe tasmindehayantre cidātmanā  
AbhTa preryamāṇo vicarati bhastrāyantragavāyuvat 
AbhTb ataḥ prāggāḍhasaṃsuptotthitavatsa prabuddhyate  
AbhTa kramāddehena sākaṃ ca prāṇanā syādbalīyasī 
AbhTb tatrāpi karmaniyatibalātsā prāṇanākṣatām  
AbhTa gṛhṇāti śūnyasuṣirasaṃvitsparśādhikatvataḥ 
AbhTb evaṃ krameṇa saṃpuṣṭadehaprāṇabalo bhṛśam  
AbhTa bhogānkarmakṛtānbhuṅkte yonyayonijadehagaḥ 
AbhTb uktaṃ ca gahvarābhikhye śāstre śītāṃśumaulinā  
AbhTa yathā gṛhaṃ viniṣpādya gṛhī samadhitiṣṭhati 
AbhTb tathā dehī tanuṃ kṛtvā kriyādiguṇavarjitaḥ  
AbhTa kiñcitsphuraṇamātraḥ prāgniṣkalaḥ sopi śabdyate 
AbhTb sphuṭendriyāditattvastu sakalātmeti bhaṇyate  
AbhTa ityādi śrīgahvaroktaṃ tata eva paṭhedbahu 
AbhTb kṣaye tu karmaṇāṃ teṣāṃ dehayantrenyathāgate  
AbhTa prāṇayantraṃ vighaṭate dehaḥ syātkuḍyavattataḥ 
AbhTb nāḍīcakreṣu saṅkocavikāsau viparītataḥ  
AbhTa bhaṅgaḥ śoṣaḥ klidirvātaśleṣmāgnyapacayoccayaiḥ 
AbhTb ityevamādi yatkiñcit prāksaṃsthānopamardakam  
AbhTa dehayantre vighaṭanaṃ tadevoktaṃ manīṣibhiḥ 
AbhTb tasminvighaṭite yantre sā saṃvitprāṇanātmatām  
AbhTa gṛhṇāti yonijenyatra vā dehe karmacitrite 
AbhTb sa dehaḥ pratibudhyeta prasuptotthitavattadā  
AbhTa tasyāpi bhogataddhānimṛtayaḥ prāgvadeva hi 
AbhTb visṛṣṭisthitisaṃhārā ete karmabalādyataḥ  
AbhTa ato niyatikālādivaicitryānuvidhāyinaḥ 
AbhTb anugrahastu yaḥ soyaṃ svasvarūpe vikasvare  
AbhTa jñaptyātmeti kathaṃ karmaniyatyādi pratīkṣate 
AbhTb karmakālaniyatyādi yataḥ saṅkocajīvitam  
AbhTa saṅkocahānirūpesminkathaṃ heturanugrahe 
AbhTb anugrahaśca kramikastīvraśceti vibhidyate  
AbhTa prāk caiṣa vistarātprokta iti kiṃ punaruktibhiḥ 
AbhTb tena dīkṣāśivajñānadagdhasaṅkocabandhanaḥ  
AbhTa dehānte śiva eveti nāsya dehāntarasthitiḥ 
AbhTb yepi tattvāvatīrṇānāṃ śaṃkarājñānuvartinām  
AbhTa svayambhūmunidevarṣimanujādibhuvāṃ gṛhe 
AbhTb mṛtāste tatpuraṃ prāpya pureśairdīkṣitāḥ kramāt  
AbhTa martyevatīrya vā no vā śivaṃ yāntyapunarbhavāḥ 
AbhTb tatra svayambhuvo dvedhā kepyanugrahatatparāḥ  
AbhTa kepi svakṛtyāyātāṃśasthānamātropasevinaḥ 
AbhTb yenugrahārthamājñaptāsteṣu yo mriyate naraḥ  
AbhTa sonugrahaṃ sphuṭaṃ yāti vinā martyāvatārataḥ 
AbhTb yastu svakāryaṃ kurvāṇastatsthānaṃ nāṃśatastyajet  
AbhTa yathā gaurī tapasyantī kaśmīreṣu guhāgatā 
AbhTb tatraiva vā yathā dhyānoḍḍāre naraharirvibhuḥ  
AbhTa vitastāṃ nayato daityāṃstrāsayandṛpta utthitaḥ 
AbhTb sāligrāme yathā viṣṇuḥ śivo vā svopabhoginaḥ  
AbhTa tapasyantau badaryāṃ ca naranārāyaṇau tathā 
AbhTb ityevamādayo devāḥ svakṛtyāṃśasthitāstathā  
AbhTa ārādhitāḥ svocitaṃ tacchīghraṃ vidadhate phalam 
AbhTb svakṛtyāṃśasthitānāṃ ca dhāmni yentaṃ vrajanti te  
AbhTa tatra bhogāṃstathā bhuktvā martyeṣvavatarantyapi 
AbhTb martyāvatīrṇāste tattadaṃśakāstanmayāḥ punaḥ  
AbhTa taddīkṣājñānacaryādikramādyānti śivātmatām 
AbhTb sthāvarādyāstiryagantāḥ paśavosmindvaye mṛtāḥ  
AbhTa svakarmasaṃskriyāvedhāttalloke citratājuṣaḥ 
AbhTb puṃsāṃ ca paśumātrāṇāṃ sālokyamavivekataḥ  
AbhTa avivekastadviśeṣānunmeṣānmauḍhyatastathā 
AbhTb sthāvarādyāstathābhāvamuttarottaratāṃ ca vā  
AbhTa prapadyante na te sākṣādrudratāṃ tāṃ kramātpunaḥ 
AbhTb haṃsakāraṇḍavākīrṇe nānātarukulākule  
AbhTa ityetadāgameṣūktaṃ tata eva pure pure 
AbhTb kṣetramānaṃ bruve śrīmatsarvajñānādiṣūditam  
AbhTa liṅgāddhastaśataṃ kṣetramācāryasthāpite sati 
AbhTb svayambhūte sahasraṃ tu tadardhamṛṣiyojite  
AbhTa tattvavitsthāpite liṅge svayambhūsadṛśaṃ phalam 
AbhTb atattvavidyadācāryo liṅgaṃ sthāpayate tadā  
AbhTa punarvidhirbhaveddoṣo hyanyathobhayadūṣakaḥ 
AbhTb ahamanyaḥ parātmānyaḥ śivonya iti cenmatiḥ  
AbhTa na mocayenna muktaśca sarvamātmamayaṃ yataḥ 
AbhTb tasmāttattvavidā yadyatsthāpitaṃ liṅgamuttamam  
AbhTa tadevāyatanatvena saṃśrayedbhuktimuktaye 
AbhTb uktaṃ śrīratnamālāyāṃ jñātvā kālamupasthitam  
AbhTa mokṣārthī na bhayaṃ gacchettyajeddehamaśaṅkitaḥ 
AbhTb tīrthāyatanapuṇyeṣu kālaṃ vā vañcayetpriye  
AbhTa ayogināmayaṃ panthā yogī yogena vañcayet 
AbhTb vañcane tvasamarthaḥ san kṣetramāyatanaṃ vrajet  
AbhTa tīrthe samāśrayāttasya vañcanaṃ tu vijāyate 
AbhTb anena ca dharādyeṣu tattveṣvabhyāsayogataḥ  
AbhTa tāvatsiddhijuṣopyuktā muktyai kṣetropayogitā 
AbhTb samyagjñānini vṛttāntaḥ purastāttūpadekṣyate  
AbhTa paśūnāmeṣa vṛttānto ye tu tattattvadīkṣitāḥ 
AbhTb te tadīśasamīpatvaṃ yānti svaucityayogataḥ  
AbhTa yogyatāvaśasaṃjātā yasya yatraiva vāsanā 
AbhTb sa tatraiva niyoktavyaḥ pureśāccordhvaśuddhibhāk  
AbhTa iti śrīpūrvakathitaṃ śrīmatsvāyambhuvepica 
AbhTb yo yatrābhilaṣedbhogānsa tatraiva niyojitaḥ  
AbhTa siddhibhāṅmantrasāmarthyādityādyanyatra varṇitam 
AbhTb ye tu tattattvavijñānamantracaryādivartinaḥ  
AbhTa mṛtāste tatra tadrudrasayuktvaṃ yānti kovidāḥ 
AbhTb teṣāṃ sayuktvaṃ yātānāmapi saṃskārato nijāt  
AbhTa tathā tathā vicitraḥ syādavatārastadaṃśataḥ 
AbhTb siddhāntādau purāṇeṣu tathāca śrūyate bahu  
AbhTa tulye rudrāvatāratve citratvaṃ karmabhogayoḥ 
AbhTb anekaśaktikhacitaṃ yato bhāvasya yadvapuḥ  
AbhTa śaktibhyorthāntaraṃ naiṣa tatsamūhādṛte bhavet 
AbhTb tena śaktisamūhākhyāt tasmādrudrādyadaṃśataḥ  
AbhTa kṛtyaṃ taducitaṃ siddhyet soṃśovatarati sphuṭam 
AbhTb ye cādharaprāptadīkṣāstadāsthānujjhitāḥ pare  
AbhTa tattve mṛtāḥ kāṣṭhavattedharepyutkarṣabhāginaḥ 
AbhTb ye tūjjhitatadutkarṣāste taduttarabhāginaḥ  
AbhTa yepyūrdhvatattvadīkṣāste vinā tāvadvivekataḥ 
AbhTb prāptādharāntā api taddīkṣāphalasubhāginaḥ  
AbhTa atyaktāsthā hi te tatra dīkṣāyāmapi śāstritāt 
AbhTb vinā vivekādāsthāṃ te śritā lokaprasiddhitaḥ  
AbhTa paśumātrasya sālokyaṃ sāmīpyaṃ dīkṣitasya tu 
AbhTb tatparasya tu sāyujyamityuktaṃ parameśinā  
AbhTa yastūrdhvaśāstragastatra tyaktāsthaḥ saṃśayena saḥ 
AbhTb vrajannāyatanaṃ naiva phalaṃ kiñcitsamaśnute  
AbhTa uktaṃ tadviṣayaṃ caitaddevadevena yadvṛthā 
AbhTb dīkṣā jñānaṃ tathā tīrthaṃ tasyetyādi savistaram  
AbhTa yastu tāvadayogyopi tathāste sa śivālaye 
AbhTb paścādāsthānibandhena tāvadeva phalaṃ bhajet  
AbhTa nadīnagahradaprāyaṃ yacca puṇyaṃ na tanmṛtau 
AbhTb utkṛṣṭaṃ tanmṛtānāṃ tu svargabhogopabhogitā  
AbhTa ye punaḥ prāptavijñānavivekā maraṇāntike 
AbhTb adharāyataneṣvāsthāṃ śritāstetra tirohitāḥ  
AbhTa tajjñānadūṣaṇoktaṃ yatteṣāṃ syātkila pātakam 
AbhTb tattatpureśadīkṣādikramānnaśyediti sthitiḥ  
AbhTa dīkṣāyatanavijñānadūṣiṇo ye tu cetasā 
AbhTb ācaranti ca tattetra sarve nirayagāminaḥ  
AbhTa jñānāyatanadīkṣādāvāsthābandhaparicyutiḥ 
AbhTb vyāpāravyāhṛtairjñeyā tānyapi dvividhāni ca  
AbhTa yāni jātucidapyeva svāsthye nodamiṣanpunaḥ 
AbhTb asvāsthye dhātudoṣotthānyeva tadbhogamātrakam  
AbhTa dhātudoṣācca saṃsārasaṃskārāste prabodhitāḥ 
AbhTb chidragā api bhūyiṣṭhajñānadagdhā na rohiṇaḥ  
AbhTa ye tu kaivalyabhāgīyāḥ svāsthyenunmiṣitāḥ sadā 
AbhTb asvāsthye conmiṣantyete saṃskārāḥ śaktipātataḥ  
AbhTa yataḥ sāṃsārikāḥ pūrvagāḍhābhyāsopasaṃskṛtāḥ 
AbhTb ityūce bhujagādhīśastacchidreṣviti sūtrataḥ  
AbhTa ye tu kaivalyabhāgīyāḥ pratyayāste na jātucit 
AbhTb abhyastāḥ saṃsṛterbhāvāttenaite śaktipātataḥ  
AbhTa vyāpāravyāhṛtaistena dhātudoṣaprakopitaiḥ 
AbhTb aprāptaniścayāmarśaiḥ suptamattopamānakaiḥ  
AbhTa viparītairapi jñānadīkṣāgurvādidūṣakaiḥ 
AbhTb tirobhāvo na vijñeyo hṛdaye rūḍhyabhāvataḥ  
AbhTa ata eva prabuddhopi karmotthānbhogarūpiṇaḥ 
AbhTb yamakiṅkarasarpādipratyayāndehago bhajet  
AbhTa naitāvatā na muktosau mṛtirbhogo hi janmavat 
AbhTb sthitivacca tato duḥkhasukhābhyāṃ maraṇaṃ dvidhā  
AbhTa ato yathā prabuddhasya sukhaduḥkhavicitratāḥ 
AbhTb sthitau na ghnanti muktatvaṃ maraṇepi tathaiva tāḥ  
AbhTa ye punaryoginastepi yasmiṃstattve subhāvitāḥ 
AbhTb cittaṃ niveśayantyeva tattattvaṃ yāntyaśaṅkitāḥ  
AbhTa śrīsvacchande tataḥ proktaṃ gandhadhāraṇayā mṛtāḥ 
AbhTb ityādi mālinīśāstre dhāraṇānāṃ tathā phalam  
AbhTa eteṣāṃ maraṇābhikhyo bhogo nāsti tu ye tanum 
AbhTb dhāraṇābhistyajantyāśu paradehapraveśavat  
AbhTa etāvānmṛtibhogo hi marmacchinmūḍhatākṣagā 
AbhTb dhvāntābilatvaṃ manasi taccaiteṣu na vidyate  
AbhTa tathāhi mānasaṃ yatnaṃ tāvatsamadhitiṣṭhati 
AbhTb ahaṃrūḍhyā pare dehe yāvatsyādbuddhisaṃcaraḥ  
AbhTa prāṇacakraṃ tadāyattamapi saṃcarate pathā 
AbhTb tenaivātaḥ prabuddhyeta paradehekṣacakrakam  
AbhTa makṣikā makṣikārājaṃ yathotthitamanūtthitāḥ 
AbhTb sthitaṃ cānuviśantyevaṃ cittaṃ sarvākṣavṛttayaḥ  
AbhTa atosya paradehādisaṃcāre nāsti melanam 
AbhTb akṣāṇāṃ madhyagaṃ sūkṣmaṃ syādetaddehavatpunaḥ  
AbhTa evaṃ paraśarīrādicāriṇāmiva yoginām 
AbhTb tattattattvaśarīrāntaścāriṇāṃ nāsti mūḍhatā  
AbhTa te cāpi dvividhā jñeyā laukikā dīkṣitāstathā 
AbhTb pūrve śivāḥ syuḥ kramaśaḥ pare tadbhogamātrataḥ  
AbhTa dīkṣāpyūrdhvādharānekabhedayojanikāvaśāt 
AbhTb bhidyamānā yogināṃ syādvicitraphaladāyinī  
AbhTa ye tu vijñāninastetra dvedhā kampretaratvataḥ 
AbhTb tatra ye kampravijñānāste dehānted śivāḥ sphuṭam  
AbhTa yato vijñānameteṣāmutpannaṃ naca susphuṭam 
AbhTb vikalpāntarayogena nacāpyunmūlitātmakam  
AbhTa ato dehe pramādottho vikalpo dehapātataḥ 
AbhTb naśyedavaśyaṃ taccāpi budhyate jñānamuttamam  
AbhTa saṃskārakalpanātiṣṭhadadhvastīkṛtamantarā 
AbhTb prāptapākaṃ saṃvarīturapāye bhāsate hi tat  
AbhTa ye tu svabhyastavijñānamayāḥ śivamayāḥ sadā 
AbhTb jīvanmuktā hi te naiṣāṃ mṛtau kāpi vicāraṇā  
AbhTa yathāhi jīvanmuktānāṃ sthitau nāsti vicāraṇā 
AbhTb sukhiduḥkhivimūḍhatve
mṛtāvapi tathā na sā  
AbhTa śrīratnamālāśāstre taduvāca parameśvaraḥ 
AbhTb svaśāstre cāpyahīśāno viśvādhāradhurandharaḥ  
AbhTa rathyāntare mūtrapurīṣamadhye caṇḍālagehe niraye śmaśāne 
AbhTb sacintako vā gatacintako vā jñānī vimokṣaṃ labhatepi cānte  
AbhTa apiceti dhvanirjīvanmuktatāmasya bhāṣate 
AbhTb sacintācintakatvoktiretāvatsaṃbhavasthitim  
AbhTa tīrthe śvapacagṛhe vā naṣṭasmṛtirapi parityajeddeham 
AbhTb jñānasamakālamuktaḥ kaivalyaṃ yāti hataśokaḥ  
AbhTa anantakārikā caiṣā prāhedaṃ bandhakaṃ kila 
AbhTb sukṛtaṃ duṣkṛtaṃ cāsya śaṅkyaṃ taccāsya no bhavet  
AbhTa apiśabdādaluptasmṛtyā vā saṃbhāvyate kila 
AbhTb mṛtirnaṣṭasmṛtereva mṛteḥ prāk sāstu kiṃ tayā  
AbhTa liṅca saṃbhāvanāyāṃ syādiyatsaṃbhāvyate kila 
AbhTb saca kāladhvaniḥ prāha mṛtermuktāvahetutām  
AbhTa kaivalyamiti cāśaṅkāpadaṃ yāpyabhavattanuḥ 
AbhTb bhedapradatvenaiṣāpi dhvastā tena viśokatā  
AbhTa paradehādisaṃbandho yathā nāsya vibhedakaḥ 
AbhTb tathā svadehasaṃbandho jīvanmuktasya yadyapi  
AbhTa ataśca na viśeṣosya viśvākṛtinirākṛteḥ 
AbhTb śivābhinnasya dehe vā tadabhāvepi vā kila  
AbhTa tathāpi prācyatadbhedasaṃskārāśaṅkanasthiteḥ 
AbhTb adhunoktaṃ kevalatvaṃ yadvā mātrantarāśrayāt  
AbhTa tānyenaṃ na vidurbhinnaṃ taiḥ sa muktobhidhīyate 
AbhTb śrīmattraiśirasepyuktaṃ sūryendupuṭavarjite  
AbhTa jugupsābhāvabhaṅgasthe sarvataḥ stambhavatsthite 
AbhTb sarvavyāpattirahite pramāṇapratyayātige  
AbhTa tasminbodhāntare līnaḥ karmakartāpyanañjanaḥ 
AbhTb pradhānaṃ ghaṭa ākāśa ātmā maṣṭe ghaṭepi kham  
AbhTa na naśyettadvadevāsāvātmā śivamayo bhavet 
AbhTb svatantrovasthito jñānī prasaretsarvavastuṣu  
AbhTa tasya bhāvo nacābhāvaḥ saṃsthānaṃ naca kalpanā 
AbhTb etadevāntarāgūrya gururgītāsvabhāṣata  
AbhTa yaṃ yaṃ vāpi smaranbhāvaṃ tyajatyante kalevaram 
AbhTb taṃ tamevaiti kaunteya sadā tadbhāvabhāvitaḥ  
AbhTa tasmātsarveṣu kāleṣu māmanusmara yudhya ca 
AbhTb yadā sattve vivṛddhe tu pralīnastvūrdhvagastadā  
AbhTa kramādrajastamolīnaḥ karmayonivimūḍhagaḥ 
AbhTb tatrendriyāṇāṃ saṃmohaśvāsāyāsaparītatā  
AbhTa ityādimṛtibhogoyaṃ dehe na tyajanaṃ tanoḥ 
AbhTb yastvasau kṣaṇa evaikaścaramaḥ prāṇanātmakaḥ  
AbhTa yadanantaramevaiṣa dehaḥ syātkāṣṭhakuḍyavat 
AbhTb sā dehatyāgakālāṃśakalā dehaviyoginī  
AbhTa tata eva hi taddehasukhaduḥkhādikojjhitā 
AbhTb tasyāṃ yadeva smarati prāksaṃskāraprabodhataḥ  
AbhTa adṛṣṭābhyāsabhūyastvaśaktipātādihetukāt 
AbhTb tadeva rūpamabhyeti sukhiduḥkhivimūḍhakam  
AbhTa yadvā niḥsukhaduḥkhādi yadi vānandarūpakam 
AbhTb kasmādeti tadevaiṣa yataḥ smarati saṃvidi  
AbhTa prāk prasphuredyadadhikaṃ dehosau cidadhiṣṭhiteḥ 
AbhTb yadeva prāgadhiṣṭhānaṃ citā tādātmyavṛttitaḥ  
AbhTa saivātra līnatā proktā sattve rajasi tāmase 
AbhTb nīlapītādike jñeye yataḥ prākkalpitāṃ tanum  
AbhTa adhiṣṭhāyaiva saṃvittiradhiṣṭhānaṃ karotyalam 
AbhTb atodhiṣṭheyamātrasya śarīratvepi kuḍyataḥ  
AbhTa dehasyāsti viśeṣo yatsarvādhiṣṭheyapūrvatā 
AbhTb tādātmyavṛttiranyeṣāṃ tanna satyapi vedyate  
AbhTa vedyānāṃ kintu dehasya nityāvyabhicaritvataḥ 
AbhTb sā ca tasyaiva dehasya pūrvamṛtyantajanmanā  
AbhTa smṛtyā prācyānubhavanakṛtasaṃskāracitrayā 
AbhTb yuktyānayāsmatsantānaguruṇā kallaṭena yat  
AbhTa dehāviśeṣe prāṇākhyadārḍhyaṃ heturudīritam 
AbhTb tadyuktamanyathā prāṇadārḍhye ko heturekataḥ  
AbhTa dehatvasyāviśeṣepītyeṣa praśno na śāmyati 
AbhTb smaranniti śatā hetau tadrūpaṃ pratipadyate  
AbhTa prāk smaryate yato dehaḥ prākcitādhiṣṭhitaḥ sphuran 
AbhTb ataḥ smaraṇamantyaṃ yattadasarvajñamātṛṣu  
AbhTa na jātu gocaro yasmāddehāntaraviniścayaḥ 
AbhTb yattu bandhupriyāputrapānādismaraṇaṃ sphuṭam  
AbhTa na taddehāntarāsaṅgi na tadantyaṃ yato bhavet 
AbhTb kasyāpi tu śarīrānte vāsanā yā prabhotsyate  
AbhTa dehasattve tadaucityājjāyetānubhavaḥ sphuṭaḥ 
AbhTb yathā purāṇe kathitaṃ mṛgapotakatṛṣṇayā  
AbhTa muniḥ kopi mṛgībhāvamabhyuvāhādhivāsitaḥ 
AbhTb tatra sonubhavo heturna janmāntarasūtaye  
AbhTa tasyaitadvāsanā hetuḥ kākatālīyavat sa tu 
AbhTb nanu kasmāttadevaiṣa smarati ityāha yatsadā  
AbhTa tadbhāvabhāvitastena tadevaiṣa smaratyalam 
AbhTb evamasmi bhaviṣyāmītyeṣa tadbhāva ucyate  
AbhTa bhaviṣyato hi bhavanaṃ bhāvyate na sataḥ kvacit 
AbhTb kramātsphuṭatvakaraṇaṃ bhāvanaṃ parikīrtyate  
AbhTa sphuṭasya cānubhavanaṃ na bhāvanamidaṃ sphuṭam 
AbhTb tadaharjātabālasya paśoḥ kīṭasya vā taroḥ  
AbhTa mūḍhatvepi tadānīṃ prāgbhāvanā hyabhavatsphuṭā 
AbhTb sā tanmūḍhaśarīrānte saṃskārapratibodhanāt  
AbhTa smṛtidvāreṇa taddehavaicitryaphaladāyinī 
AbhTb deśādivyavadhānepi vāsanānāmudīritāt  
AbhTa ānantaryaikarūpatvātsmṛtisaṃskārayorataḥ 
AbhTb tathānubhavanārūḍhyā sphuṭasyāpi tu bhāvitā  
AbhTa bhāvyamānā na kiṃ sūte tatsantānasadṛgvapuḥ 
AbhTb tattādṛktādṛśairbandhuputramitrādibhiḥ saha  
AbhTa bhāsatepi pare loke svapnavadvāsanākramāt 
AbhTb nanu mātrantarairbandhuputrādyaistattathā na kim  
AbhTa vedyate ka idaṃ prāha sa tāvadveda vedyatām 
AbhTb vyāpāravyāhṛtivrātavedye mātrantaravraje  
AbhTa svapne nāsti sa ityeṣā vākpramāṇavivarjitā 
AbhTb ya evaite tu dṛśyante jāgratyete mayekṣitāḥ  
AbhTa svapna ityastu mithyaitattatpramātṛvacobalāt 
AbhTb yānapaśyamahaṃ svapne pramātṝṃste na kecana  
AbhTa na śocanti na cekṣante māmityatrāsti kā pramā 
AbhTb yataḥ sarvānumānānāṃ svasaṃvedananiṣṭhitau  
AbhTa pramātrantarasadbhāvaḥ saṃvinniṣṭho na tadgataḥ 
AbhTb ghaṭāderastitā saṃvinniṣṭhitā natu tadgatā  
AbhTa tadvanmātrantarepyeṣā saṃvinniṣṭhā na tadgatā 
AbhTb tena sthitamidaṃ yadyadbhāvyate tattadeva hi  
AbhTa dehānte budhyate no cet syādanyādṛkprabodhanam 
AbhTb tathāhyantyakṣaṇe brahmavidyākarṇanasaṃskṛtaḥ  
AbhTa mucyate janturityuktaṃ prāksaṃskārabalatvataḥ 
AbhTb nipātābhyāmantaśabdātsmaraṇācchaturantyataḥ  
AbhTa pādācca nikhilādardhaślokācca samanantarāt 
AbhTb līnaśabdācca sarvaṃ taduktamarthasatattvakam  
AbhTa ajñātvaitattu sarvepi kuśakāśāvalambinaḥ 
AbhTb yattadorvyatyayaṃ kecitkecidanyādṛśaṃ kramam  
AbhTa bhinnakramau nipātau ca tyajatīti ca saptamīm 
AbhTb vyācakṣate tacca sarvaṃ nopayogyuktayojane  
AbhTa naca taddarśitaṃ mithyā svāntasammohadāyakam 
AbhTb taditthaṃprāyaṇasyaitattattvaṃ śrīśambhunāthataḥ  
AbhTa adhigamyoditaṃ tena mṛtyorbhītirvinaśyati 
AbhTb viditamṛtisatattvāḥ saṃvidambhonidhānādacalahṛdayavīryākarṣaniṣpīḍanottham 
AbhTc amṛtamiti nigīrṇe kālakūṭetra devā yadi pivatha tadānīṃ niścitaṃ vaḥ śivatvam  
AbhTa utsavopi hi yaḥ kaścillaukikaḥ sopi saṃmadam 
AbhTb saṃvidabdhitaraṅgābhaṃ sūte tadapi parvavat  
AbhTa etena ca vipaddhvaṃsapramodādiṣu parvatā 
AbhTb vyākhyātā tena tatrāpi viśeṣāddevatārcanam  
AbhTa purakṣobhādyadbhutaṃ yattatsvātantrye svasaṃvidaḥ 
AbhTb dārḍhyadāyīti tallābhadine vaiśeṣikārcanam  
AbhTa yoginīmelako dvedhā haṭhataḥ priyatastathā 
AbhTb prācye cchidrāṇi saṃrakṣetkāmacāritvamuttare  
AbhTa sa ca dvayopi mantroddhṛtprasaṅge darśayiṣyate 
AbhTb yoginīmelakāccaiṣovaśyaṃ jñānaṃ prapadyate  
AbhTa tena tatparva tadvacca svasantānādimelanam 
AbhTb saṃvitsarvātmikā dehabhedādyā saṅkucettu sā  
AbhTa melakenyonyasaṅghaṭṭapratibimbādvikasvarā 
AbhTb ucchalannijaraśmyoghaḥ saṃvitsu pratibimbitaḥ  
AbhTa bahudarpaṇavaddīptaḥ sarvāyetāpyayatnataḥ 
AbhTb ata eva gītagītaprabhṛtau bahuparṣadi  
AbhTa yaḥ sarvatanmayībhāve hlādo natvekakasya saḥ 
AbhTb ānandanirbharā saṃvitpratyekaṃ sā tathaikatām  
AbhTa nṛttādau viṣaye prāptā pūrṇānandatvamaśnute 
AbhTb īrṣyāsūyādisaṅkocakāraṇābhāvatotra sā  
AbhTa vikasvarā niṣpratighaṃ saṃvidānandayoginī 
AbhTb atanmaye tu kasmiṃścittatrasthe pratihanyate  
AbhTa sthapuṭasparśavatsaṃvidvijātīyatayā sthite 
AbhTb ataścakrārcanādyeṣu vijātīyamatanmayam  
AbhTa naiva praveśayetsaṃvitsaṅkocananibandhanam 
AbhTb yāvantyeva śarīrāṇi svāṅgavatsyuḥ sunirbharām  
AbhTa ekāṃ saṃvidamāviśya cakre tāvanti pūjayet 
AbhTb praviṣṭaścetpramādena saṅkocaṃ na vrajettataḥ  
AbhTa prastutaṃ svasamācāraṃ tena sākaṃ samācaret 
AbhTb sa tvanugrahaśaktyā cedviddhastattanmayībhavet  
AbhTa vāmāviddhastu tannindetpaścāttaṃ ghātayedapi 
AbhTb śrīmatpicumate coktamādau yatnena rakṣayet  
AbhTa praveśaṃ saṃpaviṣṭasya na vicāraṃ tu kārayet 
AbhTb lokācārasthito yastu praviṣṭe tādṛśe tu saḥ  
AbhTa akṛtvā taṃ samācāraṃ punaścakraṃ prapūjayet 
AbhTb atha vacmi guroḥ śāstravyākhyākramamudāhṛtam  
AbhTa devyāyāmalaśāstrādau tuhinābhīśumaulinā 
AbhTb kalpavittatsamūhajñaḥ śāstravitsaṃhitārthavit  
AbhTa sarvaśāstrārthavicceti gururbhinnopadiśyate 
AbhTb yo yatra śāstre svabhyastajñāno vyākhyāṃ carettu saḥ  
AbhTa nānyathā tadabhāvaścetsarvathā sopyathācaret 
AbhTb śrībhairavakule coktaṃ kalpādijñatvamīdṛśam  
AbhTa gurorlakṣaṇametāvatsaṃpūrṇajñānataiva yā 
AbhTb tatrāpi yāsya cidvṛttikarmibhit sāpyavāntarā  
AbhTa devyāyāmala uktaṃ taddvāpañcāśāhva āhnike 
AbhTb deva eva gurutvena tiṣṭhāsurdaśadhā bhavet  
AbhTa ucchuṣmaśavaracaṇḍagumataṅgaghorāntakograhalahalakāḥ 
AbhTb krodhī huluhulurete daśa guravaḥ śivamayāḥ pūrve  
AbhTa te svāṃśacittavṛttikrameṇa pauruṣaśarīramāsthāya 
AbhTb anyonyabhinnasaṃvitkriyā api jñānaparipūrṇāḥ  
AbhTa sarvelimāṃsanidhuvanadīkṣārcanaśāstrasevane niratāḥ 
AbhTb abhimānaśamakrodhakṣamādiravāntaro bhedaḥ  
AbhTa itthaṃ vijñāya sadā śiṣyaḥ sampūrṇaśāstraboddhāram 
AbhTb vyākhyāyai gurumabhyarthayeta pūjāpuraḥsaraṃ matimān  
AbhTa sopi svaśāsanīye paraśiṣyepivāpi tādṛśaṃ śāstram 
AbhTb śrotuṃ yogye kuryādvyākhyānaṃ vaiṣṇavādyadhare  
AbhTa karuṇārasaparipūrṇo guruḥ punarmarmadhāmaparivarjam 
AbhTb adhamepi hi vyākuryātsambhāvya hi śaktipātavaicitryam  
AbhTa liptāyāṃ bhuvi pīṭhe caturasre paṅkajatrayaṃ kajage 
AbhTb kuryādvidyāpīṭhaṃ syādrasavahnyaṅgulaṃ tvetat  
AbhTa madhye vāgīśānīṃ dakṣottarayorgurūngaṇeśaṃ ca 
AbhTb adhare kaje ca kalpeśvaraṃ prapūjyārghapuṣpatarpaṇakaiḥ  
AbhTa sāmānyavidhiniyuktārghapātrayogena cakramatha samyak 
AbhTb santarpya vyākhyānaṃ kuryātsambandhapūrvakaṃ matimān  
AbhTa sūtrapadavākyapaṭalagranthakramayojanena sambandhāt 
AbhTb avyāhatapūrvāparamupavṛhya nayeta vākyāni  
AbhTa maṇḍūkaplavasiṃhāvalokanādyairyathāyathaṃ nyāyaiḥ 
AbhTb avihatapūrvāparakaṃ śāstrārthaṃ yojayedasaṅkīrṇam  
AbhTa tantrāvartanabādhaprasaṅgatarkādibhiśca sannyāyaiḥ 
AbhTb vastu vadedvākyajño vastvantarato viviktatāṃ vidadhat  
AbhTa yadyadvyāhṛtipadavīmāyāti tadeva dṛḍhatarairnyāyaiḥ 
AbhTb balavatkuryāddūṣyaṃ yadyapyagre bhaviṣyatsyāt  
AbhTa dṛḍharacitapūrvapakṣaproddharaṇapathena vastu yadvācyam 
AbhTb śiṣyamatāvārohati tadāśu saṃśayaviparyayairvikalam  
AbhTa bhāṣā nyāyo vādo layaḥ kramo yadyadeti śiṣyasya 
AbhTb sambodhopāyatvaṃ tathaiva gururāśrayedvyākhyām  
AbhTa vācyaṃ vastu samāpya pratarpaṇaṃ pūjanaṃ bhaveccakre 
AbhTb punaraparaṃ vastu vadetpaṭalādūrdhvaṃ tu no jalpet  
AbhTa vyākhyānte kṣamayitvā visṛjya sarvaṃ kṣipedagādhajale 
AbhTb śāstrādimadhyanidhane viśeṣataḥ pūjanaṃ kuryāt  
AbhTa viśeṣapūjanaṃ kuryātsamayebhyaśca niṣkṛtau 
AbhTb avikalpamaterna syuḥ prāyaścittāni yadyapi  
AbhTa tathāpyatattvavidvargānugrahāya tathā caret 
AbhTb śrīpicau ca smṛtereva pāpaghnatve kathaṃ vibho  
AbhTa prāyaścittavidhiḥ prokta iti devyā pracodite 
AbhTb satyaṃ smaraṇameveha sakṛjjaptaṃ vimocayet  
AbhTa sarvasmātkarmaṇo jālātsmṛtitattvakalāvidaḥ 
AbhTb tathāpi sthitirakṣārthaṃ kartavyaścodito vidhiḥ  
AbhTa atattvavedino ye hi caryāmātraikaniṣṭhitāḥ 
AbhTb teṣāṃ dolāyite citte jñānahāniḥ prajāyate  
AbhTa tasmādvikalparahitaḥ saṃvṛtyuparato yadi 
AbhTb śāstracaryāsadāyattaiḥ saṅkaraṃ tadvivarjayet  
AbhTa saṅkaraṃ vā samanvicchetprāyaścittaṃ samācaret 
AbhTb yathā teṣāṃ na śāstrārthe dolārūḍhā matirbhavet  
AbhTa yatsvayaṃ śivahastākhye vidhau saṃcoditaṃ purā 
AbhTb śataṃ japtvāsya cāstrasya mucyate strīvadhādṛte  
AbhTa śaktināśānmahādoṣo narakaṃ śāśvataṃ priye 
AbhTb iti śrīratnamālāyāṃ samayollaṅghane kṛte  
AbhTa kulajānāṃ samākhyātā niṣkṛtirduṣṭakartarī 
AbhTb śrīpūrve samayānāṃ tu śodhanāyoditaṃ yathā  
AbhTa mālinī mātṛkā vāpi japyā lakṣatrayāntakam 
AbhTb pratiṣṭhitasya pūrāderdarśanenadhikāriṇā  
AbhTa prāyaścittaṃ prakartavyamiti śrībrahmayāmale 
AbhTb brahmaghno gurutalpastho vīradravyaharastathā  
AbhTa devadravyahṛdākāraprahartā liṅgabhedakaḥ 
AbhTb nityādilopakṛdbhraṣṭasvakamātrāparicchadaḥ  
AbhTa śaktivyaṅgatvakṛdyogijñānihantā vilopakaḥ 
AbhTb naimittikānāṃ lakṣādikramāddvidviguṇaṃ japet  
AbhTa vratena kenacidyukto mitabhugbrahmacaryavān 
AbhTb dūtīparigrahenyatra gataścetkāmamohitaḥ  
AbhTa lakṣajāpaṃ tataḥ kuryādityuktaṃ brahmayāmale 
AbhTb dīkṣābhiṣekanaimittavidhyante gurupūjanam  
AbhTa aparedyuḥ sadā kāryaṃ siddhayogīśvarīmate 
AbhTb pūrvoktalakṣaṇopetaḥ kavistrikasatattvavit  
AbhTa sa guruḥ sarvadā grāhyastyaktvānyaṃ tatsthitaṃ tvapi 
AbhTb maṇḍale svastikaṃ kṛtvā tatra haimādikāsanam  
AbhTa kṛtvārcayeta tatrasthamadhvānaṃ sakalāntakam 
AbhTb tato vijñapayedbhaktyā tadadhiṣṭhitaye gurum  
AbhTa sa tatra pūjyaḥ svairmantraiḥ puṣpadhūpārghavistaraiḥ 
AbhTb samālambhanasadvastrairnaivedyaistarpaṇaiḥ kramāt  
AbhTa āśāntaṃ pūjayitvainaṃ dakṣiṇābhiryajecchiśuḥ 
AbhTb sarvasvamasmai saṃdadyādātmānamapi bhāvitaḥ  
AbhTa atoṣayitvā tu guruṃ dakṣiṇābhiḥ samantataḥ 
AbhTb tattvajñopyṛṇabandhena tena yātyadhikāritām  
AbhTa gurupūjāmakurvāṇaḥ śataṃ janmāni jāyate 
AbhTb adhikārī tato muktiṃ yātīti skandayāmale  
AbhTa tasmādavaśyaṃ dātavyā gurave dakṣiṇā punaḥ 
AbhTb pūrvaṃ hi yāgāṅgatayā proktaṃ tattuṣṭaye tvidam  
AbhTa tajjuṣṭamatha tasyājñāṃ prāpyāśnīyātsvayaṃ śiśuḥ 
AbhTb tataḥ prapūjayeccakraṃ yathāvibhavasambhavam  
AbhTa akṛtvā guruyāgaṃ tu kṛtamapyakṛtaṃ yataḥ 
AbhTb tasmātprayatnataḥ kāryo guruyāgo yathābalam  
AbhTa atatrasthopi hi guruḥ pūjyaḥ saṃkalpya pūrvavat 
AbhTb taddravyaṃ devatākṛtye kuryādbhaktajaneṣvatha  
AbhTa parvapavitraprabhṛtiprabhedi naimittikaṃ tvidaṃ karma 
C atha śrītantrāloke ekonatriṃśamāhnikam
AbhTa atha samucitādhikāriṇa uddiśya rahasya ucyatetra vidhiḥ 
AbhTb atha sarvāpyupāseyaṃ kulaprakriyayocyate  
AbhTa tathā dhārādhirūḍheṣu guruśiṣyeṣu yocitā 
AbhTb uktaṃ ca parameśena sāratvaṃ kramapūjane  
AbhTa siddhakramaniyuktasya māsenaikena yadbhavet 
AbhTb na tadvarṣasahasraiḥ syānmantraughairvividhairiti  
AbhTa kulaṃ ca parameśasya śaktiḥ sāmarthyamūrdhvatā 
AbhTb svātantryamojo vīryaṃ ca piṇḍaḥ saṃviccharīrakam  
AbhTa tathātvena samastāni bhāvajātāni paśyataḥ 
AbhTb dhvastaśaṅkāsamūhasya yāgastādṛśa eva saḥ  
AbhTa tādṛgrūpanirūḍhyarthaṃ manovākkāyavartmanā 
AbhTb yadyatsamācaredvīraḥ kulayāgaḥ sa sa smṛtaḥ  
AbhTa bahiḥ śaktau yāmale ca dehe prāṇapathe matau 
AbhTb iti ṣoḍhā kulejyā syātpratibhedaṃ vibhedinī  
AbhTa snānamaṇḍalakuṇḍādi ṣoḍhānyāsādi yanna tat 
AbhTb kiñcidatropayujyeta kṛtaṃ vā khaṇḍanāya no  
AbhTa ṣaṇmaṇḍalavinirmuktaṃ sarvāvaraṇavarjitam 
AbhTb jñānajñeyamayaṃ kaulaṃ proktaṃ traiśirase mate  
AbhTa atra yāge ca yaddravyaṃ niṣiddhaṃ śāstrasantatau 
AbhTb tadeva yojayeddhīmānvāmāmṛtapariplutam  
AbhTa śrībrahmayāmalepyuktaṃ surā śivaraso bahiḥ 
AbhTb tāṃ vinā bhuktimuktī no piṣṭakṣaudraguḍaistu sā  
AbhTa strīnapuṃsakapuṃrūpā tu pūrvāparabhogadā 
AbhTb drākṣotthaṃ tu paraṃ tejo bhairavaṃ kalpanojjhitam  
AbhTa etatsvayaṃ rasaḥ śuddhaḥ prakāśānandacinmayaḥ 
AbhTb devatānāṃ priyaṃ nityaṃ tasmādetatpivetsadā  
AbhTa śrīmatkramarahasye ca nyarūpi parameśinā 
AbhTb arghapātraṃ yāgadhāma dīpa ityucyate trayam  
AbhTa rahasyaṃ kaulike yāge tatrārghaḥ śaktisaṃgamāt 
AbhTb bhūvastrakāyapīṭhākhyaṃ dhāma cotkarṣabhāk kramāt  
AbhTa dīpā ghṛtotthā gāvo hi bhūcaryo devatāḥ smṛtāḥ 
AbhTb iti jñātvā trayemuṣminyatnavānkauliko bhavet  
AbhTa tenārghapātraprādhānyaṃ jñātvā dravyāṇi śambhunā 
AbhTb yānyuktānyaviśaṅkotra bhavecchaṅkā hi dūṣikā  
AbhTa yāgauko gandhadhūpāḍhyaṃ praviśya prāgudaṅmukhaḥ 
AbhTb parayā vātha mālinyā vilomāccānulomataḥ  
AbhTa dāhāpyāyamayīṃ śuddhiṃ dīptasaumyavibhedataḥ 
AbhTb krameṇa kuryādathavā mātṛsadbhāvamantrataḥ  
AbhTa dīkṣāṃ cetpracikīrṣustacchodhyādhvanyāsakalpanam 
AbhTb tataḥ saṃśodhyavastūni śaktyaivāmṛtatāṃ nayet  
AbhTa parāsampuṭagā yadvā mātṛsampuṭagāpyatho 
AbhTb kevalā mālinī yadvā tāḥ samasteṣu karmasu  
AbhTa nandahetuphalairdravyairarghapātraṃ prapūrayet 
AbhTb tatroktamantratādātmyādbhairavātmatvamānayet  
AbhTa tena nirbharamātmānaṃ bahiścakrānucakragam 
AbhTb vipruḍbhirūrdhvādharayorantaḥ pītyā ca tarpayet  
AbhTa tathā pūrṇasvaraśmyoghaḥ procchaladvṛttitāvaśāt 
AbhTb bahistādṛśamātmānaṃ didṛkṣurbahirarcayet  
AbhTa arkāṅguletha taddvitriguṇe raktapaṭe śubhe 
AbhTb vyomni sindūrasubhage rājavarttabhṛtethavā  
AbhTa nārikelātmake kādye madyapūrṇetha bhājane 
AbhTb yadvā samudite rūpe maṇḍalasthe ca tadṛśi  
AbhTa yāgaṃ kurvīta matimāṃstatrāyaṃ krama ucyate 
AbhTb diśyudīcyāṃ rudrakoṇādvāyavyantaṃ gaṇeśvaram  
AbhTa vaṭukaṃ trīn gurūnsiddhānyoginīḥ pīṭhamarcayet 
AbhTb prācyāṃ diśi gaṇeśādha ārabhyābhyarcayettataḥ  
AbhTa siddhacakraṃ dikcatuṣke gaṇeśādhastanāntakam 
AbhTb khagendraḥ sahavijjāmba illāīambayā saha  
AbhTa vaktaṣṭirvimalonantamekhalāmbāyutaḥ purā 
AbhTb śaktyā maṅgalayā kūrma illāīambayā saha  
AbhTa jaitro yāmye hyavijitastathā sānandamekhalaḥ 
AbhTb kāmamaṅgalayā meṣaḥ kullāīambayā saha  
AbhTa vindhyojitopyajarayā saha mekhalayā pare 
AbhTb macchandaḥ kuṅkuṇāmbā ca ṣaḍyugmaṃ sādhikārakam  
AbhTa saumye marutta īśāntaṃ dvitīyā paṅktirīdṛśī 
AbhTb amaravaradevacitrālivindhyaguḍikā iti kramātṣaḍamī  
AbhTa sillāī eruṇayā tathā kumārī ca bodhāī 
AbhTb samahālacchī cāparamekhalayā śaktayaḥ ṣaḍimāḥ  
AbhTa ete hi sādhikārāḥ pūjyā yeṣāmiyaṃ bahuvibhedā 
AbhTb santatiranavacchinnā citrā śiṣyapraśiṣyamayī  
AbhTa ānandāvalibodhiprabhupādāntātha yogiśabdāntā 
AbhTb etā ovallyaḥ syurmudrāṣaṭkaṃ kramāttvetat  
AbhTa dakṣāṅguṣṭhādikaniṣṭhikāntamatha sā kanīyasī vāmāt 
AbhTb dvidaśāntordhvagakuṇḍalibaindavahṛnnābhikandamiti chu mmāḥ  
AbhTa śavarāḍabillapaṭṭillāḥ karabillāmbiśarabillāḥ 
AbhTb aḍabīḍombīdakṣiṇabillāḥ kumbhārikākṣarākhyāca  
AbhTa devīkoṭṭakulādritripurīkāmākhyamaṭṭahāsaśca 
AbhTb dakṣiṇapīṭhaṃ caitatṣaṭkaṃ gharapallipīṭhagaṃ kramaśaḥ  
AbhTa iti saṅketābhijño bhramate pīṭheṣu yadi sa siddhīpsuḥ 
AbhTb acirāllabhate tattatprāpyaṃ yadyoginīvadanāt  
AbhTa bhaṭṭendravalkalāhīndragajendrāḥ samahīdharāḥ 
AbhTb ūrdhvaretasa ete ṣaḍadhikārapadojjhitāḥ  
AbhTa adhikāro hi vīryasya prasaraḥ kulavartmani 
AbhTb tadaprasarayogena te proktā ūrdhvaretasaḥ  
AbhTa anyāśca gurutatpatnyaḥ śrīmatkālīkuloditāḥ 
AbhTb anāttadehāḥ krīḍanti taistairdehairaśaṅkitāḥ  
AbhTa prabodhitatathecchākaistajje kaulaṃ prakāśate 
AbhTb tathārūpatayā tatra gurutvaṃ paribhāṣitam  
AbhTa te viśeṣānna saṃpūjyāḥ smartavyā eva kevalam 
AbhTb tatobhyantarato vāyuvahnyormātṛkayā saha  
AbhTa mālinī kramaśaḥ pūjyā tatontarmantracakrakam 
AbhTb mantrasiddhaprāṇasaṃvitkaraṇātmani yā kule  
AbhTa cakrātmake citiḥ prabhvī proktā seha kuleśvarī 
AbhTb sā madhye śrīparā devī mātṛsadbhāvarūpiṇī  
AbhTa pūjyātha tatsamāropādaparātha parāparā 
AbhTb ekavīrā ca sā pūjyā yadivā sakuleśvarā  
AbhTa prasarecchaktirucchūnā sollāso bhairavaḥ punaḥ 
AbhTb saṅghaṭṭānandaviśrāntyā yugmamitthaṃ prapūjayet  
AbhTa mahāprakāśarūpāyāḥ saṃvido visphuliṅgavat 
AbhTb yo raśmyoghastamevātra pūjayeddevatāgaṇam  
AbhTa antardvādaśakaṃ pūjyaṃ tatoṣṭāṣṭākameva ca 
AbhTb catuṣkaṃ vā yathecchaṃ vā kā saṅkhyā kila raśmiṣu  
AbhTa māheśī vairiñcī kaumārī vaiṣṇavī caturdikkam 
AbhTb aindrī yāmyā muṇḍā yogeśīrīśatastu koṇeṣu  
AbhTa pavanāntamaghorādikamaṣṭakamasminnathāṣṭake kramaśaḥ 
AbhTb saṅghaṭṭānandadṛśā sampūjyaṃ yāmalībhūtam  
AbhTa aṣṭāṣṭakepi hi vidhau nānānāmaprapañcite bahudhā 
AbhTb vidhireṣa eva vihitastatsaṃkhyā dīpamālā syāt  
AbhTa śrīratnamālāśāstre tu varṇasaṃkhyāḥ pradīpakāḥ 
AbhTb varṇāṃśca mukhyapūjyāyā vidyāyā gaṇayetsudhīḥ  
AbhTa pīṭhakṣetrādibhiḥ sākaṃ kuryādvā kulapūjanam 
AbhTb yathā śrīmādhavakule parameśena bhāṣitam  
AbhTa sṛṣṭisaṃsthitisaṃhārānāmakramacatuṣṭayam 
AbhTb pīṭhaśmaśānasahitaṃ pūjayedbhogamokṣayoḥ  
AbhTa ātmano vāthavā śakteścakrasyātha smaredimam 
AbhTb nyasyatvena vidhiṃ dehe pīṭhākhye pārameśvaram  
AbhTa aṭṭahāsaṃ śikhāsthāne caritraṃ ca karandhrake 
AbhTb śrutyoḥ kaulagiriṃ nāsārandhrayośca jayantikām  
AbhTa bhruvorujjayinīṃ vaktre prayāgaṃ hṛdaye punaḥ 
AbhTb vārāṇasīṃ skandhayuge śrīpīṭhaṃ virajaṃ gale  
AbhTa eḍābhīmudare hālāṃ nābhau kande tu gośrutim 
AbhTb upasthe marukośaṃ ca nagaraṃ pauṇḍravardhanam  
AbhTa elāpuraṃ purastīraṃ sakthyūrvordakṣiṇāditaḥ 
AbhTb kuḍyākeśīṃ ca sopānaṃ māyāpūkṣīrake tathā  
AbhTa jānujaṅghe gulphayugme tvāmrātanṛpasadmanī 
AbhTb pādādhāre tu vairiñcīṃ kālāgnyavadhidārikām  
AbhTa nāhamasmi nacānyosti kevalāḥ śaktayastvaham 
AbhTb ityevaṃvāsanāṃ kuryātsarvadā smṛtimātrataḥ  
AbhTa na tithirna ca nakṣatraṃ nopavāso vidhīyate 
AbhTb grāmyadharmarataḥ siddhyetsarvadā smaraṇena hi  
AbhTa mātaṅgakṛṣṇasaunikakārmukacārmikavikoṣidhātuvibhedāḥ 
AbhTb mātsyikacākrikadayitāsteṣāṃ patnyo navātra navayāge  
AbhTa saṅgamavaruṇākulagiryaṭṭahāsajayantīcaritrakāmrakakoṭṭam 
AbhTb haimapuraṃ navamaṃ syānmadhye tāsāṃ ca cakriṇī mukhyā  
AbhTa bījaṃ sā pīḍayate rasaśalkavibhāgatotra kuṇḍalinī 
AbhTb adhyuṣṭapīṭhanetrī kandasthā viśvato bhramati  
AbhTa iṣṭvā cakrodayaṃ tvitthaṃ madhye pūjyā kuleśvarī 
AbhTb saṅkarṣiṇī tadantānte saṃhārāpyāyakāriṇī  
AbhTa ekavīrā cakrayuktā cakrayāmalagāpi vā 
AbhTb īśendrāgniyamakravyātkavāyūdakṣu hāsataḥ  
AbhTa trikaṃ trikaṃ yajedetadbhāvisvatrikasaṃyutam 
AbhTb hṛtkuṇḍalī bhruvormadhyametadeva kramāttrayam  
AbhTa śmaśānāni kramātkṣetrabhavaṃ sadyoginīgaṇam 
AbhTb vasvaṅgulonnatānūrdhvavartulān kṣāmamadhyakān  
AbhTa raktavartīñśrutidṛśo dīpānkurvīta sarpiṣā 
AbhTb yatkiñcidathavā madhye svānuṣṭhānaṃ prapūjayet  
AbhTa advaitameva na dvaitamityājñā parameśituḥ 
AbhTb siddhāntavaiṣṇavādyuktā mantrā malayutāstataḥ  
AbhTa tāvattejosahiṣṇutvānnirjīvāḥ syurihādvaye 
AbhTb kalaśaṃ netrabandhādi maṇḍalaṃ sruksruvānalam  
AbhTa hitvātra siddhiḥ sanmadye pātre madhye kṛśāṃ yajet 
AbhTb ahorātramimaṃ yāgaṃ kurvataścāparehani  
AbhTa vīrabhojye kṛtevaśyaṃ mantrāḥ siddhyantyayatnataḥ 
AbhTb pīṭhastotraṃ paṭhedatra yāge bhāgyāvahāhvaye  
AbhTa mūrtīrevāthavā yugmarūpā vīrasvarūpiṇīḥ 
AbhTb avadhūtā nirācārāḥ pūjayetkramaśo budhaḥ  
AbhTa eka evātha kauleśaḥ svayaṃ bhūtvāpi tāvatīḥ 
AbhTb śaktīryāmalayogena tarpayedviśvarūpavat  
AbhTa kramo nāma na kaścitsyātprakāśamayasaṃvidi 
AbhTb cidabhāvo hi nāstyeva tenākālaṃ tu tarpaṇam  
AbhTa atra krame bhedataroḥ samūlamunmūlanādāsanapakṣacarcā 
AbhTb pṛthaṅna yuktā parameśvaro hi svaśaktidhāmnīva viśaṃśramīti  
AbhTa tato japaḥ prakartavyastrilakṣādivibhedataḥ 
AbhTb uktaṃ śrīyogasañcāre sa ca citrasvarūpakaḥ  
AbhTa udaye saṅgame śāntau trilakṣo japa ucyate 
AbhTb āsye gamāgame sūtre haṃsākhye śaivayugmake  
AbhTa pañcalakṣā ime proktā daśāṃśaṃ homamācaret 
AbhTb netre gamāgame vaktre haṃse caivākṣasūtrake  
AbhTa śivaśaktisamāyoge ṣaḍlakṣo japa ucyate 
AbhTb netre gamāgame karṇe haṃse vaktre ca bhāmini  
AbhTa haste ca yugmake caiva japaḥ saptavidhaḥ smṛtaḥ 
AbhTb netre gamāgame karṇāvāsyaṃ guhyaṃ ca guhyakam  
AbhTa śatāreṣu ca madhyasthaṃ sahasrāreṣu bhāmini 
AbhTb japa eṣa rudralakṣo homopyatra daśāṃśataḥ  
AbhTa netre gamāgame karṇau mukhaṃ brahmabilāntaram 
AbhTb stanau hastau ca pādau ca guhyacakre dvirabhyaset  
AbhTa yatra yatra gataṃ cakṣuryatra yatra gataṃ manaḥ 
AbhTb haṃsastatra dvirabhyasyo vikāsākuñcanātmakaḥ  
AbhTa sa ātmā mātṛkā devī śivo dehavyavasthitaḥ 
AbhTb anyaḥ sonyohamityevaṃ vikalpaṃ nācaredyataḥ  
AbhTa yo vilpayate tasya siddhimuktī sudūrataḥ 
AbhTb atha ṣoḍaśalakṣādiprāṇacāre puroktavat  
AbhTa śuddhāśuddhavikalpānāṃ tyāga ekānta ucyate 
AbhTb tatrasthaḥ svayamevaiṣa juhoti ca japatyapi  
AbhTa japaḥ sañjalpavṛttiśca nādāmarśasvarūpiṇī 
AbhTb tadāmṛṣṭasya cidvahnau layo homaḥ prakīrtitaḥ  
AbhTa āmarśaśca purā prokto devīdvādaśakātmakaḥ 
AbhTb dve antye saṃvidau tatra layarūpāhutikriyā  
AbhTa daśānyāstadupāyāyetyevaṃ home daśāṃśatām 
AbhTb śrīśambhunātha ādikṣattrikārthāmbhodhicandramāḥ  
AbhTa sākaṃ bāhyasthayā śaktyā yadā tveṣa samarcayet 
AbhTb tadāyaṃ parameśokto rahasyo bhaṇyate vidhiḥ  
AbhTa uktaṃ śrīyogasañcāre brahmacarye sthitiṃ bhajet 
AbhTb ānando brahma paramaṃ tacca dehe tridhā sthitam  
AbhTa upakāri dvayaṃ tatra phalamanyattadātmakam 
AbhTb oṣṭhyāntyatritayāsevī brahmacārī sa ucyate  
AbhTa tadvarjitā ye paśava ānandaparivarjitāḥ 
AbhTb ānandakṛttrimāhārāstadvarjaṃ cakrayājakāḥ  
AbhTa dvayepi niraye yānti raurave bhīṣaṇe tviti 
AbhTb śakterlakṣaṇametāvattadvato hyavibheditā  
AbhTa tādṛśīṃ tena tāṃ kuryānnatu varṇādyapekṣaṇam 
AbhTb laukikālaukikadvyātmasaṅgāttādātmyatodhikāt  
AbhTa kāryahetusahotthā sā tridhoktā śāsane guroḥ 
AbhTb sākṣātparamparāyogāttattulyeti tridhā punaḥ  
AbhTa śrīsarvācārahṛdaye tadetadupasaṃhṛtam 
AbhTb ṣaḍetāḥ śaktayaḥ proktā bhuktimuktiphalapradāḥ  
AbhTa dvābhyāṃ tu sṛṣṭisaṃhārau tasmānmelakamuttamam 
AbhTb tāmāhṛtya mithobhyarcya tarpayitvā parasparam  
AbhTa antaraṅgakrameṇaiva mukhyacakrasya pūjanam 
AbhTb yadevānandasandohi saṃvido hyantaraṅgakam  
AbhTa tatpradhānaṃ bhaveccakramanucakramatoparam 
AbhTb vikāsāttṛptitaḥ pāśotkartanātkṛtiśaktitaḥ  
AbhTa cakraṃ kaseścakeḥ kṛtyā karoteśca kiloditam 
AbhTb yāgaśca tarpaṇaṃ bāhye vikāsastacca kīrtyate  
AbhTa cakrānucakrāntaragācchaktimatparikalpitāt 
AbhTb prāṇagādapyathānandasyandinobhyavahārataḥ  
AbhTa gandhadhūpasragādeśca bāhyāducchalanaṃ citaḥ 
AbhTb itthaṃ svocitavastvaṃśairanucakreṣu tarpaṇam  
AbhTa kurvīyātāmihānyonyaṃ mukhyacakraikatākṛte 
AbhTb uktaṃ ca triśirastantre vimalāsanagocaraḥ  
AbhTa akṣaṣaṭkasya madhye tu rudrasthānaṃ samāviśet 
AbhTb nijanijabhogābhogapravikāsinijasvarūpaparimarśe  
AbhTa kramaśonucakradevyaḥ saṃviccakraṃ hi madhyamaṃ yānti 
AbhTb svasthatanoraparasya tu tā dehādhiṣṭhitaṃ vihāya yataḥ  
AbhTa āsata iti tadahaṃyurno pūrṇo nāpi cocchalati 
AbhTb anucakradevatātmakamarīciparipūraṇādhigatavīryam  
AbhTa tacchaktiśaktimadyugamanyonyasamunmukhaṃ bhavati 
AbhTb tadyugalamūrdhvadhāmapraveśasaṃsparśajātasaṅkṣobham  
AbhTa kṣubhnātyanucakrāṇyapi tāni tadā tanmayāni na pṛthaktu 
AbhTb itthaṃ yāmalametadgalitabhidāsaṃkathaṃ yadeva syāt  
AbhTa kramatāratamyayogātsaiva hi saṃvidvisargasaṅghaṭṭaḥ 
AbhTb taddhruvadhāmānuttaramubhayātmakajagadudārasānandam  
AbhTa no śāntaṃ nāpyuditaṃ śāntoditasūtikāraṇaṃ paraṃ kaulam 
AbhTb anavacchinnapadepsustāṃ saṃvidamātmasātsadā kuryāt  
AbhTa anavacchinnaṃ paramārthato hi rūpaṃ cito devyāḥ 
AbhTb īdṛktādṛkprāyapraśamodayabhāvavilayaparikathayā  
AbhTa anavacchinnaṃ dhāma praviśedvaisargikaṃ subhagaḥ 
AbhTb śāntoditātmakaṃ dvayamatha yugapadudeti śaktiśaktimatoḥ  
AbhTa rūpamuditaṃ parasparadhāmagataṃ śāntamātmagatameva 
AbhTb ubhayamapi vastutaḥ kila yāmalamiti tathoditaṃ śāntam  
AbhTa śaktistadvaducitāṃ sṛṣṭiṃ puṣṇāti no tadvān 
AbhTb śāntoditātmakobhayarūpaparāmarśasāmyayogepi  
AbhTa pravikasvaramadhyapadā śaktiḥ śāstre tataḥ kathitā 
AbhTb tasyāmeva kulārthaṃ samyak saṃcārayedgurustena  
AbhTa taddvāreṇa ca kathitakrameṇa saṃcārayeta nṛṣu 
AbhTb svaśarīrādhikasadbhāvabhāvitāmiti tataḥ prāha  
AbhTa śrīmatkallaṭanāthaḥ proktasamastārthalabdhaye vākyam 
AbhTb tanmukhyacakramuktaṃ maheśinā yoginīvaktram  
AbhTa tatraiṣa sampradāyastasmātsaṃprāpyate jñānam 
AbhTb tadidamalekhyaṃ bhaṇitaṃ vaktrādvaktrasthamuktayuktyā ca  
AbhTa vaktraṃ pradhānacakraṃ svā saṃvillikhyatāṃ ca katham 
AbhTb atha sṛṣṭe dvitayesmin śāntoditadhāmni yenusaṃdadhate  
AbhTa prācyāṃ visargasattāmanavacchidi te pade rūḍhāḥ 
AbhTb ye siddhimāptukāmāstebhyuditaṃ rūpamāhareyuratho  
AbhTa tenaiva pūjayeyuḥ saṃvinnaikaṭyaśuddhatamavapuṣā 
AbhTb tadapica mitho hi vaktrātpradhānato vaktragaṃ yato bhaṇitam  
AbhTa ajarāmarapadadānapravaṇaṃ kulasaṃjñitaṃ paramam 
AbhTb yepyaprāptavibodhāstebhyuditotphullayāgasaṃrūḍhāḥ  
AbhTa tatparikalpitacakrasthadevatāḥ prāpnuvanti vijñānam 
AbhTb te tatra śakticakre tenaivānandarasamayena bahiḥ  
AbhTa dikṣu catasṛṣu proktakrameṇa gaṇanāthataḥ prabhṛti sarvam 
AbhTb saṃpūjya madhyamapade kuleśayugmaṃ tvarātraye devīḥ  
AbhTa bāhye pratyaramatha kila catuṣkamiti raśmicakramarkāram 
AbhTb aṣṭakamaṣṭāṣṭakamatha vividhaṃ saṃpūjayetkrameṇa muniḥ  
AbhTa nijadehagate dhāmani tathaiva pūjyaṃ samabhyasyet 
AbhTb yattacchāntaṃ rūpaṃ tenābhyastena hṛdayasaṃvittyā  
AbhTa śāntaṃ śivapadameti hi galitataraṅgārṇavaprakhyam 
AbhTb tacchāntapadādhyāsāccakrastho devatāgaṇaḥ sarvaḥ  
AbhTa tiṣṭhatyuparatavṛttiḥ śūnyālambī nirānandaḥ 
AbhTb yopyanucakradṛgādisvarūpabhāk sopi yattadāyattaḥ  
AbhTa tenānande magnastiṣṭhatyānandasākāṅkṣaḥ 
AbhTb paratatsvarūpasaṅghaṭṭamantareṇaiṣa karaṇaraśmigaṇaḥ  
AbhTa āste hi niḥsvarūpaḥ svarūpalābhāya conmukhitaḥ 
AbhTb raṇaraṇakarasānnijarasabharitabahirbhāvacarvaṇavaśena  
AbhTa viśrāntidhāma kiñcillabdhvā svātmanyathārpayate 
AbhTb tannijaviṣayārpaṇataḥ pūrṇasamucchalitasaṃvidāsāraḥ  
AbhTa anucakradevatāgaṇaparipūraṇajātavīryavikṣobhaḥ 
AbhTb cakreśvaropi pūrvoktayuktitaḥ procchaledrabhasāt  
AbhTa trividho visarga itthaṃ saṅghaṭṭaḥ proditastathā śāntaḥ 
AbhTb visṛjati yato vicitraḥ sargo vigataśca yatra sarga iti  
AbhTa śrītattvarakṣaṇe śrīnigame triśiromate ca tatproktam 
AbhTb kuṇḍaṃ śaktiḥ śivo liṅgaṃ melakaṃ paramaṃ padam  
AbhTa dvābhyāṃ sṛṣṭiḥ saṃhṛtistadvisargastrividho game 
AbhTb srotodvayasya niṣṭhāntamūrdhvādhaścakrabodhanam  
AbhTa viśrāmaṃ ca samāveśaṃ suṣīṇāṃ marutāṃ tathā 
AbhTb gatabhedaṃ ca yantrāṇāṃ sandhīnāṃ marmaṇāmapi  
AbhTa dvāsaptatipade dehe sahasrāre ca nityaśaḥ 
AbhTb gatyāgatyantarā vittī saṅghaṭṭayati yacchivaḥ  
AbhTa tatprayatnātsadā tiṣṭhetsaṅghaṭṭe bhairave pade 
AbhTb ubhayostannirākārabhāvasaṃprāptilakṣaṇam  
AbhTa mātrāvibhāgarahitaṃ susphuṭārthaprakāśakam 
AbhTb abhyasyedbhāvasaṃvittiṃ sarvabhāvanivartanāt  
AbhTa sūryasomau tu saṃrudhya layavikṣepamārgataḥ 
AbhTb evaṃ trividhavimarśāveśasamāpattidhāmni ya udeti  
AbhTa saṃvitparimarśātmā dhvanistadeveha mantravīryaṃ syāt 
AbhTb tatraivoditatādṛśaphalalābhasamutsukaḥ svakaṃ mantram  
AbhTa anusandhāya sadā cedāste mantrodayaṃ sa vai vetti 
AbhTb atraiva japaṃ kuryādanucakraikatvasaṃvidāgamane  
AbhTa yugapallakṣavibhedaprapañcitaṃ nādavṛttyaiva 
AbhTb śrīyogasañcarepica mudreyaṃ yoginīpriyā paramā  
AbhTa koṇatrayāntarāśritanityonmukhamaṇḍalacchade kamale 
AbhTb satatāviyutaṃ nālaṃ ṣoḍaśadalakamalakalitasanmūlam  
AbhTa madhyasthanālagumphitasarojayugaghaṭṭanakramādagnau 
AbhTb madhyasthapūrṇasundaraśaśadharadinakarakalaughasaṅghaṭṭāt  
AbhTa tridalāruṇavīryakalāsaṅgānmadhyeṅkuraḥ sṛṣṭiḥ 
AbhTb iti śaśadharavāsarapaticitragusaṃghaṭṭamudrayā jhaṭiti  
AbhTa sṛṣṭyādikramamantaḥ kurvaṃsturye sthitiṃ labhate 
AbhTb etatkhecaramudrāveśenyonyasya śaktiśaktimatoḥ  
AbhTa pānopabhogalīlāhāsādiṣu yo bhavedvimarśamayaḥ 
AbhTb avyaktadhvanirāvasphoṭaśrutinādanādāntaiḥ  
AbhTa avyucchinnānāhatarūpaistanmantravīryaṃ syāt 
AbhTb iti cakrāṣṭakarūḍhaḥ sahajaṃ japamācaran pare dhāmni  
AbhTa yadbhairavāṣṭakapadaṃ tallabhateṣṭakakalābhinnam 
AbhTb gamanāgamanevasitau karṇe nayane dviliṅgasaṃparke  
AbhTa tatsaṃmelanayoge dehāntākhye ca yāmale cakre 
AbhTb kucamadhyahṛdayadeśādoṣṭhāntaṃ kaṇṭhagaṃ yadavyaktam  
AbhTa taccakradvayamadhyagamākarṇya kṣobhavigamasamaye yat 
AbhTb nirvānti tatra caivaṃ yoṣṭavidho nādabhairavaḥ paramaḥ  
AbhTa jyotirdhvanisamirakṛtaḥ sā māntrī vyāptirucyate paramā 
AbhTb sakalākaleśaśūnyaṃ kalāḍhyakhamale tathā kṣapaṇakaṃ ca  
AbhTa antaḥsthaṃ kaṇṭhyoṣṭhyaṃ candrādvyāptistathonmanānteyam 
AbhTb evaṃ karmaṇi karmaṇi yatra kvāpi smaran vyāptim  
AbhTa satatamalepo jīvanmuktaḥ parabhairavībhavati 
AbhTb tādṛṅmelakakalikākalitatanuḥ kopi yo bhavedgarbhe  
AbhTa uktaḥ sa yoginībhūḥ svayameva jñānabhājanaṃ rudraḥ 
AbhTb śrīvīrāvaliśāstre bālopi ca garbhago hi śivarūpaḥ  
AbhTa ādīyate yataḥ sāraṃ tasya mukhyasya caiṣa yat 
AbhTb mukhyaśca yāgastenāyamādiyāga iti smṛtaḥ  
AbhTa tatra tatra ca śāstresya svarūpaṃ stutavān vibhuḥ 
AbhTb śrīvīrāvalihārdeśakhamatārṇavavartiṣu  
AbhTa śrīsiddhotphullamaryādāhīnacaryākulādiṣu 
AbhTb yugmasyāsya prasādena vratayogavivarjitaḥ  
AbhTa sarvadā smaraṇaṃ kṛtvā ādiyāgaikatatparaḥ 
AbhTb śaktidehe nije nyasyedvidyāṃ kūṭamanukramāt  
AbhTa dhyātvā candranibhaṃ padmamātmānaṃ bhāskaradyutim 
AbhTb vidyāmantrātmakaṃ pīṭhadvayamatraiva melayet  
AbhTa na paṭhyate rahasyatvātspaṣṭaiḥ śabdairmayā punaḥ 
AbhTb kutūhalī tūktaśāstrasaṃpāṭhādeva lakṣayet  
AbhTa yadbhajante sadā sarve yadvān devaśca devatā 
AbhTb taccakraṃ paramaṃ devīyāgādau saṃnidhāpakam  
AbhTa deha eva paraṃ liṅgaṃ sarvatattvātmakaṃ śivam 
AbhTb devatācakrasaṃjuṣṭaṃ pūjādhāma taduttamam  
AbhTa tadeva maṇḍalaṃ mukhyaṃ tritriśūlābjacakrakham 
AbhTb tatraiva devatācakraṃ bahirantaḥ sadā yajet  
AbhTa svasvamantraparāmarśapūrvaṃ tajjanmabhī rasaiḥ 
AbhTb ānandabahulaiḥ sṛṣṭisaṃhāravidhinā spṛśet  
AbhTa tatsparśarabhasodbuddhasaṃviccakraṃ tadīśvaraḥ 
AbhTb labhate paramaṃ dhāma tarpitāśeṣadaivataḥ  
AbhTa anuyāgoktavidhinā dravyairhṛdayahāribhiḥ 
AbhTb tathaiva svasvakāmarśayogādantaḥ pratarpayet  
AbhTa kṛtvādhāradharāṃ camatkṛtirasaprokṣākṣaṇakṣālitāmāttairmānasataḥ svabhāvakusumaiḥ svāmodasandohibhiḥ 
AbhTb ānandāmṛtanirbharasvahṛdayānarghārghapātrakramāt tvāṃ devyā saha dehadevasadane devārcayeharniśam  
AbhTa śrīvīrāvalyamaryādaprabhṛtau śāstrasañcaye 
AbhTb sa eṣa paramo yāgaḥ stutaḥ śītāṃśumaulinā  
AbhTa athavā prāṇavṛttisthaṃ samastaṃ devatāgaṇam 
AbhTb paśyetpūrvoktayuktyaiva tatraivābhyarcayedguruḥ  
AbhTa prāṇāśritānāṃ devīnāṃ brahmanāsādibhedibhiḥ 
AbhTb karandhrairviśatāpānacāndracakreṇa tarpaṇam  
AbhTa evaṃ prāṇakrameṇaiva tarpayeddevatāgaṇam 
AbhTb acirāttatprasādena jñānasiddhīrathāśnute  
AbhTa saṃvinmātrasthitaṃ devīcakraṃ vā saṃvidarpaṇāt 
AbhTb viśvābhogaprayogeṇa tarpaṇīyaṃ vipaścitā  
AbhTa yatra sarve layaṃ yānti dahyante tattvasañcayāḥ 
AbhTb tāṃ citiṃ paśya kāyasthāṃ kālānalasamaprabhām  
AbhTa śūnyarūpe śmaśānesmin yoginīsiddhasevite 
AbhTb krīḍāsthāne mahāraudre sarvāstamitavigrahe  
AbhTa svaraśmimaṇḍalākīrṇe dhvaṃsitadhvāntasantatau 
AbhTb sarvairvikalpairnirmukte ānandapadakevale  
AbhTa asaṃkhyacitisaṃpūrṇe śmaśāne citibhīṣaṇe 
AbhTb samastadevatādhāre praviṣṭaḥ ko na siddhyati  
AbhTa śrīmadvīrāvalīśāstre itthaṃ provāca bhairavī 
AbhTb itthaṃ yāgaṃ vidhāyādau tādṛśaucityabhāginam  
AbhTa lakṣaikīyaṃ svaśiṣyaṃ taṃ dīkṣayettādṛśi krame 
AbhTb rudraśaktyā tu taṃ prokṣya devābhyāśe niveśayet  
AbhTa bhujau tasya samālokya rudraśaktyā pradīpayet 
AbhTb tayaivāsyārpayetpuṣpaṃ karayorgandhadigdhayoḥ  
AbhTa nirālambau tu tau tasya sthāpayitvā vicintayet 
AbhTb rudraśaktyākṛṣyamāṇau dīptayāṅkuśarūpayā  
AbhTa tataḥ sa svayamādāya vastraṃ baddhadṛśirbhavet 
AbhTb svayaṃ ca pātayetpuṣpaṃ tatpātāllakṣayetkulam  
AbhTa tatosya mukhamuddhāṭya pādayoḥ praṇipātayet 
AbhTb hastayormūrdhni cāpyasya devīcakraṃ samarcayet  
AbhTa ākarṣyākarṣakatvena preryaprerakabhāvataḥ 
AbhTb uktaṃ śrīratnamālāyāṃ nābhiṃ daṇḍena saṃpuṭam  
AbhTa vāmabhūṣaṇajaṅghābhyāṃ nitambenāpyalaṅkṛtam 
AbhTb śiṣyahaste puṣpabhṛte codanāstraṃ tu yojayet  
AbhTa yāvatsa stobhamāyātaḥ svayaṃ patati mūrdhani 
AbhTb śivahastaḥ svayaṃ soyaṃ sadyaḥpratyayakārakaḥ  
AbhTa anenaiva prayogeṇa carukaṃ grāhayedguruḥ 
AbhTb śiṣyeṇa dantakāṣṭhaṃ ca tatpātaḥ prāgvadeva tu  
AbhTa karastobho netrapaṭagrahāt prabhṛti yaḥ kila 
AbhTb dantakāṣṭhasamādānaparyantastatra lakṣayet  
AbhTa tīvramandādibhedena śaktipātaṃ tathāvidham 
AbhTb ityeṣa samayī proktaḥ śrīpūrve karakampataḥ  
AbhTa samayī tu karastobhāditi śrībhogahastake 
AbhTb carveva vā gururdadyādvāmāmṛtapariplutam  
AbhTa niḥśaṅkaṃ grahaṇācchaktigotro māyojjhito bhavet 
AbhTb sakampastvādadānaḥ syāt samayī vācanādiṣu  
AbhTa kālāntaredhvasaṃśuddhyā pālanātsamayasthiteḥ 
AbhTb siddhipātramiti śrīmadānandeśvara ucyate  
AbhTa yadā tu putrakaṃ kuryāttadā dīkṣāṃ samācaret 
AbhTb uktaṃ śrīratnamālāyāṃ nādiphāntāṃ jvalatprabhām  
AbhTa nyasyecchikhāntaṃ patati tenātredṛk kramo bhavet 
AbhTb prokṣitasya śiśornyastaproktaśodhyādhvapaddhateḥ  
AbhTa ṛjudehajuṣaḥ śaktiṃ pādānmūrdhāntamāgatām 
AbhTb pāśāndahantīṃ saṃdīptāṃ cintayettanmayo guruḥ  
AbhTa upaviśya tatastasya mūlaśodhyāt prabhṛtyalam 
AbhTb antaśodhyāvasānāntāṃ dahantīṃ cintayetkramāt  
AbhTa evaṃ sarvāṇi śodhyāni tattvādīni puroktavat 
AbhTb dagdhvā līnāṃ śive dhyāyenniṣkale sakalethavā  
AbhTa yoginā yojitā mārge sajātīyasya poṣaṇam 
AbhTb kurute nirdahatyantadbhinnajātikadambakam  
AbhTa anayā śodhyamānasya śiśostīvrādibhedataḥ 
AbhTb śaktipātāccitivyomaprāṇanāntarbahistanūḥ  
AbhTa āviśantī rudraśaktiḥ kramātsūte phalaṃ tvidam 
AbhTb ānandamudbhavaṃ kampaṃ nidrāṃ ghūrṇiṃ ca dehagām  
AbhTa evaṃ stobhitapāśasya yojitasyātmanaḥ śive 
AbhTb śeṣabhogāya kurvīta sṛṣṭiṃ saṃśuddhatattvagām  
AbhTa athavā kasyacinnaivamāveśastaddahedimam 
AbhTb bahirantaścoktaśaktyā pateditthaṃ sa bhūtale  
AbhTa yasya tvevamapi syānna tamatropalavattyajet 
AbhTb atha sapratyayāṃ dīkṣāṃ vakṣye tuṣṭena dhīmatā  
AbhTa śaṃbhunāthenopadiṣṭāṃ dṛṣṭāṃ sadbhāvaśāsane 
AbhTb sudhāgnimaruto mandaparakālāgnivāyavaḥ  
AbhTa vahnisaudhāsukūṭāgnivāyuḥ sarve saṣaṣṭhakāḥ 
AbhTb etatpiṇḍatrayaṃ stobhakāri pratyekamucyate  
AbhTa śaktibījaṃ smṛtaṃ yacca nyasyetsārvāṅgikaṃ tu tat 
AbhTb hṛccakre nyasyate mantro dvādaśasvarabhūṣitaḥ  
AbhTa japākusumasaṃkāśaṃ caitanyaṃ tasya madhyataḥ 
AbhTb vāyunā preritaṃ cakraṃ vahninā paridīpitam  
AbhTa taddhyāyecca japenmantraṃ nāmāntaritayogataḥ 
AbhTb nimeṣārdhāttu śiṣyasya bhavetstobho na saṃśayaḥ  
AbhTa ātmānaṃ prekṣate devi tattve tattve niyojitaḥ 
AbhTb yāvatprāptaḥ paraṃ tattvaṃ tadā tveṣa na paśyati  
AbhTa anena kramayogena sarvādhvānaṃ sa paśyati 
AbhTb athavā sarvaśāstrāṇyapyudgrāhayati tatkṣaṇāt  
AbhTa pṛthaktattvavidhau dīkṣāṃ yogyatāvaśavartinaḥ 
AbhTb tattvābhyāsavidhānena siddhayogī samācaret  
AbhTa iti saṃdīkṣitasyāsya mumukṣoḥ śeṣavartane 
AbhTb kulakrameṣṭirādeśyā pañcāvasthāsamanvitā  
AbhTa jāgradādiṣu saṃvittiryathā syādanapāyinī 
AbhTb kulayāgastathādeśyo yoginīmukhasaṃsthitaḥ  
AbhTa sarvaṃ jāgrati kartavyaṃ svapne pratyekamantragam 
AbhTb nivārya supte mūlākhyaḥ svaśaktiparibṛṃhitaḥ  
AbhTa turye tvekaiva dūtyākhyā tadatīte kuleśitā 
AbhTb svaśaktiparipūrṇānāmitthaṃ pūjā pravartate  
AbhTa piṇḍasthādi ca pūrvoktaṃ sarvātītāvasānakam 
AbhTb avasthāpañcakaṃ proktabhedaṃ tasmai nirūpayet  
AbhTa sādhakasya bubhukṣostu samyagyogābhiṣecanam 
AbhTb tatreṣṭvā vibhavairdevaṃ hemādimayamavraṇam  
AbhTa dīpāṣṭakaṃ raktavartisarpiṣāpūrya bodhayet 
AbhTb kulāṣṭakena tatpūjyaṃ śaṅkhe cāpi kuleśvarau  
AbhTa ānandāmṛtasaṃpūrṇe śivahastoktavartmanā 
AbhTb tenābhiṣiñcettaṃ paścāt sa kuryānmantrasādhanam  
AbhTa ācāryasyābhiṣekoyamadhikārānvitaḥ sa tu 
AbhTb kuryātpiṣṭādibhiścāsya catuṣṣaṣṭiṃ pradīpakān  
AbhTa aṣṭāṣṭakena pūjyāste madhye prāgvat kuleśvarau 
AbhTb śivahastoktayuktyaiva gurumapyabhiṣecayet  
AbhTa abhiṣiktāvimāvevaṃ sarvayogigaṇena tu 
AbhTb viditau bhavatastatra gururmokṣaprado bhavet  
AbhTa tātparyamasya pādasya sa siddhīḥ saṃprayacchati 
AbhTb gururyaḥ sādhakaḥ prāksyādanyo mokṣaṃ dadātyalam  
AbhTa anayoḥ kathayejjñānaṃ trividhaṃ sarvamapyalam 
AbhTb svakīyājñāṃ ca vitaret svakriyākaraṇaṃ prati  
AbhTa ṣaṭkaṃ kāraṇasaṃjñaṃ yattathā yaḥ paramaḥ śivaḥ 
AbhTb sākaṃ bhairavanāthena tadaṣṭakamudāhṛtam  
AbhTa pratyekaṃ tasya sārvātmyaṃ paśyaṃstāṃ vṛttimātmagām 
AbhTb cakṣurādau saṃkramayedyatra yatrendriye guruḥ  
AbhTa sa eva pūrṇaiḥ kalaśairabhiṣekaḥ paraḥ smṛtaḥ 
AbhTb vinā bāhyairapītyuktaṃ śrīvīrāvalibhairave  
AbhTa sadya eva tu bhogepsoryogātsiddhatamo guruḥ 
AbhTb kuryātsadyastathābhīṣṭaphaladaṃ vedhadīkṣaṇam  
AbhTa vedhadīkṣā ca bahudhā tatra tatra nirūpitā 
AbhTb sā cābhyāsavatā kāryā yenordhvordhvapraveśataḥ  
AbhTa śiṣyasya cakrasaṃbhedapratyayo jāyate dhruvaḥ 
AbhTb yenāṇimādikā siddhiḥ śrīmālāyāṃ ca coditā  
AbhTa ūrdhvacakradaśālābhe piśācāveśa eva sā 
AbhTb mantranādabinduśaktibhujaṅgamaparātmikā  
AbhTa ṣoḍhā śrīgahvare vedhadīkṣoktā parameśinā 
AbhTb jvālākulaṃ svaśāstroktaṃ cakramaṣṭārakādikam  
AbhTa dhyātvā tenāsya hṛccakravedhanānmantravedhanam 
AbhTb ākāraṃ navadhā dehe nyasya saṃkramayettataḥ  
AbhTa nyāsayogena śiṣyāya dīpyamānaṃ mahārciṣam 
AbhTb pāśastobhāttatastasya paratattve tu yojanam  
AbhTa iti dīkṣottare dṛṣṭo vidhirme śaṃbhunoditaḥ 
AbhTb nādoccāreṇa nādākhyaḥ sṛṣṭikramaniyogataḥ  
AbhTa nādena vedhayeccittaṃ nādavedha udīritaḥ 
AbhTb bindusthānagataṃ cittaṃ bhrūmadhyapathasaṃsthitam  
AbhTa hṛllakṣye vā maheśāni binduṃ jvālākulaprabham 
AbhTb tena saṃbodhayetsādhyaṃ bindvākhyoyaṃ prakīrtitaḥ  
AbhTa śāktaṃ śaktimaduccārādgandhoccāreṇa sundari 
AbhTb śṛṅgāṭakāsanasthaṃ tu kuṭilaṃ kuṇḍalākṛtim  
AbhTa anuccāreṇa coccārya vedhayennikhilaṃ jagat 
AbhTb evaṃ bhramaravedhena śāktavedha udāhṛtaḥ  
AbhTa sā caiva paramā śaktirānandapravikāsinī 
AbhTb janmasthānātparaṃ yāti phaṇapañcakabhūṣitā  
AbhTa kalāstattvāni nandādyā vyomāni ca kulāni ca 
AbhTb brahmādikāraṇānyakṣāṇyeva sā pañcakātmikā  
AbhTa evaṃ pañcaprakārā sā brahmasthānavinirgatā 
AbhTb brahmasthāne viśantī tu taḍillīnā virājate  
AbhTa praviṣṭā vedhayetkāyamātmānaṃ pratibhedayet 
AbhTb evaṃ bhujaṅgavedhastu kathito bhairavāgame  
AbhTa tāvadbhāvayate cittaṃ yāvaccittaṃ kṣayaṃ gatam 
AbhTb kṣīṇe citte sureśāni parānanda udāhṛtaḥ  
AbhTa nendriyāṇi na vai prāṇā nāntaḥkaraṇagocaraḥ 
AbhTb na mano nāpi mantavyaṃ na mantā na manikriyā  
AbhTa sarvabhāvaparikṣīṇaḥ paravedha udāhṛtaḥ 
AbhTb manuśaktibhuvanarūpajñāpiṇḍasthānanāḍiparabhedāt  
AbhTa navadhā kalayantyanye vedaṃ guravo rahasyavidaḥ 
AbhTb māyāgarbhāgnivarṇaughayukte tryaśriṇi maṇḍale  
AbhTa dhyātvā jvālākarālena tena granthīn vibhedayet 
AbhTb puṣpairhanyādyojayecca pare mantrābhidho vidhiḥ  
AbhTa nāḍyāviśyānyatarayā caitanyaṃ kandadhāmani 
AbhTb piṇḍīkṛtya paribhramya pañcāṣṭaśikhayā haṭhāt  
AbhTa śaktiśūlāgragamitaṃ kvāpi cakre niyojayet 
AbhTb śaktyeti śākto vedhoyaṃ sadyaḥpratyayakārakaḥ  
AbhTa ādhārānnirgatayā śikhayā jyotsnāvadātayā rabhasāt 
AbhTb aṅguṣṭhamūlapīṭhakrameṇa śiṣyasya līnayā vyomni  
AbhTa dehaṃ svacchīkṛtya kṣādīnāntān smaranpuroktapuryoghān 
AbhTb nijamaṇḍalanirdhyānātpratibimbayate bhuvanavedhaḥ  
AbhTa bhrūmadhyoditabaindavadhāmāntaḥ kāṃcidākṛtiṃ rucirām 
AbhTb tādātmyena dhyāyecchiṣyaṃ paścācca tanmayīkuryāt  
AbhTa iti rūpavedha uktaḥ sā cehākṛtirupaiti dṛśyatvam 
AbhTb ante tatsāyujyaṃ śiṣyaścāyāti tanmayībhūtaḥ  
AbhTa vijñānamaṣṭadhā yaddhrāṇādikabuddhisaṃjñakaraṇāntaḥ 
AbhTb tat svasvanāḍisūtrakrameṇa saṃcārayecchiṣye  
AbhTa abhimānadārḍhyabandhakrameṇa vijñānasaṃjñako vedhaḥ 
AbhTb hṛdayavyomani sadyo divyajñānārkasamudayaṃ dhatte  
AbhTa piṇḍaḥ paraḥ kalātmā sūkṣmaḥ puryaṣṭako bahiḥ sthūlaḥ 
AbhTb chāyātmā sa parāṅmukha ādarśādau ca saṃmukho jñeyaḥ  
AbhTa iti yaḥ piṇḍavibhedastaṃ rabhasāduttarottare śamayet 
AbhTb tattadnalane kramaśaḥ paramapadaṃ piṇḍavedhena  
AbhTa yadyaddehe cakraṃ tatra śiśoretya viśramaṃ kramaśaḥ 
AbhTb ujjvalayettaccakraṃ sthānākhyastatphalaprado vedhaḥ  
AbhTa nāḍyaḥ pradhānabhūtāstisronyāstadgatāstvasaṃkhyeyāḥ 
AbhTb ekīkārastābhirnāḍīvedhotra tatphalakṛt  
AbhTa abhilaṣitanāḍivāho mukhyābhiścakṣurādiniṣṭhābhiḥ 
AbhTb adbodhaprāptiḥ syānnāḍīvedhe vicitrabahurūpā  
AbhTa lāṅgūlākṛtibalavat svanāḍisaṃvoṣṭitāmaparanāḍīm 
AbhTb āsphoṭya siddhamapi bhuvi pātayati haṭhānmahāyogī  
AbhTa paravedhaṃ samasteṣu cakreṣvadvaitamāmṛśan 
AbhTb paraṃ śivaṃ prakurvīta śivatāpattido guruḥ  
AbhTa śrīmadvīrāvalikule tathā cetthaṃ nirūpitam 
AbhTb abhedyaṃ sarvathā jñeyaṃ madhyaṃ jñātvā na lipyate  
AbhTa tadvibhāgakrame siddhaḥ sa gururmocayet paśūn 
AbhTb guroragre viśecchiṣyo vaktraṃ vaktre tu vedhayet  
AbhTa rūpaṃ rūpe tu viṣayairyāvatsamarasībhavet 
AbhTb citte samarasībhūte dvayoraunmanasī sthitiḥ  
AbhTa ubhayośconmanogatyā tatkāle dīkṣito bhavet 
AbhTb śaśibhāskarasaṃyoge jīvastanmayatāṃ vrajet  
AbhTa atra brahmādayo devā muktaye mokṣakāṅkṣiṇaḥ 
AbhTb nirudhya raśmicakraṃ svaṃ bhogamokṣāvubhāvapi  
AbhTa grasate yadi taddīkṣā śārvīyaṃ parikīrtitā 
AbhTb sa eṣa mokṣaḥ kathito niḥspandaḥ sarvajantuṣu  
AbhTa agnīṣomakalāghātasaṅghātāt spandanaṃ haret 
AbhTb bāhyaṃ prāṇaṃ bāhyagataṃ timirākārayogataḥ  
AbhTa niryātaṃ romakūpaistu bhramantaṃ sarvakāraṇaiḥ 
AbhTb madhyaṃ nirlakṣyamāsthāya bhramayedvisṛjettataḥ  
AbhTa saṃghaṭṭotpāṭayogena vedhayedgranthipañcakam 
AbhTb saṃghaṭṭavṛttiyugalaṃ madhyadhāma vicintayet  
AbhTa nātmavyomabahirmantradehasaṃdhānamācaret 
AbhTb dīkṣeyaṃ sarvajantūnāṃ śivatāpattidāyikā  
AbhTa dīkṣānte dīpakān paktvā samastaiḥ sādhakaiḥ saha 
AbhTb caruḥ prāśyaḥ kulācāryairmahāpātakanāśanaḥ  
AbhTa iti śrīratnamālāyāmūnādhikavidhistu yaḥ 
AbhTb sa eva pātakaṃ tasya praśamoyaṃ prakīrtitaḥ  
AbhTa parehani guroḥ kāryo yāgastena vinā yataḥ 
AbhTb na vidhiḥ pūrṇatāṃ yāti kuryādyatnena taṃ tataḥ  
AbhTa yena yena gurustuṣyettattadasmai nivedayet 
AbhTb cakracaryāntarālesyā vidhiḥ saṃcāra ucyāte  
AbhTa alipātraṃ susaṃpūrṇaṃ vīrendrakarasaṃsthitam 
AbhTb avalokya paraṃ brahma tatpivedājñayā guroḥ  
AbhTa tarpayitvā tu bhūtāni gurave vinivedayet 
AbhTb kṛtvā bhuvi guruṃ natvādāya saṃtarpya khecarīḥ  
AbhTa svaṃ mantraṃ tacca vanditvā dūtīṃ gaṇaptiṃ gurūn 
AbhTb kṣetrapaṃ vīrasaṅghātaṃ gurvādikramaśastataḥ  
AbhTa vīraspṛṣṭaṃ svayaṃ dravyaṃ pivennaivānyathā kvacit 
AbhTb parabrahmaṇyavettārogamāgamavivarjitāḥ  
AbhTa lobhamohamadakrodharāgamāyājuṣaśca ye 
AbhTb taiḥ sākaṃ na ca kartavyametacchreyorthinātmani  
AbhTa yāgādau yāgamadhye ca yāgānte gurupūjane 
AbhTb naimittikeṣu prokteṣu śiṣyaḥ kuryādimaṃ vidhim  
AbhTa iti rahasyavidhiḥ paricarcito gurumukhānubhavaiḥ suparisphuṭaḥ 
C atha śrītantrāloke triṃśamāhnikam
AbhTa atha yathocitamantrakadambakaṃ trikakulakramayogi nirūpyate 
AbhTb tāvadvimarśānārūḍhadhiyāṃ tātsiddhaye kramāt  
AbhTa pratibuddhā hi te mantrā vimarśaikasvabhāvakāḥ 
AbhTb svatantrasyaiva ciddhāmnaḥ svātantryāt kartṛtāmayāḥ  
AbhTa yamāviśanti cācāryaṃ taṃ tādātmyanirūḍhitaḥ 
AbhTb svatantrīkurvate yānti karaṇānyapi kartṛtām  
AbhTa ādhāraśaktau hrīṃ pṛthvīprabhṛtau tu catuṣṭaye 
AbhTb kṣlāṃ kṣvīṃ vaṃ kṣamiti prāhuḥ kramādvarṇacatuṣṭayam  
AbhTa haṃ nāle yaṃ tathā raṃ laṃ vaṃ dharmādicatuṣṭaye 
AbhTb ṛṃ ṝṃ ḷṃ ḷḷṃ catuṣke ca viparītakramādbhavet  
AbhTa oṃ auṃ hastrayamityetadvidyāmāyākalātraye 
AbhTb anusvāravisargau ca vidyeśeśvaratattvayoḥ  
AbhTa kādibhāntāḥ kesareṣu prāṇoṣṭasvarasaṃyutaḥ 
AbhTb sabinduko daleṣvaṣṭasvatha svaṃ nāma dīpitam  
AbhTa śaktīnāṃ navakasya syācchaṣasā maṇḍalatraye 
AbhTb sabindukāḥ kṣmaṃ prete jraṃ śūlaśṛṅgeṣu kalpayet  
AbhTa pṛthagāsanapūjāyāṃ kramānmantrā ime smṛtāḥ 
AbhTb saṃkṣepapūjane tu prāgādyamantyaṃ ca bījakam  
AbhTa ādāyādhāraśaktyādiśūlaśṛṅgāntamarcayet 
AbhTb agnimārutapṛthvyambusaṣaṣṭhasvarabindukam  
AbhTa ratiśekharamantrosya vaktrāṅgaṃ hrasvadīrghakaiḥ 
AbhTb agniprāṇāgnisaṃhārakālendrāmbusamīraṇāḥ  
AbhTa saṣaṣṭhasvarabirndvadhacandrādyāḥ syurnavātmanaḥ 
AbhTb bindunādādikā vyāptiḥ śrīmattraiśirase mate  
AbhTa kṣepākrānticidudbodhadīpanasthāpanānyatha 
AbhTb tatsaṃvittistadāpattiriti saṃjñābhiśabditā  
AbhTa etāvatī mahāvyāptirmūrtitvenātra kīrtitā
