AbhTb pariṇāmastallayaśca namaskāraḥ sa ucyate  
AbhTa eṣa tryarṇojjhitodhastāddīrghaiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ svarairyutaḥ 
AbhTb ṣaḍaṅgāni hṛdādīni vaktrāṇyasya ca kalpayet  
AbhTa kṣayaravalabījaistu dīptairbinduvibhūṣitaiḥ 
AbhTb jhakārasaṃhṛtiprāṇāḥ saṣaṣṭhasvarabindukāḥ  
AbhTa eṣa bhairavasadmāvaścandrārdhādivibhūṣitaḥ 
AbhTb mātṛkāmālinīmantrau prāgeva samudāhṛtau  
AbhTa oṃkārotha caturthyantā saṃjñā natiriti kramāt 
AbhTb gaṇeśādiṣu mantraḥ syādbījaṃ yeṣu na coditam  
AbhTa nāmādyakṣaramākārabinducandrādidīpitam 
AbhTb sarveṣāmeva bījānāṃ taccaturdaśaṣaṣṭhayuk  
AbhTa āmantritānyaghoryāditritayasya kramoditaiḥ 
AbhTb bījairvisargiṇī māyā huṃ hakāro visargavān  
AbhTa punardevītrayasyāpi kramādāmantraṇatrayam 
AbhTb dvitīyasminpadekāra ekārasyeha ca smṛtaḥ  
AbhTa tataḥ śaktidvayāmantro luptaṃ tatrāntyamakṣaram 
AbhTb hegnivarṇāvubhau pañcasvarayuktau parau pṛthak  
AbhTa akārayuktāvastraṃ huṃ ha visargī punaḥ śaraḥ 
AbhTb tāreṇa saha vasvagnivarṇārdhārṇadvayādhikā  
AbhTa eṣā parāparādevyā vidyā śrītrikaśāsane 
AbhTb pañcaṣaṭpañcavedākṣivahninetrākṣaraṃ padam  
AbhTa aghoryādau saptake syāt pivanyāḥ pariśiṣṭakam 
AbhTb pratyekavarṇagopyuktaḥ siddhayogīśvarīmate  
AbhTa devatācakravinyāsaḥ sa bahutvānna lipyate 
AbhTb māyā visargiṇī huṃ phaṭ ceti mantroparātmakaḥ  
AbhTa parāyāstūktasadvyāptirjīvaḥ sahacaturdaśaḥ 
AbhTb sānekabhedā triśiraḥśāstre proktā maheśinā  
AbhTa svarūpato vibhinnāpi racanānekasaṅkulā 
AbhTb jīvaḥ prāṇastha evātra prāṇo vā jīvasaṃsthitaḥ  
AbhTa ādhārādheyabhāvena avinābhāvayogataḥ 
AbhTb haṃsaṃ cāmṛtamadhyasthaṃ kālarudravibheditam  
AbhTa bhuvaneśaśiroyuktamanaṅgadvayayojitam 
AbhTb dīptāddīptataraṃ jñeyaṃ ṣaṭcakrakramayojitam  
AbhTa prāṇaṃ daṇḍāsanasthaṃ tu guhyaśaktīcchayā yutam 
AbhTb pareyaṃ vācikoddiṣṭā mahājñānasvarūpataḥ  
AbhTa sphuṭaṃ bhairavahṛjjñānamidaṃ tvekākṣaraṃ param 
AbhTb amṛtaṃ kevalaṃ khasthaṃ yadvā sāvitrikāyutam  
AbhTa śūnyadvayasamopetaṃ parāyā hṛdayaṃ param 
AbhTb yugmayāge prasiddhaṃ tu kartavyaṃ tattvavedibhiḥ  
AbhTa anyepyekākṣarā ye tu ekavīravidhānataḥ 
AbhTb guptā guptatarāste tu aṃgābhijanavarjitāḥ  
AbhTa yaṣṭavyāḥ sādhakendraistu kulasthāḥ siddhidāyakāḥ 
AbhTb kulakramavidhānena sūkṣmavijñānayogataḥ  
AbhTa anuṣṭheyāḥ sadā devi striyā vā puruṣeṇa vā 
AbhTb sakāro dīrghaṣaṭkena yuktoṅgānyānanāni tu  
AbhTa syāt sa eva paraṃ hrasvapañcasvarakhasaṃyutaḥ 
AbhTb oṃkāraiḥ pañcabhirmantro vidyāṅgahṛdayaṃ bhavet  
AbhTa praṇavaścāmṛte tejomālini svāhayā saha 
AbhTb ekādaśākṣaraṃ brahmaśirastanmālinīmate  
AbhTa vedavedani hūṃ phaṭca praṇavādiyutā śikhā 
AbhTb vajriṇe vajradharāya svāhetyoṃkārapūrvakam  
AbhTa ekādaśākṣaraṃ varma puruṣṭutamiti smṛtam 
AbhTb tāro dvijihvaḥ khaśarasvarayugjīva eva ca  
AbhTa netrametatprakāśātma sarvasādhāraṇaṃ smṛtam 
AbhTb tāraḥ ślīṃ paśu huṃ phat ca tadastraṃ rasavarṇakam  
AbhTa laraṭakṣavayairdīrghaiḥ samayuktaiḥ sabindukaiḥ 
AbhTb indrādayastadastrāṇi hrasvairviṣṇuprajāpatī  
AbhTa smṛtau turyadvitīyābhyāṃ hrasvābhyāṃ padmacakrake 
AbhTb namaḥ svāhā tathā vauṣaṭ huṃ vaṣaṭ phaṭ ca jātayaḥ  
AbhTa aṅgeṣu kramaśaḥ ṣaṭsu karmasvatha tadātmikāḥ 
AbhTb jape home tathāpyāye samuccāṭetha śāntike  
AbhTa abhicāre ca mantrāṇāṃ namaskārādijātayaḥ 
AbhTb akṣiṣaṇmunivargebhyo dvitīyāḥ saha bindunā  
AbhTa yonyarṇena ca mātṝṇāṃ sadmāvaḥ kālakarṣiṇī 
AbhTb ādyojjhito vāpyantena varjito vātha saṃmataḥ  
AbhTa jīvaḥ prāṇapuṭāntaḥsthaḥ kālānalasamadyutiḥ 
AbhTb atidīptastu vāmāṃghrirbhūṣito mūrdhni bindunā  
AbhTa dakṣajānugataścāyaṃ sarvamātṛgaṇārcitaḥ 
AbhTb anena prāṇitāḥ sarve dadate vāñchitaṃ phalam  
AbhTa sadbhāvaḥ paramo hyeṣa mātṝṇāṃ bhairavasya ca 
AbhTb tasmādenaṃ japenmantrī ya icchetsiddhimuttamām  
AbhTa rudraśaktisamāveśo nityamatra pratiṣṭhitaḥ 
AbhTb yasmādeṣā parā śaktirbhedenānyena kīrtitā  
AbhTa yāvatyaḥ siddhayastantre tāḥ sarvāḥ kurute tviyam 
AbhTb aṅgavaktrāṇi cāpyasyāḥ prāgvatsvaraniyogataḥ  
AbhTa daṇḍo jīvastriśūlaṃ ca dakṣāṅgulyaparastanau 
AbhTb nābhikaṇṭhau marudrudrau visargaḥ satriśūlakaḥ  
AbhTa sarvayoginicakrāṇāmadhipoyamudāhṛtaḥ 
AbhTb asyāpyuccāraṇādeva saṃvittiḥ syātpuroditā  
AbhTa mahācaṇḍeti tu yogeśvaṛ ityaṣṭavarṇakam 
AbhTb navārṇeyaṃ guptatarā sadbhāvaḥ kālakarṣiṇī  
AbhTa śrīḍāmare mahāyāge parātparataroditā 
AbhTb sudhācchedakaṣaṇṭhādyairbījaṃ chedakamasvaram  
AbhTa adhyardhārṇā kālarātriḥ kṣurikā mālinīmate 
AbhTb śatāvartanayā hyasyā jāyate mūrdhni vedanā  
AbhTa evaṃ pratyayamālocya mṛtyujiddhyānamāśrayet 
AbhTb naināṃ samuccareddevi ya iccheddīrghajīvitam  
AbhTa dvirdaṇḍāgnī śūlanabhaḥprāṇāśchettranalau tathā 
AbhTb kūṭāgnī savisargāśca pañcāpyetetha pañcasu  
AbhTa vyomasviti śivenoktaṃ tantrasadbhāvaśāsane 
AbhTb chedinī kṣurikeyaṃ syādyayā yojayate pare  
AbhTa bindvindvanalakūṭāgnimarutṣaṣṭhasvarairyutam 
AbhTb āpādatalamūrdhāntaṃ smaredastramidaṃ jvalat  
AbhTa kuñcanaṃ cāṅgulīnāṃ tu kartavyaṃ codanaṃ tataḥ 
AbhTb jānvādiparacakrāntaṃ cakrāccakraṃ tu kuñcayet  
AbhTa kathitaṃ sarahasyaṃ tu sadyonirvāṇakaṃ param 
AbhTb athocyate brahmavidyā sadyaḥpratyayadāyinī  
AbhTa śivaḥ śrībhūtirājo yāmasmabhyaṃ pratyapādayat 
AbhTb sarveṣāmeva bhūtānāṃ maraṇe samupasthite  
AbhTa yayā paṭhitayotkramya jīvo yāti nirañjanam 
AbhTb yā jñāninopi saṃpūrṇakṛtyasyāpi śrutā satī  
AbhTa prāṇādicchedajāṃ mṛtyuvyathāṃ sadyo vyapohati 
AbhTb yāmākarṇya mahāmohavivaśopi kramādgataḥ  
AbhTa prabodhaṃ vaktṛsāṃmukhyamabhyeti rabhasātsvayam 
AbhTb paramapadāttvamihāgāḥ sanātanastvaṃ jahīhi dehāntam  
AbhTa pādāṅguṣṭhādi vibho nibandhanaṃ bandhanaṃ hyugram 
AbhTb āryāvākyamidaṃ pūrvaṃ bhuvanākhyaiḥ padairbhavet  
AbhTa gulphānte jānugataṃ jatrusthaṃ bandhanaṃ tathā meḍhre 
AbhTb jahihi puramagryamadhyaṃ hṛtpadmāttvaṃ samuttiṣṭha  
AbhTa etāvadbhiḥ padairetadāryāvākyaṃ dvitīyakam 
AbhTb haṃsa hayagrīva vibho sadāśivastvaṃ parosi jīvākhyaḥ  
AbhTa ravisomavahnisaṅghadṛbindudeho hahaha samutkrāma 
AbhTb tṛtīyamāryāvākyaṃ prāksaṃkhyairekādhikaiḥ padaiḥ  
AbhTa haṃsamahāmantramayaḥ sanātanastvaṃ śubhāśubhāpekṣī 
AbhTb maṇḍalamadhyaniviṣṭaḥ śaktimahāsetukāraṇamahārthaḥ  
AbhTa kamalobhayaviniviṣṭaḥ prabodhamāyāhi devatādeha 
AbhTb āryāvākyamidaṃ sārdhaṃ rudrasaṃkhyapaderitam  
AbhTa niḥśvāse tvapaśabdasya sthānestyupa iti dhvaniḥ 
AbhTb ajñānāttvaṃ baddhaḥ prabodhitottiṣṭha devāde  
AbhTa etatpañcamamāryārdhavākyaṃ syātsaptabhiḥ padaiḥ 
AbhTb vraja tālusāhvayāntaṃ hyauḍambaraghaṭṭitaṃ mahādvāram  
AbhTa prāpya prayāhi haṃho haṃho vā vāmadevapadam 
AbhTb āryyāvākyamidaṃ ṣaṣṭhaṃ syāccaturdaśabhiḥ padaiḥ  
AbhTa granthīśvara paramātman śānta mahātālurandhramāsādya 
AbhTb utkrama he deheśvara nirañjanaṃ śivapadaṃ prayāhyāśu  
AbhTa āryāvākyaṃ saptamaṃ syāttaccaturdaśabhiḥ padaiḥ 
AbhTb prabhañjanastvamityevaṃ pāṭho niḥśvāsaśāsane  
AbhTa ākramya madhyamārgaṃ prāṇāpānau samāhṛtya 
AbhTb dharmādharmau tyaktvā nārāyaṇa yāhi śāntāntam  
AbhTa āryāvākyamidaṃ proktamaṣṭamaṃ navabhiḥ padaiḥ 
AbhTb he brahman he viṣṇo he rudra śivosi vāsudevastvam  
AbhTa agnīṣomasanātanamṛtpiṇḍaṃ jahihi he mahākāśa 
AbhTb etadbhuvanasaṃkhyātairāryyāvākyaṃ prakīrtitam  
AbhTa sanātma tripiṇḍamiti mahākośamiti sthitam 
AbhTb padatrayaṃ tu niḥśvāsamukuṭottarakādiṣu  
AbhTa aṅguṣṭhamātramamalamāvaraṇaṃ jahihi he mahāsūkṣma 
AbhTb āryyāvākyamidaṃ ṣaḍbhiḥ padairdaśamamucyate  
AbhTa alaṃ dviriti sūkṣmaṃ cetyevaṃ śrīmukuṭottare 
AbhTb puruṣastvaṃ prakṛtimayairbaddhohaṅkāratantunā bandhaiḥ  
AbhTa abhavābhava nityodita paramātmaṃstyaja sarāgamadhvānam 
AbhTb etattrayodaśapadaṃ syādāryāvākyamuttamam  
AbhTa hrīṃhūṃmantraśarīramavilambamāśu tvamehi dehāntam 
AbhTb āryārdhavākyametatsyād dvādaśaṃ ṣaṭpadaṃ param  
AbhTa tadidaṃ guṇabhūtamayaṃ tyaja sva ṣoṭkośikaṃ piṇḍam 
AbhTb syāt trayodaśamāryārdhaṃ padaiḥ saptabhirīdṛśam  
AbhTa mā dehaṃ bhūtamayaṃ pragṛhyatāṃ śāśvataṃ mahādeham 
AbhTb āryārdhavākyaṃ tāvadbhiḥ padairetaccaturdaśam  
AbhTa maṇḍalamamalamanantaṃ tridhā sthitaṃ gaccha bhittvaitat 
AbhTb āryārdhavākyamaṣṭābhiḥ padaiḥ pañcadaśaṃ tvidam  
AbhTa sakaleyaṃ brahmavidyā syātpañcadaśabhiḥ sphuṭaiḥ 
AbhTb vākyaiḥ pañcākṣaraistvasyā niṣkalā parikīrtyate  
AbhTa prativākyaṃ yayādyantayojitā paripaṭhyate 
AbhTb tāro māyā vedakalo mātṛtāro navātmakaḥ  
AbhTa iti pañcākṣarāṇi syuḥ proktavyāptyanusārataḥ 
AbhTb binduprāṇāmṛtajalaṃ marutṣaṣṭhasvarānvitam  
AbhTa etena śaktyuccārasthabījenālabhyate paśuḥ 
AbhTb kṛtadīkṣāvidhiḥ pūrvaṃ brahmaghnopi viśuddhyati  
AbhTa laghutvena tulāśuddhiḥ sadyaḥpratyayakāriṇī 
AbhTb tāraḥ śamarayaiḥ piṇḍo natiśca caturarṇakam  
AbhTa śākinīstobhanaṃ marma hṛdayaṃ jīvitaṃ tvidam 
AbhTb ṣaṣṭhaprāṇatrikūṭordhvabāhuśūlākhyabindubhiḥ  
AbhTa anackanāsādhovaktracandrakhaṇḍaiśca maṇḍitam 
AbhTb hṛdayaṃ bhairavākhyaṃ tu sarvasaṃhārakārakam  
AbhTa agnimaṇḍalamadhyasthabhairavānalatāpitāḥ 
AbhTb vaśamāyānti śākinyaḥ sthānametena ceddahet  
AbhTa visarjayettāḥ prathamamanyathā cchidrayanti tāḥ 
AbhTb hrīṃ klīṃ vleṃ kleṃ ebhirvarṇairdvādaśasvarabhūṣitaiḥ  
AbhTa priyamelāpanaṃ nāma hṛdayaṃ sampuṭaṃ japet 
AbhTb pratyekamathavā dvābhyāṃ sarvairvā vidhiruttamaḥ  
AbhTa tulāmelakayogaḥ śrītantrasadbhāvaśāsane 
AbhTb ya uktaḥ śambhunāthena sa mayā darśitaḥ kramāt  
AbhTa atha vittavihīnānāṃ prapannānāṃ ca tattvataḥ 
AbhTb deśakālādidoṣeṇa na tathādhyavasāyinām  
AbhTa prakartavyā yathā dīKṣā śrīsantatyāgamoditā 
AbhTb kathyate hāṭakeśānapātālādhipacoditā  
AbhTa śrīnātha ārya bhagavannetattritayaṃ hi kanda ādhāre 
AbhTb varuṇo macchando bhagavatta iti trayamidaṃ hṛdaye  
AbhTa dharmādivargasaṃjñāścatvāraḥ kaṇṭhadeśagāḥ pūjyāḥ 
AbhTb hrīṃśrīṃpūrvāḥ sarve sambodhajuṣaśca pādaśabdāntāḥ  
AbhTa mūrdhatale vidyātrayamuktaṃ bhāvyatha manobhiyogena 
AbhTb kusumairānandairvā bhāvanayā vāpi kevalayā  
AbhTa guruṇā tattvavidā kila śiṣyo yadi mokṣamātrakṛtahṛdayaḥ 
AbhTb mokṣaikadānacaturā dīkṣā seyaṃ paropaniṣaduktā  
AbhTa etaddīkṣādīkṣita etadvidyātrayaṃ smaran hṛdaye 
AbhTb bāhyārcādi vinaiva hi vrajati paraṃ dhāma dehānte  
AbhTa praṇavo māyā bindurvarṇatrayamāditaḥ kuryāt 
AbhTb padapañcakasya saṃbodhanayuktasyāgnidayitānte  
AbhTa siddhasādhani tatpūrvaṃ śabdabrahmasvarūpiṇi 
AbhTb samastabandhaśabdena sahitaṃ ca nikṛntani  
AbhTa bodhani śivasadbhāvajananyāmantritaṃ ca tat 
AbhTb pañcāṣṭarandhratryaṣṭārṇakrameṇa padapañcakam  
AbhTa khapañcārṇā parabrahmavidyeyaṃ mokṣadā śivā 
AbhTb anuttarecche ghāntaśca satrayodaśasusvaraḥ  
AbhTa asya varṇatrayasyānte tvantaḥsthānāṃ catuṣṭayam 
AbhTb vargādyaśvau tryasrabinduyuk pāntorṇatrayādataḥ  
AbhTa mahāhāṭakaśabdādyamīśvarītyarṇasaptakam 
AbhTb āmantritaṃ kṣamasveti tryarṇaṃ pāpāntakāriṇi  
AbhTa ṣaḍarṇaṃ pāpaśabdādivimohanipadaṃ tataḥ 
AbhTb pāpaṃ hana dhuna dvirdvirdaśārṇaṃ padamīdṛśam  
AbhTa pañcamyantaṃ ṣaḍarṇaṃ syādrudraśaktivaśāditi 
AbhTb tata ekākṣaraṃ yattadvisargabrahma kīrtitam  
AbhTa tadanackatakāreṇa sahaikībhāvataḥ paṭhet 
AbhTb randhrābdhivarṇā vidyeyaṃ dīkṣāvidyeti kīrtitā  
AbhTa māyārṇañca pare brahme caturvidye padatrayam 
AbhTb aṣṭārṇamatha pañcārṇaṃ yogadhāriṇisaṃjñitam  
AbhTa ātmāntarātmaparamātmarūpaṃ ca padatrayam 
AbhTb ekārāntaṃ bodhanasthaṃ daśārṇaṃ parikīrtitam  
AbhTa rudraśaktīti vedārṇaṃ syādrudradayitetha me 
AbhTb pāpaṃ dahadahetyeṣā dvādaśārṇā catuṣpadī  
AbhTa saumye sadāśive yugmaṃ ṣaṭkaṃ bindviṣusāvahā 
AbhTb sārdhavarṇacatuṣkaṃ tadityeṣā samayāpahā  
AbhTa vidyā sārdhārṇakhaśarasaṃkhyā sā pārameśvarī 
AbhTb etadvidyātrayaṃ śrīmadbhūtirājo nyarūpayat  
AbhTa yaḥ sākṣādabhajacchrīmāñśrīkaṇṭho mānuṣīṃ tanum 
AbhTb atra vīryaṃ puraivoktaṃ sarvatrānusaredguruḥ  
AbhTa arthabījapraveśāntaruccārādyanusārataḥ 
AbhTb nahi tatkiṃcanāpyasti yatpurā na nirūpitam  
AbhTa niṣphalā punaruktistu nāsmabhyaṃ jātu rocate 
AbhTb ityevaṃ mantravidyādisvarūpamupavarṇitam  
C atha śrītantrāloke ekatriṃśamāhnikam
AbhTa atha maṇḍalasadbhāvaḥ saṃkṣepeṇābhidhīyate 
AbhTb sādhayitvā diśaṃ pūrvāṃ sūtramāsphālayetsamam  
AbhTa tadardhayitvā madhyaprākpratīcīṣvaṅkayetpunaḥ 
AbhTb tatopyardhatadardhārdhamānataḥ pūrvapaścimau  
AbhTa aṅkayettāvatā dadyāt sūtreṇa bhramayugmakam 
AbhTb matsyasandhidvayaṃ tvevaṃ dakṣiṇottarayorbhavet  
AbhTa tanmadhye pātayetsūtraṃ dakṣiṇottarasiddhaye 
AbhTb yadi vā prākparāktulyasūtreṇottaradakṣiṇe  
AbhTa aṅkayedaparādaṅkāt pūrvādapi tathaiva te 
AbhTb matsyamadhye kṣipetsūtramāyataṃ dakṣiṇottare  
AbhTa matakṣetrārdhamānena madhyāddikṣvaṅkayettataḥ 
AbhTb sūtrābhyāṃ digdvayotthābhyāṃ matsyaḥ syātpratikoṇagaḥ  
AbhTa matsyeṣu vedāḥ sūtrāṇītyevaṃ syāccaturasrakam 
AbhTb ekasmātprabhṛti proktaṃ śatāntaṃ maṇḍalaṃ yataḥ  
AbhTa siddhātantre maṇḍalānāṃ śataṃ tatpīṭha ucyate 
AbhTb yattanmadhyagataṃ mukhyaṃ maṇḍalānāṃ trayaṃ smṛtam  
AbhTa madhyaśūlaṃ tritriśūlaṃ navaśūlamiti sphuṭam 
AbhTb tatra śūlavidhānaṃ yaduktaṃ bhedairanantakaiḥ  
AbhTa tadyoni maṇḍalaṃ brūmaḥ sadbhāvakramadarśitam 
AbhTb vedāśrite caturhaste tribhāgaṃ sarvatastyajet  
AbhTa bhāgaiḥ ṣoḍaśabhiḥ sarvaṃ tattatkṣetraṃ vibhājayet 
AbhTb brahmasūtradvayasyātha madhyaṃ brahmapadaṃ sphuṭam  
AbhTa kṛtvāvadhiṃ tato lakṣyaṃ caturthaṃ sūtramāditaḥ 
AbhTb tatastiryagvrajet sūtraṃ caturthaṃ tadanantare  
AbhTa koṣṭhe cendudvayaṃ kuryādbahirbhāgārdhabhāgataḥ 
AbhTb tayorlagnaṃ brahmasūtrāttṛtīye marmaṇi sthitam  
AbhTa koṣṭhakārdheparaṃ ceti yugmamantarmukhaṃ bhavet 
AbhTb brahmasūtrāddvitīyasmin haste marmaṇi niścalam  
AbhTa kṛtvā pūrṇenduyugalaṃ vartayeta vicakṣaṇaḥ 
AbhTb brahmasūtragatāt ṣaṣṭhāt tiryagbhāgāttṛtīyake  
AbhTa kṛtvārdhakoṣṭhake sūtraṃ pūrṇacandrāgralambitam 
AbhTb bhramayedunmukhaṃ khaṇḍacandrayugvahnibhāgagam  
AbhTa tiryagbhāgadvayaṃ tyaktvā khaṇḍendoḥ paścimāttataḥ 
AbhTb koṇaṃ yāvattathā syācca kuryāt khaṇḍaṃ bhramadvayam  
AbhTa sutīkṣṇakuṭilāgraṃ tadekaṃ śṛṅgaṃ prajāyate 
AbhTb dvitīyasminnapi proktaḥ śṛṅga eṣa vidhiḥ sphuṭaḥ  
AbhTa madhyaśṛṅgetha kartavye tṛtīye ūrdhvakoṣṭhake 
AbhTb caturthārdhe ca candrārdhadvayamantarmukhaṃ bhavet  
AbhTa tacca pūrṇendumekaṃ prāgvartitaṃ prāpnuyādyathā 
AbhTb anyonyagranthiyogena baddhāratvaṃ prajāyate  
AbhTa evaṃ dvitīyapārśvesya khaṇḍendudvayavartanāt 
AbhTb madhyābhyāṃ gaṇḍikā śliṣṭā parābhyāmagrato nayet  
AbhTa sūtraṃ pārśvadvaye yena tīkṣṇaṃ syānmadhyaśṛṅgagam 
AbhTb pārśvadvayādhare paścādbrahmasūtraṃ dvitīyakam  
AbhTa avadhānena saṃgrāhyamācāryeṇohavedinā 
AbhTb bhavetpaścānmukho mantrī tasmiṃśca brahmasūtrake  
AbhTa madhyaśṛṅgaṃ varjayitvā sarvaḥ pūrvodito vidhiḥ 
AbhTb tato yadunmukhaṃ khaṇḍacandrayugmaṃ puroditam  
AbhTa tato dvayena kartavyā gaṇḍikāntaḥsusaṃgatā 
AbhTb dvayenāgragasūtrābhyāṃ madhyaśṛṅgadvayaṃ bhavet  
AbhTa adho bhāgavivṛddhyāsya padmaṃ vṛttacatuṣṭayam 
AbhTb tataścakraṃ ṣoḍaśāraṃ dvādaśāraṃ dvidhātha tat  
AbhTa madhye kuleśvarīsthānaṃ vyoma vā tilakaṃ ca vā 
AbhTb padmaṃ vātha ṣaḍaraṃ vā viyaddvādaśakaṃ ca vā  
AbhTa tritriśūletra saptāre śliṣṭamātreṇa madhyataḥ 
AbhTb padmānāmatha cakrāṇāṃ vyomnāṃ vā saptakaṃ bhavet  
AbhTa miśritaṃ vātha saṃkīrṇaṃ samāsavyāsabhedataḥ 
AbhTb tataḥ kṣetrārdhamānena kṣetraṃ tatrādhikaṃ kṣipet  
AbhTa tatra daṇḍaḥ smṛto bhāgaḥ ṣaḍarāmalasārakaḥ 
AbhTb sutīkṣṇāgraḥ suraktābhaḥ kṣaṇādāveśakārakaḥ  
AbhTa yā sā kuṇḍalinī devī taraṅgākhyā mahormiṇī 
AbhTb sā ṣaḍaśreṇa kandākhye sthitā ṣaḍdevatātmikā  
AbhTa aṣṭabhāgaiśca vistīrṇo dīrghaścāpi tadardhataḥ 
AbhTb tato dvārāṇi kāryāṇi citravartanayā kramāt  
AbhTa vedāśrāyatarūpāṇi yadivā vṛttamātrataḥ 
AbhTb spaṣṭaśṛṅgamatho kuryādyadivā vaiparītyataḥ  
AbhTa unmukhaṃ candrayugmaṃ vā bhaṅktvā kuryāccatuṣṭayam 
AbhTb kuṭilo madhyataḥ spaṣṭodhomukhaḥ pārśvagaḥ sthitaḥ  
AbhTa uttānordhosamaḥ pūrṇaḥ śliṣṭo granthigatastathā 
AbhTb candrasyetthaṃ dvādaśadhā vartanā bhramabhedinī  
AbhTa antarbahirmukhatvena sā punardvividhā matā 
AbhTb tadbhedānmaṇḍalānāṃ syādasaṅkhyo bhedavistaraḥ  
AbhTa pīṭhavīthībahiarbhūmikaṇṭhakarṇakapolataḥ 
AbhTb śobhopaśobhāsaṃbhedādguṇarekhāvikalpataḥ  
AbhTa svastikadvitayādyaṣṭatayāparyantabhedataḥ 
AbhTb bhāvābhāvavikalpena maṇḍalānāmanantatā  
AbhTa tato rajāṃsi deyāni yathāśobhānusārataḥ 
AbhTb sindūraṃ rājavartaṃ ca khaṭikā ca sitottamā  
AbhTa uttamāni rajāṃsīha devatātrayayogataḥ 
AbhTb parā candrasamaprakhyā raktā devī parāparā  
AbhTa aparā sā parā kālī bhīṣaṇā caṇḍayoginī 
AbhTb dṛṣṭvaitanmaṇḍalaṃ devyaḥ sarvā nṛtyanti sarvadā  
AbhTa anarcitepyadīkṣeṇa dṛṣṭe dīkṣyeta mātṛbhiḥ 
AbhTb kiṃvātibahunoktena tritriśūlārasaptakāḥ  
AbhTa śūlayāgāḥ ṣaṭ sahasrāṇyevaṃ sārdhaśatadvayam 
AbhTb yā sā devī parā śaktiḥ prāṇavāhā vyavasthitā  
AbhTa viśvāntaḥ kuṇḍalākārā sā sākṣādatra vartitā 
AbhTb tattvāni tattvadevyaśca viśvamasminpratiṣṭhitam  
AbhTa atrordhve tantumātreṇa tisraḥ śūlāragāḥ sthitāḥ 
AbhTb āsanatvena cecchādyā bhogamokṣaprasādhikāḥ  
AbhTa tāstu mokṣaikakāmasya śūlārāviddhamadhyakāḥ 
AbhTb tasmādenaṃ mahāyāgaṃ mahāvibhavavistaraiḥ  
AbhTa pūjayedbhūtikāmo vā mokṣakāmopivā budhaḥ 
AbhTb asya darśanamātreṇa bhūtavetālaguhyakāḥ  
AbhTa palāyante daśa diśaḥ śivaḥ sākṣātprasīdati 
AbhTb mandaśaktibalāviddhopyetanmaṇḍalapūjanāt  
AbhTa satataṃ māsaṣaṭkena trikajñānaṃ samaśnute 
AbhTb yatprāpya heyopādeyaṃ svayameva vicārya saḥ  
AbhTa dehānte syādbhairavātmā siddhikāmotha siddhyati 
AbhTb maṇḍalasyāsya yo vyāptiṃ devatānyāsameva ca  
AbhTa vartanāṃ ca vijānāti sa gurustrikaśāsane 
AbhTb tasya pādarajo mūrdhni dhāryaṃ śivasamīhinā  
AbhTa atra sṛṣṭisthitidhvaṃsān kramāt trīnapi pūjayet 
AbhTb turyaṃ tu madhyato yadvā sarveṣu paripūrakam  
AbhTa catustriśūlaṃ vā guptadaṇḍaṃ yāgaṃ samācaret 
AbhTb tatra tat pūjayetsamyak sphuṭaṃ kramacatuṣṭayam  
AbhTa ityetatkathitaṃ gupte ṣaḍardhahṛdaye pare 
AbhTb ṣaṭke proktaṃ sūcitaṃ śrīsiddhayogīśvarīmate  
AbhTa agrataḥ sūtrayitvā tu maṇḍalaṃ sarvakāmadam 
AbhTb mahāśūlasamopetaṃ padmacakrādibhūṣitam  
AbhTa dvāre dvāre likhecchūlaṃ varjayitvā tu paścimam 
AbhTb koṇeṣvapica vā kāryaṃ mahāśūlaṃ drumānvitam  
AbhTa amṛtāmbhobhavārīṇāṃ śūlāgre tu trikaṃ trikam 
AbhTb śūla itthaṃ prakartavyamaṣṭadhā tat tridhāpivā  
AbhTa evaṃ saṃsūcitaṃ divyaṃ khecarīṇāṃ puraṃ tviti 
AbhTb sthānāntarepi kathitaṃ śrīsiddhātantraśāsane  
AbhTa kajaṃ madhye tadardhena śūlaśṛṅgāṇi tāni tu 
AbhTb śūlāṅkaṃ maṇḍalaṃ kalpyaṃ kamalāṅkaṃ ca pūraṇe  
AbhTa atha śūlābjavinyāsaḥ śrīpūrve triśiromate 
AbhTb siddhātantre trikakule devyāyāmalamālayoḥ  
AbhTa yathoktaḥ sāraśāstre ca tantrasadbhāvaguhyayoḥ 
AbhTb tathā pradarśyate spaṣṭaṃ yadyapyuktakramādgataḥ  
AbhTa vedāśrite trihaste prāk pūrvamardha vibhājayet 
AbhTb hastārdhaṃ sarvatastyaktvā pūrvodagyāmyadiggatam  
AbhTa tryaṅgulaiḥ koṣṭhakairūrdhvaistiryak cāṣṭadvidhātmakaiḥ 
AbhTb dvau dvau bhāgau parityajya punardakṣiṇasaumyagau  
AbhTa brahmaṇaḥ pārśvayorjīvāccaturthāt pūrvatastathā 
AbhTb bhāgārdhabhāgamānaṃ tu khaṇḍacandradvayaṃ dvayam  
AbhTa tayorantastṛtīye tu dakṣiṇottarapārśvayoḥ 
AbhTb jīve khaṇḍenduyugalaṃ kuryādantarbhramādbudhaḥ  
AbhTa tayoraparamarmasthaṃ khaṇḍendudvayakoṭigam 
AbhTb bahirmukhaṃ bhramaṃ kuryāt khaṇḍacandradvayaṃ dvayam  
AbhTa tadvadbrahmaṇi kurvīta bhāgabhāgārdhasaṃmitam 
AbhTb tato dvitīyabhāgānte brahmaṇaḥ pārśvayordvayoḥ  
AbhTa dve rekhe pūrvage neye bhāgatryaṃśaśame budhaiḥ 
AbhTb ekārdhendūrdhvakoṭisthaṃ brahmasūtrāgrasaṅgatam  
AbhTa sūtradvayaṃ prakurvīta madhyaśṛṅgaprasiddhaye 
AbhTb tadagrapārśvayorjīvāt sūtramekāntare dhṛtam  
AbhTa ādidvitīyakhaṇḍendukoṇāt koṇāntamānayet 
AbhTb tayorevāparājjīvāt prathamārdhendukoṇataḥ  
AbhTa tadvadeva nayetsūtraṃ śṛṅgadvitayasiddhaye 
AbhTb kṣetrārdhe cāpare daṇḍo dvikaraśchannapañcakaḥ  
AbhTa ṣaḍvistṛtaṃ caturdīrghaṃ tadadhomalasārakam 
AbhTb vedāṅgulaṃ ca tadadho mūlaṃ tīkṣṇāgramiṣyate  
AbhTa ādikṣetrasya kurvīta dikṣu dvāracatuṣṭayam 
AbhTb hastāyāmaṃ tadardhaṃ vā vistārādapi tatsamam  
AbhTa dviguṇaṃ bāhyataḥ kuryāttataḥ padmaṃ yathā śṛṇu 
AbhTb ekaikabhāgamānāni kuryādvṛttāni vedavat  
AbhTa dikṣvaṣṭau punarapyaṣṭau jīvasūtrāṇi ṣoḍaśa 
AbhTb dvayordvayoḥ punarmadhye tatsaṃkhyātāni pātayet  
AbhTa eṣāṃ tṛtīyavṛttasthaṃ pārśvajīvasamaṃ bhramam 
AbhTb etadantaṃ prakurvīta tato jīvāgramānayet  
AbhTa yatraiva kutracitsaṅgastatsaṃbandhe sthirīkṛte 
AbhTb tatra kṛtvā nayenmantrī patrāgrāṇāṃ prasiddhaye  
AbhTa ekaikasmindale kuryātkesarāṇāṃ trayaṃ trayam 
AbhTb dviguṇāṣṭāṅgulaṃ kāryaṃ tadvacchṛṅgakajatrayam  
AbhTa karṇikā pītavarṇena mūlamadhyāgrabhedataḥ 
AbhTb sitaṃ raktaṃ tathā pītaṃ kāryaṃ kesarajālakam  
AbhTa dalāni śuklavarṇāni prativāraṇayā saha 
AbhTb pīṭhaṃ tadvaccatuṣkoṇaṃ karṇikārdhasamaṃ bahiḥ  
AbhTa sitaraktapītakṛṣṇaistatpādān vahnitaḥ kramāt 
AbhTb caturbhirapi śṛṅgāṇi tribhirmaṇḍalamiṣyate  
AbhTa daṇḍaḥ syānnīlaraktena pītamāmalasārakam 
AbhTb raktaṃ śūlaṃ prakurvīta yattatpūrvaṃ prakalpitam  
AbhTa paścāddvārasya pūrveṇa tyaktvāṅgulacatuṣṭayam 
AbhTb dvāraṃ vedāśri vṛttaṃ vā saṃkīrṇaṃ vā vicitritam  
AbhTa ekadvitripuraṃ tulyaṃ sāmudgamathavobhayam 
AbhTb kapolakaṇṭhaśobhopaśobhādibahucitritam  
AbhTa vicitrākārasaṃsthānaṃ vallīsūkṣmagṛhānvitam 
AbhTb śrīdevyāyāmale tūktaṃ kṣetre vedāśrite sati  
AbhTa ardhaṃ dvādaśadhā kṛtvā tiryagūrdhvaṃ ca tiryajam 
AbhTb bhāgamekaṃ svapārśvordhvaṃ guruḥ samavatārayet  
AbhTa madhyasthaṃ taṃ tribhāgaṃ ca tadante bhramayedubhau 
AbhTb bhāgamekaṃ parityajya tanmadhye bhramayetpunaḥ  
AbhTa tṛtīyāṃśordhvato bhrāmyamūrdhvāṃśaṃ yāvadantataḥ 
AbhTb caturthāṃśāttadūrdhvaṃ tu ūrdhvādho yojayetpunaḥ  
AbhTa tanmānādūrdhvamābhrāmya caturthena niyojayet 
AbhTb ūrdhvādyojayate sūtraṃ brahmasūtrāvadhi kramāt  
AbhTa kramādvaipulyataḥ kṛtvā aṃśaṃ vai hrāsayet punaḥ 
AbhTb ardhabhāgapramāṇastu daṇḍo dviguṇa iṣyate  
AbhTa bhāgaṃ bhāgaṃ gṛhītvā tu ubhayoratha gocarāt 
AbhTb bhrāmyaṃ pippalavat patraṃ vartanaiṣā tvadho bhavet  
AbhTa ṣoḍaśāṃśe likhetpadmaṃ dvādaśāṅgulalopanāt 
AbhTb tadūrdhvaṃ madhyabhāge tu vārijanma samālikhet  
AbhTa madhyaśṛṅgāvasāne tu tṛtīyaṃ vilikhettataḥ 
AbhTb savyāsavye tathaiveha kaṭisthābje samālikhet  
AbhTa karṇikā pītalā raktapītaśuklaṃ ca kesaram 
AbhTb dalāni padmabāhyasthā śuklā ca prativāraṇī  
AbhTa śūlaṃ kṛṣṇena rajasā brahmarekhā sitā punaḥ 
AbhTb śūlāgraṃ jvālayā yuktaṃ śūladaṇḍastu pītalaḥ  
AbhTa śūlamadhye ca yatpadmaṃ tatreśaṃ pūjayetsadā 
AbhTb asyordhve tu parāṃ dakṣenyāṃ vāme cāparāṃ budhaḥ  
AbhTa yā sā kālāntakā devī parātītā vyavasthitā 
AbhTb grasate śūlacakraṃ sā tvicchāmātreṇa sarvadā  
AbhTa śāntirūpā kalā hyeṣā vidyārūpā parā bhavet 
AbhTb aparā tu pratiṣṭhā syānnivṛttistu parāparā  
AbhTa bhairavaṃ daṇḍa ūrdhvasthaṃ rūpaṃ sādāśivātmakam 
AbhTb catasraḥ śaktayastvasya sthūlāḥ sūkṣmāstvanekadhā  
AbhTa eṣa yāgaḥ samākhyāto ḍāmarākhyastriśaktikaḥ 
AbhTb atha traiśirase śūlābjavidhirdṛṣṭobhilikhyate  
AbhTa vāmāmṛtādibhirmukhyaiḥ pavitraiḥ sumanoramaiḥ 
AbhTb bhūmiṃ rajāṃsi karaṇīṃ khaṭikāṃ mūlatorcayet  
AbhTa caturaśre caturhaste madhye śūlaṃ karatrayam 
AbhTb caṇḍo dvihasta ūrdhvādhaḥpīṭhayugvipulastvasau  
AbhTa vasvaṅgulaḥ prakartavyaḥ sūtratrayasamanvitaḥ 
AbhTb dvādaśāṅgulamānena daṇḍamūle tu pīṭhikā  
AbhTa dairghyāttūcchrāyāccordhve ca caturaṅgulamānataḥ 
AbhTb ūrdhvepyucchrāyato vedāṅgulā dairghyāddaśāṅgulā  
AbhTa śūlamūlagataṃ pīṭhīmadhyaṃ khābdhisamāṅgulam 
AbhTb kṛtvā daṇḍaṃ triśūlaṃ tu tribhirbhāgaiḥ samantataḥ  
AbhTa aṣṭāṅgulapramāṇaiḥ syāddhastamātraṃ samantataḥ 
AbhTb śūlāgraṃ śūlamadhyaṃ tacchūlamūlaṃ tu tadbhavet  
AbhTa vedī madhye prakartavyā ubhayośca ṣaḍaṅgulam 
AbhTb dvādaśāṅguladīrghā tu ubhayoḥ pārśvayostathā  
AbhTa caturaṅgulamucchrāyānmūle vedīṃ prakalpayet 
AbhTb ubhayoḥ pārśvayoścaivamardhacandrākṛtiṃ tathā  
AbhTa bhrāmayet khaṭikāsūtraṃ kaṭiṃ kuryāddviraṅgulām 
AbhTb vaipulyāddairghyato devi caturaṅgulamānataḥ  
AbhTa yādṛśaṃ dakṣiṇe bhāge vāme tadvatprakalpayet 
AbhTb madhye śūlāgravaipulyādaṅgulaśca adhordhvataḥ  
AbhTa caturaṅgulamānena vaipulyāttu ṣaḍaṅgulā 
AbhTb ucchrāyāttu tataḥ kāryā gaṇḍikā tu svarūpataḥ  
AbhTa pīṭhordhve tu prakartavyaṃ śūlamūlaṃ tu suvrate 
AbhTb śūlāgramaṅgulaṃ kāryaṃ sutīkṣṇaṃ tu ṣaḍaṅgulam  
AbhTa arāmadhyaṃ prakartavyamarādhastu ṣaḍaṅgulam 
AbhTb caturaṅgulanimnaṃ tu madhyaṃ tu parikalpayet  
AbhTa pūrvāparaṃ tadeveha madhye śūlaṃ tu tadbahiḥ 
AbhTb kārayeta tribhiḥ sūtrairekaikaṃ vartayeta ca  
AbhTa kajatrayaṃ tu śūlāgraṃ vedāṃśairdvādaśāṅgulam 
AbhTb kramāddakṣānyamadhyeṣu tryaṣṭadvādaśapatrakam  
AbhTa cakratrayaṃ vātapuraṃ padmamaṣṭāṅgulārakam 
AbhTb vidyābhikhyaṃ śūlamūle rajaḥ paścātprapātayet  
AbhTa triśūlaṃ daṇḍaparyantaṃ rājavartena pūrayet 
AbhTb sūtratrayasya pṛṣṭhe tu śuklaṃ cārātrayaṃ bhavet  
AbhTa śuklena rajasā śūlamūle vidyāmbujaṃ bhavet 
AbhTb raktaṃ raktāsitaṃ śuklaṃ kramādūrdhvāmbujatrayam  
AbhTa śuklena vyomarekhā syāt sā sthaulyādaṅgulaṃ bahiḥ 
AbhTb tāṃ tyaktvā vedikā kāryā hastamātraṃ pramāṇātaḥ  
AbhTa vaipulyatriguṇaṃ dairghyāt prākāraṃ caturaśrakam 
AbhTb samantatotha dikṣu syurdvārāṇi karamātrataḥ  
AbhTa tridhā vibhajya kramaśo dvādaśāṅgulamānataḥ 
AbhTb kaṇṭhaṃ kapolaṃ śobhāṃ tu upaśobhāṃ tadantataḥ  
AbhTa prākāraṃ caturaśraṃ tu sabhūrekhāsamanvitam 
AbhTb sitaraktapītakṛṣṇai rajobhiḥ kārayettataḥ  
AbhTa raktai rajobhirmadhyaṃ tu yathāśobhaṃ tu pūrayet 
AbhTb asyā vyāptau purā coktaṃ tatraivānusarecca tat  
AbhTa arātrayavibhāgastu praveśo nirgamo bhramaḥ 
AbhTb anāhatapadavyāptiḥ kuṇḍalyā udayaḥ paraḥ  
AbhTa hṛdi sthāne gatā devyastriśūlasya sumadhyame 
AbhTb nābhisthaḥ śūladaṇḍastu śūlamūlaṃ hṛdi sthitam  
AbhTa śaktisthānagataṃ prāntaṃ prānte cakratrayaṃ smaret 
AbhTb utkṣipyotkṣipya kalayā dehamadhyasvarūpataḥ  
AbhTa śūladaṇḍāntamadhyasthaśūlamadhyāntagocaram 
AbhTb praviśenmūlamadhyāntaṃ prāntānte śaktiveśmani  
AbhTa aspandakaraṇaṃ kṛtvā ekadā spandavartanam 
AbhTb mūlamānandamāpīḍya śaktitrayapadaṃ viśet  
AbhTa tatra pūjyaṃ prayatnena jāyante sarvasiddhayaḥ 
AbhTb samastādhvasamāyogāt ṣoḍhādhvavyāptibhāvataḥ  
AbhTa samastamantracakrādyairevamādiprayatnataḥ 
AbhTb ṣaṭtriṃśattattvaracitaṃ triśūlaṃ paribhāvayet  
AbhTa viṣuvatsthena vinyāso mantrāṇāṃ maṇḍalottame 
AbhTb kāryosmin pūjite yatra sarveśvarapadaṃ bhajet  
AbhTa svastikenātha kartavyaṃ yuktaṃ tasyocyate vidhiḥ 
AbhTb nāḍikāḥ sthāpayetpūrvaṃ muhūrtaṃ parimāṇataḥ  
AbhTa śakravāruṇadiksthāśca yāmyasaumyagatāstathā 
AbhTb ekonatriṃśadvaṃśāḥ syurṛjutiryaggatāstathā  
AbhTa aṣṭau marmaśatānyekacatvāriṃśacca jāyate 
AbhTb vaṃśairviṣayasaṃkhyaiśca padmaṃ yugmendumaṇḍalam  
AbhTa rasasaṃkhyairbhavetpīṭhaṃ svastikaṃ sarvakāmadam 
AbhTb vasusaṃkhyairdvāravīthāvevaṃ bhāgaparikramaḥ  
AbhTa randhravipraśarāgnīṃśca lupyedbāhyāntaraṃ kramāt 
AbhTb marmāṇi ca caturdikṣu madhyāddvāreṣu sundari  
AbhTa vahnibhūtamunivyomabāhyagarbhe purīṣu ca 
AbhTb lopayeccaiva marmāṇi antarnāḍivivarjitān  
AbhTa dvāraprākārakoṇeṣu netrānalaśarānṛtūn 
AbhTb nāḍayo brahmavaṃśasya lopyā netrādrasasthitāḥ  
AbhTa vahnernetrānalau lopyau vedānnetrayugaṃ rasāt 
AbhTb netraṃ saumyagataṃ lopyaṃ pūrvādvedānalau rasāt  
AbhTa lokasthā nāḍikā hitvā netrādvedāgnayaḥ kramāt 
AbhTb śarairvahnigataṃ caiva yugaṃ netrāgnayo rasāt  
AbhTa netrāt pūrvagatāccaiva sumerurdvārasaṃjñitaḥ 
AbhTb svastikā ca purī ramyā caturdikṣu sthitāvubhau  
AbhTa marmaṇāṃ ca śate dve ca ṛṣibhirguṇitā diśaḥ 
AbhTb netrādikāṃśca saṃmārjya mārgamadhyāt suśobhane  
AbhTa ṛṣitrayakṛte madhye viṣayaiḥ karṇikā bhavet 
AbhTb netrīkṛtānvasūn patraṃ netraṃ sakṛdvibhājitam  
AbhTa vahniṃ vasugataṃ kṛtvā śaśāṅkasthāṃśca lopayet 
AbhTb vahnīṣuṛṣimadhyācca lopyaṃ pīṭhendukāvadhi  
AbhTa brahmaṇo netraviṣayānnetrādvedānalau haret 
AbhTb sāgare netrakaṃ lopyaṃ nāḍayaḥ pūrvadiggatāḥ  
AbhTa bhūtanetragatānmūrdhnā netrāddvivahnidṛktrikāt 
AbhTb saumyagāt pīṭhakoṇeṣu lopayeta caturṣvapi  
AbhTa dalāni kāryāṇi sitaiḥ kesaraṃ raktapītalaiḥ 
AbhTb karṇikā kanakaprakhyā pallavāntāśca lohitāḥ  
AbhTa vyomarekhā tu susitā vartulābjāntanīlabhāḥ 
AbhTb pīṭhaṃ rekhātrayopetaṃ sitalohitapītalam  
AbhTa svastikāśca caturvarṇā agnerīśānagocarāḥ 
AbhTb vīthī vidrumasaṃkāśā svadikṣvastrāṇi bāhyataḥ  
AbhTa indranīlanibhaṃ vajraṃ śaktiṃ padmamaṇiprabhām 
AbhTb daṇḍaṃ hāṭakasaṃkāśaṃ vaktraṃ tasyātilohitam  
AbhTa nīladyutisamaṃ khaḍgaṃ pāśaṃ vatsakasaprabham 
AbhTb dhvajaṃ puṣpaphalopetaṃ pañcaraṅgaiśca śobhitam  
AbhTa gadā hemanibhātyugrā nānāratnavibhūṣitā 
AbhTb śūlaṃ nīlāmbujasamaṃ jvaladvahnyugraśekharam  
AbhTa tasyopari sitaṃ padmamīṣatpītāruṇaprabham 
AbhTb cakraṃ hemanibhaṃ dīptamarā vaiḍūryasaṃnibhāḥ  
AbhTa arāmadhyaṃ supītaṃ ca bāhyaṃ jvālāruṇaṃ bhavet 
AbhTb mandiraṃ devadevasya sarvakāmaphalapradam  
AbhTa śrīsiddhāyāṃ śūlavidhiḥ prāk kṣetre caturaśrite 
AbhTb hastamātraṃ tridhā sūryānnavakhaṇḍaṃ yathā bhavet  
AbhTa madhye śūlaṃ ca tatretthaṃ madhyabhāgaṃ tridhā bhajet 
AbhTb navabhiḥ koṣṭhakairyuktaṃ tatoyaṃ vidhirucyate  
AbhTa madhyabhāgatrayaṃ tyaktvā madhye bhāgadvayasya tu 
AbhTb adhastādbhrāmayetsūtraṃ śaśāṅkaśakalākṛti  
AbhTa ubhayato bhrāmayettatra yathāgre hākṛtirbhavet 
AbhTb koṭyāṃ tatra kṛtaṃ sūtraṃ nayedrekhāṃ tu pūrvikām  
AbhTa aparadvārapūrveṇa tyaktvāṅgulacatuṣṭayam 
AbhTb rekhāṃ vināśayetprājño yathā śūlākṛtirbhavet  
AbhTa śūlāgre tvardhahastena tyaktvā padmāni kārayet 
AbhTb adhaḥ śṛṅgatrayaṃ hastamadhye padmaṃ sakarṇikam  
AbhTa mukhāgre dhārayetsūtraṃ tribhirhastaistu pātayet 
AbhTb madhye cordhvaṃ tataḥ kuryādadhastādaṅguladvayam  
AbhTa rekhādvayaṃ pātayeta yathā śūlaṃ bhavatyapi 
AbhTb adhobhāgādibhiścordhvaṃ tatra rekhā prapadyate  
AbhTa samīkṛtya tataḥ sūtre ūrdhve dve evameva tu 
AbhTb madhyaṃ padmaṃ pratiṣṭhāpyaṃ śūlādhastādyaśasvini  
AbhTa ityeṣa maṇḍalavidhiḥ kathitaḥ saṃkṣepayogato mahāgurubhiḥ 
C atha śrītantrāloke dvātriṃśamāhnikam
AbhTa atha kathaye mudrāṇāṃ gurvāgamagītamatra vidhim  b
AbhTb mudrā ca pratibimbātmā śrīmaddevyākhyayāmale 
AbhTc uktā bimbodayaśrutyā vācyadvayavivecanāt  
AbhTa bimbātsamudayo yasyā ityuktā pratibimbatā 
AbhTb vimbasya yasyā udaya ityuktā tadupāyatā  
AbhTa mudaṃ svarūpalābhākhyaṃ dehadvāreṇa cātmanām 
AbhTb rātyarpayati yattena mudrā śāstreṣu varṇitā  
AbhTa tatra pradhānabhūtā śrīkhecarī devatātmikā 
AbhTb niṣkalatvena vikhyātā sākalyena triśūlinī  
AbhTa karaṅkiṇī krodhanā ca bhairavī lelihānikā 
AbhTb mahāpretā yogamudrā jvālinī kṣobhiṇī dhruvā  
AbhTa ityevaṃbahubhedeyaṃ śrīkhecaryeva gīyate 
AbhTb anyāstadaṅgabhūtāstu padmādyā mālinīmate  
AbhTa tāsāṃ bahutvāmukhyatvayogābhyāṃ neha varṇanam 
AbhTb śrīkhecarīsamāviṣṭo yadyatsthānaṃ samāśrayet  
AbhTa devīsaṃnidhaye tatsyādalaṃ kiṃ ḍambarairvṛthā 
AbhTb kāmye karmaṇi tāśca syurmukhyāḥ kasyāpi jātucit  
AbhTa mudrā caturvidhā kāyakaravākcittabhedataḥ  
AbhTa tatra pūrṇena rūpeṇa khecarīmeva varṇaye 
AbhTb baddhvā padmāsanaṃ yogī nābhāvakṣeśvaraṃ kṣipet  
AbhTa daṇḍākāraṃ tu taṃ tāvannayedyāvatkakhatrayam 
AbhTb nigṛhya tatra tattūrṇaṃ prerayet khatrayeṇa tu  
AbhTa etāṃ baddhvā khe gatiḥ syāditi śrīpūrvaśāsane 
AbhTb dhvanijyotirmarudyuktaṃ cittaṃ viśramya copari  
AbhTa anenābhyāsayogena śivaṃ bhittvā paraṃ vrajet 
AbhTb jatrvadhastātkarau kṛtvā vāmapādaṃ ca dakṣiṇe  
AbhTa vidāryāsyaṃ kaniṣṭhābhyāṃ madhyamābhyāṃ tu nāsikām 
AbhTb anāme kuñcayetprājño bhrūbhaṅgaṃ tarjanīdvayam  
AbhTa jihvāṃ ca cālayenmantrī hāhākāraṃ ca kārayet 
AbhTb triśūlena prayogeṇa brahmarandhramupasthitaḥ  
AbhTa padaṃ santyajya tanmātraṃ sadyastyajati medinīm 
AbhTb śūnyāśūnyalaye kṛtvā ekadaṇḍenilānalau  
AbhTa śaktitritayasambaddhe adhiṣṭhātṛtridaivate 
AbhTb triśūlaṃ tadvijānīyādyena vyomotpatedbudhaḥ  
AbhTa ākāśabhāvaṃ santyajya sattāmātramupasthitaḥ 
AbhTb śūlaṃ samarasaṃ kṛtvā rase rasa iva sthitaḥ  
AbhTa ekadaṇḍaṃ sa vijñāya triśūlaṃ khacaraṃ priye 
AbhTb baddhvā tu khecarīṃ mudrāṃ dhyātvātmānaṃ ca bhairavam  
AbhTa khecarīcakrasaṃjuṣṭaṃ sadyastyajati medinīm 
AbhTb tyaktāṃśako nirācāro niḥśaṅko lokavarjitaḥ  
AbhTa avadhūto nirācāro nāhamasmīti bhāvayam 
AbhTb mantraikaniṣṭhaḥ saṃpaśyan dehasthāḥ sarvadevatāḥ  
AbhTa hlādodvegāsmitākruṣṭanidrāmaithunamatsare 
AbhTb rūpādau vā kartṛkarmakaraṇeṣu ca sarvaśaḥ  
AbhTa nāhamasmīti manvāna ekībhūtaṃ vicintayan 
AbhTb karṇākṣimukhanāsādicakrasthaṃ devatāgaṇam  
AbhTa grahītāraṃ sadā paśyan khecaryā siddhyati sphuṭam 
AbhTb vidyāśaṅkī malāśaṅkī śāstraśaṅkī na siddhyati  
AbhTa śivo raviḥ śivo vahniḥ paktṛtvātsa purohitaḥ 
AbhTb tatrasthā devatāḥ sarvā dyotayantyokhilaṃ jagat  
AbhTa kaniṣṭhayā vidāryāsyaṃ tarjanībhyāṃ bhruvau tathā 
AbhTb anāme madhyame vaktre jihvayā tālukaṃ spṛśet  
AbhTa eṣā karaṅkiṇī devī jvālinīṃ śṛṇu sāṃpratam 
AbhTb hanurlalāṭagau hastau prasāryāṅgulitaḥ sphuṭau  
AbhTa cālayedvāyuvegena kṛtvāntarbhrukuṭīṃ budhaḥ 
AbhTb vidāryāsyaṃ sajihvaṃ ca hāhākāraṃ tu kārayet  
AbhTa eṣā jvālinyagnicakre tayā cāṣṭottaraṃ śatam 
AbhTb japedyadi tataḥ siddhyettrailokyaṃ sacarācaram  
AbhTa paradeheṣu cātmānaṃ paraṃ cātmaśarīrataḥ 
AbhTb paśyeccarantaṃ hānādādgamāgamapadasthitam  
AbhTa navacchidragataṃ caikaṃ nadantaṃ vyāpakaṃ dhruvam 
AbhTb anayā hi khacārī śrīyogasañcāra ucyate  
AbhTa kulakuṇḍalikāṃ baddhvā aṇorantaravedinīm 
AbhTb vāmo yoyaṃ jagatyasmiṃstasya saṃharaṇodyatām  
AbhTa svasthāne nirvṛtiṃ labdhvā jñānāmṛtarasātmakam 
AbhTb vrajetkandapadaṃ madhye rāvaṃ kṛtvā hyarāvakam  
AbhTa yāvajjīvaṃ catuṣkoṇaṃ piṇḍādhāraṃ ca kāmikam 
AbhTb tatra tāṃ bodhayitvā tu gatiṃ buddhvā kramāgatām  
AbhTa cakrobhayanibaddhāṃ tu śākhāprāntāvalambinīm 
AbhTb mūlasthānādyathā devi tamogranthiṃ vidārayet  
AbhTa vajrākhyāṃ jñānajenaiva tathā śākhobhayāntataḥ 
AbhTb koṇamadhyaviniṣkrāntaṃ liṅgamūlaṃ vibhedayet  
AbhTa tatra saṅghaṭṭitaṃ cakrayugmamaikyena bhāsate 
AbhTb vaiparītyāttu nikṣipya dvidhābhāvaṃ vrajatyataḥ  
AbhTa ūrvādyaṅguṣṭhakālāgniparyante sā vinikṣipet 
AbhTb gamāgamanasañcāre caretsā liṅgaliṅginī  
AbhTa tatra tatpadasaṃyogādunmīlanavidhāyinī 
AbhTb yo jānāti sa siddhyettu rasādānavisargayoḥ  
AbhTa sasaṅgamamidaṃ sthānamūrmiṇyunmīlanaṃ param 
AbhTb eṣa kramastatonyopi vyutkramaḥ khecarī parā  
AbhTa yonyādhāreti vikhyātā śūlamūleti śabdyate 
AbhTb varṇāstatra layaṃ yānti hyavarṇe varṇarūpiṇi  
AbhTa nādiphāntaṃ samuccārya kauleśaṃ dehasaṃnibham 
AbhTb ākramya prathamaṃ cakraṃ khe yantre pādapīḍitam  
AbhTa nādaṃ vai śaktisadgarbhaṃ sadgarbhātkaulinīpadam 
AbhTb bījapañcakacāreṇa śūlabhedakrameṇa tu  
AbhTa hṛcchūlagranthibhedaiścidrudraśaktiṃ prabodhayet 
AbhTb vāyucakrāntanilayaṃ bindvākhyaṃ nābhimaṇḍalam  
AbhTa āgacchellambikāsthānaṃ sūtradvādaśanirgatam 
AbhTb candracakravilomena praviśedbhūtapañjare  
AbhTa bhūyastu kurute līlāṃ māyāpañjaravartinīm 
AbhTb punaḥ sṛṣṭiḥ saṃhṛtiśca khecaryā kriyate budhaiḥ  
AbhTa śrīmadvīrāvalīyoga eṣa syātkhecarīvidhiḥ 
AbhTb cumbākāreṇa vaktreṇa yattattvaṃ śrūyate param  
AbhTa grasamānamidaṃ viśvaṃ candrārkapuṭasaṃpuṭe 
AbhTb tenaiva syātkhagāmīti śrīmatkāmika ucyate  
AbhTa bhavānmuktvā drāvayanti pāśānmudrā hi śaktayaḥ 
AbhTb mukhyāsāṃ khecarī sā ca tridhoccāreṇa vācikī  
AbhTa triśiromudgaro devi kāyikī paripaṭhyate 
AbhTb nāsāṃ netradvayaṃ cāpi hṛtstanadvayameva ca  
AbhTa vṛṣaṇadvayaliṅgaṃ ca prāpya kāyaṃ gatā tviyam 
AbhTb bhavasthānābhavasthānamuccāreṇāvadhārayet  
AbhTa mānasīyamitastvanyāḥ padmādyā aṣṭa mudrikāḥ 
AbhTb mātṛvyūhakule tāḥ syurasyāstu parivāragāḥ  
AbhTa śarīraṃ tu samastaṃ yatkūṭākṣarasamākṛti 
AbhTb eṣā mudrā mahāmudrā bhairavasyeti gahvare  
AbhTa sūpaviṣṭaḥ padmake tu hastāgrāṅguliraśmibhiḥ 
AbhTb parāṅmukhairjhaṭityudyadraśmibhiḥ pṛṣṭhasaṃsthitaiḥ  
AbhTa antaḥsthitiḥ khecarīyaṃ saṃkocākhyā śaśāṅkinī 
AbhTb tasmādeva samuttambya bāhū caivāvakuñcitau  
AbhTa samyagvyomasu saṃsthānādvyomākhyā khecarī matā 
AbhTb muṣṭidvitayasaṅghaṭṭāddhṛdi sā hṛdayāhvāyā  
AbhTa śāntākhyā sā hastayugmamūrdhvādhaḥ sthitamudgatam 
AbhTb samadṛṣṭyāvalokyaṃ ca bahiryojitapāṇikam  
AbhTa eṣaiva śaktimudrā cedadhodhāvitapāṇikā 
AbhTb daśānāmaṅgulīnāṃ tu muṣṭibandhādanantaram  
AbhTa drākkṣepātkhecarī devī pañcakuṇḍalinī matā 
AbhTb saṃhāramudrā caiṣaiva yadyūrdhvaṃ kṣipyate kila  
AbhTa utkrāmaṇī jhagityeva paśūnāṃ pāśakartarī 
AbhTb śvabhre sudūre jhaṭiti svātmānaṃ pātayanniva  
AbhTa sāhasānupraveśena kuñcitaṃ hastayugmakam 
AbhTb adhovīkṣaṇaśīlaṃ ca samyagdṛṣṭisamanvitam  
AbhTa vīrabhairavasaṃjñeyaṃ khecarī bodhavardhinī 
AbhTb aṣṭadhetthaṃ varṇitā śrībhargāṣṭakaśikhākule  
AbhTa evaṃ nānāvidhānbhedānāśrityaikaiva yā sthitā 
AbhTb śrīkhecarī tayāviṣṭaḥ paraṃ bījaṃ prapadyate  
AbhTa ekaṃ sṛṣṭimayaṃ bījaṃ yadvīryaṃ sarvamantragam 
AbhTb ekā mudrā khecarī ca mudraughaḥ prāṇito yayā  
AbhTa tadevaṃ khecarīcakrarūḍhau yadrūpamullaset 
AbhTb tadeva mudrā mantavyā śeṣaḥ syāddehavikriyā  
AbhTa yāgādau tanmadhye tadavasitau jñānayogaparimarśe 
AbhTb vighnapraśame pāśacchede mudrāvidheḥ samayaḥ  
AbhTa bodhāveśaḥ sannidhiraikyena visarjanaṃ svarūpagatiḥ 
AbhTb śaṅkādalanaṃ cakrodayadīptiriti kramātkṛtyam  
AbhTa iti mudrāvidhiḥ proktaḥ sugūḍho yaḥ phalapradaḥ 
C atha śrītantrāloke trayastriṃśamāhnikam
AbhTa athāvasarasaṃprāpta ekīkāro nigadyate  b
AbhTb yaduktaṃ cakrabhedena sārdhaṃ pūjyamiti trikam 
AbhTc tatraiṣa cakrabhedānāmekīkāro diśānayā  
AbhTa viśvā tadīśā hāraudrī vīranetryambikā tathā 
AbhTb gurvīti ṣaḍare devyaḥ śrīsiddhāvīradarśitāḥ  
AbhTa māheśī brāhmaṇī skāndī vaiṣṇavyaindrī yamātmikā 
AbhTb cāmuṇḍā caiva yogīśītyaṣṭāghoryādayothavā  
AbhTa agninirṛtivāyvīśamātṛbhirdvādaśānvitāḥ 
AbhTb nandā bhadrā jayā kālī karālī vikṛtānanā  
AbhTa kroṣṭukī bhīmamudrā ca vāyuvegā hayānanā 
AbhTb gambhīrā ghoṣaṇī ceti caturviṃśatyare vidhiḥ  
AbhTa siddhirvṛddhirdyutirlakṣmīrmedhā kāntiḥ sudhā dhṛtiḥ 
AbhTb dīptiḥ puṣṭirmatiḥ kīrtiḥ susthitiḥ sugatiḥ smṛtiḥ  
AbhTa suprabhā ṣoḍaśī ceti śrīkaṇṭhādikaśaktayaḥ 
AbhTb baliśca balinandaśca daśagrīvo haro hayaḥ  
AbhTa mādhavaḥ ṣaḍare cakre dvādaśāre tvamī smṛtāḥ 
AbhTb dakṣaścaṇḍo haraḥ śauṇḍī pramatho bhīmamanmathau  
AbhTa śakuniḥ sumatirnando gopālaśca pitāmahaḥ 
AbhTb śrīkaṇṭhonantasūkṣmau ca trimūrtiḥ śaṃbareśvaraḥ  
AbhTa arghīśo bhārabhūtiśca sthitiḥ sthāṇurharastathā 
AbhTb jhaṇṭhibhautikasadyojānugrahakrūrasainikāḥ  
AbhTa dvyaṣṭau yadvāmṛtastena yuktāḥ pūrṇābhataddravāḥ 
AbhTb oghormisyandanāṅgāśca vapurudgāravaktrakāḥ  
AbhTa tanusecanamūrtīśāḥ sarvāmṛtadharoparaḥ 
AbhTb śrīpāṭhācchaktayaścaitāḥ ṣoḍaśaiva prakīrtitāḥ  
AbhTa saṃvartalakulibhṛgusitabakakhaṅgipinākibhujagabalikālāḥ 
AbhTb dviśchagalāṇḍau śikhiśoṇameṣamīnatridaṇḍi sāṣāḍhi  
AbhTa devīkāntatadardhau dārukahalisomanāthaśarmāṇaḥ 
AbhTb jayavijayajayantājitasujayajayarudrakīrtanāvahakāḥ  
AbhTa tanmūrtyutsāhadavardhanāśca balasubalabhadradāvahakāḥ 
AbhTb tadvāndātā ceśo nandanasamabhadratanmūrtiḥ  
AbhTa śivadasumanaḥspṛhaṇakā durgo bhadrākhyakālaśca 
AbhTb cetonugakauśikakālaviśvasuśivāstathāparaḥ kopaḥ  
AbhTa śrutyagnyare syurete strīpāṭhācchaktayastvetāḥ 
AbhTb juṃkārothāgnipatnīti ṣaḍare ṣaṇṭhavarjitāḥ  
AbhTa dvādaśāre tatsahitāḥ ṣoḍaśāre svarāḥ kramāt 
AbhTb halastaddviguṇeṣṭāre yādyaṃ hāntaṃ tu tattrike  
AbhTa dvātriṃśadarake sāntaṃ binduḥ sarveṣu mūrdhani 
AbhTb evamanyānbahūṃścakrabhedānasmātprakalpayet  
AbhTa eka eva cidātmaiṣa viśvāmarśanasārakaḥ 
AbhTb śaktistadvānato mātā śabdarāśiḥ prakīrtitau  
AbhTa tayoreva vibhāge tu śaktitadvatprakalpane 
AbhTb śabdarāśirmālinī ca kṣobhātma vapurīdṛśam  
AbhTa tathāntaḥsthaparāmarśabhedane vastutastrikam 
AbhTb anuttarecchonmeṣākhyaṃ yato viśvaṃ vimarśanam  
AbhTa ānandeśormiyoge tu tatṣaṭkaṃ samudāhṛtam 
AbhTb antaḥsthoṣmasamāyogāttadaṣṭakamudāhṛtam  
AbhTa tadāmṛtacatuṣkonabhāve dvādaśakaṃ bhavet 
AbhTb tadyoge ṣoḍaśākhyaṃ syādevaṃ yāvadasaṃkhyatā  
AbhTa viśvamekaparāmarśasahatvātprabhṛti sphuṭam 
AbhTb aṃśāṃśikāparāmarśān paryante sahate yataḥ  
AbhTa ataḥ pañcāśadaikātmyaṃ svaravyaktivirūpatā 
AbhTb vargāṣṭakaṃ varṇabheda ekāśītikalodayaḥ  
AbhTa iti pradarśitaṃ pūrvam ardhamātrāsahatvataḥ 
AbhTb svarārdhamapyasti yataḥ svaritasyārdhamātrakam  
AbhTa tasyādita udāttaṃ tatkathitaṃ padavedinā 
AbhTb itthaṃ saṃvidiyaṃ yājyasvarūpāmarśarūpiṇī  
AbhTa abhinnaṃ saṃvidaścaitaccakrāṇāṃ cakravālakam 
AbhTb svāmyāvaraṇabhedena bahudhā tatprayojayet  
AbhTa parāparā parā cānyā sṛṣṭisthititirodhayaḥ 
AbhTb mātṛsadbhāvarūpā tu turyā viśrāntirucyate  
AbhTa tacca prakāśaṃ vaktrasthaṃ sūcitaṃ tu pade pade 
AbhTb turye viśrāntirādheyā mātṛsadbhāvasāriṇi  
AbhTa tathāsya viśvamābhāti svātmatanmayatāṃ gatam 
AbhTb ityeṣa śāstrārthasyokta ekīkāro gurūditaḥ  
C atha śrītantrāloke catustriṃśamāhnikam
AbhTa ucyatetha svasvarūpapraveśaḥ kramasaṅgataḥ  b
AbhTb yadetadbahudhā proktamāṇavaṃ śivatāptaye 
AbhTc tatrāntarantarāviśya viśrāmyetsavidhe pade  
AbhTa tatopyāṇavasaṃtyāgācchāktīṃ bhūmimupāśrayet 
AbhTb tatopi śāmbhavīmevaṃ tāratamyakramātsphuṭam  
AbhTa itthaṃ kramoditavibodhamahāmarīcisaṃpūritaprasarabhairavabhāvabhāgī 
AbhTb antebhyupāyanirapekṣatayaiva nityaṃ svātmānamāviśati garbhitaviśvarūpam  
AbhTa kathitoyaṃ svasvarūpapraveśaḥ parameṣṭhinā 
C atha śrītantrāloke pañcatriṃśamāhnikam
AbhTa athocyate samastānāṃ śāstrāṇāmiha melanam 
AbhTb iha tāvatsama stoyaṃ vyavahāraḥ purātanaḥ  
AbhTa prasiddhimanusandhāya saiva cāgama ucyate 
AbhTb anvayavyatirekau hi prasiddherupajīvakau  
AbhTa svāyattatve tayorvyaktipūge kiṃ syāttayorgatiḥ 
AbhTb pratyakṣamapi netrātmadīpārthādiviśeṣajam  
AbhTa apekṣate tatra mūle prasiddhiṃ tāṃ tathātmikām 
AbhTb abhitaḥsaṃvṛte jāta ekākī kṣudhitaḥ śiśuḥ  
AbhTa kiṃ karotu kimādattāṃ kena paśyatu kiṃ vrajet 
AbhTb nanu vastuśatākīrṇe sthānepyasya yadeva hi  
AbhTa paśyato jighrato vāpi spṛśataḥ saṃprasīdati 
AbhTb cetastadevādāya drāk sonvayavyatirekabhāk  
AbhTa hanta cetaḥprasādopi yosāvarthaviśeṣagaḥ 
AbhTb sopi prāgvāsanārūpavimarśaparikalpitaḥ  
AbhTa na pratyakṣānumānādibāhyamānaprasādajaḥ 
AbhTb prāgvāsanopajīvyetat pratibhāmātrameva na  
AbhTa na mṛdabhyavahārecchā puṃso bālasya jāyate 
AbhTb prāgvāsanopajīvī cedvimarśaḥ sā ca vāsanā  
AbhTa prācyā cedāgatā seyaṃ prasiddhiḥ paurvakālikī 
AbhTb naca cetaḥprasattyaiva sarvo vyavahṛtikramaḥ  
AbhTa mūlaṃ prasiddhistanmānaṃ sarvatraiveti gṛhyatām 
AbhTb pūrvapūrvopajīvitvamārgaṇe sā kvacitsvayam  
AbhTa sarvajñarūpe hyekasminniḥśaṅkaṃ bhāsata purā 
AbhTb vyavahāro hi naikatra samastaḥ kopi mātari  
AbhTa tenāsarvajñapūrvatvamātreṇaiṣā na siddhyati 
AbhTb bahusarvajñapūrvatve na mānaṃ cāsti kiṃcana  
AbhTa bhogāpavargataddhetuprasiddhiśataśobhitaḥ 
AbhTb tadvimarśasvabhāvosau bhairavaḥ parameśvaraḥ  
AbhTa tataścāṃśāṃśikāyogātsā prasiddhiḥ paramparām 
AbhTb śāstraṃ vāśritya vitatā lokānsaṃvyavahārayet  
AbhTa tayaivāśaiśavātsarve vyavahāradharājuṣaḥ 
AbhTb santaḥ samupajīvanti śaivamevādyamāgamam  
AbhTa apūrṇāstu pare tena na mokṣaphalabhāginaḥ 
AbhTb upajīvanti yāvattu tāvattatphalabhāginaḥ  
AbhTa bālyāpāyepi yadbhoktumannameṣa pravartate 
AbhTb tatprasiddhyaiva nādhyakṣānnānumānādasambhavāt  
AbhTa naca kāpyatra doṣāśāśaṅkāyāśca nivṛttitaḥ 
AbhTb prasiddhiścāvigānotthā pratītiḥ śabdanātmikā  
AbhTa mātuḥ svabhāvo yattasyāṃ śaṅkate naiṣa jātucit 
AbhTb svakṛtatvavaśādeva sarvavitsa hi śaṅkaraḥ  
AbhTa yāvattu śivatā nāsya tāvatsvātmānusāriṇīm 
AbhTb tāvatīmeva tāmeṣa prasiddhiṃ nābhiśaṅkate  
AbhTa anyasyāmabhiśaṅkī syādbhūyastāṃ bahu manyate 
AbhTb evaṃ bhāviśivatvomūṃ prasiddhiṃ manyate dhruvam  
AbhTa eka evāgamaścāyaṃ vibhunā sarvadarśinā 
AbhTb darśito yaḥ pravṛtte ca nivṛtte ca pathi sthitaḥ  
AbhTa dharmārthakāmamokṣeṣu pūrṇāpūrṇādibhedataḥ 
AbhTb vicitreṣu phaleṣveka upāyaḥ śāmbhavāgamaḥ  
AbhTa tasminviṣayavaiviktyādvicitraphaladāyini 
AbhTb citropāyopadeśopi na virodhāvaho bhavet  
AbhTa laukikaṃ vaidikaṃ sāṅkhyaṃ yogādi pāñcarātrakam 
AbhTb bauddhārhatanyāyaśāstraṃ padārthakramatantraṇam  
AbhTa siddhāntatantraśāktādi sarvaṃ brahmodbhavaṃ yataḥ 
AbhTb śrīsvacchandādiṣu proktaṃ sadyojātādibhedataḥ  
AbhTa yathaikatrāpi vedādau tattadāśramagāminaḥ 
AbhTb saṃskārāntaramatrāpi tathā liṅgoddhṛtādikam  
AbhTa yathāca tatra pūrvasminnāśrame nottarāśramāt 
AbhTb phalameti tathā pāñcarātrādau na śivātmatām  
AbhTa eka evāgamastasmāttatra laukikaśāstrataḥ 
AbhTb prabhṛtyāvaiṣṇavādbauddhācchaivātsarvaṃ hi niṣṭhitam  
AbhTa tasya yattat paraṃ prāpyaṃ dhāma tat trikaśabditam 
AbhTb sarvāvibhedānucchedāt tadeva kulamucyate  
AbhTa yathordhvādharatābhāksu dehāṅgeṣu vibhediṣu 
AbhTb ekaṃ prāṇitamevaṃ syāt trikaṃ sarveṣu śāstrataḥ  
AbhTa śrīmatkālīkule coktaṃ pañcasrotovivarjitam 
AbhTb daśāṣṭādaśabhedasya sārametatprakīrtitam  
AbhTa puṣpe gandhastile tailaṃ dehe jīvo jalemṛtam 
AbhTb yathā tathaiva śāstrāṇāṃ kulamantaḥ pratiṣṭhitam  
AbhTa tadeka evāgamoyaṃ citraścitredhikāriṇi 
AbhTb tathaiva sā prasiddhirhi svayūthyaparayūthyagā  
AbhTa sāṃkhyaṃ yogaṃ pāñcarātraṃ vedāṃścaiva na nindayet 
AbhTb yataḥ śivodbhavāḥ sarva iti svacchandaśāsane  
AbhTa ekasmādāgamāccaite khaṇḍakhaṇḍā vyapoddhṛtāḥ 
AbhTb loke syurāgamāstaiśca jano bhrāmyati mohitaḥ  
AbhTa anekāgamapakṣepi vācyā viṣayabheditā 
AbhTb avaśyamūrdhvādharatāsthityā prāmāṇyasiddhaye  
AbhTa anyathā naiva kasyāpi prāmāṇyaṃ siddhyati dhruvam 
AbhTb nityatvamavisaṃvāda iti no mānakāraṇam  
AbhTa asminnaṃśepyamuṣyaiva prāmāṇyaṃ syāttathoditeḥ 
AbhTb anyathāvyākṛtau kḷptāvasatyatve prarocane  
AbhTa atiprasaṅga sarvasyāpyāgamasyāpabādhakaḥ 
AbhTb avaśyopetya ityasminmāna āgamanāmani  
AbhTa avaśyopetyamevaitacchāstraniṣṭhānirūpaṇam 
AbhTb pradhāneṅge kṛto yatnaḥ phalavānvastuto yataḥ  
AbhTa atosmin yatnavān kopi bhavecchaṃbhupracoditaḥ 
AbhTb tatra tatra ca śāstreṣu nyarūpyata maheśinā  
AbhTa etāvatyadhikārī yaḥ sa durlabha iti sphuṭam 
AbhTb itthaṃ śrīśambhunāthena mamoktaṃ śāstramelanam  
C atha śrītantrāloke ṣaṭtriṃśamāhnikam
AbhTa āyātiratha śāstrasya kathyatevasarāgatā b
AbhTb śrīsiddhādivinirdiṣṭā gurubhiśca nirūpitā 
AbhTc bhairavo bhairavī devī svacchando lākuloṇurāṭ  
AbhTa gahaneśobjajaḥ śakro guruḥ koṭyapakarṣataḥ 
AbhTb navabhiḥ kramaśodhītaṃ navakoṭipravistaram  
AbhTa etaistato guruḥ koṭimātrāt pādaṃ vitīrṇavān 
AbhTb dakṣādibhya ubhau pādau saṃvartādibhya eva ca  
AbhTa pādaṃ ca vāmanādibhyaḥ pādārdhaṃ bhārgavāya ca 
AbhTb pādapādaṃ tu balaye pādapādastu yoparaḥ  
AbhTa siṃhāyārdhaṃ tataḥ śiṣṭāddvau bhāgau vinatābhuve 
AbhTb pādaṃ vāsukināgāya khaṇḍāḥ saptadaśa tvamī  
AbhTa svargādardhaṃ rāvaṇotha jahre rāmordhamapyataḥ 
AbhTb vibhīṣaṇamukhādāpa guruśiṣyavidhikramāt  
AbhTa khaṇḍairekānnaviṃśatyā vibhaktaṃ tadabhūttataḥ 
AbhTb khaṇḍaṃ khaṇḍaṃ cāṣṭakhaṇḍaṃ proktapādādibhedataḥ  
AbhTa pādo mūloddhārāvuttaravṛhaduttare tathā kalpaḥ 
AbhTb sāṃhitakalpaskandāvanuttaraṃ vyāpakaṃ tridhā tisraḥ  
AbhTa devyotra nirūpyante kramaśo vistāriṇaiva rūpeṇa 
AbhTb navame pade tu gaṇanā na kāciduktā vyavacchidāhīne  
AbhTa rāmācca lakṣmaṇastasmāt siddhāstebhyopi dānavāḥ 
AbhTb guhyakāśca tatastebhyo yogino nṛvarāstataḥ  
AbhTa teṣāṃ krameṇa tanmadhye bhraṣṭaṃ kālāntarādyadā 
AbhTb tadā śrīkaṇṭhanāthājñāvaśāt siddhā avātaram  
AbhTa tryambakāmardakābhikhyaśrīnāthā advaye dvaye 
AbhTb dvayādvaye ca nipuṇāḥ krameṇa śivaśāsane  
AbhTa ādyasya cānvayo jajñe dvitīyo duhitṛkramāt 
AbhTb sa cārdhatryambakābhikhyaḥ saṃtānaḥ supratiṣṭhitaḥ  
AbhTa ataścārdhacatasrotra maṭhikāḥ saṃtatikramāt 
AbhTb śiṣyapraśiṣyairvistīrṇāḥ śataśākhaṃ vyavasthitaiḥ  
AbhTa adhyuṣṭasaṃtatisrotaḥsārabhūtarasāhṛtim 
AbhTb vidhāya tantrālokoyaṃ syandate sakalānrasān  
AbhTa uktāyātirupādeyabhāvo nirṇīyatedhunā 
C atha śrītantrāloke saptatriṃśamāhnikam
AbhTa uktanītyaiva sarvatra vyavahāre pravartite 
AbhTb prasiddhāvupajīvyāyāmavaśyagrāhya āgamaḥ  
AbhTa yathā laukikadṛṣṭyānyaphalabhāk tatprasiddhitaḥ 
AbhTb samyagvyavaharaṃstadvacchivabhāk tatprasiddhitaḥ  
AbhTa tadavaśyagrahītavye śāstre svāṃśopadeśini 
AbhTb manākphalebhyupādeyatamaṃ tadviparītakam  
AbhTa yathā khageśvarībhāvaniḥśaṅkatvādviṣaṃ vrajet 
AbhTb kṣayaṃ karmasthitistadvadaśaṅkādbhairavatvataḥ  
AbhTa yadārṣe pātahetūktaṃ tadasminvāmaśāsane 
AbhTb āśusiddhyai yataḥ sarvamārṣaṃ māyodarasthitam  
AbhTa tacca yatsarvasarvajñadṛṣṭaṃ taccāpi kiṃ bhavet 
AbhTb yadaśeṣopadeśena sūyatenuttaraṃ phalam  
AbhTa yathādharādharaproktavastutattvānuvādataḥ 
AbhTb uttaraṃ kathitaṃ saṃvitsiddhaṃ taddhi tathā bhavet  
AbhTa yaduktādhikasaṃvittisiddhavastunirūpaṇāt 
AbhTb apūrṇasarvavitproktirjñāyatedharaśāsane  
AbhTa ūrdhvaśāsanavastvaṃśe dṛṣṭvāpica samujjhite 
AbhTb adhaḥ śāstreṣu māyātvaṃ lakṣyate sargarakṣaṇāt  
AbhTa śrīmadānandaśāstrādau proktaṃ ca parameśinā 
AbhTb ṛṣivākyaṃ bahukleśamadhruvālpaphalaṃ mitam  
AbhTa naiva pramāṇayedvidvān śaivamevāgamaṃ śrayet 
AbhTb tadārṣe pātahetūktaṃ tadasmin vāmaśāsane  
AbhTa āśusiddhyai yataḥ sarvamārṣaṃ māyodarasthitam 
AbhTb yathā khageśvarībhāvaniḥśaṅkatvādviṣaṃ vrajet  
AbhTa kṣayaṃ karmasthitistadvadaśaṅkādbhairavatvataḥ 
AbhTb ajñatvānupadeṣṭṛtvasaṃdaṣṭedharaśāsane  
AbhTa etadviparyayādgrāhyamavaśyaṃ śivaśāsanam 
AbhTb dvāvāptau tatra ca śrīmacchrīkaṇṭhalakuleśvarau  
AbhTa dvipravāhamidaṃ śāstraṃ mamyaṅniḥśreyasapradam 
AbhTb prācyasya tu yathābhīṣṭabhogadatvamapi sthitam  
AbhTa tacca pañcavidhaṃ proktaṃ śaktivaicitryacitritam 
AbhTb pañcasrota iti proktaṃ śrīmacchrīkaṇṭhaśāsanam  
AbhTa daśāṣṭādaśadhā srotaḥpañcakaṃ yattatopyalam 
AbhTb utkṛṣṭaṃ bhairavābhikhyaṃ catuḥṣaṣṭivibheditam  
AbhTa śrīmadānandaśāstrādau proktaṃ bhagavatā kila 
AbhTb samūhaḥ pīṭhametacca dvidhā dakṣiṇavāmataḥ  
AbhTa mantro vidyeti tasmācca mudrāmaṇḍalagaṃ dvayam 
AbhTb mananatrāṇadaṃ yattu mantrākhyaṃ tatra vidyayā  
AbhTa upodbalanamāpyāyaḥ sā hi vedyārthabhāsinī 
AbhTb mantrapratikṛtirmudrā tadāpyāyanakārakam  
AbhTa maṇḍalaṃ sāramuktaṃ hi maṇḍaśrutyā śivāhvayam 
AbhTb evamanyonyasaṃbhedavṛtti pīṭhacatuṣṭayam  
AbhTa yatastasmādbhavetsarvaṃ pīṭhe pīṭhepi vastutaḥ 
AbhTb pradhānatvāttasya tasya vastuno bhinnatā punaḥ  
AbhTa kathitā sādhakendrāṇāṃ tattadvastuprasiddhaye 
AbhTb pratyekaṃ taccaturdhaivaṃ maṇḍalaṃ mudrikā tathā  
AbhTa mantro vidyeti ca pīṭhamutkṛṣṭaṃ cottarottam 
AbhTb vidyāpīṭhapradhānaṃ ca siddhayogīśvarīmatam  
AbhTa tasyāpi paramaṃ sāraṃ mālinīvijayottaram 
AbhTb uktaṃ śrīratnamālāyāmetacca parameśinā  
AbhTa aśeṣatantrasāraṃ tu vāmadakṣiṇamāśritam 
AbhTb ekatra militaṃ kaulaṃ śrīṣaḍardhakaśāsane  
AbhTa siddhānte karma bahulaṃ malamāyādirūṣitam 
AbhTb dakṣiṇaṃ raudrakarmāḍhyaṃ vāmaṃ siddhisamākulam  
AbhTa svalpapuṇyaṃ bahukleśaṃ svapratītivivarjitam 
AbhTb mokṣavidyāvihīnaṃ ca vinayaṃ tyaja dūrataḥ  
AbhTa yasminkāle ca guruṇā nirvikalpaṃ prakāśitam 
AbhTb muktastenaiva kālena yantraṃ tiṣṭhati kevalam  
AbhTa mayaitatsrotasāṃ rūpamanuttarapadāddhruvāt 
AbhTb ārabhya vistareṇoktaṃ mālinīślokavārtike  
AbhTa jijñāsustata evedamavadhārayituṃ kṣamaḥ 
AbhTb vayaṃ tūktānuvacanamaphalaṃ nādriyāmahe  
AbhTa itthaṃ dadadanāyāsājjīvanmuktimahāphalam 
AbhTb yathepsitamahābhogadātṛtvena vyavasthitam  
AbhTa ṣaḍardhasāraṃ sacchāstramupādeyamidaṃ sphuṭam 
AbhTb ṣaṭtriṃśatā tattvabalena sūtā yadyapyanantā bhuvanāvalīyam 
AbhTc brahmāṇḍamatyantamanoharaṃ tu vaicitryavarjaṃ nahi ramyabhāvaḥ  
AbhTa bhūrādisaptapurapūrṇatamepi tasmin manye dvitīyabhuvanaṃ bhavanaṃ sukhasya 
AbhTb kvānyatra citragatisūryaśaśāṅkaśobhirātrindivaprasarabhogavibhāgabhūṣā  
AbhTa tatrāpica tridivabhogamahārghavarṣadvīpāntarādadhikameva kumārikāhvam 
AbhTb yatrādharādharapadātparamaṃ śivāntamāroḍhumapyadhikṛtiḥ kṛtināmanarghā  
AbhTa prākkarmabhogipaśutocitabhogabhājā kiṃ janmanā nanu sukhaikapadepi dhāmni 
AbhTb sarvo hi bhāvini paraṃ paritoṣameti saṃbhāvite natu nimeṣiṇi vartamāne  
AbhTa kanyāhvayepi bhuvanetra paraṃ mahīyān deśaḥ sa yatra kila śāstravarāṇi cakṣuḥ 
AbhTb jātyandhasadmani na janma na kobhinindedbhinnāñjanāyitaravipramukhaprakāśe  
AbhTa niḥśeṣaśāstrasadanaṃ kila madhyadeśastasminnajāyata guṇābhyadhiko dvijanmā 
AbhTb kopyatrigupta iti nāmaniruktagotraḥ śāstrābdhicarvaṇakalodyadagastyagotraḥ  
AbhTa tamatha lalitādityo rājā nijaṃ puramānayat praṇayarabhasāt kaśmīrākhyaṃ himālayamūrdhagam 
AbhTb adhivasati yadgaurīkāntaḥ karairvijayādibhiryugapadakhilaṃ bhogāsāraṃ rasāt paricarcitum  
AbhTa sthāne sthāne munibhirakhilaiścakrire yannivāsā yaccādhyāste pratipadamidaṃ sa svayaṃ candracūḍaḥ 
AbhTb tanmanyehaṃ samabhilaṣitāśeṣasiddhernasiddhyai kaśmīrebhyaḥ paramatha puraṃ pūrṇavṛtterna tuṣṭyai  
AbhTa yatra svayaṃ śāradacandraśubhrā śrīśāradeti prathitā janeṣu 
AbhTb śāṇḍilyasevārasasuprasannā sarvaṃ janaṃ svairvibhavairyunakti  
AbhTa nāraṅgāruṇakānti pāṇḍuvikacadballāvadātacchavi prodbhinnāmalamātuluṅgakanakacchāyābhirāmaprabham 
AbhTb kerīkuntalakandalīpratikṛtiśyāmaprabhābhāsvaraṃ yasmiñśakticatuṣṭayojjvalamalaṃ madyaṃ mahābhairavam  
AbhTa trinayanamahākopajvālāvilīna iha sthito madanaviśikhavrāto madyacchalena vijṛmbhate 
AbhTb kathamitarathā rāgaṃ mohaṃ madaṃ madanajvaraṃ vidadhadaniśaṃ kāmātaṅkairvaśīkurute jagat  
AbhTa yatkāntānāṃ praṇayavacasi prauḍhimānaṃ vidatte yannirvighnaṃ nidhuvanavidhau sādhvasaṃ saṃdhunoti 
AbhTb yasmin viśvāḥ kalitarucayo devatāścakracaryastanmārdvīkaṃ sapadi tanute yatra bhogāpabargau  
AbhTa udyadgaurāṅkuravikasitaiḥ śyāmaraktaiḥ palāśairantargāḍhāruṇarucilasatkesarālīvicitraiḥ 
AbhTb ākīrṇā bhūḥ pratipadamasau yatra kāśmīrapuṣpaiḥ samyagdevītritayayajanodyānamāviṣkaroti  
AbhTa sarvo lokaḥ kaviratha budho yatra śūropi vāgmī candroddyotā masṛṇagatayaḥ pauranāryaśca yatra 
AbhTb yatrāṅgārojjvalavikasitānantasauṣumṇamārgagrastārkendurgaganavimalo yoginīnāṃ ca vargaḥ  
AbhTa śrīmatparaṃ pravaranāma puraṃ ca tatra yannirmame pravarasena iti kṣitīśaḥ 
AbhTb yaḥ svapratiṣṭhitamaheśvarapūjanānte vyomotpatannudasṛjatkila dhūpaghaṇṭām  
AbhTa āndolanoditamanoharavīranādaiḥ sā cāsya tatsucaritaṃ prathayāṃbabhūva 
AbhTb sadvṛttasāragurutaijasamūrtayo hi tyaktā api prabhuguṇānadhikaṃ dhvananti  
AbhTa saṃpūrṇacandravimaladyutivīrakāntāgāḍhāṅgarāgaghanakuṅkumapiñjaraśrīḥ 
AbhTb proddhūtavetasalatāsitacāmaraughairājyābhiṣekamaniśaṃ dadatī smarasya  
AbhTa rodhaḥpratiṣṭhitamaheśvarasiddhaliṅgasvāyaṃbhuvārcanavilepanagandhapuṣpaiḥ 
AbhTb āvarjyamānatanuvīcinimajjanaughavidhvastapāpmamunisiddhamanuṣyavandyā  
AbhTa bhogāpavargaparipūraṇakalpavallī bhogaikadānarasikāṃ surasiddhasindhum 
AbhTb nyakkurvatī harapinākakalāvatīrṇā yadbhūṣayatyavirataṃ taṭinī vitastā  
AbhTa tasmin kuverapuracārisiṃtāṃśumaulisāṃmukhyadarśanavirūḍhapavitrabhāve 
AbhTb vaitastarodhasi nivāsamamuṣya cakre rājā dvijasya parikalpitabhūrisaṃpat  
AbhTa tasyānvaye mahati kopi varāhaguptanāmā babhūva bhagavān svayamantakāle 
AbhTb gīrvāṇasindhulaharīkalitāgramūrdhā yasyākarot paramanugrahamāgraheṇa  
AbhTa tasyātmajaścukhalaketi jane prasiddhaścandrāvadātadhiṣaṇo narasiṃhaguptaḥ 
AbhTb yaṃ sarvaśāstrarasamajjanaśubhracittaṃ māheśvarī paramalaṃkurute sma bhaktiḥ  
AbhTa tāruṇyasāgarataraṅgabharānapohya vairāgyapotamadhiruhya dṛḍhaṃ haṭhena 
AbhTb yo bhaktirohaṇamavāpya maheśacintāratnairalaṃ dalayati sma bhavāpadastāḥ  
AbhTa tasyātmajobhinavagupta iti prasiddhaḥ śrīcandracūḍacaraṇābjaparāgapūtaḥ 
AbhTb mātā vyayūyujadamuṃ kila bālya eva daivaṃ hi bhāviparikarmaṇi saṃskaroti  
AbhTa mātā paraṃ bandhuriti pravādaḥ snohotigāḍhīkurute hi pāśān 
AbhTb tanmūlabandhe galite kilāsya manye sthitā jīvata eva muktiḥ  
AbhTa pitrā sa śabdagahane kṛtasaṃpraveśastarkārṇavormipṛṣatāmalapūtacittaḥ 
AbhTb sāhityasāndrarasabhogaparo maheśabhaktyā svayaṃgrahaṇadurmadayā gṛhītaḥ  
AbhTa sa tanmayībhūya na lokavartanīmajīgaṇat kāmapi kevalaṃ punaḥ 
AbhTb tadīyasaṃbhogavivṛddhaye purā karoti dāsyaṃ guruveśmasu svayam  
AbhTa ānandasaṃtatimahārṇavakarṇadhāraḥ saddaiśikairakavarātmajavāmanāthaḥ 
AbhTb śrīnāthasaṃtatimahāmbaragharmakāntiḥ śrībhūtirājatanayaḥ svapitṛprasādaḥ  
AbhTa traiyambakaprasarasāgaraśāyisomānandātmajotpalajalakṣmaṇaguptanāthaḥ 
AbhTb turyākhyasaṃtatimahodadhipūrṇacandraḥ śrīsomataḥ sakalavitkila śaṃbhunāthaḥ  
AbhTa śrīcandraśarmabhavabhaktivilāsayogānandābhinandaśivaśaktivicitranāthāḥ 
AbhTb anyepi dharmaśivavāmanakodbhaṭaśrībhūteśabhāskaramukhapramukhā mahāntaḥ  
AbhTa ete sevārasaviracitānugrahāḥ śāstrasārapauḍhādeśaprakaṭasubhagaṃ svādhikāraṃ kilāsmai 
AbhTb yat saṃprāduryadapi ca janānnaikṣatākṣetrabhūtān svātmārāmastadayamaniśaṃ tattvasevārasobhūt  
AbhTa sonugrahītumatha śāṃbhavabhaktibhājaṃ svaṃ bhrātaramakhilaśāstravimarśapūrṇam 
AbhTb yāvanmanaḥ praṇidadhāti manorathākhyaṃ tāvajjanaḥ katipayastamupāsasāda  
AbhTa śrīśaurisaṃjñatanayaḥ kila karṇanāmā yo yauvane viditaśāṃbhavatattvasāraḥ 
AbhTb dehaṃ tyajan prathayati sma janasya satyaṃ yogacyutaṃ prati mahāmunikṛṣṇavākyam  
AbhTa tadbālamitramatha mantrisutaḥ prasiddhaḥ śrīmandra ityakhilasāraguṇābhirāmaḥ 
AbhTb lakṣmīsarasvati samaṃ yamalaṃcakāra sāpatnakaṃ tirayate subhagaprabhāvaḥ  
AbhTa anye pitṛvyatanayāḥ śivaśaktiśubhrāḥ kṣemotpalābhinavacakrakapadmaguptāḥ 
AbhTb ye saṃpadaṃ tṛṇamamaṃsata śaṃbhusevāsaṃpūritaṃ svahṛdayaṃ hṛdi bhāvayantaḥ  
AbhTa ṣaḍardhaśāstreṣu samastameva yenādhijagme vidhimaṇḍalādi 
AbhTb sa rāmagupto guruśaṃbhuśāstrasevāvidhivyagrasamagramārgaḥ  
AbhTa anyopi kaścana janaḥ śivaśaktipātasaṃpreraṇāparavaśasvakaśaktisārthaḥ 
AbhTb abhyarthanāvimukhabhāvamaśikṣitena tenāpyanugrahapadaṃ kṛta eṣa vargaḥ  
AbhTa ācāryamabhyarthayate sma gāḍhaṃ saṃpūrṇatantrādhigamāya samyak 
AbhTb jāyeta daivānugṛhītabuddheḥ saṃpatprabandhaikarasaiva saṃpat  
AbhTa sopyabhyupāgamadabhīpsitamasya yadvā svātodyameva hi ninartiṣatovatīrṇam 
AbhTb sonugrahapravaṇa eva hi sadgurūṇāmājñāvaśena śubhasūtimahāṅkureṇa  
AbhTa vikṣiptabhāvaparihāramatho cikīrṣan mandraḥ svake puravare sthitimasya vavre 
AbhTb ābālagopamapi yatra maheśvarasya dāsyaṃ janaścarati pīṭhanivāsakalpe  
AbhTa tasyābhavat kila pitṛvyavadhūrvidhātrā yā nirmame galitasaṃsṛticitracintā 
AbhTb śītāṃśumaulicaraṇābjaparāgamātrabhūṣāvidhirvihitavatsalikocitākhyā  
AbhTa mūrtā kṣameva karuṇeva gṛhītadehā dhāreva vigrahavatī śubhaśīlatāyāḥ 
AbhTb vairāgyasāraparipākadaśeva pūrṇā tattvārtharatnarucirasthitirohaṇorvī  
AbhTa bhrātāpi tasyāḥ śaśiśubhramaulerbhaktyā paraṃ pāvitacittavṛttiḥ 
AbhTb sa śaurirātteśvaramantribhāvastatyāja yo bhūpatimantribhāvam  
AbhTa tasya snuṣā karṇavadhūrvidhūtasaṃsāravṛttiḥ sutamekameva 
AbhTb yāsūta yogeśvaridattasaṃjñaṃ nāmānurūpasphuradarthatattvam  
AbhTa yāmagrage vayasi bhartṛviyogadīnāmanvagrahīt trinayanaḥ svayameva bhaktyā 
AbhTb bhāviprabhāvarabhaseṣu janeṣvanarthaḥ satyaṃ samākṛṣati sorthaparamparāṇām  
AbhTa bhaktyullasatpulakatāṃ sphuṭamaṅgabhūṣāṃ śrīśaṃbhunāthanatimeva lalāṭikāṃ ca 
AbhTb śaivaśrutiṃ śravaṇabhūṣaṇamapyavāpya saubhāgyamabhyadhikamudvahati sma yāntaḥ  
AbhTa ambābhidhānā kila sā guruṃ taṃ svaṃ bhrātaraṃ śaṃbhudṛśābhyapaśyat 
AbhTb bhāviprabhāvojjvalabhavyabuddhiḥ satovajānāti na bandhubuddhyā  
AbhTa bhrātā tadīyobhinavaśca nāmnā na kevalaṃ saccaritairapi svaiḥ 
AbhTb pītena vijñānarasena yasya tatraiva tṛṣṇā vavṛdhe nikāmam  
AbhTa sonyaśca śāṃbhavamarīcicayapraṇaśyatsaṃkocahārdanalinīghaṭitojjvalaśrīḥ 
AbhTb taṃ lumpakaḥ paricacāra samudyameṣu sādhuḥ samāvahati hanta karāvalambam  
AbhTa itthaṃ gṛhe vatsalikāvitīrṇe sthitaḥ samādhāya matiṃ bahūni 
AbhTb pūrvaśrutānyākalayan svabuddhyā śāstrāṇi tebhyaḥ samavāpa sāram  
AbhTa sa tannibandhaṃ vidadhe mahārthaṃ yuktyāgamodīritatantratattvam 
AbhTb ālokamāsādya yadīyameṣa lokaḥ sukhaṃ saṃcaritā kriyāsu  
AbhTa santonugṛhṇīta kṛtiṃ tadīyāṃ hṛhṇīta pūrvaṃ vidhireṣa tāvat 
AbhTb tatopi gṛhṇātu bhavanmatiṃ sā sadyonugṛhṇātu ca tattvadṛṣṭyā  
AbhTa idamabhinavaguptaprombhitaṃ śāstrasāraṃ śiva niśamaya tāvat sarvataḥśrotratantraḥ 
AbhTb tava kila nutireṣā sā hi tvadrūpacarcetyabhinavaparituṣṭo lokamātmīkuruṣva
